 loke yeṣu  artheṣu prasiddhāni padāni tāni sati sambhave tad arthāni  eva sūtreṣu  iti  avagantavyam na adhyāhāra ādibhiḥ  eṣām parikalpanīyaḥ  arthaḥ paribhāṣitavyaḥ  vā evam hi veda vākyāni  eva ebhiḥ  vyākhyāyante itarathā veda vākyāni vyākhyeyāni sva padārthāḥ  ca vyākhyeyāḥ tad  yatna gauravam prasajyeta tatra loke ayam athaśabdaḥ  vṛttād anantarasya prakriyā arthaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ na ca iha kiñcid  vṛttam upalabhyate bhavitavyam tu tena yasmin sati  anantaram dharma jijñāsā avakalpate tathā hi prasiddha padārthakaḥ sa kalpitaḥ  bhavati tad  tu veda adhyayanam tasmin hi sati sā avakalpate na etad  evam anyasya api karmaṇaḥ  anantaram dharma jijñāsā yuktā prāk  api ca veda adhyayanāt  ucyate tādṛśīm tu dharma jijñāsām adhikṛtya atha śabdam prayuktavān ācāryaḥ yā veda adhyayanam antareṇa na saṃbhavati katham veda vākyānām anekavidhaḥ vicāra iha vartiṣyate api ca na eva vayam iha veda adhyayanāt  pūrvam dharma jijñāsāyāḥ pratiṣedham śiṣmaḥ na hi  etad  ekam vākyam purastāt  ca veda adhyayanāt  dharma jijñāsām pratiṣedhiṣyati parastāt  ca ānantaryam prakariṣyati bhidyeta hi tathā vākyam anyā hi vacana vyaktiḥ  asya purastād veda adhyāyanād dharma jijñāsām pratiṣedhataḥ anyā ca parastād ānantaryam upadiśataḥ vedān adhītya iti  ekasyām vidhīyate anūdya ānantaryam viparītam anyasyām artha eka tvāt  ca eka vākyatām vakṣyati kim tu  adhīte vede dvayam āpatati guru kulāt  ca samāvartitavyam veda vākyāni ca vicārayitavyāni tatra guru kulān mā samāvartiṣṭa katham nu veda vākyāni vicārayet  iti  evam arthaḥ  ayam upadeśaḥ yadi  evam na tarhi veda adhyayanam pūrvam dharma jijñāsāyāḥ evam hi samāmananti vedam adhītya snāyāt  iti iha ca vedam adhītya snāsyan dharmam jijñāsamāna imam āmnā ayam atikrāmet  na ca āmnāyaḥ  nāma atikramitavyaḥ tad  ucyate atikramiṣyāma imam āmnā ayam anatikrāmantaḥ  vedam arthavantam santam anarthakam kalpayema dṛṣṭaḥ  hi tasya arthaḥ karma avabodhanam nāma na ca tasya adhyayana mātrāt tatrabhavantaḥ  yājñikāḥ phalam samāmananti yad  api ca samām anantī iva tatra api dravya saṃskāra karmasu para artha tvāt  phala śrutiḥ  artha vādaḥ syāt  iti  artha vāda tām vakṣyati na ca adhīta vedasya snāna ānantaryam etad  vidhīyate na hi  atra ānataryasya vaktā kaścid  chabdaḥ  asti pūrva kāla tāyām hi ktvā smaryate na ānantarye dṛṣṭa artha tā ca adhyayanasya ānantarye vyāhanyeta lakṣaṇayā tu  eṣaḥ  arthaḥ syāt  na ca idam snānam adṛṣṭa artham vidhīyate kim tu lakṣaṇa yāsnāna ādi niyamasya paryavasānam veda adhyayana sama kālam āhuḥ vedam adhītya snāyāt  guru kulān mā samāvartiṣṭa iti  adṛṣṭa artha tā parihārāya eva tasmāt  veda adhyayanam eva pūrvam abhinirvartya ānanataram dharmaḥ  jijñāsitavya iti  athaśabdasya sāmarthyam na brūmaḥ  anyasya api karmaṇaḥ  anantaram dharma jijñāsā na kartavyā iti kim tu vedam adhītya tvaritena na snātavyam anantaram dharmaḥ  jijñāsitavya iti  atha śabdasya arthaḥ atas śabdaḥ  vṛttasya apadeśa kaḥ hetu arthena yathā kṣemasu bhikṣaḥ  ayam deśaḥ atas  aham asmin deśe prativasāmi iti evam adhītaḥ  vedaḥ  dharma jijñāsāyām hetuḥ  jñātaḥ anantaram dharmaḥ  jijñāsitavyaḥ iti  atas śabdasya sāmarthyam dharmāya hi veda vākyāni vicārayitum anadhīta vedaḥ  na śaknuyāt  atas  etasmāt  kāraṇāt  anantaram dharmam jijñāsitum icchet  iti  atas śabdasya arthaḥ dharmāya jijñāsā dharma jijñāsā sā hi tasya jñātum icchā sa punar  katham jijñāsitavyaḥ kaḥ  dharmaḥ kathaṃlakṣaṇaḥ kāny asya sādhanāni kāni sādhana ābhāsāni kiṃparaḥ  ca iti tatra kaḥ  dharmaḥ kathaṃlakṣaṇa iti  ekena eva sūtreṇa vyākhyātam codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  arthaḥ  dharma iti kāny asya sādhanāni kāni sādhana ābhāsāni kiṃparaḥ  ca iti śeṣa lakṣaṇena vyākhyātam kva puruṣa para tvam kva vā puruṣaḥ  guṇa bhūta  iti  etāsām pratijñānām piṇḍasya etad  sūtram atha atas  dharma jijñāsā iti dharmaḥ prasiddhaḥ  vā syāt  aprasiddhaḥ  vā sa ced  prasiddhaḥ na jijñāsyaḥ atha aprasiddhaḥ natarām tad  etad  anarthakam dharma jijñāsā prakaraṇam athavā arthavat dharmam prati hi vipratipannā bahu vidaḥ kecid  anyam dharmam āhuḥ kecid  anyam saḥ  ayam avicārya pravartamānaḥ kaṃcid  eva upādadānaḥ  vihanyeta anartham caṛcchet  tasmāt  dharmaḥ  jijñāsitavyaḥ sa hi niḥśreyasena puruṣam saṃyunakti iti pratijānīmahe tad  abhidhīyate codanā iti kriyāyāḥ pravartakam vacanam āhuḥ ācārya coditaḥ karomi iti hi dṛśyate lakṣyate yena tal lakṣaṇam dhūmaḥ  lakṣaṇam agneḥ  iti hi vadanti tayā yaḥ  lakṣyate saḥ  arthaḥ puruṣam niḥśreyasena saṃyunakti iti pratijānīmahe codanā hi bhūtam bhavantam bhaviṣyantam sūkṣmam vyavahitam viprakṛṣṭam iti  evaṃjātīyakam artham śaknoti  avagamayitum na anyat  kiṃcana indriyam nanu  atathābhūtam api  artham brūyāt  codanā yathā yad kiṃcana laukikam vacanam nadyāḥ  tīre phalāni santi iti tad  tathyam api bhavati vitatham api bhavati iti ucyate vipratiṣiddham idam abhidhīyate bravīti ca vitatham ca iti bravīti iti ucyate avabodhayati budhyamānasya nimittam bhavati iti yasmin   ca nimitta bhūte sati  avabudhyate saḥ  avabodhayati yadi ca codanāyām satyām agnihotrāt  svargaḥ  bhavati iti  avagamyate katham ucyate na tathā bhavati iti atha na tathā bhavati katham avabudhyate asantam artham avabudhyata iti vipratiṣiddham na ca svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti  atas  vacanāt  saṃdigdham avagamyate bhavati vā svargaḥ  na vā bhavati iti na ca niścitam avagamyamānam idam mithyā syāt  yaḥ  hi janitvā pradhvaṃsate na etad  evam iti sa mithyā pratyayaḥ na ca eṣa kāla antare puruṣa antare avasthā antare deśa antare vā viparyeti tasmāt  avitathaḥ tasmāt  avitathaḥ yad  tu laukikam vacanam tad  ced  pratyayitāt  puruṣāt  indriya viṣayam vā avitatham eva tad  atha apratyayitāt  puruṣāt  anindriya viṣayam vā tad  puruṣa buddhi prabhavam apramāṇam aśakyam hi tad  puruṣeṇa jñātum ṛte vacanāt  aparasmāt  pauruṣeyāt  vacanāt  avagatam iti ced  tad  api tena eva tulyam na evaṃjātīyakeṣu  artheṣu puruṣa vacanam prāmāṇyam upaiti jāti andhānām iva vacanam rūpa viśeṣeṣu nanu  aviduṣām upadeśaḥ  na avakalpate upadiṣṭavantaḥ  ca manu ādayaḥ tasmāt  puruṣāḥ santaḥ  viditavantaḥ  ca yathā cakṣuṣā rūpam upalabhyata iti darśanāt  eva avagatam ucyate upadeśaḥ  hi vyāmohāt  api bhavati asati vyāmohe vedāt  api bhavati api ca pauruṣeyāt  vacanāt  evam ayam puruṣaḥ veda iti bhavati pratyayaḥ na evam ayam artha iti viplavate khalu  api kaścid  puruṣa kṛtāt  vacanāt  pratyayaḥ na tu veda vacanasya mithyātve kiṃcana pramāṇam asti nanu sāmānyatas  dṛṣṭam bhaviṣyati pauruṣeyam vacanam vitatham upalabhya vacana sāmānyāt  veda vacanam mithyā iti  anumīyate na anya tvāt  na hi  anyasya vitatha bhāve anyasya vaitathyam bhavitum arhati anya tvāt  eva na hi devadattasya śyāma tve yajñadattasya api śyāma tvam bhavitum arhati api ca puruṣa vacana sādharmyāt  veda vacanam vitatham iti  anumānam pratyakṣas tu veda vacane pratyayaḥ na ca anumānam pratyakṣa virodhi pramāṇam bhavati tasmāt  codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  arthaḥ śreyaskaraḥ evam tarhi śreyaskaraḥ  jijñāsitavyaḥ kim dharma jijñāsayā ucyate ya eva śreyaskaraḥ sa eva dharma śabdena ucyate katham avagamyate yaḥ  hi yāgam anutiṣṭhati tam dhārmika iti samācakṣate yaḥ  ca yasya kartā sa tena vyapadiśyate yathā pācakaḥ  lāvaka iti tena yaḥ puruṣam niḥśreyasena saṃyunakti sa eva dharma śabdena ucyate na kevalam loke vede api yajñena yajñam ayajanta devāḥ tāni dharmāṇi prathamāni  āsan iti  yajati śabda vācyam eva dharmam samānanti ubhayam iha codanayā lakṣyate arthaḥ  anarthaḥ  ca kaḥ  arthaḥ yaḥ  niḥśreyasāya jyotiṣṭoma ādiḥ kaḥ  anarthaḥ yaḥ pratyavāyāya śyenaḥ  vajra iṣuḥ  iti  evamādiḥ tatra anarthaḥ  dharma uktaḥ  mā bhūd iti  artha grahaṇam katham punar  asau   anarthaḥ hiṃsā hi sā sā ca pratiṣiddhā katham punar  asau   anarthaḥ kartavyatayā upadiśyate ucyate na eva śyena ādayaḥ kartavya tayā vijñāyante yaḥ  hi hiṃsitum icchet  tasya ayam abhyupāya iti hi teṣām upadeśaḥ śyenena abhicaran yajeta iti hi samāmananti na abhicaritavyam iti nanu  aśaktam idam sūtram imau   artha   abhivaditum codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  dharmaḥ  na indriya ādi lakṣaṇaḥ arthaḥ  ca dharmaḥ  na anartha iti ekam hi idam vākyam tad  evam sati bhidyeta ucyate yatra vākyāt  eva arthaḥ  avagamyate tatra evam tad  tu vaidikeṣu na sūtreṣu anyatas  avagate arthe sūtram evam artham iti  avagamyate tena ca eka deśaḥ sūtryata iti sūtram tatra bhinnayoḥ  eva vākyayoḥ  imau   eka deśau   iti  avagantavyam athavā arthasya sataś codanā lakṣaṇasya dharma tvam ucyata iti  eka artham eva iti uktam asmābhiḥ  codanā nimittam dharmasya jñānam iti tad  pratijñā mātreṇa uktam idānīm tasya nimittam parīkṣiṣyāmahe kim codanā eva utāni ad api iti tasmāt  na tāvan niścīyate codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  arthaḥ  dharma iti tad  ucyate idam parīkṣyate pratyakṣam tāvat  animittam kim kāraṇam evaṃlakṣaṇakam hi tad  sat saṃprayoge puruṣasya indriyāṇām buddhi janma tad  pratyakṣam sati indriya artha saṃbandhe yā puruṣasya buddhiḥ  jāyate tad  pratyakṣam bhaviṣyaṃ   ca eṣaḥ arthaḥ  na jñāna kāle asti sataś ca etad  upalambhanam na asataḥ atas  pratyakṣam animittam buddhiḥ  vā janma vā saṃnikarṣaḥ  vā iti na eṣām kasyacid  avadhāraṇa artham etad  sūtram sati indriya artha saṃprayoge na asati iti  etāvat  avadhāryate anekasmin   avadhāryamāṇe bhidyeta vākyam pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvāt  ca anumāna upamāna artha āpattīnām api  akāraṇa tvam abhāvaḥ  api na asti yatas  autpattika iti nityam brūmaḥ utpattiḥ  hi bhāva ucyate lakṣaṇayā aviyuktaḥ śabda arthayoḥ  bhāvaḥ saṃbandhena na utpannayoḥ paścāt  saṃbandhaḥ autpattikaḥ śabdasya arthena saṃbandha s tasya agnihotra ādi lakṣaṇasya dharmasya nimittam pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ  anavagatasya katham upadeśaḥ  hi bhavati upadeśa iti viśiṣṭasya śabdasya uccāraṇam avyatirekaḥ  ca bhavati tasya jñānasya na hi tad  utpannam jñānam viparyeti yad  ca nāma jñānam utpannam na viparyeti na tad  chakyate vaktum na etad  evam iti yathā vijñāyate na tathā bhavati yathā etad  na vijñāyate tathā etad  iti anyat  asya hṛdaye anyat  vāci syāt  evam vadataḥ  viruddham idam avagamyata asti na asti ca iti tasmāt  tad  pramāṇam anapekṣa tvāt  na hi  evam sati pratyaya antaram apekṣitavyam puruṣa antaram vā svayaṃpratyayaḥ hi asau bādarāyaṇasya idam matam kīrtyate bādarāyaṇam pūjayitum na ātmīyam matam paryudasitum vṛtti kāra s tu  anyathā imam grantham varṇayāṃcakāra tasya nimitta parīṣṭiḥ  iti  evamādim na parīkṣitavyam nimittam pratyakṣa ādīni hi prasiddhāni pramāṇāni tad antargatam ca śāstram atas tad  api na parīkṣitavyam nanu vyabhicārāt  parīkṣitavyam nimittam śuktikā hi rajatavat  prakāśate yatas  tena pratyakṣam vyabhicarati tad mūla tvāt  ca anumāna ādīn i  api tatra aparīkṣya pravartamānaḥ  arthāt  vihanyeta anartham ca āpnuyāt kadācid  na etad  evam yad  pratyakṣam na tad  vyabhicarati yad  vyabhicarati na tad  pratyakṣam kim tarhi pratyakṣam tad saṃprayoge puruṣasya indriyāṇām buddhi janma sat  pratyakṣam yad viṣayam jñānam tena eva saṃprayoga indriyāṇām puruṣasya buddhi janma sat  pratyakṣam yad  anya viṣayam jñānam anya saṃprayoge bhavati na tad  pratyakṣam katham punar  idam avagamyata idam tad saṃprayoge idam anya saṃprayoga iti yad  na anya saṃprayoge tad  tad saṃprayoge etad viparītam anya saṃprayoga iti katham jñāyate yadā hi śuktikāyām api rajatam manya manaḥ  rajata saṃnikṛṣṭam me cakṣuḥ  iti manyate bādhakam hi yatra jñānam utpadyate na etad  evam mithyā jñānam idam iti tad  anya saṃprayoge viparītam tad saṃprayoga iti prāk  bādhaka jñāna utpatteḥ katham avagamyate yadā na tad kāle saṃyagjñānasya mithyājñānasya ca kaścid  viśeṣaḥ yadā kṣudh ādibhiḥ  upahatam manaḥ  bhavati indriyam vā timira ādibhiḥ saukṣmya ādibhiḥ  vā bāhyaḥ  viṣayaḥ tatas  mithyājñānam anupahateṣu saṃyagjñānam indriya manortha saṃnikarṣaḥ  hi jñānasya hetuḥ asati tasmin ajñānāt  tad antargataḥ  doṣaḥ  mithyājñānasya hetuḥ duṣṭeṣu hi jñānam mithyā bhavati katham avagamyate doṣa apagame saṃpratipatti darśanāt  katham duṣṭa aduṣṭa avagama iti ced  prayatnena anvicchantaḥ  na ced  doṣam upalabhemahi pramāṇa abhāvāt  aduṣṭam iti manyemahi tasmāt  yasya ca duṣṭam karaṇam yatra ca mithyā iti pratyayaḥ sa eva asamīcīnaḥ pratyayaḥ na anya iti nanu sarva eva nirālambanaḥ svapnavat  pratyayaḥ pratyayasya hi nirālambanatā svabhāva upalakṣitaḥ svapne jāgrataḥ  api stambha iti vā kuḍyam iti vā pratyaya eva bhavati tasmāt  saḥ  api nirālambanaḥ ucyate stambha iti jāgrataḥ  buddhiḥ su pariniścitā katham viparyasiṣyati svapne api  evam eva su pariniścitā āsīt  prāk  prabodhanāt  na tatra kaścid  viśeṣa iti ced  na svapne viparyaya darśanāt  aviparya yāc ca itarasmin tad sāmānyāt  itaratra api bhaviṣyati iti ced  yadi pratyaya tvāt  svapna pratyayasya mithyābhāvaḥ jāgrat pratyayasya api bhavitum arhati atha pratīti s tathā abhāvasya hetuḥ na śakyate pratyayāt  ayam anya iti vaditum anyatas  tu svapna pratyayasya mithyā bhāvaḥ  viparyayāt  avagataḥ kuta iti ced  sa nidrasya manasaḥ  daurbalyān nidrā mithyā bhāvasya hetuḥ svapna ādau svapna ante ca suṣuptasya pratyaya abhāva eva acetayan eva hi suṣupta iti  ucyate tasmāt  jāgrataḥ pratyayaḥ na mithyā iti nanu jāgrataḥ  api karaṇa doṣaḥ syāt  yadi syāt  avagamyeta svapna darśana kāle api na avagamyata iti ced  tad  na prabuddhaḥ  hi  avagacchati nidrā ākrāntam me mana āsīt  iti śūnya s tu katham artha jñānayoḥ  ākāra bhedam na upalabhāmahe pratyakṣā ca naḥ buddhiḥ atas tad bhinnam artha rūpam nāma na kiṃcid  asti iti paśyāmaḥ syāt  etad  evam yadi  artha ākārā buddhiḥ syāt  nirākārā tu naḥ buddhiḥ ākāravān bāhyaḥ  arthaḥ sa hi bahis deśa saṃbaddhaḥ pratyakṣam upalabhyate artha viṣayā hi pratyakṣa buddhiḥ  na buddhi antara viṣayā kṣaṇikā hi sā na buddhi antara kālam avasthāsyata iti utpadyamānā eva asau jñāyate jñāpayati ca artha antaram pradīpavat  iti yadi  ucyeta tad  na na hi  ajñāte arthe kaścid  buddhim upalabhate jñāte tu  anumānāt  avagacchati tatra yaugapadyam anupapannam nanu utpannāyām eva buddhau   arthaḥ  jñāta iti  ucyate na anutpannāyām atas  pūrvam buddhiḥ  utpadyate paścāt  jñātaḥ  arthaḥ nanu utpannāyām eva buddhau   arthaḥ  jñāta iti  ucyate na anutpannāyām atas  pūrvam buddhiḥ  utpadyate paścāt  jñātaḥ  arthaḥ satyam pūrvam buddhiḥ  utpadyate na tu pūrvam jñāyate bhavati hi kadācid  etad  yaj jñātaḥ  arthaḥ saḥ  ajñāta iti  ucyate na ca artha vyapadeśam antareṇa buddheḥ rūpa upalambhanam tasmāt  na avyapadeśyā buddhiḥ  avyapadeśyam ca naḥ pratyakṣam tasmāt  apratyakṣā buddhiḥ api ca kāmam eka rūpa tve buddheḥ  eva abhāvaḥ na tu  arthasya pratyakṣasya sataḥ na ca eka rūpyam nirākārām eva hi buddhim anumimīmahe sa ākāram ca artham pratyakṣam eva avagacchāmaḥ tasmāt  artha ālambanaḥ pratyayaḥ api ca niyata nimittaḥ  tantuṣu  eva upādīyamāneṣu paṭa pratyayaḥ itarathā tantu upādāne api kadācid  ghaṭa buddhiḥ  avikala indriyasya syāt  na ca evam asti tasmāt  na nirālambanaḥ pratyayaḥ atas  na vyabhicarati pratyakṣam anumānam jñāta saṃbandhasya eka deśa darśanāt  eka deśa antare asaṃnikṛṣṭe arthe buddhiḥ tad  tu dvividham pratyakṣatodṛṣṭa saṃbandham sāmānyatodṛṣṭa saṃbandham ca tatra pratyakṣatodṛṣṭa saṃbandham yathā dhūma ākṛti darśanāt  agni ākṛti vijñānam sāmānya toḍṛṣṭa saṃbandham ca yathā devadattasya gati pūrvikam deśa antara prāptim upalabhya āditye api gati smaraṇam śāstram śabda vijñānāt  asaṃnikṛṣṭe arthe vijñānam upamānam api sādṛśyam asaṃnikṛṣṭe arthe buddhim utpādayati yathā gavaya darśanam gaḥ smaraṇasya arthāpattiḥ  api dṛṣṭaḥ śrutaḥ  vā arthaḥ  anyathā na upapadyata iti  artha kalpanā yathā jīvataḥ  devadattasya gṛha abhāva darśanena bahirbhāvasya adṛṣṭasya kalpanā abhāvaḥ  api pramāṇa abhāvaḥ  na asti iti  asya arthasya asaṃnikṛṣṭasya tasmāt  prasiddha tvāt  na parīkṣitavyam nimittam nanu pratyakṣa ādīni  anyāni bhavantu nāma pramāṇāni śabdas tu na pramāṇam kutas  animittam vidyamāna upalambhana tvāt  animittam apramāṇam śabdaḥ yaḥ  hi  upalambhana viṣayaḥ  na upalabhyate sa na asti yathā śaśasya viṣāṇam upalambhanāni ca indriyāṇi paśu ādīnām na ca paśu kāma iṣṭi anantaram paśava upalabhyante atas  na iṣṭiḥ paśuphalā karma kāle ca karma phalena bhavitavyam yad kālam hi mardanam tad kālam mardana sukham kāla antare phalam dāsyati iti ced  na na kāla antare phalam iṣṭeḥ  iti  avagacchāmaḥ kutas  yadā tāvat  asau vidyamānā āsīt  tadā phalam na dattavatī yadā phalam utpadyate tadā asau na asti asatī ca katham dāsyati api ca karma kāla eva phalam śrūyate yāgaḥ karaṇam iti vākyāt  avagamyate karaṇam ced  utpannam kāryeṇa bhavitavyam iti pratyakṣam ca phala kāraṇam anyat  upalabhāmahe na ca dṛṣṭe kāraṇe sati  adṛṣṭam kalpayitum śakyate pramāṇa abhāvāt  evam dṛṣṭa apacārasya vedasya svarga ādi  api phalam na bhavati iti manyāmahe dṛṣṭa viruddham api bhavati kiṃcid  vaidikam vacanam pātra cayanam vidhāya āha sa eṣa yajña āyudhī yajamānaḥ  añjasā svargam lokam yāti iti pratyakṣam śarīram vyapadiśati na ca tad  svargam lokam yāti pratyakṣam hi tad  dahyate na ca eṣa yāti iti vidhi śabdaḥ evaṃjātīyakam ca pramāṇa viruddham vacanam apramāṇam ambuni majjanti  alābūni grāvānaḥ plavanta iti yathā tad sāmānyāt  agnihotra ādi codanāsv api  anāśvāsaḥ tasmāt  na codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  arthaḥ  dharmaḥ autpattikaḥ  tu śabdasya arthena saṃbandha s tasya jñānam tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati apauruṣeyaḥ śabdasya arthena saṃbandha s tasya agnihotra ādi lakṣaṇasya arthasya jñānam pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ  anavagamyamānasya tathā ca codanā lakṣaṇaḥ saṃyak pratyaya iti pauruṣeye hi sati saṃbandhe yaḥ pratyayaḥ tasya mithyā bhāva āśaṅkyeta para pratyayaḥ hi tadā syāt  atha śabde bruvati katham mithyā iti na hi tadānīm anyatas  puruṣāt  avagamaḥ bravīti iti  ucyata avabodhayati budhyamānasya nimittam bhavati iti śabde ced  nimitta bhūte svayam avabudhyate katham vipralabdham brūyān na etad  evam iti na ca asya codanā syāt  vā na vā iti sāṃśayikam pratyayam utpādayati na ca mithyā etad  iti kāla antare deśa antare avasthā antare puruṣa antare vā punar  avyapadeśyaḥ pratyayaḥ bhavati yaḥ  api  anya pratyaya viparyāsam dṛṣṭvā atra api viparyasiṣyati iti  ānumānikaḥ pratyaya utpadyate saḥ  api  anena pratyakṣeṇa pratyayena virudhyamānaḥ  bādhyate tasmāt  codanā lakṣaṇa eva dharmaḥ syāt  etad  evam na eva śabdasya arthena asti saṃbandhaḥ kutaḥ asya pauruṣeya tā vā iti katham syāt  ced  arthena saṃbandhaḥ kṣurama udaka śabda uccāraṇe mukhasya pāṭana pūraṇe syātām yadi saṃśleṣa lakṣaṇam saṃbandham abhipretya ucyate kārya kāraṇa nimitta naimittika āśraya āśrayi bhāva yaunādayaḥ  tu saṃbandhāḥ śabdasya anupapannā eva iti ucyate yaḥ  atra vyapadeśyaḥ saṃbandhaḥ tam ekam na vyapadiśati bhavān pratyayyasya pratyāyakasya ca yaḥ saṃjñā saṃjñi lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandha s tam iti āha yadi pratyāyakaḥ śabdaḥ prathama śrutaḥ kim na pratyāyayati ucyate sarvatra naḥ darśanam pramāṇam pratyāyaka iti hi pratyayam dṛṣṭvā avagacchāmaḥ na prathama śruta iti prathama śravaṇe pratyayam adṛṣṭvā yāvat kṛtvas  śrutāt  artha avagamaḥ yathā cakṣuḥ  draṣṭr na bāhyena prakāśena vinā prakāśayati iti  adraṣṭṛ na bhavati yadi prathama śrutaḥ  na pratyāyayati kṛtakas tarhi śabdasya arthena saṃbandhaḥ kutas  svabhāvataḥ  hi  asaṃbandhau   etau śabda arthau mukhe hi śabdam upalabhāmahe bhūmau   artham śabdaḥ  ayam na tu  arthaḥ arthaḥ  ayam na śabda iti ca vyapadiśanti rūpa bhedaḥ  api bhavati gauḥ  iti imam śabdam uccārayanti sāsnādimantam artham avabudhyanta iti pṛthak bhūtayoḥ  ca yaḥ saṃbandhaḥ sa kṛtakaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ yathā rajju ghaṭayoḥ  iti atha gauḥ  iti  atra kaḥ śabdaḥ gakāraukāra visarjanīyā iti bhagavān ūpa varṣaḥ śrotra grahaṇe hi  arthe loke śabda śabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ te ca śrotra grahaṇāḥ yadi  evam artha pratyayaḥ na upapadyate katham ekaika akṣara vijñāne hi  arthaḥ  na upalabhyate na ca akṣara vyatiriktaḥ  anyaḥ kaścid  asti samudāyaḥ  nāma yatas  artha pratipattiḥ syāt  yadā hi gakāraḥ na tad aukāra ādi visarjanīyau yad aukāra visarjanīyau na tadā gakāraḥ atas  gakāra ādi vyatiriktaḥ  anyaḥ  gaḥ śabdaḥ  asti yatas  artha pratipattiḥ syāt  antarhite api śabde smaraṇād artha pratyaya iti ced  na smṛteḥ  api kṣaṇika tvāt  akṣaraiḥ  tulya tā pūrva varṇa janita saṃskāra sahitaḥ  antya varṇaḥ pratyāyaka iti  adoṣaḥ nanu  evam api śabdāt  artham pratipadyām aha iti laukikam vacanam anupapannam syāt  ucyate yadi na upapadyate anupapannam nāma na hi laukikam vacanam anupapannam iti  etāvatā pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ  anavagamyamānaḥ  arthaḥ śakyaḥ  abhyupagantum laukikāni vacanāni  upapanna arthāni  anupapanna arthāni ca dṛśyante yathā devadatta gām abhyāja iti  evamādīni daśa dāḍimāni ṣaṣ  apūpā iti  evamādīni ca nanu ca śāstra kārā api  evam āhuḥ pūrva aparībhūtam bhāvam ākhyāte na ācaṣṭe vrajati pacati iti  upakrama prabhṛti  apavarga paryantam iti yathā na śāstra kāra vacanam api  alam imam artham apramāṇakam upapādayitum api ca na eva etad  anupapanna artham akṣarebhyaḥ saṃskāraḥ saṃskārāt  artha pratipattiḥ  iti bhavanti  artha pratpattau   akṣarāṇi nimittam gauṇa eṣa śabda iti ced  na gauṇaḥ  akṣareṣu nimitta bhāvaḥ tad bhāve bhāvāt  tad abhāve ca abhāvāt  atha api gauṇaḥ syāt  na gauṇaḥ śabdaḥ  mā bhūd iti  etāvatā pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ  anavagamyamānaḥ  arthaḥ śakyaḥ parikalpayitum na hi  agniḥ  māṇavaka iti  ukte agni śabdaḥ  gauṇaḥ  mā bhūd iti jvalana eva māṇavaka iti  adhyavasīyate na ca pratyakṣaḥ  gakāra ādibhyaḥ  anyaḥ  gaḥ śabda iti bheda darśana abhāvāt  abheda darśanāt  ca gakāra ādīni hi pratyakṣāṇi tasmāt  gauḥ  iti gakāra ādi visarjanīya antam padam akṣarāṇi  eva na tebhyaḥ  vyatiriktam anyat  padam nāma iti nanu saṃskāra kalpanāyām api  adṛṣṭa kalpanā ucyate śābda kalpanāyām sā ca śabda kalpanā ca tasmāt  akṣarāṇi  eva padam atha gauḥ  iti  asya śabdasya kaḥ  arthaḥ sāsnādi viśiṣṭa ākṛtiḥ  iti brūmaḥ nanu  ākṛtiḥ sādhyāsti vā na vā iti na pratyakṣā satī sādhyā bhavitum arhati rucakaḥ svastikaḥ vardhamānaka iti hi pratyakṣam dṛśyate vyamoha iti ced  na na asti pratyaya viparyāse vyamoha iti śakyate vaktum asati  api  artha antara evaṃjātīyake bhavati pratyayaḥ praṅktiḥ yūtham vanam iti yathā iti ced  na asaṃbaddham idam vacanam upanyastam kim asati vane vana pratyayaḥ bhavati iti pratyakṣam eva ākṣipyate vṛkṣā api na santi iti yadi  evam pratyuktaḥ sa mahāyānikaḥ pakṣaḥ atha kim ākṛti sadbhāva vādy upālabhyate siddhānta antaram te duṣyati vane api te asati vana pratyayaḥ prāpnoti iti evam api prakṛtam dūṣayitum aśaknuvantas te siddhānta antara dūṣaṇam nigraha sthānam āpadyate asādhaka tvāt  sa hi vakṣyati duṣyatu yadi duṣyati kim tena duṣṭena aduṣṭena vā prakṛtam tvayā sādhitam bhavati madīyaḥ vā pakṣaḥ  dūṣitaḥ  bhavati iti na ca vṛkṣa vyatiriktam vanam yasmān na upalabhyate tatas  vanam na asti iti  avagamyate yadi vane anyena hetunā sadbhāva viparītaḥ pratyaya utpadyate mithyā eṣa vana pratyaya iti  atas  vanam na asti iti  avagacchāmaḥ na ca gavā ādiṣu pratyayaḥ viparyeti atas  vaiṣamyam atha vana ādiṣu na eva pratyaya viparyāsaḥ na te na santi iti tasmāt  asaṃbaddhaḥ paṅkti vana upanyāsaḥ na te na santi iti tasmāt  asaṃbaddhaḥ paṅkti vana upanyāsaḥ ata upapannam jaimini vacanam ākṛtiḥ padārtha iti yathā ca ākṛtiḥ śabda artha s tathā upariṣṭān nipuṇataram upapādayiṣyāma iti atha saṃbandhaḥ ka iti yad  śabde vijñāte arthaḥ  vijñāyate sa tu kṛtaka iti pūrvam upapāditam tasmāt  manyāmahe kena api puruṣeṇa śabdānām arthaiḥ saha saṃbandham kṛtvā saṃvyavahartum vedāḥ praṇītā iti tad  idānīm ucyate apauruṣeya tvāt  saṃbandhasya siddham iti katham punar  idam avagamyate apauruṣeya eṣa saṃbandha iti puruṣasya saṃbandhuḥ  abhāvāt  katham saṃbandhā na asti pratyakṣasya pramāṇasya abhāvāt  tad pūrvaka tvāt  ca itareṣām nanu cira vṛtta tvāt  pratyakṣasya aviṣayaḥ  bhavet  idānīntanānām na hi cira vṛttaḥ san na smaryeta na ca himavat ādiṣu kūpa ārām ādivat  asmaraṇam bhavitum arhati puruṣa viyogaḥ  hi teṣu bhavati deśa utsādena kula utsādena vā na tu śabda artha vyavahāra viyogaḥ puruṣānām asti syāt  etad  saṃbandha mātra vyavahāriṇaḥ  niṣprayojanam kartṛ smaraṇam anādriyamānāḥ puruṣā vismareyuḥ  iti tad  na yadi hi puruṣaḥ kṛtvā saṃbandham vyavahārayet  vyavahāra kāle avaśyam smartavyaḥ  bhavet  saṃpratipattau hi kartṛ vyavahartra ūḥ  arthaḥ sidhyati na vipratipattau na hi vṛddhi śabdena apāṇineḥ  vyavahārata ādaicaḥ pratiyeran pāṇi nikṛtim ananumanyamānasya vā tathā makāreṇa api  apiṅgalasya na sarva guru s trikaḥ pratīyeta piṅgala kṛtim ananumanyamānasya vā tena kartṛ vyavahartārau saṃpratipadyete tena vedaiḥ  vyavaharadbhiḥ  avaśyam smaraṇīyaḥ saṃbandhasya kartā syāt  vyavahārasya ca na hi vismṛte vṛddhiḥ  ādaij iti  asya sūtrasya kartari vṛddhiḥ  yasya ācām ādis tad  vṛddham iti kiṃcid  pratīyeta tasmāt  asmaraṇād avagacchāmaḥ na kṛtvā saṃbandham vyavahāra artham kenacid  vedāḥ praṇītā iti yadi  api ca vismaraṇam upapadyeta tathā api na pramāṇam antareṇa saṃbandhāram pratipadyemahi yathā vidyamānasya api  anupalambhanam bhavati iti na etāvatā vinā pramāṇena śaśa viṣāṇam pratipadyemahi tasmāt  apauruṣeyaḥ śabdasya arthena saṃbandha iti nanu  arthāpattyā saṃbandhāram pratipadyemahi na hi akṛta saṃbandha āt  chabdāt  artham pratipadyamānam upalabhāmahe pratipadyeraṃ   ced  prathama śravaṇe api pratipadyeran tad anupalambha nāt  avaśyam bhavitavyam saṃbandhra iti manyāmaha iti ced  na siddhavat  upadeśāt  yadi saṃbandhuḥ  abhāvān niyogataḥ  na arthā upalabhyeran tatas  artha āpattyā saṃbandhāram avagacchāmaḥ asti tu  anyaḥ prakāraḥ vṛddhānām sva arthena vyavaharamāṇānām upaśṛṇvantaḥ  bālāḥ pratyakṣam artham pratipadyamānā dṛśyante te api vṛddhā yadā bālā āsaṃ   tadā anyebhyaḥ  vṛddhebhyaḥ te api  anyebhya iti na asti  ādiḥ  iti  evam vā bhavet  athavā na kaścid  ekaḥ  api śabdaḥ  arthena saṃbaddha āsīt  atha kenacid  saṃbandhāḥ pravartitā iti atra vṛddha vyavahāre sati na arthāt  āpadyeta saṃbandhasya kārtā api ca vṛddha vyavahāra vādinaḥ pratyakṣam upadiśanti kalpayanti itare saṃbandhāram na ca pratyakṣe pratyarthini kalpanā sādhvī tasmāt  saṃbandhuḥ  abhāvaḥ avyatirekaḥ  ca yathā asmin deśe sāsnādimati gaḥ śabdaḥ evam sarveṣu durgameṣu  api bahavaḥ saṃbandhāraḥ katham saṃgamsyante ekaḥ  api na śaknuyāt  atas  na asti saṃbandhā apara āha avyatirekaḥ  ca na hi saṃbandha vyatiriktaḥ kaścid  kālaḥ  asti yasmin na kaścid  api śabdaḥ kenacid  arthena saṃbaddha āsīt  katham saṃbandha kriyā eva hi na upapadyate avaśyam anena saṃbandham kurvatā kenacid  chabdena kartavyaḥ yena kriyeta tasya kena kṛtaḥ atha anyena kenacid  kṛtaḥ tasya kena iti tasya kena iti na eva avatiṣṭhate tasmāt  avaśyam anena saṃbandham kurvatā akṛta saṃbandhāḥ kecana śabdā vṛddha vyavahāra siddhā abhyupagantavyāḥ asti ced  vyavahāra siddhiḥ na niyogataḥ saṃbandhrā bhavitavyam iti  arthāpattiḥ  api na asti syāt  etad  aprasiddha saṃbandhā bālāḥ katham vṛddhebhyaḥ pratipadyanta iti na hi dṛṣṭe anupapannam nāma dṛṣṭā hi bālā vṛddhebhyaḥ pratipadyamānāḥ na tu  apratipanna saṃbandhāḥ saṃbandhasya kartuḥ tasmāt  vaiṣamyam arthe anupalabdhe anupalabdhe ca devatā dau   arthe anarthakam saṃjñā karaṇam aśakyam ca viśeṣān pratipattum hi saṃjñāḥ kriyante viśeṣān   ca uddiśya tad  viśeṣeṣu  ajñāyamāneṣu ubhayam api  anavakḷptam tasmāt  apauruṣeyaḥ śabdasya arthena saṃbandhaḥ atas  ca tad  pramāṇam anapekṣa tvāt  na hi  evam sati puruṣa antaram pratyaya antaram vā apekṣate tasmāt  codanā lakṣaṇa eva dharmaḥ  na anya lakṣaṇaḥ bādarāyaṇa grahaṇam uktam atha yad  uktam animittam śabdaḥ karma kāle phala adarśanāt  kāla antare ca karma abhāvāt  pramāṇam na asti iti tad  ucyate na syāt  pramāṇam yadi pañca eva pramāṇāni  abhaviṣyan yena yena hi pramīyate tad  tad  pramāṇam śabdena api pramīyate tatas  śabdaḥ  api pramāṇam yathā eva pratyakṣam na ca pramāṇena avagatam pramāṇa antareṇa anavagatam iti  etāvatā anavagatam bhavati na ca evam śrūyate kṛte karmaṇi tāvatī  eva phalam bhavati kim tu karmaṇā phalam prāpyata iti yad  ca kāla antare phalasya anyat  pratyakṣam kāraṇam asti iti na eṣa doṣaḥ tad  ca eva hi tatra kāraṇam śabdaḥ  ca iti yad  tu pratyakṣa viruddham vacanam upanyastam sa eṣa yajña āyudhī yajamānaḥ  añjasā svargam lokam yāti iti pratyakṣam śarīram vyapadiśati iti tad  ucyate śarīra saṃbandhāt  yasya tad  śarīram saḥ  api taiḥ  yajña āyudhaiḥ  yajña āyudhī iti  ucyate āha kaḥ  asau   anyaḥ na enam upalabhāmahe nanu prāṇa ādibhiḥ  enam upalabhāmahe yaḥ  asau prāṇiti  apānity ucchvasiti nimiṣati ityādi ceṣṭitavān saḥ  atra śarīre yajñāyudhī iti nanu śarīram eva prāṇiti  apān iti ca na prāṇa ādayaḥ śarīra guṇāḥ śarīra guṇa vidharmāṇaḥ  hi te ayāvat śarīra bhāvi tvāt  yāvat śarīram tāvat  asya guṇā rūpa ādayaḥ prāṇa ādayaḥ  tu sati  api śarīre na bhavanti atas  na śarīra guṇāḥ prāṇa ādayaḥ sukha ādayaḥ  ca svayam upa labhyante na rūpa ādaya iva śarīra guṇāḥ pareṇa api tasmāt  charīra guṇa vaidharmyāt  anyaḥ śarīrāt  yajñāyudhī iti āha kuta eṣaḥ saṃpratyayaḥ sukha ādibhyaḥ  anyaḥ  tadvān asti iti na hi sukha ādi pratyākhyānena tasya svarūpam upalabhāmahe tasmāt  chaśa viṣāṇavat  asau na asti atha ucyate tena vinā kasya sukha ādaya iti na kasyacid  api iti vakṣyāmaḥ na hi yaḥ  ya upalabhyate tasya tasya saṃbandhinā bhavitavyam yasya saṃbandhaḥ  api  upalabhyate saṃbandhī ca tasya ayam saṃbandhi iti gamyate na hi candramasam ādityam vā upalabhya saṃbandhi antara anveṣaṇā bhavati  kasya ayam iti na kasyacid  api iti  avadhāryate tasmāt  na sukha ādibhyaḥ  anyaḥ  tadvān asti iti atha upalabdhasya avaśyam kalpayitavyaḥ saṃbandhī bhavet  tatas  ātmānam api  anena prakāreṇa upalabhya kasya ayam iti saṃbandhi antaram anviṣyema tam api kalpayitvā anyam api kalpayitvā anyam iti  anavasthā eva syāt  atha kaṃcid  kalpayitvā na saṃbandhi antaram api kalpayiṣyasi tāvatī  eva viraṃsyasi tāvatā ca paritokṣyasi tatas  vijñāna eva parituṣya tāvatī  eva virantum arhasi atra ucyate yadi vijñānāt  anyaḥ  vijñātā na asti kas tarhi jānāti iti  ucyate jñānasya kartuḥ  abhidhānam anena śabdena upapadyate tad  eṣa śabdaḥ  arthavān kartavya iti jñānāt  vyatiriktam ātmānam kalpayiṣyāma iti āha devāḥ  enam śabdam arthavantam kalpayiṣyanti yadi kalpayitavyam maṃsyante bahavaḥ khalu  iha janā asti  ātmā asti  ātmā iti  ātma sattā vādina eva śabdasya pratyakṣa vaktāraḥ  bhavanti tathā api na ātma sattām kalpayitum ghaṭante kim aṅga punar  jānāti iti parokṣa śabda darśanāt tasmāt  asad etad  ucyate icchayā ātmānam upalabhāmahe katham upalabdha pūrve hi  abhiprete bhavati icchā na anupalabdha pūrve yathā merum uttareṇa yāni  asmad jātīyaiḥ  anupalabdha pūrvāṇi svādūni vṛkṣa phalāni na tāni praty asmākam icchā bhavati naḥ khalu  anyena puruṣeṇa upalabdhe api viṣaye anyasya anupalabdhuḥ  icchā bhavati bhavati ca anyedyus  upalabdhe aparedyus  icchā atas tena upalambhanena samāna kartṛkā sā iti  avagacchāmaḥ yadi vijñāna mātram eva idam upalambhakam abhaviṣyat  pradhvaste tasmin kasya aparedyus  icchā bhaviṣyat atha vijñānāt  anyaḥ  vijñātā nityaḥ tatas  ekasmin ahani ya upalabdhā aparedyus  api sa eva eṣiṣyati itaratha icchā anupapannā syāt  atra āha anupapannam iti naḥ kva saṃpratyayaḥ yad  na pramāṇena avagatam vijñānāt  tāvat  anyan na upalabhāmahe yad  ca na upalabhāmahe tad  chaśa viṣāṇavat  eva na asti iti  avagacchāmaḥ na ca tasmin asati vijñāna sadbhāvaḥ  anupapannaḥ pratyakṣa avagata tvāt  eva kṣaṇika tvam ca asya pratyakṣa pūrvakam eva na ca jñātari vijñānāt  anyasmin asati jñāne ca anitye aparedyus  icchā anupapannā pratyakṣa avagata tvāt  eva naḥ khalu  api  etad  dṛṣṭam ya eva anyedyus  upalabdhā sa eva aparedyus  eṣitā iti idam tu dṛṣṭam yad  kvacid  anyena dṛṣṭam anya icchati kvacid  na samānāyām santatau   anya icchati santati antare na icchati iti tasmāt  na sukha ādi vyatiriktaḥ  anyaḥ  asti iti atra ucyate na hi  asmartāra icchanti iti  upapadyate na ca adṛṣṭa pūrve smṛtiḥ  bhavati tasmāt  kṣaṇike vijñāna skandha mātre smṛtiḥ  anupapanna iti atra āha smṛtiḥ  api icchāvat  pūrva vijñāna sadṛśam vijñānam pūrva vijñāna viṣayam vā smṛtiḥ  iti  ucyate tad  ca draṣṭari vinaṣṭe api aparedyus  utpadyamānam na anupapannam pratyakṣa avagata tvāt  eva anyasmin skandha ghane anyena skandha ghanena yaj jñānam tad  tad santati jena anyena upalabhyate na atad santati jena tasmāt  chūnyāḥ skandha ghanā iti atha asmin   arthe brāhmaṇam bhavati vijñāna ghana eva etebhyaḥ  bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya tāni  eva anuvinaśyati na pretya saṃjñā asti iti atra ucyate na etad  evam anyedyus  dṛṣṭe aparedyus  aham idam adarśam iti bhavati pratyayaḥ pratyagātmani ca etad  bhavati na paratra paraḥ  hi  asau yaḥ  anyedyus  dṛṣṭavān tasmāt  tad vyatiriktaḥ  anyaḥ  asti yatra ayam ahaṃśabdaḥ āha paratra api  ahaṃśabdaḥ  bhaktyā dṛśyate tad  yathā aham eva putraḥ aham eva devadattaḥ aham eva gacchāmi iti atra ucyate na vayam  aham  iti imam śabdam prayujyamānam anyasmin   arthe hetu tvena vyapadiśāmaḥ kim tarhi śabdāt  vyatiriktam pratyabhijñā pratyayam pratīmaḥ  hi vayam imam artham vayam eva anyedyus  upalabhāmahe vayam eva adya smarāma iti tasmāt  vayam imam artham avagacchāmaḥ  vayam eva hi aḥ vayam eva adya iti ye cāmī hi aḥ adya ca na te vinaṣṭāḥ atha api  asmin   arthe brāhmaṇam bhavati sa vā ayam ātmā iti prakṛtyām ananti  aśīryaḥ  na hi śīryata iti tathā avināśī vā are ayam ātmā anucchitti dharmā iti vinaśvaram ca vijñānam tasmāt  vinaśvarād anyaḥ sa iti  avagacchāmaḥ na ca śakyam evam avagantum yathā upalabhyante arthā na tathā bhavanti yathā na khalu na upalabhyante tathā bhavanti iti tathā hi sati śaśaḥ  na asti śaśasya viṣāṇam asti iti  avagamyeta na ca aham pratyayaḥ vyāmoha iti śakyate vaktum bādhaka pratyaya abhāvāt tasmāt  sukha ādibhyaḥ  vyatiriktaḥ  asti evam ced  sa eva yajñāyudhī iti vyapadiśyate āha yadi vijñānāt  anyat  asti vijñātṛ vijñānam apāsya tad  nidarśyatām idam tad  īdṛśam ca iti na ca tad  nidarśyate tasmāt  na tatas  anyat  asti iti atra ucyate sva saṃvedyaḥ sa bhavati na asau   anyena śakyate draṣṭum katham asau nidarśyeta iti yathā ca kaścid  cakṣuṣmān svayam rūpam paśyati na ca śaknoti  anyasmai jāti andhāya tad  nidarśayitum na ca tad  na śakyate nidarśayitum iti  etāvatā na asti iti  avagamyate evam asau puruṣaḥ svayam ātmānam upalabhate na ca anyasmai śaknoti darśayitum anyasya draṣṭuḥ  tam puruṣam prati darśana śakti abhāvāt saḥ  api  anyaḥ puruṣaḥ svayam ātmānam upalabhate na para ātmānam tena sarve svena svena ātmanā ātmānam upalabhamānāḥ santi  eva yadi  api para puruṣaiḥ  na upalabhyanta iti atha asmin arthe brāhmaṇam bhavati śāntāyām vāci kiṃjyotiḥ  eva ayam puruṣaḥ ātma jyotiḥ saṃrāj  iti ha uvāca iti pareṇa na upalabhyata iti  atra api brāhmaṇam bhavati agṛhyaḥ  na hi gṛhyata iti pareṇa na gṛhyata iti  etad abhiprāyam etad  kutas  svayaṃjyotiṣṭvavacanāt  atra api brāhmaṇam bhavati atra ayam puruṣaḥ svayaṃjyotiḥ  bhavati iti kena punar  upāyena ayam  ayam  anyasmai kathyata iti atra api  upāye brāhmaṇam bhavati sa eṣa na iti na iti  ātmā iti ha uvāca iti asau   ayam evaṃrūpa iti na śakyate nidarśayitum yad  ca paraḥ paśyati tad pratiṣedhas tasya upadeśa upāyaḥ śarīram paraḥ paśyati tena ātmā upadiśyate śarīram na ātmā asti śarīrāt  anyaḥ sa ca ātmā iti śarīra pratiṣedhena ātmā upadiśyate tathā prāṇa ādayaḥ  na ātmāna iti tad pratiṣedhena tebhyaḥ  anya upadiśyate tathā para sthāḥ sukha ādayaḥ pareṇa liṅgaiḥ  upalabhyante te api na ātmāna iti tad pratiṣedhena tebhyaḥ  anya upadiśyate yaḥ svayam paśyati na tatas  anyaḥ puruṣa iti  etad  api puruṣa pravṛttyā anumīyate yadā asau puruṣaḥ pūrvedyus  sāmi kṛtānām arthānām pratisamādhāne śeṣa anuṣṭhāne ca yatate atas  pravṛttyā avagamyate nūnam asau   anityān nityam avagacchati iti upamānāt  ca upadiśyate yādṛśam bhavān svayam ātmānam paśyati anena upamānena avagaccha aham api tādṛṣam eva paśyāmi iti yathā kaścid  ātmīyām vedanām parasmā ācakṣīta dahyamānasya iva me bhavati yātyamānasya iva me bhavati rudhyamānasya iva me bhavati iti atas  svayam avagamyamāna tvāt  asti tad vyatiriktaḥ puruṣa iti yad  api  ucyate vijñānam apāsya tad  nidarśyatām iti yadi  upāyam eva niśedhasi na śakyam upāyam antareṇa upeyam upetum ayam eva abhyupāyaḥ jñātavyānām arthānām yaḥ  yathā jñāyate sa tathā iti tad  yathā kaḥ śuklaḥ  nāma yatra śukla tvam asti kim śukla tvam nāma yatra śukla śabda pravṛttiḥ kva tasya pravṛttiḥ yad  chukla śabda uccarite pratīyate tasmāt  na vijñānam pratyākhyāya kasyacid  rūpam nidarśayitum śakyam na ca niyogataḥ pratyaye pratīte pratyaya arthaḥ pratītaḥ  bhavati apratīte api hi pratyaye sati  arthaḥ pratīyata eva na hi vijñānam pratyakṣam vijñeyaḥ  arthaḥ pratyakṣa iti  etad  pūrvam eva uktam tad  avaśya karta vye apahnave kāmam vijñānam apahnūyeta na artha iti  etad  api  uktam eva tasmāt  asti sukha ādibhyaḥ  anyaḥ  nityaḥ puruṣa iti atha yad  uktam vijñāna ghana eva etebhyaḥ  bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya tāni  eva anuvinaśyati na pretya saṃjñā asti iti atra ucyate atra eva mā bhagavān moha antam āpīpadat  iti paricodana uttara kāle apahnutya moha anta abhiprāyam asya vacanasya varṇitavān na vā are aham moham bravīmi avināśī vā are ayam ātma anucchitti dharmā mātrā saṃsarga s tu  asya bhavati iti tasmāt  na vijñāna mātram tasmāt  vaiṣamyam yad  uktam na ca eṣa yāti iti vidhi śabda iti mā bhūd vidhi śabdaḥ svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti vacana antareṇa avagatam anuvadiṣyate tasmāt  avirodhaḥ uktam nityaḥ śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandha iti tad  anupapannam śabdasya anitya tvāt  vinaṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ punar  asya kriyamāṇasya arthena akṛtakaḥ saṃbandhaḥ  na upapadyate na hi prathama śrutāt  chabdāt  kaścid  artham pratyeti katham punar  anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatnāt  uttara kālam dṛśyate yatas  atas  prayatna anantaryāt tena kriyata iti gamyate nanu  abhivyañjyāt  sa enam na iti brūmaḥ na hi  asya prāk  abhivyañjanāt  sadbhāve kiṃcana pramāṇam asti saṃś ca abhivyajyate na āsan naḥ khalu  api  uccaritam muhūrtam api  upalabhāmahe atas  vinaṣṭa iti  avagacchāmaḥ na ca san na upalabhyate anupalaṃbha kāraṇānām vyavadhāna ādīnām abhāve api  anupalambhanāt  na ca asau viṣayam aprāptaḥ ākāśa aviṣaya tvāt karṇa  chidre api  anupalambhanāt  api ca śabdam kuru mā śabdam kārṣīḥ  iti vyavahartāraḥ prayuñjate na te nūnam avagacchanti sa eva ayam śabda iti nānā deśeṣu ca yugapad  chabdam upalabhāmahe tad  ekasya nityasya anupapannam iti asati viśeṣe nityasya na aneka tvam kāryāṇām tu bahūnām nānā deśeṣu kriyamāṇānām upapadyate aneka deśa saṃbandhaḥ tasmāt  api  anityaḥ api ca dadhi atra iti  atra ikāraḥ prakṛtiḥ yakāraḥ  vikṛtiḥ  iti  upapadiśanti yad  vikriyate tad  anityam ikāra sādṛśyam ca yakārasya upalabhyate tena api tayoḥ prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ  lakṣyate api ca bahubhiḥ  uccārayadbhiḥ  mahān śabdaḥ śrūyate sa yadi  abhivyajyate bahubhiḥ  alpa aiḥ  ca uccāryamāṇa s tāvān eva upalabhyeta atas  manyāmahe nūnam asya ekaikena kaścid  avayavaḥ kriyate yad  pracayāt  ayam mahān upalabhyate tuśabdāt  pakṣaḥ  viparivartate yad  uktam prayatnāt  uttara kāle darśanāt  kṛtakaḥ  ayam iti yadi vispaṣṭena hetunā śabdasya nitya tvam vaktum śakṣyāmaḥ tatas  nitya pratyaya sāmarthyāt  prayatnena abhivyajyata iti bhaviṣyati yadi prāk  uccāraṇāt  anabhivyaktaḥ prayatnena abhivyajyate tasmāt  ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ samam etad  yad  aparam kāraṇam uktam uccarita pradhvasta iti atra api yadi śakṣyāmaḥ  nityatām asya vispaṣṭam vaktum tatas  nitya pratyaya sāmarthyāt  kadācid  upalambham kadācid  anupalambham dṛṣṭvā kiṃcid  upalambhasya nimittam kalpayiṣyāmaḥ tad  ca saṃyoga vibhāga sadbhāve sati bhavati iti saṃyoga vibhāgau   eva abhivyañjakau   iti vakṣyāmaḥ uparatayoḥ saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ śrūyata iti ced  na etad  evam na nūnam uparamanti saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ yata upalabhyate śabda iti na hi te pratyakṣā iti yadi śabdam saṃyoga vibhāgā eva abhivyañjanti na kurvanti ākāśa viṣaya tvāt  chabdasya ākāśasya eka tvāt  ya eva ayam atra śrotra ākāśaḥ sa eva deśa antareṣu  api iti śrughna sthaiḥ saṃyoga vibhāgaiḥ  abhivyaktaḥ pāṭaliputre api  upalabhyeta yasya punar  kurvanti tasya vāyavīyāḥ saṃyoga vibhāgā vāyu āśrita tvāt  vāyuṣu  eva kariṣyanti yathā tantavas tantuṣu  eva paṭam tasya pāṭaliputreṣu  anupalambhaḥ  yuktaḥ śrughna stha tvāt  teṣām yasya api  abhivyañjanti tasya api  eṣa na doṣaḥ dūre satyāḥ karṇa śaṣkulyā anupakārakāḥ saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ tena dūre yad  śrotram tena na upalabhyata iti na etad  evam aprāptāḥ  ced  saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ śrotrasya upakuryuḥ saṃnikṛṣṭa vikṛṣṭa deśa sthau yugapad  chabdam upalabheyātām na ca yugapad  upalabhete tasmāt  na aprāptā upakurvanti na ced  upakurvanti tasmāt  animittam śabda upalambhane saṃyoga vibhāgau   iti na etad  evam abhighātena hi preritā vāyavas timitāni vāyu antarāṇi pratibādhamānāḥ sarvatodikkān saṃyoga vibhāgān utpādayanti yāvat  vegam abhipratiṣṭhante te ca vāyoḥ  apratyakṣa tvāt  saṃyoga vibhāgā na upalabhyante anuparateṣu  eva teṣu śabda upalabhyate na uparateṣu atas  na doṣaḥ ata eva ca anuvātam dūrāt  upalabhyate śabdaḥ yad  aparam kāraṇam uktam śabdam kuru mā kārṣīḥ  iti vyavahartāraḥ prayuñjate yadi  asaṃśayam nityaḥ śabdaḥ śabda prayogam kurv iti bhaviṣyati yathā gomayāt  kurv iti saṃhāre yad  tu  eka deśasya sataḥ  nānā deśeṣu yugapad  darśanam anupapannam iti ādityam paśya devānāṃpriya ekaḥ san   aneka deśau   asthita iva lakṣyate katham punar  avagamyata eka āditya iti ucyate prāṅmukhaḥ  devadattaḥ pūrvāhne saṃprati purastād ādityam paśyati tasya dakṣiṇatas  avasthitaḥ  na dvau paśyati ātmanaḥ  ca saṃprati na tiraścīnam devadattasya ārjave tasmāt  eka āditya iti dūra tvāt  asya deśaḥ  na avadhāryate atas  vyāmohaḥ evam śabde api vyāmohāt  anavadhāraṇam deśasya yadi śrotram saṃyoga vibhāga deśam āgatya śabdam gṛhṇīyāt  tathā api tāvat  aneka deśa tā kadācid  avagamyeta na ca tad saṃyoga deśam āgacchati pratyakṣā hi karṇaśaṣkulī tad deśā gṛhyate vāyavīyāḥ punar  saṃyoga vibhāgā apratyakṣasya vāyoḥ karṇa śaṣkulī pradeśe prādurbhavantaḥ  na upalabhyanta iti na anupapannam ata eva vyāmohaḥ  yad  nānā deśeṣu śabda iti ākāśa deśaḥ  ca śabda iti ekam ca punar  ākāśam atas  api na nānā deśeṣu api ca ekarūpye sati deśa bhedena kāmam deśā eva bhinnāḥ na tu śabdaḥ tasmāt  ayam api  adoṣaḥ na ca dadhi atra iti  atra prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ śabda antaram ikārāt  yakāraḥ na hi yakāram prayuñjānā ikāram upādadate yathā kaṭam cikrīrṣantaḥ  vīraṇāni na ca sādṛśya mātram dṛṣṭvā prakṛtiḥ  vikṛtiḥ  vā ucyate na hi dādhi piṭakam dṛṣṭvā kunda piṭakam ca prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ  avagamyate tasmāt  ayam api  adoṣaḥ yad  ca etad  bahubhiḥ  bherīm ādhmanadbhiḥ śabdam uccārayadbhiḥ  mahān  śabda upalabhyate tena prati puruṣam śabda avayava pracaya iti gamyate na evam niravayavaḥ  hi śabdaḥ avayava bhedān avagamān niravayavatvāc ca mahattva anupapattiḥ atas  na vardhate śabdaḥ mṛduḥ  ekena bahubhiḥ  ca uccāryamāṇe tāni  eva akṣarāṇi karṇa śaṣkulī maṇḍalasya sarvām nemim vyāpnuvadbhiḥ saṃyoga vibhāgaiḥ  nairantaryeṇa anekaśas  grahaṇān mahān iva avayavavān iva upalabhyante saṃyoga vibhāgā nairantaryeṇa kriyamāṇāḥ śabdam abhivyañjantaḥ  nāda śabda vācyāḥ tena nādasya eṣā vṛddhiḥ na śabdasya iti nityaḥ śabdaḥ  bhavitum arhati kutas  darśanasya para artha tvāt  darśanam uccāraṇam tad  para artham param artham pratyāyayitum uccarita mātre hi vinaṣṭe śabde na ca anyaḥ  anyān artham pratyāyayitum śaknuyāt  atas  na para artham uccāryeta atha na vinaṣṭaḥ tatas  bahuśa upalabdha tvāt  artha avagama iti yuktam arthavat  sādṛśyāt  artha avagama iti ced  na kaścid  arthavān sarveṣām nava tvāt  kasyacid  pūrvasya kṛtrimaḥ saṃbandhaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti ced  tad  uktam sadṛśa iti ca avagate vyāmohāt  pratyayaḥ vyāvarteta mālā śabdān mālā pratyaya iva yathā gāvī śabdāt  sāsnādim iti pratyayasya anivṛttiḥ tadvat  bhaviṣyati iti ced  na hi gaḥ śabdam tatra uccārayitum icchā na iha anya śabda uccicārayiṣā na ca ekena uccāraṇa āyatnena saṃvyavahāraḥ  ca artha saṃbandhaḥ  ca śakyate kartum tasmāt  darśanasya para artha tvāt  nityaḥ śabdaḥ gaḥ śabda uccarite sarva gavīṣu yugapad  pratyayaḥ bhavati ata ākṛti vacanaḥ  ayam na ca ākṛtyā śabdasya saṃbandhaḥ śakyate kartum nirdiśya hi  ākṛtim kartā saṃbadhnīyāt  gopiṇḍe ca bahūnām ākṛtīnām sadbhāvāt  chabdam antareṇa gaḥ śabda vācyām vibhaktām ākṛtim kena prakāreṇa upadekṣyati nitye tu sati gaḥ śabde bahu kṛtva uccaritaḥ śruta pūrvaḥ  ca anyāsu gaḥ vyaktiṣu  anvaya vyatirekābhyām ākṛti vacanam avagamiṣyati tasmāt  api nityaḥ aṣṭa kṛtvā u gaḥ śabda uccarita iti vadanti na aṣṭau gaḥ śabdā iti kim atas  yadi  evam anena vacanena avagamyate pratyabhijānanti iti vayam tāvat  pratyabhijānīmaḥ  na naḥ karaṇa daurbalyam evam anye api pratyabhijānanti sa eva ayam iti pratyabhijānānā vayam iva anye api na anya iti vaktum arhanti atha matam anya tve sati sādṛśyena vyāmūḍhāḥ sa iti vakṣyanti tad  na na hi te sadṛśa iti pratiyanti kim tarhi sa eva ayam iti vidite ca sphuṭe anya tve vyāmoha iti gamyate na ca ayam anya iti praty akṣam anyat  vā pramāṇam asti syāt  etad  buddhi karmaṇī api te pratyabhijñāyete te api nitye prāpnutaḥ na eṣa doṣaḥ na hi te pratyakṣe atha pratyakṣe nitye eva hi  astanasya śabdasya vināśāt  anyaḥ  adyatana iti ced  na eṣa vinaṣṭaḥ yata enam punar  upalabhāmahe na hi pratyakṣa dṛṣṭam muhūrtam adṛṣṭvā punar  upalabhyamānam pratyabhijānantaḥ  vinaṣṭam parikalpayanti parikalpayantaḥ  dvitīya saṃdarśane mātari jāyāyām pitari vā na āśvasyuḥ na hi  anupalambha mātreṇa na asti iti  avagamya naṣṭa iti  eva kalpayanti apramāṇa tāyām viditāyām na asti iti  avagacchāmaḥ na hi pramāṇe pratyakṣe sati  apramāṇa tā syāt  asti iti punar  avyāmohena avagamyamāne na kvacid  api  abhāvaḥ na ca asiddhe abhāve vyāmohaḥ na ca siddhaḥ  abhāvaḥ tasmāt  asati vyāmohe na abhāvaḥ tad  e tad  ānupūrvyā siddham tasmāt  purastād anuccāritam anupalabhamānā api na vinaṣṭa iti  avagantum arhanti yathā gṛhān nirgatāḥ sarva gṛha janam apaśyantaḥ punar  praviśya upalabhamānā api na prāk  praveśāt  vinaṣṭa iti  avagacchanti tadvat  enam api na anya iti vaktum arhanti ye api sarveṣām bhāvānām pratikṣaṇam vināśam abhyupagacchanti te api na śaknuvanti śabdasya vaditum ante hi kṣaya darśanāt te manyante na ca śabdasya antaḥ na ca kṣayaḥ  lakṣyate sa iti pratyakṣaḥ pratyayaḥ sadṛśa iti  ānumānikaḥ na ca pratyakṣa viruddham anumānam udeti sva kāryam vā sādhayati tasmāt  nityaḥ yeṣām anavagata utpattīnām dravyāṇām bhāva eva lakṣyate teṣām api keṣāṃcid  anitya tā gamyate yeṣām vināśa kāraṇam upalabhyate yathā abhinavam paṭam dṛṣṭvā na ca evam kriyamāṇam upalabdhavān athavā anitya tvam avagacchati rūpam eva dṛṣṭvā tantu vyatiṣaṅga janitaḥ  ayam tantu vyatiṣaṅga vināśāt tantu vināśāt  vā vinaśyati iti  avagacchati na evam śabdasya kiṃcid  kāraṇam avagamyate yad  vināśāt  vinaṅkṣyati iti  avagamyate idam padebhyaḥ kebhyaścid uttaram sūtram nanu vāyukāraṇakaḥ syāt  iti vāyuḥ  udgataḥ saṃyoga vibhāgaiḥ śabdaḥ  bhavati iti tathā ca śikṣā ākārā āhuḥ vāyuḥ  āpadyate śabda tām iti na etad  evam vāyavīyaḥ  ced  chabdaḥ  bhavet  vāyoḥ saṃniveśa viśeṣaḥ syāt  na ca vāyavīyān avayavāñ śabde sataḥ pratyabhijānīmaḥ  yathā paṭasya tantu mayān na ca evam bhavati syāt  ced  evam sparśa ne na upalabhemahi na ca vāyavīyān avayavāñ śabda gatān spṛśāmaḥ tasmāt  na vāyukāraṇakaḥ atas  nityaḥ liṅgam ca eva bhavati vācā virūpa nityayā iti anya param hi idam vākyam vācaḥ  nityatām anuvadati tasmāt  nityaḥ śabdaḥ yadi  api  autpattikaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ  artha saṃbandhaḥ  ca tathā api na codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  dharmaḥ codanā hi vākyam na hi  agni hotram juhuyāt  svarga kāma  iti  atas  vākyāt  anyatamāt  padād agnihotrāt  svargaḥ  bhavati iti gamyate gamyate tu pada traya uccarite na ca atra caturthaḥ śabdaḥ  asti  anyat  atas  pada traya samudāyāt  na ca ayam samudāyaḥ  asti loke yatas  asya vyavahārāt  arthaḥ  avagamyate padāni  amūni prayuktāni teṣām nityaḥ  arthaḥ aprayukta ś ca samudāyaḥ tasmāt  samudāyasya arthaḥ kṛtrimaḥ  vyāmohaḥ  vā na ca padārthā eva vākya arthaḥ sāmānye hi padam pravartate viśeṣe vākyam anya t  ca sāmānyam anyaḥ  viśeṣaḥ na ca padārtha āt  vākya artha avagatiḥ asaṃbandhāt  asati ced  saṃbandhe kasmiṃścid  padārthe avagate artha antaram avagamyeta ekasmin   avagate sarvam avagatam syāt  na ca etad  evam bhavati tasmāt  anyaḥ  vākya arthaḥ syāt  etad  aprayuktāt  api vākyāt  asati saṃbandhe svabhāvāt  artha avagama iti yadi kalpyeta śabdaḥ  dharmam ātmīyam vyutkrāmet  na ca eṣa śabda dharmaḥ  yad  aprayuktāt  api śabda arthaḥ pratīyate na hi prathama śrutāt  kutaścic chabdāt  kecid  artham pratiyanti tad  abhidhīyate pada dharmaḥ  ayam na vākya dharmaḥ vākyāt  dhi prathama avagatāt  api pratiyantaḥ  artham dṛśyante na etad  evam yadi prathama śrutāt  avagaccheyuḥ api tarhi sarve avagaccheyuḥ padārtha vidaḥ  anye ca na tu  apadārtha vidaḥ  avagacchanti tasmāt  na etad  evam nanu padārthavadbhiḥ  api  avagacchadbhiḥ  akṛta eva vākya artha saṃbandhaḥ  bhaviṣyati padārtha vedanena hi saṃskṛtā avagamiśyanti yathā tam eva padārtham dvitīya ādi śravaṇena iti na iti brūmaḥ yadi vākye antyaḥ  varṇaḥ pūrva varṇa janita saṃskāra sahitaḥ padārthebhyaḥ  artha antaram pratyāyayati upakāra s tu tadānīm padārtha jñānāt  avakalpate tasmāt  kṛtrimaḥ  vākya artha pratyayaḥ vyāmohaḥ  vā na padārtha dvāreṇa saṃbhavati vākya artha jñānam iti nanu  evam bhaviṣyati sāmānya vācinaḥ padasya gauḥ  iti vā aśva iti vā viśeṣakam śukla iti vā kṛṣṇa iti vā padam antikāt  upanipatati yadā tadā vākya arthaḥ  avagamyate tad  na na hi katham iva gauḥ  iti vā aśva iti vā sāmānya vācinaḥ padāt  sarva gavīṣu sarva aśveṣu ca buddhiḥ  upasarpantī śruti janitā vākya anurodhena kutaścid  viśeṣāt  apavarteta na ca śukla iti ādeḥ  viśeṣa vacanasya kṛṣṇa ādi nivṛttiḥ  bhavati śabda arthaḥ na ca anartha kaḥ mā bhūd iti  artha parikalpanā śakyā atas  na padārtha janitaḥ  vākya arthaḥ tasmāt  kṛtrimaḥ pada saṃghātāḥ khalu  ete saṃghāta āś ca puruṣa kṛtā dṛśyante yathā nīlotpala vaneṣu  adya carantaś cāru saṃravāḥ nīla kauśeya saṃvītāḥ praṇaśyanti iva kādambāḥ atas  vaidikā api puruṣa kṛtā iti teṣu  eva padārtheṣu bhūtānām vartamānānām  padānāṃ  kriyā arthena samuccāraṇam na anapekṣya padārthān pārtha garthyena vākyam artha antara prasiddham kutas  pramāṇa abhāvāt  na kiṃcana pramāṇam asti yena pramimīmahe na hi  anapekṣita padārthasya vākya antya varṇasya pūrva varṇa janita saṃskāra rahitasya śaktiḥ  asti padārthebhyaḥ  artha antare vartitam iti nanu  arthāpattiḥ  asti yad  padārtha vyatiriktam artham avagacchāmaḥ na ca śaktim antareṇa tad  avakalpyata iti tad  na arthasya tad nimitta tvāt  bhavet  arthāpattiḥ yadi  asatyām api śaktau na anyan nimittam avakalpyeta avagamyate tu nimittam kim padārthāḥ padāni hi svam svam padārtham abhidhāya nivṛtta vyāpārāṇi atha idānīm padārthā avagatāḥ santaḥ  vākya artham gamayanti katham yatra hi śukla iti vā kṛṣṇa iti vā guṇaḥ pratīte bhavati bhavati khalu  asau  alam guṇavati pratyayam ādhātum tena guṇavati pratyayam icchantaḥ kevalam guṇa vacanam uccārayanti saṃpatsyata eṣām yathā saṃkalpitaḥ  abhiprāyaḥ bhaviṣyati viśiṣṭa artha saṃpratyayaḥ viśiṣṭa artha saṃpratyayaś ca vākya arthaḥ evam ced  avagamyate anyata eva vākya arthaḥ kaḥ  jātucit  adṛṣṭā pada samudāyasya śaktiḥ  arthāt  avagamyata iti vadiṣyati api ca anvaya vyatirekābhyām etad  avagamyate bhavati hi kadācid  iyam avasthā mānasāt  api  ādhātāt  yad  uccaritebhyaḥ padebhyaḥ  na padārthā avadhāryante tadānīm niyogataḥ  vākya artham na avagaccheyuḥ yadi  asya apārtha garthyam abhaviṣyat  niyogatas tu na avagacchanti api ca antareṇa api pada uccāraṇam yaḥ śauktyam avagacchati avagacchati  eva asau śukla guṇakam tasmāt  padārtha pratyaya eva vākya arthaḥ na asya pada samudāyena saṃbandhaḥ yad  tu śrautaḥ padārthaḥ  na vākya anurodhena kutaścid  viśeṣāt  apavartitum arhati iti satyam evam etad  yatra kevalaḥ padārthaḥ prayujyamānaḥ prayojana abhāvāt  anarthakaḥ saṃjāyata iti  avagatam bhavati tatra vākya arthaḥ  api tāvat  bhavatu  iti viśiṣṭa artha tā avagamyate na sarvatra evam ca sati guṇa antara pratiṣedhaḥ  na śabda artha iti  etad  api parihṛtam bhavati api ca prātipadikāt  uccarantī dvitīya ādi vibhaktiḥ prātipadikā arthaḥ  viśeṣaka iti  āha sā ca viśeṣa śrutiḥ sāmānya śrutim bādheta yad  ca ete pada saṃghātāḥ puruṣa kṛtā dṛśyanta iti parihṛtam tad  asmaraṇa ādibhiḥ api ca evaṃjātīyake arthe vākyāni saṃhartum na kiṃcana puruṣāṇam bījam asti laukikeṣu punar  artheṣu pratyakṣeṇa artham upalabhya sanniyamaḥ sannibandhanam śakyam tatra saṃhartum evaṃjātīyakāni vākyāni nīlotpala vaneṣu  adya iti tasmāt  agni hotram juhuyāt  svarga kāma  iti  etebhyaḥ  eva padebhyaḥ  ye arthā avagatāḥ tebhyaḥ  eva etad  avagamyate agnihotrāt  svargaḥ  bhavati iti padebhyaḥ  eva padārtha pratyayaḥ padārthebhyaḥ  vākya artha iti uktam codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  arthaḥ  dharma iti yatas  na puruṣa kṛtaḥ śabdasya arthena saṃbandhaḥ tatra pada vākya āśraya ākṣepaḥ parihṛtaḥ idānīm anyathā ākṣepsyāmaḥ pauruṣeyāḥ  codanā iti vadāmaḥ saṃnikṛṣṭa kālāḥ kṛtakā vedā idānīm tanāḥ te ca codanānām samūhāḥ tatra pauruṣeyāḥ  ced  vedāḥ asaṃśayam pauruṣeyāḥ  codanāḥ katham punar  kṛtakā vedā iti kecid  manyante yatas  puruṣa ākhyāḥ puruṣeṇa hi samākhyāyante vedāḥ kāṭhakam kālāpakam paippalādakam mauhulam iti na hi saṃbandhāt  ṛte samākhyānam na ca puruṣasya śabdena asti saṃbandhaḥ anyatas  kartā puruṣaḥ kāryaḥ śabda iti nanu pravacana lakṣaṇā samākhyā syāt  na iti brūmaḥ asādhāraṇam hi viśeṣaṇam bhavati eka eva hi kartā bahavaḥ  api prabrūyuḥ atas  asmaryamāṇaḥ  api codanāyāḥ kartā syāt  tasmāt  na pramāṇam codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  arthaḥ  dharma iti janana maraṇavantaḥ  ca veda arthāḥ śrūyante babaraḥ prāvāhaṇiḥ  akāmayata kusuruvinda auddālakiḥ  akāmayata iti evamādyaḥ uddālakasya apatyam gamyata auddālakiḥ yadi  evam prāk  auddālaki janmanaḥ na ayam granthaḥ  bhūta pūrvaḥ evam api  anitya tā uktam asmābhiḥ śabda pūrva tvam adhyetṝṇām kevalam ākṣepa parihāraḥ  vaktavyaḥ saḥ  abhidhīyate yad  uktam kartṛ lakṣaṇā samākhyā kāṭhaka ādya iti tad  ucyate na iyam arthāpattiḥ akartṛbhiḥ  api hi  enām ācakṣīran prakarṣeṇa vacanam  ananyasādhāraṇaṃ  kaṭha ādibhiḥ  anuṣṭhitam syāt  tathā api hi samākhyātāraḥ  bhavanti smaryate ca vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ sarva śākhā adhyāyī kaṭhaḥ punar  imām kevalām śākhām adhyāpayām babhūva iti sa bahu śākhā dhyāyinām saṃnidhau   eka śākhā adhyāyy anyām śākhām anadhīyānaḥ tasyām prakṛṣṭa tvāt  asādhāraṇam upapadyate viśeṣaṇam yad  ca prāvāhaṇiḥ  iti tad  na pravāhaṇasya puruṣasya asiddhatvān na pravāhaṇasya apatyam prāvāhāniḥ praśabdaḥ prakarṣe siddhaḥ vahatiḥ  ca prāpaṇe  na tu  asya samudāyaḥ kvacid  siddhaḥ   ikāra s tu yathā eva apatye siddha s tathā kriyāyām api kartari tasmāt  yaḥ pravāhayati sa prāvāhaṇiḥ babara iti śabda anukṛtiḥ tena yaḥ  nitya artha s tam eva etau śabdau vadiṣyataḥ ata uktam param tu śruti sāmānya mātram iti atha katham avagamyate na ayam unmatta bāla vākya sadṛśa iti tathā hi paśyāmaḥ vanaspatayaḥ satram āsata sarpāḥ satram āsata iti yathā jarad gavaḥ  gāyati mattakāni katham nāma jarad gavaḥ  gāyeta katham vā vanaspatayaḥ sarpā vā satram āsīran   iti ucyate viniyuktam hi dṛśyate paraspareṇa saṃbandha artham katham jyotiṣṭoma iti  abhidhāya kartavya iti  ucyate kena iti  ākāṅkṣite somena iti kim artham iti svargāya iti katham iti ittham  anaya iti kartavyatayā  iti evam avagacchantaḥ padārthaiḥ  ebhiḥ saṃskṛtam piṇḍitam vākya artham katham unmatta bāla vākya sadṛśam iti vakṣyāmaḥ nanu  anupapannam idam dṛśyate vanaspatayaḥ satram āsata iti evamādi na anupapannam na anena agni hotram juhuyāt  svarga kāma  iti  evamādayaḥ  anupapannāḥ syuḥ api ca vanaspatayaḥ satram āsata iti evamādayaḥ  api na anupapannāḥ stutayaḥ hi  etāḥ satrasya vanaspatayaḥ  nāma acetanā idam satram upāsitavantaḥ kim punar  vṛddhāṃsaḥ  brāhmaṇāḥ tad  yathā loke sandhyāyām mṛgā api na caranti kim punar  vidvāṃsaḥ  brāhmaṇā iti api ca avigītaḥ suhṛd upadeśaḥ su pratiṣṭhitaḥ katham iva āśaṅketa unmatta bāla vākya sadṛśa iti tasmāt  codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  arthaḥ  dharma iti siddham saḥ  arodīd yad  arodīt  tad  rudrasya rudra tvam prajāpatiḥ  ātmanaḥ  vapām udakhidat  devāḥ  vai deva yajanam adhyavasāya diśaḥ  na prājānan iti evamādīni samāmnātāraḥ samāmananti vākyāni tāni kim kaṃcid  dharmam pramimate uta na iti bhavati vicāraṇā tad  abhidhīyate kriyā katham anuṣṭheya iti tām vaditum samāmnā tāraḥ  vākyāni samāmananti tad  yāni vākyāni kriyām na avagamayanti kriyā saṃbaddham vā kiṃcid  evam eva bhūtam artham anvācakṣate ruditavān rudraḥ vapām ucci kheda prajāpatiḥ devāḥ  vai diśaḥ  na prajajñira iti evaṃjātīyakāni tāni kam dharmam pramimīran atha ucyeta adhyāhāreṇa vā vipariṇāmena vā vyavahita kalpanayā vā vyavadhāraṇa kalpanayā vā guṇa kalpanayā vā kaścid  arthaḥ kalpāyiṣyata iti sa kalpyamānaḥ kaḥ kalpyeta rudraḥ kila ruroda atas  anyena api roditavyam ucci khedātmavapām prajāpatiḥ atas  anyaḥ  api  utkhidet  ātmanaḥ  vapām devāḥ  vai deva yajana kāle diśaḥ  na prajñātavantaḥ atas  anyaḥ  api diśaḥ  na prajānīyāt  iti tad  ca aśakyam iṣṭa viyogena abhighātena vā yad  bāṣpa nirmocanam tad  rodanam iti  ucyate na ca tad  icchātaḥ  bhavati na ca kaści d ātmanaḥ  vapām utkhidya tām agnau prahṛtya tatas  utthitena tu upareṇa paśuṇā yaṣṭum śaknuyāt  na ca devayajana adhyavasāna kāle kecid  diśaḥ  muhyeyuḥ ata eṣām ānarthakyam tasmāt  evaṃjātīyakāni vākyāni  anityāni iti  ucyante  yady api ca nityāni tathā api na nityam artham kurvanti  iti sa eṣa vākya eka deśasya ākṣepaḥ na kṛtsnasya vākyasya nanu  eka deśāt  vinā sa ākāṅkṣaḥ pada samūhaḥ  na paryāptaḥ svasmai prayojanāya ata ākṣipta eva iti na evam bhavati hi kaścid  pada samūhaḥ yaḥ  artha vādebhyaḥ  vinā api vidadhāti kaṃcid  artham yāni punar  taiḥ saha saṃyujya artha antare vartante tāni  eka deśa ākṣepeṇa ākṣipyate stenam manaḥ anṛta vādinī vāc  iti evaṃjātīyakānām dharmam praty aprāmāṇyam bhūta anuvādāt  vipariṇāma ādibhiḥ  api kalpyamāne steyam mṛṣodyam ca kartavyam iti  āpatati tad  ca aśakyam steya anṛta vāda pratiṣedham abādha mānena anuṣṭhātum na ca vikalpaḥ vaiṣamyāt  ekaḥ kalpyaḥ  vidhiḥ ekaḥ pratyakṣaḥ atha dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ tasmāt  dhūma eva agneḥ  divā dadṛśe na arciḥ tasmāt  arciḥ  eva agneḥ  naktam dadṛśe na dhūma iti asmāl lokāt  utkramya agniḥ  ādityam gataḥ rātrau   ādityaḥ tam iti  etad  upapādayitum idam ubhayam api dṛṣṭa viruddham ucyate tasmāt  na eṣā avadhāraṇā sidhyati iti aparaḥ  dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ na ca etad  vidmaḥ  vayam brāhmaṇā vā smaḥ abrāhmaṇā vā iti  akriyā artha tvāt  anarthakam atha ayam arthaḥ na eva etad  jñāyate kim vā brāhmaṇā vayam uta abrāhmaṇā eva iti pratyakṣa viruddham apramāṇam aparaḥ śāstra dṛṣṭena virodhaḥ kaḥ  hi tad  veda yad  amuṣmin   loke asti vā na vā iti yadi praśnaḥ  ayam akriyā artha tvāt  anarthakaḥ atha anavakḷptiḥ śāstra dṛṣṭena virodhaḥ atas  pratyakṣa viruddham apramāṇam garga tri rātra brāhmaṇam prakṛtyā ucyate śobhate asya mukham ya evam veda iti yadi bhūta anuvādaḥ anarthakaḥ atha adhyayana phala anuvādaḥ tatas  asat anuvādaḥ kāla antare phalam bhaviṣyati iti ced  na hi  atra pramāṇam asti vidhiḥ syāt  iti ced  na eṣa vidhi paraḥ dravya saṃskāra karmasu  iti cintayiṣyati  etad  upariṣṭāt  kim phala vid dhiḥ  uta artha vāda iti iha tu kim bhūta anuvādaḥ kriyā arthaḥ  vā iti āsya prajāyām vājī jāyate ya evam veda iti ca udāharaṇam pūrṇāhutyā sarvān kāmān avāpnoti paśu bandha yājī sarvān   lokān abhijayati tarati mṛtyum tarati brahmahatyām yaḥ  aśvamedhena yajate ya u ca enam evam veda iti yadi bhūta anuvāda mātram anarthakam atha phala vidhiḥ itareṣām ānarthakyam na hi akṛtvā pūrṇāhutim agnihotra ādayaḥ kriyante na ca aniṣṭvā agnīṣomīyeṇa somena yajante na ca adhītya aśvamedhena yajante tad  yathā pathi jāte arke madhu utsṛjya tena eva pathā madhu arthinaḥ parvatam na gaccheyuḥ tādṛśam hi tad  api ca āhuḥ arke ced  madhu vindeta kim artham parvatam vrajet  iṣṭasya arthasya saṃsiddhau kaḥ  vidvān yatnam ācaret  iti na pṛthivyām agniḥ  cetavyaḥ  na antarikṣe na divi iti  apratiṣedha bhāginam artham pratiṣedhanti vijñāyata eva etad  antarikṣe divi ca agniḥ  na cīyata iti pṛthivī cayana pratiṣedha artham ca yad  vākyam bhavet  cayana pratiṣedha artham eva tad  atha apramāṇam na eṣa virodhaḥ  bhavati katham tad  pramāṇam yad  vidhi antaram ākulayet  svayam ca ākulam syāt  na cetavyam hiraṇyam nidhāya cetavyam iti anitya saṃyogaḥ  ca  veda prāmāṇye sati  param tu śruti sāmānya mātram iti parihṛtaḥ idānīm veda eka deśānām ākṣiptānām punar  upodbalaka uttiṣṭhati babaraḥ prāvāhaṇiḥ  akāmayata iti idam samāmnāyate vāyavyam śvetam ālabheta bhūti kāmaḥ vāyuḥ  vai kṣepiṣṭhā devatā vāyum eva svena bhāgadheyena upadhāvati sa eva enam bhūtim gamayati iti vāyuḥ  vai kṣepiṣṭhā devatā iti  atas  yadi  api kriyā na avagamyate kriyā saṃbaddham vā kiṃcid  tathā api vidhi uddeśe na eka vākya tvāt  pramāṇam bhūti kāma iti  evam antaḥ vidhi uddeśaḥ tena eka vākya bhūtaḥ  vāyuḥ  vai kṣepiṣṭhā devatā iti evamādiḥ katham eka vākya bhāvaḥ padānām sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt  vidheḥ stuteḥ  ca eka vākya tvam bhavati bhūti kāma ālabheta  kasmāt    yatas  vāyuḥ kṣepiṣṭha iti na ayam abhisaṃbandhaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ bhūti kāmena alabdhavyam iti katham tarhi ālabheta yatas  tatas  bhūtiḥ  iti bhinnau   imau   arthau ubhaya abhidhāne vākyam bhidyeta kim arthā stutiḥ  iti ced  katham roceta na unuṣṭhīyeta iti nanu prāk  stuti vacanāt  anuṣṭhānam bhūti kāma antāt siddham stuti vacanam anarthakam na hi yadā stuti padā saṃnidhānam tadā pūrveṇa eva vidhiḥ yadā stuti pada saṃbandhaḥ na tadā bhūti kāmasya ālambhaḥ  vidhīyate yathā paṭaḥ bhavati iti paṭa utpadyata iti  arthaḥ nirākāṅkṣam ca pada dvayam yadā ca tasmin   eva rakta iti  aparam śrūyate tadā rāga saṃbandhaḥ  bhavati iti  arthaḥ bhavati ca raktam pratyākāṅkṣā evam yadā na stuti padāni vidhi śabdena eva tadā prarocanā yadā stuti vacanam tadā stavanena nanu  evam sati kim stuti vacanena yasmin sati  avidhāyakam mā bhūt  tad  tad abhāve api pūrva vidhinā eva prarocayiṣyata iti satyam vinā api tena sidhyet  prarocanam asti tu tad  tasmin vidyamāne yaḥ  arthaḥ  vākyasya saḥ  ava gamyate stuti prayojanam tayoḥ tasmin   avidyamāne vidhinā prarocanam iti nanu satsu  api stuti padeṣu pūrvasya vidhi svarūpa tvāt  vidhiḥ  abhipretaḥ syāt  na vivakṣyeta stuti pada saṃbandhaḥ āha stuti padāni hi  anarthakāni  abhaviṣyan sa ākāṅkṣāṇi bhavantu  anarthakāni iti ced  na gamyamāne arthe avivakṣita arthāni bhavitum arhanti yaḥ  asau vidhi uddeśaḥ sa śaknoti nirapekṣaḥ  artham vidhātum śaknoti ca stuti padānām vākya śeṣībhavitum pratyakṣaḥ  ca vākya śeṣa bhāvaḥ atas  asmāt  vidheḥ stutim avagacchāmaḥ nanu nirapekṣāt  api vidhim avagamiṣyām bhavatu  evam na evam sati kaścid  virodhaḥ kim tu  aśakyaḥ stuti pada saṃbandhe sati vidhi arthaḥ  vivakṣitum vākyam hi saṃbandhasya vidhāyakam dvau ced  saṃbandhau vidadhyāt  bhūti kāma ālabheta ālambhena ca eṣa guṇa u bhaviṣyati iti bhidyeta tarhi  evam sati vākyam atha yad  uktam na kriyā gamyate na tad saṃbaddham vā kiṃcid  iti stuti arthena vidhīnām syuḥ stuti śabdāḥ stuvantaḥ kriyām prarocayamāṇā anuṣṭhātṝṇām upakariṣyanti kriyāyāḥ evam imāni sarvāṇi  eva padāni kaṃcid  artham stuvanti vidadhati atas  pramāṇam evaṃjātīyakāni vāyuḥ  vai kṣepiṣṭhā devatā iti atha ucyeta prāk  stuti padebhyaḥ nirākāṅkṣāṇi vidhāyakāni vidhi svarūpa tvāt stuti padāni tu pramāda pāṭha iti tad  na evam artha avagamāt tulyam ca sāṃpradāyikam saṃpradāyaḥ  prayojanaṃ  yeṣām dharmāṇām sarve te vidhi padānām arthavāda padānām ca tulyāḥ adhyāyānadhyāyate guru mukhāt  pratipattiḥ śiṣya upādhyāya tā ca sarvasmin   evaṃjātīyake avighna arthe tulyam ādriyante smaraṇam ca dṛḍham atas  na pramāda pāṭha iti api ca yā eṣā anupapattiḥ  uktā śāstra dṛṣṭa virodhāt  iti evamādyā sā saḥ  arodīd iti evamādiṣu na prāpnoti kutas  prayoge hi steya ādīnām ucyamāne virodhaḥ syāt  śabda artha s tu  aprayoga bhūtaḥ tasmāt  upapadyeta stenam manaḥ anṛta vādinī vāc  iti yad  uktam vidheyasya prarocana arthā stutiḥ  iti tad  iha katham avakalpyeta yatra anyat  vidheyam anya t  ca stūyate yathā vetasa śākha yāvaka abhiḥ  ca agnim vikarṣati iti veta sāvake vidhīyete āpaś ca stūyante āpaḥ  vai śāntā iti tad  ucyate guṇavādas tu gauṇa eṣa vādaḥ  bhavati yad  saṃbandhini stotavye saṃbandhi antaram stūyate abhijanaḥ  hi  eṣa vetasāvakayoḥ tatas  te jāte abhijana saṃstavena ca abhijātaḥ stutaḥ  bhavati yathā aśmaka abhijanaḥ  devadattaḥ  aśmākeṣu stūyamāneṣu stutam ātmānam manyate evam atra api draṣṭavyam atha saḥ  arodīd iti kasya vidheḥ śeṣaḥ tasmāt  barhiṣi rajatam na deyam iti  asya kutas  sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt  padānām saḥ  arodīt  yad  arodīt  tad  rudrasya rudra tvam iti  atra sa iti prakṛta apekṣaḥ tad pratyayāt tasya yad  aśrv aśīryata iti tasya iti pūrva prakṛta apekṣa eva upapattiḥ  ca uparitanasya yaḥ  barhiṣi rajatam dadyāt  purā asya saṃvatsarāt  gṛhe rodanam bhavati iti asya hetu tvena ayam pratinirdiśyate tasmāt  barhiṣi rajatam na deyam iti evam sarvāṇi sa ākāṅkṣāṇi katham vidheḥ  upakurvanti iti guṇa vādena rodana prabhavam rajatam barhiṣi dadataḥ  rodanam āpadyate tad  pratiṣedhasya guṇaḥ yad  arodanam iti katham punar  arudati  arodi id iti bhavati katham vānaśru prabhave rajate aśru prabhavam iti vacanam purā asya saṃvatsarāt  asati rodane katham rodanam bhavati iti tad  ucyate guṇavādas tu gauṇā ete śabdāḥ rudra iti rodana nimittasya śabdasya darśanāt  yad  arodi id iti  ucyate varṇa sārūpyān nindan   anaśru prabhavam api  aśru prabhavam iti  āha nindan   eva ca dhana tyāge dukha darśanāt  purā asya saṃvatsarāt  gṛhe rodanam bhavati iti  āha tathā yaḥ prajā kāmaḥ paśu kāmaḥ  vā syāt  sa etam prājāpatyam tu upuram ālabheta iti ākāṅkṣita tvāt  asya vidheḥ śeṣaḥ  ayam sa ātmanaḥ  vapām udakhidad iti katham guṇa vādaḥ ittham nāma na āsan paśavaḥ yad  ātmanaḥ  vapām udakhidad iti etad  ca karmaṇaḥ sāmarthyam yad  agnau prahṛta mātrāyām vapāyām ajas tu upura udagāt  ittham bahavaḥ paśavaḥ  bhavanti iti katham punar  anutkhinnāyām vapāyām prajāpatiḥ  ātmanaḥ  vapām udakhidad iti  āha ucyate asad vṛttānta an vākhyānam stuti arthena praśaṃsāyāḥ  gamyamāna tvāt  iha anvākhyāne vartamāne dvayam niṣpadyate yad  ca vṛttānta jñānam yad  ca kasmiṃścid  prarocanā dveṣaḥ  vā tatra vṛttānta an vākhyānam na pravartakam na nivartakam ca iti prayojana abhāvāt  anarthakam iti  avivakṣitam prarocanayā tu pravartate dveṣān nivartata iti tayoḥ  vivakṣā vṛttānta an vā ākhyāne api vidhīyamāne ādimatā doṣaḥ  vedasya prasajeta katham punar  idam nirālambanam anvākhyāyata iti ucyate nityaḥ kaścid  arthaḥ prajāpatiḥ syāt  vāyuḥ ākāśaḥ ādityaḥ  vā sa ātmanaḥ  vapām udakhidad iti vṛṣṭim vāyum raśmim vā tām agnau prāgṛhṇāt  vaidyute ārcīse laukike vā tatas  aja iti  annam bījam virud vā tam ālabhya tam upayujya prajāḥ paśūn prāpnoti iti gauṇāḥ śabdāḥ ādityaḥ prāyaṇīyaḥ  caruḥ  āditya udapanīyaḥ  caruḥ  iti  asya vidheḥ śeṣaḥ devāḥ  vai deva yajanam adhyavasāya diśaḥ  na prājānann iti ākāṅkṣita tvāt  sarva vyāmohānām ādityaś caruḥ  nāśayitā api diś mohasya iti stutiḥ katham asati diś mohe diś moha śabda iti ucyate aprākṛtasya bahoḥ karma samūhasya upasthita tvāt  gauṇaḥ  moha śabdaḥ  avadhāraṇa avakāśa dāna ādibhiḥ  jñāpayati iti gauṇa tā hiraṇyam haste bhavati atha gṛhṇāti iti sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt  asya vidheḥ śeṣaḥ stenam manaḥ  anṛta vādinī vāc  iti nindā vacanam hiraṇyaḥ tuti arthena yathā kim ṛṣiṇā devadatta eva bhojayitavyaḥ katham punar  astenam manaḥ  ninditum api stena śabdena ucyate vācam ca ananṛta vādinīm api  anṛta vādinī iti brūyat  guṇavādas tu rūpāt  yathā stenāḥ pracchanna rūpāḥ evam ca mana iti gauṇaḥ śabdaḥ prāyāt  ca anṛta vādinī vāc  iti dṛṣṭa virodha udāharaṇam tasmāt  bhūma eva agneḥ  divā dadṛśe na arciḥ tasmāt  arciḥ  eva agneḥ  naktam dadṛśe na dhūma iti agniḥ  jyotiḥ  jyotiḥ  agniḥ svāhā iti sāyam juhoti sūryaḥ  jyotiḥ  jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāhā iti prātar iti miśra liṅga mantrayoḥ  vidhānasya ākāṅkṣita tvāt  cheṣaḥ ubhayoḥ  devatayoḥ saṃnidhāne homa iti stuteḥ  upapattiḥ dūra bhūyaḥ tvāt  dhūmasya agneś ca adarśane gauṇaḥ śabdaḥ dṛṣṭa virodha eva udāharaṇam na ca etad  vidma iti tad  pravare pravriyamāṇe devāḥ pitara iti brūyāt  iti  ākāṅkṣita tvāt  asya vidheḥ śeṣaḥ abrāhmaṇaḥ  api brāhmaṇaḥ pravara anumantraṇena syāt  iti stutiḥ durjñāna tvāt  ajñāna vacanam gauṇam strī aparādhena kartuḥ  ca putra darśanena apramatā rakṣata tantum enam ityādinā durjñānam śāstra dṛṣṭa virodhe udāharaṇam kaḥ  hi tad  veda iti dikṣvatī kāśān karoti iti sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt  asya vidheḥ śeṣaḥ pratyakṣa phala tvena stutiḥ ananvakḷpti vacanam viprakṛṣṭa kāla phala tvāt  gauṇam tathā phala abhāvāt  iti  atra udāhṛtam śobhate asya mukham iti garga tri rātra vidheḥ  ākāṅkṣita tvāt  cheṣaḥ veda anumantraṇasya ca asya prajāyām vājī jāyata iti śeṣaḥ mukha śobhā vājimat tvam ca guṇa vacana tvāt  gauṇaḥ śabdaḥ śobhata iva śiṣyaiḥ  udīkṣyamāṇam kule saṃtata adhyayana śravaṇān medhāvī jāyata iti sa pratigrahāt  annam prāpnoti iti anya ānarthakyavākya udāharaṇam pūrṇāhutyā sarvān kāmān avāpnoti iti pūrṇāhutim juhoti iti  ākāṅkṣita tvāt  asya vidheḥ śeṣaḥ ya u ca enam evam veda iti tarati mṛtyum iti  asya ākāṅkṣi tvāc cheṣaḥ phala vacanam stutiḥ sarva kāma phalasya nimitte sarva kāmau   āpti vacanam gauṇam asarveṣu sarva vacanam adhikṛta apekṣam anvāruhya vacanam idam yadi  api vidhiḥ tathā api  arthavat tā parimāṇataḥ sārataḥ  vā phala viśeṣāt  abhāgi pratiṣedhāt  iti ādau   udāhṛtam na pṛthivyām agniḥ  cetavyaḥ  na antarikṣe na divi iti hiraṇyam nidhāya cetavyam iti  ākāṅkṣita tvāt  asya vidheḥ śeṣaḥ pṛthivī ādīnām nindā hiraṇyastuti arthā asati prasaṅge pratiṣedhaḥ  nitya anuvādaḥ yad  ca anitya darśanam babaraḥ prāvāhaṇiḥ  akāmayata iti tad parihṛtam arthavāda ākṣepeṇa punar  utthitam idānīm arthavāda prāmāṇye tena eva parihāreṇa parihariṣyata iti iha ye vidhivan nigadā arthavādāḥ  te arthavādāḥ  te udāharaṇam audumbaraḥ  yūpaḥ  bhavati  ūrg vā uduṃbara ūrk paśava ūrjaiḥ  vā asmā ūrjam paśūn na āpnoti ūrjaḥ  avaruddhyā iti kim asya vidhiḥ kāryam uta asya api stutiḥ  iti kim tāvat  prāptam vidhiḥ  vā syāt  apūrva tvāt  vāda mātram hi  anarthakam vidhivan nigadeṣu  evaṃjātīyakeṣu phala vidhiḥ syāt  phalam hi  avagamyate tathā hi  apūrvam artham vidhāsyati itarathā stuti vāda mātram anarthakam syāt  stuta ś ca astutaḥ  ca tāvān eva saḥ  arthaḥ api ca ūrjaḥ  avaruddhyā iti prayojanam śrūyate na ca praśastaḥ  ayam artha iti kaścid  chabdaḥ  asti lakṣaṇayā tu stutiḥ  gamyate śrutiḥ  ca lakṣaṇāyāḥ  jyāyasi iti iti ced  paśyasi stutiḥ  anarthikā na ca śabdena avagamyata iti laukikāni vākyāni bhavantaḥ  vidām kurvantu tad  yathā iyam gauḥ kretavyā devadattīyā eṣā hi bahu kṣīrā strī apatyā anaṣṭa prajā ca iti kretavyā iti  api  ukte guṇa abhidhānāt  pravartanta itarām kretāraḥ bahu kṣīra iti ca guṇa abhidhānam avagamyate tadvat  vede api bhaviṣyati na etad  evam loke vidita pūrvā arthā ucyante bahu kṣīra ādayaḥ teṣām vijñānam eva na prayojanam atas  praśaṃsā gamyate avidita vāde na śraddadhīran pūrva vacanāt  iva vidita tvāt  eva ca prarocayante vaidikeṣu punar  yadi vidhi śabdena na prarocayante na tarām artha vādena jātāśaṅkaḥ  hi vidhi śabde sa tadānīm atha vidhi śabdena prarocitaḥ kim arthavāda śabdena api ca vede vyaktam asaṃvādaḥ ūrjaḥ  avaruddhyai iti  aprasiddham vacanam ūrgvā udumbara iti hetu tvam ca aprasiddham yasmāt  ūrg udumbaraḥ tasmāt  tad mayaḥ  yūpaḥ kartavya iti ūrg udumbara iti  anṛta vacanāt  anyat  asya anṛtam iti parikalpyeta uktam asmābhiḥ  vākya śeṣa tvam vidhinā tu  eka vākya tvāt  iti nanu uktam phala vacanam iha gamyate na stutiḥ  iti yad  iha phala vacanam tad  audumbarasya yūpasya na ca avihita audumbaraḥ  yūpaḥ  asti tatra phala vacanam eva anarthakam stuti vacanaḥ śabdaḥ  na asti iti ced  iha phala vacanena phalavat tā pratīyate phalavānś ca praśasta iti tatra phalavat tāyām ānarthakyam iti yaḥ  dvitīyaḥ  arthaḥ praśaṃsā nāma sa gamyate lakṣaṇa iti ced  na lakṣaṇāyām api  arthavat tā bhavati  eva lakṣaṇā api hi laukikī nanu uktam asaṃvādaḥ  vede na hi  ūrg udumbara iti guṇa vādena prarocana artha tām brūmahe gauṇa tvāt  saṃvādaḥ kim sādṛśyam yathā annam prīteḥ sādhanam evam idam api prīti sādhana śakti yuktam praśaṃsitum praśaṃsā vācinā śabdena ucyate śakyate hi tad  pakva phala saṃbandhāt  ūrg iti vaktum apsuyoniḥ  vā aśvaḥ apsujaḥ  vetasa iti apsuyoniḥ  aśvaḥ kartavya iti vidheḥ  aśakya tvāt  ānarthakyam tatra avaśyam stutiḥ kalpayitavyā śamayitrībhiḥ  adbhiḥ  aśvasya avakānām ca saṃbandhaḥ  yajamānasya kaṣṭam śamayati iti tad sāmānyāt  itareṣu tathā tvam tathā iti yāvat  tāvat  tathā tvam iti kim tad  sāmānyam vidhi asaṃbhavaḥ stuti saṃbhavaḥ  ca itas  ca paśyāmaḥ stutiḥ  iti kutas  idam samāmananti yaḥ  vidagdhaḥ sa nairṛtaḥ yaḥ  aśṛtaḥ sa raudraḥ yaḥ śṛtaḥ sa daivataḥ tasmāt  avidahatā śrapayitavyaḥ sa daivata tvāya iti yadi stutiḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  eva śṛtaḥ stāviṣyate tathā saṃbhavan   apakarṣaḥ  na kalpyeta apakṛṣyate iti  apakarṣaḥ vidhi pakṣe tu yatra nairṛtaḥ tatra vidagdha tā nīyeta tathā sati prakaraṇam bādhitam bhavet  darśa pūrṇamāsa karma prati nairṛta abhāvāt  vidagdhānam anarthakam syāt  tasmāt  stutiḥ  eva audumbaraḥ  yūpaḥ  bhavati iti vidhā   etasmin   āśrīyamāṇe ūrjaḥ  avaruddhyā iti  etasmin   ca vākyam bhidyeta ittham audumbaraḥ  yūpaḥ praśastaḥ sa ca ūrjaḥ  aviruddhyā iti tasmāt  vidhivan nigadānām api stutiḥ  eva kāryam artha vādānām iti atha ye hetuvan nigadāḥ sūrpeṇa juhoti tena hi  annam kriyata iti evamādayaḥ teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim stutiḥ  teṣām kāryam uta hetuḥ  iti kim prāptam hetuḥ syāt  anna karaṇam homasya nanu  aprasiddhe kārya kāraṇa bhāve na hetu upadeśaḥ satyam evam loke vidhāyiṣyate tu vacanena vede sūrpeṇa home kartavye anna karaṇam hetuḥ  iti  upadiśyate kim prayojanam anyat  api darvi pīṭhara ādi  anna karaṇam yad  tena api nāma katham homaḥ kriyeta iti kutas  tasya api  anna kriyāyām arthavat tā śakyate ca tena api  annam kartum etād dhi kriyata iti  ucyate na hi vartamāna kālaḥ kaścid  asti yasya ayam pratinirdeśaḥ hetau ca śrutiḥ śabdaḥ stutau lakṣaṇā yadi ca darvi pīṭhara ādi na sākṣāt  annam karoti iti na anna karaṇam iti  ucyate vyarthe tasmin sūrpa stutiḥ  anarthikā syāt  sūrpam api hi na sākṣāt  annam karoti iti tena vinā arthena sūrpasya stutiḥ  na upapadyate na tu  etad  asti śabda pūrva kaḥ  ayam arthaḥ anna karaṇam hetuḥ  iti śabdaḥ  ca anna karaṇam sūrpa home hetuḥ  iti  āha na ca darvi pīṭha rahome tena śabda pūrvam sūrpam na ca darvi piṭhara ādeḥ  codanā iti punar  yad  uktam tad  parihartavyam asmad pakṣe arthaḥ  asti vākya śeṣaḥ  hi sa vidheḥ  tadā bhavati saṃvādaḥ  ca stuti vacana tvena yathā vayam sūrpeṇa annam kriyamāṇam jānīmaḥ tathā sūrpeṇa annam kriyata iti  eva gamyate tadā ca āvartamānam stautum vartamānam iti  upadiśati tvad pakṣa eṣa doṣaḥ yasya te hetu vidhiḥ vidhau hi na paraḥ śabda arthaḥ pratīyate na ca vartamānam upadiśan vedaḥ śakyam artham vidadhyāt  āsmat pakṣe tu eṣa para śabdaḥ paratra vartate yathā loke balavān devadattaḥ  yajñadatta ādīn prasahata iti prakṛṣṭa bale api balavat  chabdaḥ  vartamānaḥ  na siṃham śārdūlam vā apekṣya prayujyate ye devadattāt  tu nikṛṣṭa balāḥ tān apekṣya bhavati evam tena hi  annam kriyata iti prakṛṣṭa anna karaṇena saṃstavaḥ sūrpasya nikṛṣṭāni  anyāni  anna ākaraṇāni  apekṣya bhaviṣyati yadi  api ca bhavet  anna karaṇam hetuḥ  darvi piṭhara prakārāṇām tathā api sūrpa etā  atiṣṭheta śabdāt  anna karaṇam hetuḥ  iti vijñāyate śadaḥ  ca sūrpasya āha na darvī piṭhara ādīnām tad  dhi nirdiśyate yasmāt  sūrpeṇa annam kriyate tasmāt  sūrpeṇa juhoti iti yathā yasmāt  balavat  upadhmātaḥ  agniḥ tena me gṛham dagdham iti na anagniḥ  api balavat  upadhmātaḥ  dahati iti gamyate atha matam yena yena annam kriyate praṇāḍyā sūrpād anyena api tena tena api homaḥ kriyata iti avyavasthā vidhīnām syāt  na kenacid  praṇāḍya annam kriyate tatra yāvat  uktam syāt  juhoti iti tāvat  eva anna karaṇena juhoti iti asmad pakṣe punar  sūrpam stūyate tena hi  annam kriyata iti vṛttānta an vākhyānam na ca vṛttānta jñāpanāya kim tarhi prarocanāya eva tasmāt  dhetuvan nigadasya api stutiḥ  eva kāryam iti atha idānīm kim vivakṣita vacanā mantrāḥ uta avivakṣita vacanāḥ kim artha prakāśanena yāgasya upakurvanti uta uccāraṇa mātreṇa iti yadi  uccāraṇa mātreṇa tadā na niyogataḥ  barhis  deva sadanam dāmi iti  eṣa barhiḥ lavane viniyujyeta abhidhānena ced  prakaraṇena vijñāta aṅga bhāvaḥ  na anyatra upakartum śaknoti iti  antareṇa api vacanam barhiḥ lavana eva viniyujyeta iti tad  evam avagacchāmaḥ uccāraṇa mātreṇa eva upakurvanti iti kutas  tad artha śāstrāt yad  abhidhāna samarthaḥ  mantraḥ tatra eva enam śāstram nibadhnāti uruprathā uru prathasva iti puroḍāśam prathayati iti vacanam idam anarthakam yadi  artha abhidhānena upakurvanti atha uccāraṇa mātreṇa tatas  vaktavyaḥ  viniyogaḥ ukta ś ca atas  na artha abhidhānena yathā sākṣaḥ puruṣaḥ pareṇa ced  nīyate nūnam akṣibhyām na paśyati iti gamyate nanu  artha vāda artham bhaviṣyati iti ced  na hi yena vidhīyate tasya vākya śeṣaḥ  arthavāda iti  uktam na ca nirapekṣeṇa vihite artha vādena kiṃcid  api prayojanam kriyate atas  na artha vāda artham vacanam tathā abhyādāna samarthā mantrā udāharaṇam liṅgāt  eva ādāne prāptā vacanena vidhīyante tām caturbhiḥ  ādatta iti catur saṃkhyā artham iti ced  na samuccaya śabda abhāvāt tathā imām agṛbhṇan rasanā amṛtasya iti  aśva abhidhānīm ādatta iti  udāharaṇam rasanā dāne prāptasya rasanādāna eva śāstram viniyojakam tad  vivakṣita artha tve na ghaṭeta iti nanu gardabha rasanām parisaṃkhyāsyati na śaknoti parisaṃkhyātam parisaṃcakṣāṇaḥ  hi sva artham ca juhyāt  para artham ca kalpeta prāptam ca bādheta tasmāt  na vivakṣita vacanā mantrāḥ atas  na pramāṇam barhiḥ deva sadanam dāmi iti  asya rūpam barhiḥ lavane viniyogasya niyata pada kramā hi mantrā bhavanti agni mūrdhā diva iti na viparyayeṇa yadi  artha pratāyana arthāḥ viparyayeṇa api  arthaḥ pratīyata iti niyamaḥ  anarthakaḥ syāt  atha uccāraṇa viśeṣa arthāḥ viparyaye anyat  uccāraṇam iti niyama āśrīyate tena yatarasmin pakṣe niyamaḥ  arthavān sa nūnam pakṣa iti nanu  arthavatsv api niyamaḥ  dṛśyate yathā indra agni iti yuktam tatra tad  viparyaye artha pratyaya abhāvāt buddhe khalu  api pāṭhād arthe tad abhidhāna samarthaḥ  mantraḥ  bhavati agnīd agnīn viharet  iti sa buddhe kim bodhayet  atha nu uccāraṇa viśeṣa arthāḥ buddhe api  uccāraṇa viśeṣaḥ  avakalpyeta iti nanu punarvacanāt  saṃskāra viśeṣaḥ  bhaviṣyati evam asmat pakṣam eva āśritaḥ  asi vacanam uccāraṇam tad  dhi śakyate kartum na artha pratyāyanam tad  pratīte aśakyam yathā sa upānatke pāde dvitīyām upānaham aśakya tvān na upādatte yajñe sādhana bhūtaḥ prakāśayitavyaḥ na ca tādṛśaḥ  arthaḥ  asti yādṛśam abhidadhati yathā catvāri śṛṅgā iti na hi catur śṛṅgam tri pādam dvi śiraskam sapta hastam kiṃcid  yajña sādhanam asti tad  atra abhidhāna arthaḥ kim abhidadhyāt  uccāraṇa arthe tu  avakalpyate tathā mā mā hiṃsīḥ  iti  asatyām api hiṃsāyām kim abhidadhyāt  acetane arthe khalu  artham nibadhnanti oṣadhe trāyasva enam iti abhidhānena upakurvanta evaṃjātīyakā oṣadhim paśu trāṇāya pratipādayeyuḥ na ca asau   acetanā śakyā pratipādayitum uccāraṇa arthe tu na eṣa doṣaḥ  bhavati tasmāt  uccāraṇa arthāḥ śṛṇota grāvāṇa iti ca udāharaṇam artha vipratiṣedhaḥ  api bhavati aditiḥ  dyauḥ  aditiḥ  antarikṣam iti sā eva dyaus tad  eva antarikṣam iti kaḥ  jātucit  avadhārayet  anavadhārayaṃ   ca kim abhidhānena upakuryāt  uccāraṇa mātre tu na eṣa virodhaḥ  bhavati tasmāt  uccāraṇa arthā mantrāḥ ekaḥ  rudraḥ  na dvitīyaḥ  avatasthe asaṃkhyātāḥ sahasrāṇi ye rudrā adhibhūmyām iti ca udāharaṇam svādhyāya kāle pūrṇikā āvahanti karoti māṇavakaḥ  avahanti mantram adhīte na asau tena mantreṇa tad abhidhānam abhyasyati  akṣara ānupūrvyā avadhāraṇa eva yatate yena ca nāma prayojanam tad  abhyasitavyam ata uccāraṇa abhyāsāt  uccāraṇena prayojanam iti  avagacchāmaḥ api ca keṣāñcin mantrāṇām aśakya eva arthaḥ  veditum yathā amyak sā ta indra ṛṣṭiḥ  asma iti sṛṇī eva jarbharī turpharītv iti indraḥ somasya kāṇuka iti ca ete kim pratyāyayeyuḥ uccāraṇa arthe tu na doṣaḥ tasmāt  uccāraṇa arthā mantrā iti anitya saṃyogaḥ khalu  api bhavet  mantreṣu  abhidhāna artheṣu yathā kim te kṛṇvanti kīkaṭeṣu gāva iti kīkaṭā nāma janapadā na ecāśākham nāma nagaram pramaṅga daḥ  rājā iti yadi  abhidhāna arthāḥ prāk  pramaṅga dān na ayam mantraḥ  anubhūta pūrva iti gamyate tad  etaiḥ  tad artha śāstra ādibhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ  mantrāṇām avivakṣita vacana tā aviśiṣṭas tu loke prayujyamānānām vede ca padānām arthaḥ sa yathā eva loke vivakṣitaḥ tathā eva vede api bhavitum arhati na evam loke taiḥ  arthaiḥ  avabuddhaiḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ iha devatābhiḥ  apratyakṣa abhi r yajña aṅga aiḥ  ca acetanaiḥ saṃlāpe na kaścid  yajñasya upakāraḥ yadi  adṛṣṭam parikalpyeta uccāraṇāt  eva tad  bhavitum arhati yad  dhi kartavyam tad  prayojanavat  uccāraṇam ca na kathaṃcid  na kartavyam yadi  apūrvāya yadi  arthāya yadi  arthaḥ  na pratyāyate na kiñcid  anarthakam yadi na prayujyate samāmnānānarthakyam tasmāt  uccāraṇāt  apūrvam tathā ca tad artha śāstrāt  uktam tad  ucyate artha pratyāyana artham eva yajñe mantra uccāraṇam yad  uktam na devatābhiḥ  yajña aṅga aiḥ  ca saṃlape prayojanam asti iti yajñe yajña aṅga prakāśanam eva prayojanam katham na hi  aprakāśite yajñe yajña aṅge ca yāgaḥ śakyaḥ  abhinirvartayitum tasmāt  tad nirvṛtti artham artha prakāśanam mahānupakāraḥ karmaṇaḥ tad  ca karoti iti  avagamyate tasmāt  asatyasya prayojanam tad  ca dṛṣṭam na śakyam apavaditum na artha abhidhānam prayojanam iti nanu  artha abhidhānena upakurvatsu tām caturbhiḥ  ādatta iti evamādy anarthakam bhavatu na jātucit  apajānīmahe dṛṣṭam artha abhidhānasya upakāraka tvam atha kim tad śāstram anarthakam eva na hi yad  uktam tām caturbhiḥ  ādatta iti samuccaya śabda abhāvān na samuccaya artham iti catur saṃkhyā viśiṣṭam ādānam kartavyam iti vākyāt  avagamyate tad  ekena mantreṇa gṛhṇan na yathāśrutam gṛhṇīyāt  iti parisaṃcakṣāṇe ca imām agṛbhṇan   iti  aśva abhidhānīm ādatta iti trayaḥ  doṣāḥ
