prāduḥṣyuḥ  iti na evam saṃbandha iti  ādatta iti katham tarhi iti  aśva abhidhānīm iti liṅgāt  raśanā mātre śabdāt  tu viśeṣe aśva abhidhānyām iti sati ca vākye liṅgam viniyojakam tad  ca asya prakaraṇāmnānā anumitam vākyam na asti katara tad etena mantreṇa ādānam kuryāt  iti yasmin sati raśanā mātre liṅgāt  prāpnoti aśva abhidhānyām tu pratyakṣam eva vacanam asmin sati tad  ānumānikam na asti tena gardabha raśanāyām na prāptiḥ  eva iti uru prathā uru prathasva iti puroḍāśam prathayati iti  artha vāda arthena punar śrutiḥ yajñapatim eva tad  prathayati iti nanu na ayam mantrasya vākya śeṣaḥ na ca prāptasya stutyā prayojanam satyam na ayam mantrasya vidhiḥ na saṃstavaḥ prathanam eva tatra stūyate mantraḥ punā rūpāt  eva prāpta iha anūdyate prathanam stotum ittham prathanam praśastam yad  kriyamāṇam evaṃrūpeṇa mantreṇa kriyate kas tadā bhavati guṇaḥ yajñapatim eva tad  prajayā paśubhiḥ prathayati kim etad  eva asya phalam bhavati na iti brūmaḥ stutiḥ katham bhaviṣyati iti  evam ucyate katham asati prathane prathayati iti śabdaḥ mantra abhidhānāt mantreṇa puroḍāśam adhvaryuḥ prathasva iti brūte yaḥ  ca evam prathasva iti brūte sa prathayati yathā yaḥ kurv iti brūte sa kārayati yad  uktam pada niyamasya arthavat tvāt  avivakṣita arthā mantrā iti kāmam anartha kaḥ niyamaḥ na dṛṣṭam apramāṇam niyata uccāraṇam adṛṣṭāya iti ced  aviruddhā adṛṣṭa kalpanā asmat pakṣe api evam pratyāyamānam abhyudaya kāri bhavati iti atha yad  uktam prokṣaṇīḥ  āsādaya iti buddha bodhanam aśakyam ata uccāraṇāt  adṛṣṭam iti tad  na kartavyam iti  api vijñāte anuṣṭhāna kāle smṛtyā prayojanam upāya antareṇa api sā prāpnoti atas  anena upāyena kartavyā iti niyama artham āmnānam saṃskāra tvāt  catvāri śṛṅgā iti  asad abhidhāne gauṇaḥ śabdaḥ gauṇī kalpanā pramāṇavat tvāt  uccāraṇāt  adṛṣṭam apramāṇam catasraḥ  hotrāḥ śṛṅgāṇi iva asya trayaḥ  asya pādā iti savana abhiprāyam dve śīrṣa iti patnī yajamānau sapta hastāsa iti chandāṃsi  abhipretya tridhā baddha iti tribhiḥ  vedaiḥ  baddhaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ kāmān varṣati iti roravīti śabda karmā mahaḥ devaḥ  martyān āviveśa iti manuṣya adhikāra abhiprāyam tad  yathā cakravāka stanī haṃsa danta āvalī kāśa vastrā śaivālakeśī nadī iti nadyāḥ stutiḥ yajña samṛddhaye sādhanānām cetana sādṛśyam upapādayitu kāma āmantraṇa śabdena lakṣayati oṣadhe trāyasva enam iti śṛṇota grāvāṇa iti atas  param prātar anuvāka anuvacanam bhaviṣyati yatra acetanāḥ santaḥ  grāvāṇaḥ  api śṛṇuyuḥ kim punar  vidvāṃsaḥ  api brāhmaṇā iti ittham ca acetanā api grāvāṇa āmantryante aditiḥ  dyauḥ  iti gauṇa eṣa śabdaḥ atas  na vipratiṣedhaḥ yathā tvam eva mātā tvam eva pitā iti tathā eka rudra daivatya ekaḥ  rudraḥ śata rudra daivatye śatam rudrā iti  avirodhaḥ yad  tu akarma kāle avahanti mantreṇa māṇavakaḥ  na pūrṇikā avahantim prakāśayitum iccati iti ayajña saṃyogāt  na yajña upakārāya etad  prakāśayitum icchati nanu prakāśanānabhyāsaḥ  akṣara abhyāsaḥ  ca paricoditaḥ ucyate saukaryāt  prakāśanānabhyāsaḥ  durgraha tvāt  ca akṣara abhyāsaḥ vidyamānaḥ  api  arthaḥ pramāda ālasya ādibhiḥ  na upalabhyate nigama nirukta vyākaraṇa vaśena dhātutaḥ arthaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ yathā sṛṇī eva jarbharī turpharītv iti evamādīn i  aśvinoḥ  abhidhānāni dvi vacana antāni lakṣyante anena aśvinoḥ kāmam aprā iti  āśvinam sūktam avagamyate devatā abhidhānāni ca ghaṭante jarbharī iti evamādīni avayava prasiddhyā ca laukikena arthena viśeṣyante evam sarvatra param tu śruti sāmānya mātram iti  atra iti āgneya āgnīdhram upatiṣṭhata iti vidhānāt  vivakṣita arthānām eva mantrāṇām bhavati liṅgeṇa upadeśaḥ yadi te agni prayojanāḥ tatas  ta āgneyā na agni śabda saṃnidhānāt ūha darśanam ca vivakṣita arthānām eva bhavati kim ūha darśanam na pitā vardhate na mātā iti anye vardhanta iti gamyate pratyakṣam kaumāra yauvana sthāviraiḥ  vardhante mātrā ādayaḥ śabdaḥ  na vardhata iti brūte kā punar  śabdasya vṛddhiḥ yad  dvi vacana bahuvacana saṃyogaḥ vidhi śabdāḥ  ca vivakṣita arthān eva mantrān anuvadanti śatam himāḥ śatam varṣāṇi jīvyāsam iti  etad  eva aha iti evam tāvat  kṛtsnasya vedasya prāmāṇyam uktam atha idānīm yatra na vaidikam śabdam upalabhemahi atha ca smaranti evam ayam arthaḥ  anuṣṭhātavyaḥ etasmai ca prayojanāya iti kim asau tathā eva syāt  na vā iti yathā aṣṭakāḥ kartavyāḥ guruḥ  anugantavyaḥ taḍāgam khanitavyam prabhā pravartayitavyā śikhā karma kartavyam iti evamādayaḥ tad  ucyate dharmasya śabda mūla tvāt  aśabdam anapekṣam syāt  iti śabda lakṣaṇaḥ  dharma iti  uktam codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  arthaḥ  dharmaḥ iti atas  nirmūla tvāt  na apekṣitavyam iti nanu ye viduḥ  ittham asau padārthaḥ kartavya iti katham iva te vadiṣyanti  akartavya eva ayam iti smaraṇa anupapattyā na hi  ananubhūtaḥ  aśrutaḥ  vā arthaḥ smaryate na ca asya avaidikasya alaukikasya ca smaraṇam upapadyate pūrva vijñāna kāraṇa abhāvāt  iti yā hi bandhyā smareta idam me dauhitra kṛtam iti na me duhitā asti iti matvā na jātucit  asau pratīyāt  samyak  etad  jñānam iti evam api yathā eva pāramparyeṇa āvicchedāt  ayam veda iti pramāṇam eṣām smṛtiḥ evam iyam api pramāṇam bhaviṣyati iti na etad  evam pratyakṣeṇa upalabdha tvāt  granthasya na anupapannam pūrva vijñānam aṣṭaka ādiṣu tu  adṛṣṭa artheṣu pūrva vijñāna kāraṇa abhāvāt  vyāmoha smṛtiḥ  eva gamyate tad  yathā kaścid  jāti andhaḥ vadet  smarāmi  aham asya rūpa viśeṣasya iti kutas  te pūrva vijñānam iti ca paryanuyuktaḥ  jāti andham eva aparam vinirdiśeta tasya kutas  jāti andha antarāt evam jāti andha paramparāyām api satyām na eva jātucit  saṃpratīyuḥ  vidvāṃsaḥ samyak darśanam etad  iti atas  na adartavyam evaṃjātīyakam anapekṣam syāt  iti api vā iti pakṣaḥ  vyāvartyate pramāṇam smṛtiḥ vijñānam hi tad  kim iti  anyathā bhaviṣyati pūrva vijñānam asya na asti kāraṇa abhāvāt  iti ced  asyāḥ  eva smṛteḥ  draḍhimnaḥ kāraṇam anumāsyāmahe tad  tu na anubhavanam anupapattyā na hi manuṣyā iha eva janmani  evaṃjātīyakam artham anubhavitum śaknuvanti janma antara anubhūtam ca na smaryate granthas tu  anumīyeta kartṛ sāmānyāt smṛti vaidika padārthayoḥ tena upapannaḥ  veda saṃyoga s traivarṇikānām nanu na upalabhanta evaṃjātīyakam grantham anupalabhamānā api  anumimīran vismaraṇam api  upapadyata iti tad  upapanna tvāt  pūrva vijñānasya tari varṇikānām smaratām vismaraṇasya ca upapanna tvāt  grantha anumānam upapadyata iti pramāṇam smṛtiḥ aṣṭaka āliṅgāś ca mantrā vede dṛśyante yān  janāḥ pratinandanti iti evamādayaḥ tathā pratyupasthita niyamānām ācārāṇām dṛṣṭa artha tvāt  eva prāmāṇyam guroḥ  anugamāt  prītaḥ  guruḥ  adhyāpayiṣyati grantha granthi bhedinaḥ  ca nyāyān parituṣṭaḥ  vakṣyati iti tathā ca darśayati tasmāt  chreyāṃsam pūrvam yantam pāpīyān paścāt  anveti iti prapāḥ taḍāgāni ca para upakārāya na dharmāya iti  eva avagamyate tathā ca darśanam dhanvan   iva prapā asi iti tathā sthalayā udakam parigṛhṇanti iti ca gotra cihnam śikhā karma darśanam ca yatra bāṇāḥ saṃpatanti kumārā viśikhā iva iti tena ye dṛṣṭa arthāḥ te tatas  eva pramāṇam ye tu  adṛṣṭa arthāḥ teṣu vaidika śabda anumānam iti atha yatra śruti virodhaḥ tatra katham yathā audumbaryāḥ sarva veṣṭanam audumbarīm spṛṣṭvā udgāyet  iti śrutyā viruddham aṣṭācatvāriṃśat  vaṛṣāṇi veda brahmacaraṇam jāta putraḥ kṛṣṇa keśaḥ  agnīn ādadhīta iti  anena viruddham krīta rāja kaḥ  bhojyān na iti tasmāt  agnīṣomīye saṃsthite yajamānasya gṛhe aśitavyam iti  anena viruddham tad  pramāṇam kartṛ sāmānyāt  iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ aśakya tvāt  vyamoha iti  avagamyate katham aśakyatā sparśa vidhānān na sarvā śakyā veṣṭayitum udgāyatā spraṣṭum ca tām udgāyatā spraṣṭavyām avagacchantaḥ kena imam saṃpratyayam bādhemahi sarva veṣṭana smaraṇena iti brūmaḥ nanu nirmūla tvāt  vyāmohas tad  smaraṇam iti vaidikam vacanam mūlam bhaviṣyati iti bhavet  vaidikam vacanam mūlam yadi sparśanam vyāmohaḥ avyāmohe tu  aśakya tvāt  anupapannam yathā anubhavanam anupapannam iti na kalpyate tathā vaidikam api vacanam katham tarhi sarva veṣṭana smaraṇam vyāmohaḥ katham vyāmoha kalpanā śrauta vijñāna virodhāt atha kim artham na imau vidhī vikalpye te vrīhi yavavat  bṛhat rathantaravat  vā na asati vyāmoha vijñāne vikalpaḥ  bhavati yadi sarva veṣṭana vijñānam pramāṇam sparśanam vyāmohaḥ yadi sparśanam pramāṇam smṛtiḥ  vyāmohaḥ vikalpam tu vadan sparśanasya pakṣe tāvat  prāmāṇyam anumanyate tasya ca mūlam śrutiḥ sā ced  pramāṇam anumatā na pākṣikī pākṣikam ca sarva veṣṭana smaraṇam pakṣe tāvan na śaknoti śrutim parikalpayitum sparśa vijñānena bādhita tvāt  tatas  ca avyāmohe ca tasmin   aśakyā śrutiḥ kalpayitum na ca asau   avyāmohaḥ pakṣe pakṣe vyāmohaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti yad  eva hi tasya ekasmin pakṣe mūlam tad  eva itarasmin   api ekasminś ced  pakṣe na vyāmohaḥ śruti prāmāṇya tulya tvāt  itaratra api  avyāmohaḥ na ca asau   ekasmin pakṣe śrutiḥ nibaddha akṣarā hi sā na pramāda pāṭha iti śakyā gaditum tena na etad  pakṣe vijñānam vyāmohāt  pakṣa antaram saṃkrāntam iti  avagamyate tatra duḥśruta svapna ādi vijñāna mūla tvam ta sarva veṣṭanasya iti virodhāt  kalpyate na hi tasya sati virodhe prāmāṇyam abhyupagantavyam iti kiṃcid  asti pramāṇam tasmāt  yathā eva ekasmin pakṣe na śakyā śrutiḥ kalpayitum evam aparasmin pakṣe tulya kāraṇa tvāt api ca itaretara āśraye anyatas  paricchedāt  kā iyam itaretara āśraya tā pramāṇāyām smṛtau sparśanam vyāmohaḥ sparśane pramāṇe smṛtiḥ  vyāmohaḥ tad  etad  itaretra āśrayam bhavati tatra sparśanasya kḷptam mūlam kalpyam smṛteḥ saḥ  asau   anyatas  paricchedaḥ kalpya mūla tvāt  smṛti prāmāṇyam anavakḷptam tad  aprāmāṇyāt  sparśanam na vyāmohaḥ tad  avyāmohāt  smārta śruti kalpanā anupapannā pramāṇa abhāvāt  nanu  evam sati vrīhi sādhanatva vijñānasya api  avyāmohāt  yava śrutiḥ  na upapadyeta satyam na upapadyate yadi  apratyakṣā syāt  pratyakṣā tu  eṣā na hi pratyakṣam anupapannam nāma asti dvayoḥ  tu śrutyoḥ  bhāvāt  dve hi  ete vākye tatra ekena kevala yava sādhana tā gamyate ekena kevala vrīhi sādhana tā na ca vākyena avagataḥ  arthaḥ  apahnūyate tasmāt  vrīhi yavayoḥ  upapannaḥ  vikalpaḥ  bṛhat rathantarayoḥ  ca tasmāt  uktam śruti viruddhā smṛtiḥ  apramāṇam iti atas  ca sarva veṣṭana ādi na ādaraṇīyam lobhāt  vāsa āditsamānā audumbarīm kṛtsnām veṣṭitavantaḥ kecid  tad  smṛteḥ  bījam bubhukṣamāṇāḥ kecid  krīta rājakasya bhojanam ācaritavantaḥ apuṃstvam pracchādayanta ś ca aṣṭācatvāriṃśat  varṣāṇi veda brahmacaryam caritavantaḥ tatas  eṣā smṛtiḥ  iti  avagamyate adhikaraṇa antaram vā vaisarjana homīyam vāsaḥ  adhvaryuḥ  gṛhṇāti iti yu upahastinaḥ  dānam ācaranti iti tad kartṛ sāmānyāt pramāṇam iti prāpte apramāṇam smṛtiḥ atra anyan mūlam lobhāt  ācaritavantaḥ kecid  tatas  eṣā smṛtiḥ upapannataram ca etad  vaidika vacana kalpanāt  ācāntena kartavyam yajña upavītinā kartavyam dakṣiṇa ācāreṇa kartavyam iti evaṃlakṣaṇāni  udāharaṇāni kim etāni śruti viruddhāni na kartavyāni uta aviruddhāni kāryāṇi iti iti ced  paśyasi taiḥ  api  anuṣṭhīyamānaiḥ  vaidīkam kiṃcid  na kupyati tasmāt  aviruddhāni iti na etad  evam śāstra paricchinnam hi kramam bādheran katham vedam kṛtvā vedim kurvīta iti imām śrutim uparundhyād antarā vedam vedim ca anuṣṭḥīyamānam ācamana ādi dakṣiṇena ca eka hastena anuṣṭhīyamāneṣu padārtheṣu kadācid  pradhānam sva kālam atikrāmeta ubhābhyām hastābhyām anutiṣṭhan pradhāna kālam saṃbhāvayiṣyati api vā iti pakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ agṛhyamāṇa kāraṇā evaṃjātīyakāḥ pramāṇam nanu krama kālau virundhanti virudhnantu na eṣa doṣaḥ ācamanam padārthaḥ padārthānām ca guṇaḥ kramaḥ na ca guṇa anurodhena padārthaḥ  na kartavyaḥ  bhavati api ca prāptānām padārthānām uttara kālam krama āpatati yadā padārthaḥ prāpnoti tadā krama eva na asti kena saha virodhaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti tathā yadi dakṣiṇena na ācaryate kālaḥ  mā virodhi id iti tatra kāla anurodhena padārthaḥ  na anyathātvam abhyupagacchet  prayoga aṅgam hi kālaḥ padārthānām upakārakaḥ atas  na kāla anurodhena vyathayitavyaḥ padārthaḥ api ca śaucam dakṣiṇa ācāra tā yajña upavīti tvam ca evaṃjātīyakā arthā vyavadhātāraḥ  na bhavanti sarva padārthānām śeṣa bhūta tvāt  tasmāt  ācam ana ādīnām prāmāṇyam yava mayaḥ  caruḥ vārāhī upānahau vaitase kaṭe prājāpatyān saṃcinoti iti yava varāha vetasa śabdān samāmananti tatra kecid  dīrghaśūkeṣu yava śabdam prayuñjante kecid  priyaṅguṣu varāha śabdam kecid  śūkare kecid  kṛṣṇa śakunau vetasa śabdam kecid  vañjulake kecid  jambvām tatra ubhayathā padārtha avagamāt  vikalpaḥ vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati yava śabdaḥ  yadi dīrghaśūkeṣu sādṛśyāt  priyaṅguṣu bhaviṣyati yadi priyaṅguṣu sādṛśyāt  yaveṣu kim sādṛśyam pūrva saśye kṣīṇe bhavanti dīrghaśūkāḥ priyaṅga vaḥ  ca etad  tayoḥ sādṛśyam kaḥ punar  atra niścayaḥ ya śāstra sthānām sa śabda arthaḥ ke śāstra sthāḥ śiṣṭāḥ teṣām avicchinnā smṛtiḥ śabdeṣu vedeṣu ca tena śiṣṭā nimittam śruti smṛti avadhāraṇe te hi  evam samāmananti yava mayeṣu karambha pātreṣu vihiteṣu vākya śeṣam yatra anyā oṣadhayaḥ  mlāyante atha ete modamānā iva uttiṣṭhanti iti dīrghaśūkān yavān darśayati vedaḥ vede darśanāt  avicchinna pāramparyaḥ  dīrghaśūkeṣu yava śabda iti gamyate tasmāt  priyaṅguṣu gauṇaḥ tasmāt  dīrghaśūkānām puroḍāśaḥ kartavyaḥ tasmāt  varāham gāvaḥ  anudhāvanti iti śūkare varāha śabdam darśayati apsujaḥ  vetasa iti vañjule vetasa śabdam śūkaram hi gāvaḥ  anudhāvanti vañjulaḥ  apsu jāyate jambū vṛkṣa sthale giri nadīṣu vā atha yān  chabdān āryā na kasmiṃścid  arthe ācaranti mleccha as tu kasmiṃścid  prayuñjate yathā pikanema sata ta āmarasa ādi śabdāḥ teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim nigama nirukta vyākaraṇa vaśena dhātutaḥ arthaḥ kalpayitavya uta yatra mlecchā ācaranti sa śabda artha iti śiṣṭa ācārasya prāmāṇyam uktam na āśiṣṭa smṛteḥ tasmāt  nigama ādi vaśena artha kalpanā nigama ādīnām ca evam arthavat tā bhaviṣyati anabhiyogaḥ  ca śabda artheṣu  aśiṣṭānām abhiyogaḥ  ca itareṣām tasmāt  dhātutaḥ arthaḥ kalpayitavya iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ coditam aśiṣṭaiḥ  api śiṣṭa an avagatam pratīyeta yad  pramāṇena aviruddham tad  avagamyamānam na nyāyyam tyaktum yad  tu śiṣṭa ācāraḥ pramāṇam iti tad  pratyakṣān avagate arthe yad  tu  abhiyuktāḥ śabda artheṣu śiṣṭā iti tatra ucyate abhiyuktatarāḥ pakṣiṇām poṣaṇe bandhane ca mlecchāḥ yad  tu nigama nirukta vyākaraṇānām arthavat tā iti tatra eṣām arthavat tā bhaviṣyati na yatra mlecchaiḥ  api  avagataḥ śabda arthaḥ api ca nigama ādibhiḥ  arthe kalpayamāne avyavasthitaḥ śabda arthaḥ  bhavet  tatra aniścayaḥ syāt  tasmāt  pika iti kokilaḥ  grāhyaḥ nema u ardham tāmarasam padmam sata iti dāru mayam pātram parimaṇḍalam śata chidram iha kalpasūtrāṇi  udāharaṇam māśakam hāstikam kauṇḍinyakam iti evaṃlakṣaṇakāni kim pramāṇam apramāṇam vā iti saṃdigdhāni kim prāptam prayogasya śāstram pramāṇam evaṃjātīyakam iti brūmaḥ satya vācām etāni vacanāni katham avagamyate vaidikaiḥ  eṣām saṃvādaḥ  bhavati ya eva hi vede grahāḥ ta eva iha yā eva vede iṣṭakāḥ tā eva iha tasmāt  satya vāca ācāryāḥ ācārya vacaḥ pramāṇam iti ca śrutiḥ pratyakṣataḥ prāmāṇyam anavagatam iti yadi  ucyeta pramāṇa antareṇa vacanena avagatam iti na doṣaḥ veda vākyaiḥ  ca eṣām tulya ādaraḥ tasmāt  pramāṇam na etad  evam asat niyamāt  na etad  samyak nibandhanam svara abhāvāt ṛtvijaḥ  vṛṇīte vṛtā yajanti deva yajanam adhyavasyanti iti na atra vidhiḥ  gamyate vartamāna kāla pratyaya nirdeśāt na ca atra vākya śeṣaḥ stāvakaḥ  asti tasmāt  apramāṇam yaḥ  ca ādara uktaḥ sa na antarīyaka tvāt  veda vākya miśra samāmnānāt  yad  tu śrutiḥ  iti na etad  arthavāda tvāt  katham artha vādaḥ vidhi antaram hi  asti āgneyaḥ  aṣṭākapāla iti atra ācāryaḥ  vedaḥ  abhipretaḥ ācinoti  asya buddhim iti yad  vā ācārya vacanam pramāṇam tad apekṣam katara tad yad  pramāṇa gamyam yad  ca uktam satya vācām etāni vacanāni iti tad  na ācārya vacanam hi bhavati pūrva pakṣe sarvāsu tithiṣu  amāvāsyā iti saṃnihitam ca śāstram paurṇamāsyām paurṇamāsyā yajeta amāvāsyāyām amāvasyayā yajet  iti tena śruti viruddha vacanān na satya vācaḥ tasmāt  apramāṇam anumānāt  smṛteḥ  ācārāṇām ca prāmāṇyam iṣyate yena eva hetunā te pramāṇam tena eva vyavasthitāḥ prāmāṇyam arhanti tasmāt  holāka ādayaḥ prācyaiḥ  eva kartavyāḥ āhnī naibukādayaḥ  dākṣiṇātyaiḥ  eva udvṛṣabha yajñādaya udīcyaiḥ  eva yathā śikhā kalpaḥ  vyavatiṣṭhate kecid  tri śikhāḥ kecid  pañcaśikhā iti api vā iti pakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ evaṃjātīyakaḥ sarva dharmaḥ syāt  kutas  tad nyāya tvāt  vidhānasya vidhīyate anena iti vidhānam śabdaḥ saḥ  anumīyate smṛtyāḥ na ca tasya ākṛti vacana tā nyāyyā na ca vyakti vacana tā na sarveṣām anuṣṭhātṝṇām yad  ekam sāmānyam tasya vācakaḥ kaścid  śabdaḥ  asti yaḥ  anumīyeta tasmāt  sarva dharmatā vidheḥ  nyāyyā kutas  padārthāḥ kartavyā iti pramāṇam asti vyavasthāyām tu na kiñcid  pramāṇam asti atha yad  uktam yathā śikhā kalpaḥ  vyavatiṣṭhata iti gotra vyavasthayā śikhā kalpa vyavasthāyām darśanam spaṣṭam idam padebhyaḥ kebhyaścid uttaram sūtram kāni tāni padāni atha kim artham na liṅgāt  vyavasthā yathā śuklaḥ  hotā iti na asti tad  nityam eṣām liṅgam yad  yathādarśanam anuvartate ye api śyāmā bṛhantaḥ  lohita akṣāḥ te api na sarva ārhnī naibuka ādīn kurvate anevaṃliṅgā api ca anutiṣṭhanti tasmāt  na vyavasthā śuklaḥ  hotā iti pratyakṣā śrutiḥ atha kasmān na samākhyayā niyamaḥ ye dākṣiṇātyā iti samākhyātāḥ ta āhnī naibuka ādīn kariṣyanti ya udīcyā iti samākhyātāḥ ta udvṛṣabha yajña ādīn ye prācyā iti te holāka ādīn yathā rājā rājasūyena iti na etad  evam deśa saṃyogāt  ākhyā bhavati dākṣiṇa deśān nirgataḥ prākṣu vā udakṣu vā avasthita āhnī naibuka ādīn karoti  eva udīcya aḥ  ca deśa antara udvṛṣabha yajña ādīn prācyāś ca holāka ādīn anya deśaḥ  ca deśa antara gataḥ  na niyogataḥ para padārthān karoti tasmāt  na vyavasthā rājā rājasūyena iti tu niyatā jātiḥ iti ced  paśyasi yadi deśa saṃyogāt  ākhyā bhavet  deśa antara sthasya na bhavet  bhavati ca deśa ānatara sthasya māthura iti  asaṃbaddhasya api mathurayā tasmāt  na deśa saṃyogāt  ākhyā deśa saṃyoga nimittāyām api  ākhyāyām deśān nirgatasya tad ākhyā na viruddhā yata eṣā yoga ākhyā yoga mātra apekṣā na bhūta vartamāna bhaviṣyat saṃbandha apekṣā yatas  dṛśyate mathurām abhiprasthitaḥ  māthura iti mathurāyām vasan mathurāyā nirgataś ca yasya tu  atas  anyatamaḥ saṃbandhaḥ  na asti na sa māthuraḥ tasmāt  na samākhyayā vyavasthā atha kasmān na karma aṅgam deśaḥ yaḥ kṛṣṇamṛtikā prāyaḥ sa āhnī naibuka ādīnām yathā prācīna pravaṇe vaiśvadevena yajeta iti yathā kartary avyavasthitam liṅgam śyāma ādi na padārthaiḥ saṃvādam upaiti tadvat  deśa liṅgam avyavasthitam kṛṣṇamṛtikā prāye api  anye na kurvanti tathā anya liṅge api kurvanti tasmāt  na deśataḥ  vyavasthā prācīna pravaṇam tu śrutyā niyatam vaiśvadevasya gauḥ  gāvī goṇī gopotalikā iti evamādayaḥ śabdā udāharaṇam gaḥ śabdaḥ  yathā sāsnādim iti pramāṇam kim tathā gāvyādayaḥ  api  uta na iti saṃdehaḥ kim atra ekaḥ śabdaḥ  avicchinna pāramparyaḥ  artha abhidhāyī itare apabhraṃśāḥ uta sarve anādayaḥ sarva iti brūmaḥ kutas  pratyayāt  pratīyate hi gāvi ādibhyaḥ sāsna ādimān arthaḥ tasmāt  itas  varṣa śate api  asya arthasya saṃbandha āsīt  eva tatas  pareṇa tatas  ca paratareṇa iti  anāditā kartā ca asya saṃbandhasya na asti iti vyavasthitam eva tasmāt  sarve sādhavaḥ sarvaiḥ  bhāṣitavyam sarve hi sādhayanti  artham yathā hastaḥ karaḥ pāṇiḥ  iti arthāya hi  eta uccāryante na adṛṣṭāya na hi  eṣām uccāraṇe śāstram asti tasmāt  na vyavatiṣṭheta kaścid  eka eva sādhuḥ  itare asādhava iti mahatā prayatnena śabdam uccaranti vāyuḥ  nābheḥ  utthitaḥ urasi vistīrṇaḥ kaṇṭhe vivartitaḥ mūrdhānam āhatya parāvṛttaḥ vaktre vicaran vividhān śabdān abhivyanakti tatra aparādhyeta api  uccārayitā yathā śuṣke patiṣyāmi iti kardame patati sakṛt  upasprakṣyāmi iti dvis  upaspṛśati tatas  aparādhāt  pravṛttā gāvyādayaḥ  bhaveyuḥ na niyogataḥ  avicchinna pāramparyā eva iti na ca eṣa nyāyaḥ yad  sadṛśāḥ śabdā ekam artham abhiniviśamānāḥ sarve avichinna pāramparyā eva iti pratyaya mātra darśanāt  abhyupagamyate sādṛśyāt  sādhu śabde api  avagate pratyayaḥ avakalpyate tasmāt  amīṣām ekaḥ  anādiḥ  anye apabhraṃśāḥ hastaḥ karaḥ pāṇiḥ  iti evamādiṣu tu  abhiyukta upadeśāt  anādiḥ  amīṣām arthena saṃbandha iti katham punar  tatra tattvam śakyam vijñātum śakyam iti  āha arthinaḥ  hi  abhiyuktā bhavanti dṛśyate ca abhiyuktānām guṇayatām avismaraṇam upapannam pratyakṣam ca etad  guṇyamānam na bhraśyata iti tasmāt  yam abhiyuktā upadiśanti eṣa eva sādhuḥ  iti  avagantavyaḥ atha yad  uktam arthaḥ  avagamyate gāvi ādibhyaḥ ata eṣām api  anādi arthena saṃbandha iti tad aśaktiḥ  eṣām gamyate gaḥ śabdam uccārayitu kāmena kenacid  aśaktyā gāvī iti  uccāritam apareṇa jñātam sāsna ādimān asya vivakṣitaḥ tad  artham gauḥ  iti  uccārayitu kāmaḥ  gāvī iti  uccārayati tatas  śikṣitvā apare api sāsnādim iti vivakṣite gāvī iti  uccārayanti tena gāvi ādibhyaḥ sāsna ādimān avagamyate anurūpaḥ  hi gāvi ādi gaḥ śabdasya ata eva hi vibhakti vyatyaye api pratyayaḥ bhavati aśmakaiḥ  āgacchāmi iti  aśmaka śabda eka deśa upalabdhe aśmakebhyaḥ  iti  eva śabdaḥ smaryate tatas  aśmakebhyaḥ  iti  eṣaḥ  artha  upalabhyata iti evam gāvi ādi darśanāt  gaḥ śabda smaraṇam tatas  sāsna ādimān avagamyate atha gauḥ  iti evamādayaḥ śabdāḥ kim ākṛteḥ pramāṇam uta vyakteḥ  iti saṃdehaḥ ucyate idam tāvat  parīkṣyatām kim ya eva laukikāḥ śabdāḥ ta eva vaidikā uta anya iti yadā ta eva tadā api kim ta eva eṣām arthāḥ ye loke uta anya iti saṃśayaḥ tatra anye laukikāḥ śabdāḥ anye vaidikā anye ca eṣām arthā iti brūmaḥ kutas  vyapadeśa bhedāt  rūpa bhedāt  ca ime laukikāḥ ime vaidikā iti vyapadeśa bhedaḥ agniḥ  vṛtrāṇi jaṅghana d iti  anyat  idam rūpam laukikāt  agni śabdāt  śabda anya tvāt  ca na ta eva arthāḥ api ca samāmananti uttānā vai deva gavā vahanti iti ye devānām gāvaḥ ta uttānā vahanti iti  ukte gamyata eva ya uttānā vahanti te gaḥ śabdena ucyanta iti tasmāt  anyaḥ  vaidika gaḥ śabdasya arthaḥ tathā devebhyaḥ  vanaspate havīṃṣi hiraṇyaparṇa pradivaḥ te artham iti hiraṇya parṇaḥ  vai devaḥ  vanaspatiḥ  vede etad  vai daivyam madhu yad  ghṛtam iti veda ghṛte madhu śabdaḥ tasmāt  amīṣām anye arthā iti prāpte brūmaḥ ya eva laukikāḥ śabdāḥ ta eva vaidikāḥ ta eva eṣām arthā iti kutas  prayoga codanā bhāvāt evam prayoga codanā saṃbhavati yadi ta eva śabdāḥ ta eva arthāḥ itarathā śabda anya tve arthaḥ  na pratīyeta tasmāt  eka śabda tvam iti ucyate prayojanam idam hetuḥ  vyapadiśyatām iti tatas  hetuḥ  ucyate avibhāgāt  iti na teṣām eṣām ca vibhāgam upalabhāmahe ata eva eka śabda tvam tānś ca tānś ca arthān avagacchāmaḥ atas  na anya tvam ca vadāmaḥ yad  ca uktam ya uttānā vadanti te deva gāvāḥ yad  ghṛtam tad  madhu yaḥ  hiraṇya parṇaḥ sa vanaspatiḥ  iti na asti vacanam yad  uttānānām vahatām gaḥ tvam brūyāt  ye gāvaḥ ta uttānā vahanti iti  evam tad  yadi ca anena vacanena gaḥ tvam vidhīyate uttānā vahanti iti  anuvādaḥ syāt  na ca uttānā vahantaḥ prasiddhāḥ kecid  te niyogataḥ  vidhātavyāḥ teṣu vidhīyamāneṣu na śakyam gaḥ tvam vidhātum bhidyate hi tathā vākyam yadi ca anye vaidikāḥ tatas  uttāna ādīnām arthaḥ  na gamyeta tatra natarām śakyeta avijñāta lakṣaṇam gaḥ tvam vijñātum na ca uttāna vahana vacanam api  anarthakam stuti arthena arthavat  bhaviṣyati iti evam ghṛtasya madhu tvam hiraṇyaparṇa tā ca vanaspateḥ tasmāt  ta eva śabdā arthāś ca yadi laukikāḥ  ta eva arthāḥ tadā saṃdehaḥ kim ākṛtiḥ śabda arthaḥ  atha vyaktiḥ  iti kā punar  ākṛtiḥ kā vyaktiḥ  iti dravya guṇa karmaṇām sāmānya mātram ākṛtiḥ asādhāraṇa viśeṣā vyaktiḥ kutas  saṃśayaḥ gauḥ  iti  ukte sāmānya pratyayāt  vyaktau ca kriyā saṃbandhāt tad  ucyate vyaktiḥ śabda artha iti kutas  prayoga codanā bhāvāt ālambhana prokṣaṇa viśasana ādīnām prayoga codanā ākṛti arthe na saṃbhaveyuḥ yatra uccāraṇa ānarthakyam tatra vyakti arthaḥ atas  anyatra ākṛti vacana iti ced  uktam anyāyaḥ  ca aneka artha tvam iti katham sāmānya avagatiḥ  iti ced  vyakti padārthasya ākṛtiḥ  cihna bhūtāḥ  bhaviṣyati ya evam ākṛtikaḥ sa gauḥ  iti yathā yasya daṇḍaḥ  asti sa daṇḍī iti na ca daṇḍa vacanaḥ  daṇḍi śabdaḥ evam iha api dravya āśrayasya śabdaḥ  dravya śabdaḥ na tatra dravya āśraya vacanaḥ śabdaḥ  bhavet  yadi  ākṛtiḥ śabda arthaḥ  bhavet  ṣaṣ  deyā dvādaśa deyā caturviṃśatiḥ  deyā iti na hi  ākṛtiḥ ṣaṣ ādibhiḥ saṃkhyābhiḥ  yujyate tasmāt  na ākṛti vacanaḥ yadi paśuḥ  upākṛtaḥ palāyeta anyam tad varṇam tad vayasam ālabheta iti yadi  ākṛti vacanaḥ śabdaḥ  bhavet  anyasya ālambhaḥ  na upapadyate anya sva api paśu dravyasya sā eva ākṛtiḥ tasmāt  vyakti vacana iti tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati ākṛti śabda arthaḥ kutas  kriyā artha tvāt śyena citam cinvīta iti vacanam ākṛtau saṃbhavati yadi  ākṛti arthaḥ śyena śabdaḥ vyakti vacane tu na cayanena śyena vyakti r utpādayitum śakyata iti  aśakya artha vacanāt  anarthakaḥ tasmāt  ākṛti vacanaḥ nanu śyena vyaktibhiḥ  cayanam anuṣṭhāsyate na sādhakatamaḥ śyena śabda arthaḥ īpsitatamaḥ  hi  asau śyena śabdena nirdiśyate atas  cayanena śyenaḥ  nivartayitavyaḥ sa ākṛti vacana tve avakalpyate nanu ubhayatra kriyāyāḥ  asaṃbhava eva vyapadiśyate na ākṛtiḥ śabda arthaḥ kutas  kriyā na saṃbhavet  ākṛtau śabda arthe vrīhīn prokṣati iti tathā na vyaktiḥ śabda arthaḥ kriyā eva na saṃbhavet  vyakteḥ śabda artha tve śyena citam cinvīta iti yad  api  ucyate vrīhīn prokṣati iti vyakti lakṣaṇa artha ākṛtiḥ  iti śakyam anyatra api śyena citam cinvīta iti vaditum ākṛti lakṣaṇa arthā vyaktiḥ  iti kim punar  atra jyāyaḥ ākṛtiḥ śabda artha iti yadi vyaktiḥ śabda arthaḥ  bhavet  vyakti antare na prayujyeta atha vyakti antare prayujyate na tarhi vyaktiḥ śabda arthaḥ sarva sāmānya viśeṣa vinirmuktā hi vyaktiḥ  iti  ucyate na eṣa doṣaḥ vyakti antare sarva sāmānya viśeṣa vinirmukta eva pravartiṣyate yadi vyakti antare sarva sāmānya viśeṣa viyukte pravartiṣyate sāmānyam eva tarhi tad  na iti  ucyate yaḥ  hi  arthaḥ sāmānyasya viśeṣāṇām ca āśrayaḥ sā vyaktiḥ vyakti vacanaḥ  ca śabdaḥ  na sāmānye na viśeṣe vartate teṣām tu  āśrayam eva abhidadhāti tena vyakti antare vṛttiḥ  adoṣaḥ na hi tad  sāmānyam yadi vyakti antareṣu  api bhavati sarva sāmānya viśeṣa viyuktāyām aśva vyaktau gaḥ śabdaḥ kim iti na vartate āha yeṣu  eva prayogaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ teṣu vartiṣyate na sarvatra na ca aśva vyaktau gaḥ śabdasya prayogaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt  tatra na vartiṣyate yadi yatra prayogaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ tatra vṛttiḥ adya jātāyām gavi prathama prayogaḥ  na prāpnoti tatra adṛṣṭa tvāt sāmānya pratyayaś ca na prāpnoti iyam api gauḥ  iti iyam api gauḥ  iti iyam vā gauḥ  iti iyam vā gauḥ  iti syāt  bhavati tu sāmānya pratyayaḥ adṛṣṭa pūrvāyām api gaḥ vyaktau tasmāt  na prayoga apekṣaḥ  gaḥ śabdaḥ  vyakti vacana iti śakyata āśrayitum evam tarhi śakteḥ svabhāva eṣaḥ yad  kasyāṃcid  vyaktau vartate kasyāṃcin na yathā agniḥ  uṣṇaḥ udakam śītam evam etad  bhaviṣyati iti na evam sidhyati na hi  etad  gamyate kasyāṃcid  vyaktau vartate kasyāṃcin na iti satyam etad  gaḥ tvam lakṣaṇam bhaviṣyati iti yatra gaḥ tvam tasyām vyaktau   iti evam tarhi viśiṣṭā vyaktiḥ pratīyeta yadi ca viśiṣṭā pūrvataram viśeṣaṇam avagamyeta na hi  apratīte viśeṣaṇe viśiṣṭam kecana pratyetum arhanti iti astu viśeṣaṇa tvena ākṛtim vakṣyati viśeṣya tvena vyaktim na hi  ākṛti padārthakasya vyaktiḥ  na padārthaḥ vyakti padārthakasya vā na ākṛtiḥ ubhayam ubhayasya padārthaḥ kasyacid  kiṃcid  prādhānyena vivakṣitam bhavati tena atra ākṛtiḥ  guṇa bhāvena vyaktiḥ pradhāna bhāvena vivakṣyata iti na etad  evam ubhayoḥ  ucyamānayoḥ  guṇa pradhāna bhāvaḥ syāt  yadi ca atra ākṛtiḥ pratīyate śabdena tadā vyaktiḥ  api padārtha iti na śakyate vaditum kutas  ākṛtiḥ  hi vyaktyā nitya saṃbaddhā saṃbandhinyām ca tasyām avagatāyām saṃbandhi antaram avagamyate tad  etad  ātma pratyakṣam yad  chabda uccarite vyaktiḥ pratīyata iti kim śabdāt  uta ākṛteḥ  iti vibhāgaḥ  na pratyakṣaḥ saḥ  anvaya vyatirekābhyām avagamyate antareṇa api śabdam śabda vyāpāraḥ  asti nanu ca daṇḍī iti na tāvat  daṇḍi śabdena daṇḍaḥ  abhidhīyate atha ca daṇḍa viśiṣṭaḥ  avagamyate evam iha api na tāvat  ākṛtiḥ  abhidhīyate atha ca ākṛti viśiṣṭā vyaktiḥ  gamyeta iti na etad  sādhu ucyate satyam daṇḍi śabdena daṇḍaḥ  na abhidhīyate na tu  apratīte daṇḍe daṇḍi pratyayaḥ asti asti tu daṇḍi śabda eka deśa bhūtaḥ  daṇḍa śabdaḥ yena daṇḍaḥ pratyāyitaḥ tasmāt  sādhv etad  yad  pratīte viśeṣaṇe viśiṣṭaḥ pratīyata iti nanu gaḥ śabda avayavaḥ kaścid  ākṛteḥ pratyāyakaḥ anyaḥ  vyakteḥ yata ucyate tatas  ākṛtiḥ  avagatā na gaḥ śabda ākṛti vacana iti na ca yathā daṇḍi āghārayati iti prasiddhiḥ  evam anugrahīṣyate guṇa vidhiḥ  ca darvi home āghāraḥ  ca upāṃśu yāje tatra etayoḥ  arthavat tā pravṛtti viśeṣa kara tvam ca na ca guṇa vidhi pakṣe lakṣaṇā bhavati yathā udbhidā yajeta iti agnihotre samāsena avagatam guṇa vidhānam āghāre api āghāram nirvartayati iti śrutyā eva guṇa u vidhīyate tasmāt  guṇa vidhī iti  evam prāpte brūma h tad prakhyam ca anya śāstram yau guṇau   etābhyām vidhīyeta iti  āśaṅkyate tau   anyata eva avagatau yad  agnaye ca prajāpataye ca sāyam juhoti iti devatā vidhānam caturgṛhītam vā etad  abhūt  tasya ādhāram ādhāryā iti  ādhāre ca dravya vidhiḥ avidita vedanam ca vidhiḥ  iti  ucyate viditam ca atra anyatas  guṇa vidhānam tasmāt  na guṇa vidhī karma nāmadheye tu saṃbhavataḥ yasmin   agnaye hotram homaḥ  bhavati tad  agnihotram dīrgha dhārā kṣaraṇa kriyā prasiddha eva āghāraḥ tasmāt  karma nāmadheye prasiddhi ādayaḥ  ca ukta uttarāḥ prajāpati nivṛtti artham agni vidhānam bhaviṣyati iti ced  na etad  evam agnim hi  eṣa vidhātum śaknoti na parjāpatim pratiṣeddhum pratiṣidhyamānasya ca prajāpateḥ  vidhānam anarthakam syāt  prajāpatiḥ  devatā iti gamyate gamyamānam ca na śakyam mithyā iti kalpayitum atas  ayam asamādhiḥ ucyate āghāram āghārayati iti dravya parā codanā yaiḥ  tu dravyam cikīrṣyata iti dravyam hi  anayā kriyayā kṣāryate kṣāritam ca yāgam sādhayati tad  kasya pradhānasya karmaṇaḥ  nāmadheyam iti ucyate etad  eva āghāraṇam pradhāna karma nanu  asya dravya deva taṇ na asti asti iti brūmaḥ tasya āghāram āghārya iti  ājyam dravyam māntra varṇikī devatā indra ūrdhva uddhara iti  āghāram āghārayati iti mantraḥ  hi  abhidadhat  karma tad sādhanam vā karmaṇi samavaiti eṣa ca mantra indram abhidhātum śaknoti sa yadi indras tad sādhanam bhavet  evam anena mantreṇa āghāraḥ śakyate kartum tasmāt  indraḥ  devatā dravya devatā saṃyuktam āghāraṇam tasmāt  yajatiḥ tasya yajateḥ  nāmadheyam iti atha eṣa śyenena abhicaran yajeta atha eṣa saṃdaṃśena abhicaran yajeta atha eṣa gavā abhicaran yajeta iti samāmnāyante tatra guṇa vidhiḥ karma nāmadheyam iti saṃdehaḥ prasiddhi ādibhiḥ pūrva pakṣaḥ udbhida ādīnām iva te tu udbhida ādayaḥ kriyā nimittāḥ śaknuvanti yāgam vaditum ime punar  jāti nimittā na śaknuvanti tena guṇa vidhaya iti  evam prāptam evam prāpte brūmaḥ tad vyapadeśam ca tena śyena ādīnā prasiddhena yasya vyapadeśaḥ tad  ca karma nāmadheyam śrutiḥ  hi nāmadheya tve lakṣaṇā guṇa vidhau yad  tu jāti śabdāḥ ime na yāgam abhivadanti iti sādṛśya vyapadeśāt  abhivadiṣyanti evam hi vyapadeśaḥ  bhavati yathā vai śyenaḥ  nipatya ādatte evam ayam dviṣantam bhrātṛvyam nipatya ādatte yam abhicaranti śyenena iti nipatya ādatta iti  anena sādṛśyena śyena śabdaḥ  yāge yathā siṃhaḥ  devadatta iti tasmāt  karma nāmadheyam saṃdaṃśe saṃdaṃśena yathā durādānam ādatta iti gavi yathā gāvaḥ  gopāyanti iti tasmāt  saṃdaṃśa śabdaḥ  api karma nāmadheyam gaḥ śabdaḥ  api vājapeyena svārājya kāmaḥ  yajeta iti śrūyate tatra kim guṇa vidhiḥ karma nāmadheyam iti saṃdehaḥ evam ced  saṃdehaḥ dṛśyate guṇa vidhiḥ na saṃdehaḥ śrūyate hi guṇaḥ saḥ  avagamyamānaḥ  na śakyaḥ  na asti iti vaditum tasmāt  guṇa vidhiḥ na etad  evam tulye hi ime kriye syātām yā ca vājypeya kriyā yā ca darśa purṇamāsa kriyā ubhayatra dārśa paurṇamāsikaḥ  vidhyantaḥ syāt  tathā ca dīkṣāṇām upasadām ca darśanam na avakalpyeta saptadaśa dīkṣaḥ  vājapeya iti saptadaśa upasatkaḥ  vājapeya iti atha vā tulya tvāt  kriyayoḥ  na iti yadi na guṇa vidhiḥ tatas  tulyā eṣā vājapeya kriyā jyotiṣṭoma kriyayā tatra dīkṣāṇā m upasadām ca darśanam upapannam tasmāt  karma nāmadheyam iti liṅgam tu  etad  prāptiḥ punar  uttara sūtreṇa yadi guṇa vidhiḥ syāt  sva arthavat  para arthavat  ca abhidhānam vipratiṣidhyeta yajeta iti  asya śabdasya yadi svārājya kāmaḥ  yajeta iti svārājya kāmasya yāgam vidhātum sva artham ucyate na tarhi vājapeyena guṇena saṃbaddhum para artham anūdyeta yāgena vājapeya guṇakena iti bhidyeta hi tathā vākyam nanu dve eva ete vākye pratyakṣam upalabhāmahe svārājya kāmaḥ  yajeta iti  etad  ekam pratyakṣam pada dvayam yajeta vājapeyena iti  etad  api pratyakṣam eva na etad  evam evam sati catvāri padāni  upalabhemahi trīṇi ca etāni  upalabhyante ucyate yajeta iti  etad  ubhābhyām saṃbhantsyate katham sakṛt  uccāritam saṃbandham ubhābhyām eṣyati iti rūpa abhedāt  īdṛśam eva asya rūpam svārājya kāmena saṃbadhyamānasya īdṛśam eva vājapeyena atas tantreṇa ubhābhyām saṃbhantsyata iti na etad  asti īdṛśena eva rūpeṇa iti yadi  ajñātaḥ tatas  vidhiḥ yadi jñātaḥ tatas  anuvādaḥ na ca jñātaḥ  ajñāta ś ca yugapad  saṃbhavati iti āha yad  idam uktam guṇa vidhi pakṣe anuvādaḥ  yajeta iti yadi  ayam anuvādaḥ kena idānīm guṇa u vidhīyate vājapeya śabdena iti mā vocaḥ na hi  ākhyātam antareṇa kṛtyam vā nāma śabda arthasya vyāpāraḥ  vidhīyate yaḥ  ca atra ākhyāta śabdaḥ  yajeta iti saḥ  anuvāda iti  uktam kena idānīm tasya vyāpāraḥ  vidhīyate atas  svārājya kāmam guṇam ca prati yajeta iti vidhiḥ tasmāt  ubhābhyām saṃbadhyata iti yadi  ubhayatra vidhiḥ vājapeyaḥ  na svārājya kāmasya yāgena saṃbadhyeta dve hi  ete tadā vākye na svārājya kāmasya yāgena saha guṇa vidheḥ  eka vākyatā prakaraṇāt  saṃbandhaḥ svārājya kāmasya yāgena iti ced  na vākyena yāga mātre vidhānāt  astu yāga mātreṇa saṃbandha iti ced  na svārājya kāmasya yāgena saha eka vākyatāyāḥ  gamyamāna tvāt  tad  evam prakaraṇasya vākyasya ca bādhaḥ  yujyate yadi karma nāmadheyam guṇa vidhi pakṣe hi sarva ime vākya bhedāt ayaḥ  doṣāḥ prādurbhaveyuḥ tasmāt  karma nāmadheyam vājapeya śabda iti siddham yad  āgneyaḥ  aṣṭākapālaḥ  amāvāsyāyām paurṇamāsyām ca acyutaḥ  bhavati iti evamādayaḥ śrūyante tatra saṃdehaḥ kim āgneyaḥ  agnīṣomīya iti evamādayaḥ  guṇa vidhayaḥ karma nāmadheyāni iti kim tāvat  prāptam guṇa vidhau sati  anekaḥ  guṇa u vidhīyeta agni puroḍāśa aṣṭākapālā iti tasmāt  na guṇa vidhaya iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ tad  ca karmam guṇāḥ  ca asya vidhīyeran avibhaktā hi te karmaṇaḥ  vidhāna arthe tad  dhita ante śabde tatra hi  aṣṭākapālasya āgneya tā vidhīyate sa eṣa evam āgneyaḥ  bhavati yadi  agnaye saṃkalpya dīyate tena ayam anena prakāreṇa yāgaḥ  vihitaḥ  bhavati sa evam vidhīyamānaḥ  na śakyaḥ  agnim aṣṭākapālam ca avidhāya vidhātum saṃbandhaḥ  hi vidhīyamānaḥ  na śakyate saṃbandhinā av avidhāya vihita iti vaktum tasmāt  guṇa vidhayaḥ aṣṭasu kapāleṣu saṃskriyamāṇaḥ  vrīhimayaḥ  yavamayaḥ  vā puroḍāśa eva bhavati saḥ  anuvādaḥ siddhaḥ  ca atra aṣṭākapāla ucyate kapāleṣu śrayayati iti vaca nād na anyena śrapitam gṛhṇanti tena asmin pakṣe na vākya bhedaḥ  bhavati na ced  anyena śiṣṭāḥ yatra punar  anyena vacanena śiṣṭā guṇā bhavanti bhavati tatra nāmadheyam yathā agni hotram juhoti iti barhi rājyayoḥ puroḍāśe ca saṃdehaḥ kim ete saṃskāra śabdā uta jāti śabdā iti saṃskāra śabdā iti brūmaḥ saṃskṛteṣu tṛṇeṣu barhiḥ śabdam upacaranti sarvatra na asaṃskṛteṣu saṃskṛte ca ghṛte ājya śabdam tathā saṃskṛte piṣṭe puroḍāśa śabdam nanu  asaṃskṛte api kasmiṃścid  deśa upacaryate yathā barhis  ādāya gāvaḥ  gatā iti bhavanti vaktāraḥ tathā ājyam krayam iti puroḍāśena me mātā prahelakam dadāti iti sādṛśyāt  teṣu prayogaḥ yathā upaśaye yūpa śabdaḥ kuta etad  yata eka deśe hi śabda prayogaḥ tasmāt  saṃskāra śabdā iti  evam prāptam evam prāpte brūmaḥ barhiḥ ādiṣu  asaṃskṛteṣu  api śabda lābhān na saṃskāra śabdāḥ nanu uktam sādṛśyāt  eka deśe bhaviṣyanti tad  na prasiddhe hi saṃskāra śabda tve sādṛśyāt  iti śakyate vaktum tad  ca aprasiddham katham barhiḥ ādi śabdaiḥ  uddiśya saṃskārā vidhīyante tena satsu śabdeṣu saṃskāraiḥ  bhavitavyam sati ca saṃskāre śabda lābha iti itaretara āśrayam bhavati na ca avihitāḥ saṃskārā bhavanti yān ālocya lokaḥ prayuñjīta tasmāt  na lokāḥ saṃskṛteṣu barhiḥ ādīn prayuñjate tatas  eka deśe api jāti nimittā dṛṣṭāḥ sarvatra jāti nimittā bhavitum arhanti na ca alaukikānām satām vedāt  eva pūrva uttara pada saṃbandham anapekṣya śakyate arthaḥ  adhyavasātum pūrva uttara pade anarthake mā bhūtām iti  evam sa parikalpyeta aśakya s tu  anavagamyamānaḥ parikalpayitum arthavatī ca te pade pūrva uttare laukikena asaṃskṛta prayogeṇa bhaviṣyataḥ tasmāt  jāti śabdā evaṃjātīyakāḥ prayojanam barhiṣā yūpāvaṭam avastṛṇāti iti saṃskṛtaiḥ  eva staritavyam yadi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ viparītam siddhānte prokṣaṇīḥ  āsādaya iti śrūyate tatra prokṣaṇī śabdam prati saṃdehaḥ kim saṃskāra nimitta uta jāti nimitta uta yaugika iti tatra saṃskāreṣu satsu darśanāt  saṃskāra śabda tāyām avagamyamānāyām asaṃskṛte śabda lābhāj jāti śabdaḥ asaṃskṛtāsv eva apsu prokṣaṇībhiḥ  udvejitāḥ sma iti kasmiṃścid  deśe bhavanti vaktāraḥ tena jāti śabda iti prāpte yaugika iti  ucyate kutas  artha saṃyogāt  prokṣaṇya iti  upasarga dhātu pratyaya samudāyasya jāti nimitta tā prayogāt  anumīyate secana saṃyogāt  tu upasarga dhātu karaṇa pratyaya sahitaḥ  apsu pravatata iti prasiddhiḥ  anugṛhītā bhaviṣyati yadā anyat  api secanam prokṣaṇa śabdena ucyate tadā tad saṃyogāt  eva apsu bhaviṣyati iti na samudāya arthaḥ kalpayitum śakyate tasmāt  yaugikaḥ prayojanam ghṛtam prokṣaṇam bhavati iti yadi saṃskāra śabdāḥ prokṣaṇīḥ āsādayā iti praiṣaḥ yadi jāti śabdaḥ ghṛtam āsādaya iti yadi yaugikaḥ prokṣaṇam iti nirmanthyena iṣṭakāḥ pacanti iti saṃskṛte darśanāt  saṃskāra śabdaḥ  nirmanthya iti asaṃskāre api dṛśyate nirmanthyamānayāda enam pakṣyāma iti nirmanthana yogāt  pūrvavat  yaugika iti saṃsthitam prayojanam saṃskāra nimitte saṃskṛtena iṣṭakāḥ paktavyāḥ jāti śabde yathā upapannena yaugike acira nirmathite yathā na avanītena bhuṅkta iti  acira nirdagdhena iti gamyate cāturmāsyeṣu prathame parvaṇi vaiśvadeve saṃdehaḥ vaiśvadevena yajeta iti kim vaiśvadeva śabdaḥ  guṇa vidhiḥ  uta karma nāmadheyam iti yadi saṃdehaḥ  na saṃdehaḥ vaiśvadeve vikalpaḥ guṇa vidhiḥ  vaiśvadeva śabdaḥ gamyate hi guṇa vidhānam viśvedevā vidhīyanta āgneya ādiṣu yāgeṣu tatra agni ādīnām viśvaiḥ  devaiḥ  vikalpaḥ evam prasiddhiḥ  arthavatī bhaviṣyati na etad  evam pratyakṣa śruti vihitā agni ādayaḥ  teṣām yāgānām viśvedevā vākyena prakaraṇāt  tena eva na anyena iti gamyate na ca ayam viṣama śiṣṭhaḥ  vikalpaḥ  bhavitum arhati na hi prakaraṇam śrutasya dravyasya bādhane samartham tasmāt  karma nāmadheyam atha ucyate vaiśvadeva iti  anena śabdena pratyakṣam agni ādi guṇa viśiṣṭaḥ  yāga guṇa u lakṣyate vaiśvadevī hi tatra āmikṣā samavaiti yadi vaiśvadeva śabdena yāga guṇa u lakṣyate na tarhi viśvedevā vidhīyante katham sakṛt  uccaritaḥ  vaiśvadeva śabdaḥ  yāga guṇam lakṣayiṣyati viśvāṃ   ca devān vidhāsyati iti na ayam vaiśvadeva śabdasya viśvaiḥ  devaiḥ  mithas  saṃbandhaḥ  ghaṭate tasmāt  karma nāmadheyam eva guṇa vidhiḥ  iti parārthāḥ  ca guṇāḥ te na śaknuvanti pradhānam āvartayitum tena sakṛt  yāga kartavyaḥ  na guṇa anurodhena āvartitum arhati saṃpratipanna devata tvāt  ca na virodhaḥ tatra ekasyām pradhāna āhutau triṃśat āhutayaḥ  hūyanta iti triṃśat saṃkhyā saṃpattiḥ  āhavanīya āhutīnām na avakalpate tasmāt  karma nāmadheyam iti siddham vaiśvānaram dvādaśa kapālam nirvapet  putre jāta iti śrūyate tatra yad aṣṭākapālaḥ  bhavati gāyatryā eva enam brahmavarcasena punāti iti evamādayaḥ kapāla vikalpāḥ śrūyante teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim aṣṭa tvādayaḥ  guṇa vidhaya uta artha vādā iti tatra guṇa vidhaya iti  evam brūmaḥ katham ye hi pūrvavantaḥ   vidita pūrvam artha m abhivadanti  te avidhāna arthāḥ tad  etad  asya vākyasya samāmnāye sāmarthyam yad avihita pūrvaka abhidhānam kim tad  vidhāna sāmarthyam evam avihitam artham vidhāsyati itaratha artha vādāḥ santaḥ  anarthakāḥ syuḥ na ca dvadaśa kapālasya śeṣa bhāvam upagantum arhati pratyakṣā hi  aṣṭānām kapālānām stutiḥ parokṣā dvādaśānām pratyakṣa abhāve ca parokṣā syāt  tasmāt  guṇa vidhayaḥ na etad  asti guṇa vidhaya iti guṇasya vidhāna arthā ete santaḥ puroḍāśasya kapāleṣu saṃkhyā vidadhyuḥ na śaknuvanti yāga prayogasya vidhātum dvādaśa kapāla tā hi yāgasya vākyena aṣṭākapāla ādayaḥ prakareṇa tena te yāge na bhaviṣyanti api ca aṣṭatva ādayaḥ puroḍāśena eka vākya bhūtāḥ prakaraṇam bādhitvā na yāgasya bhaviṣyanti yāga asaṃbandhe ca anarthakāḥ puroḍāśa saṃbandhe phala abhāvāt arthavāda tvena tu vaiśvānara yāgasya stutiḥ  upapadyate tasmāt  artha vādā iti iti yad  uktam tad  parihartavyam iti  ābhāṣā antam sūtram yadā tu  aṣṭākapāla ādi prarocana arthā anarthakā iti  avagatam tadā lakṣaṇayā dvādaśa kapālasya stutiḥ  vaiśvānara yāga prarocana arthā bhaviṣyati santi hi dvādaśa saṃkhyāyām aṣṭatva ādayaḥ saṃkhyā viśeṣā avibhaktāḥ atas  dvādaśa kapālasya stuti artha tvena avayava stutiḥ  upapadyate yathā śobhanam asya cakrasya nemi tumbāram śobhanam asyāḥ senāyāḥ  hasti aśva ratha pādātam iti tasmāt  upapannā stutiḥ  iti iti ced  bhavān paśyati  artha vādā iti kāraṇam aṣṭatva ādīnām brahmavarcasa ādi kasmān na bhavati brahmavarcasa kāmasya aṣṭākapālaḥ evam uttareṣu yathākāmam kim evam bhaviṣyati puroḍāśasya guṇa vidhāne api  ānarthakyam na bhaviṣyati na ca lakṣaṇayā dvādaśa kapālasya stutiḥ kalpitā bhaviṣyati tasmāt  kāmebhyaḥ  vidhayaḥ  baviṣyanti yadi kāmāya vidhayaḥ bhinnāni vākyāni bhaveyuḥ ekam ca idam vākyam vaiśvānaram dvādaśa kapālam nirvapet  putre jāta iti  edam apakrāntam yad  dvādaśa kapālaḥ  bhavati jagatyā eva asmin paśūn dadhāti yasmin  jāta etām iṣṭim nirvapati pūta eva sa tejasv yad  nāda indriyāvī paśumān bhavati iti  evam antam tasya madhye aṣṭatva ādayaḥ śrūyamāṇā yadi na saṃbadhyeran   tatas  vākya antarāṇi bhaveyuḥ kartuḥ  hi kāraṇāni pūtatva ādīni bhaveyuḥ sa eṣa guṇa arthaḥ  atra vidhīyate vaiśvānara yāge pūta eva iti evamādiḥ tena ca ete aṣṭatva ādayaḥ sākṣāt  dhetu tvena saṃbadhyante yasmāt  gāyatryā eva enam brahmavarcasena punāti tena pūta eva saḥ yasmāt  trivṛtā eva asmin   tejaḥ  dadhāti tena tejasvī yasmāt  virājā eva asmin   annādyam dadhāti tena anna ādaḥ yasmāt  triṣṭubhā eva asmin   indriyam dadhāti tena indriyāvī yasmāj jagati  aiva asmin paśūna dadhāti tena paśumān iti tatas  kāmāya vidhayaḥ  asaṃbhavantaḥ  yadi  artha vādā api na bhaveyuḥ  ānarthakyam eva eṣām syāt  tasmāt  akāraṇam brahma varcaḥ tvāt  yaḥ  aṣṭatva ādīnām tasmāt  aṣṭa tvādayaḥ  artha vādā iti yajamānaḥ prastaraḥ yajamāna eka kapāla ityādi samāmnāyate tatra saṃdehaḥ kim yajamānaḥ prastara iti  eṣa guṇa vidhiḥ kim arthavāda iti tathā yajamāna eka kapāla iti kim tāvat  prāptam guṇa vidhiḥ  iti kim evam bhaviṣyati evam apūrvam artham vidhāsyati itaratha artha vādaḥ  anarthakaḥ syāt  arthavat tvam ca nyāyyam tasmāt  vidhiḥ na etad  evam yadi vidhiḥ syāt  tatas  prastara kārye yajamānaḥ  niyamyeta yajamāna kārye vā prastaraḥ prastare juhūm āsādayati sarvā vā sruva iti yajamāne juhūr āsādyeta sarvā vā sruva iti tathā asati na yājamānam śakyate kartum dīkṣaṇataḥ  brahma yajamānau   āsāte karmaṇa kriyamāṇasya iti na ca prastaraḥ  yājamānam śaknoti kartum tathā yadi yajamāna eka kapāla kārye viniyujyeta sarva hutaḥ kriyeta tatra sarva tantra parilopaḥ syāt  na ca eka kapālaḥ  yājamānam śaknoti kartum tasmāt  na vidhiḥ vidhi antaram ca asti prastaram uttaram barhiṣaḥ sādayati eka kapālam sarva hatam karoti iti tasmāt  api na vidhiḥ kim hi artha vādaḥ yajamānaḥ  jñāyata eva prastara eka kapāla iti ca katham punar  anayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam jñāyate na hi prastara eka kapālaḥ  vā yajamānaḥ na ca yajamāna ekasmin kapāle saṃskṛtaḥ puroḍāśaḥ prathamaḥ  vā kaśam ṣṭiḥ  lūnaḥ katham para śabdaḥ paratra vartate kim artham vā jñāyamānasva saṃkīrtanam iti ucyate jñāyamānaḥ saṃkīrtyate stotum prastara uttaraḥ  barhiṣaḥ sādayitavyaḥ  yajamāna tvāt  tathā yajamāna eka kapālaḥ sarva hutaḥ kartavyaḥ svarga āhavanīya s tatra pratiṣṭhāpitaḥ  bhavati iti katham paratra vartate para śabda iti guṇavādas tu guṇāt  eṣa vādaḥ katham aguṇa vacanaḥ  guṇam brūyāt  sva artha abhidhānanā iti brūmaḥ sarva eva ete gauṇāḥ śabdā na sva artham hitvā guṇeṣu vartante prasiddha hāniḥ  hi tathā syāt  aprasiddha kalpanā ca na ca sarve guṇa samudāya vacanāḥ guṇa hīne api darśanāt  aprasahya kāry api hi kadācid  rogeṇa upahataḥ siṃhyāḥ putraḥ siṃha eva samudāya vācī ca na avayave pravartitum arhati sarva siṃha vyāktiṣu yad  sāmānyam tad  vacanaḥ śabda iti sthitaḥ  nyāyaḥ pratyuddhriyeta na ca asati siṃhaḥ  parikalpanayā pravarteta kalpanāyāḥ  aśakya tvāt  katham nu sva artha abhidhānena pratyaya vyavasthā iti ced  artha saṃbandhāt  siṃha iti nirjñāyate prasahya kāri tā tatra prāyeṇa iti prasahya kārī iti gamyate artham pratyaya sāmarthyāt  yaḥ  hi manyate prasahya kāriṇam pratyāyayeyam iti sa yadi siṃha śabdam uccārayati sidhyati  asya abhipretam siṃha arthaḥ pratītaḥ prasahya kāri iti saṃbandhāt  itaram artham pratyāyayati evam sva artha abhidhānena tad guṇa saṃbandhaḥ pratīyate iha tu yajamānaḥ prastaraḥ yajamāna eka kapāla iti kīdṛśaḥ  guṇa saṃbandhaḥ pratīyate tad siddhi kara iti sarvaḥ  hi  ātmanah kārya siddhim karoti anyaḥ  api yaḥ  tasya kārya siddhim karoti sa tasmin   uccarite hṛdayam āgacchati yathā rājā patti gaṇaka iti patti gaṇa kaḥ  rājñaḥ kāryam sādhayati sa rāja śabda uccarite pratīyate evam iha api yajamāna kāryam prastara eka kapālau sādhayataḥ tau yajamāne pratīte pratīyete tasmāt  tau yajamāna śabdena pratyāyete katham stutau syātām barhiṣa upari sādane sarva home ca iti tasmāt  evaṃjātīyakā artha vādā na vidhaya iti āgneyaḥ  vai brāhmaṇaḥ aindraḥ  rājanyaḥ vaiśyaḥ  vaiśvadeva iti evamādayaḥ śrūyante tatra guṇa vidhayaḥ ārthavādā iti saṃdehaḥ guṇa vidhaya iti brūmaḥ evam apūrvam artham vidhāsyanti itaratha artha vādāḥ santaḥ  anarthakāḥ syuḥ na vidhiḥ  vidhi antarasya bhāvāt  tasmāt  saṃvādaḥ tasya saṃkīrtanam vidhistuti artham anāgneya ādiṣu  āgneya ādi śabdāḥ kena prakāreṇa guṇa vādena kaḥ  guṇa vādaḥ agni saṃbandhaḥ katham eka jātīyaka tvāt  kim eka jātīyaka tvam prajāpatiḥ  akāmayata prajāḥ sṛjeyam iti sa mukhatas trivṛtam nirabhimīta tam agniḥ  devatā an vasṛjyata gāyatrī chandaḥ rathantaram sāma brāhmaṇaḥ  manuṣyāṇām ajaḥ paśūnām tasmāt  te mukhyāḥ mukhataḥ hi  asṛjyanta urasaḥ  bāhubhyām pañcadaśam nirmimīta tam indraḥ  devatān asṛjyata triṣṭubh  chandaḥ bṛhat  sāma rājanyaḥ  manuṣyāṇām aviḥ paśūnām tasmāt  te vīryavantaḥ vīrya āt  dhi asṛjyanta ūrubhyām madhyatas  saptadaśam niramimīta tam viśvedevā devatā anvasṛjyanta jagatī chandaḥ vairūpam sāma vaiśyaḥ  manuṣyāṇām gāvaḥ paśūnām evam ukte sati  ekasmin   evaṃjātīyake vijñāte anyaḥ  api tad jātīyakaḥ  hṛdayam āgacchati tasmāt  arthavāda śabdāḥ yajamānaḥ  yūpaḥ āditye yūpa ityādi śrūyate tatra guṇa vidhiḥ artha vādaḥ iti saṃdehaḥ arthavat tvāt  guṇa vidhi aśakya tvāt  yūpa kārya sādhane yajamānasya yajamāna kārya sādhane vā yūpasya vidhi antara bhāvāt  ca na vidhiḥ vidhistuti artham saṃvādaḥ guṇavādāt  sāmānādhikaraṇyam kaḥ  guṇaḥ sārūpyam kim sārūpyam ūrdhva tā tejasvi tā ca tasmāt  evaṃjātīyakā artha vādāḥ apaśavaḥ  vā anye gaḥ aśvebhyaḥ paśavaḥ  gaḥ aśvāḥ ayajñaḥ  vā eṣa yaḥ  asāmā asatram vā etad  yad  achandomam iti śrūyate tatra vidhi artha vāda saṃdehe arthavat tvāt  vidhaya iti prāpte abhidhīyate yadi vidhayaḥ  bhaveyuḥ gaḥ aśvā eva paśavaḥ syuḥ sāmavān eva yajñaḥ chandomavat  eva satram anyeṣām paśūnām yajñānām satrāṇām ca utpattiḥ  anarthikā syāt  vidhi antaram ca na avakalpeta atas  stuti artham saṃvādaḥ gaḥ aśvān praśaṃsitum anyeṣām paśūnām nindā sāmavataḥ praśaṃsitum asāmnām nindā chandomavanti praśaṃsitum acchan domakāni nidyante yathā yad  aghṛtam abhojanam tad  yad  malinam avāsas tad  iti sṛṣṭīḥ  upadadhāti iti śrūyate tatra guṇa vidhiḥ  arthavāda iti saṃdehe apūrva tvāt  vidhiḥ  iti prāpte ucyate yadi vidhiḥ sṛṣṭi mantrakā upadadhāti iṣṭakā iti  arthaḥ tatra na iṣṭakānām viśeṣaḥ kaścid  āśrīyate evaṃrūpāḥ sṛṣṭi mantrakā na evaṃrūpā iti tatra sarvāsām sṛṣṭi liṅgā mantrāḥ prāpnuyuḥ anyeṣām asaṃyuktānām mantrāṇām ānarthakyam syāt  tasmāt  anuvādaḥ  mantra samāmnānāt  prāptānām upadhāne mantrāṇām sṛṣṭīnām saṃkīrtanam sarjana artha vāda artham api ca vidhi tve lakṣaṇā ekayā stuvata iti  atra yā asṛṣṭayaḥ  tā lakṣayet  nanu  anuvāde api lakṣaṇā na anuvāda pakṣe lakṣaṇāyām doṣaḥ katham tu  asṛṣṭiṣu sṛṣṭiṣu ca sṛṣṭi śabda iti bhūmnā bahavas tatra sṛṣṭi liṅgā mantrāḥ alpaśas  viliṅgā iti prāṇabhṛta upadadhāti ājya anīḥ  upadadhāti iti vidhi tve prāṇa bhṛt  mantra kāsu upadhīyamānāsu viliṅgānām mantrāṇām ānarthakyam tasmāt  anuvādaḥ liṅga samavāyāt para śabdaḥ paratra vartate yathā chatriṇaḥ  gacchanti iti  ekena chatriṇā sarve lakṣyante na ca ayam prāṇabhṛt  chaśabdaḥ sṛṣṭi śabdaḥ  ca jahatsva artham mantra gaṇam lakṣayet  yad  gaṇe ca sṛṣṭi prāṇa bhṛt  chabdau samavetau tau   api parigṛhyete yathā chatri śabdena sva artha lakṣaṇa arthena saḥ  api chatrī gṛhyata iti aktāḥ śarkarā upadadhāti tejaḥ  vai ghṛtam iti śrūyate tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ghṛta taila vasānām anyatamena dravyeṇa añjanīyāḥ śarkarā uta ghṛtena eva iti katham saṃdehaḥ añjana sāmānyena vākyasya upakramaḥ  ghṛtena viśeṣeṇa nigamanam yathā upakramam nigamayitavyam ekasmin vākye tatra yad  vā sāmānyam ādau viśeṣa upalakṣaṇa artham vivakṣyate yad  vā nigamane viśeṣaḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇa arthaḥ tad ārambha nigamanayoḥ kim samañjasam iti saṃśayaḥ evam saṃdigdheṣu upakrame sāmānya vacane virodha abhāvān na viśeṣaḥ parikalpyaḥ nigamane tu upajātaḥ sāmānya pratyaya iti virodhāl lakṣaṇa artham ghṛta vacanam yathā sṛṣṭiṣu  asṛṣṭiṣu ca sṛṣṭi śabdaḥ evam ghṛtam aghṛtam ca ghṛtam iti  ucyate saṃdigdheṣu  evam prāpte brūmaḥ sāmānya vacanena viśeṣa apekṣiṇa upakramaḥ  vākyasya viśeṣe nigamana vaśena kutas  na hi sāmānyam vihitam yena virodhaḥ  nigamanasya katham avihitam saṃdigdheṣu vidhāna śabda abhāvāt na hi vidhāna śabdaḥ  asti aktāḥ śarkarā upadadhāti iti vartamāna kāla nirdeśāt na api sāmānyasya sākṣāt  stutiḥ pratyakṣam tu ghṛtasya stavanam śrutyā ghṛtasya stutiḥ lakṣaṇayā sāmānyasya śrutiḥ  ca lakṣaṇāyāḥ  jyāyasī tasmāt  ghṛta vidhānam evam vāsaḥ paridhatte etad  vai sarva devatyam vāsaḥ  yad  kṣaumam iti tathā imām spṛṣṭvā udnāyet  imām hi  audumbarīm viśvābhūtāni  upajīvanī iti sruveṇa avadyati svadhitinā avat yati hastena avadyati iti śrūyate tatra saṃdehaḥ kim sruveṇa avadātavyam sarvasya dravasya saṃhatasya māṃsasya ca tathā svadhitinā hastena ca uta sarveṣām arthataḥ  vyavasthā dravāṇām sruveṇa māṃsānām svadhitinā sahatānām hastena iti aviśeṣa abhidhānāt  avyavasthā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ arthāt  vā kalpanā sāmarthyāt  kalpanā iti sruveṇa avadyet  yathā śaknuyāt  tathā yasya śaknuyā tasya ca iti ākhyāta śabdānām artham bruvatām śaktiḥ sahakāriṇī eva ced  yathāśakti vyavasthā bhavitum arhati tathā añjalinā saktūn pradāvye juhoti iti dvi hasta saṃyogaḥ  añjaliḥ sa vyākośaḥ  arthāt  kartavyaḥ tathā hi śakyate homaḥ  nirvartayitum tad  yathā kaṭe bhuṅkte kāṃsya pātryām bhuṅkta iti  arthāt  kalpyate kaṭe samāsīnaḥ kāṃsya pātrī ām odanam nidhāya bhuṅkta iti prathame adhyāye pramāṇa lakṣaṇam vṛttam tatra vidhi artha vāda mantra smṛtayaḥ  tattvataḥ  nirṇītāḥ guṇa vidhiḥ  nāmadheyam ca parīkṣitam sandigdhānām arthānām vākya śeṣāt  artha adhyavasānam uktam tad  na prasmartavyam anantaram pradhāna apradhānāni parīkṣiṣyante bhinnāni  abhinnāni ca iti eṣa eva arthaḥ  varṇanīyaḥ  na anyaḥ eṣa eva ca adhyāya saṃbandhaḥ tad  iha ṣaḍvidhaḥ karma bhedaḥ  vakṣyate śabda antaram abhyāsaḥ saṃkhyā guṇaḥ prakriyā nāmadheyam iti vakṣyamānam anusaṃkīrtyate pradarśitam ucyamānam sukham grāhayiṣyata iti śrotuḥ  ca buddhiḥ samādhīyate tad  etad  nānā karma lakṣaṇam iti  adhyāyam ācakṣate etad  tātparyeṇa atas  anyat  upodghāta prasakta anuprasaktam ca iti tatra prathamam tāvat  idam cintyate prathame adhyāya idam uktam codanā lakṣaṇaḥ  arthaḥ  dharma iti codanā ca kriyāyāḥ  abhidhāyakam vākyam vākye ca padānām arthāḥ tatra kim padena padena dharma ucyate uta sarvaiḥ  eka eva iti kim tāvat  prāptam prati padam dharma iti evam prāpta ucyate yadā ekasmāt  apūrvam tadā anyat tad artham bhaviṣyati evam alpīyasy adṛṣṭa anumāna prasaṇga kalpanā bhaviṣyati tasmāt  ekam apūrvam yadā ekam tadā sandehaḥ kim bhāva śabdebhyaḥ uta dravya guṇa śabdebhya iti kaḥ punar  bhāvaḥ ke te punar  bhāva śabdā iti yajati dadāti juhoti iti evamādayaḥ nanu yāga dāna homa śabdā ete na bhāva śabdāḥ na etad  evam yāga ādi śabda āḥ  ca ete bhāva śabda āḥ  ca yajyādi arthaḥ  cātas  avagamyate bhāvayet  iti ca tathā yateta yathā kiṃcid  bhavati iti tena ete bhāva śabdāḥ dravya guṇa śabdebhyaḥ  dravya guṇa pratyayaḥ na bhāvanāyāḥ atas te na bhāva śabdā iti kim tāvat  prāptam aviśeṣeṇa iti tatas  ucyate bhāva arthāḥ karma śabdāḥ tebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyeta yajeta iti evamādibhyaḥ kutas  bhāva artha tvāt  eva ya āhuḥ kim api bhāvayet  iti te svarga kāma pada saṃbandhāt  svargam bhāvayet  iti brūyuḥ tasmāt  tebhyaḥ kriyā pratīyeta phalasya kriyā karaṇam niṣpattiḥ  iti te ca yāga dāna homa saṃbaddhāḥ svargasya utpattim vadanti kutas  eṣa hi  arthaḥ  vidhīyate yathā yāga ādinā svarga kāmaḥ kena bhāvayet  svargam yāga ādinā iti yasya ca śabdasya arthena phalam sādhyate tena apūrvam kṛtvā na anyathā iti tatas  apūrvam gamyate atas  yaḥ tasya vācakaḥ śabdaḥ tatas  apūrvam pratīyata iti tena bhāva śabdā apūrvasya ca udakā iti brūmaḥ na tu kaścid  chabdaḥ sākṣāt  apūrvasya vācakaḥ  asti bhāva arthaiḥ kim api bhāvayitavyam svarga kāmasya ca kena api bhāvyata iti tayoḥ  naṣṭa aśva dagdha  rathavat  saṃprayogaḥ yajeta iti evamādayaḥ sa ākāṅkṣāḥ yajeta kim kena katham iti svarga kāma  iti  anena prayojanena nirākāṅkṣāḥ na evam dravya guṇa śabdāḥ tasmāt  bhāva arthāḥ karma śabdā apūrvam codayanti iti atha kasmāt  ubhayam sūtritam bhāva arthāḥ karma śabdā iti ucyate bhavanti kecid  karma śabdā na bhāva arthāḥ yathā śyena eka trika ādayaḥ kecid  bhāva arthā na karma śabdāḥ yathā bhavanam bhāvaḥ bhūtiḥ  iti kim punar  iha udāharaṇam śyenena abhicaran yajeta citrayā yajeta paśu kāma iti kim śyenena abhicaran   uta yajeta abhicaran   iti tathā citrayā paśu kāmaḥ uta paśu kāmaḥ  yajeta iti sthite etasmin   adhikaraṇe guṇa vidhiḥ nāmadheyam iti vicāraḥ  bhaviṣyati tathā darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti darśaḥ kālaḥ pūrṇamāsa iti ca kim tābhyām svarga kāmaḥ uta svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām iti ca śyenena iti ca citrayā iti ca na ete bhāva vacanāḥ na ca eṣām arthinā kaścid  saṃbandhaḥ  asti vivibhaktika tvāt  tasmāt  na dravya guṇa śabdā apūrvasya vidhāyakā iti evam ced  bhāvan paśyati abhāva śabda tvān na dravya guṇa śabdā apūrvasya vidhāyakā iti sarveṣām bhāvaḥ arthaḥ svarga kāmaḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām iti  etayoḥ saṃbandham yajeta iti vakṣyati śyenena abhicaran   iti  etayoḥ  ca tathā citrayā paśu kāma iti tasmāt  ete api sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt  bhāva vacanāḥ sarveṣu bhāva vacaneṣu na asti vinigamanāyām hetuḥ karma śabdā eva apūrvasya vidhāyakāḥ na dravya guṇa śabdā iti yeṣām śabdānām uccāraṇa utpattau sve arthe prayujyamānānām rūpa m upalabhyate yad  sakṛt  utpannam kāla antaran tiṣṭhati na kriyā iva utpanna mātram vinaśyati iti  arthaḥ tāni nāmāni te dravya guṇa śabdāḥ īdṛśaḥ  dravya guṇa śabdānām arthaḥ te dravya guṇa śabdā iti vaktavye tāni nāmāni iti sūtritam atas  nāmāni iti eṣām paryāya śabdaḥ katham gamyate yata eṣām vibhaktayaḥ  nāmikya ucyante katamāḥ tāḥ vṛkṣaḥ vṛkṣau vṛkṣāḥ śuklaḥ śuklau śuklā iti evamādayaḥ tasmāt  samyak  sūtritam yata eṣām na kṣaṇikaḥ  arthaḥ tatas  tebhyaḥ parākāṅkṣā pradhāna ākāṅkṣā na vidyata iti na eṣām utpattiḥ kartavyā bhūta tvāt  sve prayoge sva prayoga kāle vidyamāna tvāt  iti  arthaḥ yeṣām tu śabdānām uccāraṇa utpattau sve arthe prayogaḥ  na vidyate prayoga kāle yeṣām arthaḥ  na upalabhyata iti  arthaḥ tany ākhyātāni iti bhāva śabdān paryāya śabdena upadiśati katham paryāya śabda tā bhāva śabdānām yata eṣām vibhaktaya ākhyātikya iti  ucyante katamāḥ tāḥ pacati pacataḥ pacanti iti evamādyaḥ tasmāt  tebhyaḥ  apūrvam pratīyeta bhavya artha aḥ  te bhūta arthaiḥ samuccaritāḥ bhūtasya bhavya artha tāyām dṛṣṭa artha tā bhavya arthasya prayojanayata utpattiḥ  arthavatī sā ca bhūtena kriyata iti dṛṣṭaḥ  arthaḥ bhavyasya punar  bhūta artha tāyām na kiñcid  dṛśyate kalpyate ca adṛṣṭam tasmāt  na yāgaḥ  dravya arthaḥ kim ca āśrita tvāt  prayogasya eteṣām prayogaḥ puruṣeṇa āśritaḥ  bhavati puruṣa saṃbaddhā bhāvanā ucyate puruṣam hi vadati bhāvayet  iti tena svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti puruṣaḥ  api pratīyate yāgaḥ  api saṃbandhaḥ  api svarga kāmaḥ  dravyeṇa iti dravye pratīyate puruṣaḥ  ca na tu saṃbandhaḥ nanu etad  uktam bhavati arthinaḥ  ca dravyasya ca saṃbandham yajeta iti vakṣyati dravyeṇa bhāvayet  iti atas  dravyeṇa arthasya bhāvanā gamyeta ākāṅkṣā ca iti satyam gamyate dravyeṇa bhāvayet  iti tu vākyena yāgena bhāvayet  iti tu śrutyā yadā tu yāgena bhāvāyet  iti yāga saṃbandhaḥ  vidhīyate na tadā dravyeṇa bhāvayet  iti dravya saṃbandhaḥ na ca dravya saṃbandhe vidhīyamāne yajeta iti  anena saṃbandhaḥ anūdyamāne tu saṃbhavati na ca yaugapādyena vidhi anuvādau saṃbhavataḥ tasmāt  chruti vākyayoḥ  virodhaḥ virodhe ca śruti balīyasī tena arthinā na dravya saṃbandhaḥ tatra dravyam asati svarga kāma saṃbandhe svarga artham bhaviṣyati iti  anupapannam eṣa vinigamanāyām hetuḥ yena bhāva śabdā eva apūrvasya ca udakāḥ na dravya guṇa śabdā iti yadā yāgena kuryāt  iti tadā yāga vacanam eva bhavati darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām iti lakṣaṇayā darśe ca pūrṇamāse ca yāgaḥ  vihita iti katham punar  idam avagamyate asti tad  apūrvam iti ucyate codanā iti  apūrvam brūmaḥ apūrvam punar  asti yata ārambhaḥ śiṣyate svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti itarathā hi vidhānam anarthakam syāt  bhaṅgi tvā ād yāgasya yadi  anyat  anutpādya yāgaḥ  vinaśyet  phalam asati nimitte na syāt  tasmāt  utpādayati iti yadi punar  phala vacana sāmarthyāt  tad  eva na viniśyati iti kalpyate na evam śakyam na hi karmaṇaḥ  anyat  rūpam upalabhāmahe yad  āśrayam deśa antaram prāpayati tad  karma iti  ucyate na tad  ātmani samavetam sarva gata tvāt  ātmanaḥ sarvatra kārya upalambhaḥ sarvatra bhāve liṅgam na tu tad  eva deśa antarāt  āgamanasya na hi  asati  āgamane kiṃcid  viruddham dṛśyate yatra samavetam āsīt  tad  vinaṣṭam dravyam tasya vināśāt  tad  api vinaṣṭam iti  avagamyate āśrayaḥ  api  avinaṣṭa iti ced  na bhasma upalambhanāt  sati  api basmany asti iti ced  na vidyamāna upalambhane api  adarśanāt  phala kriyā liṅgam iti ced  evam sati  adarśane samādhiḥ  vaktavyaḥ saukṣma ādīnām anyatamad bhaviṣyati iti yadi cintyate kalpitam evam sati kiṃcid  bhavati iti tatra apūrvam vā kalpyeta tad  vā iti aviśeṣa kalpanāyām asti hetuḥ na viśiṣṭa kalpanāyām anāśritam karma bhaviṣyati iti ced  tad  api tādṛśam eva svabhāva antara kalpanena deśa antaram na prāpayiṣyati iti tādṛśam eva tasmāt  bhaṅgī yajiḥ tasya bhaṅgi tvā ād apūrvam asti iti kim cintāyāḥ prayojanam yadi dravya guṇa śabdā api  apūrvam codayanti dravya guṇa apacāre na pratinidhiḥ  upādātavyaḥ yathā tarhi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ yathā tarhi siddhāntaḥ dravyam guṇam vā pratinidhāya prayogaḥ  anuṣṭhātavya iti avagatam etad  bhāva śabdāḥ karmaṇaḥ  vācakā iti bahu prakārāś ca bhāva śabdāḥ yajati juhoti dadāti iti eva ṃprakārāḥ dogdhi pinaṣṭi vilāpayati iti evamādayaḥ  ca teṣu sandehaḥ kim sarve pradhāna karmaṇaḥ  vidhāyakāḥ uta kecid  saṃskāra karmaṇa iti bhāva arthatva aviśeṣāt  sarve pradhāna karmaṇaḥ  vācakā iti prāptam tatas  brūmaḥ tāni dvaidham bhavitum arhanti iti dvi prakārāṇi kānicid  pradhāna karmaṇaḥ  vācakāni kānicid  saṃskāra karmaṇaḥ evam api sarvāṇi  arthavanti arthavat tve sati sarvebhyaḥ na śakyam apūrvam kalpayitum atas  na sarvāṇi pradhāna karmaṇaḥ  vācakāni evam sati  alpīyasy aḍṛṣṭa kalpanā nyāyyā na tu vinigamanāyām hetuḥ  avagacchāmaḥ kutaḥ apūrvam kutaḥ na iti tad  ucyate yaiḥ  bhāva karmabhiḥ  na dravyam saṃskartum iṣyate utpādayitum vā tāni pradhāna bhūtāni pradhāna karmaṇaḥ  vācakāni dravyasya guṇa bhūta tvāt  dravyam hi guṇa bhūtam karma nirvṛtteḥ  īpsitatama tvāt  yaiḥ  tu dravyam cikīrṣyate guṇa s tatra pratīyeta karma kutas  tasya dravya pradhāna tvāt  pratyakṣam yajeta iti evamādibhiḥ  dravyam na cikīrṣyate tasmāt  tāni pradhāna karmaṇaḥ  vācakāni dravyasya guṇa bhūta tvāt  pinaṣṭi iti evamādibhiḥ  dravyam saṃskriyate tasmāt  tāni guṇa karma vacanāni eṣa eva vinigamanāyām hetuḥ prayojanam tu pūrvasmin pakṣe praiyaṅgave api carau vrīhaya utpādyā avadhāta artha tvena siddhānte na utpādyāḥ srucaḥ saṃmārṣṭi agnim saṃmārṣṭi paridhim saṃmārṣṭi puroṅāśam paryagni karoti iti śrūyate tatra sandehaḥ kim paryagnikaraṇam saṃārjanam ca pradhāna karma uta guṇa karma iti kim tāvat  prāptam tatas  ucyate karma mātram evaṃjātīyakam aparyāptam yad  prayojanasya dṛṣṭasya tad  dharma mātram iti brūmaḥ tatra pradhāna karma tvam syāt  kasmāt  anirvṛtteḥ  upakārasya na hi  evaṃjātīyakam dravyasya upakārakam dravyam tu  evaṃjātīyakam abhinirvartayat  guṇa bhūtam tasya guṇa bhūta tvāt  idam pradhāna bhūtam vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati itaraiḥ  guṇa karmabhiḥ sadharmaḥ syāt  evaṃjātīyakaḥ yathā vrīhīn avahanti tathā kutas  tulya śruti tvāt  tulyā hi dvitīyā śrutiḥ  eṣām dravyeṣu yathā vrīhīn avahanti iti evam agnim saṃmārṣṭi puroṅāśam paryagni karoti iti kim guṇa karmaṇi dravye dvitīyā dṛṣṭā iti yatas  dvitīya adarśanāt  iha api sāmānyatas  dṛṣṭena guṇa karma tā na iti brūmaḥ dvitīyā vibhaktiḥ kartuḥ  īpsitatame smaryate sā ca iha dvitīyā vibhaktiḥ tatas  eva tad īpsitatamam iti gamyate tad  ced  īpsitatamam karma guṇa bhūtam yadi  api pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ  guṇa bhāvaḥ  na gamyate pramāṇa antareṇa śabdena gamyate tasmāt  guṇa bhūtam evaṃjātīyakam iti iti ced  paśyasi dvitīya adarśanāt pradhāna bhūtam atra dravyam iti na etad  evam guṇa bhūte api dvitīyā bhavati tathā hi dṛśyate saktūñ juhoti mārutam juhoti eka kapālam juhoti iti na guṇa bhūte api dvitīyā evam hi  abhiyuktā upadiśanti karmaṇi dvitīyā kartuḥ  īpsitatamam karma iti na ca loke guṇa bhūte kvacid  dvitīyām paśyāmaḥ yad  api ca taṇḍulān odanam paca iti odana artham taṇḍulān saṃskurv iti īpsitā eva taṇḍulāḥ balvajān śikhaṇḍakān kurv iti balvjā eva tena kāreṇa saṃbaddhā īpsitā iti tatra abhiprāyaḥ laukikaḥ  ca prayogaḥ śabda artha paricchede hetuḥ  na vaidikaḥ yad  tu laukike juhoti iti prayoge dvitīyā śakyate tatra vaktum īpsitatama eva sa prayoga iti taṇḍulān adya juhudhi taṇḍulān adya homena saṃbandhayā iti loke bhavati hi bahu prakārā vivakṣā anyāyaḥ  ca aneka artha tvam tena pradhāna bhāvena siddhā satī dvitīyā guṇa bhāvena kalpyeta vede tu katham dvitīya anirdiṣṭe guṇa bhāva iti dvitīya anirdeśāt pradhānyam eva avagacchāmaḥ evam avagate pradhānye balīyasā hetunā na asti prādhānyam iti  avagamyate kutas  na homasya kecid  prakāreṇa saktvartha tā  akalpyate kutas  saktūnām niṣprayojana tvāt  na saktūnām anyat  prayojanam dṛśyate śrūyate vā yadi vā homa s tad arthaḥ  homaḥ  api niṣprayojanaḥ atha ārād upakāra kaḥ  homaḥ tatas  prayojanavān jyotiṣṭoma prakaraṇe pāṭhād gamyate prayojanavat tā na aprayojana iti śakyate vaktum prayoga vacanena hi sa ākāṅkṣyate nanu saktūnām api prakaraṇa pāṭhāt  prayojanavat tvam bhaviṣyati kaḥ  vā brūte na iti prayojanavat tā eva prayojanavat tvan tu homam abhinirvartayatām na anyena prakāreṇa nanu te api prayoga vacanena ākāṅkṣyante tad  ucyate na dravyam tena ākāṅkṣyate itikartavya tām hi sa ākāṅkṣati homaś ceti kartavyatā na dravyam nanu home kṛte saktubhyaḥ  adṛṣṭam niṣpatsyate na asti  atra pramāṇam nanu dvitīyā vibhaktiḥ pramāṇam na hi dvitīyā vibhaktiḥ  homasya saktvartha tām jñāpayati na saktavaḥ prayojanavanta iti bhavet  dhomaḥ saktvarthaḥ homa saṃbaddhāḥ saktavaḥ syuḥ  iti bhavanti home kṛte saktavaḥ  homa saṃbaddhāḥ na homasya saktvartha tā niṣprayojaneṣu saktuṣu ghaṭate saktv artha tā vacanam tu na puruṣasya upakārakam na kratoḥ tad anarthakam eva syāt  yatas  na tad vacanāt  chakyam anyatarat  kalpayitum sa eṣa dvitīya antar  saktūnām homasya ca saṃbandham karoti saṃbandhe ca sati dravyāṇām karma saṃyoge guṇa tvena abhisaṃbandha iti bhūta tvāt  guṇa bhāve ca tṛtīyā tena ucyate tṛtīyāyāḥ sthāne dvitīya iti tena tad artha tvāt  dhoma artha tvāt  saktūnām na pradhānyam dvitīyā saṃyoge api evam sati  arthavat  vacanam na ca arthavat tve sati  ānārthakyam iti  ucyate tasya ca puroḍāśa ādeḥ  yāga ādiṣu śeṣa bhāvaḥ tena prayojanavantaḥ tatra saṃskāraḥ  na anarthakaḥ na sa dṛṣṭa upakārāya iti ced  adṛṣṭa arthaḥ  bhaviṣyati adṛṣṭaḥ  api saṃskāraḥ  asti iti  avagamyate loke yathā grāma antarāt  āgatānām puruṣānām paryagnikareṇa adṛṣṭa upakāraḥ kriyata iti  ucyate loke ca na anupapattiḥ prayojanam ca varuṇa praghāseṣu śrūyate śamī mayaḥ srucaḥ  bhavanti hiraṇmayaḥ  vā iti prakṛtau nānā vṛkṣa sruj saṃmārga sādhyam apūrvam iti nānā vṛkṣa sruca utpādayitavyāḥ saṃmārga artha tvena yathā pūrva pakṣaḥ yathā tarhi siddhāntaḥ śamī maya eva hi hiraṇmayaḥ  vā saṃmārṣṭavyāḥ tathā yatra bāṇavantaḥ paridhayas tatra api pālāśā utpādayitavyāḥ pūrva pakṣe siddhānte bāṇavanta eva saṃmārṣṭavyāḥ avabhṛthe ca pūrva pakṣa utpādayitavyaḥ  agniḥ saṃmārgāya siddhānte cāpaḥ saṃmārjanīyāḥ tathā ṣaṭtriṃśat saṃvatsaretara samayāḥ puroḍāśāḥ savanīyā iti śrūyate tatra api piṣṭa mayaḥ puroḍāśa utpādayita vayaḥ paryagnikaraṇa artha tvena pūrva pakṣe siddhānte māṃsa mayā eva paryagnikartavyā iti praugam śaṃsati niṣkevalyam śaṃsati ājyaiḥ stuvate pṛṣṭaiḥ stuvate iti guṇa vacanam stavanam śaṃsanam ca yathā indrasya tu vīryāṇi pravocam iti yad  etad  guṇa vacanam śrūyate kim etad  guṇa bhūtam devatām prati uta pradhānam iti tatra ucyate stuta śastre saṃskāra karmaṇi iti kutas  devatā abhidhāna tvāt guṇa vacane nirvartyamāne guṇinī devatā saṃkīrtyate na anyathā tad guṇa vacanam bhavati tatra pratyakṣam devatā abhidhānam gamyate devatā prakāśanena ca pratyakṣa upakāraḥ  yāga siddhiḥ tasmāt  saṃskāra karmaṇī yājyāvat  yathā yājyām anāha puraḥ anuvākyām anvāha iti stuti vacanam devatā prakāśanena arthavat  tadvat  etad  api iti yadi saṃskāra karmaṇī eva stotra śastre arthena apakṛṣyeta devatānām naḥ  codanā arthasya guṇa bhūta tvāt  devatā arthasya guṇa bhūtaḥ  mantra iti tad pradhāna bhāve yatra pradhānam tatra nīyeta tatra krama sannidhī uparudhyeyātām tasmāt  eṣa duṣṭaḥ pakṣaḥ iti paryudasitavyaḥ katamaḥ punar  asau mantraḥ abhi tvā śūra iti  aindraḥ pragāthaḥ māhendrasya graha yajeḥ sannidhau   āmnātaḥ  yatra indras tatra apakṛṣyeta na paryudasiṣyāma imam pakṣam saṃskāra karmaṇī eva stotra śastre devatā abhidhāna tvāt  eva yad  uktam pragāthasya utkarṣa iti tad  na indra śabdena mahā indraḥ  abhidhāyiṣyate sa eva indraḥ  mahat tvena guṇena mahā indra iti  ucyate pratyakṣam hi indra śabdam devatā vacanam upalabhāmahe mahattva vacanam ca mahat śabdam yathā rājā mahā rājaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ  mahā brāhmaṇa iti vaśāvat  yathā sā vā eṣā sarva devatyā yad  ajā vaśā vāyavyām ālabheta iti  ajā vaśā śabdena codite karmaṇi chāga śabdena nigamā bhavanti tadvat  saguṇe codite nirguṇena abhidhānam bhaviṣyati tena na bhaviṣyati  utkarṣa iti na etad  evam indraḥ  asya grahasya devatā iti tad hita saṃyogena vijñāyeta na ca asya mahat tvam apekṣamāṇasya tad hita saṃyoga upapadyate tad hita saṃyoga apekṣasya vā mahattva saṃbandhāt  samāsa kalpanā na ca tad dhita arthe vṛttasya mahattva saṃbandhaḥ na ca samāsārthe vṛttasya tad hita saṃbandhaḥ na ca asmin   eva prayoge samāsārthe vṛttiḥ  iṣyate etasmin   eva tad dhita arthe na ca ayam indra śabdaḥ  avihitavat  sva artham tad dhita arthena saṃbadhyeta vihita vac ca para artham mahat tvena saṃbaddham anūdyeta vispaṣṭaḥ  ca ayam anyaḥ  arthaḥ  mahā indraḥ  bhavati mahān indraḥ  bhavati iti mahā indraḥ anyaḥ  ca indraḥ  haviṣaḥ  devatā bhavati iti sakṛt  uccāraṇe ca na ubhayam śakyeta tasmāt  na indraḥ  devatā mahattva viśiṣṭaḥ mahā indra śabdāt  tu tad hita utpannaḥ tasmāt  tad prātipadikam arthavat  iti gamyate na tu  avayava saṃbandhena tasmāt  devatā antaram indrān mahā indraḥ tena aindrasya pragāthasya utkarṣaḥ prāpnoti atas  paryudastitavyaḥ eṣa pakṣaḥ yad  api  ucyate indrasya vṛtra vadha uttara kālam mahā indra tvam darśayati mahān vā ayam abhūt  yaḥ  vṛtram avadhīt  iti tathā vedasya ādimattā doṣaḥ prasajyeta atas  anya indraḥ  mahā indrāt  vyapadeśa bhedaḥ  ca bhavati bahu dugdhi indrāya devebhyaḥ  havir iti bahu dugdhi mahā indrāya devebhyaḥ  havir iti atas  api devatā antaram eka devatā tve mantra vikalpaḥ syāt  yadā vidhi śabdāt  avagatam etad  bhavati indraḥ  devatā iti tadā asya guṇān vā ākhyāne kim prayojanam mahat tvam nāma indrasya guṇa u bhavati iti devatā abhidhānam katham tasyai devatāyai dīyata iti guṇe api hi vihite sati tasyāḥ  eva devatāyai dīyate avihite api tasmāt  guṇa vidhānam anarthakam atha ucyate yaḥ  asmin grahe indraḥ sa mahān iti na evam graha saṃbandhasya aprasiddha tvāt  viśeṣaṇam na atra kalpyate guṇa saṃbandhasya ca aprasiddha tvāt  guṇena viśeṣaṇam anavakḷptam tasmāt  api devatā antaram evam sati yājyā puronuvākyayoḥ  bhedena darśanam upapadyate endra sānasim rayim iti  aindra yājyā puronu vākyād vayam mahān indraḥ  ya ojasā iti bhedena māhendram darśayati tad ekatve vikalpyeta tatra pakṣe bādhaḥ syāt  yad  uktam ajā vaśā śabdena codite karmaṇi chāga śabdena nigamā bhavanti iti tad  yuktam vaśāyām artha samavāyi tvam vayam pratyakṣam avagacchāmaḥ chāgasya vapāyā medasaḥ  anubrūhi iti yā eva vaśā sā eva chāga iti tasmāt  pragāthasya utkarṣaḥ saṃskāra pakṣe atas  pradhāna karmaṇī iti vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati saṃskāra karmaṇī eva stotra śastre yad  ca etad  praghāthasya utkarṣa iti utkṛṣyatām yatra indras tatra praghāthaḥ liṅgena hi krama sannidhī bādhita vyāv eva apareṣām mantrāṇām utkṛṣṭānām anyatra arthavat tā na asti teṣām ānarthakyam syāt  yathā yām yāḥ śaṃsanti śipiviṣṭavatīm pita devatyām āgni mārute kuṣumbhaka sūktam akṣasūktam mūṣikāsu uktam iti evamādīnām tad  ucyate sarveṣām arthavat tā asti maṇḍūka sūktasya agnau akṣa sūktasya rājasūye mūṣikā su uktasya ekādaśinyām sarveṣām vācastome sarvā ṛcaḥ sarvāṇi yajūṃṣi sarvāṇi sāmāni vācastome pāriplavam aśvamedhe śaṃsati iti tathā yasya āśvine śasyamāne sūryaḥ  na udiyāt  api sarvā dāśa tayīḥ  anubrūyāt  iti tasmāt  asti  arthavat tā utkṛṣṭānām atas  saṃskāra karmaṇī stotra śastre iti api vā pradhāna karmaṇī stotra śastre syātām kutas  śruti saṃyogāt  saptamī śruti saṃyogaḥ  hi bhavati kavatīṣu stuvate śipiviṣṭavatīṣu stuvate iti yadi stutiḥ tatas  kavati akṣareṣu  āhitā yadi prakāśanam tatas  devatāyām tatra karaṇam kavati as tṛtīyayā āśroṣyam na saptamyā api ca śruti saṃyogaḥ  bhavati praugam śaṃsati niṣkevalyam śaṃsati iti atas  stutiḥ  abhinirvartayitavyā tena mantreṇa guṇa vacanaḥ śabdaḥ stuti nirvartana arthaḥ  adṛṣṭam artham kariṣyati tasmāt  pradhāna karmaṇī api ca śruti saṃyogaḥ  bhavati ṣaṣṭhī vibhakti saṃyogaḥ yathā indrasya tu vīryāṇi pravocam iti tena devatā śabdaḥ stuti saṃbandha artha  iti  ucyate devatā abhidhāna arthe prātipadikā artha tvāt prathamā syāt  atha yad  prathama antam tad  devatā artham bhavitum arhati yathā indraḥ  yātaḥ  vasitasya rājā iti na iti  ucyate tad  api vākya saṃyogāt  stuti artham eva nanu vākyāl liṅgam balīyaḥ satyam etad  api liṅgam yad  stuti vākyasya sa ākāṅkṣasya nirākāṅkṣīkaraṇa sāmarthyam tathā api  ubhayathā liṅge anugṛhyamāṇe kutaḥ nirṇayaḥ vākya śeṣāt  eva na devatā abhidhāna artha iti devatā abhidhāna artha iti  etasmin pakṣe stuti artham sākāṅkṣa vacanam anarthakam eva syāt  tasmāt  adṛṣṭa artha tvāt stuti vacanasya pradhāna karmaṇī stotra śastre api ca stautiśaṃsati iti sākṣāt  guṇavacanau lakṣaṇayā abhidhāna arthau syātām tasmāt  kriyā utpattim apūrva utpattim vidadhyātām iti śabdena pṛthaktvam eva gamyate dvādaśa stotra śastraḥ agniṣṭomaḥ itarathā hi dvādaśa tvam na syāt  stotrāṇām śastrāṇām ca ekam eva śaṃsanam stavanam ca atha bheda āśrīyate tatas  na dvādaśa tve avatiṣṭhate agniṣṭuti śrūyate āgneyā grahā bhavanti iti tatra punar  ucyate āgneyīṣu śaṃsanti iti tad  na vidhātavyam eva yadi saṃskāra karma tasmāt  api pradhāna karmaṇī iti saṃbaddhe vai stotra śastre vā iti yadi  anyat  stotram anya t  chastram tatas  tayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ yadi vāpūrva vacane tatas  anyat  stotram anya t  chastram itarathā yad  eva stotram tad  eva śastram syāt  pradhāna karmaṇa iva ca abhidhānam bhavati dvitīyā saṃyogena praugam śaṃsati iti niṣkevalyam śaṃsati iti phala nirvṛtti darśanam ca bhavati stutasya stutam asi iti evamādi indravantaḥ  manemahi bhakṣīmahi prajām iṣam sā me sati  āśīryajñasya bhūyāt  iti stotra phalam anūdyate na devatāyāḥ tasmāt  pradhāna karmaṇī stotra śastre anyatra sūtra baddham prayojanam daśame adhyāye grahāṇām devatā anya tve stuta śastrayoḥ pradhāna karma tvāt  adhikāraḥ syāt  idam samāmnāyate na tā naśanti na dabhāti taskaraḥ  na āsām ā mitraḥ  vyathiḥ  ā dadharṣati devānś ca yābhiḥ yajate dadāti ca jyog ittābhiḥ sa ca te gopatiḥ saha iti yajate dadāti iti  udāharaṇam kim yadvat  brāhmaṇe bhāva śabdaḥ  vidhāyakas tadvat  mantre api uta mantre abhidhāyaka iti kim tāvat  prāptam vidhau matre ca āmnāyamānasya bhāva śabdasya eka eva arthaḥ syāt  aika śabdyāt  sa eva ayam ekaḥ śabdaḥ  brāhmaṇa gataḥ  vidhāsyati mantra gataḥ  na śaknoti vidhātum iti  anupapannam tasmāt  vidhāyakaḥ api vā iti pakṣaḥ  vyāvartyate evaṃjātīyakaḥ  mantraḥ  abhidhāna vacanaḥ syāt  prayoga sāmarthyāt  prayoge kriyamāṇe asya sāmarthyam vidyate gaḥ dānam goyāgam ca pratyāyayitum na vidhātum kutas  vihita tvāt  godānasya dakṣiṇā vidhāne goyāgasya tu  anubandhyāyām karma antaram bhaviṣyati iti ced  na asakṛt  api  ucyamāne tad pratyayāt  eva stuti artha kalpanāyām api  ānarthakyam parisamāptena sārthavādakena vākyena vihita tvāt  yāgasya tasmāt  na mantra gataḥ  bhāva śabda evaṃjātīyakaḥ  vidhāyaka iti mantra gataḥ  bhāva śabdaḥ  vidhāyakaḥ  na iti parīkṣitam kaḥ  ayam mantraḥ  nāma iti ucyate ajñāte mantre tad gataḥ  bhāva śabdaḥ katham vicārita iti idam arthaḥ  adhikaraṇam pūrvam draṣṭavyam katham lakṣaṇaḥ  mantra iti tad ca udakeṣu mantra ākhyā abhidhānasya ca udakeṣu  evaṃjātīyakeṣu  abhiyuktā upadiśanti mantrān adhīmahe mantrān adhyāpayāmaḥ mantrā vartanta iti prāyikam idam lakṣaṇam anabhidhāyakā api kecid  mantrā iti  ucyanta yathā vasantāya kapiñjalān ālabhata iti na śakyam pṛṣṭhā koṭeṇa tatra tatra upadeṣṭum iti lakṣaṇam uktam ṛṣayaḥ  api padārthānām na antam yānti pṛthakkaśas  lakṣaṇena tu siddhānām antam yānti vipaścitaḥ udāharaṇam medhaḥ  asi iti evamādayaḥ  asi antāḥ iṣe tvā iti  evamādayaḥ  tvā antāḥ āyuḥ dā asi iti  āśīḥ agniḥ mūrddhā iti stutiḥ saṅkhā ekaḥ  mama iti pralapitam akṣī te indra piṅgale duleḥ  iva iti parivedanam ambe ambika iti praiṣa agnīd agnīn iti anveṣaṇam kaḥ  asi katamaḥ  asi iti pṛṣṭham pṛṣṭhāmi tvā iti ākhyānam iyam vediḥ  iti anuṣaṅgaḥ  acchidreṇa pavitreṇa iti prayogaḥ traisvaryam cātu svaryam ca sāmarthyam abhidhānam tad  ca etad  vṛtti kāraṇena udāharaṇa upadeśena ākhyātam etad  api prāyikam eva asi madhyā api ca mantrā bhavanti īḍyaḥ  ca asi vandyaḥ  ca vājin iti tvā madhyāś ca tadtva āyāmi iti āśīr brāhmaṇam api saḥ  akāmayata prajāḥ sṛjeya iti stutiḥ  api vāyuḥ  vai kṣepiṣṭhā devatā iti pralāpaḥ  na ca etad  vidmaḥ  yadi brāhmaṇā vā sma u abrāhmaṇāḥ sma u vā iti paridevanam ye mām adhukṣanta te mām pratyamuñcanta iti praiṣa amutas  somam āhara iti anveṣaṇam iha vā sa iha vā iti praśnaḥ veda karṇavatīm sūrmim iti prativacanam vidmaḥ  vā iti anuṣaṅgaḥ hṛdayasya agre avadyati  atha jihvāyāḥ  atha vakṣasi iti prayogaḥ traisvaryam cātu svaryam ca iti sāmarthyam sruveṇa avadyati draveṣu  iti lakṣaṇa karmaṇi prayojanam prasiddha tvāt  na vaktavyam laghīyasī pratipattiḥ  lakṣaṇena ākṣepeṣu  apavādeṣu prāptyām lakṣaṇa karmaṇi prayojanam na vaktavyam yaḥ  ca kṛtvā pravartate ākṣepeṣu pūrva adhikaraṇasya prayojanam apavādeṣu utsargasya prāptyām uttara vivakṣā kṛtvā acintāyām pūrva adhikaraṇasya prayojanam asti vede mantra śabdaḥ  yasya ayam arthaḥ parīkṣitaḥ ahe budhniya mantram me gopāya yam ṛṣayas trayī vidā viduḥ ṛcaḥ sāmāni yajūṃṣi iti atha kim lakṣaṇam brāhmaṇam mantrāś ca brāhmaṇam ca vedaḥ tatra mantra lakṣaṇa ukte pariśeṣa siddha tvāt  brāhmaṇa lakṣaṇam avacanīyam mantra lakṣaṇa vacanena eva siddham yasya etal lakṣaṇam na bhavati tad  brāhamaṇam iti pariśeṣa siddham brāhmaṇam vṛtti kāra s tu śiṣya hita artham prapañcitavān iti karaṇa bahulam iti  āha upanibaddham ākhyāyikā svarūpam hetuḥ sūrpeṇa juhoti tena hi  annam kriyata iti nirvacanam tad  dadhnaḥ dadhi tvam nindā upavītā vā etasya agnayaḥ praśaṃsā vāyuḥ  vai kṣepiṣṭhā devatā iti saṃśayaḥ hotavyam gārhapatye na hotavyam iti vidhiḥ yajamāna saṃmita audambarī bhavati parakṛtiḥ māṣān eva mahyam pacati iti purākalpaḥ ulmukhaiḥ  ha sma pūrve samājagmuḥ  iti vyavadhāraṇa kalpanā yāvataḥ  aśvān pratigṛhnīyāt  iti hetuḥ  nirvacanam nindā praśaṃsā saṃśayaḥ  vidhiḥ para kriyā purākalpaḥ  vyavadhāraṇa kalpanā upamānam daśā ete tu vidhayaḥ  brāhmaṇasya tu etad  vai sarva vedeṣu niyatam vidhi lakṣaṇam etad  api prāyikam iti karaṇa bahulaḥ  mantraḥ  api kaścid  iti vā iti me manaḥ iti  āha upanibaddhaś ca bhagam bhakṣi iti  āha ākhyāyikā svarūpam ca ugraḥ  ha bhujyam iti hetuḥ  idam vaḥ  vāmuśanti hi nirvacanam tasmāt  āpaḥ  nu sthanā iti nindā mogham annam vindata apraceta iti praśaṃsā agniḥ  mūrddhā iti saṃśayaḥ adhas  khidāsīt  upari khidāsīt  iti vidhiḥ pṛṇīyādinn ādhamānāya iti parakṛtiḥ sahasram ayutādadat  purākalpaḥ yajñena yajñam ayajanta devāḥ  iti ūha pravara nāmadheyeṣu saṃśayaḥ mantrā uta na iti abhidhāyaka tvān mantrā iti prāpte brūmaḥ anāmnāteṣu mantra tvam na syāt  abhidhāyakeṣu  api na abhidhāyaka tvam mantra tve hetuḥ kim tarhi  abhiyukta prayogaḥ ye abhiyuktaiḥ  mantrā iti na ucyante na te mantrāḥ na ca evamādāya u mantra samāmnāye santi tasmāt  amantrāḥ prayojanam mantre duṣṭe yad  prāyaścittam amantreṣu tad  na ṛca iti  asti vede ahe budhniya mantram me gopāya yam ṛṣayas trayī vidā viduḥ ṛcaḥ  yajūṃṣi sāmāni iti kathaṃlakṣaṇikā ṛcaḥ teṣām ṛc  yatra artha vaśena pāda vyavasthā yatra pāda kṛtā vyavasthā sa mantra ṛc  nāmā yathā agnim īla iti evaṃjātīyakeṣu mantreṣu  abhiyuktā upadiśanti ṛcaḥ  adhīmahe ṛcaḥ  adhyāpayāmaḥ ṛcaḥ  vartanta iti yadi  artha vaśena iti  ucyate yatra vṛtta vaśena tatra na prāpnoti agniḥ pūrvebhiḥ  ṛṣibhiḥ  iti yatas  na artha vaśena iti vṛtta ādi va śa vyāvṛtti artham kim tarhi  anuvāda eṣa pradarśana arthaḥ avaśyam ca etad  evam vijñeyam vṛtta ādi nirvṛtti arthe sati vākyam bhidyeta tasmāt  yatra pāda kṛtā vyavasthā sā ṛc  iti atha sāmnaḥ kim lakṣaṇam viśiṣṭā kācid  gītiḥ sāma iti  ucyate pragīte hi mantra vākye sāma śabdam abhiyuktā upadiśanti sāmāny adhīmahi samāni  adhyāpayāmaḥ sāmāni vartanta iti abhiyukta upadeśaḥ  ca naḥ pramāṇam yathā amlam dadhi madhuraḥ  guḍa iti gīti viśiṣṭe tāvan mantre gīti śabdaḥ gīti saṃbandhān mantre saṃpratyaya iti  avagantavyam atha yajuṣaḥ kim lakṣaṇam iti yajuṣaḥ  lakṣaṇam na vaktavyam ṛc lakṣaṇa sāma lakṣaṇābhyām eva yajuḥ  vijñāsyate vaiparītyena yā na gītiḥ  na ca pāda baddham tad  praśliṣṭa paṭhitam yajuḥ  iti atha nigadaḥ  nāma kim yajūṃṣy uta yajuṣaḥ  anya iti nigadāḥ na yajūṃṣi kutas  dharma viśeṣāt  uccais  ṛcā kriyate uccais  sāmnā upāṃśu yajuṣā uccais  nigadena iti  eṣa dharma viśeṣaḥ uccais  nigadena iti  anūdyate yadi yajuṣaḥ  nigada tvam syāt  na ca tasya uccais  tvam dharmaḥ  dṛśyeta dṛśyate tu tasmāt  caturtham mantra jātam nigadaḥ  nāma vyapadeśaḥ  api bhavati yajūṃṣi vartante na nigadāḥ nigadā vartante na yajuṃṣi iti tasmāt  api mantra antaram yajūṃṣy eva vā nigadāḥ kutas  tad rūpa tvāt tad  eva eṣām rūpam yad  yajuṣām praśliṣṭa pāṭhaḥ ṛc sāma lakṣaṇa vilakṣaṇa tā ca vacanāt  pratyāyana sāmarthyāt  asti hi puruṣa antara pratyāyana sāmarthyam keṣāṃcid  yajuṣām asti ca taiḥ puruṣa antaraiḥ pratyāyitaiḥ prayojanam na upaṃśu uccāryamāṇāḥ puruṣa antaram pratyāyayeyuḥ tasmāt  dharma viśeṣaḥ  arthavān yāni ca yajaṃṣy uccais  uccāryante te nigadāḥ kutas  niśabda prakarṣasya vaktā yathā prakarṣeṇa raktam nitarām raktam iti  ucyate gadatiḥ  gadana arthaḥ pāṭha vacanaḥ eṣa eva hi prakarṣaḥ  yad  uccais tvā avacchinna tvam nanu vācanikaḥ  guṇa u yajuṣām upāṃśu tvam na iti brūmaḥ guṇa u nāma sa bhavati yaḥ sva kāryam kurvatām upakāre vartate na ca para saṃbodhana arthānām yajuṣām upāṃśu tvam sāhāyye vartate tad  dhi sva karma kriyā vighātam karoti tena puruṣa antara saṃbodhana artham uccais tvam guṇaḥ itara artham tu vacanam bhaviṣyati itarāṇi yāni yajūṃṣi na para saṃbodhana arthāni teṣu upāṃśu tvam nivekṣyate atha yad  uktam vyapadeśa iti sa ca eka tve api guṇataḥ  bhavati yathā ita u brāhmaṇā bhojyantām itas  parivrājakā iti evam uccaistvena guṇena tāni  eva yajūṃṣi vyapadiśyante nigadā iti yadi ya uccais  gadyate sa nigadaḥ ṛc  api nigadaḥ prāpnoti na ṛcaḥ  nigadā vyapadiśyante ayājyā vai nigadā ṛcā eva yajanti iti pṛthaktva nimittā hi vyapadeśā bhavanti ucyate vyapadeśaḥ  liṅgam prāptiḥ  ucyatām iti apāda baddhe gadatiḥ  vartate apāda baddhaḥ  hi gadya iti  ucyate atha praśliṣṭa paṭhiteṣu yajuḥṣu katham avagamyeta iyat  ekam yajuḥ  iti yāvatā pada samūhena ijyate tāvān pada samūhaḥ ekam yajuḥ kiyatā ca ijyate yāvatā kriyāyāḥ  upakāraḥ prakāśyate tāvat  vaktavya tvāt  vākyam iti  ucyate tena abhidhīyate artha eka tvāt  ekam vākyam iti etasmāt  ced  kāraṇāt  eka vākyatā bhavati tasmāt  eka arthaḥ pada samūhaḥ  vākyam yadi ca vibhajyamānam sa ākāṅkṣam padam bhavati kim udāharaṇam devasya tvā savituḥ prasava iti nanu padam padam atra ekārtham satyam na tu tad vibhāge sa ākāṅkṣam na tarhi  artha eka tvam upapadyate bahu tvāt  padārthānām pada samudāyasya ca pṛthak arthaḥ  na asti iti  uktam bhedaḥ saṃsargaḥ  vā vākya artha iti yadi  ucyate tathā api  eka artha tā na syāt  bahu pade bhedānām saṃsargāṇām ca bahu tvāt  eka
