atha kim niyata agnihotrān niyatābhyām ca darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām karma antara vidhānam iti kim tāvat  prāptam niyateṣu kāla vidhiḥ  iti kutas  kāla vidhi sarūpa eṣa śabdaḥ  māsam iti katham kāla vidhi sarūpa tā yad  agni hotram juhoti iti viditam māsam iti  aviditam evam ca agnihotra śabdaḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsa śabdaḥ  ca na artha antara vṛttau bhaviṣyataḥ tasmāt  kāla vidhiḥ nanu kuṇḍapāyinām ayana prakaraṇam bādhyeta evam kāmam bādhyatām vākyam hi balavattaram evam prāpte brūmaḥ prakaraṇa antare śrūyamāṇam vākyam yasya prakaraṇe tasya vācakam bhavitum arhati nanu pratyakṣaḥ  agnihotrasya darśa pūrṇa māsayoḥ  ca guṇa vidhiḥ na iti  ucyate katham upasiddhaḥ  caritvā iti hi  uktvā idam abhidhīyate na ca upasadaḥ  agnihotrasya darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  ca santi tasmāt  aśakya s tatra māsa vidhiḥ atha ucyate upasadaḥ  api vidhīyanta iti tathā guṇa vidhāna arthaḥ  asmin vākye aneka guṇa vidhānāt  vākyam bhidyeta asmin pakṣe punar  atantram agnihotra śabdaḥ  na karma viśekṣyati tena vākya bhedaḥ  na bhaviṣyati tasmāt  karma antaram iti siddham anārabhya kiṃcid  chrūyata āgneyam aṣṭākapālam nirvapet  ruj kāmaḥ agnīṣomīyam ekādaśa kapālam nirvapet  brahmavarcasa kāmaḥ aindrāgnam ekādaśa kapālam nirvapet  prajā kāma iti atra sandihyate kim prākṛteṣu  āgneya ādiṣu phalam vidhīyate uta prākṛtebhyaḥ karma antarāṇi  etāni kim prāptam prākṛteṣu phala vidhiḥ  iti kutas  viditā āgneya ādayaḥ pratyabhijñāyante tasmāt  teṣām anuvādaḥ phala saṃbandha artha  iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ phalam ca bhedakam akarma sannidhau śrūyamāṇam katham anuvāde sati na śakyeta phalam vidhātum vidhāyakasya abhāvāt na hi avidhīyamānaḥ  hi  upāyaḥ rucaḥ  bhavati iti gamyate api ca ruj kāme atra vidhīyamāne kāmasya anitya tvāt  āgneya ādīnām nitya tvāt  saṃbandhaḥ  na avakalpeta evam sarvatra tasmāt  karma antarāṇi asti  aveṣṭiḥ āgneyaḥ  aṣṭākapālaḥ puroḍāśaḥ  bhavati iti evamādiḥ tām prakṛtyā ucyate etayā annādya kāmam yājayeta iti tatra sandehaḥ kim karma antaram aveṣṭeḥ  uta āveṣṭiḥ  eva iti kim prāptam karma antaram iti uktena nyāyena evam prāpte brūmaḥ sannidhau phala arthena punar śrutiḥ  aveṣṭeḥ  eva na karma antaram iti kutas  avibhāgāt  etayā iti  eṣa śabdaḥ  na śaknoti  aveṣṭyā vibhaktam yāgam anyam vaktum sannihitasya pratinirdeśaka eṣa śabdaḥ tasmāt  aveṣṭiḥ  eva annādya kāmasya vidhīyata iti kim prayojanam yadi  aveṣṭiḥ āgneya ādīni havīṃṣi atha karma antaram anya haviṣkaḥ  yāga iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  āgneyaḥ  aṣṭākapālaḥ  amāvāsyābhyām paurṇamāsyām ca acyutaḥ  bhavati iti vidhāya punar  ucyate āgneyaḥ  aṣṭākapālaḥ  amāvāsyāyām bhavati iti tatra sandehaḥ kim amāvāsyāyām dvis  āgneyena yaṣṭavyam uta sakṛt  iti kim prāptam āgneya sūkta hetu tvāt  abhyāsena pratīyate ekasya evam punar śrutiḥ  aviśeṣāt  anarthakam hi syāt  iti na etad  asti punar  abhyasitavya āgneya iti kutas  na abhyāsasya vācakaḥ śabdaḥ  asti iti nanu  āgneyaḥ punar uccaritaḥ param karma vidhāsyati na iti brūmaḥ śabdaḥ punar uccaritaḥ  na punar  arthaḥ kartavya iti śaknoti vaditum yaḥ  asya prathamam uccaritasya arthaḥ śata kṛtvā u api  uccaritasya sa eva arthaḥ  bhaviṣyati na anyaḥ nanu vihitam eva punar  viśiṣṭam vidadhat  anartha kaḥ bhavati bhavatu kāmam anarthaka tvam na tu  anyam śaknoti vaditum bhavet  upapannam anarthaka tvam na tu  artha antara vacana tā tasmāt  na dvis  abhyasyeta iti atha vā na anarthikā punar śrutiḥ artha vāda arthā bhaviṣyati iti  ucyate kim artha vādena prayojanam yadā pūrvena eva vākyena sārthavādakena vihitaḥ āgneyaḥ kam anyam artham vidhātum śrutiḥ prayujyeta śruti mātram yad  na kasyacid  vidhāna artham tad  anarthakam iti  uktam āmnāyasya kriyā artha tvāt  ānarthakyam atad arthānām iti śrutaḥ  ca aśrutaś ca tāvān eva saḥ  arthaḥ yathā śrutā ca aśru tā ca devatā aṅga bhāvam sādhayati evam etad  iti tad  ucyate anya arthā vā punar śrutiḥ na āgneyam vidhātum aindrāgna vidhāna arthā āgneyaḥ  aṣṭākapālaḥ  amāvāsyāyām bhavati  eva na kevalena agninā sa sādhuḥ  bhavati iti indra sahitaḥ  agniḥ samīcīnataraḥ tasmāt  aindrāgnaḥ kartavya iti bahvṛca brāhmaṇe śrūyate yāvajjīvam agni hotram juhoti iti yāvat jīvam darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta iti atra sandeheḥ kim karma dharmaḥ  abhyāsaḥ  yāvat jīvika tā uta kartṛ dharmaḥ  niyamaḥ  codyate yāvat jīvikatā iti katham karma dharmaḥ  abhyāsaḥ katham vā kartṛ dharmaḥ  niyama iti yadi juhotiḥ  anuvādaḥ yāvajjīvam iti vidhiḥ tatas  karma dharmaḥ  abhyāsaḥ yadi viparītam tatas  kartṛ dharmaḥ  niyama iti kim tāvat  prāptam karma dharmaḥ  abhyāsaḥ kutas  prakaraṇāt  yadi iyam vacana vyaktiḥ juhoti yajati śabdau   anuvādau yāvajjīvam iti ca vidhiḥ tatas  prakaraṇam anugṛhyate tasmāt  abhyāsaḥ evam kṛtvā satrasan  tavaḥ  yuktaḥ  bhaviṣyati jarā maryam vā etad  satram yad  agnihotram darśa pūrṇamāsau ca iti dīrgha kāla sāmānyāt  tasmāt  abhyāsaḥ atra brūmaḥ yāvat jīvikaḥ  abhyāsaḥ  na syāt  kartuḥ  dharmaḥ  niyamaḥ  codyata iti kutas  śruti saṃyogāt  evam śruti paricchinnaḥ  arthaḥ  bhaviṣyati itarathā lakṣaṇā syāt  katham yāvat jīvanam tāvatā kālena kuryāt  iti tad  etad  pradoṣa parisamāptam agnihotram anabhyasya na śakyate yāvat jīvana kālena kartum paurṇamāsyam āvāsya aparisamāptau ca darśa pūrṇamāsau yadi  ucyeta jīvana kālasya eka deśe api kṛtam tena kālena kṛtam bhavati iti na etad  evam artha prāptam hi tad  na vidhātavyam śabdena jīvana parimitaḥ kālaḥ  yaḥ tena parisamāpayitavyam iti  arthāt  abhyāsaḥ sa hi kartavya tayā śrūyate na ca asau   juhoti yajatibhyām ucyate lakṣaṇayā tu gamyate yāvat jīvam juhuyāt  yāvajjīvam abhyasyet  iti śrutiḥ  ca prakaraṇāt  balīyasī yadi iyam vacana vyaktiḥ  asya vākyasya yāvajjīvam iti  anuvādaḥ  juhoti yajati iti ca vidhānam iti  evam yajati juhoti śabdau sva arthau   eva bhaviṣyataḥ yāvat jīva śabdaḥ  api jīvana vacana eva na abhyāsa lakṣaṇaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti jīvane nimitte karma vidhīyate jīvanś ced  dhotavyam iti jīvanam nimittam na kālaḥ niyata nimitta tvāt  niyatam karma tena ucyate kartuḥ  dharmaḥ  niyamaḥ  codyata iti liṅgam ca bhavati  api ha vā eṣa svargāl lokāt  chidyate yaḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsa yājī paurṇamāsīm amāvāsyām vā atipātayeta iti katham liṅgam karma dharme hi prakrāntam satram yāvat jīvana kālena parisamāpyeta na tatra kāla atipātaḥ syāt  tatra ca anarthakam anyat  syāt  prāyaścitta ādi vidhīyamānam vyapavargasya samāpanasya darśanam bhavati darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām iṣṭvā somena yajeta iti yadi darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām iṣṭvā somasya kālaḥ  asti vyaktam na yāvat jīvana kālena tau parisamāpyete atha jīvanam nimittam upapadyate karma bhedaḥ darśa pūrṇamāsau parisamāpya somam karma antaram kuryāt  iti api ca āhitāgniḥ  vā eṣa yaḥ  agnihotram juhoti na darśa pūrṇamāsau yajeta yā āhuti bhājaḥ  devatā as tā anudhyāyinīḥ karoti iti  anudhyāyinī vacanam bhavati niyataḥ  ya āhuti bhāgaḥ tasmin adīyamāne anudhyāyinī vacanam bhavati yaḥ  tu  aniyata āhuti bhāga s tam anudhyāyanti idam naḥ bhaviṣyati iti niyata ś ca bhāgaḥ  niyama pakṣe bhavati na kāmya pakṣe karma dharme ca kāmyam agni hotram ca darśa pūrṇamāsau ca tasmāt  niyama pakṣaḥ api ca śrūyate jarā maryam vaitat  satram yad  agni hotram darśa pūrṇamāsau ca jarayā ha vaitābhyām nirmucyate mṛtyunā ca iti jarā maraṇa nirmocana avadhāraṇa vacanam ca niyama pakṣa upapadyate kāmya pakṣe hi  aprayogāt  api mucyeta tuśabdaḥ  anvācaye itaraḥ  ca paśyāmaḥ kartuḥ  dharmaḥ  niyamaḥ  codyata iti yadi pūrvasya homasya guṇa vidhiḥ  bhavet  sa ekaikaḥ pūrvaḥ agnihotra homaḥ  anityaḥ syāt  kāma saṃyogena śrutaḥ  na anyaḥ kaścid  nityaḥ tatra liṅgam virudhyeta jarā maryam vaitat  satram yad  agni hotram darśa pūrṇamāsau jarayā vaitābhyām nirmucyate mṛtyunā ca iti katham virudhyate jarā maraṇa nirmocana ādhāraṇa vacanam niyama pakṣa upapadyate kāmya pakṣe aprayogāt  api mucyeta itas  ca paśyāmaḥ  na pūrva abhyāsaḥ  guṇaḥ  codyata iti kutah virodhāt  virodhaḥ  bhavati darśa pūrṇamāsa vikārāḥ sauryādayaḥ  api yāvajjīvam abhyasitavyā bhaveyuḥ saḥ  anārabhya arthaḥ pratijñātaḥ syāt  atas  api paśyāmaḥ  niyama iti satra saṃstavaḥ  ca santata bhāvam upapatsyate yadi kartuḥ  dharmaḥ  niyamaḥ  codyeta tatas  jīvanam nimittam jīvane nimitte karma vidhīyate tatra prayoge parisamāptam karma tathā vyapavargasya darśanam akḷptam bhavati tasmāt  kartṛ dharmaḥ  niyamaḥ  codyata iti siddham bhavati iha śākhā antarāṇi  udāharaṇam kāṭhakam kālāpakam paippalādakam iti evamādīni tatra sandehaḥ kim ekasyām śākhāyām yad  karma agni hotra ādi śrūyate tad  chākhā antare punar  śrūyamāṇam bhidyeta tasmāt  uta na bhidyeta bhidyeta iti paśyāmaḥ kutas  nāma bhedāt  ekam kāṭhakam nāma anyat  kālāpakam nāma evam nāma bhedāt  bhedaḥ nanu grantha nāma etad  satyam karmaṇām api iti brūmaḥ karmabhiḥ  api  evamādīnām sāmānādhikaraṇyam eka vibhakti tvam ca iti rūpa bhedāt  ca ekasyām śākhāyām agnīṣomīyam ekādaśa kapālam āmananti ekasyām dvādaśa kapālam evam bhinnam rūpam katham iva na karma antaram bhaviṣyati dharma viśeṣāc ca kārīrī vākyāni  adhīyānāḥ  taittirīyā bhūmau bhojanam ācaranti apare śākhinaḥ  na ācaranti tathā agnim adhī yānāḥ kecid  upādhyāyasya uda kumbhān āharanti apare na aśvamedham adhīyānāḥ kecid  aśvasya ghāsam āharanti apare na pare anyam dharmam ācaranti aśva ghāsa ādeḥ  ekeṣām upakāram ākāṅkṣati  aśvamedha ādiḥ ekeṣām na ākāṅkṣati sa eva ekaḥ katham na ākāṅkṣeta katham vānyat  ākāṅkṣitum arhati atas  gamyata anyat  iti punarukti prasaṅga āt  ca yadi sarva śākhā pratyayam ekam karma ekasyām śākhāyām vihitasya karmaṇaḥ śākhā antare vacanam punaruktam anarthakam syāt  na tu bheda pakṣa eṣa doṣaḥ  asti tasmāt  api karma bhedaḥ nindā vacanāt  ca prātar  prātar anṛtam te vadanti purā udayā juhvati ye agnihotram divākīrtyam ādivā kīrtayantaḥ sūryaḥ  jyotiḥ  na tadā jyotiḥ  eṣām iti kecid  chākhinaḥ  anudita homam nindanti apare punar  udita homam nindanti yathā atithaye pradrutāya annam āhareyuḥ  tādṛś  tad  yadi  udite juhvati iti sarva śākhyā pratyaye viruddham na tu karma bhede tasmāt  api bheda iti aśakteḥ  ca na śaknuyuḥ khalu  api sarva śākhā pratyayam upasaṃhartum tatra anārabhyaḥ  arthaḥ  vidhīyata iti pratijñātam bhavet  śakyam tu karma bhede atas  karma bheda iti samāpti vacanāt  ca asamāpte api samāpteḥ  vacanam bhavati kecid  āhuḥ atra asmākam agniḥ parisamāpyata iti apare anya parisamāptim vyapadiśanti tad  eka karma tve na upapadyate na hi tatra ca parisamāpyeta anyatra na bhede tu yuktam tasmāt  bheda iti prāyaścitta vidhānāt  ca kecid  anudita homa vyatikrame prāyaścittam āmananti kecid  udita homa vyatikrame vṛddhe ca prāyaścittam na ca karma ekatva ubhayathā vṛddhiḥ saṃbhavati karma bhede tu yad  anudite homa karma tad  udite vṛddham itarat  api  udite tasmāt  api bhedaḥ anya artha darśanāt  ca idam śrūyate yadi purā didīkṣāṇāḥ syuḥ yadi vā eṣām gṛhapatiḥ  gṛhapateḥ  vā anusatriṇa iti ta enam eva bṛhatsāmānam kratum upeyuḥ  upetam hi  eṣām rathantaram atha yadi  adidīkṣāṇā iti iṣṭava tām aniṣṭa pūrvāṇām ca dvādaśa ahe darśanam upapadyate yadi karma bhedaḥ eka karma tve na avakalpyate katham tāṇḍake śrūyate eṣa vāva prathamaḥ  yajñaḥ  yajñānām yaj jyotiṣṭomaḥ ya etena aniṣṭvā atha anyena yajeta gartapatyam eva tad  jāyeta pravām īyata iti tad  sarvatra syāt  tatra ādidīkṣāṇām dvādaśa ahe darśanam na upapadyate tasmāt  api karma bhedaḥ atha aparam liṅga darśanam yad  pakṣa samitām pinuyāt  kanīyāṃsam yajña kratum upeyāt  kanīyasīm prajñām kanīyasaḥ paśūn kanīyaḥ  annādyam pāpīyān syāt  atha yadi vedi saṃmityā minoti iti pakṣa samāne pratiṣiddhe vedi saṃmānasya darśanam bhavati tad  tu karma bheda upapadyate pākṣikasya vedi saṃmānasya darśanam eka karma tve na upapadyate katham eke hi samāmananti ratha akṣa mātrāṇi yūpa antarālāni bhavanti iti tad  sarvatra syāt  tatra ca naḥ pakṣa saṃmānam naḥ vedi saṃmānam syāt  vedi saṃmāna darśanam na upapadyate tasmāt  api karma bhedaḥ aparam ca liṅga darśanam keṣāṃcid  jyotiṣṭome śrūyate dve saṃstutānām virājam atiricyeta iti pareṣām tisraḥ saṃstutānām virājam atiricyanta iti  eka karma tve virodhaḥ nānā karma tve kasmiṃścid  jyotiṣṭome dve kasmiṃścid  tisraḥ tasmāt  karma bheda iti api ca sārasvate śrūyate ye puroḍāśinaḥ  te upaviśanti ye sānnāyinaḥ  te vatsān vārayanti sānnāyina iṣṭa prathama yajñāḥ puroḍāśinaḥ viparītāḥ ubhayeṣām sārasvate darśanam avakalpate karma bhede eka karma tve sarveṣām jyotiṣṭoma pūrva tvam syāt  tatra darśanam na upapadyate api ca śrūyate upahavyaḥ  niruktaḥ agniṣṭomaḥ  yajñaḥ rathantara sāmā aśvaḥ śyāvaḥ  dakṣiṇā pareṣām śrūyate upahavyaḥ  aniruktaḥ ukthaḥ  yajñaḥ  bṛhatsāmā aśvaḥ śvetaḥ  rukma lalāṭaḥ  dakṣiṇā iti karma ekatve rathantara vacanam bṛhat vacanam ca anarthakam śākhā dvaya pratyaya tvāt  bṛhatsāmā rathantara sāmā vā syāt  sa ca ayam prakṛtita evaṃlakṣaṇakaḥ prāptaḥ nānā karma tve tu  anyaḥ  bṛhat sāmānyaḥ  rathantara sāma iti yuktam bhavati tasmāt  chākhā antare karma bhedaḥ  bhavitum arhati na ca etad  asti yad  uktam śākhā antareṣu karma bheda iti sarva śākhā pratyayam sarva brāhmaṇa pratyayam ca ekam karma artha saṃyogasya aviśeṣāt  tad  eva prayojanam uddiśya tad  eva vidhīyamānam pratyabhijānīmaḥ rūpam api  asya tad  eva dravya devatam puruṣa prayatnaḥ  ca tādṛśa eva codyate nāmadheyam ca aviśiṣṭam tena tad  eva karma sarva śākhā ādiṣu  iti pratyayaḥ yad  uktam nāma bheda iti parihṛtam tad  granthanām ata iti atha yad  uktam karmaṇaḥ  api nāma sāmāna adhikaraṇya darśanāt  iti na eṣa doṣaḥ grantha saṃyogāt  karma kāṭhaka ādi na karma saṃyogāt  granthaḥ kāṭhakaḥ katham gamyate yad  karma kāṭhaka ādi saṃyuktam tad  kāṭhaka ādi śabdena ucyate kim atas  api yad  grantha saṃyogāt  kāṭhakam kālāpakam karma ucyate ekatve api kāṭhaka grantha saṃyogāt  kāṭhakam kālāpaka grantha saṃyogāt tu kālāpakam bhaviṣyati yadi śabda bhedāt  bhedaḥ  bhavet  śabda aikyāt  tarhi karma aikyam bhavet  tatra kāṭhaka śabda abhidhānāt  aikyam bhavet  agnihotrasya darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  jyotiṣṭomasya ca tad śabda tvāt  na ca etad  evam tasmāt  api  abhedaḥ idānīṃtanam ca etad  abhidhānam bhavet  asya na pūrvam āsīt  yatas  prabhṛti kaṭhasya prakṛṣṭam vacanam tatas  prabhṛti pravṛttam pūrvam na āsīt  bhedaḥ idānīm bheda iti viruddham eka karma tve api rūpa bhedaḥ  bhavati vacanāt  na ca vācanike rūpa bhede asatyām api bheda buddhau karmaṇaḥ  bhedaḥ  abhyavasīyeta atha yaḥ  dharma viśeṣa uktaḥ vidyā grahaṇa arthaḥ saḥ na karmaṇa upakārakaḥ katham gamyate śruti ādīnām abhāvāt  vidyā saṃyoga āt  ca na karma prayukta iti atha yad  uktam yathā amāvāsyāyām āgneyasya punarukta doṣān madhyamaḥ pakṣaḥ  nirastaḥ evam ayam api tasmāt  eva doṣāt  karma ekatva pakṣaḥ  nirasitavya iti etad  parihartavyam  ity ābhāṣā antam sūtram  na eva khalu  etad  dvis vacanam sa eva ayam arthaḥ punar  śrāvitaḥ  agnihotra ādiḥ  bahu kṛtvā u bahubhiḥ  tu puruṣaiḥ na ca ekaḥ arthaḥ  bahubhiḥ  ucyamānaḥ punaruktaḥ  bhavati yadi bhavet  ekasmin   eva vede bahubhiḥ  ucyamāne bhavet  tasmāt  na bahu karma samavāyaḥ  ayam ekam eva idam karma iti artha āsannidheś ca śākhā śabda upapannaḥ  bhaviṣyati śākhā iva homāḥ śākhāḥ tad  yathā vṛkṣasya śākhāḥ evam iha api vṛkṣa sthānīyasya vedasya śākhāḥ kim śākhā sārūpyam yathā nānā avasthānam na ca ekaikasyām kṛtsnam puṣpam phalam sannihitam evam iha api na eka ekasyām kṛt sam guṇa kāṇḍam sannihitam iti  artha asannidheḥ śākhā śabda upapattiḥ tasmāt  api  ekam karma iti na ca yad  kāṭhake agnihotram tad  kāṭhakam eva ekam puruṣam prati vidhīyate taittirīyasya api tad vihitam eva puruṣa viśeṣa vacana abhāvāt yad  ca agnihotrasya kiṃcid  aṅgam vidhīyate sarva avasthasya tad  agnihotrasya yad  ca kāṭhakasya agnihotram tad  ca taittirīyakasya iti viśeṣa vacana abhāvāt tasmāt  sarva śā ākhyābhiḥ  ekam samāptam karma ucyata iti atra asmākam agniḥ parisamāpyata iti  utprekṣitāraḥ  bhavanti anvāroheṣu maitrāyaṇīyānām agniḥ parisamāpyate asmākam teṣu na parisamāpyata iti yadi  anyat  eva maitrāyaṇīyānām anya t  ca teṣām katham te brūyuḥ  eṣu  asmākam na parisamāpyata iti eka tvam upapannam teṣām api hi te santi na hi nindā nindyam ninditum prayujyate kim tarhi ninditāt  itarat  praśaṃsitum tatra na ninditasya pratiṣedhaḥ  gamyate kim tarhi ninditāt itarat  praśaṃsitum tatra na ninditasya pratiṣedhaḥ  gamyate kim tu  itarasya vidhiḥ tatra ekasmin   agnihotre dvau kālau vihitau vikalpyete atas  na kaścid  virodhaḥ tathā asamarthānām ekasmin   api vede vihitam kṛtsnam aṅga jātam upasaṃhartum aśaktiḥ samarthānām tu sarva śākhā abhyaḥ  api  āgamitam adhikam vidhim upasaṃhartum śaktiḥ  asti iti tena eka karma tve api na viruddham iti tathā ekasmin   api karmaṇi kiṃcid  vastu samāptam iti kṛtvā samāpti śabdaḥ prayujyate yathā ādhvaryave samāpte jyotiṣṭomasya samāptaḥ  jyotiṣṭoma iti bhavati yad  uktam udita homasya api prāyaścitta antā na avṛddha tā gamyate anudita homasya api tad  ekatve virudhyate aviruddham nānātva iti tad  parihartavyam  ābhāṣā antam sūtram  vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na eṣa doṣaḥ udite hoṣyāmi iti prakānte anyathā kriyamāṇe bhavati doṣaḥ tatra prāyaścittasya viṣayaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti karma ekatve api na doṣaḥ pūrvavati samāpti vacanam bhavati yad  prārabdham tad  parisamāpyate tatra asmākam parisamāptaḥ  agniḥ  iti yaḥ  asmābhiḥ  jñāyate prārabdhaḥ  ca parisamāpyata iti  abhiprāyaḥ yad  uktam yadi purā didīksāṇā iti dvādaśa āha iṣṭa prathama yajñānām aniṣṭa prathama yajñānām ca darśanam karma bheda upapadyate na sarva śākhā pratyaya eka karmaṇi iti na eṣa doṣaḥ yadi didīkṣāṇā dvādaśa ahena adidīkṣāṇā dvādaśa śāhena iti  evam tad  na hi sāmavede jyotiṣṭomasya vidhānam kim atas  api yatra vihita s tatra anūdyate tena karma bhede api sarva jyotiṣṭomānām eṣa dharmaḥ prāthamyam nāma atas  nānā karma pakṣe api  avaśyam dvādaśa ahasya āhāra vyapadeśaḥ kalpanīya s tasmāt  adoṣaḥ dravye ca agnau   acodita tvāt  ekādaśinyāḥ saṃmāna parimāṇam parti na eṣā vyavasthā syāt  na eva agnau   ekādaśinī codyate kutas  pakṣa saṃmānam vedi saṃmānam vā syāt  dvayam api  etad  para artham kīrtyate paśu ekādaśinī vidhāna artham yadi pakṣa saṃmitā syāt  ayam doṣaḥ syāt  vedi saṃmāne na doṣaḥ  bhavet  ka etad  saṅkaṭa madhyavasānam arhati ekasmin yūpa ekādaśa paśavaḥ  niyoktavā iti vācastoma ādiṣu tu yūpa ekādaśinyām asya nitya anuvāda tvāt  ratha akṣa mātrāṇi  eva yūpa antarālāni bhaviṣyanti nitya anuvāda tvāt  ca asati  api pakṣa saṃmāne vedi saṃmāne vā ekādaśinī vidhāna artham vacanam upapadyata eva iti na doṣaḥ atirātre gṛhṇāti ṣoḍaśinam iti vihitaḥ ṣoḍaśī na atirātre gṛhṇāti ṣoḍaśinam iti pratiṣiddhaḥ tena pakṣe dvayoḥ stotrīyayoḥ  atirekaḥ pakṣe tisṝṇām tasmāt  adoṣaḥ katham punar  ayam dvayoḥ  tisṝṇām vātiḥ ekaḥ trivṛt  bahiṣpavamānam tad  tāvan navakam pañcadaśāni  ājyāni tāni tāvac catvāri tena sā ṣaṣṭiḥ pañcadaśaḥ  mādhyaṃdinaḥ pavamānaḥ tayā pañcadaśa saṃkhyayā saha pūrvayā ca nava saṃkhyayā caturaśītiḥ saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni catvāri saptadaśa ārbhavaḥ pavamānaḥ pañca saptadaśakāni tāni iti pañca aśītiḥ pūrvayā catur śītyā saha ekonasaptati śatam ekaviṃśam yajñāyajñiyam tayā ekaviṃśatyā saha tasya navati śatam stotriyā iti brāhmaṇa vādaḥ agniṣṭoma mātram abhipretya ucyate sā virāj  saṃpūrṇā virāj  iti daśaka ākhyāḥ traya ekaviṃśakā uktha paryāyāḥ sā triṣaṣṭiḥ ekaviṃśaḥ ṣoḍaśī tayā ekaviṃśatyā saha caturaśītiḥ pañcadaśakā rātri paryāya as trayaḥ tatra ekaika paryāyaḥ catur stotraḥ tad  aśīti śatam saṃpūrṇā virāj  trivṛt  rathantaram pañcasāma tad  navakam tatas  caturaśīteḥ  ekam navakam āgacchati tathā tisraḥ saṃstutānām virājam atiricyante yadā ṣoḍaśī na gṛhyate tadā ekaviṃśatyā vinā dve saṃstutānām virājam atiricyete evam eka karma tve api liṅgam upapadyate yad  uktam puroḍāśinām sānnāyinām ca sārasvate darśanam bhavati iti jyotiṣṭoma pūrvaka tvāt  sarva karmaṇām vipratiṣiddham etad  iti tena yadā sānnāyinaḥ puroḍāśina iti kalpyate atham yad  uktam upahavye bṛhat rathantara vidhānam prakṛti prāptam eva eka karma tve pratiprasava tayā api  asaṃbhavāt  vidhīyamānam anarthakam syāt  iti tad  parihartavyam ābhāṣā antam sūtram yadā rathantara sāmā tadā aśvaḥ śvetaḥ  dakṣiṇā yadā bṛhatsāmā tadā rukma lalāṭa iti yadā na sarva śākhā pratyayam ekam karma iti katham ekasyām śākhāyām samāmnāyate anyasyām guṇa u vidhīyate yathā maitrāyaṇīyānām samidh ādayaḥ prayājā na samāmnāyante atha ca guṇāḥ śrūyante ṛtavaḥ  vai prayājāḥ samānīya hotavyā iti tathā yeṣām śākhinām kuṭaruḥ  asi iti  aśma ādāna mantraḥ  na āmnā atar  teṣām api hi dṛśyate kukkuṭaḥ  asi iti  aśmānam upapādatte kuṭaruḥ  asi iti vā iti tasmāt  ekam karma iti pratīmaḥ yaḥ  hi  anya śākhā avasthitān vidhīn upasaṃharati sa sva śākhā vihitam kramam uparuṇaddhi iti tena śākhā antareṣu karma bheda iti ucyate na eṣa śākhā antara vihitānām aika karmye sati virodhinā saṃyogaḥ na hi kramaḥ  vākyena virudhyate durbalaḥ  hi kramaḥ balavat  vākyam vākyena ca śākhā antarīyāṇām upasaṃhāraḥ tasmāt  sarva śākhā pratyayam sarva brāhmaṇa pratyayam ca ekam karma codyata iti siddham bhavati nānā karma lakṣaṇam vṛttam anantaram śeṣa lakṣaṇam vartayiṣyāmaḥ kaḥ śeṣaḥ kena hetunā śeṣaḥ katham ca viniyujyate iti śruti ādīni ca viniyoge kāraṇāni iti vakṣyate teṣām ca balavat abalavattā etad  tātparyeṇa anyat  api  upoddhātā ādinā iha sūtre śeṣasya lakṣaṇam yena ca hetunā śeṣa iti  ucyate tad  ubhayam ākhyāyate yaḥ parasya upakāre vartate sa śeṣa iti  ucyate tad  yathā ye para arthāḥ te vaktāraḥ  bhavanti śeṣa bhūtā vayam iha iti nanu yaḥ  api pradhāna bhūtaḥ saḥ  api kadācid  para arthe vartate yathā upādhyāyaḥ pradhāna bhūtaḥ śiṣyāṇām vidyā vinaya ādhāne vartate satyam vartate yaḥ  tu  atyantam para arthaḥ tam vayam śeṣa iti brūmaḥ yathā garbha dāsaḥ karma artha eva svāminaḥ  anaḍvān   ca krīyate vakṣyati iti  eva nanu garbha dāsasya api sa vāmī saṃvid adhānaḥ  guṇa bhāva māyāt  na iti brūmaḥ ātmana eva asau saṃvid adhānaḥ  guṇa bhāvam gacchati na antarīyaka tvāt  garbha dāsasya upakaroti anaḍuhaḥ vā yaḥ  tu  atyantam para arthaḥ tam vayam śeṣa iti brūmaḥ atha tatra kim vṛttam yaiḥ  tu dravyam cikīrṣyate guṇa s tatra pratīyeta iti tatra apūrva artha tā vyāvartitā dṛṣṭa prayojanānām ākhyātānām iha tu sarveṣām eva śeṣāṇām lakṣaṇam ucyate vādariḥ  ācāryaḥ  atra dravya guṇa saṃskāreṣu  eva śeṣa śabda iti mane na yāga phala puruṣeṣu dravyam kriyā artham yadi prayojanavatī kriyā vyaktam sā dravyeṇa nirvartayitavyā tasyāḥ  nirvṛttiḥ  dravyāt ṛte na bhavati iti tad nirvṛttaye dravyam eṣitavyam bhavati tasmāt  kriyā artham dravyam guṇaḥ śaknoti viśiṣṭam dravyam coditam lakṣayitum lakṣitena ca tena prayojanam viśiṣṭasya kriyā sādhana tvāt  tasmāt  saḥ  api dravya dvāreṇa kriyāyāḥ  upakaroti iti kriyā artha eva saṃskāraḥ  nāma sa bhavati yasmin jāte padārthaḥ  bhavati yogyaḥ kasyacid  arthasya tena api kriyāyām kartavyāyām prayojanam iti saḥ  api para arthaḥ tasmāt  dravya guṇa saṃskārāḥ parārtha tvāt  cheṣa bhūtāḥ na tu yāga phala puruṣāḥ yāga s tāvat  kartavyaḥ puruṣasya na hi tasmin nirvartite kiṃcid  aparam asti kartavyam sa hi puruṣa arthaḥ yad  anyat  dravya ādi tad  tad artham tasya śeṣa bhūtam sa tu na kiṃcid  abhinirvartayitum kriyate phalam api na tena kriyate tasmin   tu kṛte svayam eva tad  bhavati tasmin kṛte phalam asya bhavati iti  etāvat  gamyate na asti śabdaḥ  yāgena kriyate phalam iti tasmāt  yāgaḥ  na śeṣa bhūtaḥ kasyacid  arthasya phalam api na puruṣam pratyupadiśyate yaḥ svargam kāmayate sa yāgam kuryāt  iti  etāvat  chabdena udiśyate na ātmanaḥ parasya vā iti svargam pratīcchā mātreṇa svarga kāma  iti bhavati tasmāt  puruṣam prati guṇa bhāvena na śrūyate svargaḥ tasmāt  saḥ  api na śeṣa bhūtaḥ na ced  phala yāgau guṇa bhāvena codyete kasya puruṣaḥ pradhāna bhūtaḥ  bhavati pratyakṣaḥ  ca asya dravya tvāt  karma prati guṇa bhāvaḥ tasmāt  dravya guṇa saṃskāreṣu  eva śeṣa bhāvam vādariḥ  mena iti jaimini s tu khalu  ācāryaḥ karmāṇi  api śeṣa bhūtāni manyate sma na vādariḥ  iva avadhāraṇām anumene sa hi dadarśa na yāgaḥ kartavya tayā codyate phala kāmasya tu tad sādhana upāya tvena iti evam śrutaḥ  arthaḥ parigṛhītaḥ  bhaviṣyati arthavānś ca upadeśaḥ enam eva artham ṣaṣṭhe adhyāye sūtraiḥ  eva sādhayiṣyati iha tu tad siddhena eva phala artha tvena śeṣa bhāvam yāgasya āpādayati sma tasmāt  anavadhāraṇā dravya guṇa saṃkārāḥ śeṣa bhūtāḥ yāgaḥ  api śeṣa bhūtaḥ phalam prati iti phalam api puruṣam pratyupadiśyate yaḥ svargaḥ  me bhavet  iti  evam kāmayate tasya yāgaḥ na yaḥ svargaḥ sa ātmānam labheta iti kutas  ātma nepada prayogāt  kartṛ abhiprāya etad  bhavati kriyā phalam anubhavet  katham puruṣa iti yāgaḥ prayujyate tasmāt  phalam puruṣa artham yāgāt  chrūyate na ātma nirvṛtti artham tasmāt  cheṣa bhūtam iti puruṣaḥ  api  audumbarī saṃmāna ādiṣu guṇa bhūtaḥ śrūyate tasmāt  anavadhāraṇā eṣā dravya guṇa saṃs kāreṣu śeṣa tvam vādariḥ  mena iti atha idānīm atra bhagavān vṛtti kāraḥ pariniścikāya dravya guṇa saṃskāreṣu  eva niyataḥ  yajim prati śeṣa bhāvaḥ āpekṣika itareṣām yāgasya dravyam prati pradhāna bhāvaḥ phalam prati guṇa bhāvaḥ phalasya yāgam prati prādhānyam puruṣam prati guṇa tā puruṣasya phalam prati pradhāna tā audumbarī saṃmāna ādi prati guṇa tvam tasmāt  saṃmata avadhāraṇā dravya guṇa saṃskārā yāgam prati niyogataḥ  guṇa bhūtā eva iti staḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti tatra śrūyante dharmāḥ nir vapaṇam prokṣaṇam avahananam iti evamādaya auṣadha dharmāḥ tathā utpavana vilāpa nayahaṇā sādana ādaya ājya dharmāḥ tathā śākhā haraṇam gavām prasthāpanam gavām prastāvanam iti evamādayaḥ  api sāntāyyasya teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim sarve auṣadhe ājye sānnāyye ca kartavyāḥ uta ye yatra kriyamāṇā arthavantaḥ te tatra kartavyā iti nanu saṃyuktā eva śrūyante yathā vrīhīn avahanti taṇḍulān pinaṣṭī iti bāḍham saṃyuktāḥ avaghāta ādayaḥ  tu padārthā vidhīyante śrutyā vākyena eṣām vrīhi ādi saṃyogaḥ atas  asti saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat  prāptam teṣām arthena saṃbandhaḥ arthena prayojanena ye yatra kriyamāṇāḥ prayojanavantaḥ te tatra kartavyāḥ prathana ādaya ājya sāntāyyayoḥ  anupakārakā iti na tatra karaṇīyāḥ evam utpavana ādaya auṣadha sānnāyyayoḥ śākhā āharaṇa ādaya ājya auṣadhayoḥ nanu śrūyante sarve sarvatra etad  eva na jānīmaḥ śrūyante na śrūyanta iti tad  vicārāyitavyam yadi  api śrūyaran tathā api  anupakāraka tvān na eva kartavyā bhaveyuḥ ucyate yaḥ  arthāt  prāptaḥ syāt  sa yatra prayojanam tatra eva kriyeta śabdena tu sarve amī padārthā vihitāḥ tena na yatra kevalam prayojanam pratyakṣam dṛśyate tatra eva kartavyā ah kva tarhi yatra yatra vihitāḥ te cāmī sarvatra vihitāḥ gamyante kutas  saṃyogataḥ  aviśeṣāt  prakaraṇa aviśeṣa āc ca sarveṣām tāvat  ājya auṣadha sānnāyyānām apūrveṇa sādhya sādhana saṃyogaḥ  aviśiṣṭaḥ yatra kriyamāṇā apūrvasya kṛtā bhavati iti vijñāyate tathā prakaraṇam aviśiṣṭam yasmin vihitāḥ sarveṣām vihitā bhavanti iti gamyate atas  sarve sarvatra kartavyāḥ yad  tu  amī na sarvatra upakurvanti iti vidhāna sāmarthyāt  sarvatra upakārakā iti gamyate sa ca ayam adṛṣṭa upakāraḥ  bhaviṣyati na etad  sarve sarvatra karaṇīyā iti ye yatra na upakurvanti na te tatra kriyām arhanti iti  uktam eva nanu vidhāna sāmarthyāt  sarve sarvatra upkariṣyanti na iti brūmaḥ na asti vidhānam yena sarve sarvatra upakurvanti na ca pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ  upakāram avagacchāmaḥ arthāpattiḥ  api niyogatas tatra eva bhavet  yatra eva śabena codanā bhavati na anyathā yadi ca prathana ādīnām ājyasān nāyyayoḥ  anupakurvatām api tad prakaraṇe samāmnāyaḥ  anupapannaḥ  bhavet  tatas  arthāt  adṛṣṭa upakāraḥ kalpyeta te tu  avaśyam samāmnānīyā auṣadha artham phalam hi saha ceṣṭayā avahanana ādikayā avagamyate tuṣa vimocana ādi prayojanam ca tena na tasmāt  ṛte puroḍāśaḥ sidhyati sati ca asmin   arthavān prakaraṇe samāmnāyaḥ arthavati ca tasmin na adṛṣṭa kalpanāyām pramāṇam asti iti  atas  na śakyam kalpayitum yadi ca tatra taṇḍula ādi niṣpādanam dṛṣṭam na abhaviṣyat tatas  viprayoge taṇḍula ādīnām abhāvāt  upakārasya śabda artha mātram dṛṣṭa upakāra anapekṣam kartavyam iti  ājyasān nāyyayoḥ  api kriyamāṇānām adṛṣṭam abhaviṣyat  tasmāt  na prathana ādayaḥ sarvatra evam utpavana ādayaḥ śākhā haraṇa āt ayaḥ  ca tasmāt  na sarve sarvtra kartavyāḥ prathanāt ayaḥ  na ājya sānnāyayyoḥ auṣadhe eva te utpavana ādaya ājyasya na auṣadha sānnāyyayoḥ śākhā haraṇa āt ayaḥ  ca sānnāyyasya na ājya auṣadhayoḥ  iti siddham staḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau tatra samāmananti sphyaḥ  ca kapālāni ca agnihotra havaṇī ca śūrpam ca kṛṣṇājinam ca śamyā ca ulūkhalam ca musalam ca dṛṣṭa c ca upalā ca etāni vai daśa yajñāyudhāni iti tatra saṃdihyate kim yaḥ  ya iha śakyata ebhiḥ kartum tasmai tasmai padārthāya etāni samāmnātāni uta yad  yena saṃyuktam tasmā eva iti kim tāvat  prāptam yad  yena śakyam iti kutas  evam vidhayaḥ  bhaviṣyanti tathā arthanvataḥ itarathā te anuvādā niṣprayojanāḥ prakaraṇa aviśeṣaḥ  ca sarva padārthān prati yajñāyudhāni iti ca yajña saṃyogaḥ  aviśiṣṭaḥ tasmāt  sarve sarvatra iti  evam prāptam evam prāpte brūmaḥ dravyam ca utpatti saṃyogāt  tad artham eva codyeta yaḥ  yena padārthena saha utpatti vākyena saṃyuktaḥ sa padārthaḥ tena eva kartavyaḥ yathā sphyena uddhanti iti  uddhana artha tā sphyasya vākyena tad  uddhaṇanam na sphyāt  anyena kartavyam yadā ca evam tadā prāpta eva sphyaḥ tasya ayam anuvādaḥ  bhavitum arhati etāni vai daśa yajña āyudhāni iti evam ekaisya anuvādaḥ tena tena vacanena prāptasya yathā kapāleṣu śrapayati agni hotra havaṇyā havīṃṣi nirvapati śūrpeṇa vivinakti kṛṣṇājinam adhastāt  ulūkhalasya avastṛṇāti śamyāyām dṛṣady upadadhāti ulūkhala musalābhyām avahanti dṛṣad upalābhyām pinaṣṭī iti prakaraṇāt  sarvāṇi sarvatra prāpnuyuḥ vacanāt  tu yathāvacanam yajña āyudha śabdaḥ  api sāmānyena prayojanam vidadhat  tad  vā adhyeta eva parokṣam hi sāmānya vacanena viśeṣa vidhānam bhavati pratyakṣam tu viśeṣa vacanena viśeṣa vidhānam tasmāt  yad  yena utpattyā saṃyuktam tad  tatra eva viniyujyata iti siddham jyotiṣṭome krayam prakṛtya śrūyate aruṇayā piṅga akṣya eka hāyanyā somam krīṇāti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim aruṇimā kṛtsna prakaraṇe niviśete uta kraya eva eka hāyanyām iti katham punar  aruṇayā krīṇāti iti  evam vispaṣṭe kraya saṃbandhe gamyamāne saṃśaya iti ucyate iha hi guṇam aruṇimānam amūrtam santam kriyāyāḥ karaṇam iti śabda upadiśati yad  karaṇa abhidhāyinyā tṛtīyā vibhaktyā saṃyujya nirdiśati aruṇayā iti na ca amūrtaḥ  arthaḥ kriyāyāḥ sādhanam bhavitum arhati atas  asam bandham krīṇātinā aruṇa guṇasya avagacchāmaḥ na ca aśaṅkanīyam artham pramāṇa bhūtaḥ śabdaḥ  abhidhāsyati iti  evam prakalpanā kadācid  upapadyeta api kenacid  prakāreṇa saṃbandha iti vacana prāmāṇya prakāra anveṣaṇe buddhiḥ  bhavati tad  yadi param vicārayantaḥ kriyā saṃbandha sāmarthyam avagamiṣyāmaḥ eka vākyatayā kraya eva aruṇi mānam niveśayiṣyāmaḥ atha tu  apramādyadbhiḥ  anviṣyamāṇaḥ  na kathaṃcana saṃbandha upapatsyate tatas  vākya bhedam abhyupagamya prakaraṇa dharmam enam adhyavasāsyāmaḥ tasmāt  avaśyam vicāraṇīyam etad  iti kim tāvat  prāptam kṛtsne prakaraṇe niveśaḥ kasmāt  saṃyogataḥ  aviśeṣāt  prakaraṇa aviśeṣa āc ca nanu prakaraṇāt  vākyam balīyaḥ  bhavati iti  eka vākya tvāt  aruṇimā krayeṇa saṃbhantsyata iti na etad  evam avagamyate na hi vacana śatena api  anāra bhyaḥ  arthaḥ śakyaḥ  vidhātum yaḥ  hi brūyāt  udakena dagdhavyam agninā kledayitavyam iti kim sa vacana prayojana sāmañjasyam aśnuvīta na ca amūrtaḥ  arthaḥ kriyāyāḥ sādhanam upapadyate tasmāt  aruṇayā krīṇāti iti saṃbandha abhāvāt  eka vākyatā na bhavati iti nanu na eva ayam guṇa vacanaḥ kim tarhi dravya vacanaḥ kutas  strī liṅga saṃbandhāt  dravya viśeṣā hi  ete strī pumān napuṃsakam iti strīyām yad  prātipadikam vartate tasmāt  strī pratyayaḥ bhavati iti strī pratyayam cāruṇayā iti  upalabhāmahe tasmāt  dravya vacanaḥ aruṇa śabda iti tad  etad  apeśa lam tad  eva hi dravyam aruṇimnā parichidyamānam aruṇa śabda abhidhānīyatām labhate tad  eva anya guṇakam na aruṇa śabdaḥ śaknoti  abhivaditum aruṇimānam eṣa śabdaḥ  na vyabhicarati vy abhicarati punar  dravyam avyabhicāri ca kāraṇam kāraṇavatām iṣṭam atas  asya guṇaḥ sva artha iti gamyate tad  asya pratyakṣataḥ guṇavacana tā gamyate strī pratyaya darśanāt  tu nūnam aruṇā prātipadikam dravya vacanam iti  anumānam pratyakṣam ca anumānāt  balīyaḥ tasmāt  guṇa vacanaḥ katham tarhi strī pratyaya saṃbandhaḥ bhavati hi guṇa vacanasya api strī liṅga tā yathā cāruṇā buddhiḥ evam aruṇa iti guṇa vacanaḥ  ced  krīṇātinā na saṃbadhyate tasmāt  vākya bhedam kṛtvā prakaraṇe sarvasmin   eva saṃniveśa iti atha yadi krīṇātinā na saṃbadhyate tasmin eva vākye eka hāyanī śabdena saṃbhantsyate na bhaviṣyati vākya bheda iti tad  na kevalam hi guṇam aruṇa śābdaḥ  abhidadhāti na dravya guṇau kevalam ca dravyam eka hāyanī śabdaḥ na guṇa sahitam iti tayoḥ saṃbandhasya vācikām ṣaṣṭhīm antareṇa katham saṃbandhaḥ  gamyate āha antareṇa api ṣaṣṭhīm eka vibhakti nirdeśāt sāmānādhikaraṇyam avagamiṣyāmaḥ yathā nīlam utpalam iti tad  anupapannam rūpāt  aruṇa śabdasya guṇavacana tā kalpanīyam tu  eka vibhakti saṃyogāt  eka hāyanī śabda saṃnidhāna āt  ca tad  eka vākyatām abhyupagamya eka hāyanī śabda sāmānādhikaraṇyam na ca liṅgāt  vākyam balīyaḥ tasmāt  asad etad  tatra ucyate yadā kevala guṇavacana tāyām śabdaḥ pravartamānaḥ  na anyena saṃbandham labhate tadā anupadeśaka tvāt  ānarthakyam mā bhūd iti dravya para tām āpadyate tasyām avasthāyām eka vibhakti yuktena eka hāyanī śabdena saṃnihitena eka vākyatām āpadyamānaḥ samāna adhikaraṇaḥ  bhavati tathā ca kṛtvā nīlam utpalam iti  upapadyate sa ca ayam aruṇā śabdas tasyām avasthāyām vartate na hi  asya sva artham abhidadhata itas  vicchinnasya prakaraṇe api  arthavat tā kutas  yena eva hetunā saṃbadhyate krīṇātinā na na amūrtaḥ  arthaḥ kriyāyāḥ sādhanam bhavati iti na ca kriyā sādhanaiḥ  dravyaiḥ na hi kevala guṇa vacanaḥ śaknoti dravyam abhidhātum iti sa eva hetuḥ prakaraṇa saṃbandha abhāve api tatra api saṃbadhyamānaḥ kriyābhiḥ  vā saṃbadhyeta tad sādhanaiḥ  vā dravyaiḥ tad  ca ubhayam api  anupapannam atas  anarthakatva parijihīrṣayā saṃnihitena eka hāyanī śabdena aruṇā śabdaḥ saṃbadhyate na asti vākya bhedaḥ na etad  evam na hi  ayam aruṇā śabda eka hāyanī viśeṣaṇam bhavitum arhati kim kāraṇam karaṇa vibhaktyā tṛtīyayā samuccaritaḥ  ayam tena etena tṛtīyā śruti sāmarthyāt kriyā viśeṣaṇena bhavitavyam kārakāṇām hi kriyayā saṃbandhaḥ  na dravyeṇa iti sa eṣa śruti sāmarthyāt  kriyā viśeṣaṇam eka vākya tvāt  eka hāyanī viśeṣaṇam śrutiḥ  ca vākyāt  balīyasī tasmāt  na asya ekahāyanī saṃbandha iti nanu ca guṇasya kriyā saṃbandha abhāvāt  avivakṣitā kāraka śaktiḥ  iti  eka hāyanī saṃbandhaḥ  ayam adhyavasitaḥ evam api na upapadyate yadi kāraka abhidhānam avivakṣitam iti guṇa śabdena etena dravyam abhidhātum iṣyate tadā prātipadikā arthasya avyatireka iti prathamā vibhaktiḥ prāpnoti na hi tṛtīya anta s tam abhisaṃbandham śaknoti vaktum na ca anyathā anupapattiḥ  iti  anyaḥ  asya anupapadyamānaḥ  arthaḥ śakyate kalpayitum yathā agnau tiṣṭhati māṇavaka iti  ukte jvalane anupapadyamānaḥ  na aśve gavi vā kalpyate agni samīpa vacana eva adhyavasīyate tadvat  iha api  aprathama antaḥ śabdaḥ  na kathaṃcid  api  avyatirikte prātipadikā arthe bhavitum arhati iti tasmāt  kāmam anartha kaḥ avagamyatām na asya ekahāyanī saṃbandhaḥ  adhyavasātavyaḥ āha na brūmaḥ na kārakam aruṇā śabdena abhidhīyata iti vyaktam aruṇa guṇa viśiṣṭam etena kārakam abhidhīyate kadācid  tu kiṃcid  vidhitsitam bhavati kadācid  upasarjanī bhūtaḥ  arthaḥ  vidhitsitaḥ pradhānībhūtaḥ  anuvādaḥ tad  yathā daṇḍī iti  upasarjanī bhūta daṇḍaka puruṣa pradhānakaḥ śabdaḥ  avagamyate kadācid  tu nirjñāte puruṣe daṇḍa guṇa vidhāna artham uccāryate daṇḍī praiṣā ananvāha iti tathā lohiteṣṇīṣā ṛtvijaḥ pracaranti iti evam iha api yadi  anupasarjana bhūtaḥ  aruṇaḥ  guṇaḥ pradhāna bhūtam kārakam tathā api  anūdite kārake aruṇa guṇa vidhāna artham vacanam yujyate tasmāt  eka hāyanī saṃbandha upapadyate na asti vākya bheda iti na etad  sāram atra hi  eka hāyanī krīṇātyoḥ  anavabuddham saṃbandham bodhayitum ayam eka hāyanī śabda uccaritaḥ sa eṣa katham iva aruṇa aśabena saṃbadhyte tad  etad  abhihitam api punar  punar  paryanuyujjyate katham punar  eka hāyanī śabdasya krīṇātinā aruṇa guṇena ca samāne samabhivyāhāre krīṇātinā saṃbandhaḥ  abhyupagamanīyaḥ na punar  āruṇyena iti śabda prāmāṇyāt  bhavati hi kriyā saṃbandhasya vācikā vibhaktiḥ  eka hāyanī śabdam anuniviṣṭā na tu guṇa saṃbandhasya vācikā kā punar  kriyā saṃbandhasya vācikā kā vā guṇa saṃbandhasya iti kāraka lakṣaṇā kriyā saṃbandhe vivakṣite bhavati dvitīya ādiḥ avivakṣite punar  kārake saṃbandha mātra vivakṣāyām ṣaṣṭhī na ca atra ṣaṣṭīm paśyāmaḥ paśyāmas tu khalu tṛtīyām atas  krīṇātinā saṃbandham abhyupagacchāma eka hāyanī śabdasya na aruṇā śabdena iti katham tarhi bhavati  atra saṃbandhaḥ nīlam uta palam iti ucyate bhavati na tu śruti lakṣaṇaḥ kim tu vākya lakṣaṇaḥ utpala śabda saṃnidhāne tad apekṣī nīla śabdas tena eka vākyatām abhyupagacchan na ajahat  sva artha vṛttiḥ  upala viśeṣa abhidhāna para uccāryamāṇaḥ saṃbandham abhyupaiti nanu  iha api vākya lakṣaṇa s tadvat  eva aruṇimnā samam saṃbandha eka hāyanyā yujyate na iti brūmaḥ śrutiḥ  hi vākyāt  balīyasī śrutiḥ  ca asyāḥ kriyā saṃbandham āha na guṇa saṃbandham yadi punar  śruti sāmarthyāt  kriyā saṃbandhaḥ  abhyupagamyeta eka vākyatavat  api guṇa saṃbandhaḥ na evam śakyam yaḥ  hi  anyena saha saṃbandhum uccāryate na tad samīpa gataḥ  api  anyas tena saha saṃbanddhum arhati yathā bhāryā rājñaḥ puruṣaḥ  devadattasya iti bhāryā viśeṣaṇa artham uccāryamāṇaḥ  rāja śabdaḥ  na puruṣeṇa saṃbadhyate tadvat  iha krayā viśeṣaṇa artham uccāryamāṇa  eka hāyanī śabdaḥ  na aruṇā śabdena saṃbandham arhati āha satyam evam etad  asatyām ākāṅkṣāyām ānantaryam akāraṇam sarvatra tu bodhite padārthe vākya artha upapadyate na anyathā sāmānya vṛtti hi padam viśeṣa vṛtti vākyam sāmānyena abhipravṛttānām padārthānām yad  viśeṣe avasthānam sa vākya arthaḥ tad  etad  uktam tad bhūtānām kriyā arthena samāmnāyaḥ  arthasya tad nimitta tvāt  iti tatra pratyakṣataḥ padārthaḥ vākya arthaḥ punar  ānumānikaḥ tad  etad  avagamyatām kevala sva artha vṛtti padam anupadeśakam iti pada antareṇa saṃnihitena eka vākya tvam abhyupaiti na anyathā iti tad  iha yadi  api  eka hāyanī śabdaḥ krīṇātinā saṃbandhyamānaḥ kṛtārthaḥ  na pada antareṇa saṃbandham ākāṅkṣati aruṇā śabdas tu pada antareṇa saṃbandham alabhamānaḥ  anarthaka iti  eka hāyanī śabdena eka vākyatām abhyupaiti nanu uktam kriyā saṃbandha arthaḥ na aruṇa asaṃbandha artha iti āha aruṇā śabdasya anarthakya parihārāya ubhaya saṃbandha artha iti vadāmaḥ anya artham api kṛtam anya artham api śaknoti kartum tad  yathā śāli artham kulyāḥ praṇīyante tābhyaś ca pānīyam pīyata upaspṛśyate ca evam iha api kraya saṃbandha artham eka hāyanī śabda uccāryamāṇaḥ  aruṇā śabdena saha saṃbhantyate na kiṃcid  duṣyati tasmāt  na vākya bheda iti na etad  asti yadi  api  ayam aruṇā śabdaḥ  anartha kaḥ  mā bhūd iti  eka hāyanyā saṃbadhyeta tathā api sarvasmin prakaraṇe niveṣṭum arhati na ca enam somam krīṇāti iti  eṣa śabdaḥ śaknoti viśeṣṭum na hi  ayam viśeṣaṇa tvena ucāryate kim tarhi apūrva u ayam vidhīyate nanu  apūrva u api vidhīyamāna eka hāyanī śabdavat  itareṇa saṃbhantsyate katham prayojanāya hi  uccāryamāṇaḥ śabdaḥ  yena arthaḥ tasmai tāvat  prayojanāya avakalpyate saṃnihit ś ca buddhau bhavati tena buddhau saṃnihitena śakyate sa ākāṅkṣaḥ śabdaḥ saṃbandhayitum iti na etad  evam yaḥ  hi  asaṃbadhyamānaḥ  anartha kaḥ  bhavati sa saṃbadhyate na anyaḥ kuta etad  saṃbadhyamāne hi sāmānyam viśeṣe avasthāpyeta tatra vākyena śrutiḥ pīḍitā syāt  na ca ayam asaṃbadhyamānaḥ krīṇātinā anartha kaḥ bhavati prakaraṇa gatābhiḥ eka hāyanībhiḥ  abhisaṃbhantsyate nanu  etad  uktam prakaraṇe api  asya saṃbandhaḥ  anupapanna iti na anupapannaḥ ekasmin vākye anyaḥ  arthaḥ  vidhīyamānaḥ  na anyena saṃbadhyate vacana vyakti bhedāt  anyā hi vacana vyaktiḥ  vidhīyamānasya anyā guṇena saṃbadhyamānasya ajñāta vaj jñāpyate vidhīyamānaḥ  arthaḥ jñātavat  anūdyate guṇa saṃbandha artham na ca sakṛt  uccāryamāṇaḥ  jñātavat  ajñātavat  ca bhavitum arhati eka hāyanī śabdaḥ kraye vidhīyamānaḥ  ajñātavat  syāt  aruṇā śabdena saṃbadhyamānaḥ  ca jñatavat  vākya bhede punar  na doṣaḥ  bhavati prakaraṇe tu vākya antaraiḥ kriyā dravya antarāṇī ca prāptāni taiḥ  idam vākya antara vihitam saṃbadhyate tatra anyasmin vidhīyate anyasmin vākye anūdyata iti  upa pannam bhavati tasmāt  saṃyogataḥ  aviśeṣāt  prakaraṇa aviśeṣa āc ca sarvasmin prakaraṇe dravyeṣu niveśa iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ artha eka tve dravya guṇayoḥ  aika karmyān niyamaḥ syāt  iti yatra artha eka tvam śrūyate dravya guṇayoḥ tatra dravya guṇau   ekasmin padārthe niyamya īyātām kutas  aika karmyāt  eka kārya tvāt ekam hi kāryam dravya guṇayoḥ śrūyate kraya saṃbandhaḥ katham etad  avagamyate eka vākya tvāt  katham eka vākya tvam aruṇayā piṅga akṣya ekahāyanyā iti  aparyavasitaḥ  arthaḥ sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt  abhidhātṛ pratipatroḥ somam krīṇāti iti tu paryavasyati tayoḥ  evam naiḥ utsukyāt  yadi  eka kārya tā kim iti vikalpaḥ  na bhavati na etad  evam eka artha aḥ  tu vikalperan   iti vikalpa dharmāṇau prāpnuta iti  ayuktaḥ  ayam paryanuyogaḥ katham paryanuyogaḥ  nāma sa bhavati yaḥ sva pakṣam sādhayati vipakṣasya ca pratīpam ācarati na ca vikalpaḥ  asmad pakṣasya pratīpam ācarati krayeṇa aruṇim āsaṃbandha iti  eṣa naḥ pakṣaḥ na ca vikalpaḥ  nānā kārya tvāt nanu  idānīm eva uktam ekam kāryam iti tad  ca api viruddham evam hi pūrvam abhihitam amūrta tvād guṇa u na kriyayā saṃbadhyata iti idānīm viparītam abhidhīyate ubhau   api dravya guṇau   eka arthau krayam abhinirvartayata iti ucyate na etad  viruddham na ca vikalpaḥ ekam kāryam sāmarthya bhedas tu sākṣāt  dhi dravyam kriyām pratyupakaroti guṇa s tu viśiṣṭānām sādhanam yadi  evam na tarhi guṇaḥ kriyām abhinirvartayati sādhanasya asau viśeṣaka iti na etad  evam guṇasya kriyām abhinirvartayata etad  eva sāmarthyam yad  sādhanam viśiṣyāt  ākāṅkṣati ca kriyā sādhana viśeṣaṇam cihna bhūtaḥ  hi guṇaḥ sādhanam lakṣayati asati cihne na lakṣyeta katamat  sādhanam kriyāyāḥ  iti tatas  kriyā na adhyavasyema kartum iti bhavati kriyā sādhanam gunaḥ na ca eva sati vikalpaḥ  bhavati yathā adhikaraṇasya kartṛ ādīnām ca adhikaraṇam hi kartṛ ādīni dhārayati tāni  adhāryamāṇāni na śaknuvanti kriyām abhinirvartayitum tathā kartā karaṇa ādīni samādhatte tāni  asamāhitāni na śaknuvanti svam svam artham abhinirvartayitum yasmin   tu sādhana upakāre kārye tasmin   eva upakāre anyat  sādhanam vidhīyate tatra vikalpaḥ yathā vrīhim iryajeta yavaiḥ  yajeta iti ubhaye api taṇḍula nirvṛti arthāḥ evam tarhi tad  eva idam saṃjātam bhavati eka hāyanī vidhanam tad viśeṣaṇam cāruṇaḥ  guṇaḥ tatra sa eva doṣaḥ  vākya bhedaḥ prasajjyeta iti na brūmaḥ aruṇā śabda eka hāyanī śabdena saṃbadhyata iti kim tarhi krīṇātinā eva saṃbadhyate evam hi śrūyate aruṇa guṇena krayam abhinirvartayet  iti yathā ca tena nirvartyate tathā yatitavya bhavati na ca aviśiṃṣan sādhanam guṇaḥ kriyā m abhinivartayati iti  arthāt  sādhana viśeṣaṇa tām pratipadyate yathā sthālyām pacet  iti kriyā sādhana tvena nirdiṣṭe arthāt  saṃbhavane dhāraṇe ca syālīm vyāpārayati tadvat  iha api draṣṭavyam tasmāt  na asti vākya bheda prasaṅga iti nanu  evam api vākyam bhidyeta katham pratyekam vākya parisamāptiḥ  dṛṣṭā iti yathā deva datta yajñadatta viṣṇu mitrā bhojyantām iti pratyekam bhujiḥ samāpyate yathā ca yasya pitā pitāmahaḥ somam na pivet  iti evam iha api  aruṇayā krīṇāti eka hāyanyā krīṇāti iti na etad  asmad pakṣasya bādhakam evam api kraya eva aruṇimā nivekṣyati na sarvasmin prakaraṇa iti satyam eṣa doṣaḥ  na bhavati kim tu  anaruṇayā api  eka hāyanyā krayaḥ prāpnoti aruṇayā ca aneka hāyanyā tatra yad  uktam dravya guṇayoḥ  niyama iti sā pratijñā hīyate na tarhi brūmaḥ vākya bheda iti katham krayasya hi dravya aruṇi mānau   upadiśyete na krayas tayoḥ na ca pradhānam pratiguṇam bhidyate pratipradhānam hi guṇa u bhidyata iti asti ca ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ samudāye vākya parisamāptiḥ  iti yathā gargāḥ śatam daṇḍyantām iti tathā abhiṣutya hutvā bhakṣāyanti iti tasmāt  ubhaya viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭaḥ krayaḥ vidhīyate katham punar  tasmin   cetariṃś ca dṛṣṭānte sati  ekāntena avadhāryate samudāya eva vākya parisamāptiḥ  na pratyavayavam iti atra brūmaḥ iha dravya aruṇi mānau   ubhau   api kriyā saṃbaddhau   upalabhyete paraspareṇa asaṃbaddhau krayaḥ api dravya aruṇimābhyām viśiṣṭa upalabhyate na anyayatareṇa tatra yadi dravya param aruṇim aparam ca bhavati vacanam idam tatas  pratyavayavam asaṃśayam kraya saṃbandhaḥ atha kraya vidhitsayā abhidhīyate tatas  yathā eva ayam eka hāyanī vi śiṣṭaḥ evam aruṇim aviśiṣṭa iti niyamata ubhaya saṃbandhaḥ  abhyupagamanīyaḥ na ca atra dravya aruṇi mānau   īpsitau īpsita s tu krayaḥ tena hi jyotiṣṭoma dravyam somaḥ pariprāpyate dravya aruṇi mānau kraya arthau santau   īpsitau syātām na anyathā tasmāt  krayaḥ vidhīyate sa ca na anyatara viśiṣṭaḥ pratīyata iti samudāye vākya parisamāptiḥ  iha niścīyate yadā ca evam tadā na eka hāyanīm muktvā anyat  dravyam kraya sādhanam asti na cāruṇād anyaḥ sādhanasya viśeṣa kaḥ  guṇa iti niyamaḥ siddhaḥ  bhavati atra vadāmaḥ yadi krayasya sādhane guṇa u abhisaṃbandhum upaiti tadā vākye bhinne api kraya sa adhana tvāt  aruṇimā asmin dravye na nivekṣyate kim artham eka vākyatā prayatnena sādhyata iti tad  etad  abhidhīyate bhinne hi vākya ekāhāyanī sādhanakaḥ krayaḥ avabuddhaḥ  bhavati aruṇā sādhanam api kraya antaram na tasmin   eva eka hāyanī sādhane kraye aruṇimā vihitaḥ  bhavati tatra yad  kraya antaram aruṇa guṇa viśiṣṭam tatra arthāt  prāptam anyat  api sādhanam bhavati tad  api viśiṃṣan aruṇaḥ  guṇa s tena saṃbadhyeta eka vākya tve tu tad  parihṛtam bhavati tasmāt  sādhv abhidhīyate artha eka tve dravya guṇayoḥ  aika karmyān niyamaḥ syāt  iti asti jyotiṣṭomaḥ ya evam vidvān somena yajata iti tatra śrūyate daśā pavitreṇa graham saṃārṣṭi iti tathā agnihotre srūyate agneḥ  tṛṇāni  apacinoti iti tathā darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate puroḍāśam paryagnikaroti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ekasya grahasya ekasya agneḥ ekasya puroḍāśasya ca saṃmārjana ādi kartavyam uta sarveṣām grahāṇām sarveṣām agnīnām sarveṣām puroḍāśānām iti kim prāptam ekaḥ  grahaḥ ekaḥ  agniḥ ekaḥ puroḍāśa iha grahītavyaḥ kutas  śruti saṃyogāt  ekatva śruti saṃyuktā ete padārthāḥ ekam hi dravyam eṣa śrūyate śabda lakṣaṇe ca hi karmaṇi yad  chabda āha tad  asmākam pramāṇam yathā paśum ālabheta iti  ukta eka eva paśuḥ pumānś ca ālabhyate evam atra api  ekaḥ  grahaḥ saṃmārjanīyaḥ ekasya agneḥ  tṛṇāni  apaceyāni ekaḥ puroḍāśaḥ paryagnikartavya iti na etad  asti yad  uktam graha ādiṣu  ekatva yukteṣu  amī padārthāḥ kartavyā iti sarve grahāḥ saṃmārṣṭavyāḥ sarvebhyaḥ  agnibhyaḥ  tṛṇāni  apaceyāni puroḍāśa mātram ca paryagnikartavyam iti kutas  graha jātyā dravyam lakṣayitvā saṃmārga ādi vidhīyate aviśiṣṭam ca lakṣaṇam sarva dravyeṣu tatra na gamyate viśeṣaḥ kaḥ  grahaḥ saṃmārṣṭavyaḥ kaḥ  na iti sāmānya avagamāt  viśeṣān avagamāt  ca sarva pratyayaḥ tathā agni puroḍāśānām api nanu  eka vacanam śrūyate tad  viśekṣyati na etad  asti eka tvam hi śrūyamāṇam graha ādiṣu  eka tvam brūyāt  na dvitīya ādīn pratiṣedhet  eka tvasya asau vācakaḥ  na dvitīya ādeḥ pratiṣedhakaḥ tena apratiṣiddhe dvitīya ādau sāmānya vacanena prāptam saṃmārjana ādi kim iti na kriyeta tatra etad  syāt  eka vacanam iha śrūyamāṇam prāpta eva ekasmin dravye dvitīya ādiṣu ca kim anyat  kuryāt  anyatas  parisaṃkhyāyāḥ na ced  eka vacanam parisaṃcakṣīta dvitīya ādīn anarthakam eva syāt  śaknoti ca dvitīya ādīn nivartayitum yathā aśva abhidhānīm ādatta iti gardabha abhidhānam parisaṃcaṣṭe evam atra api draṣṭavyam iti na etad  evam tatra mantrasya abhidhānyāḥ  ca yaḥ saṃbandhaḥ tad  abhidhāna param vacanam imām agṛbhṇān iti  aśva abhidhānīm iti na anena mantreṇa ādatta iti liṅgena eva ādāne prāpta tvān mantrasya parisaṃkhyā yuktā iha punar  yad  eka vacanam dravye śrūyate tad  chrūyamāṇam api  avidhīyamāna tvena na nivartakam bhavitum arhati yathā kaścid  odanam nirdiśya brūyāt  ya enam bhakṣayet  kaścid  chvā mārjāraḥ  vā sa nivārayitavya iti tatra yadi bhakṣaṇam nimitta tvena vidhīyate na śva mārjāra saṃbandhaḥ tatas  kākaḥ api  āgacchan nivāryate śrūyamāṇe api śuni mārjāre vā śva mārjāra saṃbandhasya nimitta tvena avidhīyamāna tvāt  evam iha api  ekatva saṃbandhasya avidhīyamāna tvāt  chrūyamāṇe api  ekatve graha mātram saṃmṛjyeta iti na ca atra dravya ekatva saṃbandha vidhāyakaḥ kaścid  chabdaḥ  asti nanu saṃmārṣṭi iti na hi  etad  dravya ekatva saṃbandhasya vidhāyakam kasya tarhi dravya saṃmārga saṃbandhasya vidhāyakam evam śrutyā sva padārthaḥ  vihitaḥ  bhavati itarathā vākyena para padārthaḥ  vidhīyate śruti asaṃbhave ca vākyam kramate na saṃbhavantyām śrutau atas  avidhīyamānam viśeṣaṇa tvena eka tvam na dvitīya ādīn pratiṣeddhum arhati evam sati na dvitīya ādau saṃmārga ādi kriyamāṇam acoditam bhavati pratiṣiddham vā yathā eva hi tad  ekasya śrutam avagamyate tathā dvitīya ādeḥ  api ayam ca aparaḥ  doṣaḥ na tad  eka tvam dravyasya saṃmārga ādau viṣaye niyamyeta na hi saṃmārga ādiḥ yasmin dravya eka tvam niyamyeta tasya viśeṣaṇa tvena bhavati vidhīyate hi  atra saṃmārga ādiḥ na prāptaḥ  lakṣaṇa tvena dravyasyāmnāyate na hi yaugapadyena vidhātum śakyate lakṣaṇa tvena coc cārayitum prasiddha saṃbandhaḥ  hi śaknoti lakṣayitum na ca avihita evaṃjātīyakaḥ śabdau  agamyaḥ prasiddha saṃbandhaḥ  bhavati vidhīyate ca saṃmārga ādiḥ tasmāt  na viśeṣakaḥ na ced  viśeṣakaḥ na dravya eka tvam niyamyata iti śakyam āśrayitum atha eka tvam saṃmārga ucyate tatra api dvayī gatiḥ syāt  eka tvam pradhānam saṃmārgaḥ  vā tad  ca ubhayam api  anupapannam na tāvat  eka tvasya saṃmārgaḥ śākyate kartum na ca dravye kriyamāṇa  eka tvasya upakaroti kenacid  prakaraṇam na ca eka tvasya upakṛtena kiṃcid  prayojanam asti na hi tad  guṇa bhūtam śrutam atha eka tvam saṃmārgam prati guṇa bhūtam iti tad  api na katham amūrta tvāt  na hi tad  saṃmārgam niṣpādayati yadi  api  anyat  amūrtam kriyām niṣpādayati sādhanam viśiṃṣat  tathā api  etad  na bhavitum arhati na hi  atra grahaḥ saṃmārga arthaḥ saṃmārgaḥ  atra grahāya codyate sa hi prayojanavān kalpya prayojanaḥ saṃmārgaḥ yadi grahaḥ saṃmārgasya upakuryāt  tad  upakāriṇa upakaroti iti saṃmārgasya upakārakam eka tvam bhavet  na tu  etad  evam tasmāt  ekatva saṃmārgayoḥ  asaṃbandhaḥ nanu pradhāna bhutam api graha ādi saṃmārgam niṣpādayati  eva atas tad sādhanam tad  ca viśiṃṣat  tad  upakariṣyati yathā ijyā arthe dadhani payasi ca praṇītā dharmāḥ pāka upakurvanti paridhāna arthe ca paridau yūpa dharmā bandhane tasmāt  ayam asamādhiḥ  iti atra ucyate na brūmaḥ atad arthe sādhake na śaknuvanti  upakartum iti kim tarhi yadā pradhāna bhūtam graha ādi lakṣaṇa tvena ucyate na tadā ekatvasya graha ādinā saṃbandhaḥ na saṃmārga ādinā iti katham yāvat  iha lakṣaṇa tvena kiṃcid  ucyate saṃvādas tatra bhavati na tu tad vidhīyate vijñānāya kim artham tarhi  uccāryate anyat  tasya kiṃcid  vidhāyiṣyata iti tad  etad  graha ādi lakṣayitvā tasya saṃmārga ādi vidhīyate tad  yadi  ekatva saṃbandhaḥ  aparaḥ  graha dravye saṃmārga ādau vā padārthe vidhīyeta dvayoḥ saṃbandhayoḥ  vidhānāt  bhidyeta vākyam atha ucyeta graha ādi lakṣayitvā tasya ekatva saṃbandhaḥ  vidhīyate na saṃmārga ādi saṃbandha iti tathā ca saṃmārga ādīnām adhyayanam pramāda iti  abhyupagatam syāt  na ca etad  evam tasmāt  ubhābhyām eka vacanasya asaṃbandha iti evam etad  eka tvam grahasya na kiṃcid  upakāram karoti na saṃmārgasya evam eva sadanūdyate tasmāt  na etad  kiṃcid  api kartum vivakṣyata iti sarveṣām graha ādīnām saṃmārga ādi kartavyam iti kutas  saṃyogataḥ  aviśeṣāt  prakaraṇa aviśeṣa āc ca yadi  avivakṣitam eka tvam katham trahy eka vacanam uccāryate nanu bahuṣu vivakṣiteṣu bahuvacanena bhavitavyam ucyate na vayam etad  vicārayāmaḥ eka vacanam uccārayitavyam na uccārayitavyam iti uccāryamāṇe sati kim pratipattavyam ekasmin   eva saṃmārga ādi uta sarveṣu  iti tad  ca sarveṣu  iti sthāpitam api ca na vibhakteḥ  vacanam eva ekam prayojanam kim tarhi kāraka saṃbandhaḥ  api avivakṣita ekatve kāraka saṃbandha artham asya uccāraṇam bhaviṣyati tasmāt  na anarthakam api ca grahaḥ prātipadikā artha eka tvam vibhakti arthaḥ kim atas  yadi  evam etad  atas  bhavati prātipadikā artha gatam hi vibhaktiḥ svam artham śrutyā eva vadati atha evam sati kim na saṃmārgeṇa saṃbhantsyata iti tena hi saṃbadhyamānam vākyena saṃbadhyeta na ca śrutyā anyena saṃbadhyamānam vākyena acchidya an yena saṃbandham arhati asaṃbadhyamāna s tu  eka tvena saṃmārgaḥ yadi na ekatva viśiṣṭaḥ kriyate na kiṃcid  vipannam bhavati na ca ekatva viśiṣṭaḥ saṃmārga ādiḥ graha ādi mātrasya ca vidhīyata iti kim iti dvitīyasya tṛtīyasya ca na kriyeta iti atha yad  uktam yathā paśum ālabheta iti  eka eva paśuḥ puṃpaśuś ca ālabhyate evam idam api iti asti  atra vaiparītyam iha graha arthaḥ saṃmārgaḥ tatra punar  yāga arthaḥ paśuḥ kim evam sati bhavati yaḥ  yāga artham paricchinati sa yāgasya upakaroti aparicchinnena na śakyaḥ  yāgaḥ kartum iti na tu graheṇa kenacid  viśiṣṭena saṃmārgaḥ kartavyaḥ yad  graham viśiṃṣat  saṃmārgasya upkuryāt  paśoḥ  ca etad  eka tvam yāgam pratyupadiśyate nanu uktam prātipadikā artha gatam svam artham vibhaktiḥ śrutyā eva abhivadati iti yāga etad  vākyena vidhāsyati tatra vākyāt  chrutiḥ  balīyasi iti  uktam satyam yatra śrautaḥ  abhisaṃbandhaḥ  vivakṣyate avivakṣyamāṇe ca vākya avagataḥ san aparyudasitavyaḥ  bhavati tasmāt  ekaḥ puṃpaśuś ca alabhyata iti graha eka tvam na saṃmārgasya upakaroti iti na graham śaknoti viśeṣṭum tasmāt  avivakṣitam iti asti jyotiṣṭomaḥ tatra śrūyate daśā pavitreṇa graham saṃmārṣṭi iti tatra eṣaḥ  arthaḥ  adhigataḥ sarve grahāḥ saṃmārjitavyā iti idam idānīm saṃdihyate kim camasā api saṃmārṣṭavyā uta na iti kim tāvat  prāptam camasa ādi  api sarvam saṃmārjyam iti kutas  saṃyogataḥ  aviśeṣāt  prakaraṇa aviśeṣa āc ca iti yathā eva hi grahāṇām apūrva saṃbandhaḥ evam camasānām api yathā eva ca grahā asmin prakaraṇe evam camasā api tasmāt  sarvatra saṃmārgaḥ nanu grahāḥ śrūyante te camasānām nirvartakā bhaviṣyanti ucyate pradarśana artham graha grahaṇam bhaviṣyati graha ādi soma pātram yasmin gṛhyamāṇaḥ somaḥ  vyavasicyeta iti  evam āśaṅkyate tad  sarvam saṃmārjitavyam yathā bhojana kālaḥ  vartate sthālāni saṃmṛjyantām iti  ukte yāni yāni bhojana upayogam arhanti tāni tāni sarvāṇi saṃmṛjyante sthāla grahaṇam lakṣaṇa artham iti gamyate evam iha api draṣṭavyam iti ucyate loke artha lakṣaṇaḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ yena yena arthaḥ saṃmṛṣṭena uktaḥ  anuktaḥ  vā sa sa saṃmṛjyeta eva iha tu vede śabda lakṣaṇaḥ śabdaḥ  ca grahasya saṃmārgam āha tatra kim artham śrutau saṃbhavantyām graha śabdaḥ  lakṣaṇayā kalpyate ucyate saṃmārṣṭi iti saṃmārge puruṣa prayatnam vidhātum eṣa śabdaḥ śaknoti śravaṇena eva graha saṃbandhe tu vākyena śrutiḥ  ca vākyāt  balīyasī tasmāl lakṣaṇayā graha śabdaḥ  varṇyate na yathāśruta iti tena yaḥ  yaḥ saṃmārjana saṃskāra arhaḥ sa sa saṃmārjitavyaḥ na iti graheṣu  eva vyavatiṣṭheta evaṃjātīyakaḥ  guṇa iti vyavatiṣṭheta vā graheṣu  eva saṃmārgaḥ na camaseṣu  api prasajyeta iti kutas  arthasya śruti saṃyogāt  śrūyamāṇaḥ  hi grahaḥ  na utsraṣṭavyaḥ utsṛjyamāne śrutiḥ  eva bādhyate graham iti pramatta gītam tatra bhavatām iti  avagamyate na ca etad  nyāyyam tasmāt  graha śabdena graham lakṣayitvā tasya saṃmārga saṃbandhaḥ  vidhīyate na ca avidadhat  saṃmārgam śaknoti tad saṃbandham vidhātum atas  vidadhāti  eva eṣa śabdaḥ saṃmārgam na ca śrutiḥ  bādhiṣyate kutas  saṃmārṣṭi iti saṃmṛji gatam puruṣa prayatnam śrutyā śaknoti vidhātum na tatra kaścid  viśeṣaḥ utpādyamāne vā saṃmṛjau pareṇa vā saṃbadhyamāna iti tena na graha saṃbandhe api śrutiḥ  bādhitā bhavati atas  graheṣu  eva saṃmārgaḥ  vyavasthātum arhati iti nanu  apūrva saṃyoga aviśeṣāt prakaraṇa aviśeṣa āc ca camaseṣu  api prasajyate na graheṣu  eva asya vidhānam iti  uktam atra ucyate prakaraṇavadbhiḥ  eka vākyatām kṛtvā śaknoti tatra vidhātum na akṛtvā eka vākyatām sā ca prakaraṇāt  anumīyate iyam punar  graha śabdena saha pratyakṣā tasmāt  na prakaraṇe vidhānam graha ekatva saṃbandhe punar  utsṛjya sva artham na śaknoti vidhātum tasmāt  vaiṣamyam asya graha ekatva vidhānena yad  uktam yathā sthālāni saṃmṛjyantām iti lakṣaṇā tadvat  iha api iti parihṛtam etal loke karma artham lakṣaṇam śabda lakṣaṇam punar  veda iti vājapeye śrūyate saptadaśa aratniḥ  vājapeyasya yūpaḥ  bhavati iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim saptadaśa aratni tā vājapeyasya ūrdhva pātre niviśate uta paśoḥ  yūpe niviśata iti kim tāvat  prāptam ūrdhva pātra iti kutas  vājapeyasya yūpa abhāvāt yad  vājapeyasya asti pātram yūpa sadṛśam tatra bhavitum arhati asti ca ṣoḍaśi pātram tad  ca khādira tvāt  ūrdhva tvāt  ca yūpa sadṛśam tatra niveśe sati vājapeya śabda āñjasyena bhavati itarathā vājapeya aṅga paśu yāge lakṣaṇayā vājapeya śabdaḥ  vṛtta iti gamyate nanu tvad pakṣe api yūpa śabdaḥ  lakṣaṇayā ūrdhva pātre ucyate sarvathā vayam lakṣaṇā śabdān na mucyāmahe mad pakṣe tu vājapeya prakaraṇam anugṛhyate tasmāt  ūrdhva pātre niveśa iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ānarthakyāt  tad aṅgeṣu vājapeya śabda s tāvat  soma yāga viśeṣa vacanaḥ tasya sākṣāt  yūpena na prayojanam asti tu tasya aṅgam paśu yāgaḥ tasya tu paśum bandhum yūpena kāryam sākṣāt  vājapeya yūpasya yadi saptadaśa aratni tā vidhīyate tasya abhāvāt  anarthakam eva vacanam prāpnoti tad  anarthakam mā bhūd iti yaḥ  asya paśu yāge yūpaḥ tatra niveśam arhati ūrdhva pātre ca yūpa śabdaḥ  lakṣaṇayā syāt  nanu  itarasmin   api pakṣe vājapeya śabdaḥ  lakṣaṇayā iti na iti brūmaḥ vājapeya eva vājapeya śabdaḥ  bhaviṣyati śakṣyati ca sa paśu yūpam viśeṣṭum saḥ  asya aṅgasya upakārakaḥ yaḥ  ca yasya upakāriṇa upakaroti bhavati sa tasya saṃbaddhaḥ  mukhyena eva saṃbandhena na ca eka antaritam iti kṛtvā asaṃbaddhaḥ  bhavati yathā devadattasya naptā iti putreṇa ca asau   antaritaḥ atha ca devadattena mukhyena eva saṃbandhena saṃbaddhaḥ tasmāt  eṣa eva pakṣa āśrayaṇīyaḥ na hi  etasmin pakṣe kaścid  api lakṣaṇa śabdaḥ  bhavati iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ prayāja vākye śrūyate abhikrāmam juhoti  abhijitya iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim abhikramaṇam prayājeṣu  eva niviśata uta kṛtsne prakaraṇa iti kim tāvat  prāptam kartṛ guṇe abhikramaṇe brūmaḥ vākya bhedaḥ syāt  iti karmaṇā karmaṇaḥ  asamavāyāt  abhikramaṇam karma amūrtam na tad  karma havanam sādhayitum śaknoti tasmāt  na tena eka vākyatām yāti atas  sarvasmin prakaraṇe niviśate saṃyogataḥ  aviśeṣāt  prakaraṇa aviśeṣa āc ca iti nanu  anena eva hetunāni asmin   api na nivekṣyate ucyate anyatra puruṣaiḥ saṃbhantsyate nanu prayājeṣu  api puruṣaiḥ saṃbadhyeta na etad  evam juhḥti iti havana eṣa śabdaḥ puruṣa prayatnam vidhātum śaknoti na puruṣa abhikramaṇa asaṃbandham nanu  anyatra api puruṣa abhikramaṇa saṃbandhasya avidhānam na eṣa doṣaḥ anyatra prakaraṇāmnānād aṅga bhāve nirjñāte prayoga vacanaḥ  asya kartavyatām vakṣyati tasmāt  sarvasmin prakaraṇe abhikramaṇasya niveśa iti na etad  asti yad  uktam abhikramaṇam prakaraṇe niviśata iti prayā jeṣu  eva bhavitum arhati kutas  taiḥ saha asya eka vākyatā yatas  sa ākāṅkṣam etad  pūrveṇa padena asamāptam vākyam abhikrāmam juhoti iti  atra paryavasyati prakaraṇa āc ca vākyam balavat  iti prayājeṣu  eva abhikramaṇam niviśate nanu  abhikramaṇam amūrta tvāt  dhoma nirvṛttau   asamartham iti  uktam ucyate sākṣāt  asamartham kartrā saṃbadhyamānam śakṣyati nirvartayitum katham abhikramaṇena samāsīdati  āhavanīyam kartā dvayam abhyupāya bhūtam homasya dūrāt  vā abhiprasārya hastam juhuyāt  samāsīdet  anvābhikramaṇena tasmāt  abhikramaṇam upakaroti homasya iti  avagamyate atas  prayājeṣu  eva niveśa iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ saptama aṣṭamayoḥ  brāhmaṇa anuvākayoḥ sāmidhenya uktāḥ navame nividaḥ daśame kāmyāḥ sāmidhenī kalpāḥ idam kāmasya etāvatīḥ  anubrūyāt  idam kāmasya etāvatīḥ  iti ekādaśe ca yajñopavītam āmnātam upavyayate deva lakṣmam eva tad  kuruta iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim sāmidhenīḥ  eva anubruvāṇa upavyayeta uta prakaraṇe sarvān eva padārthān anutiṣṭhatā upavyātavyam iti kutas  saṃśayaḥ upavītam sāmidhenīnām prakaraṇe samāmnātam atha nivṛtte vā tāsām prakaraṇa iti na jñāyate nanu darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  eva prakaraṇam idam para prakaraṇe sāmidhenyaḥ śrūyante satyam para prakaraṇe śrūyante tathā api tāsām avāntara prakaraṇam aparam bhavati hi sāmidhenīḥ  anubrūyāt  iti viśeṣa ākāṅkṣam vacanam yena tad saṃnidhau   abhidhīyamānam tasya iti jñāyate katham punar  nivṛttam tāsām prakaraṇam iti  āśaṅkyate nivid padāni tāsām prakaraṇam vyavadadhati iti yadi  evam katham anuvartate prakaraṇam iti  āśaṅkā parastān nividām sādmidhenī guṇā eva kāmyā vidhīyamānāḥ śrūyante yad  anantaram yajñopavītam āmnātam tena anivṛttam sāmidhenīnām prakaraṇam iti bhavati matiḥ atas  para prakaraṇe nividaḥ samupanipatitā na vyavadadhati yathā dvādaśa upasattā hīna dharmaḥ  jyotiṣṭoma prakaraṇa iti tena bhavati saṃdehaḥ asmin saṃdehe kim tāvat  prāptam sāmidhenī prakaraṇam anivṛttam tatra upavītam samāmnātam iti kutas  kāmyānām sāmidhenī kalpānām ānantarya vacanāt  hṛdayam anuviparivartamānāsu sāmidhenīṣu upavītam āmananti kartuḥ  ca vāsaḥ vinyāsa mātram guṇa u bhavati  upavītam nāma kim kurvatā tad  kartavyam iti bhavati tatra padārtha ākāṅkṣā tatra buddhau saṃnihitena aviprakṛṣṭena sāmidhenī vākyena eka vākyatām upagamya sāmidhenīṣu upavītam upavyayata iti  eṣa śabdaḥ  vidadhāti iti gamyate evam prāpte brūmaḥ na asmin saṃdehe yaḥ  tu  ayā uktaḥ sa nirṇayaḥ asmin saṃdehe vākya bheda iti nirṇaya iti kutas  vyavāyāt  iha samāptasya sa anubandhasya sāmidhenī vākyasya asya ca upavyayata iti vacanasya nividām vidhāyakena sāmidhenībhiḥ  asaṃbaddhena granthena vyavadhānam bhavati yasya ca paryavasite api vacane tad saṃbaddham eva artha antaram prakramante na tatra ananuvṛttam prakaraṇam āgacchati hi tad saṃbaddha abhidhāne hṛdayam yatra tu paryavasite vacane tad asaṃbaddham eva artha antaram prakramante na tatra buddhau pūrvaḥ padārthaḥ saṃnidhīyate na ca buddhau   asaṃnihitena eka vākyatā bhavati dvābhyām hi buddhābhyām padārthābhyām vākya arthaḥ saṃjanyate na anyatareṇa saṃnidhau samāmnānasya etad  eva prayojanam katham ubhābhyām padārthābhyām viśiṣṭām buddhim utpādayeyuḥ  iti anantarau   abuddhena saha vākya arthaḥ śakyate kartum asaṃbaddha pada uccāraṇe ca na anantarau   abuddhaḥ  bhavati tasmāt  vyavahitena saha na eka vākyatā bhavati iti atha anyena prakāreṇa dhyāna ādinā pūrva padārtham avagamya vākya artham saṃjanayet  avaidikaḥ sa puruṣa buddhiḥ  pūrva kaḥ  vākya arthaḥ  bhavet  yathā anyasmāt  anuvākāt  ākhyāta padam gṛhītvā anyasmāt  ca nāma padam yaḥ  vākya arthaḥ saṃjanyate tādṛśam tad  bhavet  yatra anyena dhyāna ādinā pūrva padārtham avagamya vākya artham saṃjanayet  tasmāt  na asaṃbaddha artha vyavadhāna eka vākya tā bhavati iti niścīyate tasmāt  na sāmidhenībhiḥ  eka vākyatā upavītasya iti nanu sāmidhenī kalpānām anantara buddhānām saṃnidhau   upavītam āmnāyate tena sāmidhenībhiḥ saṃbhantsyata iti na iti brūmaḥ ativṛttam eva hi sāmidhenīnām prakaraṇam nivitpadaiḥ  vyavadhānāt  vākyena hi sāmidhenī kalpāḥ kāmyāḥ saṃbandham upagacchanti na prakaraṇam anuvartate na ca punar  kalpa vacanena sāmidhenyaḥ prakṛtā bhavanti na hi tatra tāsām vacanam kartavyā iti kim tarhi saṃkhyābhiḥ saṃbandhayitavyā iti tad  api vākyena na prakaraṇena tatra aprakṛtāsu samidhenīṣu yasya eka vākya tā guṇasya sāmidhenībhiḥ  na asti na tasya tābhiḥ saṃbandhaḥ tasmāt  prakaraṇe yad  anuṣṭheyam tad  yajñopavītinā iti siddham agnyādheye vāraṇa vaikaṅkata pātrāṇi  ahoma arthāni homa arthāni ca śrūyante tasmāt  vāraṇaḥ  vai yajña avacaraḥ syāt  na tu  etena juhuyāt  vaikaṅkataḥ  yajña avacaraḥ syāt  juhuyāt  etena iti na ca vāraṇa vaikaṅkatānām pātrāṇām agnyādheyena saṃbandhaḥ kutas  yajñauv acara vacanāt  yajñasya etāni pātrāṇi vākyena prakaraṇam bādhitvā bhavanti tatra eṣa saṃdehaḥ kim pavam āneṣṭiṣu niviśante uta darśa pūrṇamāsa ādiṣu sarva yāgeṣu  iti kim tāvat  prāptam pavamāna haviḥṣu  iti kutas  uktam etad  pradhāne asaṃbhavan padārtha s tad guṇe kalpyata iti agni ādheya prakaraṇe ca samāmnānāt  pavamāna haviṣām tad guṇa tā tasmāt  pavamāna haviḥṣu  iti  evam prāptam evam prāpte brūmaḥ guṇānām sama tvāt  pavamāna haviṣām agnyādheyasya ca na paraspareṇa saṃbandhaḥ yathādhānam agneḥ  guṇaḥ saṃskāra arthaḥ evam pavam ānahavīṃṣy api  agneḥ  eva guṇa bhūtāni kas tatra paraspareṇa saṃbandha iti yad  uktam ādhānasya prakaraṇe samāmnāyanta iti yadi  api samāmnāyante tathā api prakaraṇam bādhitvā vākyena agneḥ  bhavanti kim iha vākyam yad  āhavanīye juhoti tena saḥ  asya abhīṣṭaḥ prītaḥ  bhavati iti nanu  āhavanīyaḥ  atra yāgasya adhikaraṇa tvena guṇa bhūtaḥ śrūyate satyam adhikaraṇam āhavanīyaḥ tathā api tu  āhavanīya artha eva yāgaḥ prayojanavat tvāt  āhavanīyasya niṣprayojana tvāt  pavamāna haviṣām katham eṣām niṣprayojana tā phala aśravaṇāt kalpyam phalam iti ced  satyam kalpyam agni saṃskāra s tu tad phalam na svargaḥ svarge kalpyamāne dvis  adṛṣṭam kalpyeta homāc ca svargaḥ  bhavati tasya ca āhavanīyena aparaḥ  adṛṣṭaḥ saṃskāra iti tasmāt  agni artha tā pavamāna haviṣām na eṣām ādhānena saṃbandhaḥ tasmāt  na ādhāne śrūyamāṇam pavamāna haviṣām bhavitum arhati kim tarhi sarva yāgeṣu darśa pūrṇamāsa prabhṛtiṣu  ādhānasya pradhāna bhūteṣu niveśa iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate vārtraghnī paurṇamāsyām anūcyete vṛdhanvati  amāv asyāyām iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim anuvākyāt vi tvasya pradhāne niveśaḥ uta ājya bhāgayoḥ  iti kim tāvat  prāptam pradhāna iti kutas  paurṇamāsīsamabhivyāhārāt  amāv asya asamabhivyāhārāt  ca pradhānam paurṇamāsī cāmā   asyāḥ  ca na ājya bhāgau tasmāt  sākṣāt  vākyāt  pradhānasya iti prāptam tatra brūmaḥ mithas  saha dvābhyām anuvākyābhyām na pradhānasya kāryam asti yatra tu dva anuvākye tatra tayoḥ  vārtraghna tā vṛdhanvat tā ca vidhīyate pradhāne ca eka anuvākyā tatra dvi tvam vārtraghna tām vṛdhanvat tām ca vidadhat  vākyam bhidyeta ājya bhāgayoḥ  tu dve prāpte āgneyī saumī ca tatra vārtraghna tām vṛdhanvat tām kevalām śakṣyati vidhātum nanu pradhāna gāmi tve api dvayoḥ pradhānayoḥ  dve anuvākye āgneyasya agnīṣomīyasya ca iti ucyate ekā vārtraghny āgneyī ekā saumī tathā vṛdhanvatyai tatra yāgneyī sā vidhīyamānā saṃbadhyeta na saumī amāv asyāyām tāvan na asti  eva paurṇamāsyām api  agnīṣomīya eva kriyamāṇe kriyeta tatra api  eka devatyā na śaknuyād devatā dvi tve kāryam kartum atha ubha agnīṣomīye prāpte iti na ekasya yāgasya dvābhyām anuvākyābhyām prayojanam upādeya tvena hi  anuvākyā codyate tatra ekatvam vivakṣitam tena tatra api na dve tasmāt  ājya bhāgayoḥ  niveśa iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate muṣṭīkaroti vācam yacchati dīkṣitam āvedayati iti tathā hastau   avanenikte ulaparājim stṛṇāti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim muṣṭīkaraṇam vāgyam aś ca āvedana artham uta kṛtsna prakaraṇe niveśa iti tathā hastau   anejanam kim ulaparājim staritum uta prakaraṇe sarva padārthān kartum iti kim tāvat  prāptam hastau   anejanam hasta saṃskāra artham vāgyamaḥ puruṣa saṃskāra arthaḥ āmantrayamāṇa  ekāgraḥ  bhavati padārthān anutiṣṭhati tena keṣāṃ keṣāṃ padārthānām ime saṃskārau   iti  ākāṅkṣā asti satyām ākāṅkṣāyām ānantaryeṇa nirākāṅkṣīkaraṇam tasmāt  ānantaryāt  āvedana arthaḥ  vāc yamaḥ  muṣṭīkaraṇam ca hastau   anejanam cola parājim staritum evam prāpte brūmaḥ sarvaiḥ prakaraṇa adhītaiḥ saṃbandha iti kutas  vākya bhedāt  katham vākya bhedaḥ artha dvayasya abhidhānāt  na hi dīkṣitam āvedayitum iti  asmin   artha āvedayati iti na ca staritum iti  asmin   arthe stṛṇāti iti staraṇam api vidhīyate avanejanam ca muṣṭīkaraṇam vāgyam aś ca vidhīyate āvedanam ca na ca eṣām paraspareṇa kaścid  saṃbandhaḥ  asti na ca padārtha ākāṅkṣāyām satyām ānantaryam eka vākya tve kāraṇam bhavati tasmāt  prakaraṇa dharmā evaṃjātīyakāḥ svena svena pada samūhena paripūrṇam ekam vākyam tathā aparam tathā sarvāṇi yāni  udāhṛtāni tasmāt  vispaṣṭam artha dvayam vibhāge ca nirākāṅkṣatā tena vākya bhedaḥ atas  saṃyogataḥ  aviśeṣāt  prakaraṇa aviśeṣa āc ca kṛtsne parkaraṇe niveśa iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ samāmnāyate āgneyam caturdhā karoti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim āgneye agnīṣomīye aindra agne ca sarvatra caturdhā karaṇam kim vā āgneya eva iti kim prāptam śeṣaḥ  caturdhā karaṇam āgneyam iti devatā guṇa saṃyuktaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ pratīyate agnīṣomīye api syāt  aindra agne api kutas  tau   api  āgneyau yasya agniḥ  devatā anyā ca bhavati asau   āgeyaḥ tad  yathā yā ḍitthasya ḍavitthasya ca mātā sā ḍavitthasya bhavati evam iha api yadi  āgneya agnīṣomasya ca puroḍāśasya mithas  saṃbandhaḥ  na bhavet  tatas  āgneya eva caturdhā karaṇam vyavatiṣṭheta bhavati tu saṃbandhaḥ tasmāt  avyavasthā yathā āgneyasya mastakam vibhajya prāśitram avadyati iti sarvebhyaḥ prāśitrau   adānam evam caturdhā karaṇam api vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati vyavatiṣṭheta vā caturdhā karaṇam āgneya eva na sādhāraṇam bhavitum arhati kutas  artha saṃyogāt  agninā devatayā arthena eka devatyasya saṃyogaḥ na dvi daivatyasya agnīṣomīyasya aindrāgnasya ca iti kutas  yasya hi  agnīṣomau devatā ubhaya viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭaḥ saṃkalpaḥ kriyate tasya agniḥ somam apekṣamāṇaḥ  devatā na nirapekṣaḥ yasya ca agniḥ somam apekṣamāṇaḥ  devatā na tasmāt  tad hita utpadyate samarthānām hi sa ucyate sa apekṣam ca asamartham tasmāt  na tad hita antena nirapekṣā agni daivatyena dvi devati asya abhidhānam atas  yatra nirapekṣaḥ  agniḥ  devatā tatra eva caturdhā karaṇam iti devatā liṅgasya hi sa amartyena saṃyogaḥ  bhavati tad hita arthasya na asati sāmarthye atha yad  uktam yathā prāśitrau   adānam sarvebhyaḥ kriyate evam caturdhā karaṇam api iti yuktam prāśitrau   adānena tatra eva saṃbandhaḥ kriyate āgneyasya prāśitram avadyati iti katham tarhi āgneyasya mastakam vibhajya iti ekam hi  etad  vākyam prāśitram avadyati iti dvitīyam āgneyasya mastakam vibhajya iti tatra āgneyasya mastakāt  avadyati iti gamyate anyasya mastakāt  anyasmāt  vā iti  aniyamaḥ yadi tu tatra kevala agni daivatyaḥ  na abhaviṣyat tad ānarthakya parihārāya dvi daivatyaḥ  api  agrahiṣyata yad  tu ḍitthasya mātā iti yuktam tatra avyāsaṅgi mātṛ tvam tatas  jātaḥ  ḍitthaḥ etāvatā saṃbandhena mātā iti  ucyate na atra kiṃcid  apekṣyate sa ca tāvāṃ   tatra saṃbandhaḥ  asti iti ḍitthasya mātā iti yuktam vacanam iha mantrā udāharaṇam bahis deva sadanam dāmi iti evamādayaḥ kim mukhya  eva abhidheye mantrāṇām viniyogaḥ uta gauṇe api iti kaḥ punar  mukhyaḥ kaḥ  vā gauṇa iti ucyate yaḥ śabdāt  eva avagamyate sa prathamaḥ  arthaḥ  mukhyaḥ mukham iva bhavati iti mukhya  iti  ucyate yaḥ  tu khalu pratītāt  arthāt  kenacid  saṃbandhena gamyate sa paścāt  bhāva at  jaghanam iva bhavati iti jaghanyaḥ guṇa saṃbandha āt  ca gauṇa iti yadi  evam sarva eva mukhyaḥ sarvaḥ  hi śabdāt  gamyate yathā eva hi  agniḥ  jvalati iti  ukte jvalane saṃpratyayaḥ evam eva agniḥ  māṇavaka iti śabda eva uccārite māṇavake saṃpratyayaḥ atha ucyate yasmin nirupapadāt  chabdāt  saṃpratyayaḥ sa mukhyaḥ yasmin sa upapadāt  sa gauṇa iti na etad  yuktam yasya hi śabdasya rūpam kasyacid  arthasya nimittam sa upapadasya api tad  eva rūpam nirupapadasya api na ca śakyam nimitte sati naimittikena na bhavitum kim atas  yadi  evam idam na śakyate vaditum upapadāt  ṛte na saḥ  arthaḥ  bhavati upapade tu saṃjāte saḥ  arthaḥ saṃjaniṣyata iti na ca asau samudāya arthaḥ śakyate vijñātum anvaya vyatirekābhyām hi vibhāgaḥ  avagamyate atha vāc  yārthaḥ  ayam iti  ucyate na evam śakyam na hi  ananvitaḥ padārthaḥ  bhavati vākya arthaḥ tad  evam dṛśyatām agni śabda eva ayam jvalana vacanaḥ agni śabda eva māṇavakasya abhidhātā iti tasmāt  na gauṇaḥ  mukhya  iti kaścid  viśeṣaḥ atha ucyate yaḥ suṣṭhu prasiddhaḥ sa mukhyaḥ yaḥ  manāg iva sa gauṇa iti idam api na upapadyate prasiddhiḥ  nāma prajñānam na ca prajñāne kaścid  viśeṣaḥ  asti atha ucyate yasya bahuśas  prayogaḥ  asti sa mukhyaḥ alpaśas  prayujyamānaḥ  gauṇa iti na etad  evam alpaśas  api prayujyamānaḥ  na asati sāmarthye pratyāyayet  atas  saḥ  api śabdāt  pratīyata iti mukhya  eva atra ucyate asti  atra viśeṣaḥ māṇavakaḥ  na agni śabdāt  pratīyate katham avagamyate uktam anyāyaḥ  ca aneka artha tvam iti katham na viparyayaḥ ucyate anādṛtya eva māṇavaka pratyayam jvalanam agni śabdāt  pratiyantaḥ  dṛśyante na tu  anādṛtya jvalanam mānavakam agni śabdāt  pratiyanti kuta etad  yaḥ  yaḥ  agni sadṛśaḥ  vivakṣyate tatra tatra agni śabdaḥ  niyata iti ata eva vigata sādṛśyāt  ayam tu dṛśyate atas  agni sādṛśyam asya pravṛttau nimittam na ca jvalane apratīte tad sādrṛśyam pratīyate tasmāt  jvalanasya agni śabdaḥ  nimittam na māṇavakasya tasmāt  jvalane mukhyaḥ  na māṇavake evam eva tṛṇa pratyayasya barhiḥ śabdaḥ  nimittam na tṛṇa sadṛśa pratyayasya tad  evam dvaite sati mukhya para tā śabdasya uta gauṇapara tā api iti yuktaḥ  vicāraḥ kim tāvat  prāptam mukhye gauṇe ca viniyogaḥ kutas  ubhayasya śakya tvāt  ubhayam api barhiḥ śabdena śakyate pratyāyayitum tṛṇam ca tṛṇa sadṛśam ca tṛṇam sākṣāt  tṛṇa sadṛśam tṛṇa pratyayena yad  ca nāma darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ sādhana bhūtena barhiḥ śabdena śakyate pratyāyayitum tad  sarvam pratyāyayitavyam vinigamanāyām hetu abhāvāt  api ca evam āśrīyamāṇe pūṣā ādi anumantraṇa ādīni darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām na utkṛṣyante tatra eva gauṇena abhidhānena prakṛtām devatām abhivadiṣyanti evam prāpte brūmaḥ mukhya  eva viniyoktavyaḥ  mantraḥ  na gauṇa iti kutas  ubhaya aśakya tvāt prakaraṇe hi samāmnānāt  pradhānena eka vākyatām upaiti tatra etad  āpatati yad  chaknuyād anena mantreṇa sādhayitum tathā sādhayet  iti sa ca asau   artha abhidhāna saṃyoga āt  chaknoti  upakartum na gauṇam artham śakyoti  abhidhātum tasmāt  na gauṇe viniyogaḥ nanu mukhya pratyayāt  chakyate gauṇaḥ pratyāyayitum satyam etad  mukhya pratyāyanena eva asya prayojanavat tā nirvṛtta iti na gauṇam prati viniyoge kiṃcid  pramāṇam asti mukhye viniyogena tu  ānarthakyam parihriyate parihṛta ānarthakye na gauṇa abhidhānam āpatati na hi  anabhidhāya mukhyam gauṇam abhivadati śabdaḥ atas  pramāṇa abhāvān na gauṇe viniyujyeta api ca gauṇasya pratyāyane sāmarthyāt  bahavaḥ  abhyupāyāḥ prāpnuvanti sāmarthyam ca śabda eka deśa iti  uktam arthāt  vā kalpana eka deśātvāt  iti tatra mantre niyogataḥ  gauṇam prati viniyujyamāna upāya antaram vinā pramāṇena bādhyeta mantrāmnānam pramāṇam iti ced  na tasya upāya antara nivṛttau sāmarthyam asti nanu mukhye api viniyujyamān sya eṣa eva doṣaḥ na iti  ucyate yadi mukhye api na viniyujyeta na eva pradhānasya upakuryāt tatra ca asya utpattiḥ  anarthikā eva syāt  tasmāt  asti gauṇe mukhye ca viśeṣaḥ api ca yaḥ  gauṇe mantram viniyuṅkte sa vaktavyaḥ kim artham mukhyam pratyāyayasi iti sa ced  brūyāt  na anyathā gauṇa pratyayaḥ asti iti pratibrūyāt  enam anye api gauṇa pratyayasya abhyupāyāḥ santi iti atha sa evam abhiyuktaḥ pratibrūyāt  mukhya pratyayaḥ api pākṣikaḥ  abhyupāya iti brūyāt  enam na tarhi niyogataḥ  gauṇe viniyojanīyaḥ yadā gauṇa pratyayāya mukham upādatte tadā etad  āpatitam bhavati mukhya  eva viniyoga iti arthena ca pratītena prayojanam na pratyāyakena mantreṇa atas  anyena api  upāyena gauṇaḥ praty āyayitavyaḥ na sa eva mantra ādartavyaḥ atha api mantreṇa pratyāyakena prayojanam syāt  tathā api mukhya pratyāyanena eva nirvṛttam prayojanam iti natarām gauṇe viniyujyeta tasmāt  mukhya gauṇayoḥ  mukhye kārya saṃpratyaya iti siddham atha yad  uktam pūṣā ādi anumantraṇa ādīnām utkarṣaḥ  na bhaviṣyati iti yukta s teṣām utkarṣaḥ saṃskāra kaḥ hi mantraḥ saḥ  asati saṃskārye anarthaka iti yatra arthavān   tatra na āyayiṣyate na ca kaścid  doṣaḥ  bhaviṣyati agnau śrūyate niveśanaḥ saṃgamanaḥ  vasūnām iti  aindryā gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhata iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim indrasya upasthānam kartavyam uta gārhapatyasya iti kutas  punar  gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhata iti  evam vispaṣṭe vacane saṃśaya iti ucyate yad  dhi vākyena upasthānam tad  stuti vacanena saṃskaraṇam na samīpa sthāna mātram na ca aindreṇa mantreṇa agneḥ  abhidhānam śakyate kartum atas  gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhata iti na gārhapatya artham upasthānam etad  iti jāyeta śaṅkā gārhapatya upasthāna arthaḥ  bhavet  iti tādṛśaḥ  ca śabdaḥ  na asti tṛtīya antaḥ saptamī antaḥ  vā tasmāt  vicāraḥ katham upapannam bhavati iti kim tāvat  prāptam sāmarthyāt  indra upasthānam aśakya tvāt  ca gārhaptyā upasthānasya katham dvitīyā vibhaktiḥ  iti ced  avivaksita īpsita arthā vā saṃbandha mātra pradhānā yad  vā upasthāna viśeṣaṇam saṃbandhāt  gārhapatya śabdaḥ tasmāt  gārhapatya viśiṣṭam upasthānam indra artham kartavyam iti gārhapatyaḥ  ca deśena viśiṃṣyān mukhyam eva kāryam mantrāṇām evam prāpte brūmaḥ vacanāt  tu  ayathārtham aindrī syāt  na etad  asti indra artham upasthānam iti ayathārtham aindrī syāt  kutas  vacana sāmarthyāt  vacanam idam bhavati aindryā gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhata iti gārhapatye dvitīyā vibhaktiḥ prādhānyam āha kim iva vacanam na kuryāt  na asti vacanasya ati bhāraḥ tasmāt  gārhapatya artham upasthānam atra āha nanu  etad  uktam na aindreṇa mantreṇa gārhapatya upasthānam bhaviṣyati iti ucyate vacanāt  bhaviṣyati āha na vacana śatena api śakyam etad  indra śabdena agninam pratyāyayet  iti bruvan vihanyeta yathā agninā siñcet  iti udakena dīpayet  iti na hi śāstra hetukaḥ śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ  bhavati nityau asau lokataḥ  avagamyata iti  uktam autpa ttikas tu śabdasya arthena saṃbandha iti nanu śabda lakṣaṇaḥ  api bhavati śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ kṛtrimaḥ yathā devadattaḥ  yajñadatta iti bhavati kaścid  yatra saṃbandhasya vidhāyakam vākyam bhavati na tu  etad  vākyam śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandhasya vidhāyakam gārhapatyasya indra śabdaḥ  nāma iti katham tarhi siddha saṃbandhena indra śabdena gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhata iti na ca śakyate para śabdena paraḥ  vaditum kim atra vacanam kariṣyati atra ucyate guṇāt  vā api  abhidhānam syāt  saṃbandhasya aśāstra hetu tvāt  iti yadi  api na idam vākyam śabda artha saṃbandhasya vidhāne hetu bhūtam tathā api  anena indra śabdena śakyam kartum gārhapatya abhidhānam kutas  guṇa saṃyogāt  gauṇam idam abhidhānam bhaviṣyati bhavati hi guṇāt  api  abhidhānam yathā siṃhaḥ  devadattaḥ agniḥ  māṇavaka iti evam iha api  anindre gārhapatya indra śabdaḥ  bhaviṣyati asti ca asya indra sādṛśyam yathā eva indraḥ  yajña sādhanam evam gārhapatye api iti athavā indrater aiśvarya karmaṇa indraḥ  bhavati bhavati ca gārhapatyasya api svasmin kārya īśvara tvam tasmāt  indra śabdena yaḥ pratyāyate arthaḥ sa pratītaḥ sādṛśyāt  gārhapatyam pratyāyayiṣyati aiśvaryāt  vā pratyāyayiṣyati iti na doṣaḥ staḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau tatra idam samāmnāyate haviṣkṛt  ehi iti tris  avaghnan   āhvayati iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim eṣa mantraḥ  avahantim pratyupadiśyate uta hantiḥ  asya kālam lakṣayati iti katham hantim pratyupadiśyate katham vā kālam lakṣayet  yadi  evam saṃbandhaḥ kriyeta haviṣkṛt  ehi iti  avaghnan   iti tatas  hantim pratyupadiśyate atha avaghnan   āhvayati iti tatas  asya kālam lakṣyati iti kim tāvat  prāptam tathā āhvānam api yathā aindrī gārhapatyam pratyupadiśyate evam eṣa mantraḥ  hantim pratyupadiśyate evam śrutiḥ  anugṛhītā bhavati itarathā lakṣaṇā syāt  hanti kālasya mantrasya ca saṃbandhaḥ  bhavet  na hanteḥ  mantrasya evam ca satyāhvayati iti  ayam anuvādaḥ āhvānam karoti yaḥ  hi  ehi iti brūte sa āhvayati tatra kenacid  guṇena mantraḥ  hantim pratyāyayiṣyati tasmāt  na āhvāne viniyoktavyaḥ na etad  asti hantim pratyupadiśyata iti kim tarhi kāla lakṣaṇā syāt  kutas  tris  āhvayati iti tri tvam atra vidhīyate yadi  asmin   eva vākye mantraḥ  vidhīyeta aneka guṇa vidhānāt  vākyam bhidyeta tasmāt  na evam abhisaṃbandha evam avaghnan   iti katham tarhi avaghnan   āhvayati iti nanu  asmin   api pakṣe mantraḥ  vidhīyate kālaḥ  ca tatra sa eva doṣaḥ  bhavet  na iti brūmaḥ avahanana kāla eva arthena haviṣkṛt  āhvātavyā tatra ayam eva saṃbandhaḥ  anūdyate kevalā tu tris  āvṛttiḥ  vidhīyate yad  tu kāla lakṣaṇa arthaḥ śabda iti na eṣa doṣaḥ laukikī hi lakṣaṇā mantraḥ  api ca rūpāt  eva āhvāne prāptaḥ saḥ  api  anūdyata eva coditaś ca vākya antareṇa avaghātaḥ śaknoti kālam lakṣayitum tasmāt  āhvāne viniyoktavya iti idam pada uttaram sūtram atha kasmān na guṇāt  avahantim brūte haviṣkaroti hi  avahantiḥ tasmāt  dhaviṣkṛt  kim evam bhaviṣyati rūpāt  eva avahantau mantre prāpte kevalam tris  āvṛttim eva vakṣyati na bhaviṣyati vākya bheda iti atra ucyate guṇa abhāvāt  gauṇam abhidhānam avahantau na saṃbhavati iti na hi  asau   āhūtaḥ  asmi iti  avagacchati tatra adṛṣṭa artham āhvānam syāt  yajamānasya patnyām haviṣkṛti dṛṣṭa artham āhvānam tasmāt  na hanti mantra iti liṅgam ca bhavati vāc  vai haviṣkṛt  vācam eva etad  āhvayati iti na ca vācaḥ  avahantinā sādṛśyam asti asti tu yajamānasya patnyā sā hi strī vāc  iti ca strī liṅgaḥ śabdaḥ avahantis tu na strī na pumān na napuṃsakam iti nanu  avahanteḥ  api strī liṅgaḥ śabdaḥ  asti kriyā iti atra brūmaḥ na niyogataḥ  avahanteḥ strī liṅgaḥ śabdaḥ puṃliṅgaḥ  api tasya asti avaghāta iti napuṃsaka siṅgaḥ  api karma iti api ca patnyāḥ sva rūpeṇa sādṛśyam avahanteḥ para rūpeṇa śabdena tasmāt  patnyām haviṣkṛti liṅgam anurūpataram bhavati avahanti mantre sati  asmin mantre vidhi antara kopaḥ syāt  apahatam rakṣa iti  avahanti  apahatā yātudhānā iti  avahanti iti tatra pakṣe abhāvān nityavat  śrūtiḥ  upadhyeta tasmāt  avaghnan   iti kāla lakṣaṇa artha iti mantraḥ  api  ahvāna artha iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate uttiṣṭhan   anvāha agnīd agnīn vihara iti tathā vratam kṛṇutā iti vācam visṛjati iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim utthānam vāc visarjanam ca prati mantrayoḥ  upadeśaḥ uta kāla arthaḥ saṃyoga iti atra pūrva adhikaraṇyā yaḥ atidiśyate yaḥ  tatra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ sa iha pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ yaḥ  tatra siddhāntaḥ sa iha siddhāṇtaḥ agnīd agnīn iti  evam uttiṣṭhan   anvāha iti vratam kṛṇutā iti  evam vācam visṛjati iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ lakṣaṇa abhāvāt uttiṣṭhan   anvāha iti siddhānte saṃbandhaḥ vratam kṛṇutā iti  ucyamāne vācam visṛjati
