iti vākyena pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ liṅgena siddhāntaḥ yadi  api ca śakyate utthāna kriyā agni id agnīn vihara iti vaktum utthānena agniḥ  idhyate vahniḥ  ca vihriyata iti vratam kṛṇutā iti ca vāc abhidhānam tathā api  adṛṣṭa artham vacanam bhavati iti na mantrayoḥ  utthāna visarjana artha tā kalpyeta kalpyamānāyām ca mantra antaram vihitam bādhyeta yāḥ paśūnām ṛṣabhaḥ  vāca iti api ca utthāna vāc visargau prati mantrau vidhīyamānauv adṛṣṭa arthau syātām preṣaṇe tu dṛṣṭha arthau tal lakṣaṇa eva atra nyāyyā darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate sūktavākena prastaram praharati iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim sūktavākaḥ prastara prakaraṇam pratyupadiśyate uta iyam kāla lakṣaṇa iti tad  ucyate kāla lakṣaṇa iti kutas  sūktavākasya devatā saṃkīrtana artha tvāt prastara prakaraṇam ca pratyaśakteḥ prastarasya ca sruc dhāraṇa artha tvāt upadeśaḥ  vā prastara prakaraṇam prati mantrasya syāt  evam śruti vihitaḥ  arthaḥ  bhavati sūktavākena iti karaṇa vibhakti saṃyogāt  itarathā lakṣaṇā syāt  sūktavākena lakṣaṇena prastaram praharet  iti evam ca kṛtvā yājyā śabda upapannaḥ  bhavati sūktavāka eva yājyā prastara āhutiḥ  iti yad  uktam devatā saṃkīrtane sūktavākaḥ samarthaḥ na prastara prakaraṇa iti ucyate na devatā vacanaḥ parkaraṇena saṃbadhyate prakaraṇam hi yajiḥ māntra varṇikaḥ  devatā vidhiḥ evam abhisaṃbandhaḥ agniḥ  idam havir ajuṣatāvīvṛdhata iti  evam devatām anukramya āśāste ayam yajamāna iti  uktvā idam idam āśāsta iti ca yad  anena haviṣā āśāste tad  asya syāt  iti prastaram havir nirdiśati agni ādīn   ca devatā viśeṣān tena praharatiḥ  yajatiḥ evam sūktavākena prastaraḥ prahartum śakyate yadi praharatiḥ  yajatiḥ agni ādi devatākaś ca tasmāt  sūktavākasya harati saṃyogaḥ  api devatā artha tā ghaṭata eva yadi  agniḥ  idam havir ajuṣatāvī vṛdhata iti evamādy eva śrūyeta na āśāste ayam yajamāna iti evamādīn i  aparāṇi tatas  agni ādaya eva iṣṭā na antaritā iti  eva paryavasitam vākyam bhavet  yatas  tu khalu  āśāste ayam yajamāna iti evamādīn i  aparāṇi śrūyante tena iha paryavasānam agni ādayaḥ puroḍāśa ādibhiḥ  iṣṭāḥ aparam tu yajamāna āśāste tad  anena prastareṇa prāpnuyāt  iti nanu satsu  api  eteṣu devatā saṃkīrtana eva paryavasyet  puroḍāśa ādibhiḥ  iṣṭā agni ādayaḥ tatas  eva yajamāna āyuḥ  ādīni  api  āśāsānaḥ prāpnuyāt  iti ucyate ubhayathā saṃbandhe sati praharaṇe viniyoktavyaḥ liṅam ca na bādhitam bhaviṣyati vākyam ca anugrahīṣyata iti athavā agniḥ  idam havir ajuṣata iti prastara eva havir nidiśyate evam idam iti saṃnihita vacanam upapannam bhaviṣyati iti atha sruc dhāraṇe viniyuktasya prastarasya prakaraṇam pratiprattiḥ  iti  ucyate tatra prativacanam su iṣṭakṛtvat  etad  syāt  iti yathā ijyā arthāt  puroḍāśāt  vacana prāmāṇyāt  sviṣṭakṛt  ijyate yāgaḥ  ca sa bhavati pratipādyate ca puroḍāśaḥ evam pratipādyeta eva hi prastaraḥ yāgaḥ  ca nirvartyata iti na doṣaḥ pratipādyamānaḥ  api hi tyajyate pratyakṣataḥ pratipādyate vacanāt  ijyām sādhayati iti  evam gamyate tasmāt  sūktavākaḥ praharati mantra iti atha sruc dhāraṇe viniyuktasya prastarasya prakaraṇam pratiprattiḥ  iti  ucyate su iṣṭakṛtvat  ubhaya saṃskāraḥ syāt  ṃś darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ sūktavākena prastaram praharati iti śrūyate tatra saṃdehaḥ kim paurṇamāsyām kṛtsnaḥ sūktavākaḥ prayoktavyaḥ kṛtsnaḥ  amāvāsyāyām uta yathāsāmarthyam niṣkṛṣya yathāyatham prayoga iti tad  ucyate ubhayatra sarva vacanam iti kutah kṛtsnaḥ  hi mantraḥ sūktavāka iti  ucyate sa padena api vinā sūktavākaḥ  na syāt  tatra sūktavākena na prahṛtam bhavet  tasmāt  ubhayatra kṛtsnaḥ sūktavākaḥ  vaditavyaḥ ye paurṇamāsī devatātā vācinaḥ śabdāḥ te paurṇamāsyām prayoktavyāḥ na amāvāsyāyām ye amāvāsyā devatā vācinaḥ te amāvāsyāyām na paurṇamāsyām śeṣa bhūtam artham saṃskurvantaḥ  mantrā upakurvanti na anyathā iti  uktam tasmāt  ye yatra upakurvanti te tatra prayoktavyā iti na kṛtsnaḥ paurṇamāsyām na kṛtsnaḥ  ca amāvāsyāyām iti atha yad  uktam vacanam idam bhaviṣyati sūktavākena praharati iti tatra padena api  ūnena na sūktavākena prahṛtam bhavet  kṛtsnasya hi sūktavākasya upadeśa iti tad  ucyate ubhe paurṇamāsya māvāsye prati eṣa kṛtsna śabdaḥ ubhayoḥ prakaraṇāt  ubhayoḥ  asau kṛtsna ucyate avayave avayava iti na etad  evam na hi sa apekṣāṇām itikartavya tayā saṃbandhaḥ na hi iti kartavyatā etad  viśiṣṭā śrūyate itikartavya tā viśiṣṭa aḥ  tu  ete gamyate kutas  na hi iti kartavya tām prati karmaṇi vidhīyaṇte phalam prati teṣām vidhiḥ itikartavya tā tu karmaṇām vidhīyate tatra saṃnidhāna aviśeṣāt kasya kim vidhīyate kasya na iti na gamyate viśeṣaḥ sādhana tvena ca sarveṣām nirdeśāt  itikartavya tāyāḥ saṃnidhānāt  ca vacanāt  ca asya prakaraṇa liṅgasya aviśeṣāt  ekaikasya kṛtsnam prakaraṇam nirākāṅkṣasya na sahāyam apekṣamāṇasya tasmāt  ekaikam prati kṛtsnaḥ sūktavāka upadiśyate sa vibhāge api pradhānānām kṛtsna eva prayoktavya iti yāni yatra anarthakāni padāni tāni  api tatra prayoktavyāni  adṛṣṭāya bhaviṣyanti sūktavākena praharati iti vacanāt  na asti vacanasya ati bhāraḥ guṇena vā kenacid  abhidhānam tāsām devatānām nirvartayiṣyanti iti atra ucyate na etad  evam uktam mukhyam eva kāryam mantrāṇām na gauṇam iti saṃskāra artha tvāt  vā utkarṣaḥ  nyāyyaḥ na gauṇam abhidhānam iti kas tarhi kṛtsna saṃyogasya samādhiḥ  ucyata iti eṣa samādhiḥ na hi  etad  ekam vākyam yaḥ kṛtsnaḥ sūktavākaḥ bahūni  etāni vākyāni yeṣām pradhāna devatā abhidhāyīni padāni madhye sādhāraṇāni tantra padāni purastād uccāryante tathā parastāt  yathā agniḥ  idam havir ajuṣatāvī vṛdhata mahojya ayaḥ kṛta agnīṣomau  idam havir ajuṣetām avī vṛdhetām iti evamādīni teṣām purastāt  tantram yathā idam dyāvāpṛthivī iti parastād api yathā asya amṛdhet  iti tāni  etāni sarvāṇi sūkta vacanena sūktavāka śabdam labhyante na ca teṣām samudāyaḥ kiṃcid  artham vadati tasmāt  na samudāyaḥ sūktavākaḥ na ca sākṣāt  sādhanam sūktavāka sāmānyasya eka tvāt  sūktavākaḥ  vartata iti  eka vacanam bhavati sūktavākena prastaram praharati iti tu yena kenacid  sūktavākena prahriyamāṇe yathāśrutam kṛtam bhavati tasmāt  samudāyaḥ sūktavākaḥ yad  tu  amāvāsyā devatā vācīni padāni na paurṇamāsyām prayujyante na tatra sūktavāka śabdaḥ  bādhyate prakaraṇam tatra liṅgena bādhitam tad  ca nyāyyam eva tasmāt  paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāyām ca vibhajya sūktavākaḥ prayoktavya iti iha kāmya yājya anuvākyā kāṇḍam udāharaṇam indra agnī rocanā divaḥ pravarṣaṇibhyaḥ indra agnī navatim puras  ślatha d vṛtram iti evamādyā ṛcaḥ aparā api kāmyā iṣṭayaḥ aindrāgnam ekādaśa kapālam nirvapet  yasya sajātā viyāyuḥ aindrāgnam ekādaśa kapālam nirvapet  bhrātṛvyavān agnaye vaiśvānarāya dvādaśa kapālam nirvapet  ruj kāmaḥ agnaye vaiśvānarāya dvādaśa kapālam nirvapet  sapatnam abhidroṣyan   iti evamādyāḥ tad  etā yājya anuvākyāḥ prati saṃdehaḥ kim yāvat  kiṃcid  aindrāgnam karma tatra sarva tra anena aindra agnena yājyā anuvākyā yugalena bhavitavyam uta etasyām eva aindra agnyām iṣṭau kāmyāyām iti evam vaiśvānarīyayoḥ  yājyā anuvākyayoḥ evam sarvatra kim tāvat  prāptam yāvat  kiṃcid  aindrāgnam vaiśvāvarīyam agnīṣomīyam jātavedasam ca sarvatra etā yājyā anuvākyā bhaveyuḥ kutas  liṅgāt  nanu krama samākhyāne viśeṣake bhaviṣyataḥ satyam tathā api kramam samākhyām ca śaknoti liṅgam bādhitum iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ liṅga krama samākhyānāt tāsu  eva kāmyāsu  etā yājyā anuvākyā iti gamyate ya eva hi liṅga krama eṣām karmaṇām sa eva āsām yājyā anuvākyānām tena tāsām eva tāḥ śeṣa bhūtā iti nanu liṅgam balavattaram iti  uktam satyam etad  iha tu samākhyā balīyasī na hi  etāḥ samākhyānāt  ṛta eṣām kāmyānām karmaṇām prāpnuvanti na bhinna deśānām karmaṇām kutas  samākhyām antareṇa āsām ṛtām yājyā anuvākyātvam eva na vijñāyate kutaḥ bhinna deśānām karmaṇām yājyā anuvākyā bhaviṣyanti iti yā ca eṣām samākhyā sā kāmyānām eva yājyā anuvākyātvam ācaṣṭe na sarveṣām yadi samākhyā na ādriyate yājyā anuvākyātvam eva eṣām na bhavati yadi  ādriyate tadā kāmyānām eva evam hi tad  samākhyāyate kāmya yājya anuvākyā kāṇḍam iti atha kim artham ubhayam upadiśyate liṅga kramāt  iti samākhyānāt  iti ca asti tatra pāthikṛtīyam vrātapatīyam ca karma sāmidhenī kāryam api  asti yājyā anuvākya akāryam api yadi liṅga kramāt  iti  etāvat  eva ucyate sāmidhenī kārye api liṅgena tāsām viniyogaḥ syāt  atha kim artham liṅga kramau vyapadiśyete sarvā yājyā anuvākya akārya eva viniyujyeran sāmidhenīṣu viniyogaḥ  na syāt  atha punar  samākhyā nāl liṅga kramāt  ca nirvṛtte yājyā anuvākya akārye sāmidhenīṣu viniyogaḥ siddhaḥ  bhavati yathā agnivāruṇyā iṣṭeḥ krame atīte saumāraudrīṇām anāgate manor ṛcas tāḥ sāmidhenīṣu dhāyyā iti  ucyante tathā pṛthuyāja aḥ  tam saṃbādha iti dve dhāyye kalpyete tasmāt  ubhayam vyapadeṣṭavyam iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate āgneyyā agnīdhram upatiṣṭhate aindryā sadaḥ vaiṣṇavyā havir dhānam iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim prakṛtābhiḥ  evaṃliṅgavatībhiḥ  upasthātavyam uta dāśatayībhya evaṃliṅgā āgamayitavyā iti kim tāvat  prāptam prakaraṇe ca mantraḥ  liṅgena vidhīyamānaḥ  dāśatayībhya eva āgamayitavyaḥ āgneyī iti evamādibhiḥ  hi śakyā dāśatayaḥ  abhivaditum yaḥ  ca ayam prakṛtaḥ sa kārya antare viniyuktaḥ na iha api  upadeśam arhati upadiṣṭa upadeśaḥ  hi na nyāyya evaṃjātīyakasya katham jātīyakasya yaḥ kasmiṃścid  viśeṣeṇa upadiṣṭaḥ na asau sāmānyena liṅgena anyātra upadeśam arhati katham yadi tal liṅgam tasya lakṣaṇa tvena tatas  sa viśiṣṭaḥ  lakṣyeta yena anena evaṃliṅgena etad  karoti iti tatas  na upadiṣṭaḥ  bhavati atha upadiśyate evaṃliṅgena karoti iti tatas  na lakṣyate tena upadiṣṭasya evaṃjātīyakasya evaṃjātīyakaḥ punar  upadeśaḥ  na nyāyyaḥ tasmāt  dāśa tayā liṅgavantaḥ  mantrā grahītavyāḥ nanu prakaraṇa sāmarthyataḥ prakṛtā grahītum nyāyyāḥ na iti  ucyate liṅgam hi prakaraṇāt  balīyaḥ āha virodhe sati liṅgena prakaraṇam bādhyeta na ca etayoḥ  virodhaḥ na vayam prakaraṇam anujighṛkṣantaḥ prakṛtam liṅgavantam upādadānā liṅgam upabādhemahi yadi tu prakṛtam viliṅgam upadademahi tatas  bādhemahi liṅgam ubhayam saṃpādayiṣyāmaḥ prakaraṇam liṅgam ca na etad  evam liṅgena pratyayaḥ bhavati dāśatayena api kartavyam iti dāśatayaḥ  api hi  āgneyī śabdena śakyante vaditum sa pratyayaḥ liṅga janitaḥ  yad  mithyā iti kalpyate tad  prakaraṇa anurodhāt sa ced  prakaraṇam anurudhyate mithyā iti kalpyate atha na anurudhyate samyak  iti tasmāt  virodhaḥ virodhe ca prakaraṇa daurbalyam ucyate tal liṅgavat tā anena upasthānena anugrahītavyā na dāśatayī mantra vyāktiḥ sā ca prakṛte mantra upādīyamāne niravaśeṣā upāttā bhavati dāśa tayām punar  mantra vyaktau   upādīyamānāyām prakaraṇāt  yā mantra vyaktiḥ prāpnoti sā bādhitā bhavati asati virodhe na ca iha liṅga prakaraṇayoḥ  virodhaḥ prakaraṇāt  vyāktiḥ pratīyate liṅgāt  sāmānyam anyā ca vyaktiḥ anyat  sāmānyam tasmāt  prakṛtaḥ  liṅgavān upādeya iti ucyate satyam evam etad  prakṛta upādīyamāne prakaraṇam na bādhitam bhavati liṅgam api  anugṛhītam liṅga janitas tu pratyayaḥ kaścid  mithyā iti kalpitaḥ  bhavati nanu vyaktiḥ  apadārthaḥ katham vyaktau   anupādīyamānāyām pratyayaḥ bādhyeta ucyate etad  eva na vijānīmaḥ  liṅgavat tātra aṅgam na vā iti kim tu tad  dhitarniḥ deśaḥ  ayam tatra devatāyāḥ  mantraḥ  lakṣyate mantra vyaktiḥ  hi sādhanam na sāmānyam nāma kiṃcid  aparam devatā eva atra sāmānyam yayā sādhanam lakṣayitavyam na ca gamyate viśeṣaḥ ayam asau mantraḥ  na ayam asau   iti anavagamyamāne viśeṣe sarve tad liṅgā grahītavyā iti dāśatayām api mantra vyaktau bhavati pratyayaḥ sa prakaraṇa anurodhena bādhyeta iti  anyāyyam evam sati na dāśataya eva upādātavyā bhavanti prakṛtam api  upādadīran nanu  etad  uktam kārya antare prakṛtasya upadeśaḥ  na asau   artha antara upadekṣyata iti ucyate na niyogataḥ sa eva artha antare vartate sa ca anyaḥ  ca sāmānyena liṅgena na evam sati kiṃcid  duṣyati nanu  etad  duṣyati na ubhayam anugṛhītam bhavati liṅgam prakaraṇam ca satyam na anugṛhītam bhavati kim tu  ananugrāhyam eva prakaraṇam liṅga pratyaya viruddha tvāt api ca na liṅgam prakaraṇam ca anugrahītavyam iti tad paricchinne pravṛttiḥ  bhavati yad  avagamyate etad  phalavat  iti tatra pravartate kim atas  yadi  evam etad  atas  bhavati na liṅgam anugṛhītam kvacid  iti  aparasmin   tad paricchinne na pravṛttiḥ  bhavitum arhati tasmāt  dāśatayaḥ  grahītavyā iti gamyate tad ākhyaḥ  jyotiṣṭoma samākhyātaḥ eva grahītavyaḥ kutas  prakaraṇa upapattibhyām prakṛtaḥ  hi  asau prakṛta pratyayaś ca nyāyyaḥ katham na jyotiṣṭomam prati mantrasya vyāpāra vidhānam upapadyate prāpta tvāt  eva vyāpāra viśeṣa vidhānam tu upapadyate aprāpta tvāt  vyāpāra viśeṣasya anapekṣya ca prakaraṇam dāśataye vidhīyamāne vākyam bhidyeta upasthānam ca kuryāt  tad  ca evam liṅgena iti nanu ca prakaraṇa āj jyotiṣṭomasya upakārakam syāt  yadi  upasthāna jyotiṣṭma saṃbandhaḥ  vivakṣyeta tadā upasthānam jyotiṣṭome upadiśyeta prakaraṇāt  tena eka vākyatām iyāt  yadā tu kha lūpa sthānasya mantra saṃbandhaḥ  vivakṣyate sarva upasthāneṣu tadā mantraḥ prāpnoti prakaraṇam bādhitvā na prakaraṇam viśeṣakam bhavitum arhati ubhaya saṃbandhe vākya bhedaḥ asmad pakṣe na punar  ayam doṣaḥ yena āgneyena aindreṇa vā jyotiṣṭome vyāpāraḥ kriyate tena upasthāna vyāpāra viśeṣaḥ tadā jyotiṣṭomi kaḥ  vidhīyate anyat  sarvam anūdyata iti na doṣaḥ  bhavati athavā agnīdhra haviḥ  dhānasadaḥ saṃbandha mātram vidhīyate upatiṣṭhata iti  ayam anuvādaḥ anena mantreṇa āgnīdhram upatiṣṭhata iti samāsīdati iti  arthaḥ tasmāt  prakṛtā mantrā evaṃjātīyakā upādātavyā iti yad  api  uktam upadiṣṭā hi te prakṛtāḥ kāryantara iti tad  ucyate ukta uttaram etad  api ca na kenacid  na upadiṣṭāḥ sarve vācā stoma āśvine śasyamāne sūrye anudyati tena na prakṛte kaścid  viṣeśaḥ tasmāt  prakṛtasya eva grahaṇam bhakṣa mantraḥ śrūyate bhakṣe hi mā viśa dīrgha āyu tvāya śaṃtanu tvāya rāyaspoṣāya varcase suprajāḥ tvāya ehi vasaḥ  purovasaḥ priyaḥ  me hṛdaḥ  asy aśvinoḥ  tvā bāhubhyām sadhyāsam nṛ cakṣasam tvā deva soma sucakṣā avakhyeṣam hinva me gātrā harivaḥ  gaṇān me mā vitītṛṣaḥ śivaḥ  me saptarṣīn upatiṣṭhasva mā me avāṅ nābhim ati gāḥ mandra abhibhūtiḥ ketuḥ  yajñānam vāc  juṣāṇā somasya tṛpyatu vasumat  gaṇasya rudramad gaṇasya ādityavat  gaṇasya soma devate mati vidaḥ prātaḥsavanasya mādhyaṃdinasya savanasya tṛtīyasavanasya gāyatra  chandasas triṣṭubh chandasaḥ  jagacchandasaḥ  agni huta indra pītasya nara aśaṃsa pītasya pitṛ pītasya madhumata upahūtasya upahūtaḥ  bhakṣayāmi iti evamādiḥ tatra saṃdehaḥ kim kṛtsna eṣaḥ  anuvākaḥ  bhakṣaṇe viniyojanīyaḥ uta kaścid  asya avayavaḥ  anyatra api iti kim prāptam liṅga samākhyānābhyām bhakṣa artha tā anuvākasya sarvaḥ  anuvākaḥ  bhakṣaṇe viniyojanīyaḥ kutas  bhakṣayāmi iti  eṣa śabdaḥ  vyaktam bhakṣaṇe viniyojanīyaḥ bhakṣaṇam eṣa śaknoti vaditum na anyat  kiṃcid  anyāni ca asya padāni bhakṣaṇa viśeṣaṇa vacanāni  eva yatra yatra bhakṣayāmi iti tatra tatra prayujyante nanu ehi vasaḥ  iti evamādi sadhyāsam iti  evam antam grahaṇa artham svena pada samūhena paraspara ākāṅkṣiṇa eka artham vibhinnam bhakṣaṇa vākyāt  nṛ cakṣasam iti evamādy avakhyeṣam iti  evam antam avekṣaṇa vacanam hinva me gātrā har iva iti evamādi ca mā me vāc  nābhim ati gā iti  evam antam samyak  jaraṇa artham tad  bahu tvāt  arthānām bahūni vākyāni katham etad  chakyam vaditum sarvam idam ekam vākyam bhakṣaṇe viniyujyata iti ucyate sarvāṇi  etāni bhakṣaṇa viśeṣa viśeṣaṇāni iti  uktam āha evam api bhidyeta vākyam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyāṇām yugapad  vacana asaṃbhavāt ucyate na viśeṣaṇāni vivakṣiṣyāmaḥ viśeṣaṇaiḥ  grahaṇa avekṣaṇa ādibhiḥ  viśiṣṭa ekaḥ  arthaḥ  vivakṣyate na evam samyak  bhavati viśeṣaṇa vacanānām avivakṣita sva artha vacana tā bhakṣaṇa viśeṣaṇa para tā ca iti lakṣaṇayā tu gamyate śruti lakṣaṇa aviṣaye ca śrutiḥ  nyāyyā na lakṣaṇā tasmāt  na ekam vākyam iti atra ucyate yadi  api  amī grahaṇa ādayaḥ  bahavaḥ  arthā gamyante na tu sarva īpsitā iti bhakṣaṇam eva ekam pratyāyayitavyam tad  dhi śrutam viśeṣaṇāni  aśrutāni na taiḥ pratītaiḥ prayojanam prayojanam ca yāvataḥ pada samūhasya ekam tāvat  ekam vākyam tasmāt  viśiṣṭa bhakṣaṇa artham etad  ekam vākyam iti bhakṣaṇe viniyoktavyam samākhyānam ca bhavati bhakṣānuvāka iti kṛtsnaḥ  ca anuvākaḥ  na avayavaḥ nanu ca samākhyā laukikaḥ śabdaḥ katham vaidikam aṅgam niyaṃsyati iti yadi  api laukikaḥ tathā api  anādiḥ tasya anuvākena saṃbandhaḥ kim atas  yadi  evam etad  atas  bhavati bhakṣaṇa samabhivyāhṛtam anuvākam brūte samabhivyāhāraḥ  ca sati saṃbandhe bhavati yathā pācakaḥ  lāvaka iti samabhivyāhārāt  saṃbandham anumāsyāmahe āha na anumāna gamya evaṃjātīyakeṣu  aṅga bhāvaḥ vidhānāt  eva avagamyate na anyathā na ca samākhyā vidhātrī atra ucyate samākhyā saṃbandhinau buddhau saṃnidhim upaneṣyati prayoga vacanaḥ  vidhāsyati iti tasmāt  kṛtsnaḥ  anuvākaḥ  bhakṣaṇe viniyoktavya iti na etad  evam kṛtsnaḥ  anuvākaḥ  bhakṣaṇe viniyujyata iti rūpāt  grahaṇa vākyam grahaṇe viniyujyeta ehi iti evamādi sadhyāsam iti  evam antam nṛ cakṣasam iti evamādi ca avakhyeṣam iti  evam antam darśane kutas  mukhya artham evam tad  vākyam bhavati itarathā lakṣaṇa artha tā syāt  mukhya artha tā ca nyāyyā na lakṣya artha tā ucyate viśeṣaṇānām abhidhāne na kiṃcid  asti prayojanam iti  uktam atra ucyate na eva etāni viśeṣaṇāni pṛthak  eva etāni grahaṇa ādīni svaiḥ svaiḥ  vākyaiḥ  ucyanta iti kutas  asti hi taiḥ prayojanam coditāni hi tāni kānicid  tu pṛthak vākyaiḥ kānicid  artha prāptāni tāni  avaśyam prakāśayitavyāni tāni prakāśayiṣyanti  etāni vākyāni rūpam ca eṣām tad prakāśana sāmarthyam atas  nānā artha tvān na ekam vākyam ucyate nanu bhakṣaṇa vākya śeṣī bhavitum api  eṣām rūpam iti ucyate bāḍham asti rūpam na tu tad viśeṣaṇāni  etāni kalpyante kasya hetoḥ  adṛṣṭa arthāni tathā bhavanti uktaiḥ  anuktaiḥ  vā viśeṣaṇaiḥ  tāvān eva saḥ  arthaḥ itarathā grahaṇa ādīni prakāśayiṣyanti tathā dṛṣṭa arthāni bhaviṣyanti tasmāt  rūpa upadeśābhyām apakrṣaḥ  bhavet  keṣāṃcid  atra iti bhakṣa anuvāke śrūyate mandra abhibhūtiḥ ketuḥ  yajñānām vāc ju ṣāṇā somasya tṛpyatu vasu mad guṇasya soma devate mati vidaḥ prātaḥsavanasya gāyatra chandasaḥ  agni huta indra pītasya madhumata upahūtasya upahūtaḥ  bhakṣayāmi iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim mandra ādiḥ tṛpyatv iti  evam anta ekaḥ  mantraḥ vasumat  gaṇa ādiḥ  aparaḥ uta mandra ādiḥ  bhakṣayāmi  anta eka eva mantra iti kim tāvat  prāptam dvau mantrau dvau hi  etau   arthau anyā tṛptiḥ  anyat  bhakṣaṇam tatas  artha bhedāt  vākya bhedaḥ tad  uktam tasya rūpa upadeśābhyām apakarṣaḥ  arthasya codita tvāt  iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ guṇa abhidhānān mandra ādiḥ  eka mantraḥ syāt  iti tṛptiḥ  bhakṣaṇā viśeṣaṇa tvena abhidhīyata iti bhakṣayāmi vāc  tarpsyati iti nanu tṛpyatv iti  eṣaḥ  anyaḥ śabdaḥ anyaḥ  ca tarpsyati iti eṣā bhaviṣyantī kriyāyām upapada bhūtāyām bhavati iti tatra dvayoḥ kriyayoḥ  asti saṃbandhaḥ  bhakṣayāmi vāc  tarpsyati iti iha punar  bhakṣayāmi tṛpyatv iti na asti kaścid  saṃbandhaḥ ucyate na hi  ayam vidhau tṛpyatv iti vijñāyate kva tarhi prārthanāyām vā prāpta kāle vā yadi bhakṣayāmi vāc  tarpsyati iti  evam abhisaṃbandhaḥ kriyate yadi vā bhakṣayāṃi vācas tarptum prāptaḥ kāla iti tena viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvāt  eka artha tāyām eka vākya tve mantra aikyam upapadyate nanu nirākāṅkṣa ete vākye bhaṅktvā rūpam sa ākāṅkṣe kriyete atra ucyate yadi  api  ete vākye bhinna arthe nirākāṅkṣe dvau   artha   abhivadeyātām tathā api bhakṣaṇasya prakāśanam dṛṣṭam prayojanam na tarpaṇasya iti kṛtvā ekārthyam eva bhavet  kim aṅga punar  guṇa bhāve gamyamāna eva atra tasmāt  guṇa abhidhānān mandra ādiḥ  eka mantraḥ syāt  iti eṣa eva mantra udāharaṇam iha ca pradānāni  aindrāṇi  anaindrāṇi ca vidyante teṣām bhakṣaṇāni  api santi tatra saṃdehaḥ kim aindreṣu  anaindreṣu ca mantraḥ uta aindreṣu  eva mantraḥ anaindrāṇām amantrakam bhakṣaṇam iti kim tāvat  prāptam anaiṇdrāṇām amantrakam bhakṣaṇam iti kutas  samāna vidhānāni  etāni pradānāni teṣu  indra pītasya iti mantraḥ  anindra pītam na śaknoti vaditum na ca samāna prakaraṇa ūhaḥ saṃbhavati asati vacane anya artha an abhidhānāt  tasmāt  amantrakam bhakṣaṇam evaṃjātīyakeṣu  iti athavā yathādevatam ūhena lakṣayitavyam kasmāt  dhruva camasā hi prakṛti bhūtāḥ ke punar  dhruva camasāḥ ye śukrām anthi pracāre savana mukhīyāḥ aindra as te bhavanti teṣām prakṛti bhūtam pradānam vikṛti bhūtāni  anyāni katham avagamyate tad prakṛti tvam hi darśayati katham anuṣṭubh chanda sa iti ṣoḍaśinī  atirātre bhakṣa mantram namati iti kim atra darśanam namati iti vipariṇāmam darśayati nanu vacanam etad  syāt  na iti  ucyate na etad  namati iti śrūyate katham tarhi evam namati iti anuṣṭubh chanda sa iti bhakṣa mantram namati iti sa eṣa ūhaḥ vikāreṣu upapadyate tasmāt  ete vikārāḥ atas  anaindreṣu  api ca udaka prāptaḥ  mantra ūhitavyaḥ  bhavati ucyate vikārā eta iti liṅgam apadiṣṭam nyāyaḥ  abhidhīyatām iti ucyate aindraḥ somaḥ  gṛhyate mīyate ca tena aindreṣu somaḥ  anaindreṣu soma eva na asti iti sarve somadharmā aindreṣu  eva adharmakā itare sa ākāṅkṣāḥ katham punar  jñāyate aindraḥ somaḥ  gṛhyate mīyate ca iti mantra varṇāt  indrāya tvā vasumata iti evamādiḥ  mantra aindram somam vaditum śaknoti na anyam tasmāt  aindraḥ somaḥ tena aindreṣu soma dharmāḥ anyāni tu pradānāni sa ākāṅkṣāṇi atas  dharmān grahīṣyanti iti nyāyaḥ tasmāt  yathādevatam ūhitavyaḥ  mantra iti evam sthitam tāvat  aparyavasitam tatas  evam sati cintā antaram vartiṣyate santi punar abhyunnītāḥ somāḥ śukrām anthi pracāra eva savana mukhīyāḥ teṣām hotuḥ  vaṣatkāre anuvaṣatkāre ca caturbhiḥ  madhyataḥkāriṇām camasaiḥ  hutvā hotrakāṇām camasaiḥ sakṛt  sakṛt  vaṣaṭkāra eva hutvā punar  sa śeṣeṣu  eva pātreṣu somaḥ  abhyunnītaḥ evam hi tatra adhvaryuḥ saṃpreṣyati madhyataḥkāriṇām camasa adhvaryavaḥ  vaṣaṭkṛte anuvaṣaṭkṛte jahuta hotrakāṇām camasādhvaryavaḥ sakṛt  dhutvā śukrasya abhyunnīya upāvartadhvam iti tatra hotrakā nānā devatā yajanti maitrāvaruṇaḥ  mitrāvaruṇau mitram vayam havāmaha iti brāhmaṇāt  chaṃsī indram indra tvā vṛṣabham vayam iti potā marutaḥ marutaḥ  yasya hi kṣaya iti na iṣṭā tvaṣṭāram patnīś ca agne patnīḥ  iha avaha iti āgnīdhra u agnim ukṣānnāya vaśānnāya iti tatra taiś camasaiḥ pūrvasmin vaṣaṭkāra indra iṣṭaḥ punar  abhyunnīya mitrāvaruṇa ādyā devatā iṣṭāḥ śeṣaḥ  tatra indrasya mitrāvaruṇa ādīnām ca tatra saṃdehaḥ kim prasthita devatāyāḥ  ca indrasya mitrāvaruṇa ādīnām ca upalakṣaṇam uta indraḥ  na upalakṣayitavya iti kim tāvat  prāptam punar  abhyunnīteṣu sarveṣām upalakṣaṇam kasmāt  dvi śeṣa tvāt  camase camase tatra dvayoḥ śeṣaḥ prakṛtau yasyai hutam tad  cheṣas tad pīta iti  uktam iha api tadvat  eva vaditavyam tasmāt  camase camase dvayoḥ  upalakṣaṇam apanītam prasthita devatāyāḥ śeṣam manyāmahe kutas  mitrāvaruṇa ādibhyas tad pātra stham abhyāśrāvyate katham etad  ucyate mitrāvaruṇādayaḥ  hi ijyante tad  yathā ācārya śeṣam devadattaḥ  bhuñjānaḥ  yadi śeṣam pūrṇakāya prayacchati pūrṇakaḥ  devadattam upalakṣayati devadatta śeṣam bhuñja iti na ācārya śeṣam tasmāt  na prasthita devatā indra upalakṣayitavya iti na ca etad  asti indraḥ  na upalakṣaṇīya iti tasya api hi  asau śeṣaḥ pratyakṣam avagamyate nanu  apanīta iti ucyate na asau   apanīyate sakṛt  dhutāṃś camasa anabhidroṇa kalaśāt  gṛhṇāti sa śeṣaḥ  camasaḥ lakṣaṇam anyasya unnīyamānasya tatas  camasasthaḥ  hotum unnetavyaḥ preṣitaḥ  vā yad  tu yakṣyamāṇā devatāḥ praty āśrā vita iti ucyate āśrāvyate tatra devatā abhyaḥ  na tu  idam vā tad  vā iti tena yad  dhotum gṛhītam tad  āśrāvitam iti gamyate na ca āśrāvaṇa velāyām devatā abhisaṃbandhaḥ yad  yad  devatā abhisaṃbaddham tad  āśrāvyate tasmāt  asti indraśeṣaḥ lakṣyate ca atas  sarveṣām upalakṣaṇam iti kṛtvā acintā eṣā na atra prayojanam vaktavyam pūrva adhikaraṇasya eva etad  prayojanam avadhāryate asti pātnīvataḥ  grahaḥ yad  upāṃśu pātreṇa agrayaṇāt  pātnīvatam gṛhṇāti iti dvi devatyānām śeṣā āgrayaṇa sthālyām upanītāḥ tatas  pātnīvataḥ  gṛhyate atha hute pātnīvate tad  cheṣe bhakṣyamāṇe bhavati saṃdehaḥ kim indravāyu ādaya upalakṣayitavyā na vā iti kim tāvat  prāptam upalakṣayitavyāḥ teṣām api hi  asau śeṣaḥ  yathā prasthita devatāyāḥ  iti apanīyate hi sa śeṣa iha na yathāpūrvavat  tatra hi pātra lakṣaṇa tvena saṃkīrtyate na somaḥ  grāhya tvena iha tu āgrayaṇāt  gṛhṇāti iti sthālī sthaḥ somaḥ  nirdiśyate hotum yakṣyamāṇa devatām prati nanu sthālyām āgrayaṇaḥ  na agrayaṇaḥ  ca tatra yaḥ  tasmāt  āgrayaṇāt  gṛhyate sa pātnīvataḥ yaḥ  tu saṃpātān n āsau pātnīvata iti ucyate āgrayaṇaḥ  apādānam tasmāt  yaḥ  apaiti  āgrayaṇaḥ  anāgrayaṇaḥ  vā sa sarvaḥ pātnīvataḥ āgrayaṇāc ca eṣa sarvaḥ  apetaḥ nanu  anāgrayaṇāt  api  apetaḥ na eṣa doṣaḥ āgrayaṇāt  tāvat  apetaḥ tena asau pūrva devatābhiḥ pīta iti na śakyate vaktum yaḥ  hi indra arthasya somasya avayavaḥ śeṣaḥ sa indra pīta iti prakṛtau   ucyate iha api tadvat  eva pūrva devatā arthasya avayavaḥ  vaditavyaḥ nanu yaḥ  asau pūrva devatā arthaḥ tasya eva ayam avayavaḥ na iti brūmaḥ na hi hutasya avayavaḥ  dṛśyate nanu prakṛtau   api hutasya avayavaḥ  na dṛśyate ucyate huta āhutasya samudāyasya tatra avayava upalakṣyate tad devatasya nanu  iha api samudāya eva āsīt  tad devatyaḥ tasya eva ayam avayavaḥ na iti  ucyate āsīt  ayam samudāya s tad devatyaḥ idānīm tasya avayavaḥ  anya devatyaḥ  jātaḥ tena samudāya s tad devatya tvāt  apetaḥ āha pūrva devatā pītasya asau   avayava āsīt  tena bhūta pūrva gatyā bhaviṣyati ucyate prakṛtau na bhūta pūrva gatyā abhidhānam kṛtam iha api tadvat  eva na kartavyam iti api ca indra devatyaḥ  tatra indra pīta iti  uktam anapanītā ca tasya indra devatya tā asya punar  pūrva devatā saṃbandhaḥ  apagataḥ tasmāt  na atra pūrva devatā upalakṣaṇīyā iti asti pātnīvataḥ somaḥ tatra mantraḥ agnā i patnī ivan sa jūr devena tvaṣṭrā somam pibā iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim tvaṣṭā upala kṣayitavyaḥ  na vā iti kim prāptam upalakṣayitavyaḥ kutas  pānāt  pānam śrūyate sa jūr devena tvaṣṭrā somam pibā iti tena ayam agnaye patnīvate saha tvaṣṭrā dīyata iti gamyate yasmai ca yena saha dīyate ubhābhyām tad  dīyate evam tad  saha dānam bhavati yathā devadattāya yajñadattena saha śatam dīyatām iti  ukte tatra ubhābhyām api dīyate tasmāt  tvāṣṭraḥ api  asau soma iti tvaṣṭā upalakṣayitavyaḥ asau   api indra iva pibati iti na etad  evam śabda pramāṇakā vayam yad  chabda āha tad  asmākam pramāṇam śabdaḥ  ca agneḥ patnīvataḥ pānam āha tvaṣṭuḥ sahabhāva mātram na hi  ananuṣṭhīyamāne sahabhāvaḥ sidhyati iti tvaṣṭari pānam anumīyate nanu tvaṣṭre pānam coditam satyam coditam mantra varṇena na codanayā codanā hi pātnīvatam gṛhṇāti iti loke tu kāryam dṛṣṭvā coditam acoditam api  anuṣṭhīyata eva lokataḥ  ca etad  paricchinnam na evaṃjātīyakena vākyena tvaṣṭuḥ somaḥ kṛtaḥ  bhavati iti tasmin   eva pātnīvate mantraḥ aibhiḥ  agne sa ratham yāhi  arvāṅ nānā ratham vā vibhavaḥ  hi  aśvāḥ patnīvata s triṃśatam trīnś ca devān anuṣvadham ā vaha mādayasva iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim trayastriṃśataḥ  devānām upalakṣaṇam kartavyam uta na iti kim prāptam trayastriṃśatam devān upalakṣayet  katham dīyate hi somas trayastriṃśate devebhyaḥ evam hi  agnim agnīd adhīcchati āyāhy agneḥ  avācīnam trayastriṃśatā devaiḥ saha samānam ratham adhiṣṭhāya nānā rathaiḥ  vā vibhavanti hi te aśvāḥ tad  idam anuṣvadham āvaha trayastriṃśatam patnīvataḥ  devān āgamaya tarpaya ca iti atra hi  agnim agnīd adhīcchati trayastriṃśataḥ  devānām tṛptaya iti gamyate yad  pradhāna ś ca atra mantraḥ tad  paraḥ somaḥ tasmāt  ucyate trayastriṃśat  devāḥ  upalakṣayitavyā iti nanu codanāyām patnīvān kevalaḥ  agniḥ  devatā tvena śrūyate satyam codanāyām patnīvān devatā tvena śrūyate na tu devatā antaram niṣidhyate kim atas  yadi  evam etad  atas  bhavati māntra varṇikā s trayastriṃśat  devāḥ  aviruddha āḥ  codanāyām pratīyanta iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ na trayastriṃśat  devāḥ  upalakṣayitavyā iti na atra mantre agniḥ  āhvātā pariveṣṭā vā tarpayitā vā adhyeṣyate na atra trayastriṃśat  deveṣu  iṣṭeṣu prayojanam nirvartyate kas tarhi yaṣṭavyaḥ patnīvān kuta etad  sa hi codyate pātnīvatam gṛhṇāti iti nanu māntra varṇikānām trayastriṃśataḥ  devānām atra saṃkīrtanam ucyate parārtha tvena tāḥ saṃkīrtyante katham na hi  aprattam agneḥ tad  bhavati na ca parakīyasya dānam avakalpate tasmāt  tvam amūbhyas trayastriṃśat  devatā abhyaḥ  dehi iti  asamañjasam vacanam agnaye tu  anena dānam uktam bhavati katham īśānaḥ  hi vilaṃbhayati dravyam tad  iha vilaṃbhanam saṃkīrtayan tvam asya īśāna iti pratyāpayati nanu mādayasva iti  ucyate na vilaṃbhaya iti ucyate na hi mādyanti devatāḥ tasmāt  mada karaṇa saṃkīrtanam adṛṣṭāya syāt  dṛṣṭāya tu tyāga saṃkīrtanam lakṣaṇayā lakṣaṇā hi  adṛṣṭa kalpanāyā jyāyasī pramāṇāt  dhi sā bhavati nanu tyāge api lakṣyamāṇe agniḥ kartā ādhīṣyate tad  ucyate agneḥ  api  adhyeṣaṇa adṛṣṭāya eva tasmāt  agneḥ  aiśvarya karaṇam etad  vākyam lakṣayati iti nyāyyam api ca pātnīvate somaś codyate pātnīvatam gṛhṇāti iti nanu uktam māntravarṇikam ca pratiṣedhati codanā iti ucyate tad  api māntravarṇikam na asti iti  uktam api ca sāmarthyāt  pratiṣedhati iti gamyate na hi sa apekṣaḥ patnī ivac chabdaḥ tad  dhita arthena saṃlakṣyate tasmāt  kevalaḥ patnīvān devatā iti etad  codanā vaśena mantraḥ  varṇanīyaḥ tasmāt  yathā eva asmābhiḥ  varṇitaḥ  mantraḥ tathā eva bhavitum arhati iti patnī iva aṃ   ca agniḥ  agne patnī ivat n iti sāmānādhikaraṇyena nirdiśyate tasmāt  agniḥ  upalakṣayitavyaḥ  na trayastriṃśat  devatā iti asti  anuvaṣaṭkāra devatā somasya agne vīhi iti  anuvaṣaṭkaroti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim anuvaṣaṭkāra devatā upala kṣayitavyā na vā iti kim prāptam upalakṣayitavyā iti na tatra pārārthyam kiṃcid  pūrva d upalakṣyate tasmāt  upalakṣayitā ivyati evam prāpte brūmaḥ anuvaṣaṭkāra devatā na upalakṣayitavyā kartṛvat  yathā kartā na upalakṣyate hotṛ pīta sya adhvarī upītasya iti evam eva anuvaṣaṭkāra devatā api na hi sā prakṛtau   upalakṣitā yad  ca nāma prakṛtau kṛtam tad  iha karaṇīyam tasmāt  na upalakṣayitavyā iti sthitāt  uttaram ucyate na etad  asti yad  uktam ūhena mantravat  bhakṣaṇam kartavyam iti amantrakam bhakṣaṇam kartavyam kasmāt  ucyate samāna vidhāna tvāt  na asti  atra prakṛti vikṛti bhāvaḥ katham prakaraṇasya tulya tvāt  yal liṅgam uktam chandaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ sa iti  ucyate tṛtīyasavana tvāt  jagati icchandasa iti prāpte anuṣṭubh chanda sa iti ṣoḍaśini bhakṣa mantram namati iti samāna vidhāne api  avakalpyate yad  tu uktam aindraḥ somaḥ  gṛhyate mīyate ca iti na eta aindrā anaindrāḥ  ca bhinnā yāgāḥ ekasya eva ete abhyāsa viśeṣāḥ na ca ābhāsa viśeṣāṇām dharmā guṇa tvāt  sarva ete yāga dharmāḥ tena kṛtsnā yāgasya codyante soma dharmāḥ somaś ca iti yad  ca indraḥ  gṛhyate mīyate ca iti indrasya mantrāmnānān mantreṇa grahaṇam prakāśayitavyam itarāsām devatānām dhyāna ādinā iti tasmāt  anaindrāṇām amantrakam bhakṣaṇam iti evam sthite cintyate asti tatra aindrāgnaḥ somaḥ aindrāgnam gṛhṇāti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim mantravat  bhakṣaṇam amantrakam vā iti kim prāptam aindra agne tu mantraḥ syāt  yasya hi indra agnī devatā tasya na indraḥ śakyate hi sa indra pīta iti vyapadeṣṭum yasya hi  avayava antaram indreṇa pītam sa indra pītaḥ tasya indra agnibhyām pibadbhyām pītam avayava antaram indreṇa tasmāt  mantravat  bhakṣaṇam iti na asya avayava antaram indreṇa pīyate na ca avayava antareṇa indra pītena tad  pītam bhavati tena pīta iti lakṣaṇā śabdaḥ  ayam indram uddiśya yaḥ saṃkalpitaḥ  indraḥ  yasya devatā iti yathā eva ca sa ākāṅkṣasya tad  dhita arthena asaṃbandhaḥ evam samāsaḥ  api indra pītasya iti sa ākāṅkṣasya na avakalpate tad  uktam vyavasthā vā artha saṃyogāt  iti āha nanu tena eva adhikaraṇena etad  gatam kim artham punar  cintyata iti ucyate yad  tatra vicāritam siddham eva tad  katham punar  vicāryate na eva sa ākāṅkṣasya devatā saṃbandha iti na eva iha devatā saṃbandha iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ pāna mātra saṃbandhaḥ  atra iti pāna mātra saṃbandhena yatra dvābhyām pīyate tatra ekena devatā saṃbandha iti  uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ tasmāt  na punaruktam iti asmin mantre gāyatra chanda sa iti  ucyate tatra saṃdehaḥ kim eka  chandasi some mantraḥ uta nānācchandasi api iti ucyate chandaś ca devatāvat  yathā anya sahita indre na mantraḥ evam aneka  chandaske some na syāt  mantra iti atra api hi gāyatra  chanda sa iti sa viśeṣaṇasya samāsaḥ  na avakalpate sarveṣu vā mantraḥ syāt  kutas  abhāvāt  ekacchandasaḥ na eva kaścid  ekacchandasāḥ somaḥ  asti tena yathābhūtaḥ  ayam tathābhūtasya chandaḥ viśeṣaṇam tasmāt  aneka  chandaske some mantraḥ syāt  iti yad  uktam anaindrāṇām amantrakam bhakṣaṇam iti tad  na sarveṣām sa mantrakam bhakṣaṇam iti yathāsamāmnāta ś ca mantraḥ syāt  na indra pīta iti soma ucyate kim tarhi savanam prātaḥsavana śabdena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt nanu some api ṣaṣṭhī satyam asti ṣaṣṭhī na tu tena sāmānādhikaraṇyam na asau   indreṇa somaḥ pītaḥ na api indrāya dattaḥ anya eva pītaḥ  dattaḥ  vā sa gata eva na ca atītaḥ samudāyaḥ  vyapadiśyate pratyakṣa vacanaḥ  hi  ayam śabdaḥ savane tu na doṣaḥ indra pītam bhavati savanam yatra indreṇa pītam tasmāt  anaindraḥ  apītasavane antarbhavati iti śakyate mantreṇa vaditum śakyate ced  samāna vidhāne katham iva mantraḥ  na bhaviṣyati bhaktyā hi  api itaḥ pīta iti  ucyate evam eva aitiśāyana ācāryaḥ  manyate sma asmākam api  etad  eva matam ācārya grahaṇam tasmāt  āgatam iti tasya saṃkīrti artham jyotiṣṭome śrūyate uccais  ṛcaḥ kriyate uccais  sāmnā upāṃśu yajuṣā iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ṛc ādi jātim adhikṛtya ete śabdāḥ pravṛttāḥ uta vedam adhikṛtya iti kim tāvat  prāptam jāta adhikāraḥ syāt  kutas  śruteḥ eṣām śabdānām śravaṇāt  eva jātim pratipadyāmahe tena upāṃśu tvam jātyā adhikṛtayā saṃbadhyate vedānām adhikārakaḥ śabdaḥ  na asti iti api ca ṛgveda vyatikrāntānām ṛcām yajurveda uccais  prayogaḥ  bhaviṣyati itarathā tasyāḥ  eva ṛca ubhau dharmau vaikalpikau syātām tatra pakṣe bādhaḥ syāt  prakaraṇam ca evam anugṛhītam bhavati itarathā veda saṃyoge sarvasmin   api kratau   upāṃśu tvam syāt  tasmāt  jāta adhikārā ete śabdā iti vedam vā adhikṛtya idam ucyate kutas  prāya darśanāt  kim idam prāya darśanāt  iti veda prāye vākye veda upakrame nigamyamānā ime śabdāḥ śrūyante prajāpatiḥ  vā idam eka āsīt  sa tapaḥ  atapyata tasmāt  tapas te pānāt  trayaḥ  devāḥ  asṛjyanta agniḥ  vāyuḥ  ādityaḥ te tapaḥ  atapyanta tebhyas te pānebhyas trayaḥ  vedā asṛjyanta agneḥ  ṛgvedaḥ  vāyoḥ  yajurveda ādityāt  sāmaveda iti  evam upakramya nigamana idam śrūyate uccais  ṛcā kriyate ucchaiḥ sāmnā upāṃśu yajuṣā iti etasmāt  kāraṇāt  ebhiḥ prakṛtaiḥ  upāṃśva ādi kartavyam na jātyā ṛc ādibhiḥ  iti  ucyate kuta etad  avagamyate vākya upasaṃhāre śruta tvāt  yasmāt  ita ete vedā jātāḥ tasmāt  etaiḥ  upāṃśva ādi kartavyam iti ṛc ādibhiḥ  api veda vacanaiḥ  eva upasaṃhāreṇa bhavitavyam itarathā vākyam eva na avakalpeta tatra anarthakā eva bhaveyuḥ tasmāt  veda adhikārā iti liṅgam api  asmin   arthe bhavati yathā ṛc ādayaḥ śabdāḥ śaknuvanti vedam abhivaditum iti ṛgbhiḥ prātar divi deva īyate yajurvedena tiṣṭhati madhye ahnaḥ sāmavedena astamaye mahīyate vedaiḥ  aśūnyaiḥ  tribhiḥ  eti sūrya iti dvau vedau saṃkīrtya ṛc śabdam ca triṣu pādeṣu caturthe pāda upasaṃharati bahuvacanena vedaiḥ  aśūnyas tribhiḥ  eti sūrya iti  ṛc śabdam veda vacanam darśayati tasmāt  api paśyāmaḥ veda adhikārā ete śabdā iti dharma upadeśaḥ  ca bhavati sāmnaḥ uccais  sāmnā iti sa veda adhikāra pakṣe yujyate jāta adhikāre tu  ṛca uccais tvena sāmna uccais tvam siddham na asya sāma dravyeṇa saha saṃbandhaḥ  veditavyaḥ tasmāt  api veda adhikārā iti trayī yasya vidyā sa trayīvidyaḥ yaḥ  trīn vedān adhīte sa evam prakhyāyate trayī iti ca eṣa śabdā ṛc sāma yajuḥṣu prasiddhaḥ yadi  ṛc sāmayajūṃṣi iti trayaḥ  vedā ucyante evam tad vidi trayīvidyā ākhyā yujyate bhavati ca tasmāt  veda adhikārā ete atha yad  uktam ṛgvedam atikrāntānām ṛcām yajurvede api  uccais tvam bhaviṣyati iti tatra mad pakṣe yathāśrutaḥ prayogaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti yad  uktam tad parihartavyam iti ābhāṣā antam sūtram na eṣa doṣaḥ sarvasmin   ṛgveda uccais tvam sarvasminś ca yajurveda upāṃśu tvam tatra yadi  ṛgveda vyatikrāntāyāḥ  ṛcaḥ  yajurveda upāṃśu tvam bhavati iti na etad  dūṣyati veda dharmaḥ san ṛc dharma iti vedasya ca na dharma dvayena saṃbandhaḥ yad  uktam prakaraṇam evam anugṛhītam bhavati iti veda saṃyogāt  vākyena prakaraṇe bādhyamāne na doṣaḥ  bhaviṣyati asti  ādhānam ya evam vidvān agnim ādhatta iti tad  yājuḥ vaidikam tatra sāma gānam āmananti ya evam vidvān vāravantīyam gāyati ya evam vidvān yajñāyajñīyam gāyati ya evam vidvān vāmadevyam gāyati iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ādhāne sāma gānam uccais  uta upāṃśu  iti uccais  iti prāptam kutas  sāmavedena etad  kriyate yad  vāravantīya ādibhiḥ tasmāt  uccais  etāni sāmāni geyāni iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ guṇa anurodhena vā mukhyam vyatikramet  mukhya anurodhena vā guṇam iti guṇa u vyatikramitavyaḥ  nyāyyaḥ mukhyaḥ  ca anugrahītavya iti kutas  mukhya artha tvāt  guṇasya guṇasya anuṣṭhānena mukhyaḥ sa guṇaḥ katham syāt  iti guṇe pravartate guṇa pravṛttyā ced  mukhyasya guṇa hāniḥ  bhavati guṇa pravṛttau phalam eva na avāptam bhavati atha pradhānam sa guṇam kariṣyāmi iti guṇe pravartamānaḥ  guṇasya guṇam vinipātayati na asya sva arthaḥ  hīyate na asau guṇam sa guṇam kartum pravartate guṇaḥ  ca sāma gānam pradhānam ādhānam ādhānasya yājuḥ vaidika tvāt  upāṃśu tā guṇaḥ sa gaṇa dharmam uccais tvam sāma vaidikam bādhate tasmāt  upāṃśu sāmāni geyāni iti yajurvede jyotiṣṭomam samāmananti jyotiṣṭomena svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti tathā sāmavede api  asya evam eva samāmnānam sakṛc ca kṛtāyām buddhau dvitīyam guṇa artham śravaṇam bhavati tatra saṃdehaḥ kim yājuḥ vaidikam āmnānam kriyā artham sāma vaidikam guṇa artham uta viparītam iti yatara t  ca āmnānam kriyā artham tad dharmā bhaviṣyanti kim tāvat  prāptam sāmavedikam kriyā artham yājurvedikam vā iti  aniścayaḥ  viśeṣān avagamāt  iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ bhūyastvena guṇānām paricchidyeta yatra bhūyāṃsaḥ  guṇāḥ samāmnātāḥ tatra kriyā arthā codanā iti gamyate yatra hi kartavya tayā codanā tatra itikartavyatā ākāṅkṣyate yatra ākāṅkṣitā iti kartavyatā tatra iti kartavyatā vacanam nyāyyam ye ca bhūyāṃsaḥ  guṇāḥ sa iti kartavyatā tad  itikartavya tāliṅgena kartavyatā codanām anumimīmahe yathā bahuṣu rāja pratimeṣu upaviṣṭeṣu yasya śvetam chatram bāla vyajanam ca sa rājā iti  avagamyate anākhyātaḥ  api rāja liṅgena evam kartavyatā āliṅgena guṇānām bhūyastvena jyotiṣṭomasya yājuḥ vaidikasya codanā anumīyate tasmāt  jyotiṣṭomasya upāṃśu prayogaḥ yajurvedena hi jyotiṣṭomaḥ kriyate yad  tena codyate acoditam na śakyate kartum iti uktāni viniyoga kāraṇāni śrutiḥ  liṅgam vākyam iti śrutiḥ  aindryā gārhapatyam iti dvitīyā vibhaktiḥ liṅgam mantreṣu vacana sāmarthyam bahis deva sadanam dāmi iti vākyam aruṇayā krīṇāti iti atha kim etāvanti  eva viniyoga kāraṇāni na iti  ucyate kim aparam kāraṇam iti praśnena eva upakramaḥ bhavati ca praśnena eva upakramaḥ yathā kā nāma iyam nadī kaḥ  nāma ayam pravataḥ kim idam phalam iti tad  ucyate asaṃyuktam prakaraṇāt  itikartavya tā arthi tvāt yad  asaṃyuktam śrutyā liṅgena vākyena vā tad  prakaraṇāt  itikartavya tā arthi tvāt yad  itikartavya tā kāṅkṣiṇaḥ saṃnidhau pūraṇa samartham upanipatati yad  vacanam tad  tena prakṛtena saha eka vākyatām yāti tasmāt  prakṛte viniyujyate kim iha udāharaṇam kim ca prayojanam iti darśa pūrṇamāsau prakṛtya śrūyate samidhaḥ  yajati tanūna pātam yajati iḍaḥ  yajati barhis  yajati svāhākāram yajati iti tāni tatra eva prakaraṇa sāmarthyāt  viniyujyante na agnihotre jyotiṣṭome vā atha kim etāvanti  eva viniyoga kāraṇāni na iti  ucyate kim ca kramaś ca deśa sāmānyāt  kramavatām ānupūrveṇa upadiśyamānānām yasya paryāye yam dharmam āmananti tasya tam praty ākāṅkṣā anumīyate satyām ākāṅkṣāyām eka vākya bhāvaḥ tasmāt  tatas  viniyoga iti kim iha udāharaṇam kim ca prayojanam ānupūrvyavatām yāgānām anumantraṇeṣu  āmnāteṣu upāṃśuyājasya krame dabdhiḥ  nāma asi iti samāmnātaḥ tasya ākāṅkṣām utpādya tena eka vākyatām yāt  vā tatra eva viniyogam arhati iti tathā ca aindrāgnam karma viyāta sajātasya asti bhrātṛ vyavataḥ tasya yājyā anuvākyā yugalam api  āmnāyata aindrāgnam indra agnī rocanā ādivaḥ pravarṣaṇibhya iti  ekam aparam indra agnī navatim puras  ślatha d vṛtram iti tatra liṅgāt  viniyoge siddhe viśeṣa viniyogaḥ  bhavati pūrvam yugalam pūrvasya aindrāgnasya uttaram uttarasya iti etad  udāharaṇam prayojanam ca iti atha kim etāvanti  eva viniyoga kāraṇāni iti na iti  ucyate kim ca samākhyā ca evam syāt  katham viniyoga kāraṇam iti samākhyā sati saṃbandhe bhavati yathā pācakaḥ  lāvaka iti tatra pācaka śabdam upalabhya pacatinā asya saṃbandha iti gamyate evam vede api iti akṛtaka artha saṃbandham samācakṣāṇam śabdam upalabhya bhavati saṃbandhe tasmin saṃpratyayaḥ kim iha udāharaṇam prayojanam ca ādhvaryavam iti samākhyātāni karmāṇi  adhvaryuṇā kartavyāni hautram iti ca hotrā etad  udāharaṇam prayojanam ca iti uktāni viniyoga kāraṇāni śruti liṅgam vākyam prakaraṇam sthānam samākhyānam iti teṣām samavāye kim balīya iti cintyate eka artha vṛtti tvāt  vācaḥ  yugapad  asaṃbandhāt  dvayoḥ  dvayoḥ saṃpradhāraṇā tatra śruti liṅgayoḥ kim śruti balīyasy āhosvil liṅgam iti kim punar  atra udāharaṇam aindryā gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhata iti atra cintyate kim indrasya gārhapatyasya vā upasthānam kartavyam iti  aniyamaḥ uta gārhapatyasya eva iti yadi tulya bale ete kāraṇe tatas  vikalpaḥ atha śrutiḥ  balīyasī gārhapatya eva upastheyaḥ kā punar  atra śrutiḥ kim liṅgam śrutiḥ  gārhapatya śabda śravaṇam liṅgam punar  kadā ca na starī rasi na indrasaḥ casi dāśuṣe iti indra śabdasya viśiṣṭa devatā abhidhāna sāmarthyam atha kim vākyam nāma saṃhatya artham abhidadhati padāni vākyam yadi  evam idam api vākyam aindryā gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhata iti idam api kadā cana starīḥ  asi iti ubhayatra api saṃhatya artham abhidadhati padāni tena vākyasya vākyasya ca eṣā saṃpradhāraṇā na śruti liṅgayoḥ yadi vā śruti liṅga vākyāni vivektavyāni idam śruti vākyayoḥ  antaram idam liṅga vākyayoḥ  iti tad  abhidhīyate yad  tāvac chabdasya artham abhidhātum sāmarthyam tad liṅgam yad  arthasya abhidhānam śabdasya śravaṇa mātrāt eva avagamyate sa śrutyā avagamyate śravaṇam śrutiḥ eka artham anekam padam vākyam iti  uktam eva tad  etad  sarveṣu  eva vākyeṣu samavetam viviktam ca dṛśyate iha tāvat  kadā cana starīḥ  asi iti  anena mantreṇa indra upasthātavya iti na etad  kasyacid  chabdasya śravaṇāt  eva avagamyate na api śabda antarasya samīpa uccāritasya sāmarthyam asti yena etad  avagamyate etasyām khalu  ṛci indra śabdaḥ  vidyate yaḥ  viśiṣṭām devatām avagamayitum śaknoti tayā ca avagamitayā prayojanam asti iti tena indra upasthāna indra śabdaḥ prayujyate tad eka vākyatā c ca avaśiṣṭāni padāni na tu  evam asyām ṛci kasyacid  chabdasya sāmarthyāt  gārhapatyasya upasthānam bhavati śravaṇāt  eva tu gārhapatya śabdasya vayam agnim pratīmaḥ  na liṅgāt  yadi tu liṅgam balīyaḥ indra upasthātavyaḥ yadi gārhapatya śravaṇam tatas  gārhapatyaḥ evam tarhi liṅga vākye virudhyamāna iha saṃpradhārye na śruti liṅge indra śabdasya viśiṣṭa devatā abhidhāna sāmarthyāt  indra upasthānam yadi liṅgam balīyaḥ atha tu vākyam gārhapatya upastheyaḥ vākyam hi  etad  aindryā gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhata iti na etad  evam yadi  api  etad  vākyam śrutiḥ  api  atra asti yā tu  atra śrutiḥ sā liṅgena virudhyate na yad  vākyam katham balīyasy api hi liṅge aindrya upatiṣṭhata iti  etad  gārhapatya śabdena saha eka vākyatām upaitya eva yadi hi na upeyāt tatas  liṅgena virudhyate yaḥ  tu gārhapatya śravaṇāt  eva arthaḥ pratīyate sa liṅge balīyasi parityaktaḥ  bhavati na asau   upasthānena saṃbadhyate tadā hi indram gārhapatya śabdaḥ  abhivadet  agni samīpam vā atha nu śrutiḥ pramāṇam bhavati tatas  liṅgena avagatam indra upasthānam bādhyeta tasmāt  chruti liṅgayoḥ  eva eṣa virodhaḥ na liṅga vākyayoḥ  iti athavā na atra eka vākya tvāt  indra prādhānyam gārhapatya prādhānyam vā upasthānasya kutas  tarhi indra śabdavat tvān mantrasya indra prādhānyam dvitīya avibhakti śravaṇāt  gārhapatya prādhānyam tasmāt  chruti liṅgayoḥ  virodhaḥ kim tāvat  prāptam tulya bale ete kāraṇa iti katham idam api kāraṇam idam api śrutiḥ  api liṅgam api na hi vijñānasya vijñānasya ca kaścid  viśeṣa upalabhyate rūpam prati asya bhaṅgurasya iva rūpam asya dṛḍhasya iva iti nanu liṅgasya bhaṅgurasya iva rūpam sa vicikitsaḥ hi bhavati liṅgāt  pratyayaḥ nirvicikitsaḥ śruteḥ na etad  yuktam yatas  liṅgāt  sa vicikitsaḥ pratyayaḥ tasya ca śruteḥ  ca na eva saṃpradhāraṇā asti yatas  tu khalu liṅgān nirvicikitsaḥ pratyayaḥ sa śrutyā vikalpitum arhati nanu na eva kadācid  liṅgān nirvicikitsaḥ pratyayaḥ asti na etad  evam evam hi sati na eva liṅgam nāma kiṃcid  pramāṇam abhaviṣyat  kāmam mā bhūt  pramāṇam bhavati tu saṃśayaḥ  liṅga parijñāteṣu  artheṣu yadi vā vispaṣṭam eva aprāmāṇyam na saṃśayaḥ katham samartham etad  imam artham abhinirvartayitum iti liṅgāt  etāvat  avagamyate na ca yad  yasya nirvartanāya alam tad  asati  eva vacane tad  nirvartayitum arhati tasmāt  na liṅgam viniyojakam iti atra abhidhīyate prakaraṇavataḥ  arthasya saṃnidhāne yam artham āmananti sa tasya sādhana bhūta  iti  eva gamyate katham khalu upakariṣyati iti saṃdihyamāne bhavati sāmarthyāt  pariniścayaḥ yatra ayam samarthaḥ tatra śakyaḥ  viniyoktam iti tasmāt  bhavati liṅgam pramāṇam iti na ca liṅga prāmāṇye vinigamanāyām hetuḥ  asti tasmāt  tulya bale ete kāraṇe kadā cana starīḥ  asi iti liṅgāt  indra upasthātavyaḥ śruteḥ  gārhapatya iti avirodhāt  khalu  api imam eva artham pratipadyāmahe balīyān api hetuḥ  virudhyamānm abalīyāṃsam bādhitum arhati na aviruddham na ca kaścana virodhaḥ yad  indram upatiṣṭheta anena mantreṇa gārhapatyam api nanu  ayam eva virodhaḥ sakṛt  upasthānam coditam asakṛt  abhinirvartyata iti upastheya bhedāt  pratipradhānam āvartante guṇā iti nyāya eva eṣa na virodhaḥ ayam tarhi virodhaḥ gārhapatya upasthīyamāne agni vacana indra śabdaḥ  guṇam kriyā yogam vā apekṣamāṇaḥ  bhavitum arhati indre tu upasthātavye nirapekṣa indra vacana eva gauṇa mukhyayoḥ  ca mukhye saṃpratyaya iti na iti brūmaḥ virodhe mukhyena gauṇaḥ  bādhyeta na ca kaścid  virodhaḥ yugapad  abhhidhāne hi virudhyeyātām iha ca anyasmin prayoge agni vacanaḥ  anyasmin   indra vacanaḥ atas tulya bale ete kāraṇe iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ śruti liṅgayoḥ śruti balīyasī kutas  artha viprakarṣāt  kim idam artha viprakarṣāt  iti arthasya viprakarṣaḥ  artha viprakarṣaḥ kaḥ punar  arthaḥ śrutyā arthaḥ gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhata iti saṃnikṛṣṭaḥ śruti arthaḥ indra upastheya iti viprakṛṣṭaḥ katham kadā cana starīḥ  asi iti  anena mantreṇa indra upasthātavya iti na śrūyate sati  api indra abhidhāna sāmarthye vacana abhāvāt  anupasthānīya indra iti  eva gamyate nanu  idam uktam prakaraṇāmnānād aṅgam iti  avagamyate sāmarthyāt  viniyoga iti na etad  asti uktam eva etad  dharmasya śabda mūla tvāt  aśabdam anapekṣam syāt  iti yad  etad  prakaraṇam liṅgam ca ubhayam api  etad  śabdam na ca atikrānta pratyakṣa viṣaya evaṃlakṣaṇake arthe śabdam antareṇa paricchedaḥ  avakalpate atas  manyāmahe viprakṛṣṭam śruti arthāl liṅgam iti yadi  evam śrutiḥ  yatra virodhinī na vidyate tatra api na liṅgāt  artha paricchedaḥ tatra etad  eva na asti liṅgam pramāṇam iti kuta eva etena śrutiḥ  virotsyata iti tatra śruti liṅgayoḥ  balīyaḥ tvam prati saṃpradhāraṇā eva na upapadyata iti brūmaḥ atra ucyate itikartavyatha arthinaḥ prakaraṇavataḥ  arthasya saṃnidhau   upanipatitaḥ  mantra āmnāna sāmarthyāt  itikartavya tā kāṅkṣasya vāki aśeṣa tām abhyupetya etena mantreṇa yajeta iti kim uktam bhavati yāgena abhīpsite sādhyamāne anena mantreṇa upakuryāt  iti na ca antareṇa indra abhidhānam ayam mantra upakartum śaknoti tena etad  uktam bhavati anena indraḥ  abhidhātavya iti atas  śruti mūla eva ayam arthaḥ yadi śruti mūlaḥ na śruti antareṇa bādhitum śakyaḥ tad  etal liṅgam yadi vā na eva pramāṇam yadi vā śrutyā vikalpitum arhati iti na api  apramāṇam bhaviṣyati na api vikalpiṣyata iti brūmaḥ katham śruti lakṣaṇaḥ  ayam artha iti  upapāditam tasmāt  na apramāṇam yatas  tu khalu  ānumānikīm eka vākyatām liṅga sāmarthyam ca apekṣya śrautaḥ  ayam arthaḥ yad  indrasya upasthānam anena mantreṇa iti  avagamyate pratyakṣā tu śruti gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhata iti sa eṣaḥ  artha viprakarṣaḥ prathamam tāval liṅga jñānam tatas  sāṃarthyāc chabdena ayam arthaḥ  abhihitaḥ  bhavati tad  etad  chruti virodhe na avakalpate vispaṣṭam hi  avagatam etad  anena mantreṇa gārhapatya upastheya iti tatra vijñātam etad  evam ayam upakaroti mantra iti  etasmin   ca nirjñāte kṛta sāmarthyayoḥ  vākya prakaraṇayoḥ  na etad  evam kalpayitum śakyam indra upasthānam śabdena abhihitam iti tasmāt  artha viprakarṣā t  chrutyā liṅgam bādhyata iti vikalpasya ca anyāyya tvāt  anyāyi aś ca vikalpaḥ tatra hi  abhāvaḥ pakṣe nityavat  ca aindryā gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhata iti śrūyamāne yad  abhāvaḥ pakṣe parikalpyate tad  aśrutam bhavati śrutam ca hīyate yāvānś ca śrutasya arthasya utsarge doṣaḥ tāvān aśruta parikalpanāyām ubhayatra hi prasiddhiḥ  bādhyate tasmāt  anyāyya tvāt  vikalpasya śruti liṅgayoḥ śruti balīyasi iti  avagacchāmaḥ atha yad  uktam sati virodhe nyāyyaḥ  bādhaḥ na ca atra asti virodha iti ayam asti virodhaḥ yad  akṛta sāmarthyayoḥ  vākya prakaraṇayoḥ  indra upasthāna vācinī śrutiḥ  bhavati kṛta sāmarthyayoḥ  tu na avakalpate na ca vākya prakaraṇābhyām yugapad  kṛta sāmarthyābhyām akṛta sāmarthyābhyām ca śakyam bhavitum tasmāt  virodhaḥ virodhe ca śrutiḥ  liṅgāt  balīyasi iti liṅga vākyayoḥ  virodhe kim udāharaṇam syonam te sadanam kṛṇomi ghṛtasya dhārayā suṣevam kalpayāmi tasmin sīdā amṛte pratitiṣṭha vrīhīṇām medha sumanasyamāna iti atra saṃdehaḥ kim kṛtsnaḥ  mantra upastaraṇe puroḍāśa āsādane ca prayoktavyaḥ uta kalpayāmi  anta upastaraṇe tasmin sīdā iti evamādiḥ puroḍāśa āsādana iti yadi vākyam balīyaḥ tatas  kṛtsna ubhayatra katham suṣevam kalpayāmi iti  etad  apekṣya tasmin sīdā iti evamādiḥ pūrveṇa eka vākyatām upaiti yad  kalpayāmi tasmin sīdā iti atha liṅgam balīyaḥ tatas  kalpayāmi  antar  sadana karaṇe katham syonam te sadanam kṛṇomi iti sadana karaṇam abhivaditum alam iti tasmin sīda iti  ayam api puroḍāśam sādayitum iti sādane viniyujyate kim tāvat  prāptam tulya bale ete kāraṇa iti yathā liṅgam prati śruteḥ  balīyaḥ tvam uktam na tathā vākyam prati liṅgasya ucyate athavā vākyam eva liṅgāt  balīyaḥ kutas  tad  dhi śrutyā api bādhyate na ca balīyaḥ kāraṇam śakyate bādhitum tena asya bhaṅgura tām adhyavasyāmaḥ yaḥ  tu  ekena bādhyate śakyaḥ  asau   anyena api bādhitum iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ liṅga vākyayoḥ  liṅgam balīya iti kutas  artha viprakarṣāt  kaḥ  atra artha viprakarṣaḥ prakaraṇavataḥ saṃnidhau   āmnānād darśa pūrṇamāsa aṅgam ayam mantra iti  avagamyate tasmin sīdā iti puroḍāśa āsādana abhidhāna sāmarthyāt  sādane viniyujyamāne kṛta sāmarthyam mantrāmnānam iti na asti pramāṇam yena upastaraṇe api viniyujyeta tathā syonam te sadanam kṛṇomi iti  eṣaḥ  api prakaraṇa āmnāna sāmarthyāt  eva darśa pūrṇamāsa aṅga tām āpannaḥ sāmarthyāt  eva upastaraṇe viniyogāt  kṛta prayojane na puroḍāśa āsādane viniyogam arhati na hi  asmin viniyuj yamānasya kiṃcid  api prayojanam asti evam upastaraṇe tasmin sīda iti  asya na asti sāmarthyam pūroḍāśa āsādane api syonam ta iti  asya pūrveṇa eka vākyatām upetya upastaraṇe sāmarthyam pūrvasya pareṇa eka vākya tvāt  sādane na tu sva rūpeṇa ubhayoḥ tad  eṣaḥ  artha viprakarṣaḥ yad  syonam ta iti  asya pratyakṣam sadana karmaṇaḥ  abhidhāna sāmarthyam tad  mukhyam tasmin sīda iti  asya punar  pūrveṇa saha eka vākyatām upagatasya bhavati jaghanyam tad  atra pūrvasya mantrasya abhidhāna sāmarthyāt  upastaraṇe viniyoga uktaḥ  bhavati iti saṃnikṛṣṭaḥ  liṅgasya śruti arthaḥ uttarasya tu upajanite abhidhāna sāmarthye tatas  śruti artha iti liṅga antaritaḥ  viprakṛṣṭaḥ  bhavati evam uttarasya sādane saṃnikṛṣṭaḥ pūrvasya ca liṅga antaritaḥ tasmāt  artha viprakṛṣṭāl liṅga vākyayoḥ  liṅgam balavattaram tatas  syonam iti  eṣa śabdaḥ  yadi  api  uttareṇa akāṅkśita iti sādane api prayogam arhati tathā api bhitvā vākyam upastaraṇa eva viniyoktavyaḥ tasmin sīda iti  eṣa ca sādane nanu syonam ta iti  asya śabdasya yathā eva upastaraṇa abhidhāna sāmarthyam evam uttareṇa eka vākyatām upagantum sāmarthyam sāmarthyam ca liṅgam iti  ucyate tasmāt  bhidyamāne vākye liṅgam eva bādhitam bhavati iti satyam evam etad  api liṅgam liṅgam api khalu  etad  evaṃlakṣaṇakam viprakṛṣṭa artham eva bhavati liṅgāt  eka vākyatā tasmāt  abhidhāna sāmarthyam tatas  śruti artha iti viprakṛṣṭa artha tā viprakṛṣṭa artha tā ca bādhane hetu bhūtā tasmāt  na uttaraṇa eka vākya tām yāsyati iti evam tasmin sīda iti  uttaram na pūrveṇa api api ca uttareṇa eka vākyatām upagatasya na kiṃcid  api dṛṣṭam asti kāryam upastaraṇa pratyāyanam tu dṛṣṭam kutas  śruta tvāt  upastaraṇasya sādanasya ca evam uttarasya sādana pratyāyanam na tu pūrveṇa eka vākyatāyām na ca etau pūrva uttarābhyām eka vākyatām antareṇa pṛthak  yathāyatham kārye na kurutaḥ tasmāt  pūrvaḥ pūrvatra viniyojanīyaḥ uttara uttaratra iti atha yad  uktam śrutyā api tad  bādhitam iti vākyena api tad  bādhitavyam iti na etad  evam na hi bādhitasya anyena api bādhanam eva nyāyyam bādhitam hi  anugṛhītavyam arthavat tvāya śrutim prati viprakṛṣṭa artham vākyam prati saṃnikṛṣṭa artham tasmāl liṅgam balīya iti atha vākya prakaraṇayoḥ  virodhe katham iti kim punar  prakaraṇam nāma kartavyasya iti kartavyatā kāṅkṣasya vacanam prakaraṇam prārambhaḥ  hi sa tasyāḥ  vacana kriyāyāḥ na eṣa vidhi ādiḥ  vidhi anta apekṣaḥ vākyam tu uktam eva tayoḥ  virodhe kim udāharaṇam sūkta vāka nigadaḥ tatra hi paurṇamāsī devatā amāvāsyā devatāḥ  ca āmnātāḥ tāḥ paraspareṇa eka vākyatām na abhyupayanti tatra liṅga sāmarthyāt  paurṇamāsī prayogāt  indra agni śabda utkraṣṭavyaḥ  amāvāsyāyām prayoktavyaḥ atha idānīm saṃdihyate yaḥ  asya śeṣaḥ avīvṛdhetām mahojyāyaḥ krātām iti sa kim yāvat  kṛtvas  sūktavāke samāmnātaḥ tāvat  kṛtva ubhayoḥ paurṇamāsyam āvāsyayoḥ prayoktavyaḥ prakaraṇam balavattaram iti uta yatra indra agni śabda utkṛṣya nītaḥ tatra eva prayoktavyaḥ vākyam balavattaram iti evam sarveṣu saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat  prāptam tulya bale ete kāraṇa iti kutas  itaratra api  ākāṅkṣā itaratra api tulyāyām ākāṅkṣāyām na asti vinigamanāyām hetuḥ tasmāt  tulya bala iti athavā vākyam durbalam bādhitam hi tad liṅgena iti  evam prāpte brūmaḥ prakaraṇāt  vākyam balīyaḥ katham artha viprakarṣāt  kaḥ  atra artha vipra karṣaḥ vākya ekaikam padam vibhajyamānam sa ākāṅkṣam bhavati kṛtsnam paripūrṇam bhavati tatra pratyakṣa eka vākya bhāvaḥ prakaraṇe tu  apratyakṣaḥ katham itikartavya tā kāṅkṣasya samīpa upanipatitam pūrṇam iti tasya prakṛtasya sa ākāṅkṣa tvam avagamyate na eka vākya bhūtam iti  anumīyate eka vākyatayā ca abhidhāna sāmarthyam avakalpya abhihitaḥ  ayam evam bhavati iti parikalpanā eṣaḥ  atra artha viprakarṣaḥ yad  vākyasya samāsannā śrutiḥ prakaraṇasya viprakṛṣṭā tasmāt  sūktavākena prastaram praharati iti paurṇamāsī devatā vācinām amāv āsyā devatā vācinām ca niṣkṛṣya prayoge tad  cheṣāṇām api niṣkṛṣya prayogaḥ tena yadi  api prakaraṇa sāmarthyāt  paurṇamāsī devatāpad śeṣāṇām amāv āsyā devatā vācibhiḥ saha eka vākyatā anumīyate pratyakṣā tu  amāv āsyā devatā padaiḥ saha na ca pratyakṣa virodhe anumānam saṃbhavati arthavati ca prakaraṇe saṃjāte na nirākāṅkṣāṇām ākāṅkṣā śakyā upapādayitum atha yad  uktam liṅgena api hi tad  bādhyate atas  prakaraṇena api bādhitavyam iti na yad  anyena api bādhyate tad  bhaṅguram anyatra api iti  avagantavyam atha bhaṅguram pramāṇam eva na abhaviṣyat kiṃcid  tu prati kasyacid  prabhāvaḥ vākyasya prakaraṇam prati bādhaka śaktiḥ  na tu liṅgam prati liṅgam prati viprakṛṣṭa artham etad  prakaraṇam prati saṃnikṛṣṭa artham tena vākyena prakaraṇam bādhyata iti atha prakaraṇasya kramasya ca virodhe kim udāharaṇam rājasūya prakaraṇe abhiṣecanīya krame śaunaḥ śepha ākhyānādi  āmnātam yadi prakaraṇam balavat  sarveṣām tad  aṅgam yadi kramaḥ abhiṣecanīyasya eva kim tāvat  prāptam tulya bala ete kāraṇa iti kutas  na tāvat  viśeṣam upalabhāmahe yena avagacchāma idam balīya iti tasmāt  tulya bale ete kāraṇa iti api ca prakaraṇam vākyena bādhitam tasmāt  bādhyeta krameṇa api iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ prakaraṇam kramāt  balīyaḥ kutas  artha viprakarṣāt  kaḥ  atra artha viprakarṣaḥ prakaraṇavataḥ sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt  tad saṃnidhāna āmnātena paripūrṇena api  avakalpeta eka vākya tvam na tu kramavataḥ krama āmnātena anekasya āmnāyamānasya saṃnidhi viśeṣa āmnāna mātram hi kramaḥ tatra saṃnidhi viśeṣa āmnānasāmarthyāt  kramavataḥ saṃnidhau   āmnātasya anupalabhyamānam eva akāṅkṣāvat tvam asti iti  avagantavyam prakaraṇe tu prakaraṇavataḥ pratyakṣam na ca prakaraṇavatā kramavatā ca yaugapadyena eka vākyatā saṃbhavati  āmnātasya iti virodhaḥ tatra prakaraṇe pratyakṣam sa ākāṅkṣa tvam krama ānumānikam bādhitum arhati sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt  eka vākya tvam eka vākya tvāt  abhidhāna sāmarthyam sāmarthyāt  chruti artha iti saṃnikṛṣṭaḥ prakaraṇasya śruti arthaḥ viprakṛṣṭaḥ kramasya tasmāt  krama karaṇayoḥ prakaraṇam balavattaram iti atha yad  uktam vākyena api hi tad  bādhitam atas  anyena api tad  bādhitavyam iti na etad  bādhitasya anugrahaḥ  nyāyyaḥ na bādhitam bādhitavyam iti atha krama samākhyayoḥ  virodhe kim udāharaṇam kim balavattaram iti pauroḍāśikam iti samākhyāte kāṇḍe sāṃnāyya krame śundhadhvam daivyāya kramaṇa iti śundhana arthaḥ  mantraḥ samāmnātaḥ tatra saṃdihyate kim samākhyānasya balīyaḥ tvāt  puroḍāśa pātrāṇām śundhane viniyoktavyaḥ uta kramasya balīyaḥ tvāt  sāṃnāyya pātrāṇām iti kim tāvat  prāptam tulya bale ete karaṇe syātām kutas  aviśeṣāt  yadi vā samākhyā eva balīyasī bādhitaḥ  hi kramaḥ prakaraṇena api iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ kramaḥ  balīyān kutas  artha viprakarṣāt  kaḥ punar  atra artha viprakarṣaḥ nirjñāte prakaraṇena kena api saha eka vākya tve yad  saṃnidhau   āmnāyate tatra ākāṅkṣām parikalpyate na eka vākyata iti  avagamyate laukikaḥ  ca śabdaḥ samākhyā na ca loka evaṃvidheṣu  artheṣu pramāṇam tasmāt  kramaḥ  balīyān iti yadi  evam bhavati  evaṃlakṣaṇakeṣu krameṇa viniyogaḥ na tu  artha aviprakarṣāt  kramaḥ  balīyān katham dvayoḥ  hi pramāṇayoḥ  balīyaḥ tvam prati saṃpradhāraṇam na ca evam sati samākhyā pramāṇam laukika tvāt  chabdasya puruṣasya pramāṇa tā bhavati iti na eṣa doṣaḥ na atra aṅga bhāvaḥ puruṣa prāmāṇyāt  gamyate pauroḍāśika śabda etasya kāṇḍasya iti  etad  atra puruṣa pramāṇakam bhavati ca asmin   arthe puruṣaḥ pramāṇam yathā sāṃnāyya krama āmnānam puruṣa pramāṇakam yathā prakaraṇam eka vākya tvam veda śabdaḥ  ca ayam iti na hi  ete anindriya viṣayā arthā upapadyante eṣu  abhiyuktānām prāmāṇyam ye tu  anindriya viṣaya aḥ  teṣu  abhiyuktā na pramāṇam tasmāt  samākhyā kāraṇam kāraṇa tve ca sati balīyaḥ tvam parīkṣyam iti ucyate artha viprakarṣas tarhi vaktavyaḥ samākhyāyāḥ ayam artha viprakarṣaḥ upadiśyate hi krame samāmnānāt  sāṃnāyya saṃbandhaḥ na upadiśyate samākhyāyām śabdam uccāryamāṇam upalabhya artha āpattyā nūnam asti iti kalpyate tasmāt  pūrvaveda artha viprakarṣāt  krameṇa samākhyā bādhyata iti atha yad  tatra tatra ucyate idam anena bādhyate idam anena iti tatra yad  bādhyate tad  kim bādhaka viṣayam prāptam uta aprāptam iti kim ca atas  yadi  aprāptam kim bādhyate atha prāptam katham śakyeta bādhitum prāptam bādhaka viṣayam pūrva vijñānam iti brūmaḥ katham sāmānyasya kāraṇasya vidyamāna tvāt  atha katham nivartate mithyājñānam iti pratyaya antaram bhavati kim tu khalu  amithyājñānasya svarūpam yasya bādhakaḥ pratyayaḥ vimṛṣyamāṇasya api na upapadyate na tad  mithyā tad  eteṣām śruti liṅga vākya prakaraṇa sthāna samākhyānām pūrvam pūrvam yad  kāraṇam tad  param param prati balīyaḥ  bhavati na etasya utpannasya vimṛṣyamāṇasya bādhakam vijñāna antaram asti tasmāt  teṣām samavāye virodhe para daurbalyam artha vipralkarṣāt  iti jyotiṣṭomam prakṛtya samāmananti tisra eva sāhnasya upasadaḥ  dvādaśa ahīnasya iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim dvādaśa upasattā jyotiṣṭoma uta ahīna iti kim tāvat  prāptam jyotiṣṭoma iti kutas  prakaraṇāt  evam prakaraṇam anugṛhītam bhavati nanu vākyena bādhyate na bādhyate ahīna śabdena jyotiṣṭomam vakṣyāmaḥ kutas  na hīyata iti  ahīnaḥ dakṣiṇayā kratu karaṇaiḥ  vā phalena vā na hīyate tena jyotiṣṭomaḥ  ahīnaḥ vā śabdena saṃśayaḥ  nivartyate apakṛṣyeta dvādaśa upasattā kutas  asaṃyoga āt  jyotiṣṭomena katham asaṃyogaḥ ahīnena eka vākya tvasya pratyakṣa tvāt  nanu jyotiṣṭoma eva gauṇaḥ  ahīnaḥ na iti  ucyate na hi mukhya saṃbhave gauṇa grahaṇam arhati nanu nañsamāsaḥ  bhaviṣyati na iti brūmaḥ tathā sati  ādi udāttaḥ  ahīna śabdaḥ  abhaviṣyat  madhya udātta s tu  ayam tasmāt  prakaraṇam bādhitvā hīnasya dharmaḥ api ca vyapadeśaḥ  bhavati tisra eva sāhnasya upasadaḥ  dvādaśa ahīnasya iti yadi  anyaḥ sāhnaḥ  anyaḥ  ca ahīnaḥ tatas  evam vyapadeśaḥ  avakalpate vidyate ca vyapadeśa vacanam tasmāt  ahīnasya iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate yuvam hi sthaḥ svaḥpatī iti dvayoḥ  yajamānayoḥ pratipadam kuryāt  ete asṛgram indava iti bahubhyaḥ  yajamānebhya iti tatra saṃdehaḥ jyotiṣṭoma eva niviśete pratipādāu uta dvi yajñam kiṃcid  kulāya ādim bahu yajñam ca dvi rātra ādim utkraṣṭavya iti kim prāptam dvitva bahutva yukte jyotiṣṭomena asaṃyogāt  utkṛṣyeyātām pratipadau na hi jyotiṣṭomasya dvau yajamānau śrūyete yathā kulāyasya etena rāja purohitau sāyujya kāmau yajeyātām iti iti ced  paśyasi parti padau   utkraṣṭavya iti na etad  evam prakaraṇam hi bādhyeta bādhyatām asaṃyogāt  dvābhyām yajamānābhyām bahubhiḥ  ca yajamānaiḥ  jyotiṣṭomasya iti ced  asati  api vacane arthāt  dvau yajamānau bhaviṣyataḥ ya ekaḥ  na śakṣyati sa mahāyaḥ sa upakraṃsyate avaśya yaṣṭavye sati yathā śakyate tathā yaṣṭavyam iti bādhitvā api kāṃcid  prāptim yajamānaḥ sahāyam upādāsyate evam prakaraṇe pratipadau bhaviṣyataḥ tasmāt  na utkraṣṭavya iti prakṛtiḥ  hi jyotiṣṭomaḥ pratyakṣāḥ  tatra dharmā āmnātāḥ na kutaścic ca udakena prāpyante kim atas  yadi  evam pratyakṣa śrutā na śakyā bādhitum vikṛtau tu ca udaka prāptāḥ santa ānumānikā bādhyeran   iti vivakṣitam hi jyotiṣṭome kartuḥ  eka tvam pratyakṣa śrutam na sāmarthyena bādhyate yatra api hi  avaśya kartavyatā śrūyate tatra api  eka eva yajamānaḥ śrūyate vasante vasante jyotiṣā yajeta iti tasmāt  jyotiṣṭomāt  utkraṣṭavya ete pratipādau   iti atha kasmāt  patnī abhiprāyam etad  na bhavati ekasyām patnyām yajamāne ca yuvam hi stha iti dvayoḥ  bahuṣu vā patnīṣu  ete asṛgram indava iti yathā kṣaume vasānau   agnim ādadhīyātām iti kṣauma vasān aparam vacanam evam iha api pratipad  vidhāna param ucyate asaṃbhavāt  tatra mukhyasya lakṣaṇā śabdaḥ puṃsaḥ vācakaḥ striyām iha tu dvi yajñe bahu yajñe ca saṃbhavati na lakṣaṇā śabdaḥ  bhavitum arhati bahubhyaḥ  yajamānebhya iti yad  api  etad  dvivacanam dvayoḥ  yajamānayoḥ  iti atra api yaḥ eka śeṣaḥ pumān striyā iti  asau   api lakṣaṇā śabda eva api ca upa asmai gāyatā nara iti pratipadoḥ  niravakāśa tvam eva syāt  tasmāt  utkraṣṭavye ete pratipadau   iti siddham darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate jāghanyā patnīḥ saṃyājayanti iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim etad  vidhānam darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ uta paśauv iti katham darśa pūrṇa māyayoḥ katham ca paśauv iti yadi jāghanyām patnī saṃyājā vidhīyante tatas  utkarṣaḥ atha patnī saṃyājeṣu jāghanī vidhīyate tatas  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  eva kim prāptam utkarṣaḥ kuta etad  utkṛṣyate jāghanyām patnī saṃyājā vidhīyanta iti katham śabdāt  patnī saṃyājānām vidhānam vākyena jāghanyāḥ śabdaḥ  ca balavān na vākyam nanu patnī saṃyājā vihitā eva satyam vihitāḥ jāghanyām idānīm punar  vidhīyante sā tad saṃbaddhā kartavyā iti  ucyate evam sati darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ patnī saṃyājā vinā api jāghanyā na viguṇāḥ jāghanī tu tatra pratipādyate tasmāt  yatra jāghanī prayojanavatī tatra tasyāḥ pratipattiḥ paśau ca sā na darśa pūrṇa māsayoḥ eka deśaḥ  ca jāghanī pratipādyamānā na paśum prayokṣyate tasmāt  asya vidhānasya utkarṣa iti jāghanī vā patnī saṃyājānām guṇa tvena vidhīyate kutas  apūrva tāt  aprāptā jāghanī patnī saṃyājānām guṇa tvena tatra sva śabdena patnī saṃyājā vihitā jāghanī saṃbandha s teṣām avihitaḥ yatra ca saṃbandhaḥ  vidhīyate tatra anyatarasya anyatra vidhānam saṃbandhaḥ  na antarīyakaḥ yad  vā saṃbandhasya vidhānam na antarīyakau saṃbandhinau yatra ubhau lakṣaṇa tvena tatra sva śabdena saṃbandhaḥ  vidhīyate yatra tu  anyataraḥ  lakṣaṇa tvena tatra ekam lakṣayitvā anyataraḥ  vidhīyate lakṣaṇa tvena ca atra patnī saṃyājāḥ katham avagamyate patnī saṃbandhān na sarvaḥ  yāgaḥ kaścid  eva tu lakṣyate yasya patnyaḥ sādhana tvena atha kasmān na jāghanīm lakṣayitvā patnī saṃyājā vidhīyante na asya apūrvasya yāgasya patnyaḥ śak yante vidhātum jāghanyām tu lakṣyamāṇāyām yāge sa patnīke vidhīyamāne vākyam bhidyeta asti tu  atra vihitaḥ sapatnī kaḥ yāgaḥ  ya patnībhiḥ  lakṣyate tasmāt  yāgam lakṣayitvā jāghanī vidhīyate yad  tu vākyena jāghanī vidhānam śrutyā yāgasya iti tad  iha yāga vidhānam na saṃbhavati iti  uktam vākya bheda prasaṅgāt  tasmāt  jāghanī vidhānam evam ced  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  vinā jāghanyā viguṇaḥ patnī saṃyāja yāgaḥ syāt  tasmāt  anutkarṣam iti atha yad  uktam eka deśaḥ  jāghanī na paśum prayokṣyate tasmāt  utkarṣa iti tad  parihartavyam na prakṛtau darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  jāghanī śāstrena ucyate evam paśoḥ  niṣpannayā jāghanyā patnī saṃyājā yaṣṭavyā iti aviśiṣṭā jāghanī vidhīyate sā saṃbhavati darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ krītyā api  ānīyamānā tasmāt  anutkarṣa iti jyotiṣṭome abhiṣavaṇa phalake prakṛtya śrūyate dīrgha some saṃtṛdyāt  dhṛtyā iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim saṃtardanam jyotiṣṭoma eva āhosvit  dīrgha kāleṣu someṣu  iti ucyate naital lupta artham prakṛtau tasmāt  na utkṛṣyeta iti āha nanu  asaṃtardanam api śrūyate asaṃtṛṇe bhavata iti ucyate krayaṇavat  vikalpiṣyate yathā hiraṇyena krīṇāti gavā krīṇāti iti evamādīnām vikalpaḥ evam atra api vikalpaḥ  bhaviṣyati saṃtardanam asaṃtardanam vā bhaviṣyati iti utkṛṣyate vā saṃtardanam gṛhyate hi viśeṣaḥ dīrgha some saṃtṛdyāt  iti jyotiṣṭomam apekṣya satrāṇi kālataḥ  dīrghāṇi bhavanti na utkṛṣyeta vā saṃtardanam jyotiṣṭomāt  evam prakaraṇam anugṛhītam bhavati dīrghasoma śabdaḥ  ca kartṛ taḥ  bhaviṣyati dīrghasya yajamānasya somaḥ  dīrghasoma iti na ca etad  asti jyotiṣṭome saṃniveśa iti dīrgha kāle some kriyeta kratu ta eva dīrgha tvam na kartṛtaḥ kutas  artha vāda anupapatteḥ dhṛtya iti  artha vādaḥ  bhavati dhāraṇāya iti  arthaḥ dīrgha kāle some punar  punar  grāvabhiḥ  abhihanyamāne soma abhiṣavaṇa phalakayoḥ  dāraṇa śaṅkāyām dhṛtya iti  arthavāda upapadyate tasmāt  utkarṣa iti idam pada uttaram sūtram kāni padāni atha kim artham saṃsthāsu na niveśaḥ tathā sati prakaraṇam anugṛhītam bhaviṣyati dīrghasoma śabdaḥ  ca dīrgha kālaḥ  hi  agniṣṭomam apekṣya ukthi ādiṣu saṃsthāsu soma iti ucyate na saṃsthāsu dīrgha kāla tve api some arthavāda upapadyate tāvān eva hi tatra somaḥ  daśa muṣṭīḥ  mimīta iti vacanāt  tatra dhāraṇe na viśeṣaḥ kaścid  tasmāt  utkarṣa eva na ca etad  asti utkarṣa iti prakaraṇa anugrahāt  anutkarṣaḥ dīrghasoma śabdaḥ  ca dīrgha kāla tvāt  upapadyate tatra api  adhikaḥ  agniṣṭomāt  somaḥ pradānāni hi vivardhante tāni  avivṛddhe pradeye na śakyāni vivardhayitum pūrṇe grahe graha śabdaḥ  bhavati tena na śakyāni nyūnāni pātrāṇi grahītum tasmāt  dāraṇa āśaṅkāyām dhāraṇam āśaṃsitavyam bhavati tatra dhṛtya iti  upapadyata iti iti ced  paśyasi saṃsthāsu  api  artha vādaḥ  avakalpate pradeya vivṛddhyā iti na etad  evam vyarthā eva hi stutiḥ  bhavet  kutas  soma aviśeṣāt yāvān eva agniṣṭome somaḥ tāvān eva ukthī ādiṣu  api saṃsthāsu ukthi ādiṣu  api daśamuṣṭiḥ  eva somaḥ  grahītavyaḥ nanu  arthāt  pradeyam vivartsyati iti daśamuṣṭiḥ sa katham śakyeta vivardhayitum tri parva iti ca parva saṃkhyā niyamān na śakyaḥ  bahu parvā grahītum tasmāt  dhāraṇā viśeṣāt  artha vāda anupapattiḥ saṃsthāsu syāt  tasmāt  utkarṣaḥ na etad  asti utkarṣa iti saṃsthāsu syāt  prakaraṇa anugrahāt arthāc ca pradeya vivṛddhyā dāraṇa śaṅkāyām arthavāda upapadyate kena prakāreṇa pradeyam vivardhiṣyata iti viprakṛṣṭa parvā somaḥ  grahīṣyate api ca tṛtīye savana aśuḥ  ekaḥ  abhiṣūyate tasya pramāṇam ca na āmnātam tam aneka parvāṇam sthūlaparvāṇam ca grahīṣyati tena pradeya vivṛddhiḥ  bhaviṣyati atas  artha vādaḥ  avakalpiṣyate tasmāt  saṃsthāsu niveśa iti siddham jyotiṣṭome pravargyam prakṛtya samāmnāyate na prathama yajñe pravṛñjyāt  dvitīye tṛtīye vā pravṛñjyāt  iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim jyotiṣṭome sarveṣu  eva prayogeṣu na pravarjitavyam uta prathame prayoge pratiṣedha iti kim tāvat  prāptam jyotiṣṭome pratiṣedhaḥ kutas  yajña saṃyogāt  prathama śabdena yajñaḥ  abhidhīyate jyotiṣṭomaḥ tasya hi prathama saṃyogaḥ evam samāmnāyate eṣa vāva prathamaḥ  yajñānām yaj jyotiṣṭomaḥ  ya etena anṣṭvā atha anyena yajeta iti yajñānām prathama  iti kṛtvā prathama śabdena jyotiṣṭomaḥ  abhidhīyate evam ca prakaraṇam anugṛhyate yadi kratoḥ  eṣa vādaḥ tasmāt  saṃkhyā yuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ  jyotiṣṭomasya pravargyam pratiṣedhet  iti na ca etad  asti yajñasya eṣa vāda iti caturṣu  api vedeṣu na prathama yajña iti evaṃsaṃjñakaḥ kaścid  yajñaḥ  asti bhavati tu prathamaḥ  yajñasya prayogaḥ kartṛ saṃyogāt  pūrvasya dvitīya ādīn apekṣya prathama śabdaḥ  bhavati sa prayogasya upapadyate na kratoḥ prayogaḥ śravaṇāt  gamyate kratuḥ prayoga saṃbaddha tvāt  śrutiḥ  ca balīyasī na lakṣaṇā tasmāt  prathame prayoge na pravarjitavyam iti atha yad  uktam jyotiṣṭomena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt tad  vacana iti laksaṇayā sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti tad  parihṛtam yad  tu prathama yajña iti yajña śabdena sāmānādhikaraṇyam tad  api yajña śabdasya yāga vacana tvāt  asmad pakṣasya ābādhakam darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ samāmananti tasmāt  pūṣā prapiṣṭa bhāgaḥ  adantakaḥ  hi sa iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim pauṣṇam peṣaṇam prakṛtau uta vikṛtau   iti kim prāptam prakṛtau   iti kutas  prakaraṇāt  nanu prakṛtau pūṣaṇam na kasyacid  dhaviṣaḥ devatām samāmananti iti ucyate prākṛtīm kāṃcid  devatām pūṣa śabdaḥ  vakṣyati evam prāpte brūmaḥ yatra pauṣṇam havir asti tatra tasya pesaṇam vidhātsum śakyam na ca prakṛtau pūṣā asti tasmāt  utkraṣṭavyam peṣaṇam iti yad  uktam kāṃcid  devatām pūṣa śabdaḥ  vakṣyati iti brūyāt  yadi  anyatra api mukhyaḥ pūṣā na syāt  nanu  anyatra kriyamāṇe prakaraṇam uparudhyeta uparudhyatām vākyam hi  asya uparodhakam athavā na eva atra saṃdehaḥ evam eva prāptam ucyate pauṣṇam peṣaṇam vikṛtau na prakṛtau   iti na asti puṣṇaḥ prakṛtau codanā iti kim artham prāptam ucyate uttaratra kathā vartiṣyate pauṣṇam peṣaṇam prakṛtau śrūyamāṇam vikṛtau   iti  uktam tatra saṃdehaḥ kim carau paśau puroḍāśe ca uta cara av eva iti kim tāvat  prāptam tad  sarvatra syāt  carau paśau puroḍāśe ca kutas  aviśeṣāt  na kaścid  viśeṣa ādhhīyate tasmāt  sarvatra iti carau pauṣṇam peṣaṇam viniyujyeta puroḍāśe tāvat  peṣaṇam arthāt  eva prāpnoti na evām yathā puroḍāśaḥ  bhavati tad  artham tāvan na vacanam paśau ca na syāt  hṛdaya ādiṣu piṣyamāṇeṣu teṣām ākāra vināśaḥ syāt  tatra kaḥ  doṣaḥ hṛdayasya agre avadyati iti na hṛdayāt  avadāyiṣyate tathā anyat  api  avadānam na yathā aśrutād avadāsyate nanu śakyate piṣṭebhyaḥ  api hṛdaya ādibhyaḥ  avadātum na iti brūmaḥ ākārā hṛdaya ādayaḥ na māṃsāni uktam etad  ākṛtiḥ śabda artha iti yadi  api punar  tadākṛtikaḥ kriyate tathā api  asya utsādana pradeśam prati muhyeyuḥ tasmāt  carau pauṣṇam peṣaṇam bhaviṣyati iti  evam artham vacanam iti ced  paśyati bhavān artha vipratiṣedhān na paśu artham iti nanu cara av api  artha vipratiṣedhaḥ viśada siddha  odane caru śabdam upacaranti piṣyamāṇaḥ  hi piṣṭakam yavāgūḥ vā syāt  khaliḥ  vā atra ucyate satyam viśada siddha  odane caru śabdaḥ prayujyate viśada siddhaḥ  caruḥ  dīyata iti na tu  asya viśada siddhiḥ  nimittam yadi viśada siddhiḥ  nimittam syāt  na piṣṭa siddhe prayujyeta tatra api hi prayujyate piṣṭaka caruḥ sādhyata iti atas  anyat  etayoḥ sāmānyam tad  nimittam tad  etad  ucyate na pakti nāma tvāt  iti na carau vipratiṣedhaḥ katham pakti nāma tvāt  pakti nāma etad  caruḥ  iti anavasrāvita antaruṣma pākena abhinirvartyasya bhavati caru śabdaḥ  vācakaḥ tena piṣṭa odane viśada odane ca prayoktāraḥ  bhavanti caruḥ  iti pakṣa uktam eva prayojanam pūrva pakṣe paśauv api peṣaṇam siddhānte cārau   eva pauṣṇam peṣaṇam vikṛtau bhavati cara av eva iti  uktam atha idānīm saṃdihyate kim eka devatye pauṣṇa etad  bhavati uta dvi devatye api iti kim dvi devatya udāharaṇam rājasūya uttare tri saṃyukte saumāpa auṣṇe ekādaśa kapāle aindrāpa auṣṇaḥ  caruḥ śyāvaḥ  dakṣiṇā iti tatra aindrāpa auṣṇa udāharaṇam kim prāptam eka devati asya eva peṣaṇam iti kutas  kevala saṃyogāt  yathā caturdhā karaṇe dvi devatye vipratiṣidhyeta dharmaḥ pūṣṇaḥ peṣaṇam na itarasya tatra yadi pūṣṇaḥ  bhāgaḥ piṣyeta apiṣṭa itarasya syāt  tatra viṣamaḥ pākaḥ  bhavet  pāka nimittaḥ  ca caru śabdaḥ sa vipratiṣidhyeta atha avirodham manyamānā aparasya api bhāgam piṃṣyuḥ bhāga saṃmohaḥ syāt  tatra kaḥ  doṣaḥ anyasya bhāgaḥ  anyasymā avadīyeta tathā yathā aśrutam kriyeta tasmāt  api  eka devatye peṣaṇam iti devatā nimittam etad  peṣaṇam śrūyate pūṣā prapiṣṭa bhāgaḥ kartavya iti sa ca dvi devatye api bhāge piṣyamāṇe prapiṣṭa bhāgaḥ kṛtaḥ  bhavati na yathā caturdhā karaṇe tatra hi tad  dhitaḥ  nirapekṣasya bhavati na sa dvitīyasya indra pīta iti samāsaḥ  api nirapekṣasya na sa dvitīyasya iha tu prapiṣṭa śabdasya bhāga śabdena saha anya padārthaḥ  bahuvrīhiḥ samāsaḥ eṣaḥ  api samarthayoḥ  eva na tu  atra dvi devatye kaścid  evaṃjātīyakaḥ  doṣaḥ tasmāt  eka devatye dvi devatye api vā cara av asya bhāgaḥ peṣṭavya eva liṅgam api  evam bhavati tasmāt  pūṣā prapiṣṭa bhāgaḥ  adantakaḥ  hi iti devatā nimittam peṣaṇam iti stutiḥ  darśayati tathā saumāpa auṣṇam carum nirvapen nema piṣṭam paśu kāma iti nema piṣṭa tām darśayati tathā ardham piṣṭam ardham apiṣṭam bhavati dvi devatya tvāya iti devatā nimittam eva peṣaṇam darśayati idam pada uttaram sūtram nema piṣṭam bhavati iti kasmāt  etad  na vacanam iti ucyate yadi vacanam etad  bhavet  saumāpa auṣṇa mātram anūdya sarvatra peṣaṇam vidadhyāt  carau paśau puroḍāśe ca tatra somāpauṣṇasya caru saṃbandhe nema piṣṭa saṃbandhe ca ubhayasmin vidhīyamāne vākyam bhidyeta tasmāt  yaḥ  yaḥ saumāpa auṣṇas tatra tatra nema piṣṭa tā tam prati saumāpa auṣṇa mātram prati śāstravat tvam ardha peṣaṇasya puroḍāśe arthāt  sarva peṣaṇe prāpte artha abhāvāt  ca paśau carau vāpeṣaṇe prāpte vacanam idam bhavet  tatra caru śabdaḥ  na vivakṣita sva arthaḥ syāt  pradarśana arthaḥ kalpyeta peṣaṇa anuvāda pakṣe punar  na eṣa virodhaḥ  bhavati tasmāt  bhavati  eva liṅgam nanu  aṅga nāśa bhayāt paśoḥ  apeṣaṇam na iti brūmaḥ ardha peṣaṇe na aṅga nāśaḥ  apiṣṭād avadāsyate peṣaṇam ca adṛṣṭa artham eka devatye vā pauṣṇam peṣaṇam bhavitum arhati na aindrāpa auṣṇe kutas  na eṣa devatā dharmaḥ  vidhīyate pūṣṇaḥ  bhāgaḥ piṣṭa upayoktavya iti kasya tarhi arthasya dharmaḥ kaḥ punar  arthaḥ yāgaḥ katham avagamyate na devatā dharma iti ucyate na hi tasyāḥ  bhāgaḥ  asti nanu yad  devatāyai dīyate tad  tasyāḥ  bhāgaḥ  bhavati ucyate etad  dhi devatām uddiśya tyajyate na ca tyāga mātreṇa devatā svatvam bhavati parigrahaṇena hi sva svāmi saṃbandha āpadyate na ca parigṛhītam devatayā iti kiṃcana pramāṇam asti yaḥ  ca yam bhajate sa tasya bhāgaḥ na ca havir devatā bhajate tasmāt  na asti pūṣṇaḥ  bhāgaḥ atha api kathaṃcid  bhavet  bhāgaḥ tathā api na devatāyāḥ  dharmaḥ peṣaṇam bhavitum arhati niṣprayojanaḥ  hi tathā syāt  ayāga dharma tvāt  katham tarhi prakaraṇa antare samāmnātaḥ  yāga dharmaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti ucyate vākya saṃyogāt  nanu ca devatayā eṣa saṃyogaḥ śrūyate na yāgena iti ucyate bhāga abhāvāt  anarthaka tvāt  ca na devatā saṃyoga iti  uktam tathā api tu yathā yāga saṃbandhaḥ  bhavati tathā vaktavyam tad  ucyate ayam atra pūṣṇaḥ  bhāgaḥ  yaḥ pūṣaṇam uddiśya tyajyate yasya dravyasya tyāge pūṣā devatā na ca aindrāpa auṣṇe bhavati pūṣā devatā na sa caruḥ pūṣṇaḥ sva tvena saṃbadhyate tasmāt  aindrāpa auṣṇe na kaścid  asti pūṣṇaḥ  caruṇā saṃbandhaḥ kevale tu pūṣaṇi devatā bhūte tasmai saṃkalpitaḥ  bhāgaḥ  bhavati katham yam uddiśya saṃkalpaḥ  bhavati sa tasya bhāga iti prasiddhiḥ  eṣā tena yadi  api pūṣā svena uccāraṇena indra apūṣṇoḥ  upakārakam uccāraṇam kurvan   upakāra kaḥ  bhavet  tathā api na tasya dvi devatyaḥ  bhāga iti  ucyate asaṃkalpanāt  kevale pūṣaṇi devatāyām caroḥ peṣaṇam kriyate na aindrāpa auṣṇeṣu dvi devatyeṣu  iti yad  uktam adantakaḥ  hi iti devatā dharmam darśayati iti arthavāda eṣa itarasmin   api pakṣa upapadyate atha aparam yad  kāraṇam uktam nema piṣṭam iti dvi devatye peṣaṇam darśayati ardha piṣṭam bhavati  ardham apiṣṭam dvi devatya tvāya iti devatā dharmam darśayati iti atra ucyate evam sati vacanam idam aprāpte bhavati iti nanu  aneka artha vidhidhānam ekam vākyam prāpnoti ucyate sati pakṣa antare aneka artha vidhiḥ pakṣa antara āśrayaṇena parihriyate asati punar  pakṣa antare uccāraṇa anarthakya prasaṅga parijihīrṣayā aneka artham vākyam abhyupagantavyam bhavati tasmāt  na dvi devatye peṣaṇam iti siddham darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  āmnātam nivītam manuṣyāṇām prācīnāvītam pitṝṇām upavītam devānām upavyayate deva lakṣmam eva tad  kuruta iti nivītam manuṣyāṇām iti  atra saṃdehaḥ kim ayam vidhiḥ  uta artha vāda iti yadā vidhiḥ tadā kim ayam puruṣa dharma uta karma dharmaḥ atha yad  prakaraṇe manuṣyāṇām tatra vidhiḥ uta manuṣya pradhāne karmaṇi niviśata iti kim prāptam vidhiḥ  manuṣya dharmaś ca iti yadi vidhiḥ  evam apūrvam artham vidadhat  arthavān bhavati itaratha artha vāda mātram anarthakam vidhiḥ  ced  puruṣa dharmaḥ  nivītam manuṣyāṇām iti puruṣa pradhānaḥ  nirdeśaḥ katham avagamyate na atra manuṣyā vidhīyante manuṣyāṇām nivītam vidhīyate na ca avihitam aṅgam bhavati yadi manuṣyā api vidhīyeran vākyam bhidyeta tasmāt  nivītam manuṣyāṇām upakārakam nanu prakaraṇāt  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  upakārakam prakaraṇāt  dhi vākyam balavattaram api ca guṇa bhūteṣu manuṣyeṣu kāraka saṃbandhasya vivakṣita tvāt  tṛtīyā bhavet  ṣaṣṭhī tu  eṣā saṃbandha lakṣaṇā tatra guṇa bhūteṣu manuṣyeṣu manuṣya grahaṇam na eva kartavyam syāt  manuṣyaiḥ  eva tad  kriyamāṇam kriyeta manuṣya pradhāna pakṣe tu kartavyam apadeśa iti jñāyamānasya vacanam sa eṣa na vidhiḥ anuvāda eṣaḥ kutas  arthasya vidyamāna tvāt  prāpta eva arthaḥ yad  nivītam manuṣyāṇām nivītam hi manuṣyāḥ prāyaśas  sva artham kurvanti tasmāt  anuvādaḥ vidhiḥ  eva bhavet  tathā prayojanavān itarathā vāda mātram anarthakam pūrvavān anuvādaḥ  bhavati ayam tu  apūrvaḥ yad  niyamena nivyātavyam iti yad  uktam vidhiḥ  iti etad  gṛhyate yad  tu manuṣya dharma iti tad  na anumatam kratu dharmaḥ  ayam prakaraṇāt  prakṛtyā eva hi karma prāyeṣu dharmeṣu ucyamāneṣu  etad  abhidhīyate tasmāt  karma dharmaḥ nivītam manuṣyāṇām iti  asya vākya śeṣaḥ samākhyā ādhvaryavam iti yadi darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śeṣaḥ tatas  adhvaryuṇā kartavyam tatra samākhyā anugṛhīṣyate ucyate prakaraṇāt  samākhyānāt  ca karma dharmaḥ  vijñāyate vākyān manuṣya dharmaḥ tasmāt  utkarṣam arhati na iti brūmaḥ prakaraṇa eva abhiniviśamānasya manuṣya pradhāna tā avakalpiṣyate katham yad  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  manuṣya pradhānam tatra nivekṣyate anvāhārya karmaṇi prakaraṇam ca evam anugrahīṣyate vākyam ca na etad  asti prakaraṇe niveśa iti manuṣya pradhāne karmaṇi nivītam syāt  ātithye kutas  tulyavat  prasaṃkhyānāt  tulyāni ca etāni prasaṃkhyāyante yad  tāvat  upavītam devānām upavyayata iti tad  prakṛtayoḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  upavītam vidadhāti yad  prācīnāvītam piṭṝṇām iti tad  pitṛ pradhāne karmaṇi prācīnāvītam vidadhāti yad  api  etad  nivītam manuṣyāṇām iti tad  api  ātithye nirapekṣam vidadhāti katham gamyate manuṣya pradhāne vidadhāti iti manuṣyāṇām iti ṣaṣṭhī antena saṃbandhāt  manuṣyāṇām eva prāpnoti na manuṣya pradhāne ucyate manuṣyāṇām kalpyamāne phalam kalpanīyam manuṣya pradhāne punar  ṣaṣṭhī bhaviṣyati saṃbandhaḥ  ca evam avakalpiṣyate phalam ca evam na kalpanīyam tad  uktam sameṣu vākya bhedaḥ syāt  iti nanu manuṣya pradhānena saha eka vākyatām prāptam punar  prakṛtābhyām darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām eka vākyatām yāsyati na hi dvau saṃbandhau   ekasmin vākye vidhīyete bhidyeta hi tathā vākyam itarasya manuṣya grahaṇasya nivīta saṃbandha artha tvāt tena eva saha eka vākyatā bhaviṣyati pratyakṣeṇa śabdena tad  eka vākyatayā ca arthavat tve sati na prakṛtena eka vākyatau  akalpyate tasmāt  prakaraṇam bādhitva ātithye nivekṣyata iti na etad  asti vidhiḥ sa ca manuṣya pradhāne karmaṇi iti manuṣyāṇām iti manuṣya saṃbandhaḥ  atra śrūyate na manuṣya pradhānena karmaṇā saṃbandhaḥ manuṣya prādhānye ca sati phalam kalpanīyam ātithya karmaṇā tu  anirdiṣṭena aprakṛtena anumeyena saṃbadhyeta tatra kaḥ  doṣaḥ prakaraṇāt  utkṛṣyeta saṃbhavan   tatra katham saṃbhava iti ced  arthavāda eṣaḥ sa prakṛtam stuvan prakaraṇe saṃbhaviṣyati vidhiḥ san   utkṛṣyeta tasmāt  na vidhiḥ  manuṣya pradhāne karmaṇi iti itas  ca na vidhiḥ kutas  vidhinā eka vākya tvāt upavyayate deva lakṣmam eva tad  kurute iti  eṣa vidhiḥ anena asya saha eka vākyatā bhavati yadi itaraḥ  api vidhiḥ syāt  vākyam bhidyeta na hi vidheś ca vidheś ca eka vākya tā bhavati vacana vyakti bhedāt  tatra eka vākya tā rūpam bādhyeta kim eka vākyatā rūpam nivītam manuṣyāṇām iti prāpta anuvādaḥ prāptasya kim arthena punar  vacanam upavītastuti arthena katham upavīta stutiḥ nivītam ayogyam deva karmaṇi darśa pūrṇamāsa saṃjñake manuṣyāṇām hi tad  tathā prācīnāvītam pitṝṇām na deva karmaṇi upavītam tu tatra yogyam tasmāt  upavyātavyam iti yathā yādṛśaḥ  asya veśaḥ tādṛśaḥ  naṭānām yādṛśaḥ  devadattasya tādṛśaḥ  brāhmaṇānām iti devadatta veśa praśaṃsā artham itaraveśa saṃkīrtanam evam iha api  upavyānaḥ tuti arthena nivīta saṃkīrtanam na asti  atra vidhāyakaḥ śabdaḥ nivītam manuṣyāṇām kartavyam iti ātithya prayoga vacanam tasya kartavyatā vidhāyakam iti ced  na etad  evam stuti arthena arthavat tve sati na śakyam kalpayitum parokṣam hi tad  ānarthakya parijihīrṣayā kalpyeta parihṛte tu  ānarthakya iha punar  na kiṃcid  kalpanīyam tasmāt  artha vādaḥ evam ca vākyena aviruddham prakaraṇam arthavat  bhavati upavītam liṅga darśanāt  sarva dharmaḥ syāt  b na vā prakaraṇāt  tasya darśanam c vidhiḥ  vā syāt  apūrva tvāt  d udak tvam
