ca apūrva tvāt  e sataḥ  vā liṅga darśanam f vidhis tu dhāraṇe apūrva ṛtvāt  jyotiṣṭomam prakṛtya śrūyate prācīm devāḥ  abhajanta dakṣiṇām pitaraḥ pratīcīm manuṣyā udīcīm asurā iti apareṣām udīcīm rudrā iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim vidhiḥ  uta artha vādaḥ vidhiḥ san kim manuṣya dharmaḥ uta karma dharmaḥ atha vā prakaraṇe manuṣya pradhāne karmaṇi niveśaḥ kim vā ātithya iti kim tāvat  prāptam diś vibhāgaḥ  ca tadvat  saṃbandhasya artha hetu tvāt  ya eṣa diś vibhāgaḥ sa nivītavat  vicāryaḥ yaḥ  nivīte pūrva pakṣaḥ sa iha pūrva pakṣaḥ yaḥ  madhyamaḥ sa madhyamaḥ yaḥ siddhāntaḥ sa siddhāntaḥ arthavat tvāt  vidhiḥ  manuṣya saṃbandhān manuṣya dharma iti pūrva pakṣaḥ pratyaṅmukhā udaṅmukhā vā pṛṣṭhata ādityam prāṃśu padārthān anutiṣṭhanti manuṣyā iti  anuvādaḥ vidhiḥ  eva prakaraṇa anugrahāt  ca jyotiṣṭoma dharmaḥ vākya prakaraṇa anugrahāya jyotiṣṭome manuṣya pradhāne dakṣiṇā vyāpāre niveśa iti  aparaḥ pakṣaḥ bhinna tvāt  vākyānām ātithye niveśa iti  aparam matam artha vādaḥ  ayam prakaraṇa anugrahāya prācīna vaṃśam karoti iti  anena vidhinā eka vākya tvasya pratyakṣa siddha tvāt  iti siddhāntaḥ darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  āmnātam yad  puruṣi ditam tad  devānām yad  antarā tad  manuṣyāṇām yad  sa mūlam tad  pitṝṇām iti tathā yaḥ  vidagdhaḥ sa nairṛtaḥ yaḥ  aśṛtaḥ sa raudraḥ ya śṛtaḥ sa sa devatyaḥ tasmāt  avidahatā śrapayitavyam sa devatyāya iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate yad  pūrṇam tad  manuṣyāṇām upari adhas  devānām adhas  pitṝṇām iti tathā ghṛtam devānām mastu pitṝṇām niṣpakvam manuṣyāṇām iti tatra manuṣya saṃbaddheṣu raudre ca saṃdehaḥ kim manuṣyāṇām dharmā vidhayaḥ uta karma dharmā anūvādāḥ atha yad  prakaraṇam manuṣya pradhānam raudram ca tatra niviśeran uta ātithye uta artha vāda iti kim tāvat  prāptam etāni  api tadvat  yaḥ  nivīte pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ sa eteṣām pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ yaḥ  madhyamaḥ sa madhyamaḥ yaḥ siddhāntaḥ sa eva siddhāntaḥ arthavat tvān manuṣya saṃbandha āt  ca vidhayaḥ  manuṣya dharmāś ca iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ upari mūle ca aniya māl lāghavam aśṛtam roga tvāt  raudram pūrṇe api ślakṣṇa tvāl lāghavam evam ghṛtam śirasi nihitam manuṣyāṇām sukha karam eva artha prāpta tvāt  anuvāda iti  uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ vidhiḥ karma dharma prāyāt  samākhyānāt  ca karma dharma iti pakṣaḥ anvāhārye dakṣiṇāsu ca iti vākya prakaraṇa anugrahāt pakṣaḥ ātithya iti vākya bheda prasaṅgāt  arthavāda iti prakaraṇāt  vidhinā eka vākya tvāt  iti parva pratilunāti upari vilād gṛhṇāti navanītena abhyaṅkte avidahatā śrapayitavyam iti  ebhiḥ saha eṣām eka vākya bhāvaḥ tasmāt  ete na vidhayaḥ  artha vādā iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  āmnāyate na anṛtam vadet  iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ayam pratiṣedhaḥ  dārśa paurṇamāsikasya padārthasya prakaraṇa eva niveśaḥ atha prāyeṇa prāptasya karmaṇaḥ puruṣam prati pratiṣedhaḥ puruṣa dharmaḥ  ayam iti kim prāptam puruṣa dharmaḥ syāt  puruṣasya ayam upadiśyate na darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ kutas  puruṣa prayatnasya śravaṇāt  vadet  iti vadanam anutiṣṭhet  iti śrutyā gamyate tasya puruṣa saṃbandhaḥ śrutyā eva karma saṃbandhaḥ prakaraṇāt  śrutiḥ  ca prakaraṇāt  balīyasī itarathā vadanam bhavati iti  etāvatī  arthe vadanam anutiṣṭhet  iti  avivakṣita sva arthaḥ para arthaḥ  vidhi arthaḥ  bhavet  puruṣasya upadeśe punar  vivakṣita sva artha  eva śabdaḥ tasmāt  puruṣasya upadeśaḥ yasya ca upadeśaḥ tasya ayam pratiṣedhaḥ sa ca ayam artha upanayana kāla eva puruṣasya pratiṣiddhaḥ tena saṃyogena ayam nitya anuvādaḥ nanu  eṣā śruti s tasyāḥ smṛteḥ  mūlam na eṣā tasyāḥ  mūlam bhavitum arhati yadi iyam tad mūlikā bhavet  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  iti smaryeta upanayana kāla eva ca asya upadeṣṭāraḥ  bhavanti api ca puruṣa dharma iti  upadiśanti tasmāt  na eṣā smṛtiḥ  atas  śruteḥ  iti vidhiḥ  vāyam darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  na anṛtam vadet  iti na anuvādaḥ kutas  saṃyoga antarāt niyama anuṣṭhānena puruṣasya saṃbandhaḥ smaryate padārtha pratiṣedhena iha saṃyogaḥ puruṣasya katham anya t  chrūyamāṇam anyasya anuvādaḥ  bhaviṣyati tasmāt  vidhiḥ pratiṣedhasya ayam āha gṛhṇāma etad  vidhiḥ  iti puruṣa dharma iti tu gṛhṇāmaḥ puruṣa prayatnasya śruta tvāt  atra brūmaḥ sarveṣu  ākhyāteṣu kriyā anuṣṭhānam śrūyate na kārakam kiṃcid  katham etad  gamyate pratyayāt  yatas  kriyām anuṣṭheyām pratīmaḥ nanu kartāram api pratiyanti satyam pratiyanti na tu śabdāt  kutas  tarhi arthāt  yadā kriyā anuṣṭhātavyā vidhīyate tadā arthāt kārakavyāpāraḥ  gamyate yaḥ  ca arthāt  gamyate na sa śrautaḥ yaḥ  ca na śrautaḥ  na sa vākyāt  gamyate katham asau prakaraṇam bādhiṣyate āha prakṛti pratyayau pratyaya artham saha brūta iti  ācārya upadeśāt kartā śabda arthaḥ karma ca iti  avagamyate kartari śap karmaṇi yag iti pratyaya artham kartāram karma ca samām ananty ācāryāḥ tasmāt  chabda arthaḥ kartā karma ca iti ucyate na ācārya vacanāt  sūtra kāra vacanāt  vā śabda arthaḥ  bhavati pratyayāt  asau gamyate anuṣṭheyā ca kriyā pratītā satī kārakāṇi pratyāyayati iti  avagatam etad  api ca na eva kartā pratyaya arthaḥ karma vā iti  ācāryā āhuḥ nanu kartari karmaṇi ca lakāraḥ śrūyate na asau kartari karmaṇi vā śrūyate kim tu  ekasmin eka vacanam dvayoḥ  dvivacanam bahuṣu bahuvacanam iti tatra aparam vacanam tatra evam abhisaṃbandhaḥ kriyate ekasmin kartari dvayoḥ kartroḥ  bahuṣu kartṛṣu  iti evam karmaṇi  ekatva ādi saṃbandhaḥ tatra na evam bhavati kartari bhavati  ekasminś ca iti katham tarhi kartary ekasmin   eka vacanam kartuḥ  ekatva iti  arthaḥ evam dvi tve bahu tve karmaṇi ca evam varṇyamāne laukika nyāya anugataḥ sūtra arthaḥ  varṇitaḥ  bhavati sūtra akṣarāṇi ca nyāya anugatāni bhavanti āgamaḥ  api ca ayam eva yadā eka tvāt ayaḥ  vibhakti arthāḥ tadā karma ādayaḥ  viśeṣaṇa tvena iti nanu  etad  api  asti yadā karma ādayaḥ  vibhakti arthāḥ tadā eka tvāt ayaḥ  viśeṣaṇa tvena iti ucyate artha prāptā hi karma ādayaḥ  te na bhavanti śabdasya abhidheya bhūtāḥ na tu  eka tvāt ayaḥ  arthāt  prāpnuvanti tena te śabda artha bhūtāḥ tasmāt  api viśeṣaṇam ekatva ādayaḥ tathā api viśeṣaṇam eva abhidhīyate yathā hiraṇyamālina ṛtvijaḥ pracaranti iti hiraṇya māli tvam viśeṣaṇa tvena tathā api tad  eva vidhīyate tasmāt  kartuḥ  eka tvam śabda arthaḥ  na kartā nanu kartuḥ  eka tvāt  eka vacanam kartuḥ  dvi tvāt  dvivacanam kartuḥ  bahu tvāt  bahuvacanam tena nūnam kartā śabda artha iti gamyate ucyate na etad  anumānāc chakyam kartā anuṣṭheya kriyā avagamād eva avagamyata iti pratyakṣam tad  tāvat  kenacid  na bādhyate ekavacana nirdeśe kartṛ eka tvam gamyate dvivacana nirdeśe kartuḥ  dvi tvam bahuvacana nirdeśe kartṛ bahu tvam tad  api pratyakṣam katara t  atra anumāṇam bādhitum arhati iti yathā ākṛti vacane śabde dvivacane dravya bhedaḥ  avagamyate eka vacane dravya eka tvam evam iha api draṣṭavyam tasmāt  na śrautaḥ na ced  chrautaḥ na prakaraṇam bādhiṣyate yad  tu puruṣa prayatnaḥ  anartha kaḥ  bhavati karma dharma pakṣe prayoga vacanena kartavyatā vacanāt  iti tad  ucyate aṅgam sat  prakaraṇena gṛhyeta na ca avihitam aṅgam bhavati tasmāt  aṅga tvāya vidhātavyam asmin   api pakṣe atas  manyāmahe prākaraṇikasya ayam niṣedha iti tasmāt  tad  aṅgam yad  anṛtam tad  na vācyam iti tena yad  saṃkalpitam tad  aṅgam tad  eva kartavyam vrīhim ayam saṃkalpya na yava mayaḥ pradeyaḥ āha yadā ubhayoḥ  api pakṣayoḥ  na anṛtam vaditavyam tadā kaḥ  vicāreṇa artha iti ucyate pūrvasmin pakṣe puruṣa dharmaḥ tatra bhraṃśe smārtam prāyaścittam siddhānte darśa pūrṇamāsa dharmaḥ tatra bhraṃśe yājurvedikam prāyaścittam jyotiṣṭome śrūyate aṅgirasaḥ  veta uttamāḥ suvargam lokam āyante apsu dīkṣā tapasī prāveśayan   tīrthe snāti tīrtham eva hi sajātānām bhavati iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  āmnāyate tasmāt  jañjabhyamānaḥ  anubrūyāt  mayi dakṣa kratū iti prāṇa apānau   eva ātmandhatta iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ayam dharmaḥ prakaraṇe niviśate uta puruṣasya upadiśyata iti kim tāvat  prāptam ahīnavat  puruṣaḥ tad artha tvāt eṣa vidhiḥ prakaraṇāt  utkṛṣyeta kutas  puruṣa śruteḥ brūyāt  iti puruṣa prayatnasya vivakṣita tvāt  nanu prakaraṇam bādhyate ucyate bādhyatām prakaraṇam vākyam tu  asya bādhakam jañjabhyamāna saṃyogāt  prakaraṇāt  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  upadiśyata iti gamyate vākya at  jañjabhyamānasya vākyam ca prakaraṇāt  balīyaḥ tasmāt  utkṛṣyeta iti phalam api  āmananti prāṇa apānau   eva ātmandhatta iti sa ca saṃyogaḥ  bādhyate tasmāt  puruṣa dharmaḥ prakaraṇāt  utkṛṣyeta ahīnavat  yathā hīna saṃyogāt  dvādaśa upasattā prakaraṇāt  utkṛṣyate evam jañjabhyamāna saṃyogān mayi dakṣa kratū iti vacanam na vā utkraṣṭavyam kutas  prakaraṇa viśeṣāt  prakaraṇa yukta eva jañjabhyamānaḥ  vacanena saṃskriyate yathā yava ādi dravyam prokṣaṇā dinā nanu na śaknoti prakaraṇam jañjabhyamāna śabdam eka deśe avasthāpayitum vākyam hi prakaraṇāt  balavattaram iti ucyate na brūmaḥ  jañjabhyamāna śabdaḥ prakaraṇena aprākaraṇikāt  puruṣān nivartyata iti kim tu phalam tatra kalpanīyam nanu pratyakṣam śrūyate phalam prāṇa apānau   eva ātmandhatta iti na iti brūmaḥ na atra vidhāyakam śabdam upalabhāmahe ya eṣaḥ prāṇa apānau   eva ātmandhatta iti vartamāna apadeśa eṣa na vidhāyakaḥ stāvakas tu bhavati mantra vacanasya tasmāt  darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām anyatra etad  na phalavat  atas  puruṣasya darśa pūrṇamāsau kurvataḥ saṃskāra karma iti gamyate āha puruṣa saṃskāra karma iti gṛhyate darśa pūrṇamāsau   eva kurvata iti  etad  na katham yaḥ  api hi  anyatra darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām jañjabhyate saḥ  api jañjabhyamāna śabdena ucyata eva na ca prakaraṇena vyāvartyata iti  etad  uktam tasmāt  utkṛṣyate atra ucyate na eva vyāvartyate saṃskṛtena tu tena na asti prayojanam nanu prakaraṇe puruṣa saṃskāreṇa api na asti prayojanam ucyate saṃskṛta puruṣaḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau   anuṣṭhāsyati āha utkarṣe api sati saṃskṛtaḥ  anyat  anuṣṭhāsyati ucyate na anyasya saṃskāraḥ  guṇa u bhavati aprakṛta tvāt  āha prakṛtasya api na guṇaḥ vākyena puruṣa dharma iti  avagamāt  ucyate ānarthakyān na puruṣa dharmaḥ  avagamyate tasmāt  asya prakṛtābhyām darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām eka vākyatā na anyena phalavatā api karmaṇā prakaraṇa abhāvāt  tasmāt  na utkarṣaḥ yad  tu prakaraṇe niveśa etasmin pakṣe brūyāt  iti  anuṣṭhāna vacanam avivakṣita sva artham iti evam sati ati anuvādaḥ  bhaviṣyati na puruṣa saṃbandha vidhānasya prayojanam asti iti atha yad  upavarṇitam dvādaśa upasattā yathā utkṛṣyate tathā idam api  utkraṣṭavyam iti ucyate tad  dhi vākyena ahīnānām vyapadiśyate phalavantaḥ  ca ahīnāḥ na ca tatra jyotiṣṭome ahīna śabdaḥ gauṇa tvāt  vyapadeśāt  ca tisra eva sāhnasya upasadaḥ  dvādaśa ahīnasya iti tatas  yuktam dvādaśa upasattā yad  prakaraṇāt  utkṛṣyate na tu  iha puruṣa saṃbandhaḥ  niṣprayojana tvāt  anyasya ca prayojanavataḥ prakaraṇe abhāvāt  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate devāḥ  vai śaṃyum bārhaspatyam abruvan havyam naḥ vahā iti prakṛtya vacanam idam bhavati kim me prajāyā iti te abruvan yaḥ  brāhmaṇāya avaguret  tam śatena yātayād yaḥ  nihanat  tam sahasreṇa yātayāt  yaḥ  lohitam karavat  yāvataḥ praskandya pāṃsūn saṃgṛhaṇāt  tāvataḥ saṃvatsarān pitṛ lokam na prajānīyāt  iti tasmāt  na brāhmaṇāya avaguren na hanyān na lohitam kuryāt  iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  avagoraṇa pratiṣedhaḥ uta puruṣa asya upadiśyata iti kim prāptam prakaraṇāt  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  avagoraṇa ādi pratiṣedhaḥ na darśa pūrṇamāsya ūr brāhmaṇasya avagoritavyam vadhaḥ  vā kāryaḥ  lohitam vā praskandanīyam anya upāya āsthātavya ānataye te na anvāhāryeṇa ānam anti iti prakaraṇāt  prāpnoti evam prāpte brūmaḥ śaṃyau ca prakaraṇāt  utkarṣaḥ kasmāt  sarva paridānāt sarva avasthasya brāhmaṇasya ayam pratiṣedha uktaḥ na darśa pūrṇamāsa gatena eva na avagoraṇa ādi kartavyam iti nanu prakaraṇāt  darśa pūrṇamāsa dharmaḥ  ayam satyam prakaraṇāt  evam vākyena avaguramāṇasya dharmaḥ vākyam ca prakaraṇāt  balīyaḥ nanu jañjabhyamānasya iva prakaraṇe niveśaḥ  bhavet  na iti  ucyate tatra phalam kalpanīyam iha kḷptam asti hi  atra vidhāyaka vibhaktiḥ śatena yātayāt  sahasreṇa yātayāt  svargam lokam prajānīyāt  iti tasmāt  utkarṣa evaṃjātīyakasya iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate malavat  vāsasā na saṃvadet  na asyāḥ  annam adya āt  iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim malavat  vāsasā saha darśa pūrṇamāsa aṅgasya saṃvādasya pratiṣedhaḥ uta puruṣasya sarvatra pratiṣedha iti kim prāptam prakaraṇāt  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ pratiṣedha vidhiḥ evam prāpte brūmaḥ malavat  vāsasā saha saṃvāda utkṛṣyeta prakaraṇāt  kasmāt  prāc aparodhāt  evam śrūyate yasya vratye ahani patnī  anālambhukā syāt  tām aparudhya yajeta iti patnyā ca saha saṃvādaḥ  adhvaryoḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  asti patni patnī  eṣa te loka iti prasajyamānaḥ pratiṣidhyeta sa ca aprāpta eva prāc aparodhāt  apanīyatām yāgam anutiṣṭhatām katham saṃvādaḥ prasajyeta yatas  pratiṣedham arhet  tasmāt  utkṛṣyeta malavat  vāsasā saha saṃvādaḥ anna pratiṣedhaḥ  ca bhavati na asyāḥ  annam adya āt  abhyañjanam vai striyā annam iti  upagamana pratiṣedha eṣa vidhīyate sa ca prakaraṇe na prasakta iti prakaraṇāt  utkṛṣṭaḥ puruṣa dharma eṣa niścīyate anārabhya śrūyate tasmāt  suvarṇam hiraṇyam bhāryam durvarṇaḥ  asya bhrātṛvyaḥ  bhavati iti su vāsasā bhavitavyam rūpam eva bibharti iti tatra kim prakaraṇa dharma uta puruṣa dharma iti saṃśayaḥ atra ucyate aprakaraṇe tu tad  dharmaḥ tatas  viśeṣāt  puruṣa dharma evaṃjātīyakaḥ syāt  kutas  tatas  prakaraṇa adhītāt  viśeṣaḥ  asya na ayam prakaraṇa adhītaḥ yadi  aprakaraṇe samāmnātaḥ sarva prakaraṇa dharmaḥ syāt  aprakaraṇe samāmnānam na kaṃcid  viśeṣam kuryāt  tasmāt  evaṃjātīyakaḥ puruṣa dharma iti tuśabdaḥ pakṣa vyāvṛttau na puruṣa dharmaḥ  bhavet  agnihotra ādīnām śeṣaḥ syāt  kasmāt  adravya tvāt  na atra dravya devatam śrūyate yad  chravaṇāt  bhāryam yaṣṭavyam iti parikalpyeta asati tu dravya devatā saṃbandhe vibhartiḥ  ayam dhāraṇā vacanaḥ saṃskāra vācī saṃskāraḥ  ca śeṣa bhūtasya avakalpate na anyathā tasmāt  karmaṇām agnihotra ādīnām śeṣaḥ evam su vāsasā bhavitavyam iti ādhvaryavam iti veda saṃyogaḥ śeṣa bhūtasya yujyate śeṣa bhūtaḥ  hi  adhvaryuṇā kriyate na puruṣa dharmaḥ darśa pūrṇamāsa ādīnām hi karmaṇām sa aṅgānām aṅgānām ardhvayuḥ kartā tasmāt  api karma dharmā evaṃjātīyakā iti dravya paraś ca atra bhavati nirdeśaḥ suvarṇam bhāryam iti dvitīya artha saṃyogāt dravya saṃskāraḥ  ca karma śeṣa pakṣe prayojanavān anarthakaḥ puruṣa dharme syāt  vā phalena evaṃjātīyakānām saṃbandhaḥ puruṣa dharma iti  arthaḥ suvarṇasya vāsasaḥ  vā dharmaḥ  bhavan niṣprayojanaḥ syāt  nanu saṃskṛtena suvarṇena vāsasā ca karma setsyati na etad  evam suvarṇasya aṅgam na karmaṇa upakuryāt  śruti ādīnām abhāvān na karma aṅgam tasmāt  durvarṇaḥ  asya bhātṛ vyaḥ  bhavati iti evamādinā evaṃjātīyakānām phalena saṃbandhaḥ nanu vartamāna apadeśaḥ  ayam satyam evam etad  ānarthakya parihārāya phala codanayā saṃbandha eṣi tavya u bhavati anyasmāt  caiṣitavyād eka vākya gatasya vipariṇāmaḥ  laghīyān kutas  pratyakṣā tena eka vākyatā parokṣānyena vipariṇāmaḥ  ca vartamāna kālasya avivakṣā saṃbandhasya ca tātparyā adhyavasānam tasmāt  evaṃjātīyakaḥ pradhāna karma upadeśaḥ syāt  yathā prajāpati vratānām phalena saṃbandhaḥ etāvatā ha ena sā viyuktaḥ  bhavati iti evam atra api draṣṭavyam tasmāt  evaṃjātīyakaḥ puruṣa dharma iti iha karma saṃyuktā homā jaya ādaya udāharaṇam yena karmaṇetsat  tatra jayān  juhuyāt  rāṣṭrabhṛtaḥ  juhoti iti abhyātānān  juhoti iti tatra ete kim sarva karmaṇām kṛṣi ādīnām śeṣa bhūtāḥ uta vaidikānām agni hotra ādinām iti śeṣa tvam tu nirjñāta karma saṃbandhāt phala aśravaṇa āt  ca kim tāvat  prāptam sarva karmaṇām śeṣāḥ viśeṣān abhidhānāt  iti na ca etad  asti sarva karmaṇām karṣaṇa ādīnām api  aṅga bhūtā iti homā ete atas  vyavatiṣṭheran āhavanīya saṃyogaḥ  bhavati homeṣu yad āhavanīye juhoti tena saḥ  asya abhīṣṭaḥ prītaḥ  bhavati iti tena yasya āhavanīyaḥ tasya ete aṅgam na ca kṛṣi ādīni  āhavanīye vartante na ca eṣām gārhapatyaḥ  asti yatas  praṇīta āhavanīyaḥ syāt  tasmāt  na karmaṇā ādīnām jaya ādayaḥ itas  ca paśyāmaḥ  vaidikānām śeṣa bhūtā iti kutas  sāma khyānāt ādhvaryavam iti hi samākhyāte vede jaya ādayaḥ samāmnātāḥ santaḥ  adhvaryuṇā kariṣyante karṣaṇa ādiṣu  adhvaryoḥ  abhāvāt  anadhvaryuṇā api kriyamāṇāḥ samākhyām bādheran tasmāt  vaidikānām śeṣa bhūtā iti asti  aśva pratigraha iṣṭiḥ varuṇaḥ  vā etam gṛhṇāti yaḥ  aśvam pratigṛhṇāti yāvataḥ  aśvān pratigṛhṇīyāt  tāvataḥ  vāruṇān   catuṣkapālān nirvapet  iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim laukike aśva pratigraha iṣṭiḥ atha vaidika iti kaḥ punar  laukikaḥ  aśva pratigrahaḥ kaḥ  vā vaidika iti loke bhikṣamāṇaḥ  vā abhikṣamāṇaḥ  vā yatra aśvam labhate tatra laukika aśva pratigrahaḥ vaidikaḥ  api pauṇḍarīke aśva sahasram dakṣiṇā jyotiṣṭome gauḥ  ca aśvaś ca iti tatra ucyate vaidikatva sāmānyāt  vaidika iti prāpte ucyate doṣāt  tu iṣṭiḥ  laukike syāt  doṣaḥ  hi śrūyate varuṇaḥ  vā etam gṛhṇāti yaḥ  aśvam pratigṛhṇāti iti sa ca ayam anuvādaḥ  yatra doṣaḥ tatra iti sa ca laukike aśva pratigrahe śūdrāt  anyasmāt  vā pāpa karmaṇaḥ kṛtaḥ  bhavati iti  upapadyate doṣa saṃyoga āl laukika iti gamyate āha na doṣa saṃkīrtanam prāyaścitta viṣaya viśeṣaṇam kim tu prāyaścitta stuti arthena ucyate doṣa nirdhāta arthe sati  evam syāt  varuṇa pramocanam idam karma tal laukike bhavitum arhati loke varuṇa grahaṇasya vidyamāna tvāt  vaidike tu  aśva pratigrahe tad  na syāt  śāstra ād dhi vacanena tasya kartavyatā avagamyate yadi ca tatas  pāpam syāt  na tasya kartavyatau  agamyeta akartavyam hi pāpa phalam nanu vaidike api pratigrahe apratigrāhyāt  pratigṛhṇataḥ pāpam asti ucyate bhavet  evam yadi pratigrahasya kartuḥ  iṣṭiḥ  bhavet  sā tu khalu yathā hetu kartuḥ tathā uttara adhikaraṇe vakṣyāmaḥ tasmāt  na veda codite aśva pratigrahe iṣṭiḥ  iti  etāvat  iha adhikaraṇe siddham na ca etad  asti yad  uktam yaḥ śūdrāt  anyasmāt  vā pāpa kṛtaḥ  loke aśvam pratigṛhṇīyāt  sa etām iṣṭim nirvapet  sa hi varuṇa gṛhīta iti  ucyate jala udareṇa yaḥ  gṛhītaḥ yasya udaram jala vṛddhyā śvayati jalodaram iti  eva loke tad  prasiddham na ca tasya aśva pratigrahaḥ  laukikaḥ  nidānam iti prati jñāyate na ca anena vidhīyate tasmāt  na aśva pratigraha at  jala udara upapātaḥ atha pāpam varuṇa śabdena ucyate vṛṇīta iti  eṣaḥ  abhiprāya iti tadā prasiddhau tyaktāyām kleśa mātram vṛṇvat  varuṇa śabdena ucyate tatra yājñe api pratigrahe varuṇa gṛhītaḥ syāt  rakṣaṇa poṣaṇa vicikitsā ādinā kleśena na eṣa pakṣaḥ  vyavatiṣṭheta laukike aśva pratigraha iti prasiddhiḥ  ca bādhyeta tasmāt  arthavāda eṣaḥ yāvat  varuṇa gṛhītasya varuṇa unmocane śreyaḥ tāvat  eta iti  upamānena eṣā stutiḥ yaḥ  asya pratigrahaḥ tad  varuṇa grahaṇam iva yā iṣṭiḥ sā tad  unmocanī iva yathā varuṇa gṛhītena unmocanam avaśya kartavyam tādṛś  eva etad  iti tasmāt  yajñe pratīyeta laukike hi phalam kalpanīyam vaidike yasmin   aśva pratigrahaḥ tasya aṅga bhūtā bhaviṣyati tatra prayoga vacanena saha eka vākyatā saṃbandhāt  avakalpyamānā parokṣāyāḥ phala vacanena saha eka vākyatāyāḥ  laghīyasi iti yuktam iṣṭiḥ  vaidike dāna iti yāvataḥ  aśvān pratigṛṇīyāt  tāvataḥ  vāruṇān   catuṣkapālān nirvapet  iti tatra etad  samadhigatam vaidike aśva pratigraha iṣṭiḥ  iti atha idānīm saṃdihyate kim pratigraha kartrā kartavyā yasmai dīyate uta hetu kartrā yaḥ  dadāti iti kim prāptam acoditam ca karma bhedāt  na dānasya kartuḥ  iṣṭiḥ  codyate pratigrhakartuḥ  tām avagacchāmaḥ yāvataḥ  aśvān pratigṛhṇīyāt  tāvataś catuṣkapālān vāruṇān nirvapet  iti tasmāt  pratigrahītra ṛtvijā kartavyā iti na eṣā pratigraha kartuḥ kim tarhi hetu kartuḥ syāt  kutas  liṅgāt  kim liṅgam pūrva padānām uttaraiḥ padaiḥ  yathārtham abhisaṃbandhaḥ idam śrūyate prajāpatiḥ  varuṇāya aśvam anyat  iti prajāpatiḥ  aśvasya dātā kīrtitaḥ varuṇaḥ pratigrahītā sa svām devatām ārcchat  iti sa iti sa apekṣam pūrva prakṛtam vākya śeṣam apekṣate sa iti prajāpatim pratinirdiśati iti tena saha aikya vākyatām yāti sāmānādhikaraṇyāt  ca prajāpateḥ  eva pratinirdeśaḥ  avakalpate na tu varuṇasya vaiyadhikaraṇyāt  sa paryadīryata iti  eṣaḥ  api prajāpatim eva pratinirdiśati pūrva prakṛtam tena ca saha eka vākyatām yāti sa eva etam vāruṇam catuṣkapālam apaśyat  iti prajāpatiḥ  eva iti niravapat  prajāpatiḥ  eva iti tatas  vai sa varuṇa pāśāt  amucyata prajāpatiḥ varuṇa etam gṛhṇāti iti hetu apadeśaḥ  ayam yasmāt  eva prajāpatiḥ  varuṇāya aśvam dattvā paridīrṇaḥ tasmāt  yaḥ  aśvam prati gṛhṇāti prayacchati tam varuṇaḥ  gṛhṇāti sa paridīryata iti yatas  tu vāruṇena pratimuktaḥ tasmāt  anyena api  aśvam prayacchatā vāruṇaḥ  nirvaptavya iti  aśvasya dātuḥ  vāruṇī iṣṭiḥ praśasyate karta vyā anena ākhyātena tasmāt  aśvam dattvā vāruṇīm iṣṭim nirvapet  iti āha nanu yaḥ  asvam pratigṛhṇāti sa nirvapet  iti  ucyate evam sati  anyathā upakrānte vākye anyathā upasaṃhṛta upakramaḥ  api  anarthakaḥ syāt  upasaṃhāraḥ  api tasmāt  upakrame vā śabda artha upasaṃhāra vaśena kalpanīyaḥ upasaṃhāre vā upakrama vaśena tatra prajāpatiḥ  varuṇāya aśvam anayat  iti varuṇād aśvam pratyagṛhṇāt  iti  upasaṃhāra anurodhena kalpyeta yad  vā upakrama vaśena upasaṃhāram yaḥ  aśvam pratigṛhṇāti iti yaḥ  aśvam pratigrāhayati iti tatra mukhyam vā pūrvam coda nāl lokavat  iti prathamam anugrahītavyam virodha abhāvāt paścāt  tanam tu virodhāl lakṣaṇayā kalpanīyam api ca prajāpatiḥ  varuṇāya aśvam anayat  iti varuṇād aśvam pratyagṛhṇāt  iti bahu asamañjasam kalpayitavyam pratigṛhṇāti iti  eṣa śabdaḥ pratigrāhayati iti  etam artham śaknoti yayā kayācid  chaktyā vaktum yaḥ  hi tad  ācarati yena ca kriyā praṇāḍya api sidhyati sa tasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ kartā iti śakyate vaditum yathā ṣaḍbhiḥ  halaiḥ karṣati iti saṃvidhānam kurvan vilekhanam akurvan   api  ucyate tad samartham ācarati iti evam iha api sa pratigraha samartham ācarati yaḥ  dadāti tasmāt  dadat  pratigṛhṇāti iti śakyate vaditum tasmāt  adhyavadhārya idam avakḷptam dadat  pratigṛhṇāti iti  ucyate tasya ca vāruṇīṣṭiḥ  iti idam samāmananti somendram carum nirvapet  chyāmākam soma vāmina iti tatra saṃdehaḥ laukikasya soma pānasya vamane saumendraś caruḥ uta vaidikasya iti kim laukikam soma pānam kim ca vaidikam ucyate vaidikam soma pānam jyotiṣṭome tad vikṛtiṣu ca laukikam soma pānam yad  sapta rātreṣu daśa rātreṣu dhātu sāmya artham āsevyamāne some kim tāvat  prāptam pānavyāpac ca tadvat  laukike vamana iṣṭiḥ  bhavitum arhati na vaidike tadvat  iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ pratinirdiṣṭaḥ yathā tatra doṣa saṃyogena śravaṇāt  laukike aśva pratigraha iti  uktam evam iha api doṣa saṃyogena śravaṇam bhavati indriyeṇa vā eṣa vīryeṇa vyṛdhyate yaḥ somam pibati iti loke dhātu sāmya artham āsevite vamanena vinaṣte dhātu sāmya vyāpadā indriyeṇa vyṛddhiḥ  upapadyate śās trād dhi vaidike na doṣaḥ syāt  tatra śeṣaḥ pātavya iti śabdāt  codite nirvṛtte na asti doṣaḥ yadi  api vamyate tathā api pāna kriyā tatra nirvartitā kṛtaḥ  vacana artha iti na doṣaḥ syāt  tasmāl laukikasya soma pānasya vyāpadi sauma indraḥ syāt  vaidikasya pānasya vyāpadi bhavitum arhati na laukikasya kasmāt  doṣāt  doṣa saṃbandhaḥ  atra śrūyate indriyeṇa vā iti kalpanā nyāyyā tad  etad  soma pāna vyāpadi saumendram karma sarvatra vamane syāt  ārtvije yājamāne ca kutas  aviśeṣāt  na viśeṣaḥ kaścid  āśrīyate asya vamane syāt  na asya iti tasmāt  sarvatra śrūyate tad  soma vāminaḥ yajamānasya upakartum śaknoti na ārtvijaḥ na hi tad  ṛtvij  artham karma yatra somaḥ  vamyate atha ucyate soma vāminaḥ  adhvaryoḥ  hotuḥ  vā ātmīyā ṛtvijaḥ tadīyeṣu  agniṣu iti yajamānaḥ soma saṃskāre vinaṣṭe viguṇam asya karma iti vyṛdhyeta na kathaṃcid  ṛtvijaḥ  vyṛddhiḥ ṛtvijaḥ  yasya somam vamanti iti vamanena saṃbandhaḥ syāt  na yaḥ somam vamati iti tasmāt  api paśyāmaḥ  yajamānasya vamane sauma indram iti staḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau tatra sāmāmnāyate yad  āgneyaḥ  aṣṭākapālaḥ  amāv āsyāyām paurṇamāsyām ca acyutaḥ  bhavati iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim kṛtsnam haviḥ agnaye pradātavyam uta śeṣayitavyam kiṃcid  kiṃcid  dātavyam iti kim prāptam kṛtsnam haviḥ pradīyeta kutas  tad artha tvāt puroḍāśa āgneyaḥ kartavya iti vacanam tasmāt  sarvam pradātavyam iti niṣkṛṣya anyathā ucyate yadā dvis  avakhaṇḍana viṣiṣṭam home śrutam tadā sakṛt  avadānam yāvat  chrutam tad  sarvam kṛtam tadā na aparam dravyam asti iti punar  yāgaḥ  na āvartitavyaḥ katham tad  dhi dravyam punar  yāga āvarteta na tu yāgaḥ  dravya saṃbandha arthaḥ kim tarhi dravyam yāge guṇa bhūtam yāgaḥ katham nirvṛttim upeyāt  iti dravyam upādīyate tena nirvṛtte yāge siddhe ca puruṣa arthe na niyogena pratyakṣaḥ  dvis  avadāne api ca akṛtsna saṃbandhe api tad  dhitasya upapattiḥ tatas  grahītavyam iti sāmānyam khalu  āgneya iti dvi avadānam juhoti iti viśeṣaḥ tasmāt  cheṣayitavyam kiṃcid  iti śeṣāt puroḍāśaḥ  bahūnām karmaṇām sādhāraṇaḥ tatra saṃdehaḥ kim pratikarma sviṣṭakṛt  iḍam kartavyam sakṛt  eva vā iti kim prāptam codanā anugrahāt pratikarma kartavyam ekasmin   api dravye bahu tvāt gamyate viśeṣaḥ kasya avattam kasya na iti evam iḍāyām api tasmāt  sakṛt  avadātavyam iti asti jyotiṣṭomaḥ jyotiṣṭomena svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti tatra aindra vāyave grahe saṃdehaḥ kim sakṛt  bhakṣaṇam uta dvis  iti soma saṃskāra artha tvāt sakṛt  iti prāpte brūmaḥ aindra vāyave dvis  bhakṣayitavyam iti kutas  vacanāt  vacanam idam bhavati dvis  aindra vāyavasya bhakṣayati dvis  hi  etasya vaṣaṭkaroti iti na asti vacanasya ati bhāraḥ jyotiṣṭome samāmananti somān teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim teṣām śeṣaḥ  bhakṣayitavyaḥ uta na iti kim prāptam some bhakṣaḥ  na vidyate kasmāt  avacanāt  na śakyam asati vacane adhyavasātum bhakṣaṇam tasmāt  soma śeṣaḥ  na bhakṣayitavya iti bhavet  vā bhakṣaḥ anya artham hi vacanam bhakṣam darśayati sarvatas  parihāram āśvinam bhakṣayati bhakṣitā api  āyitāṃ   camasān dakṣiṇasya anasaḥ  avalambe sādayanti iti na asati bhakṣaṇa evaṃjātīyakā bhakṣa viśeṣāḥ saṃbhavanti nanu darśanam idam prāptiḥ  vaktavyā ucyate vacanāni tarhi bhaviṣyanti sarvatas  parihāram āśvinam bhakṣayati tasmāt  sarvā diśaḥ śṛṇoti iti viśiṣṭam bhakṣaṇam vidhīyate apūrva tvāt  bhakṣa anuvādaḥ  na avakalpate api ca evam apūrvam artham vidadhataḥ  arthavat tā bhaviṣyati tasmāt  yatra eva viśiṣṭam bhakṣaṇam śrūyate tatra eva bhavati na ati prasajyate jyotiṣṭoma eva śruyate praitu hotuḥ  camasaḥ pra brahmaṇaḥ prodgātṝṇām pra yajamānasya prayantu sadasyānām iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim camasinām asti bhakṣaḥ na iti kim prāptam na iti brūmaḥ na atiprasajyata iti  uktam evam prāpte brūmaḥ camaseṣu  asti bhakṣa iti kutas  samākhyānāt  hotuḥ  camasaḥ brahmaṇaḥ  camasa udgātuḥ  camasa iti samākhyayā nirdiśyate hotā yatra camati camiṣyati acamīd vā sa hotuḥ  camasaḥ yadi  atra hotā na camen na hotuḥ  camasaḥ bhavet  tasmāt  camati iti āha kā asya liṅgasya prāptiḥ  iti sāmarthyam iti brūmaḥ hotuḥ  camasena praitavyam yadi ca atra hotā na camet  na śakyam bhavet  dhotuḥ  camasena praitum na ca atra anyat  dhotā odana ādi camiṣyati soma camasa iti hi tam samācakṣate api ca na tad  dhotuḥ  dravyam yajamānasya tad  dravyam hotuḥ  tatra camanam kartavyam some ca bhakṣyamāṇe tena homaḥ  avakalpate pavitram hi somaḥ na tasmin bhakṣite pātram vyāpadyate tatra camasena śakyate hotum vacana prāmāṇyāt  ucchiṣṭena hoṣyati iti ced  na etad  evam asati avakāśe vacanam bādhakam bhavati asti ca avakāśaḥ soma bhakṣaṇam tasmāt  camasibhiḥ  bhakṣayitavyaḥ somaḥ iti atha takṣaṇa ādīni  āśrīyeran tathā saṃbandha apahnavāt  atat camasatā eva syāt  dravya antaram syāt  tasmāt  ca abrāhmaṇasya somam pratiṣedhati sa yadi rājanyam vaiśyam vā yājayet  sa yadi somam vibhakṣayiṣet  nyagrodhasti bhīra āhṛtya tāḥ saṃpiṣya dadhanī  unmṛja tasmai bhakṣam prayacchet  na somam iti bhakṣā nivṛttim darśayati sa eṣa bhakṣa āśaṅkā evam sati  upapadyate yadi camasinaḥ  asti bhakṣaḥ tasmāt  asti iti manyāmahe asti jyotiṣṭomaḥ jyotiṣṭomena svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti tatra asti praitu hotuḥ  camasaḥ pra brahmaṇaḥ prodgātṝṇām iti tatra asti samākhyānāt  bhakṣa iti  uktam tatra saṃdehaḥ kim eka eva enam camasam udgātā bhakṣayet  uta sarve bhakṣayeyuḥ atha subrahmaṇya varjitāḥ  chandogā bhakṣayeyuḥ athavā saha subrahmaṇyena iti kim tāvat  prāptam ekaḥ  bhakṣayet  udgātā eva kutas  śruti saṃyogāt  udgātā ekaḥ śrutyā saṃyujyate camasena prodgātṝṇām iti nanu bahuvacanam śrūyate tena bahavaḥ  bhakṣayeyuḥ ucyate śrūyate bahuvacanam tad  udgātṛ prātipadika gatam tad  vivakṣitam sat  udgātṛ bahu tvam brūyāt  ekaḥ  ca ugātā tatra bahu tvam śrūyamāṇam api na śaknuyād udgātṛ bhedam kartum tasmāt  avivakṣitam bahuvacanam anumānam hi  etad  bahūnām camasa iti katham yad  bahuṣu prātipadikam vartate tatas  bahuvacanam bhavati bahuvacanam tu tatas  dṛśyate prodgātṝṇām iti tasmāt  nūnam bahūnām camasa iti  anumānam pratyakṣam tu  eka udgātā na dvitīyaḥ na tṛtīyaḥ anumānāc ca pratyakṣam kāraṇam balavat  bhavet  tasmāt  ekasya camasaḥ sa ca udgātuḥ  iti sarve vā bhakṣayeyuḥ ekasmin   udgātari bhakṣayati bahuvacanam pramāda adhītam iti gamyate na hi tad  anūdyate na vidhīyata iti nanu sarveṣu  api bhakṣayat su udgātṛ śabdaḥ pramādaḥ  gamyate ucyate lakṣaṇa arthaḥ  api tāvat  saṃbhaviṣyati udgātṛ prabhṛtaya iti ucyate na etad  asti bahūnām camasa iti kutas  udgātṛ śabdasya camasena saṃbandhaḥ pratyakṣeṇa vākyena bahuvacanasya punar  udgātṛ śabdena śrutyā saṃbandhaḥ anyena ṛtvijā tu bahuvacanasya na eva kaścid  asti saṃbandhaḥ tasmāt  bahūnām camasa iti  anupapannam iti atra ucyate śaknoti  ayam udgātṛ śabdaḥ  bahu tvam vaditum kriyā yogena udnāyanti iti  udgātāraḥ ke te prastotā udgātā pratihartā iti tad  etena bahuvacana nirdeśena anumānika kriyā yoga nimitta udgātṛ śabdaḥ  vivakṣita iti  avagamiṣyāmaḥ bahuvacanam hi  evam avakḷptam bhaviṣyati udgātṛ śabdaḥ  ca tasmāt  stotra kāriṇām camasa iti sarve chandogāḥ sahasubrahmaṇyā bhakṣayeyuḥ kim iti gāna saṃyogāt  iti na ayam pakṣa upapadyate katham ekas tatra udgānena saṃbandhaḥ itaraḥ  gānena anyat  dhi gānam anyat  udgānam gīti mātram gānam laukikam vaidikam ca dvitīyam sāmnaḥ parva utpūrvasya gāyateḥ  abhidheyam prasiddham tatra eka eva udgītham karoti iti  eka eva udgātā na bahavaḥ tasmāt  gāna saṃyogāt  bahavaḥ  bhaviṣyanti iti  etad  api na upapadyate katham tarhi veda saṃyogāt  audgātram nāma pravacanam tathā audgātrāṇi karmāṇi audgātrasya kartā vā adhyetā vā udgātā iti  ucyate katham udgātuḥ karma audgātram iti prasiddham evam ced  vyaktam audgātrasya kartā udgātā iti gamyate yasya udgātā prasiddhaḥ tad  viśiṣṭam karma anākhyātam api  audgātram iti vadati śabdaḥ  ca yasya audgātram prasiddham sa tasya kartāram udgātā iti vadati anākhyātam api yathā yasya uda meghaḥ prasiddhaḥ sa tasya anākhyā tam api  apatyam audameghir iti brūte yasya oda meghiḥ sa tasya pitaram anākhyātam api  udamegham pratipadyate evam audgātra saṃbandhāt  upapadyata udgātṛ śabdaḥ prastotā api  udgātā api pratihartā api subrahmaṇyaḥ  api evam bahuvacanam udgātṛ śabdaḥ  ca ubhayam api  upapannam bhaviṣyati na ca anyaḥ kaścid  doṣaḥ tasmāt  audgātreṇa saṃbaddha aśva tvāra udgātṛ camasam bhakṣayeyuḥ  iti yatra kāraṇam asti tatra api subrahmaṇyā udgātāraḥ yathā udgātṛ śabdaḥ  viniṣadya udgātāraḥ sāmnā stuvata iti stotra kāriṣu tathā idam api vacanam udgātāraḥ  na apavyāhareyuḥ  uttamāyām eṣā uttamā iti  apasubrahmaṇyānām eva jyotiṣṭome grāvaḥ tun nāma hotṛ puruṣaḥ tatra saṃdehaḥ kim sa somam bhakṣayet  na iti ucyate grāvaḥ tun na bakṣayet  kutas  yatas  asya bhakṣam nāmananti hāri yojane camasinām adhikāra iti manyamāna evam ha sma āha na asyām nāyate bhakṣa iti hāri yojanasya vā grāva stutam bhakṣayitāram manyāmahe evam hi  āmananti yathā camasam anyān   camasāṃś camasinaḥ  bhakṣayanti atha etasya hāri yojanasya sarva eva lipsanta iti yadā hāri yojanasya sarve lipsante tadā grāvaḥ tud api iti vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na etad  asti grāvastutaḥ hāri yojane bhakṣa iti camasinām tatra adhikāraḥ  na sarveṣām katham camasinām eṣa vibhāgaḥ camasinaḥ  anyān   camasān yathā camasam bhakṣayanti iti  anūdya camasina eva vadati atha etasya hāri yojanasya sarva eva lipsanta iti ekam hi idam vākyam atha etasya iti  atha śabda prayogāt  anantara vṛttam apekṣate atha sarva eva iti  eva śabdaḥ sāmarthyāt  sarvān pūrva prakṛtān apekṣate atas  manyāmahe yathā camasam anyān   camasāṃś camasinaḥ  bhakṣayanti iti  anena pūrveṇa atha etasya hāri yojanasya iti  etasya eka vākya tā bhavati iti tena camasinām saṃnihitānām eṣa vibhāgaḥ yathā camasam anyatra hāri yojane tu sarva eva iti tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na etad  asti camasina eva hāri yojane lipsanta iti sarve tu vidhīyante hāri yojane sarve bhakṣayanti iti na punar  camasina iti saṃbandhaḥ śakyate vidhātum dvau hi saṃbandhau bhakṣayantaḥ  yathā camasam eva atha etasya hāri yojanasya na kevalam camasinaḥ sarva eva iti kim evam bhaviṣyati sarva śabdaḥ  ca sarvān vadan na eka deśe kalpitaḥ  bhaviṣyati na ca dvau saṃbandhau   apūrvauv ekasmin vākye bhaviṣyataḥ tasmāt  eṣa pakṣaḥ  jyāyān iti tad arthā hi  eṣā camasiśrutiḥ hāri yojanasya praśāṃsa arthā camasinaḥ kīrtyante hāri yojanam praśaṃsitum katham mahābhāgaḥ  hi hāri yojanaḥ yasmāt  tatra sarve lipsante anyān   camasān ekaikaḥ na te mahābhāgāḥ nyūnā hāri yojanāt  iti atha kim samākhyā eva ekā bhakṣa kāraṇam na iti brūma h vaṣaṭkārāc ca bhakṣayet  vaṣaṭkāraḥ  ca bhakṣaṇe nimittam katham vacanāt  evam hi śrūyate vaṣaṭkartuḥ prathama bhakṣa iti bhakṣaṇasya aprāpta tvāt  na prāthamy avidhāna artha eṣa śabdaḥ prāthamy aviśiṣṭam bhakṣaṇam eva vidadhāti iti aparam api kāraṇam homa abhiṣavau katham havirdhāne grāvabhiḥ  abhiṣutya āhavanīye hutvā pratyañcaḥ para iti  sadasi bhakṣān bhakṣayanti iti na tāvat  eṣa kramaḥ  vidhīyate home nirvṛtte tatas  bhakṣaṇasya camasinaḥ prati praitu hotuḥ  camasa iti evamādibhiḥ  viśeṣa vacanaiḥ homa abhiṣava kāriṇām sāmānya vākyena yaḥ somaḥ  bhakṣaṇena saṃskartavyaḥ sa camaseṣu camasibhiḥ  iti atha idānīm anyan nimittam kva bhaviṣyati avyaktaḥ sāmānya nimittaḥ kva śeṣe bhaviṣyati yatra na camasinaḥ syāt  vā camaseṣu vaṣaṭkartṛ ādīnām bhakṣaḥ prāpyate hi teṣām tatra kāraṇam na ca pratiṣidhyate nanu camasinām pratyakṣaḥ  padeśān nivarteran ucyate anirdeśaḥ  camasānām kartuḥ  tad vacana tvāt  praitu hotuḥ  camasa iti evamādayaḥ śabdāḥ na śaknuvanti vaṣaṭkartṛ ādīn pratiṣeddhum upadeṣṭāraḥ  hi te na pratiṣeddhāraḥ tasmāt  vaṣaṭkartrādayaḥ  api camaseṣu bhakṣayeyuḥ camase ca anyāṃ   camasinaḥ  darśayati camasāṃś camasādhvaryave prayacchati tān sa vaṣaṭkartre harati iti ekaḥ  hi sva ś camasaḥ vaṣaṭkartre hriyate tena bahu haraṇa darśanam na avakalpate yadi vaṣaṭkartrādayaḥ  na camaseṣu bhakṣayeyuḥ tasmāt  bhakṣayanti iti atha yatra ekasmin pātre bahavaḥ  bhakṣayanti kas tatra krama iti ucyate tasya hi kramaḥ  bhakṣayitum yasya haste somaḥ hotā vā pūrvaḥ bhakṣayet  mantra varṇāt  mantra varṇaḥ  hi tathā hotuḥ  cit  pūrve haviradyam āśata iti tathā hotā iva naḥ prathamaḥ pāhi iti somaḥ  anekena bhakṣyate kim tatra anujñāpya ananujñāpya vā bhakṣayitavyam uta anujñāpya eva iti lāghavāt  aniyamaḥ  prāpta ucyate anujñāpya bhakṣayitavyam iti kasmāt  vacanāt  idam vacanam bhavati tasmāt  somaḥ  na anupahūtena peya iti upahvānam ca anujñāpanam prāpti sūtram etad  atha anujñātena bhakṣayitavyam iti sthite kim laukikena vacanena anujñāpayitavyam uta vaidikena iti aniya māl laukikena iti prāpta ucyate anujñāpana liṅgaḥ  ayam mantraḥ liṅgāt  anujñāpane samāmnātaḥ sāmarthyāt  vinijujyate tatra kṛte arthe laukikaḥ  nivartate etad  avagatam tad upahūta upahūyasva iti  anena anujñāpayet  iti atha prativacane saṃdehaḥ kim laukikam prativacanam uta etad  eva iti kim prāptam etad  vaidikam praśne viniyuktam laukikam anyat  prativacanam bhavitaum arhati evam prāpte brūmaḥ tatra etad  eva prativacanam iti nanu praśna liṅgam etad  upahūyasva iti ucyate yad  asya pūrvam upahūta iti prativacanasya samartham tad  prativacana kārye baviṣyati āha viparītam etad  samāmnānam pūrvam hi praśnena bhavitavyam tatas  prativacanena ucyate arthāt  pūrvam prativacana kārye bhaviṣyati arthaḥ  hi kramāt  balīyān iti idam saṃdihyate kim yaḥ kaścid  anujñāpayitavyaḥ uta samāna pātra iti aviśeṣa abhidhānāt  yaḥ kaścid  iti prāpta ucyate tad  khalu  anujñāpanam eka pātrāṇām syāt  kutas  anujñāpanam iha aṅgam anujñāpanasya ca etad  rūpam yatra anyena kartavyam anyaḥ  cikīrṣet  saḥ  anumanyasva iti brūte sahabhoja na ādi vācaritu kāmaḥ  cittam anyasya anukūlayati tad  etad  nānā pātreṣu na eva saṃbhavati na hi tatra anyena kartavyam anyaḥ  vā cikīrṣati iti sahabhojana ādau vā padārthe saṃmānayati eka pātre tu some sādhāraṇe saṃskartavye nyāyena samaḥ  vibhāgaḥ prāpnoti tatra avibhajya pīyamāne kadācid  anyena pātavyam anyaḥ pibet  tatra anujñāpanam saṃbhavati tvayā ardham pātavyam mayā ar dham kadācid  aham abhyādhikam nyūnam vā pibeyam tad anujñātum arhasi iti eka pātre vā pānam tvayā saha ācaran   aham tava citta prasādānam vyāhanyām iti saṃbhavati  anujñāpanā tasmāt  eka pātreṣu  eva etad  syāt  iti asti jyotiṣṭomaḥ tatra ṛtu yāgeṣu śrūyate yajamānasya yājyā saḥ  abhipreṣyati hotar etad  yaja iti svayam yā niṣpadya yajati iti yadā svayam yajati tadā saṃdehaḥ kim asya bhakṣaḥ  asti na asti iti tad  ucyate yājyāyām apanīyamānāyām na apanīyeta bhakṣaṇam hotuḥ  eva tu bhakṣaṇam syāt  na yajamānasya iti kutas  anyā hi yājyā anyat  bhakṣaṇam na ca anyasmin   apanīyamāne anyat  apanīyate yathā tasyām eva yājyāyām apanīyamānāyām pravaraḥ  na apanīyate tadvat  etad  api iti nanu yājyāyāḥ  adhi vaṣaṭkaroti iti yatra yājyā tatra vaṣaṭkāraḥ yatra vaṣaṭkāraḥ tatra bhakṣaṇam api iti na iti  ucyate na tāvat  yājyāyām avayava bhūtaḥ  vaṣaṭkāraḥ yena yājya agrahaṇena asau gṛhyeta yad  tu tasyāḥ  adhi vaṣaṭkaroti iti anyena api prayujyamānāyāḥ  upari hotā vaṣaṭkariṣyati yājyā apanayaḥ  hi vacanāt  na vaṣaṭkāra apanayaḥ yāvat  vacanam vācanikam bhavati  eva vacanam hi tad viṣayam eva yaṣṭuḥ  vā bhakṣaḥ syāt  kutas  kāraṇa āgamāt bhakṣasya kāraṇam vaṣaṭkāraḥ sa ca yājyāyām āgacchantyām āgacchati evam hi śrūyate yājyāyāḥ  adhi vaṣaṭkaroti iti nanu  etad  uktam yajamānena api prayujyamānāyām hotā adhi vaṣaṭkaroti iti na eṣa samādhiḥ anavāna tā yaṣṭavyam vaṣaṭkāreṇa yāgaḥ kriyate na yājyām atreṇa tasmāt  ā vaṣaṭkārān na avānitavyam yajamānena anyaḥ  ced  vaṣaṭkuryāt  avānyāt  yajamānaḥ na ca yajeta yaṣṭavye ca asau codyate na yājyā mātra vacane svayam nipadya yajati iti sa aṅgasya niṣadya yāge vidhānāt  atha yad  uktam yathā pravaraḥ  na apanīyate evam bhakṣaḥ  api iti ucyate aśakya tvāt  pravaraḥ  na apanīyate atikrāntaḥ  hi sa katham apanīyeta hotuḥ bhraṣṭe ca avasare anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ  yajamānasya viguṇaḥ syāt  na ca viguṇaḥ kathaṃcid  artham sādhayet  na atra ca udakena prāpnoti atha ucyate yad  chakyam tad  ca udakena prāpitam yad  na śakyam na tad  prāpitam iti prakṛtiḥ  iyam apūrvasya atra vidhānam yādṛśam uktam tādṛśam yadi śakyate kartavyam yadi na śakyate yatra eva śakyate tatra eva kāryam na yatra viguṇam iti tasmāt  pravarasya anapāyaḥ  yuktaḥ  na bhakṣasya iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate sa yadi rājanyam vā vaiṣyam vā yājayet  sa yadi somam vibhakṣayiṣet  nyagrodhasti bhīḥ  āhṛtya tāḥ saṃpiṣya dadhanī  unmṛjya tam asmai bhakṣam prayacchet  na somam iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim phala camasaḥ  bhakṣa vikāraḥ uta ijyā vikāra iti kim phala camasam bhakṣayet  iti  arthaḥ uta phala camasena yajeta iti kim prāptam phala camasaḥ  naimittikaḥ  bhakṣa vikāraḥ bhakṣaṇena hi śrutena eka vākya tā bhavati iti tasmai bhakṣam prayacchet  iti na tena yajeta iti śabdaḥ  asti tasmāt  bhakṣa vikāraḥ ijyā vikāraḥ  vā phala camasaḥ phala camasena yajeta iti  arthaḥ katham yad  etad  bhakṣaṇam etad  soma saṃskāra artham phala camasya api yadi bhakṣaṇam phala camasa saṃskāra artham phala camasasya anyatra anupayogāt  anarthakam atha bhakṣaṇam pradhānam tathā na somam iti  anuvādaḥ  na avakalpate yadi tu  ijyā vikāraḥ  bhavet  tatas  phala camasa saṃskāraḥ  avakalpate tasmāt  ijyā vikāraḥ āha katham yaji saṃbandhe asati ijyā vikāraḥ  bhaviṣyati iti ucyate asti yaji saṃbandhaḥ katham iti yadi rājanyam vā vaiṣyam vā yājayet  nyagrodhasti bhīḥ saṃpiṣya tam asmai bhakṣam prayacchet  yājayitum iti gamyate bhakṣa saṃbandhe hi na pūrvam uttareṇa saṃbadhyate yadi somam bhakṣaṇena saṃskartum icchet  nyagrodhasti bhīḥ saṃskuryāt  iti tasmāt  na bhakṣaṇa saṃbandhaḥ yāgaḥ  hi prakṛtaḥ  asti tena saha saṃbhantsyate na doṣaḥ  bhaviṣyati nanu tasmai bhakṣam prayacchet  iti vacanāt  bhakṣa sādhanam iti gamyate na yāga sādhanam iti bhakṣa śabda anantaryāt ucyate śrūyamāṇe saṃbandhe anarthakam iti kṛtvā prakṛta saṃabdha iti  ucyate katham tu bhakṣa saṃbandha iti yad  dhi yāga dravyam bhakṣayitavyam tad  ca udakena bhavati tasmāt  bhakṣa saṃbandham labhate bhakṣa saṃbandhena ca yāga saṃbandha eva lakṣyate yadi tena ijyate tatas  sa bhakṣaḥ  bhavati tasmāt  bhakṣa vacanāt  sutarām tena ijyata iti gamyate sā eṣā vyavadhāraṇa kalpanā tasmai bhaksam prayacchet  tam asmai bhakṣam kuryāt  iti  arthaḥ yathā sa bhakṣaḥ  bhavati tathā kuryāt  iti yadi ca tena ijyate tatas  ayam bhakṣaḥ  bhavati tasmāt  tena yaṣṭavyam iti homa viśeṣa vacanam bhavati yadā anyān   camasān  juhvati atha etasya darbha taruṇakena upahatya juhoti iti ijyā vikāre sati darbha taruṇakena iti juhotau guṇa vacanam avakalpate tasmāt  api ijya avikāraḥ yadā anyān   cāmasān unnayanti atha enam camasam unnayanti iti ijyā vikāre sati  unnayana darśanam yujyate na bhakṣa vikāre tasmāt  api ijya avikāraḥ itas  ca paśyāmaḥ ijyā vikāra iti kutas  liṅga darśanāt  kim liṅgam bhavati soma pratiṣedha anuvādaḥ tasmai bhakṣam prayacchet  na somam iti ijyā vikāre sati somaḥ  na bhakṣyate tasmāt  paśyāmaḥ ijyā vikāra iti asti rājasūye daśa peyaḥ tatra śrūyate śatam brāhmaṇāḥ somān bhakṣayanti daśa daśa ekaika camasam anuprasarpanti iti atra rājan yacamase saṃdehaḥ kim tam rājanyā anuprasarpeyuḥ uta brāhmaṇā iti kim prāptam rājī anyā iti katham daśa daśa ekaikam camasam anuprasarpeyuḥ  iti  anuprasarpatām saṃkhyā vidhīyate ekasyām rājanya jātau daśa saṃkhyā vidhīyate rājanya jātiḥ sā eva tena tam daśa rājanyā anuprasarpeyuḥ  evam śatam brāhmaṇā rājanyāḥ  ca teṣu śata śabdaḥ  anuvādaḥ anuvāda sarūpaḥ  ca śatam bhakṣayanti iti tasmāt  rājanyā rājan yacamasam anuprasarpeyuḥ  iti kecid  āhuḥ brāhmaṇa rājanyānām ekasminś camase bhakṣaṇam virudhyata iti na sa doṣaḥ na hi somena ucchiṣṭā bhavanti iti śrūyate brāhmaṇā vā rājan yacamasam anuprasarpeyuḥ katham śatam brāhmaṇāḥ somam bhakṣayanti iti vidhiḥ śrutyā brāhmaṇa gatām eva saṃkhyām āha tasmāt  chatam brāhmaṇāḥ teṣām bhakṣaṇa artham anuprasarpatām ekaikasminś camase daśa daśa upadiśyante tasmāt  brāhmaṇa aśatasya daśa brāhmaṇā rājan yacamasam anuprasarpeyuḥ  iti anārabhya kiṃcid  ucyate yasya khādiraḥ sruvaḥ  bhavati sa chadasām eva rasena avadyati sarasā asya āhutayaḥ bhavanti yasya parṇa mayī juhūr bhavati na sa pāpam ślokam śṛṇoti iti  evamādi tatra saṃdehaḥ kim khādira tā sruve pālāśa tā juhvām prakṛtau niviśate uta prakṛtau vikṛtau ca iti kim prāptam sarva artham aprakaraṇāt  prakṛti vikṛti artham evaṃjātīyakam kutas  aprakaraṇāt  na kasya cit  prakaraṇe śrūyante tāni vākyena sarvatra bhaveyuḥ  iti prakṛtau vā niviśerann anārabhya adhītāni pātrāṇi kutas  advirukta tvāt  evam adviruktam bhaviṣyati iti dvis uktāyām kaḥ  doṣaḥ asaṃbhava iti brūmaḥ yad  dhi prakṛtau vikṛtau ca bhavati asti tad  prakṛtau prakṛtau ced  asti ca udakena eva vikṛtim prāpnoti tatas  nānā ārabhya vidhim ākāṅkṣati tasmāt  anākāṅkṣita tvāt  anārabhya vidhiḥ  na tatra vidadhāti tena brūmaḥ prakṛti artha eva iti aprakaraṇāt  prakṛti vikṛti artham eva iti  ucyate yad  tu coda kena prāpnoti iti  anārabhya vidhinā prāpte na ca udakam ākāṅkṣati tasmāt  anārabhya vidhi varjam ca udakaḥ prāpayiṣyati anārabhya vidhi vākyena pratyakṣeṇa sruve khādira tā ca udaka vākyena anumānikena vikṛtau ānumānikāc ca pratyakṣam balavat  tasmāt  prakṛti vikṛti arthaḥ  anārabhya vidhiḥ yadi  anārabhya vidhiḥ  ca udakāt  balīyān anārabhya vidhinā prāpte na ca udakam ākāṅkṣati nirākāṅkṣe vaikṛte karmaṇi codakaḥ  na eva prāpnoti tatra prayāja ādīnām darśanam na eva upapadyeta dṛśyante ca prayāja ādayaḥ kvacid  prayāje prayāje kṛṣṇalam juhoti iti atha codakaḥ  balīyān tatas  etad darśanam upapadyate tasmāt  prakṛti arthaḥ  anārabhya vidhiḥ na prakṛti arthaḥ sarva artha iti brūmaḥ aprakaraṇe samāmnānāt  yad  uktam anārabhya vidhinā nirākāṅkṣasya na ca udaka iti tad  na upapadyate na hi  anārabhya vidhiḥ  codanām nirākāṅkṣīkaroti prāpte hi ca udake na sruve kha ādira tāna ārabhya vidhinā śakyā vidhātum asati ca udake anārabhya vidhiḥ  api na asti na ca anārabhyavidhiḥ sruvam prāpayati tasya ca khādira tām kutas  codana eka arthyāt  eka arthā hi codanā yasya khādiraḥ sruvaḥ  bhavati iti na ca atra sruvaḥ khādira tā ca ubhayam vidhīyate sruvasya sataḥ khādira tām eṣa śabda āha sa ca ca udakena prāptaḥ tasmāt  asti ca udakaḥ sa hi  anārabhya vidhi vākyasya pratyakṣa tvāt  tam varjayitvā anyam prāpayati tasmāt  prakṛti vikṛti arthaḥ  anārabhya vidhiḥ iti ced  paśyasi utpattiḥ  eṣām prakṛti vidhibhiḥ  tulyā prakṛtau   aṅgāni saṃkṣepeṇa vistareṇa cocyante pañca prayājān yacati iti saṃkṣepeṇa samidhaḥ  yajati iti  evamādinā vistareṇa iha api yasya khādiraḥ sruvaḥ  bhavati iti evamādiḥ  vistāraḥ yasya evaṃrūpāḥ sruva iti saṃkṣepaḥ evaṃrūpaḥ prakṛtau vidhiḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ ayam api  evaṃrūpaḥ tasmāt  prākṛta iti sāmānyatas  dṛṣṭa anumānam tasmāt  prakṛti arthaḥ  anārabhya vidhiḥ  iti na etad  evam na hi  evaṃjātīyakam sāmānyatodṛṣṭam sādhakam bhavati kevalam atra prākṛta vidhi sārūpyam na tu prakṛtau   etad  bhavati iti pramāṇam asti api ca vikṛtau   api saṃkṣepa vistārābhyām aṅgāni vidhīyante tisra āhutīḥ  juhoti iti saṃkṣepaḥ āmanam asya āmanasya devāḥ  iti vistāraḥ atas  vaikṛtaiḥ  api  anārabhya vidhayaḥ  tulyāḥ tasmāt  ayam ahetuḥ prakṛti niveśasya tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na sarva arthaḥ  anārabhya vidhiḥ prakṛti arthaḥ sa iti brūmaḥ kutas  codanā arthakārtsnyāt kṛtsnam ca udakaḥ prāpayati nānā rabhya vidhinā vaikṛtam apūvam nirākāṅkṣam pātrāṇām hi tad  vākyena na yāgānām yāgāḥ  codanā liṅga saṃyogāt prakṛtim apekṣante tayā saha eka vākyatām yānti prākṛta āḥ  ca tān  śaknavanti nirākāṅkṣīkartum nānā ārabhya vidhayaḥ tasmāt  avaśyam ca udaka utpādayitavyaḥ sa ced  utpādyate na arthaḥ  anārabhya vidhinā na ca asau prakaraṇa ādīnām abhāvāt  pravartamānaḥ  api vaikṛtena yāgena saṃbadhyeta tasmāt  vaikṛtena karmaṇā nānā rabhya vidhiḥ saṃbadhyate tasya vaikṛtasya mukhyasya anārabhya vidhiḥ  vākya śeṣaḥ prakṛtau vā iti vipratiṣedhe ca udaka sāmarthyāt  prākṛte vākya śeṣe prāpte anārabhya vidhiḥ  na bhaviṣyati tasmāt  anārabhya vidhiḥ prakṛti artha iti anārabhya kiṃcid  sāmidhenīnām parimāṇam āmnātam saptadaśa sāmidhenīḥ  anubrūyāt  iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim etad  prakṛtau uta vikṛtau   iti kim prāptam pūrveṇa nyāyena prakṛtau   iti prāptam prakṛtau ca pāñcadaśyam āmnātam tena vikalpa iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ vikṛtau   evaṃjātīyakaḥ  vidhiḥ syāt  kasmāt  prakṛteḥ pāñcadaśyena nirākāṅkṣa tvāt  nanu vikalpaḥ  bhavaiṣyati iti  uktam prakaraṇa viśeṣāt  pāñcadaśyena na vikalpaḥ viṣama śāsanāt  vikṛtau tu  ānumānikam pāñcadaśyam bādhitvā anārabhya vidhi vākyena pratyakṣeṇa sāptadaśyam nivekṣyate advi ruktam ca etad  prayoga vacanam upasaṃhariṣyati tasmāt  evaṃjātīyakam vikṛti artham darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  āmnātam gaḥ dohanena paśu kāmasya praṇayet  iti tathā agnīṣomīye paśau śrūyate yūpam prakṛtya bailvaḥ  brahmavarcaskāmena kartavya iti evaṃjātīyakeṣu saṃdehaḥ kim prakṛtau niveśaḥ vikṛtau vā iti kim prāptam vikṛtau   iti prakṛtīḥ  anyena pātreṇa yūpena ca nirākāṅkṣāḥ evam prāpte brūmaḥ prakṛtau naimittikam niviśate nimitta saṃyogena vidhānāt  khādira pālāśa rauhitakā aviśeṣeṇa uktāḥ camasaḥ  ca gaḥ dohanam bailvaḥ  ca viśeṣa vihitau viśeṣa vidhinā ca aviśeṣa vidhiḥ  bādhyate prakaraṇam sāmānyam nimitta saṃyogaḥ  viśeṣaḥ sāmānyena yad  prāpnoti tad  parokṣam lakṣaṇayā yad  tu viśeṣeṇa tad  pratyakṣam śrutyā śrutiḥ  ca lakṣaṇāyāḥ  balīyasī pratyakṣam ca parokṣāt  tasmāt  prakṛtau   eva syāt  santi pavamāna iṣṭayaḥ agnaye pavamānāya aṣṭākapālam nirvapet  agnaye pāvakāya agnaye śucaya iti tāsām prakaraṇe samāmnātam brāhmaṇaḥ  vasante agnim ādadhīta iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim agnyādheyam pavamāna iṣṭi artham uta na iti kim prāptam iṣṭi artham iti kutas  prakaraṇāt  tāsām prakaraṇe śrūyate atas tad artham pavamāna iṣṭayaḥ hi  agni arthāḥ yadi  agniḥ  iṣṭi arthaḥ syāt  tatas  tad artham agnyādheyam iṣṭīnām upakuryāt  niṣphalās tu  iṣṭayaḥ tad artham agnyādheyam api niṣphalam syāt  katham punar  agni artha tā pavamāna iṣṭīnām niṣprayojana tvāt  eva prayojanavat tvāc ca agnīnām bhāvayitavyā api iṣṭayaḥ  bhūtānām agnīnām arthena kriyeran tasmāt  agnyādheyam pavamāna iṣṭi artham liṅgam darśayati yathā agni arthāḥ pavamāna iṣṭaya iti kim liṅgam jīryati vā eṣa āhitaḥ paśuḥ  yad  agniḥ tad  etāni  eva agnyādheyasya havīṃṣi saṃvatsare nirvapet  tena vā eṣa na jīryati tena enam punar  navam karoti tad  na sūkṣmam iti tad  etad  ādhānam kim prakṛti artham uta sarva karma artham iti saṃdehaḥ kim prāptam ucyate tad  prakṛti artham katham yathā anye anārabhyavādāḥ prakṛti arthāḥ tena eva hetunā sarva karma artham vādhānam kaḥ  arthaḥ sarva karma artham yad  agni dravyam tad artham ādhānam na prakṛti artham na prakṛtīḥ prakṛtya śrūyate na ca śruti ādayaḥ asya santi ye aṅga bhāvam upapādayanti anyeṣu  anārabhyavādeṣu  anyatas  nirjñāte aṅga bhāve tatas  vicāraḥ kim prakṛteḥ  aṅga bhūtāni vikṛteḥ  iti tasmāt  teṣu yuktam iha tu  aṅga bhāve na kāraṇam asti tasmāt  agni prayuktam ādhānam na karma prayuktam sarva karma arthā agnaya iti sarva artham iti  ucyate api ca asya svatas  kālaḥ  vidhīyate sa na vidhātavyaḥ yadā jyotiṣṭomasya prayogaḥ tadā idam kartavyam tadā ca vasantaḥ evam yadā darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ prayogaḥ tadā kartavyam tadā paurṇamāsy amāvāsyā vā aprakṛti artham tu na prakṛti prayoge kriyeta tatra kāla vacanam yuktam tasmāt  na prakṛti artham santi pavamāna iṣṭavyaḥ agnaye pavamānāya iti  evamādyāḥ tatra saṃdehaḥ kim pavamāna iṣṭi saṃskṛte agnau pavamāna iṣṭayaḥ kartavyāḥ uta na iti kim prāptam tāsām khalu pavamāna iṣṭīnām pavamāna iṣṭi saṃskṛtaḥ  agniḥ prakṛtitaḥ syāt  kutas  ca udaka sāmarthyāt  prayājavat  yathāsu prayājā bhavanti ca udakena evam pavamāna iṣṭi saṃskṛtā agnayaḥ  api bhaveyuḥ na veṣṭi saṃskāraḥ agnīnām pavamāneṣtiṣu syāt  kasmāt  tāsām tad artha tvāt tāḥ pavamāna iṣṭayaḥ agni saṃskāra arthā iti  uktam yad  ca nāma aṅga bhūtam tad  ca udakena gṛhyate agni prayukta ś ca pavamāna iṣṭi saṃskāraḥ  na darśa pūrṇamāsa prayuktaḥ tena na ca udakena ākṛṣyate api ca pavamāneṣ ṭaya iṣṭi saṃskāra varjitām prakṛtim apekṣante avihita tvāt  tasyām avasthāyām pavam āpana iṣṭīnām jyotiṣṭome paśuḥ  agnīṣomīyaḥ yaḥ  dīkṣitaḥ  yad  agnīṣomīyam paśum ālabhata iti tathā savanīyaḥ  anubandhyaḥ  ca santi ca paśu dharmāḥ upākaraṇam upānayanam akṣayā bandhaḥ yūpe niyojanam saṃjñapanam viśasanam iti evamādayaḥ te kim sarveṣām agnīṣomīyasavanīya anubandhyānām uta agnīṣomīyasya savanīyasya vā uta agniṣomīyasya eva iti kim prāptam aviśeṣat  sarva paśūnām katham aviśeṣaḥ jyotiṣṭoma prakaraṇe sarve paśavaḥ samāmnātāḥ tad prakaraṇa āpanna tvāt sarve paśu dharmāḥ saṃbadhyante na ca eṣām tatra kaścid  viśeṣaḥ evam prāpte brūmaḥ savanīyasya ete dharmāḥ bhaveyuḥ tulyaḥ sarveṣām paśu vidhiḥ syāt  yadi prakaraṇe viśeṣaḥ  na bhavet  bhavati tu prakaraṇe viśeṣaḥ savanīyānām prakaraṇe paśu dharmāḥ samāmnāta ah āgneyaḥ paśuḥ  agniṣṭoma ālabhyaḥ āgneyaḥ  hi  agniṣṭomaḥ aindrāgnaḥ paśuḥ  ukthya ālabhyaḥ aindrāgnāni hi  ukthyāni aindraḥ  vṛṣṇiḥ ṣoḍaśinī  ālabhyaḥ aindraḥ  vai vṛṣṇiḥ  aindraḥ ṣoḍaśī sārasvatī meṣy atirātra ālabhyā vāc  vai sarasvatī iti prakṛtya paśu dharmā āmnātāḥ tasmāt  savanīyasya prakaraṇāt  bhavitum arhati ṃś yad  uktam prakaraṇāt  savanīya arthā iti etad  gṛhṇīmaḥ kramāt  ca agnīṣomīyasya tasya hi krama aupavasathye ahani samāmnātam tasmāt  dvayoḥ  api iti ekeṣām śākhinām śvas  savanīyānām āmnānam tad  apekṣyeyam eṣām guṇa arthā punar śrutiḥ kaḥ punar  guṇaḥ yad  arthā eṣā śrutiḥ ucyate paśūn saṃkīrtya yathā vai matsyaḥ  aviditaḥ  janam avadhuute evam vaite aprajñāyamānā janam avadhunvata iti  eṣām avijñāne doṣam abhidhāya ebhiḥ katham savanāni paśu mantīti praśna rūpakeṇa vapā pracāraḥ  guṇa u vidhīyate tad  arthā eṣā śrutiḥ vapā pracāreṇa eka vākya tvāt kim atas  yadi  evam na savanīyānām prakaraṇena paśu dharmāḥ kramāt  agnīṣomīya arthā eva iti kim punar  tad  chva āmnānam āśvinam graham gṛhītvā trivṛtā yūpam parivīya āgneyam savanīya paśum upākaroti iti na etad  asti kramāt  agnīṣomīya arthā eva iti prakaraṇāt  savanīya arthāḥ pūrvedyus  eva āmnānam vidhāna artham āśvina vākyam kālaguṇa vidhāna artham katham tena vapā pracāreṇa ukṛṣṭasya kāla eṣa vidhīyate prātaḥsavane vapā pracāre codite sati paśu ālambhaḥ  api tatra eva prapnoti tatra kāla aniyame prāpte āśvinam graham gṛhītvā iti kāla mātram vidhīyate trivṛtā yūpam parivīya upākaroti iti  anuvādaḥ itarathā hi parivyāṇasya kālaḥ  vidhīyeta upākaraṇasya ca tatra aneka guṇa vidhānāt  vākyam bhidyeta tasmāt  savanīya arthāḥ paśu dharmā iti na etad  evam agnīṣomīya arthā eva ete kramāt  āśvina kālam hi  āmnānam vidhāna artham guṇa artha etasmin vākyam bhidyeta na vidhāna arthe na hi vapā pracāreṇa utkṛṣṭasya kāla vidhiḥ saṃbhavati eka deśaḥ  hi vapā dravyam tena saṃnipātinaḥ  vapā saṃskārāt  utkarṣet  na upākaraṇam āha arthena tarhi  utkṛṣṭasya kālaḥ  vidhīyate muṣṭinā pidhāya vapa uddharaṇam āsīta ā vapā homāt  iti śrūyate pūrvedyus  vapa uddharaṇam muṣṭinā pidhāya na śaknuyād etāvantam kālam āsīnena avasthātum avaśyam āhāra vihāra ādayaḥ  tena kartavyā iti na etad  evam śruti vipratiṣedhaḥ  bhavet  evam na ca śruti vipratiṣedhaḥ tṛṇa muṣṭinā parṇa muṣṭinā vā pidhāyiṣyate nanu  āsta iti  upaveśane bhavati na avaśyam upaveśana eva audāsīnye api dṛśyate tad  yathā gṛhyāṇi parigṛhya āḥ te kṣetrāṇi parigṛhya asta iti  anupadeśane api bhavati vyāpāra nivṛttau iha api tṛṇa muṣṭinā parṇa muṣṭinā vā pidhāya ā vapā homāt  udāsiṣyate tasmāt  āśvina kālam āmnānam vidhāna artham na savanīyānām prakaraṇe paśu dharmāḥ tasmāt  na savanīya arthāḥ na asti savanīyānām prakaraṇam iti  evam sati pūrveṇa eva hetunā sthānena pūrvasya agnīṣomīyasya bhavitum arhati saṃskāraḥ  ayam paśu yāga prayuktaḥ na jyotiṣṭoma prayuktaḥ jyotiṣṭoma prayukta tve na viśeṣaḥ paśūnām syāt  paśu yāgā api hi dharmān prayoktum apūrva tvāt  samarthāḥ prakaraṇavanta ś ca tasmāt  kramāt  agnīṣomīya dharmā iti itas  ca paśyāmaḥ  agnīṣomīya ārtāḥ paśu dharmā iti kutas  liṅga darśanāt  liṅgam asmin   arthe bhavati vapayā prātaḥsavane caranti puroḍāśena mādhyaṃdine savana iti paśu puroḍāśam darśayati itarathā samāna vidhāneṣu sarveṣu paśuṣu  agnīṣomayoḥ  devatayoḥ saṃskāra arthaḥ san puroḍāśaḥ sāmarthyāt  agnīṣomīyasya bhavet  na savanīyasya tayoḥ  devatayoḥ  abhāvāt  darśayati ca tasmāt  agnīṣomīya arthā iti idam pada uttaram sūtram āha nanu chidra apidhāna arthaḥ paśu puroḍāśaḥ na iti brūmaḥ acodanā guṇa arthena tasya chidra apidhāna arthena na codanā artha vādaḥ sa iti  uktam tasmāt  devatā saṃskāra arthaḥ tasmāt  agnīṣomīya artha tve savanīye puroḍāśasya darśanam upapadyate na sādhāraṇye tasmāt  agnīṣomīya arthāḥ paśu dharmā iti asti sāyaṃdohaḥ tathā asti prātar dohaḥ santi tu doha dharmāḥ śākhā haraṇam gavām prasthāpanam prasāvanam gaḥ dohanam iti evamādayaḥ te kim sāyaṃdoha arthāḥ uta ubhaya arthā iti kim tāvat  prāptam dohayoḥ  tayoḥ  asaṃyuktam dharmaiḥ śṛtam bhavet  kasmāt  sāyaṃdohasya hi krama aupavasathye ahani śākhā haraṇa ādīn samāmananti tasmin   eva ahani sāyaṃdohaḥ tasmāt  kramāt  sāyaṃdoha arthā doha dharmā iti prakaraṇam hi sādhāraṇam yathā eva dadhna evam payasaḥ kramāt  ca prakaraṇam balavattaram tasmāt  ubhaya arthā doha dharmāḥ api ca na sāyaṃdohasya pūrvedyus  āmnānam kva tarhi uttaredyus  katham evam āmananti aindram dadhy amāvāsyāyām aindram payaḥ  amāvāsyāyām iti amāvāsyāyām hi  ubhayam sa aṅgam codyate sa eṣa sāyaṃdohaḥ  arthāt  pūrvedyus  anuṣṭhīyate svabhāva eṣa dadhnaḥ yad  pūrvedyus  upakrāntam aparedyus  abhinirvartate tasmāt  sāyaṃdohasya krama āmātā iti  etad  eva tāvan na asti ata ubhaya arthā doha dharmā iti asti jyotiṣṭomaḥ jyotiṣtomena svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti tatra aindra vāya vādyā grahāḥ prātaḥsavane daśa āmnātāḥ tatra dharmā śrūyante upopte anye grahāḥ sādi ante anupopte dhruvāḥ daśā pavitreṇa graham samārṣṭi iti santi  apare mādhyaṃdine savane apare tṛtīyasavane grahāḥ teṣu mādhyaṃdinīyeṣu tārtīyeṣu ca savaneṣu saṃdehaḥ kim sarveṣu graha dharmāḥ kartavyāḥ uta prātaḥsavane ye grahās teṣu  iti kim prāptam prātaḥsavana graheṣu bhaveyuḥ teṣām hi krame samāmnānāt  na itareṣām evam prāpte brūmaḥ savana antare prātaḥsavanāt  mādhyaṃdine tṛtīyasavane ca grahāmnānam tadvat  eva bhavitum arhati sarveṣām hi tulyam prakaraṇam yatra ete dharmāḥ samāmnātāḥ vākyena graha mātrasya vidhīyante kramāt  ca vākya prakaraṇe balīyasī tasmāt  sarva arthā graha dharmā iti asti jyotiṣṭome paśuḥ  agnīṣomīyaḥ yaḥ  dīkṣitaḥ  yad  agnīṣomīyam paśum ālabhata iti tatra raśanā śrūyate raśanā dharmāś ca trivṛt  bhavati darbha mayī bhavati prapiṣṭānām kartavyā ca iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ete dharmā agnīṣomīya raśanāyāḥ savanīya raśanāyāś ca sādhāraṇāḥ uta agnīṣomīya raśanāyā eva iti kim prāptam prakaraṇāt  agnīṣomīya raśanāyā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ubhayoḥ sādhāraṇā iti kutas  liṅga darśanāt  liṅgam bhavati evam āha āśvinam graham gṛhītvā trivṛtā yūpam parivīya āgneyam paśum upākaroti iti savanīya parivyāṇe raśanām darśayati sā yadi sādhāraṇī tatas  etad  darśanam avakalpate yadi  agnīṣomīya arthāḥ tatas  aprākṛtāt  savanīya parivyāṇān nivarteta savanīye ca parivyāṇa antara prākṛtam yatra trivṛt tvam dṛśyate katham sa vai āśvinam graham gṛhītvā upaniṣkramya yūpam parivyayati iti tatra yadi na sādhāraṇī raśanā vāsasā parivyāṇam prāpnoti raśaṇām tu darśayati tasmāt  sādhāraṇī raśanā tad  sā dhāraṇyāc ca tad dharmā api sādhāraṇāḥ tad  etal liṅgāt  raśanā sādhāraṇyam kaḥ  atra khalu nyāya iti ucyate prakaraṇāt  agnīṣomīyasya vākyāt  yūpa mātrasya iti dūrāt  yad  chiṣyate jyotiṣṭomasya yathā aupasada anuvākyā kāṇḍe aṃśvadābhyau tatra saṃdehaḥ kim jyotiṣṭoma samāmnātā graha dharmāḥ kartavyāḥ uta na iti kim prāptam na kartavyāḥ asaṃnidhānāt  yathā payasā maitrāvaruṇam śrīṇāti iti vacanāt  maitrāvaruṇasya eva śravaṇam na sarveṣām evam idam api dharma jātam prakaraṇa sthānām eva na sarveṣām iti saṃyuktam vā dharmaiḥ evaṃjātīyakam syāt  aprakaraṇa stham api kutas  yatas  prakaraṇāt  vākyam balīyaḥ nanu  anyatra kriya māṇā jyotiṣṭomasya na upakuryuḥ ucyate upakariṣyanti aṃśvadābhyayoḥ  tad artha tvāt  jyotiṣṭoma artha tvāt  cheṣaḥ  ayam graha dharmaḥ graha nimittaḥ  jyotiṣṭomasya upakārakaḥ yāvān grahaḥ  jyotiṣṭomasya upakaroti tasya sarvasya bhavitum arhati tasmāt  aṃśvadābhyayoḥ  api graha dharmāḥ kartavyā iti yad  uktam yathā maitrāvaruṇam payasā śrīṇāti iti tad  yuktam śrayaṇe vacanāt  prakaraṇam bādhitvā vyavasthānam iha tu viparītam tatra sarveṣu graheṣu prakaraṇam viśiṣṭeṣu vākyam iha tu sarveṣu graheṣu vākyam viśiṣṭeṣu prakaraṇam tasmāt  aprakaraṇa sthasya api dharmā iti anārabhya agnim ucyate citriṇīḥ  upadadhāti vajriṇīr upadadhāti bhūta iṣṭakā upadadhāti iti santi tu prakaraṇe iṣṭakā dharmāḥ akhaṇḍām akṛṣṇalām iṣṭakām kuryāt  iti tatha bhasmanā iṣṭakāḥ saṃyujyāt  iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim aprakaraṇe samāmnātānām ime dharmāḥ kartavyāḥ uta na iti kim prāptam na kartavyāḥ kutas  asaṃnidhānāt  iti prāpte ucyate agni aṅgam evaṃjātīyakam tadvat  eva syāt  yadvat  grahāḥ prakaraṇāt  dhi vākyam balavat  amūṣām ca iṣṭakānām agni artha tvāt  jyotiṣṭome śrūyate sa yadi rājanyam vā vaiśyam vā yājayet  sa yadi somam vibhakṣayiṣet  nyagrodhasti bhīḥ  āhṛtya tāḥ saṃpiṣya dadhanī  unmṛjya tam asmai bhakṣam prayacchet  na somam iti jyotiṣṭome santi soma dharmāḥ mānam upāvaharaṇam krayaḥ abhiṣava iti evamādayaḥ tatra saṃdehaḥ kim samāna vidhānā ime dharmāḥ somasya phala camasya ca uta soma dharmāḥ phala camasasya tu tad vikāra tvāt  iti guṇa kāmānām pravṛttiḥ  vā prayojanam adhikaraṇa cintāyāḥ kim prāptam samāna vidhānāḥ prakaraṇa avibhāgāt  iti prāpte ucyate naimittikam evaṃjātīyakam asamāna vidhānam syāt  kutas  atulya tvāt  atulyaḥ somena phala camasaḥ somaḥ  nityavat  āmnātāḥ phala camasaḥ  naimittikaḥ kim atas  yadi  evam dharmā api nityavat  āmnātāḥ na śakyā anityavat  kartum yadi sādhāraṇāḥ tatra anārabhyaḥ  arthaḥ  vidhīyeta api ca naimittikaḥ phala camasaḥ sa soma dharmān gṛhṇāti tatra dharmāḥ sādhāraṇāḥ santaḥ  dvis uktā iti  ucyeran tasmāt  asamāna vidhānāḥ asti pratinidhiḥ śrute dravye apacarati yathā vrīhiṣu  apacaratsu nīvārāḥ tatra saṃdehaḥ kim nīvārāḥ samāna vidhānāḥ uta na iti kim prāptam pratinidhiḥ  ca tadvat  yathā naimi ttikam nityena asamāna vidhānam evam pratinidhiḥ atulya tvāt  kātulya tā vrīhīṇām vihitāḥ na nīvārāṇām iyam atulya tā vrīhīṇām vihitāḥ nīvārāṇām arthāpattyā bhavanti na etad  asti asamāna vidhānaḥ pratinidhiḥ  iti tadvat  syāt  yad vac chrutaḥ na prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ kutas  vrīhi tvam hi vrīhi dharmāṇām vrīhi vyaktau nimittam na ca vrīhitvasya sthāne nīvāra tvam bhavati iti śrūyate tasmāt  na prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ katham tarhi nīvāreṣu dharmā bhavanti iti ucyate yā vrīhi tvena paricchinnā vrīhi vyaktayaḥ nīvāreṣu tāḥ santi tāsām arthena te dharmāḥ kriyante tāsām ca vyaktīnām anyāsām ca vrīhi gatānām tulya eṣa vidhiḥ kā tulya tā ubhaye api vrīhitva lakṣitā iti tasmāt  samāna vidhānā iti itas  ca na pratinidheḥ śrutena saha prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ kutas  artha lakṣaṇa tvāt  arthāt  dhi pratinidhiḥ kriyate na ca arthena etad  avagantum śakyate vrīhitvasya sthāne nīvāra tvam bhavati iti tasmāt  na pratinidheḥ śrutena saha prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ  bhavati iti atha yaḥ śrutaḥ pratinidhiḥ tatra kim sāmāna vidhyam uta na iti yathā yadi somam na vindeta pūtīkān abhiṣuṇuyāt  iti asāmāna vidhyam iti brūmaḥ aśrutād dhy etad  viparītam evam prāpta ucyate niyama arthā guṇa śrutiḥ atra api  artha lakṣaṇa eva pratinidhiḥ some avidyamāne soma sadṛśam dravyam prāptam tatra su sadṛśe dravye prāpta īṣat sadṛśam niyamyate anyasmin pratinidhātavye anyat  pratinidhīyate śrutasya sthāne na yāga dravya tvena asti jyotiṣṭomaḥ tatra saṃsthāḥ samāmnātā agniṣṭomaḥ ukthyaḥ ṣoḍaśī atirātra iti tatra dīkṣaṇīyādayaḥ  dharmāḥ teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim sarva saṃstham jyotiṣṭomam prakṛtya dīkṣaṇīyādayaḥ  dharmā uktāḥ uta agniṣṭoma saṃsthyam abhipretya iti kim prāptam sarva saṃsthāsu samānam vidhānam kutas  prakaraṇa aviśeṣāt  na asti prakaraṇe viśeṣaḥ yena jñāyeta agniṣṭoma saṃstham prakṛtyā iti tasmāt  samāna vidhānāḥ saṃsthā iti tulya iva prakaraṇe vyapadeśaḥ  bhavati yadi  agniṣṭomaḥ  juhoti yadi  ukthyaḥ paridhimanakti yadi  atirātra etad  eva yajuḥ  japan havirdhānam pratipadyeta iti sarva avasthasya viśeṣa vacanāt  avagamyate yadi api sāmānyam tad  api sarva avasthasya eva iti yadi hi na samānam vidhānam agniṣṭoma saṃsthasya eva syāt  na iha agniṣṭomam saṃkīrtayet  asaṃkīrtyamāne api dharma saṃbandhaḥ  bhavati iti sarva avasthasya kīrtanāt  sarva avastha prakaraṇam iti  avagacchāmaḥ api ca śrūyate āgneyam ajam agniṣṭoma ālabheta aindrāgnam dvitīyam ukthye aindram vṛṣṇim tṛtī yam ṣoḍaśinī iti dvitīyasya tṛtīyasya ca darśanam sāmāna vidhye ghaṭate ukthye hi dve nimitte staḥ agniṣṭoma stotram ukthya stotram ca iti tatra dvau naimittikau   āgneyaḥ paśuḥ aindrāgnaḥ  ca iti tena dvitīya darśanam tatra yujyate evam ṣoḍaśinī  atirātre ca prakṛti vikāra bhāve tu pratyakṣa śrutaiḥ  aindra agna ādibhiḥ  atideśena prāpta āgneyaḥ  bādhyeta tatra dvitīya ādi darśanam na upapadyeta bhavati ca tasmāt  sarva avasthasya jyotiṣṭomasya dīkṣaṇīyādayaḥ  dharmā iti na etad  asti samāna vidhānā iti kim tarhi  ukthi ādayaḥ saṃsthā vikāra bhūtāḥ syuḥ agniṣṭoma saṃsthyam urīkṛtya dīkṣaṇīyādayaḥ  dharmāḥ samāmnātāḥ kutas  ukthi ādīnām kāma saṃyogena śravaṇāt  paśu kāma ukthyam gṛhṇīyāt  ṣoḍaśinā vīrya kāmaḥ stuvīta atirātreṇa prajā kāmam yājayet  iti kāmyaḥ  guṇaḥ śrūyamāṇaḥ  nityam artham vikṛtya niviśate katham guṇāt  evaṃjātīyake kāmye phala nirvṛttiḥ paśu kāma ukthyam gṛhṇīyāt  na jyotiṣṭoma kāma ukthya grahaṇa kāmaḥ  vā yathā paśavaḥ  bhavanti tathā gṛhṇīyāt  iti  arthaḥ katham iti tatra avaśyam itikartavya tā apekṣitavyā saṃnidhānān nityasya itikartavyatayā iti gamyate katham punar  yā iyam itikartavya tā sā nityasya iti  avadhāryate na punar  asya eva kāmyasya sādhāraṇī vā iti ucyate yatra yatra guṇe kāmaḥ  bhavati tatra tatra kriyāyām sādhyamānāyām na anyathā sā tatra iti kartavyatā yāntikam upanipatati sā sādhanasya vā sādhyasya vā iti saṃdihyamānā sādhyasya bhavitum arhati na asau sādhyasya abhavantī sādhanena saṃbadhyate evam hi sa itikartavya tā viśeṣaḥ  codyate anena sādhane sādhakam upakuryāt  iti na ca asti sa prakāraḥ yena asādhyamānāyām kriyāyām tena sādhakaḥ kṛtaḥ  bhavet  tasmāt  sādhakasya api iti kartavyatā viśeṣam abhyupagacchatā sādhyasya api iti  etad  abhyupagamanīyam sādhyaś ca jyotiṣṭomaḥ sādhikāḥ saṃsthāḥ tasmāt  jyotiṣṭomasya tāvat  sa itikartavyatā iti siddham atha kasmān na sādhāraṇī nityavat  āmnānāt  yadā eva jyotiṣṭomaḥ tadā eva dīkṣā yadā tu jyotiṣṭome paśu kāmaḥ tad ā ukthya saṃsthāḥ sarvadā jyotiṣṭome dharmāḥ kartavyāḥ ekadā ukthya saṃsthāḥ tatra sarvadā jyotiṣṭomasya dharmāḥ kartavyāḥ te ca ukthya ādi saṃsthasya arthena iti pūrvam uttareṇa virudhyate yadi sarvadā na ukthya ādīnām arthena atha ukthī ādīnām arthena na sarvadā ubhayam viprati ṣiddham tasmāt  na sādhāraṇī nityavat  āmnānam ca yadi  anityasya syāt  nityavat  āmnānam tad  anityam kriyeta tatra nityavat  āmnānam bādhyeta tasmāt  nitya saṃsthasya jyotiṣṭomasya na kāmyasya ukthya ādi saṃsthasya iti nanu  agniṣṭoma saṃsthā api kāmyā śrūyate dve hi tatra āmnāte ekam nityavat  ekam kāmyam tatra dvayoḥ  vākyayoḥ sāmarthyān nitya eva sa kāmaḥ  bhaviṣyati nitya tā vidhātaḥ na asti iti  agniṣṭoma saṃsthasya jyotiṣṭomasya dīkṣaṇīyādayaḥ  dharmā bhaviṣyanti iti atha yad  uktam dvitīya tṛtīya darśanam samāna vidhi tve avakalpate na anyathā iti vacanam tad  bhaviṣyati na darśanam aindrāgna ukthye dvitīyaḥ  vidhīyate tathā aindraḥ ṣoḍaśini tṛtīyaḥ itas  ca paśyāmaḥ prakṛti vikāra bhāva iti kutas  pratiṣedhāt  pūrva liṅgānām yadi  agniṣṭomaḥ  juhoti yadi  ukthyaḥ paridhimanakti na juhoti iti homa abhāva darśanam na syāt  prāpte nimitte vacana prāmāṇyāt  sāmāna vidhye atha yad  uktam vyapadeśa iti ekasya eva adhikṛtasya yathā uktena nyāyena ayam anadhikṛtena guṇena vyapadeśaḥ agniṣṭoma grahaṇam ca anuvāda iti staḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau tatra barhis  barhis  dharmāś ca tathā vediḥ  vedi dharmāś ca tatra saṃdehaḥ kim barhirādayaḥ  barhiḥ ādi dharmāś ca pradhānasya utāṅga pradhānānām iti kim tāvat  prāptam prakaraṇa viśeṣāt  asaṃyuktam pradhānasya pradhānasya evaṃjātīyakā dharmāḥ kasmāt  prakaraṇa viśeṣāt  pradhānānām hi prakaraṇam na aṅgānām prakaraṇena ca eṣām saṃbandhaḥ tasmāt  pradhānasya sarveṣām vāṅga pradhānānām ime dharmāḥ na atra śeṣa tvam prakaraṇāt  bhavati upakāra lakṣaṇam hi tad  yad  yasya upakaroti tad  tasya śeṣa bhūtam sarveṣām ca aṅga pradhānānām ime dharmā upakurvanti katham avagamyate vākyāt  vedyām havīṃṣy āsādayati iti haviḥ mātram vākyāt  gamyate pradhāna havīṃṣi prakaraṇāt  vākyam ca prakaraṇāt  balīyaḥ tasmāt  barhiṣi havīṃṣy āsādayati iti āha yadi prakaraṇam vākyena bādhyate loke api barhiṣām ime dharmā uktā bhavanti tatra kaḥ  doṣaḥ sarvatra dharmāḥ kartavyāḥ prāpnuvanti ucyate prakaraṇāt  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  upakārakā eva iti gamyate tasmāl laukikeṣu na kartavyāḥ evam ced  aṅgāni  api na darśa pūrṇamāsa śabadakāni tasmāt  teṣu  api na prāpnuvanti ucyate yadi  api  aṅgāni na darśa pūrṇam āsa śabdakāni darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  upakārakāṇi eṣu kriyamāṇā dharmā darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  upakariṣyanti tasmāt  aṅga pradhāneṣu kartavyā iti piṇḍa pitṛ yajñe api barhis  dharmaiḥ  yujyeta saḥ  api dāte barhiṣi vartate tasya ca api barhiṣā asti prayojanam tad  api  ārāt  chiṣṭa dharmavat  syāt  na tasya barhis  etaiḥ  dharmaiḥ  dharmavat  vākyam hi  ekam darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām saha dharmāṇām tena darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  upakārakā dharmāḥ yad  darśa pūrṇamāsa artham tatra prāpnuvanti na anyatra tasmāt  piṇḍa pitṛ yajña barhiṣaḥ na bhaviṣyanti liṅgam bhavati evam āha sa vai dhruvām eva agre abhidhārayati tatas  hi prathama avājya bhāgau yakṣyan bhavati iti  abhidhāraṇasya ājya bhāga artha tām darśayati jyotiṣṭome keśa śmaśruṇoḥ  vapanam payaḥ vratāni tapaḥ  ca āmnātāni teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim aṅga pradhāna arthāni  uta pradhāna arthāni kim tāvat  prāptam aṅga pradhāna arthāni iti pūrveṇa nyāyena prāptam evam prāpte brūmaḥ svāmi yuktam etad  tasmāt  pradhānasya kasmāt  phala saṃyogāt  puruṣasya yogena ayam saṃbandhaḥ yāgaḥ  apūrvasya dātā puruṣaḥ pratigrahītā nanu  aparaḥ  api  asti saṃbandhaḥ yāgaḥ  nirvartyaḥ puruṣaḥ  abhinirvartaka iti phalena tu saṃbandhaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti  evam arthaḥ puruṣaḥ śrūyate na hi yāgam sa sādhayati yāgaḥ sat tayā saṃbhantsyata iti kim iti tarhi nirvartayataḥ phalam bhavati iti saṃskāra aś ca saṃskurvanti iti  ucyante yad  tasya saṃskartavyasya prayojanam tatra sāmarthyam janayanti iti phalam ca grahītum puruṣasya prayojanam na yāgam abhinirvartayitum tasmāt  ye puruṣa saṃskāra aḥ  te puruṣam phala pratigrahaṇa samartham kurvanti na yāga nirvṛtti samartham āha yadi yāga nirvṛttau na sāmarthyam janayanti katham tarhi yāga dharma as te bhavanti ucyate yāgasya sva artham sādhayataḥ sāhāyye vartante kaś ca tasya sva arthaḥ yad  asya kartā phalena saṃbadhyate tasmāt  svāmi saṃskārāḥ pradhāna arthā iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate ṣaṭtriṃśat prakamā prācī caturviṃśatiḥ  agreṇa triṃśaj jaghanena iyati śakyāmaha iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim eṣā vediḥ  aṅga pradhāna arthā uta pradhāna artha iti kim tāvat  prāptam cikīrṣayā ca saṃyogāt  pradhāna artha iti kā cikīrṣā iyati śakṣyāmaha iti yad  cikīrṣitam tasya arthena eṣā śrūyate śakṣyāmahe asyām kartum iti pradhānam ca tasya cikīrṣitam na aṅgāni pradhānam hi phalavan na aṅgāni āha yadi  aṅgāni na cikīrṣitāni kim artham kriyanta iti ucyate acikīrṣitāni  api  aṅgāni kriyante yadi  api tāni na cikīrṣyante tathā api taiḥ  acikīrṣitaiḥ  anyāt  cikīrṣyate tasmāt  tāni kriyanta iti yad  cikīrṣitam tasya vediḥ tasmāt  pradhāna artha iti sthitam tāvat  aparyavasitam staḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau tatra śrūyate caturhotrā paurṇamāsīm abhimṛśet  pañca hotrā amāv āsyām iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim aṅga pradhāna artham abhimarśanam uta pradhāna artham iti kim tāvat  prāptam pradhāna artham iti pradhāna nāmadheyam ca etad  paurṇamāsy amāvāsyā iti ca tasmāt  pradhānasya abhimarśanam iti sthitāt  uttaram yad  uktam pradhānam cikīrṣitam na aṅgāni tasmāt  pradhānasya vediḥ  iti tad  na tad  yukte phala śrutiḥ sa aṅgāt  phalam śrūyate tasmāt  sa aṅgam cikīrṣitam yadi  api  aṅgāni na cikī rṣitāni tathā api vedyām kartavyāni anyathā na sa aṅgam vedyām kṛtam bhavati yad  uktam pradhāna nāma tvāt  paurṇamāsī śabdasya amāvāsyā śabdasya ca pradhāna haviṣām abhimarśanam iti na etad  evam aṅga haviṣām api  abhimaṛśanam syāt  kutas  guṇa abhidhānāt  guṇa u abhimarśanam iti  abhidhānam bhavati katamat  tad abhidhānam yad  guṇa u abhimarśanam iti brūte paurṇamāsīm amāvāsyām iti ca dvitīya antam paurṇamāsī artham abhimarśanam kartavyam amāvāsyā artham abhimarśanam kartavyam iti atas  yatra yatra kriyamāṇam paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāyām vā upakaroti tatra tatra kartavyam yad  yad  paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāyām vā abhisaṃbadhyate sāksāt  praṇāḍyā vā tatra tatra kriyamāṇam tayoḥ  upakaroti tasmāt  pradhāna haviṣām aṅga haviṣām ca kartavyam iti jyotiṣṭome dīkṣāḥ śrūyate tisraḥ  dīkṣā iti tathā dakṣiṇāḥ śrūyante tasya dvādaśa śatam dakṣiṇā iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim dīkṣā dakṣiṇam aṅga pradhāna artham uta pradhāna artham iti kim prāptam puruṣāṇām aṅga pradhāna artha tvāt  dīkṣā dakṣiṇasya aṅga pradhāna artha tā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ dīkṣā dakṣiṇam pradhānasya kutas  vacanāt  vacanam hi bhavati dīkṣāḥ somasya dakṣiṇāḥ somasya iti na hi vacanasya ati bhāraḥ  nāma kvacid  tasmāt  dīkṣā dakṣiṇam vacanāt  somasya iti nivṛttim dīkṣāṇām darśayati katham adhvaryaḥ  yad  paśunāya akṣīḥ atha kā asya dīkṣā iti yad  ṣaṣ ḍhotāram juhoti sā asya dīkṣā iti asatyām api dīkṣāyām vacanam bhavati tasmāt  aṅgānām dīkṣā dakṣiṇam iti asti jyotiṣṭome paśuḥ  agnīṣomīyaḥ yaḥ  dīkṣitaḥ  yad  agnīṣomīyam paśum ālabhata iti tatra yūpam prakṛtya śrūyate vajraḥ  vai yūpaḥ  yad  antarvedi muniyāt  tad  nirdahet  yad  barhiḥ vedy anavaruddhaḥ syāt  ardham antarvedi minoti  ardham bahis vedy anavaruddhaḥ  bhavati na nirdahati iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim antar vedī iti yūpāṅga bhāvena vediḥ  upadiśyate uta ardham antar vedy ardham bahis vedī iti deśa lakṣaṇa artham ucyata iti katham yūpāṅga bhāvena katham vā deśa lakṣaṇa iti yadi yūpa ardhasya vedi antarasya ca saṃbandhaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ evam vedi saṃbaddhaḥ  yūpaḥ kartavyaḥ tatas  yūpāṅga bhāvena atha yasmin deśe mīyamānasya ardham vedi abhyantare ardham ca bahis  sa deśa upadiśyate tatas  deśa lakṣaṇā kim prāptam tathā yūpasya vediḥ yathā dīkṣā dakṣiṇam pradhānasya tathā yūpasya vediḥ tathā yūpaḥ  mātavyaḥ tathā mīyamānasya ardham vedi abhyantare bhavati evam vedi śrutiḥ  api  anugrahīṣyate itarathā vedi śabdaḥ  lakṣayet  deśam śruti lakṣaṇa aviṣaye śrutiḥ  nyāyyā na lakṣaṇā tasmāt  yūpāṅga bhāvena vediḥ  nirdiśyate deśā mātram vā vedi śabdena lakṣyate na vediyūpa aṅgam kutas  aśiṣyeṇa eka vākya tvāt  ardham antarvedi minoti  ardham bahis vedī iti  etena eka vākyatā yā sā śāsitavyena yadi deśa lakṣaṇā atha yūpāṅga bhāvena vedyā nirdeśaḥ tatas  na śāsitavyaḥ  bahis vedi nirdeśaḥ  bhavati vedyām yūpasya aṅga bhāvena upadiśyamānāyām ardham bahis vedī iti  etad  uccāryamāṇam na kasmiṃścid  upakāre vartate atha bahis vedi deśam api yūpāṅga bhāvena upadiśet vākyam bhidyeta tasmāt  yūpāṅga bhāvena vedyā nirdeśe bahis vedi śabdaḥ sarvathā na śāsitavyaḥ yadi tu deśa lakṣaṇā tatas  viśiṣṭe deśe lakṣyamāṇe avaśya vaktavyaḥ  bahis vedi śabdaḥ  bhavati anucyamāne vedi abhyantare yasmin kasmiṃś ca pradeśe yūpa iti gamyate atha punar  bahis vedi śabde śrūyamāṇe yatarasmin deśe mīyamānasya ardham antar vedy ardham bahis vedi sa deśaḥ  lakṣayitum iṣṭaḥ  bhavati sa ca bahis vedi śabdena vinā na śakyate lakṣayitum iti  avaśyam śāsitavyaḥ  bhavati tasmāt  deśa lakṣaṇa iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate uta yad  sunvanti sāmidhenī s tad  anvāhuḥ  iti havirdhānayoḥ  yasmin havirdhāne sunvanti tad  sāmidhenībhiḥ saṃbandhayet  iti  arthaḥ tatra saṃdehaḥ kim sāmīdhenīnām aṅga bhāvena havirdhānam codyate havirdhāna viśiṣṭāḥ sāmidhenyaḥ  anuvaktavyāḥ uta havirdhānena amūṣām anūcyamānānām deśaḥ  lakṣyata iti kim tāvat  prāptam sāmidhenīnām aṅga tvena havirdhānam codyate yasmin havirdhāne sunvanti tad  sāmidhenībhiḥ saṃbandhayet  iti tena havirdhāna saṃbaddhāḥ sāmidhenyaḥ  anuvaktavyā iti vacanāt  sāmidhenī aṅga bhāve sati havirdhāna śrutiḥ  anugrahīṣyate itarathā deśam lakṣayet  iti tasmāt  sāmidheni aṅgam havirdhānam deśa lakṣaṇa artham vaitat  ucyate yasmin sunvanti tasmin deśe sāmidhenyaḥ  anuvaktavyā iti pratyakṣam hi  artha karma somasya tena kriyate dakṣiṇe havirdhāne somam āsādayati iti soma āsādana artham tāvat  etad  upādeyam sāmidhenyaḥ  api  agni samindhana artham upādeyā iti iha tu  etāvat  chrūyate yasya havirdhānasya samīpe sunvanti tad saṃbaddhāḥ sāmidhenyaḥ  api  agni samindhana artham upādeyā iti tatra na jñāyate kim sāmidhenyaḥ saṃbaddhāḥ havirdhānasya upakurvanti kim havirdhānam sāmidhenīnām iti tad  ucyate sāmidhenya s tāvat  dhavirdhānasya na upakurvanti na hi tāvat  vidhīyante sāmidhenyaḥ  anuvaktavyā iti kim tarhi havirdhāna viśeṣa saṃbandha s tāsām vidhīyate na ca avihitam aṅgam bhavati na api  evam vidhīyate havirdhānam āsām anucyamānānām upādātavyam saṃbandhayitum iti katham tarhi havirdhānī viśeṣa saṃbandhaḥ sāmidhenīnām śrūyate havirdhāna saṃbandhaḥ  vidhīyate na ca sāmidhenī saṃbandhaḥ  havirdhānasya prāptaḥ yaḥ  viśeṣa artham anūdyeta kena tarhi havirdhānasya saṃbandhaḥ pratyakṣam hi  artha karma somasya na tu sāmidhenīkarma pratyakṣam havirdhānasya bhavati tu deśasya sāmidhenī saṃbandhaḥ apareṇa vedim iti hotuḥ  deśaḥ  lakṣitaḥ sa uttarasya dakṣiṇasya vā havirdhānasya samāsannaḥ tatra yad  sunvanti tad  anvāhuḥ  iti  upapadyate vacanam tasmāt  deśa lakṣaṇa artham havirdhāna grahaṇam atha evam abhisaṃbandhaḥ kasmān na bhavati yasmin havirdhāne sunvanti tasya havirdhānasya sāmidhenī saṃbandha iti na evam śakyam evam dvau   arthau vidhātavyau bhavataḥ havirdhāna saṃbandhaḥ  havirdhāna viśeṣa saṃbandhaḥ  ca tatra vākyam bhidyate tasmāt  na evam abhisaṃbandha iti samākhyānam ca tadvat  eva bhavati yathā asmābhiḥ  nyāya upadiṣṭaḥ soma artham havirdhānam iti iha karmāṇi  udāharaṇam agni hotram juhuyāt  svarga kāmaḥ darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta jyotiṣṭomena svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim etāni karmāṇi svayam anuṣṭhātavyāni uta atra utsarga mātram svayam kuryāt  śeṣam anyaḥ svayam vā uta śeṣam anya eva iti kim prāptam svayam prayoge syāt  kutas  yatas  svayam prayuñjānasya phalam bhavati katham avagamyate tad lakṣaṇa tvāt śabdaḥ  asya arthasya lakṣaṇam svayam prayuñjānasya phalam bhavati iti katamaḥ sa śabdaḥ svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti yaḥ svargam kāmayate sa eva ucyate yāge kartā bhavan phalam sādhayet  iti sa aṅge ca kartā bhavan phalam prāpnoti tasmāt  svayam prayoge syāt  utsarge prādhānyam asti katham ya utsargam karoti tena sarvam kṛtam bhavati katham parikraya utsargaḥ tena anantāḥ sarvam kurvanti tasmāt  yaḥ parikrayam karoti tena svayam eva sarvam kṛtam bhavati tasmāt  utsarga mātram svayam kuryāt  śeṣam anyaḥ svayam vā śeṣasya anya eva syāt  kartā kutas  parikrayasya āmnāna tvāt puruṣān ati prakāreṣu bahuṣu prāpteṣu parikrayaḥ  niyataḥ tasmāt  parikrayeṇa ānataiḥ sarve padārthāḥ kartavyā iti vipratiṣeddhaḥ  ca ātmani parikrayaḥ yadi svayam kuryāt  aparikrītena kṛtam syāt  tatra parikrayāmnānānarthakyam adṛṣṭa arthaḥ  vā pratijñāyeta tasmāt  anyaiḥ parikrītaiḥ śeṣāḥ padārthāḥ kartavyā iti utsargam tu svayam kurvatā sarvam svayam kṛtam bhavati tatra taiḥ parikrītaiḥ kartavyeṣu  aniyamena kartṛ parimāṇam syāt  kutas  aviśeṣāt  na kartṛ parimāṇe viśeṣaḥ kaścid  āmnāyate arthena tad parimāṇam yāva adbhiḥ  asau   itikartavya tā nirvartate tāvataḥ  vṛṇīta yāvanti kartṛ nāmadheyāni karmāṇi śrūyante tāvantaḥ  varītavyā bhidyante tāni ca nāmadheya śravaṇāni tān puraḥ adhvaryuḥ  vibhajati pratiprasthātā manthinam juhoti na iṣṭā patnīm abhyudāyati unnetā camasān unnayati iti tathā prastotā prastauti udgātā udgāyati pratihartā pratiharati subrahmaṇyaḥ subrahmaṇyām āha hotā prātaranuvākam anubrūte maitrāvaruṇaḥ preṣyati ca anuca āha acchāvākaḥ  yajati grāva stotrīyām anvāha etāvadbhiḥ karmaṇi prayojanam tena te avaśyam etāni yathā aśrutāni kartum varītavyāḥ etad  vyatiriktaḥ  anyaḥ padārthaḥ  na vidyate yaḥ  api vākyena na upadiṣṭaḥ sa samākhyayā gamyate tasmāt  etāvataḥ  vṛṇīta iti evam ced  pratijñāyate etāvataḥ  vṛṇīta iti tad  na yaḥ  yaḥ  tad karma kariṣyati iti saṃkalpate sa sa tad  tad  chabda abhidheyaḥ  bhavati ekaḥ  api bahūn padārthān kartum bahubhiḥ  nāmadheyaiḥ  ucyeta tasmāt  aniyamaḥ na etad  evam utpattau puruṣāṇām utpādyamāneṣu puruṣeṣu nāmadheyāni bhidyante brāhmaṇam vṛṇīte hotāram vṛṇīte udgātāram vṛṇīte adhvaryum vṛṇīta iti evamādi tasmāt  karmaṇi taiḥ  evam nāmakaiḥ prayojanam avaśyante varītavyāḥ tasmāt  eṣām varaṇe saṃkīrtanam na vidhiḥ prayojanasya abhāvan na anuvādaḥ na vede tāvantaḥ  varītavyā iti brūyāt  anarthakam eva syāt  śaknoti ca idam pratyāyayitum saṃkhyā viśeṣam tasmāt  yaḥ saṃkhyā viśeṣaḥ  eṣām pratīyate tad artham etad  vacanam tasmāt  ṣoḍaśa kartāraḥ  varītavyāḥ somas tāvat  kartṛkaḥ  ca syāt  evam darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  api santi jyotiṣṭome camasādhvaryavaḥ cama sa adhvaryūn vṛṇīta iti teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim eṣām anyatamāḥ uta etebhyaḥ  anya iti kim tāvat  prāptam etāvatām saṃkīrtanāt  eṣām eva anyatamāḥ iti prāpte brūmaḥ camasādhvarya vaś ca apare bhaveyuḥ  tebhyaḥ  anya iti kutas  taiḥ  vyapadeśāt  taiḥ parigaṇitaiḥ  eṣām vyapadeśaḥ  bhavati madhyataḥkāriṇām camasādhvaryavaḥ hotrakāṇām camasa adhvaryava iti nanu ya eva prakṛtā as te camasa adhvaryavaḥ  bhaveyuḥ na iti brūmaḥ kutas  taiḥ  vyapadeśāt  madhyataḥkāriṇām camasa adhvaryavaḥ  hotrakāṇām camasa adhvaryava iti ṣaṣṭhī saṃbandhe sati bhavati ṛtvigbhiḥ  te vyapadiśyante ṛtvijas teṣām svāminaḥ  na yajamānaḥ yajamāna puruṣebhyaś ca ete anya iti naḥ pratijñātam na yajamānena camasādhvaryavam kartum varītavyāḥ ṛtvigbhiḥ  te varītavyā iti api ca eṣām utpatti vākya eva bhedaḥ cama sa adhvaryūn vṛṇīta iti teṣu  va saṃdehaḥ kim aniyamaḥ ekaḥ  dvau bahavaḥ  vā uta bahava eva iti aniyama iti prāpta ucyate bahava iti kutas  utpattau bahu śruteḥ camasa adhvaryava iti  eṣām utpattau bahu śrutiḥ  bhavati tasmāt  bahava iti jyotiṣṭome santi camasādhvaryavaḥ te ca bahava iti  uktam kiyantaḥ  bahava iti saṃdehe trayaḥ bahuvacana sāmarthyāt  iti prāpte brūmaḥ daśa tvam liṅga darśanāt  te daśa bhaveyuḥ tathā hi liṅgam jyotiṣṭoma vikāre daśa peye śrūyate daśa camasa adhvaryavaḥ  daśa daśa ekaikam camasam anusarpanti iti etasmāt  kāraṇāt  daśa peyaḥ  bhavati iti bruvan daśa cama sa adhvaryūn darśayati yadi trayaḥ  bhaveyuḥ etad darśanam na upapadyate tasmāt  trīn atītya eṣā saṃkhyā yadi ca daśa na bhaveyuḥ  na upapadyeta etad darśanam tasmāt  bhavanti daśa daśa ca eṣām svāminaḥ tasmāt  prayojana bhāvāt  daśa saṃkhyā upādīyate tasyām ca upādīyamānāyām aparā api saṃkhyā anugṛhyate tena api daśa bhaveyuḥ asti śamitā śamitāram upanayīta iti sa kim saṃkīrtitānām anyatamaḥ uta anya s tebhya iti kim prāptam teṣām varaṇe saṃkīrtanāt  teṣām anyatamaḥ iti prāpte ucyate śamitā ca śabda bhedāt  śabdaḥ  bhidyate evaṃsaṃjñakena idam karma kartavyam iti tasmāt  evaṃsaṃjñaka utpādayitavyaḥ asya saṃkīrtanāt  saṃkhyā av vṛddhiḥ  gamyate tasmāt  anyaḥ śamitā syāt  api ca klomā cordham vaikartanam ca śamituḥ tad  brāhmaṇāya dadyāt  yad brāhmaṇaḥ syāt  iti  abrāhmaṇa āśaṅkā bhavati sā ṛtviji na upapadyate satyam saṃkhyā vivṛddhiḥ  gamyate na tu utpadyamāneṣu yā tu  anutpattiḥ  teṣu gamyate tatra ekasya karma bhedāt  iti  evam api  avakalpate yad  tu
