bhavet  śākhām anuniṣpannaḥ  gṛhyate katham tad prādhānyam śākhām parivāsya iti dvitīya anirdeśāt nanūpa veṣam karoti iti  api dvitīyā ucyate na asau parivāsayateḥ karma kasya tarhi karoteḥ āha kasmāt  evam abhisaṃbandhaḥ  na bhavati śākhām parivāsya mūlata upaveṣam karoti iti śākhā śabdaḥ  ca yathā eva agre tathā mūle api tatra ayam arthaḥ chedena agra mūle vibhajet  kim prayojanam vibhajya mūlam upaveṣam kariṣyāmi iti ucyate na evam vyavahita kalpanā hi  evam bhavet  avayava dhānena śākhā artham parivāsanam vṛtte tasmin   upaveṣa karaṇam nanu prakṛta tvāt  mūlam upaveṣa śabdena saṃbadhyate ucyate ubhaya saṃbandhe virodhaḥ virodhe ca prakaraṇāt  vākyam balīyaḥ atha saṃnihitena saṃbadhyate tathā api śākhā prayuktena iti  āpatati atas  siddham eva uva veṣaḥ  na prayojayati chedanam iti etad  atra vaiṣamyam śākhayā vatsān apākaroti śākhayā gāḥ prāpayati śākhayā dohayati iti  evamādiṣu śākhā grahaṇeṣu na upaveṣasya vyāpāraḥ  tatas  śākhā śabdaḥ  apaiti na hi tad mūlam śākhā iti  ācakṣate kim atas  yatra evam yatra śākhā śabdaḥ tad artham chedanam dvitīya anirdeśāt atha api mūle śākhā śabdaḥ  bhavet  evam api śākhā śabda upadiṣṭeṣu na mūlam amūla parivāsita tvāt  yad  ca evam saṃskṛtayā śākhayā kriyate tad artham chedanam na ca upadhānam mūla parivāsitayā kriyate tasmāt  na tad artham chedanam kim bhavati prayojanam paurṇamāsyām api śākhā utpādyā yathā pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ yathā siddhāntaḥ tathā na utpādayitavyā iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  āmananti saha śākhayā prastaram praharati iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim śākhā praharaṇam pratipatti karma uta artha karma iti kim prāptam haraṇe tu juhotiḥ syāt  artha karma iti  arthaḥ kutas  yoga sāmānyāt yogaḥ  asyāḥ samānaḥ prastareṇa saha śākhayā prastaram praharati iti saha yoge yatra tṛtīyā tasya guṇa bhāvaḥ yatra dvitīyā tasya prādhānyam prastare ca vispaṣṭaḥ  yajiḥ śākhā api tasmin   eva yajau prastarasya viśeṣaṇam samāna yogi tvāt  āha nanu tatra tatra guṇa bhūtā śākhā tasyāḥ pratipattiḥ  nyāyyāḥ itaratha aneka guṇa bhāvaḥ prasajyeta iti ucyate dravyāṇām ca artha śeṣa tvāt  utpattyā cikīrṣitasya śeṣa bhūtāni  eva dravyāṇi  upadiśyante bhūtam bhavyāya upadiśyata iti tasmāt  aneka guṇa tā eva dravyānām nyāyyā iti pratipattiḥ  vā śākhā praharaṇam śabdasya tad pradhāna tvāt  śabdaḥ  atra śākhā pradhānaḥ katham dvitīya aśravaṇāt nanu  anyatra eva sā dvitīyā prastare na śākhāyām ucyate prastare dvitīya arthaḥ śākhāyām api katham tulya yogāt  saha śākhayā evam prastaraḥ prahṛtaḥ  bhavati yadi śākhā api prahriyate tena tulya yoge saha śabdaḥ  ayam yadi prastaraḥ praharaṇe pradhānam śākhā api prastara viśeṣaṇam na tarhi tulya yogaḥ tasmāt  yaḥ prastare dvitīya arthaḥ sa śākhāyām api atas  śākhā pradhānam api ca tatra tatra śākhā guṇa bhūtā tasyām anyatra upadiśyamānāyām aneka guṇa bhāvaḥ tatra kaḥ  doṣaḥ dṛṣṭam kāryam hitvā adṛṣṭam kalpyeta kṛta prayojanāyāḥ śākhāyāḥ  apanayanena vedi vivecanāt  sukha pracāraḥ  dṛṣṭam kāryam na tu prahareṇa kiṃcid  sūkṣmam api dṛṣṭam asti tasmāt  pratipattiḥ  nyāyyā āha nanu tṛtīyā śravaṇāt para arthena śākhā uccāraṇena bhavitum nyāyyam ucyate bhavet  etad  nyāyyam yadi nirjñāta kālā śākhā syāt  tatas  prastarasya kāla paricchedāya kīrtyamānā para arthā uccāryeta iha punar  etad  viparītam nirjñāta kālaḥ prastaraḥ  anirjñāta kālā śākhā tasmāt  sati  api tṛtīya aśravaṇe prastara eva śākhāyāḥ kālam paricchetsyati yathā dvitīyā nirdiṣṭaḥ tathā śākhā draṣṭavyā yathā tṛtīyā nirdiṣṭā tathā prastaraḥ sāmarthyam hi balavattaram iti āha nanu guṇa bhāve api dvitīyā bhavati yathā saktu māruta eka kapāleṣu na etad  saktvā ādibhiḥ  tulyam tasya saktvādeḥ  anyatra anadhikārāt  iha ca śākhayā anyasya arthasya kṛta tvāt  vatsa apākaraṇa ādeḥ āha nanu punaruktam etad  saktvādīnām pradarśanam samādhiḥ  ca iti ucyate na punarukta tā mahān doṣaḥ bahu kṛtvā u api pathyam veditavyam bhavati grantha bhayena punaruktam na icchanti artha agrahaṇāt  tu bibhyataḥ punar  punar  abhidhīyamānam bahu manyanta eva kim cintāyāḥ prayojanam yadi  artha karma paurṇamāsyām api śākhā utpādyā atha pratipattiḥ  na utpādayitavyā iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  āmnāyate apaḥ praṇayati  āpaḥ  vai śraddhā śraddhām eva ālabhya yajata iti ubhayatra ca praṇītānām vyāpāraḥ praṇītābhiḥ  havīṃṣi saṃyauti iti tathā antarvedi praṇītā ninayati iti atra saṃdehaḥ kim ubhayam āsām prayojakam saṃyavanam ninayanam ca uta saṃyavana arthānām ninayanam pratipattiḥ  iti kim prāptam utpatti saṃyogaḥ  nāsām kenacid  prayojanena ubhābhyām utpannānām saṃyogaḥ tasmāt  na gamyate viśeṣaḥ agamyamāne viśeṣe ubhaya arthānām vibhāgaḥ  ayam kaścid  yāgaḥ saṃyavane kaścid  ninayana iti ājyavat  yathā sarvasmai vā etad  yajñāya gṛhyate yad  dhruvāyām ājyam iti saṃyavana arthāḥ praṇītāḥ kutas  tṛtīyā nirdeśāt saṃyavane apām guṇa bhāvaḥ dvitīyā nirdeśāt  ca ninayane prādhānyam cintāyāḥ prayojanam puroḍāśa abhāve praṇītānām abhāvaḥ yathā payasyāyām jyotiṣṭome śrūyate vāc  vai devebhyaḥ  apākrāmat  yajñāya atiṣṭhamānā sā vanaspatīn prāviśat  sā eṣā vāc  vanaspatiṣu vadati yā dundubhau yā ca tūṇave yā ca vīṇāyām yad  dīkṣitāya daṇḍam prayacchati vācam eva avarundhe krīte some maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍam prayacchati iti maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍam prayacchati iti  etad  udāharaṇam tatra saṃśayaḥ kim dīkṣita dhāraṇe śeṣa bhūtasya daṇḍasya maitrāvaruṇa dhāraṇam pratipattiḥ athavā artha karma iti kim prāptam maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍa dānam pratipattiḥ kutas  dīkṣita dhāraṇe kṛtārtha tvāt daṇḍena dīkṣayanti iti śeṣa bhūtasya anyatra vyāpāraḥ pratipattiḥ  nyāyyā yathā cātvāle kṛṣṇa viṣāṇām prāsyati iti kaṇḍūyane śeṣa bhūtāyāḥ prāsanam pratipattiḥ evam atra api draṣṭavyam dvitīyā ca daṇḍe vibhaktiḥ tasmāt  prādhānyam iti artha karma vā syāt  kutas  kartṛ saṃyogāt  kartṛ saṃyogaḥ  bhavati maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍam iti kartṛ daṇḍa saṃyogaḥ  bhavati tasmin   ca daṇḍaḥ  guṇa bhūtaḥ puruṣaḥ pradhāna bhūtaḥ puruṣam hi sa pracaritum samartham karoti katham yathā pūrvam tamaḥ  avagāhate apaḥ sarpati gām ca sarpam ca vārayati avalambanam ca bhavati atas  puruṣa prādhānyān na pratipattiḥ srajvat  ca draṣṭavyam yathā srajam udgātre dadāti iti  asati  api  upakāre puruṣasya prayojanavat tvāt  niṣprayojana tvāt  ca srajaḥ bhavati puruṣa prādhānyam evam iha api draṣṭavyam tasmāt  na pratipattiḥ  iti atha yad  uktam dvitīya aśravaṇāt  daṇḍa prādhānyam iti ucyate tathā yuktam ca anīpsitam iti dvitīyā draṣṭavyā kutas  maitrāvaruṇe caturthī nirdeśāt saṃpradāne hi caturthī bhavati saṃpradānam ca karmaṇā abhipreyate tatra daṇḍāt  abhipretataraḥ  maitrāvaruṇa iti gamyate daṇḍī praiṣān anvāha iti  anūdyate tena pracarataḥ  daṇḍam pradarśayati tad  artha kara maṇi sati  upapadyate pratipattau tu daṇḍaḥ  maitrāvaruṇāya datta s tatas  apavṛjyeta kṛtam ca kartavyam iti na tena prayojam iti na dhāryeta tatra etad darśanam na upapadyate tathā ahis tvām daśati iti maitrāvaruṇam brūyāt  ahir iva hi  eṣa iti tathā muśalyan vāha iti muśala śabdaḥ  ca daṇḍe prasiddhaḥ yathā kva nu khalu muśalinaḥ  māṇavakā gaṅgām avatareyuḥ  iti tasmāt  api  artha karma yad  uktam yathā kṛṣṇa viṣāṇa aprāsanam iti tatra ucyate yuktam tatra utpadyamānam yad  yena prayojanena saṃbaddham utpadyate tad  tad artham eva nyāyyam tasya anyatra gamane pratipattiḥ  iti  etad  upapadyate yadi na dṛṣṭam prayojanam bhavati iha tu dṛṣṭam prayojanam maitrāvaruṇasya dhāraṇae tasmāt  viṣamam etad  athavā adhikaraṇa antaram viṣāṇāyāḥ kaṇḍūyanam prāsanam ca ubhayam api prayojakam iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ eka niṣpatteḥ sarvam samam syāt  iti utttaraḥ pakṣaḥ kaṇḍūyane tṛtīyā nirdeśāt  viṣāṇāyāḥ  guṇa bhāvaḥ prāsane ca dvitīya anirdeśāt anyatra ca kṛtārtha tvāt prādhānyam iti asti jyotiṣṭome avabhṛthaḥ vāruṇena eka kapālena avabhṛtham abhyavapanti iti tatra āmnāyate varuṇa gṛhītam vaitat  yajñasya yadṛjīṣam yad grāvāṇa yad aunduvarī yad abhiṣavaṇa phalake tasmāt  yad kiṃcid  soma liptam dravyam tena avabhṛtham yanti iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim soma liptānām dravyāṇām avabhṛtha gamanam pratipattiḥ athavā artha karma iti kim tāvat  prāptam pratipattiḥ  iti kutas  kṛtārtha tvāt kṛtārthāni  etāni dravyāṇi tatra tatra teṣām avabhṛtha gamanam pratipattiḥ  nyāyyā artha karma vā abhidhānena saṃyogāt  tena avabhṛtham yanti iti tena avabhṛtha saṃjñakam niṣpādayanti iti tṛtīyā tena iti dvitīya avabhṛtham iti tasmāt  soma liptam guṇa bhūtam avabhṛthaḥ pradhāna bhūta  iti pratipattiḥ  vā kutas  tad nyāya tvāt  eva eṣa hi nyāyaḥ yad  anyatra kṛtārtham anyatra pratipādyate tad  iha yadi soma liptam dravyam avabhṛthe karaṇam vidhīyate tatas  artha karma atha soma liptena yānam vidhīyate tatas  pratipattiḥ na hi  atra soma liptam vidhīyate avabhṛthe tathā sati  avabhṛtha soma lipta saṃbandhaḥ  abhyavayanti iti  anena ākhyātena vidhīyeta tatra vākyena vidhānam syāt  na tu śrutyā yāne amunā vidhīyamāne śrutyā vidhānam tad  parigṛhītam bhavati śrutiḥ  ca vākyāt  balīyasī tasmāt  pratipattiḥ atha yad  uktam artha karma abhidhānena saṃyogāt  iti tatra brūmaḥ evam sati deśa arthā avabhṛtha śrutiḥ avabhṛtham yanti iti avabhṛthena deśam lakṣayati yasmin deśe avabhṛthaḥ tam deśam yanti iti tasmāt  pratipattiḥ  iti idam śrūyate paśubandhasya yajña kratoḥ ṣaṣ  ṛtvijaḥ darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  yajña kratoḥ  catvāra ṛtvijaḥ cāturmāsyānām yajña kratūnām pañca ṛtvijaḥ agnihotrasya yajña kratoḥ  eka ṛtvij  saumyasya adhvarasya yajña kratoḥ saptadaśa ṛtvijaḥ tathā same darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta prācīna pravaṇe vaiśvadevena yajeta paurṇamāsyām paurṇamāsyā yajeta amāvāsyāyām amāvāsyayā iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim kartṛ deśa kālā vidhīyante uta ānūdyanta iti kim tāvat  prāptam kartṛ deśa kālānām acodanam anuvādaḥ kutas  prayoge nitya samavāyāt  prayoge nitya samavetā eta iti na ṛte kartṛ deśa kālebhyaḥ prayogaḥ sidhyati tena prayoga codanayā eva prāptānām anuvādaḥ nanu viṣama ādi pratiṣedha artham etad  vacanam bhaviṣyati na iti brūmaḥ upadeśakam evaṃjātīyakam vacanam na pratiṣedhakam tasmāt  anuvāda iti ucyate na ca etad  asti  anuvāda iti anuvāda mātram anarthakam yadi vidhiḥ evam apūrvam artham prakariṣyati tasmāt  vidhiḥ  iti nanu prayoga aṅga tvāt prāpta eva iti ucyate niyama arthā śrutiḥ  bhaviṣyati kaḥ  ayam niyamaḥ aniyatasya niyata tā prayoga aṅga tayā sarve deśāḥ prāpnuvanti na tu samuccayena yadā samaḥ an tadā viṣamaḥ yadā viṣamaḥ na tadā samaḥ sa eṣa samaḥ prāpta ś ca aprāpta ś ca yadā na prāptaḥ sa pakṣaḥ  vidhim prayojayati atas  viṣama cikīrṣāyām api samaḥ  vidhīyate tasmāt  viṣamasya aprāptiḥ  vidhau sati bhavati iti samaḥ  vidhīyate evam itareṣu  api tasmāt  vidhiḥ  iti adhikaraṇa pradeśaḥ  ayam idam āmamanti vāyavyam śvetam ālabheta bhūti kāmaḥ tathā somāraudram ghṛte carum nirvapet  chuklānām vrīhīṇām brahmavarcaskāmaḥ tathā nairṛtam carum nirvapet  kṛṣṇānām vrīhīṇām iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim śveta ādi varṇaḥ  vidhīyata uta anūdyate uta anūdyata iti kim prāptam anūdyate dravya śruti gṛhīta tvāt  vidhiḥ  vā pakṣe prāptasya niyama artha iti pakṣa uktam prayojanam ubhayoḥ  api  adhikaraṇayoḥ ayam api  adhikaraṇa apradeśaḥ darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate vrīhīn avahanti taṇḍulān pinaṣṭī iti tad  kim imau vidhī uta anuvādau   iti saṃśaye artha prāpta tvāt  anuvādau   iti prāpte niyama artha tvāt  vidhī iti śeṣa viniyoga uktaḥ kim tad  pradhānam yasya ete śeṣā iti ucyate yajati dadāti juhoti iti  evaṃlakṣaṇam atha kiṃlakṣaṇa kaḥ  yajati juhotiḥ  dadātiḥ  ca iti yajati codanā tāvat  dravya devatā kriyam dravyam devatā ca tasya dravasya kriyā yayā tayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ  bhavati samudāye samuditeṣu  eṣu yajati śabdaḥ  bhavati loke iṣṭaḥ  anena paśupatiḥ  iti tena manyāmahe dravya devatā kriyasya arthasya yajati śabdena pratyāyanam kriyata iti lakṣaṇa karmaṇi prayojanam na vaktavyam jñānam eva atra prayojanam iti atha kiṃlakṣaṇa kaḥ  juhotiḥ  iti tad  ukte yajati  ukte arthe juhotiḥ śrūyate āsecana adhike tasmāt  yajatiḥ  eva āsecana adhikaḥ  juhotiḥ hutam anena iti  evaṃjātīyake vaktāraḥ  bhavanti loke vede api yajati coditam juhotinā anuvadati saṃgrāmiṇam caturhotrā yājayet  catur gṛhītam ājyam kṛtvā catur hotāram vyācakṣīta pūrveṇa graheṇa ardham juhuyāt  uttareṇa ardham iti atha dadātiḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaka iti ātmanaḥ svatva vyāvṛttiḥ parasya sva tvena saṃbandhaḥ yajati dadā ati juhotiṣu sarveṣu utsargaḥ samānaḥ tatra yajatiḥ  devatām uddiśya utsarga mātram juhotiḥ  āsecana adhikaḥ dadāti utsarga pūrvakaḥ para sva tvena saṃbandha iti  eṣa eṣām viśeṣa iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate yad  ātithyāyām barhiḥ tad  upasadām tad  agnīṣomīyasya iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim para dravyasya upadeśaḥ uta niriṣṭikasya athavā dharma vidhi pradeśaḥ athavā dravya sādhāraṇyam iti kim prāptam para dravyasya upadeśaḥ kutas  para dravyasya upadeśa sadṛśaḥ śabdaḥ yad  ātithyāyām tad  upasadām iti yathā yaḥ  devadattasya gauḥ sa viṣṇu mitrasya kartavya iti devadattāt  ācchidya viṣṇu mitrāya dīyata iti atas  para dravyasya updeśa iti na ca etad  asti tathā sati  ātithyāyām tasya vidhānam yad  pūrvam tad  anarthakam syāt  evam tarhi niriṣṭikasya upadeśaḥ tena ātithyāyām yad  vihitam ātithyāyām yad  upāttam iti tathā sati  arthavat  ātithyāyām tad  vacanam niriṣṭikena tu upasadaḥ kartavyā bhavanti na ca eṣa śiṣṭānām ācāraḥ na ca sarve ca udaka prāptā dharmā bhaveyuḥ atas  brūmaḥ vidheḥ karma apavargi tvāt  artha antare vidhi pradeśaḥ syāt  tad  barhiḥ parisamāptāyām ātithyāyām apavṛktam pūrvam tad  ātithyāyāḥ upasat kāle ātithya asaṃbandha s tasya na asti bhūta pūrveṇa ātithyayā karmaṇā lakṣyeta lakṣaṇā śabdaḥ  ca na nyāyyaḥ tasmāt  ātithya ābarhiṣa āñjasya abhāvāt  yad  dharmakam ātithyābarhiḥ tad  dharmakam upasadām agnīṣomīyasya ca iti nyāyyam api vā iti pakṣaḥ  vyāvartate utpatti saṃyoga eva eṣaḥ  asya barhiṣaḥ yadi hi  utpannam ātithyāyām barhis  viśiṣṭam syāt  tasya dharmā aupasade barhiṣy atidiśyeran na tu tad  asti kenacid  vākyena evam prakṛtya barhiṣaḥ  viśeṣaḥ  vakṣyate āśvavālaḥ prastaraḥ vidhṛtī ca aikṣavyāv iti tena na para vihitam barhis  ucyate na niriṣṭikam na kutaścid  dharmā pratidiśyante kim tarhi sādhāraṇam amīṣām barhis  ucyate yad  ātithyāyām vidhīyate tad  eva upasadām agnīṣomīyasya ca vidhīyata iti aviśiṣṭānām barhiṣā saṃyoga ekena sarveṣām yad  ādau barhis  lūyate tal lavanam sarveṣām arthena sādhāraṇaḥ  barhiṣaḥ prayogaḥ evam śrutiḥ śabdasya parigṛhītā bhaviṣyati itarathā dharma lakṣaṇā bhavet  śruti lakṣaṇa aviśaye ca śrutiḥ  nyāyyā na lakṣaṇā tasmāt  trayāṇām sādhāraṇam barhis  iti pakṣa uktam prayojanam yasya khādiraḥ sruvaḥ  bhavati sa chandasām eva rasena avadyati sarasā asya āhutayaḥ bhavanti yasya parṇa mayī juhūr bhavati na sa pāpam ślokam śṛṇoti iti yasya aśvatthy upabhṛt  bhavati brahmaṇā eva asya annam avarundhe yasya vaikaṅkatī dhruvā bhavati praty eva asya āhutayas tiṣṭhanti athaḥ praiva jāyate yasya evaṃrūpāḥ sruvā bhavanti sarvāṇi  eva enam rūpāṇi paśūnām upatiṣṭhante na asya aparūpam ātman jāyata iti tathā jyotiṣṭoma saṃskāre phala śrutiḥ yadā aṅkte cakṣuḥ  eva bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte tathā keśa śmaśrū vapate dataḥ dhāvate nakhāni nikṛntati snāti mṛtā vā eṣā tvac  amedhyam vā asya etad  ātmani śamalam tad  eva upahate medhya eva medham evam upaiti karmaṇi phalam śrūyate abhīṣū vā etau yajñasya yad  ādhārau cakṣuṣī vā etau yajñasya yad  ājya bhāgau yad  prayājā anuyājā ijyante varma vā etad  yajñasya kriyate varma yajamānasya bhārtṛvyasya abhibhūtyai iti atra saṃdehaḥ kim ime phala vidhayaḥ uta artha vādā iti kim prāptam phala vidhayaḥ pravṛtti viśeṣa kara tvāt  phala vidheḥ yathā khādiram vīrya kāmasya yūpam kūryāt  pālāśam brahmavarcaskām asya bailvam annādya kāmasya iti yathā ete phala vidhayaḥ evam iha api draṣṭavyam evam prāpte brūmaḥ phala artha vādā iti kutas  para artha tvāt  kratu arthāni  etāni juhūḥ pradāne guṇa bhūtāḥ upabhṛt  upadhāraṇe sruvā ājya dhāraṇe añjana vapana ādi ca yajamāne āghārau   ājya bhāgau prayāja anuyāja aḥ  ca āgneya ādiṣu yadi phale api guṇa bhāvaḥ syāt  anyatra upadiṣṭānām anyatra punar  guṇa bhāva upadiṣṭa iti pratijñāyeta na ca etad  nyāyyam parārtha tā hi guṇa bhāvaḥ kratu arthā ca eṣām śabdena juhvā juhoti juhvā homam abhinirvartayati iti evam sarvatra tasmāt  na ete puruṣa arthāḥ atha ucyeta puruṣam api prati guṇa bhāva upadiṣṭaḥ yasya parṇa mayī juhūr bhavati na sa pāpam ślokam śṛṇoti iti evamādibhiḥ  vākyaiḥ  iti tad  ca na kasmāt  utpatteḥ  atad pradhāna tvāt  tatra pālāśyā juhvāpa apa śloka śravaṇam kriyata iti na kaścid  chabda āha etāvat  chrūyate yasya asau bhavati na sa pāpam ślokam śṛṇoti iti etāvat  atra śabdena gamyate yasya evaṃlakṣaṇā juhūḥ tasya apāpa śloka śravaṇam iti tatra juhvā tad  kriyate juhūr vā tad artha iti na etad  chabda āha nanu  anumānāt  etad  gamyate dhruvam pālāśyā juhvā tad  kriyate yatas  tasyām satyām tad  bhavati iti atra ucyate na evaṃjātīyakam kārya kāraṇa tve anumānam bhavati kārya kāraṇa saṃbandhaḥ  nāma sa bhavati yasmin sati yad  bhavati yasmin   ca asati yad  na bhavati tatra eva kārya kāraṇa saṃbandhaḥ iha tu tad bhāve bhāvaḥ jñātaḥ na abhāve abhāvaḥ yasya pālāśī na bhavati tasya apāpa śloka śravaṇam na asti iti na evaṃjātīyakaḥ śabdaḥ  asti tena na niyogataḥ  avagamyate tena idam kriyata iti lakṣaṇam etad  puruṣasya gamyate tasmāt  na anumānam api ca yasya api juhūḥ pālāśī bhavati tasya api pāpa śloka śravaṇam bhavati katham avagamyate pratyakṣataḥ nanu  evam sati  agnihotreṇa api phalam na sādhyeta na hutā mātreṇa phalam dṛśyata iti na eṣa doṣaḥ na hi tatra ucyate tāvatā eva phalam bhavati iti iha tu vartamānāyām juhūsattāyām vartamānasya pāpa śloka śravaṇasya pratiṣedhaḥ tasmāt  na tatra anumānam idam kāryam idam kāraṇam iti agnihotra ādiṣu tu śabdena eva kārya kāraṇa saṃbandha ucyate tasmāt  tatra tad kāle adṛśyamāne api phale kāla antare phalam bhaviṣyati iti gamyate na tu  evaṃjātīyakeṣu tasmāt  na evaṃjātīyakebhyaḥ phalam asti iti nanu yasya pālāśī juhūr bhavati na sa pāpam ślokam śṛṇoti iti  evam ukte tad  eva tad  phalam bhavati iti gamyate tasmāt  iha api kāla antare phalam bhaviṣyati iti ucyate satyam gamyate pramāṇam tatra kim iti vicārayāmaḥ na tāvat  pratyakṣam na anumānam na itarad dṛṣṭa viṣayam upamāna ādi naḥ khalu  api śabda iti  etad  uktam vākya arthaḥ  api padārtha upajanitaḥ  bhavati na anyathā tad  uktam tad bhūtānām kriyā arthena samāmnāya iti tasmāt  apramāṇa mūla tvāt  mithyā vijñānam etad  laukikeṣu tu vākyeṣu  atha evam gamyate tāni hi vijñāte arthe prayujyamānāni  adhyāhārya padāni gauṇāni vipariṇata vyavahita arthāni ca prayujyante tasmāt  tad sādṛśyāt  vacanau  agamyeṣu  api  artheṣu bhavati tattva rūpaḥ  mithyā pratyayaḥ yathā mṛgatṛṣṇā ādiṣu api ca vartamāna apadeśaḥ  ayam na ca ayam arthaḥ  vartamānaḥ tasmāt  na khādira sruva ādi sadbhāve tad phalam bhavet  tad  evam āpatati khādira ādau sati bhavati tad phalam na api bhavati asati  api bhavati vā na vā iti na evam vijñāyate kutas  tad phalam iti tasmāt  evaṃjātīyakeṣu uccariteṣu na kvacid  pravṛttiḥ  na kutaścin nivṛttiḥ  iti  ānarthakyam akriyā artha tvāt artha vāde tu sati bhavati prayojanam khadira ādeḥ sruva ādiṣu karma artheṣu prayojanavatsu yadi  eṣām kratum prati prayojanavat tā na syāt  tatas  etad  eva phalam kasyācid  chabda vṛttyā bhavet  vā na vā iti vicāryeta sati tu pārārthye na eva kācid  chabda pravṛttiḥ  āśrayitum śakyate kaimarthye hi sā kalpyeta tasmāt  evaṃjātīyakā artha vādāḥ artha vāda tve ca āvartamāne lakṣaṇayā vartamāna śabdaḥ praśaṃsā artha upapatsyate atha yad  uktam yathā khādiram vīrya kāmasya yūpam kuryāt  bailvam annādya kāmasya pālāśam brahmavarcasa kāmasya iti yuktam teṣu vidhi vibhaktiḥ kuryāt  iti vīrya khādira saṃbandhasya vidhātrī na ca vartamāna apadeśinī tasmāt  tatra avirodha iti evam hi pada vākya artha nyāya vidaḥ ślokam āmananti kuryāt  kriyeta kartavyam bhavet  syāt  iti pañcamam etad  syāt  sarva vedeṣu niyatam vidhi lakṣaṇam iti vidhi vibhaktim hi vidhāyikām liṅgam manyamānāḥ ślokam imam samāmananti asti ca atra vidhi vibhaktiḥ tasmāt  anupavarṇanam etad  iti asti jyotiṣṭome naimittikam bārhadgiram brāhmaṇasya brahmasāma kuryāt  pārthuḥ  aśmām rājanyasya rāyā uvājīyam vaiśyasya iti tathā agnau naimittikam sāhasram prathamam cinvānaḥ  cinvīta dvi sāhasram dvitīyam tri sāhasram tṛtīyam iti tathā darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate gaḥ dohanena paśu kāmasya praṇayet  kāṃsyena brahmavarcasa kāmasya mārtikena pratiṣṭhākāmasya iti  etāni naimittikāni teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim etāni  eva naimittikāni nitya arthe uta anyat  tatra tatra nitya artha iti kim prāptam etāni  eva iti kutas  atra brahma sāma ādibhiḥ  avaśyam bhavitavyam coditāni hi tāni saṃnihitāni sādhanāni  ākāṅkṣanti na ca eṣām santi vihitāni sādhanāni samīpatas  ca naimittikāni  upanipatanti taiḥ prakṛtaiḥ saṃnihitaiḥ  etāni nirākāṅkṣīkriyanta iti  etad  nyāyyam katham naimittikam hi saṃnihitam vākyāt  avagamyate na anya t  chrūyate yāvānś ca śrutasya utsarge doṣaḥ tāvān eva aśruta kalpanāyām āha nanu nimitta arthāni tāni prakṛtāni ucyate na eṣa doṣaḥ anya artham api prakṛtam anyena saṃbadhyate yathā śāli artham kulyāḥ praṇīyante tābhyaś ca pānīyam pīyate upaspṛśyate ca evam iha api draṣṭavyam athavā asti  eva atra avāntara vākyam yathā gaḥ dohanena praṇayet  iti tad  akāma saṃbaddham gaḥ dohanena praṇayanam prāpayati na ca śakyam śrutam utsraṣṭum yaḥ  api  ayam paśu kāmasya iti śabdaḥ sa paśu kāma saṃbandham śaknuyāt  kartum nāva antara vākyasya artham nivārayitum na ca gamyamānam vinā kāraṇena avivakṣitam iti śakyam vaditum bhavanti ca dviṣṭhāni vākyāni yathā śvetaḥ  dhāvati alambusānām yātā iti tasmāt  naimittikāni  eva nitya arthe bhavitum arhanti iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ naimittike śrūyamāṇe kratu artham anyat  syāt  iti kutas  vikāra tvāt  viśeṣe śruta tvāt  iti  arthaḥ viśeṣe hi tatra naimittikam śrūyate tad  asati tasmin viśeṣe na bhavitum arhati yad  uktam avaśya kartavyāni iti na eṣa doṣaḥ avaśyam kartavya tvāt  kariṣyante yad  tu na anyat  eṣām vihitam sādhanam iti sāmānya vihitam bhaviṣyati iti na doṣaḥ kim tad  abhīvartaḥ  brahmasāma aṣṭādaśa mantra gataḥ  agniḥ vāraṇam praṇayana pātram atha yad  uktam saṃnihitaiḥ prakṛtaiḥ  naimittikaiḥ  brahma sāma ādīni saṃbhatsyanta iti na iti brūmaḥ na hi bārhadgira ādīnām prakaraṇam atha ucyeta prakṛtaiḥ stotra ādibhiḥ saṃbadhyanta iti etad  api na upapadyate yadi  api prakṛtāni nityāni stotra ādīni tathā api vākyena nimitta saṃyoge śrūyante bārhadgira ādīni vākyam ca prakaraṇāt  balīyaḥ yad  uktam saṃnidhānāt  vākyāt  avagataḥ  ayam artha iti na evaṃjātīyakaḥ  vākya arthaḥ sāmānyam padārtham bādhitum arhati nimitta saṃyoge hi bārhadgira ādīnām arthavat tā tasmāt  tatra tatra anyan naimittikāt  iti atha yad  uktam avāntara vākyena gaḥ dohanam api prāpitam na śakyam utsraṣṭum ṛte kāraṇāt  avivakṣitam kalpayitum dviṣṭham hi tad  bhavati iti ucyate kāraṇāt  avivakṣitam kim kāraṇam na hi idam yugapad  bhavati paripūrṇena ca artha abhidhānam avāntara vākyena ca iti katham praṇayati iti prapūrve nayatau vidhi vibhaktiḥ sva pada gatam artham śrutyā vidadhāti praṇayana ādi saṃbaddham api gaḥ dohana ādi śrutyā vākyena ca vastu phalasya gaḥ dohana ādeḥ  ca saṃbandhaḥ sa hitvā śruti artham kevalena vākyena atha praṇayanasya gaḥ dohana ādi saṃbandham gaḥ dohana ādeḥ  ca phalena saṃbandham vadati iti  ucyate na dvi artha abhidhānāt  bhidyeta nitarām vākyam na ca etad  nyāyyam yad  tu śvetaḥ  dhāvati iti evamādi bhavet  tatra viśeṣān avagamāt  ubhaya artha avagatiḥ iha tu gamyate viśeṣaḥ kamipadā uccāraṇam sa iha śrautaḥ  arthaḥ manyeta yadi gaḥ dohana ādeḥ kriyā saṃbandhaḥ  vivakṣyate kamipadam pramādaḥ  bhavet  na ca ayam pramādaḥ na eva avāntara vākya arthe vivakṣite kamipada saṃbandhaḥ  avakalpate tasmāt  na dviṣṭham vākyam gaḥ dohana ādi kami saṃbandha eva atra abhidhīyate na nitya kārye bhavitum arhati iti evam sarvatra agnihotre śrūyate dadhnā juhoti iti punar  ca dadhna indriya kāmasya juhuyāt  iti tathā agnīṣomīye paśauv āmnāyate khādire badhnāti iti punar  ca khādiram vīrya kāmasya yūpam kuryāt  iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim atra api  anyan nitya artham uta naimittikam eva iti kim prāptam pūrveṇa nyāyena anyat  iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ekasya ubhaya tve nitya tve naimittika tve ca saṃyoga pṛthak tvam kāraṇam tad  iha saṃyoga pṛthaktvam asti ekaḥ saṃyogaḥ  dadhnā juhoti iti ekaḥ  dadhnā indriya kāmasya iti tathā ekaḥ khādire badhnāti iti aparaḥ khādiram vīrya kāmasya iti tasmāt  nitya arthe kāmāya ca dadhikhādiḥ ādi iti iti ced  paśyasi kasmān na pūrvasya ayam api śeṣaḥ  bhavati yad  etad  uktam dadhnā juhoti khādire badhnāti iti tasya eva tu dadhnaḥ phalam indriyam tathā khādirasya vīryam tad  ca idam ca ekam vākyam iti na etad  evam pṛthak  etau   arthau yaḥ  ca dadhi homa saṃyogaḥ yaḥ  ca dadhi indriya saṃyogaḥ tathā khādirasya badhnātinā saṃyogaḥ  vīryeṇa ca dvau   etau   arthau dvau   api ca vidhitsitau artha eka tvāt  ca ekam vākyam samadhigatam iha artha dvayena bhidyeta vākyam katham juhoti samabhi vyāhṛtā vidhi vibhaktiḥ asaṃbhave śrautasya homa vidhānasya guṇam samabhivyāhṛtam vidhātum arhati tad  asaṃbhave guṇa phala saṃbandham tatra hi  atyantāya śrutiḥ  utsṛṣṭā vākya anurodhena syāt  na ca yugapad  saṃbhava asaṃbhavau saṃbhavataḥ tasmāt  yad  eva naimittikam tad  eva nitya artham iti jyotiṣṭome samāmananti payaḥ vratam brāhmaṇasya yavāgū rājanyasya āmikṣā vaiśyasya iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ayam puruṣa dharmaḥ uta kratoḥ  iti prakaraṇam bādhitvā vākyena viniyuktaḥ puruṣasya iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ puruṣāṇām kriyā arthānām śarīra dhāraṇa arthaḥ  bala karaṇa arthaḥ  ca ayam saṃskāraḥ  vratam nāma sa kratu dharmaḥ  bhavitum arhati prakaraṇa anugrahāya nanu vākyāt  puruṣa dharma iti na iti brūmaḥ tathā sati phalam kalpyam kḷptam itaratra prayoga vacanena upasaṃhṛtam hi tad pradhānasya tasmāt  kratu dharmaḥ atha puruṣa saṃyogaḥ kim arthaḥ vyavasthāpana artha iti brūmaḥ payaḥ vratam jyotiṣṭomasya bhavati tad  tu brāhmaṇa kartṛkasya eva na anya kartṛkasya iti evam sarvatra idam āmananti tasmāt  pitṛbhyaḥ pūrvedyus  karoti iti tathā sarvebhyaḥ  vā eṣa devebhyaḥ sarvebhyaś chandobhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pṛṣṭhebhyaḥ  ātmānam āgurate yaḥ satrāya agurate sa viśvajitā atirātreṇa sarva pṛṣṭhena sarva stomena sarva vedasa dakṣiṇena yajeta iti  evaṃlakṣaṇake śrute bhavati saṃdehaḥ kim niṣphalam etad  karma mātram uta saphalam iti kim prāptam niṣphalam iti kutas  phala aśruteḥ śabda pramāṇake karmaṇi  evaṃjātīyake na hi  aśabdam pratīyate nanu vaidikāni karmāṇi phalavanti bhavanti iti  evam uktam ucyate phala darśanāt  tāni phalavanti iti  uktam na vaidika tvāt  evam tarhi kartavyatā avagamāt phalavanti iti  adhyavasyāmaḥ sukha phalam hi kartavyam bhavati iti ucyate pratyakṣa viruddham evaṃjātiyakasya kartavya tvam sākṣāt  dhi tad  duḥkha phalam agacchāmaḥ na ca evaṃjātīyakam pratyakṣa viruddham vacanam pramāṇam bhavati yathā ambuni majjanti  alābūni śilāḥ plavante pāvakaḥ śīta iti api ca anumānāt  atra sukha phala tā yasmāt  kartavyam atas  sukha phalam iti pratyakṣam ca anumānāt  balīyaḥ tasmāt  niṣphalam evaṃjātīyakam iti evam hi  atra phalam kalpyeta yadi  etad  phalavat  evam upadeśaḥ  arthavān bhavati iti ucyate kāmam vākyam anarthakam iti nyāyyam vacanam bhavet  bhavanti hi  anarthakāni  api vacanāni daśa dāḍimāni ṣaṣ apūyā iti  evaṃjātīyakāni nanu viśva jit vyāpāraḥ sukha phala iti uttaram sukha phalam hi bhavati  apūrvam na vyāpāraḥ na ca ayam apūrvasya kartavyatām āha phala kartavyatāyām hi satyām tad  avagamyate vākya arthaś ca phalasya kartavyatām āha na padārthaḥ na ca atra phala saṃbaddham vākyam asti tasmāt  na ayam apūrvasya vidhāyakaḥ śabdaḥ vyāpāra mātram eva vidadhāti sa ca vyāpāraḥ  na tadātve sukhaphalaḥ na api  āyatyām bhaṅgi tvāt  tatra apūrvam kalpayitvā phalam avagamyeta phalam ca kalpayitvā apūrvam evam itaretara āśrayam bhavati itaretara āśrayāṇi ca na prakalpante tasmāt  niṣphalam evaṃjātīyakam iti āha adhyāhariṣyāmahe phala vacanam ucyate na śakyam paripūrṇe vākye adhyāhartum paripūrṇam hi idam vākyam viśvajit yāgaḥ kartavya iti na kiṃcid  padam asti sa ākāṅkṣam yena adhyāhṛtya phalam saṃbadhyeta yathākṣeme api pathi bhavati vipralambha ka upa deśaḥ kṣemaḥ  ayam yathā gacchatu bhavān anena iti paripūrṇam eva idam vākyam na adhyāhāram arhati vipralambhaka kartṛkam evam idam api paripūrṇam vākyam na adhyāhāram arhati api ca adhyāhriyamāṇena eva idam vākyam saṃbadhyeta viśvajit yāgaḥ kartavyaḥ idam ca phalam bhavati iti dvau   imau   arthau eka artham ca vākyam samadhigatam tasmāt  anarthakam evaṃjātīyakam karma iti api vā iti pakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ na ca etad  asti aphalam iti phala codanā arthena gamyeta katamena arthena kartavyatā vacanena āha nanu vyāpārasya pratyakṣa viruddhā kartavyatā na vyāpārasya ucyate kasya tarhi vyāpāreṇa anyasya kasyacid  iti bhavati tena idānīm vākyam sa ākāṅkṣam tatra adhyāhāraḥ  avakalpate bhavati ca adhyāhāreṇa api kalpanā yathā dvāram dvāram iti  ukte saṃvriyatām apāvriyatām iti katham punar  avagamyate iha adhyāhāreṇa kalpayitavyam iti āmnāna sāmarthyāt  evam idam āmnānam arthavat  bhaviṣyati śaknoti ca artham avagamayitum tasmāt  na anarthakam nanu yad  padam adhyāhriyate tad  pauruṣeyam tena avagatam ca apramāṇam ucyate na apūrvam adhyāhariṣyāmaḥ vaidikena eva asya saha anyatra samāmnātena eka vākyatām adhyavasāmaḥ āha na evam śakyam antikāt  upanipatitam hi padam vākya artham upajanayitum alam bhavati na dūrāt  avatiṣṭhamānam atra ucyate vyavahitam api hi parāṇudya vyavadhāyakam ānantaryeṇa manasi viparivartamānam alam eva bhavati viśeṣam upajanayitum yathā itas  paśyasi dhāvantam dūre jātam vanaspatim tvām bravīmi viśāla akṣi yā pinakṣi jarad gavam iti itas  paśyasi iti śabdaḥ  buddhau bhavati saḥ dūre jātam vanaspatim etaiḥ padaiḥ  vyavahitena jarad gavam iti  anena śabdena vyavadhāyakāni  apodya saṃbadhyamānaḥ saṃbadhyate arthānām hi  arthavat tvena hetunā vyavahitāni  api vacanāni saṃbadhyante yāni punar  arthataḥ  hi  asamarthāni tāni  ānantarye api sati na paraspareṇa saṃbandham arhanti yathā yā pinakṣi jarad gavam iti evamādīni tasmāt  na pauruṣeya tā bhaviṣyati āha nanu  atra api  apekṣā pauruṣeyī ucyate na apekṣā vede veda artha pratipattau   abhyupāya eṣa bhavati ananatara apekṣāyām asaṃbhavantyām āmnāna sāmarthyāt  itara apekṣā vṛttiḥ  āśrīyate tasmāt  chruty eka deśaḥ saḥ phala kāma padam dūre api sat  tasya vākyasya eka deśa bhūtam iti  arthaḥ indrāya rājñe śūkara iti yathā vākya antara sthena vidhi śabdena guṇa vidhānam bhavati evam phala vidhānam api bhavitum arhati iti yathā varuṇaḥ  vaitam agre pratyagṛhṇāt  iti vyavadhāraṇa kalpanā evam idam api draṣṭavyam tasmāt  pitṛbhyaḥ pūrvedyus  karoti iti viśvajitā yajeta iti phalavat  evaṃvidham karma iti  etad  samadhigatam idam tu saṃdihyate kim sarva phalam etad  karma uta eka phalam iti kim prāptam tad  sarva artham iti kutas  anādeśāt  na kiṃcid  iha atidiśyate idam nāma phalam iti asti ced  vijñāyeta tasmāt  sarva artham aviśeṣāt  ekam phalam syāt  na vā sarva artham kutas  codana eka tvāt  sa kāṅkṣa tvāt  etad  arthi padena saṃbadhyata iti  uktam yad  ca anekena api saṃbaddhum śaknoti tad  ekena saṃbadhyate ekena saṃbaddham san nirākāṅkṣam bhavati na tad  apareṇa api saṃbandham arhati tasmāt  ekā eva kartavyatā codanā nyāyyā tasmāt  ekaphala tā iti evaṃjātīyakeṣu  eva udāhāraṇeṣu  etad  samadhigatam ekam phalam iti idam idānīm saṃdihyate kim yad kiṃcid  uta svarga iti yad kiṃcid  iti prāptam viśeṣān abhidhānāt tatas  ucyate sa svargaḥ syāt  sarvān pratyaviśiṣṭa tvāt  sarve hi puruṣāḥ svarga kāmāḥ kuta etad  prītiḥ  hi svargaḥ sarvaś ca prītim prārthayate kim atas  yadi  evam aviśeṣa vacanaḥ śabdaḥ  na viśeṣe vyavasthāpitaḥ  bhaviṣyati yajeta kuryāt  iti tasmāt  svarga phalam evaṃjātīyakam iti bhavati ca anādiṣṭa phale karmaṇi svargaḥ phalam iti pratyayaḥ loke evam ucyate ārāma kṛt  devadattaḥ niyataḥ  asya svargaḥ taḍāga kṛt  devadattaḥ niyataḥ  asya svarga iti kim atas  yadi  evam ittham anena nyāyena svarge saṃpratyayaḥ  bhavati yasmāt  svarga phaleṣu karmasu kartavyeṣu phala vacanam na eva uccārayanti gamyata eva iti tasmāt  api  avagacchāmaḥ evaṃjātīyakeṣu svargaḥ phalam iti rātrīḥ prakṛtya śrūyate pratitiṣṭhanti ha vaite ya etā upayanti brahma varcasvinaḥ  anna ādā bhavanti ya etā upayanti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim te phala artha vādāḥ uta phala vidhaya iti kim prāptam phala artha vādā iti kārṣāji niḥ  mene kutas  phala artha vāda sarūpā ete śabdā iti kim sārūpyam vidhi vibhakteḥ  abhāvaḥ aṅgavat  yathā yasya khādiraḥ sruvaḥ  bhavati sa chandasām eva rasena avadyati iti evamādiṣu ātreyaḥ punar  ācārya evaṃjātīyakebhyaḥ phalam asti iti mene na phala arthavāda iti kutas  aśruta phala tve api  amīṣām phala codanayā vākya śeṣa bhūtayā bhavitavyam tasmāt  anyā vyavahitā satī avyavahitā kalpanīyā iyam tu  avyavahitā kḷptā eva pratiṣṭhayā brahmavarcasa sattayā ca samabhivyāhāra āsām pratyakṣaḥ vidhi vibhakti mātram anyatas  apekṣyam āha katham kevalam vidhi vibhakti mātram anyatas  bhaviṣyati yad  anena pratiṣṭhā ādinā dhātu arthena saṃbhantsyata iti ucyate saha dhātu arthena bhaviṣyati na kevalam tasmāt  adoṣaḥ athavā rātrīṇām yā vidhāyikā vibhaktiḥ sā imam api pratiṣṭhā ādi viśeṣam vidhāsyati prayoga vacanena stutiḥ  vā saha pratiṣṭhā ādibhiḥ  vidhātrī bhaviṣyati iti atha yad  uktam yathā yasya khādiraḥ sruvaḥ  bhavati iti evamādiṣu phala śrutiḥ  artha vādaḥ  bhavati evam iha api syāt  iti yuktam tatra phala artha vādaḥ phala vidhi asaṃbhavāt  phala arthavāda saṃbavāt  ca tad  uktam dravya saṃskāra karmasu para artha tvāt  phala śrutiḥ  artha vādaḥ syāt  iti kāmyāni karmāṇi  udāharaṇam sauryam carum nirvapet  brahmavarcasa kāma iti evamādīni iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim eṣām svargaḥ phalam kāmaḥ  ca uta kāma eva iti kim prāptam kāmye karmaṇi nityaḥ svargaḥ syāt  katham sarva puruṣa artha abhidhāyī sāmānya vacanaḥ śabdaḥ  na viśeṣe avasthāpitaḥ  bhavati śakyate hi  asya dūra sthena api svarga kāma śabdena saṃbandhaḥ āha nanu viśeṣakaḥ śabdaḥ śrūyate brahmavarcasa kāma iti na eṣa viśeṣakaḥ upādhikara eṣaḥ yathā kāṣṭhāni  āhartum prasthita ucyate bhavatā śākam api  āhartavyam iti kāṣṭhā haraṇe śāka āharaṇam upādhiḥ kriyata iti kim idam upādhiḥ kriyata iti kāṣṭhā haraṇa adhikāra samīpe dvitīyam karma upadhīyate sati kāṣṭhā haraṇe idam aparam kartavyam iti evam iha api svarga phale phalam aparam upadhīyate brahmavarcasa kāmaḥ  yāgena svargam abhinirvartayet  iti na hi tatra brahmavarcasa phala vacanam svarga phalasya pratiṣedhakam yathā yajña aṅge kratu arthaḥ gaḥ dohanena paśu kāmasya praṇayet  iti yaḥ paśu kāmaḥ sa gaḥ dohanena praṇayanam abhinirvartayet  iti vīte ca kāraṇe vītāyām phala icchāyām avāpte vā phale samāpti niyamaḥ  dṛśyate vṛṣṭikāma iṣṭyām yadi varṣet  tāvatī  eva juhuyāt  yadi na varṣet  śvobhūte juhuyāt  iti yadi na svargaḥ kim arthaḥ samāpti niyamaḥ  bhavet  tasmāt  nityaḥ svarga iti kāmaḥ  vā phalam bhavet  na svargaḥ tad saṃyogena asya codanā bhavati na svarga kāma saṃyogena ānumānikaḥ  asya svarga kāmena eka vākya bhāvaḥ pratyakṣas tu kāma vacanena pratyakṣam ca anumānāt  balīyaḥ tasmāt  kāma eva phalam iti atha yad  uktam yathā yajña aṅga iti yuktam aṅge guṇa tvāt  pratyakṣas tatra ṛtunā saṃyogaḥ kāmena ca yaḥ paśu kāmaḥ syāt  sa gaḥ dohanena praṇayanam abhinirvartayet  iti na tu  atra pratyakṣaḥ śabdaḥ  asti yaḥ  brahmavarcasa kāmaḥ syāt  sa yāgena svargam abhinirvartayet  iti katham tarhi yaḥ  brahmavarcasa kāmaḥ syāt  sa tad  yāgena nirvartayet  iti tasmāt  na aṅgavat  bhavitum arhati iti atha yad  uktam vītāyām phala icchāyām avāpte vā phale samāpti niyamaḥ  dṛśyata iti tatra brūmaḥ vīte niyamas tad artham vīte niyamaḥ  bhavati tasmai prayojanāya kasmai śiṣṭā vigarhaṇāya upakramya aparisamāpayataḥ tad anantaram eva enam śiṣṭā vigarhayeyaḥ prākramikaḥ  ayam kāpuruṣa iti vadantaḥ ye hi devebhyaḥ saṃkalpya haviḥ na yāgam abhinirvartayanti tān śiṣṭā vigarhante tasmāt  avaśyam samāpayitavyam tatra etad  darśanam yuktam bhaviṣyati yadi varṣet  tāvatī  eva juhuyāt  iti tasmāt  kāmyānām kāma eva phalam iti idam āmnāyate ekasmai vā anyā iṣṭayaḥ kāmāya ahriyante sarvebhyaḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau ekasmai vā anye kratavaḥ kāmāya ahriyante sarvebhyaḥ  jyotiṣṭoma iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim aṅga kāmaiḥ  aṅga aṅga kāma aiḥ  ca saha asya anuvādaḥ athavā vidhiḥ  iti kim prāptam anuvāda iti yad  etad  sārvakāmyam tad  anūdyate aṅga kāma aiḥ  ca aṅga aṅga kāma aiḥ  ca saha santi hi  aṅgakāmāś ca aṅga aṅgakāmāś ca yathā āhārya purīṣām paśu kāmasya vedim kuryāt  khanana purīṣām pratiṣṭhākām asya iti evamādayaḥ tathā yadi kāmayeta varṣet  parjanya iti nīcais  sadaḥ  minuyāt  iti tad  vihitam eva idam abhidhīyata iti  anuvādam nyāyyam manyāmahe phala vidhiḥ  vā kutas  pradhāna śabdena phala saṃyogaḥ  bhavati sarvebhyaḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau sarvebhyaḥ  jyotiṣṭoma iti ca pradhāna abhidhānena ca pradhānasya sarva phalavat tā vihitā tasmāt  na anuvādaḥ atha aṅga kāmān aṅga aṅga kāmān   ca apekṣate tathā lakṣaṇā śabdaḥ syāt  śrutiḥ  ca lakṣaṇāyāḥ  garīyasī tasmāt  prayoga vacanena vidhiḥ  iti evaṃjātīyakeṣu  eva udāharaṇeṣu  etad  uktam pradhāne sarva kāmānām vidhiḥ  iti idam idānīm saṃdihyate kim sakṛt  prayoge sarve kāmāḥ uta paryāyeṇa iti kim prāptam sakṛt  prayoge sarve kāmā iti katham sarveṣām kāmānām darśa pūrṇamāsau nimittam jyotiṣṭoma ś ca iti nimittam ced  sarveṣām kāmānām kaḥ  atra khalu kāmaḥ  na bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt  yaugapadyena sarve kāmā iti na ca etad  asti sarve yugapad  kāmā iti paryāyaḥ  yoga siddhiḥ paryāyeṇa bhaveyuḥ kāmā iti kutas  arthasya utpatti asaṃyogi tvāt  arthā ime kāmā nāma na sarva eva yugapad  utpadyante asaṃbhavaḥ  yugapad  utpatteḥ sarveṣām virodhāt  athavā utpatti asaṃyogi tvāt  iti na kāmānām etad  utpatti vacanam utpannānām lakṣaṇa tvena vacanam ye sarve kāmāḥ  tebhyaḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau jyotiṣṭoma ś ca iti na sarve kāmāḥ karmaṇaḥ śrūvante ye sarve kāmāḥ  tebhyaḥ  hi karma vidhīyate tasmāt  na kāmānām sāhityam gamyata iti kāmyāni karmāṇi  udāharaṇam sauryam carum nirvapet  brahmavarcasa kāmaḥ aindrāgnam ekādaśa kapālam nirvapet  prajā kāmaḥ citrayā yajeta pasūkāmaḥ vaiśvadevīm sāṃgrahāyaṇīm nirvapet  grāma kāma  iti teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim iha loke kāmāḥ uta amuṣmil loka iti kim prāptam tatra amuṣmil loke kāmāḥ aviśeṣāt  yathā svargaḥ evam ime api na hi  anantara nirvṛtte karmaṇi phalam upalabhyate paśu ādi yad  ca anantaram upalabhyate tad  tatas  iti vijñāyate yathā yad kālam mardanam tad kālam mardana sukham yad  ca kāla antara upalabhyate tasya api  anyat  eva kāraṇam asti pratyakṣam śarīra grahaṇasya tu na adṛṣṭāt ṛte kiṃcid  kāraṇam asti tasmāt  viśiṣṭa indriya śarīra ādi phalam paśu saṃbandha samartham paśu phalāt  karmaṇaḥ  bhavati iti  evam boddhavyam tad  dhi darśayati kaikayaḥ  yajñam vivitsan dālbhyam uvāca anayā mā rāṣṭra pratipādanīyayā iṣṭyā yājaya iti saḥ  abravīt  na vai saumya rāṣṭra pratipādanīyām vettha amuṣmai kāmāya yajñā āhriyanta iti janma antara phala tām darśayati tasmāt  janma antara phalāni kāmyāni iti iha eva eṣām siddhiḥ  yogasya utpattyā yogaḥ  na saṃbhavati yaḥ paśubhyaḥ kāmayate sa etena yāgena kuryāt  iti na atra etad  gamyate iha janmani na saṃbhavati iti yad  ca anantaram na upalabhyata iti tad  na pratyakṣa anumānābhyām na gamyate śabdena tu  asti gatiḥ yad  tu kāla antare anyat  kāraṇam iti na eṣa doṣaḥ anyat  api bhaviṣyati etad  api yad  ca amuṣmai kāmāya yajñā āhriyanta iti atra ucyate evam asya ṛṣeḥ  matam iha yasya phalam tena tvām na yājayāmi yasya amutra phalam tena ca yājayiṣyāmi iti tasmāt  etad  parihṛtam iti agnim citvā sautrāmaṇyā yajeta vājapeyena iṣṭvā bṛhaspati savena yajeta iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim aṅga prayojana saṃbandha eṣaḥ uta kāla arthaḥ saṃyoga iti aṅga prayojana saṃbandha iti brūmaḥ evam hi śruti viniyuktaḥ  arthaḥ itarathā kālaḥ  lakṣyeta śruti lakṣaṇa aviśaye ca śrutiḥ  nyāyyā na lakṣaṇā tasmāt  agni aṅgam sautrāmaṇī vājapeya aṅgam bṛhaspati sava iti evam ced  paśyasi aṅga prayojana saṃbandha iti atha kāla vidhānam kasmān na bhavati kāla vidhi rūpaḥ  hi śabdaḥ citvā cayane abhinirvṛtta iti na etad  evam asamavāyāt  śabda prayojanena śabda arthena iti  arthaḥ ekaḥ śabdaḥ anunirvapati iti ekasmin   eva vākye na dvau saṃbandhau śaknoti vidhātum vaimṛdhasya darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām pūrṇamāsī kālena ca eka artha tvāt  dhy ekam vākyam samadhigatam prakaraṇāt  iti yad  uktam tad  parihartavyam na etad  evam etad  eva vaimṛdhasya utpatti vākyam tad  darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām vā prakaraṇāt  eka vākya bhāvam iyāt  pratyakṣam vā paurṇamāsyā tatra pratyakṣa saṃyogaḥ prakaraṇāt  balavān pratyakṣaḥ  ca paurṇamāsyā saṃyogaḥ parokṣaḥ kālena tasmāt  paurṇamāsya aṅgam vaimṛdha iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate āgni mārutāt  ūrdhvam anuyājaiḥ  caranti prahṛtya paridhīñ juhoti hāri yojanam iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim aṅgam vidhīyate uta kāla iti aṅga vidhāne śrutiḥ kāla vidhāne lakṣaṇā tasmāt  aṅga vidhānam iti prāpte brūmaḥ anutpatti vākye kālaḥ syāt  āgni mārutam soma aṅgam anuyājāḥ paśu aṅgam tatra na tayoḥ paraspareṇa saṃbandhaḥ tathā paridhayaḥ paśu aṅgam hāri yojanam anyat  eva pradhānam anuyājā āgni mārutam ca prāptam ānantaryam eva tayoḥ  na prāptam tad  vidhīyate tathā hāri yojanasya paridhi grahaṇasya ca evam ca sati na hāri yojanasya paridhi praharaṇena kaścid  upakāraḥ kriyate hāri yojanena vā paridhi praharaṇasya nanu paridhi praharaṇasya upariṣṭāt  bhāvena tasya upakriyeta iti ucyate na hi  upari bhāva artham paridhi praharaṇam anuṣṭheyam vidyata eva etad  paśu artham tasmin   ca sati tasya upari bhāvaḥ  vidyata eva iti tasmāt  kāla arthaḥ saṃbandha iti idam āmnāyate darśa pūrṇamāsau iṣṭvā somena yajeta iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim etad  aṅgasya vidhānam uta kālasya iti kim prāptam śruteḥ  aṅgasya iti prāpte ucyate asmin kāla aṅga vidhāna saṃśaye kālaḥ syāt  vākyasya tad pradhāna tvāt  kāla pradhānam hi  etad  vākyam na yāga vidhāna param atatpara tāsya rūpāvacanāt  katham rūpāvacanam devatā bhāvāt katham abhāvaḥ aśruta tvāt  yā hi yasya śrūyate sā tasya devatā bhavati śrutyā hi devatā gamyate na pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ tasmāt  na apūrvasya yāgasya vidhānam kāla arthe anuvāde na ayam doṣaḥ vihita devatā kaḥ  hi  anūdyate tasmāt  atra kāla arthaḥ saṃbandha iti tad  ca darśayati eṣa vai deva rathaḥ  yad  darśa pūrṇamān sau yad  darśa pūrṇamāsau   iṣṭvā somena yajate ratha spaṣṭa eva avasāne vare devānām avasyati iti pradarśite mārge rathena yātum sukham bhavati evam darśa pūrṇamāsau   iṣṭvā somena yaṣṭum sukham bhavati darśa pūrṇamāsa prakṛtīni tasya dīkṣaṇīya ādīni su abhyas tāni bhavanti evam artha vādaḥ  arthavān bhavati vaiśvānaram dvādaśa kapālam nirvapet  putre jāta iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ātma niḥśreyasāya uta putra niḥśreyasāya iti ātma niḥśreyasāya iti brūmaḥ na imāni phala dāni parasya bhavanti karmāṇi kutas  ādhāna ātmanepada nirdeśāt yathā yadi  ekam kapālam naśyet  ekaḥ  māsaḥ saṃvatsarasya apetaḥ syāt  atha yajamānaḥ pramīyeta dyāvāpṛthivī iyam eka kapālam nirvapet  yadi dve naśyeyātām dvau māsau saṃvatsarasya apetau syātām atha yajamānaḥ pramīyeta āśvinam dvi kapālam nirvapet  saṃkhyāya udvāsayati yajamānasya gopīthāya iti kapāla nāśe nimitta ātma niḥśreyasa phalam karma darśayati evam iha api draṣṭavyam tasmāt  ātma niḥśreyasa artham iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ phala saṃyogaḥ  na syāt  pituḥ phala vacanam śeṣa bhūtam putrasya na pituḥ katham evam śrūyate vaiśvānaram dvādaśa kapālam nirvapet  putre jāte yad  aṣṭākapālaḥ  bhavati gāyatryā eva enam brahmavarcasena punāti yad  nava kapālaḥ  bhavati trivṛtā eva asamins tejaḥ  dadhāti yad  daśa kapālaḥ  virājā eva asmin annādyam dadhāti yad  ekādaśa kapāla s triṣṭubhā eva asmin   indriyam dadhāti yad  dvādaśa kapālaḥ  jagatyā eva asmin paśūn dadhāti yasmin  jāta etām iṣṭim nirvapati pūta eva sa tejasvī  anna ād indriyāvī paśumān bhavati iti yaḥ  jātaḥ tatra phalam śrūyate na asti vacanasya ati bhāraḥ tasmāt  putrasya phalam iti yad  uktam na parasya phala dāny etāni karmāṇi iti tad  ucyate yad  putrasya phalam ātmanaḥ sā prītiḥ tasmāt  ātmanepadam na virudhyate etām eva ātmanaḥ prītim abhipretya bhavati vacanam ātmā vai putra iti aṅgād aṅgāt  saṃbhavasi hṛdayāt  abhijāyase ātmā vai putra nāmā asi sa jīva śaradaḥ śatam iti atha yad  uktam yadi  ekam kapālam naśyet  iti evamādi tatra ucyate aṅgānām upaghāta saṃyogaḥ  nimitta artha upapadyate na anyathā na hi kapāle naṣṭe tad  anveṣaṇa arthā iṣṭiḥ  yuktā na hi kākinyām naṣṭāyām tad  anveṣaṇam kārṣāpaṇena kriyate evam vā vaiśvānaram dvādaśa kapālam nirvapet  putre jāta iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim jāta mātre uta kṛte jātakarmaṇi iti jāta mātra iti brūmaḥ saṃprāpte hi nimitte naimittikena bhavitavyam evam prāpte brūmaḥ kṛte jātakarmaṇi iti kutas  sāmarthyāt  kṛte hi jātakarmaṇi prāśanam tasya vidhīyate yadi prāk  jātakarmaṇaḥ iṣṭiḥ kriyate prāśana kālaḥ  viprakṛṣyeta tatra asya śarīra dhāraṇam na syāt  atha yad  uktam saṃprāpte nimitte hi naimittikena bhavitavyam iti ucyate aṅgānām upaghāta saṃyogaḥ  nimitta arthaḥ upaghātaḥ putra janma tad  bhūtam nimittam na tad kālaḥ  aṅgam tad  ca nimittam kṛte api jātakarmaṇi na apaiti itarasmin pakṣe kālaḥ  apeyāt  lakṣaṇā ca asmin pakṣe syāt  tasmāt  kṛte jātakarmaṇi iti atha kim antar daśa ahe yasmin kasmin vāhani uta sva kāla iti kim prāptam yasmin kasmin vāhani iti evam aniyamaḥ prāptaḥ atra ucyate paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāyām vā kutas  śruteḥ evam hi śrūyate ya iṣṭvā paśunā somena vā yajeta sa paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāyām vā yajeta iti na ati bhāraḥ  vacanasya itarasmin pakṣe kālaḥ  apeyāt  lakṣaṇā api  asmin pakṣe syāt  anyasyām tithau  antardaśa ahe vā kurvan sarvāṇi  aṅgāni  upasaṃhartum na śaknuyāt  kālam śaucam ca na upasaṃgṛhṇīyāt  tasmāt  atīte daśa ahe paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāyām vā kuryāt  iti agnim citvā sautrāmaṇyā yajeta vājapeyena iṣṭvā bṛhaspati savena yajeta iti aṅga prayojana saṃbandha iti  uktam etad  idānīm saṃdihyate kim cita mātre tantra madhya eva kartavyam uta sva kāle kartavyam iti tathā vājapeye kim bṛhaspati save uta sva kāla iti mukhya kāla tvam anayoḥ syāt  kutas  pradhāna akāla tvāt  aṅgānām ekaḥ  hi kālaḥ pradhānānām aṅgānām ca iti vakṣyate aṅgāni tu vidhāna tvāt  pradhānena upadiśyeran   iti agni cayanam kṛtvā na tāvatī  eva sthātavyam sautrāmaṇī saṃjñakaḥ  aparaḥ  yāgaḥ kartavya iti tathā vājapeyam abhinirvartya na etāvatā kṛtī syāt  bṛhaspati sava saṃjñakam yāgam abhinirvartayet  iti apavṛtte yāge codyate yāga antaram idam apavṛttiḥ  ca sarveṣu yāga aṅgeṣu  akṛteṣu na bhavati na yathā bhavān manyate yāga mātre nirvṛtta iti kutas  karaṇa vibhaktyā saṃyogāt  vājapeyena iṣṭyā vājapeyena phalasya vyāpāram kṛtvā sa aṅgena ca vyāpāraḥ  gamyate na niraṅgena bhavet  tantra madhye prayogaḥ vadi vājapeyam abhinirvartyetīpsita bhāvaḥ  vājapeyasya syāt  tatas  pradhāna mātram vājapeya saṃjñakam abhinirvartya iti gamyeta na tu  evam asti tasmāt  yathā uktāni sarvāṇi  aṅgāni kṛtvā iti  arthaḥ evam ced  nirvṛtte prayoge atikrānte vājapeya kāle yāga prayujyate tasya codanā sāmānyāt  jyotiṣṭaumike vidhyante prāpte svena ca udaka prāptena kālena bhavitavyam sautrāmaṇyāḥ  codanā sāmānyāt darśa pūrṇamāsa kālena iti āha vājapeye tāvat  iṣṭvā iti vacanāt  yāgam abhinirvartya iti gamyate agnau tu na upapadyate tatra citvā iti vacanāt  cayanam abhinirvartya iti  arthaḥ syāt  ucyate na etad  evam agnim citvā iti hi śrūyate agni cayanena saṃskṛtya iti  arthaḥ agniḥ  iti jvalanaḥ  abhidhīyate na tasya sthala sthāpana mātram upakāraḥ yadi sthala sthite yāgaḥ  bhavati tatas  cayanena agneḥ  upakāraḥ  asti tam abhinirvartya iti sthala sthite agnau yāgam abhinirvartya iti gamyate yāvat  sthala sthite agnau yāgaḥ  na bhavati na tāvat  agniḥ  cayanena upakriyate yena agniḥ  yajamānasya upakaroti saḥ  agneḥ  upakāraḥ  na sthala sthāpana mātram tasmāt  tatra api yāgam abhinirvartya iti gamyate santi  anumati ādīni  aiṣṭikāni karmāṇi malha ādayaḥ paśavaḥ pavitra ādayaḥ somāḥ valmīka vapāyām homa iti evamādīni dārvihomikāni tathā yaṣṭauhīm dīvyati rājanyam jināti śaunaḥ śepham ākhyāpayati abhiṣicyata iti eteṣām sannidhau śrūyate rājasūyena svārājya kāmaḥ  yajeta iti sa eṣa rūpavatām yāgānām saṃnidhau   arūpaḥ śabdaḥ śrūyamāṇaḥ samudāya vācakaḥ samadhigataḥ tatra saṃdehaḥ kim sarveṣām anumati ādīnām samudāyasya rājasūya śabdaḥ  vācakaḥ uta keṣāṃcid  vācakaḥ keṣāṃcid  na iti kim prāptam sarveṣām vācaka iti kutas  prakaraṇa śabda sāmānyāt  prakaraṇa śabdaḥ sarveṣām samānaḥ  rājasūyena iti rājā tatra sūyate tasmāt  rājasūyaḥ rājñaḥ  vā yajñaḥ  rājasūyaḥ tad  prakaraṇa saṃnidhāne sati viśeṣa abhāve ca sarveṣām vācakaḥ  bhavitum arhati yaḥ  ca rājasūya śabditas tatas  phalam bhavati tasmāt  sarvāṇi pradhānāni iti api vā iti pakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ yā anijyā as tā aṅgam yathā videvana ādayaḥ rājasūya saṃjñakena yāgena svārājyam kuryāt  iti  ucyamāne yāgena eva svārājyam sādhyate na āyāgena ayāgāḥ  ca videvana ādayaḥ tasmāt  aṅgam bhaveyuḥ ijyānām phalavatīnām śrūyamānā iti rājasūye abhiṣecanīya madhye yaṣṭauhīm dīvyati iti videvana ādayaḥ samāmnātāḥ te kim abhiṣecanīyasya aṅgam uta kṛtsnasya rājasūyasya iti saṃśayaḥ ucyate madhyāmnānād abhiṣecanīyasya iti tathā ānantaryam anugrahīṣyata iti sarvāsām ca anumati ādīnām codanānām aṅgam videvana ādi syāt  kutas  codanātaḥ sama tvāt  samānā etā anumati ādyāś codanāḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ phalavatī aś ca pradhāna bhūtāḥ sarvāsām āsām prakaraṇam na hi  abhiṣecanīyasya kevalasya kramāt  abhiṣecanīyasya prāpnuvanti prakaraṇāt  sarvāsām prakaraṇam ca kramāt  balīyaḥ tasmāt  na abhiṣecanīyasya kevalasya iti abhiṣecanīyasya tu madhye sthānam videvana ādīnām tatra kriyamāṇāḥ sarvāsām upakurvanti iti rājasūya upasadaḥ prakṛtya śrūyate purastād upasadām saumyena pracaranti antarā tvāṣṭreṇa upariṣṭāt  vaiṣṇavena iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim upasadaṅgam saumya ādayaḥ uta upasad kālā iti upasadaṅgam iti brūmaḥ kutas  upasat saṃyogasya śruta tvāt  kāla vidhau sati lakṣaṇā syāt  tasmāt  upasadaṅgam iti nanu kālavat  aṅgam bhaviṣyati tathā sati  ubhayam anugṛhyeta upasat saṃyogaḥ  ca purastād iti ca kāla abhidhānam upasat śabda saṃyogāt  upasadaṅga tā bhaviṣyati purastāt śabda sāmarthya āt  ca pūrva ādiṣu prayoga iti ucyate vipratiṣiddham hi  ubhayam na śaknoti  upasadām iti  eṣa śabdaḥ saumya ādīn   ca viśeṣṭum ekasmin vākye pūrva ādīn   ca bhidyate hi tathā vākyam tasmāt  na kālavat  aṅgam api vā iti pakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ kāla mātram syāt  na aṅga prayojana saṃbandhaḥ kutas  adarśanāt  viśeṣasya na anyaiḥ kāla abhidhānaiḥ  asya kaścid  viśeṣaḥ  lakṣyate āgni mārutāt  ūrdhvam anuyājaiḥ  caranti iti evamādibhiḥ atra api hi saumya ādayaḥ  vihitā upasadaḥ  api idam ānupūrvyam avihitam tad  vidhīyate tasmāt  kāla mātram iti vaiśvadevīm sāṃgrahāyaṇīm nirvapet  grāma kāma  iti tatra āmana homāḥ śrūyante āmanasya iti tisra āhutīḥ  juhoti iti atra saṃdehaḥ kim sama pradhāna bhūtā āmana homāḥ sāṃgrahāyaṇi iṣṭyā uta aṅgam tasyāḥ  iti kim prāptam sama pradhāna bhūtā iti kutas  tulya hetu tvāt  itarasya tulyam hi yajimat tvam nanu  aphalā homāḥ ucyate grāma kāma  iti  atra anupajyate tasmāt  sama pradhāna bhūtā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ phalavat  vā ukta hetu tvāt  itarasya pradhānam syāt  na ca etad  asti sama pradhāna bhūtā homā iṣṭyā iti phalavat  dhy aphalasya pradhānam phalavatī ceṣṭiḥ aphalā homāḥ nanu uktam anuṣaṅgaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti ucyate na anuṣaṅgaḥ prāpnoti kutas  vyavāyāt  tad  uktam vyavāyān na anuṣajyeta iti kena vyavāyaḥ paridhi mantraiḥ ugraḥ  asy ugraḥ tvam deveṣu  adhi ugraḥ aham sajāteṣu bhūyāsam priyaḥ sajātānām ugraḥ  ced  tā vasu vid iti evamādibhiḥ etān anukramya āmanasya iti tisra āhutīḥ  juhoti iti  āmananti tasmāt  sāṃgrahāyaṇyā aṅgam āmana homā iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate yām vai kāṃcid  adhvaryuḥ  ca yajamānaḥ  ca devatām antaritaḥ tasyāḥ  āvṛśceta yad  prājāpatyam dadhigraham gṛhṇāti śamayati  eva enām iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim nityaḥ  dadhigrahaḥ uta naimittika iti kim prāptam dadhigrahaḥ  naimittikaḥ syāt  śruti saṃyogāt  devatā antarāye nimitte śrūyate na ca nityaḥ  antarāyaḥ tasmāt  naimittika iti yad  uktam naimittika iti tad  gṛhyate kim tu nityaś ca kutas  jyeṣṭha śabdāt  jyeṣṭha śabdaḥ  bhavati jyeṣṭhaḥ  vā eṣa grahāṇām yasya eṣa gṛhyate jyaiṣṭhyam eva gacchati iti jyeṣṭha śabdaḥ  ca prādhānye prāthamye vā syāt  eṣa prathamaḥ na pradhānam yadi nityaḥ evam praśasya tvāt  upapadyate na jātu cala acalam hi praśaṃsanti tasmāt  nityaś ca naimittikaḥ  ca iti vinā api nimittena grahītavyaḥ nimittena api punar  iti sarva rūpa tā ca śrūyate sarveṣām vaitat  devānām rūpam yad  eṣa grahaḥ  yasya eṣa gṛhyate sarvāṇi  eva enam rūpāṇi paśūnām upatiṣṭhanta iti na hi devatā rūpam asmākam kiṃcid  anyat  pratyakṣam anyat  atas  nitya tvāt  tasmāt  api nityaś ca naimittikaḥ  ca iti yad  uktam nityaḥ  naimittikaḥ  ca iti tatra nitya eva syāt  jyeṣṭha śabdāt  sārvarūpya āc ca yad  uktam devatā antarāye nimitte śrūyata iti na devatā antarāyaḥ nimitta tvena gamyate tayoḥ  adhvaryu yajamānayoḥ karmaṇi  antarāyeṇa saṃbandhāt  na hi  etad  chrūyate adhvaryuṇā devatā antaritavyā yajamānena vā iti anityaḥ  hi antarāyaḥ na ca evaṃśabdaḥ  asti antarāye sati dadhigrahaḥ  grahītavya iti vinā eva saṃyogena dadhigrahasya grahaṇam antarāya sam ādhānam tu  asya prayojanam iti tad  etad  nityavat  grahaṇam anityam prayojanam nityam gṛhṇīyāt  anityam antarāyam samādhātum iti na avakalpate tatra prayojane anitya tvāt  grahaṇe nityavat  chrutiḥ  bādhyeta artha vāda tve tu na bādhyate na hi tad  antarāyam samādhātum gṛhyate anyat  eva prayojanam asya asti iti praśaṃsitum abhidhīyate dadhigrahasya tu soma aṅga tā eva prayojanam iti bhaṅgi tvā c ca antarāyasya bhaṅgī ca antarāyaḥ  anityaḥ  nitya praśaṃsā artham saṃkīrtyate tasmāt  na eṣa doṣaḥ nitya eva dadhigraha iti asti  agniḥ ya evam vidvān agnim cinuta iti tatra śrūyate yaḥ  vai saṃvatsara mukhyam abhṛtvā agnim cinute yathā sāmigarbhaḥ  vipadyate tādṛś  eva tadā ārtim ārcchet  vaiśvānaram dvādaśa kapālam purastān nirvapet  saṃvatsaraḥ  vā agniḥ  vaiśvānaraḥ yathā saṃvatsaram āptvā kāla āgate vijāyate evam eva saṃvatsaram āptvā kāla āgate agnim cinute na ārtim ārcchet  iti eṣā vā agneḥ priyā tanūr yad  vaiśvānaraḥ priyām eva asya tanūm avarundha iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim nityaḥ  vaiśvānaraḥ atha naimittika iti kim prāptam atra api nitya eva artha vādaḥ ukhyasya saṃvatsara ābharaṇena kṛtaḥ  doṣaḥ vaiśvānareṇa vihanyata iti nityaiḥ  ca asya samāna saṃkhya tvam bhavati trīṇi  etāni havīṃṣi bhavanti traya ime lokā eṣām lokānām ārohāya iti lokānām haviṣām sāmānyam na asti yadi yathā lokā nityās trayaḥ evam imāni havīṃṣi nityāni trīṇi evam lokaiḥ saṃstavaḥ  ghaṭate tasmāt  nityaḥ  vaiśvānara iti utpannasya nimitta ukhya ābharaṇe nirghātena saṃyogaḥ na asaṃyuktasya utpannasya doṣa nirghāta prayojana tā tasmāt  iha na dadhigrahavat  virodhaḥ  asti tena na artha vādaḥ naimittika iti atha yad  uktam lokaiḥ samāna saṃkhya tvam nitya tvāt  upapadyate na anyathā iti tatra brūmaḥ tri tvāl lokānām haviṣām ca sāmānyāt  artha vādaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti asti  agniḥ ya evam vidvān agnim cinuta iti tatra śrūyate saṃvatsaraḥ  vā enam pratiṣṭhāyai nudati yaḥ  agnim citvā na pratitiṣṭhati pañca pūrvāś citayaḥ  bhavanti atha ṣaṣṭhīm citim cinuta iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim yaḥ  ayam nitya eva agniḥ sa eva ayam ṣaṭcitika ucyate uta ekacitikaḥ  naimittika iti kim prāptam tasmin   eva nitye agnau ṣaṣṭhī citiḥ  eṣā vidhīyate nityāyām eva ṣaṣṭhyām eṣaḥ  artha vādaḥ yaḥ  api na pratiṣṭhā arhaḥ saḥ  api  anayā ṣaṣṭhyā cityā pratiṣṭhātum arhati iti citi praśaṃsā kim artham evam varṇyate ṣaṣṭhī śabda śravaṇāt  ṣaṇṇām hi pūraṇī ṣaṣṭhī ekasyām hi citau ṣaṣṭhī śabdaḥ  na sāmañjasyena syāt  tasmāt  ṣaṭcitikaḥ  agniḥ  nitya iti tābhiḥ  ca pūrvābhiḥ  asya as tulyavat  prasaṃkhyānam bhavati katham iyam vāva prathamā citiḥ oṣadhayaḥ purīṣam antarīkṣam vāva dvitīyā citiḥ vayāṃsi purīṣam asau vāva tṛtīyā citiḥ nakṣatrāṇi purīṣam yajñaḥ  vāva caturthā citiḥ dakṣiṇā purīṣam yajamānaḥ  vāva pañcamī citiḥ prajāḥ purīṣam saṃvatsaraḥ  vāva ṣaṣṭhī citiḥ ṛtavaḥ purīṣam iti tulyānām ca tulyavat  anukramaṇam bhavati yathā devāḥ  ṛṣayaḥ  gandharva as te anyata āsan asurā rakṣāṃsi piśācāḥ te anyata āsann iti tulyavat  cāmūṣām citīnām anukramaṇam anayā ṣaṣṭhyā tasmāt  etayā tad tulyayā bhavitavyam yadi ca yasmin   eva kratau tāḥ tasmin   eva eṣā tatas  etābhis tulyā tasmāt  api sa eva nityaḥ  agniḥ ṣaṭcitika iti artha vādaḥ  ca bhavati ṣaḍ  citayaḥ  bhavanti ṣaḍ  purīṣāṇi tāni dvādaśa saṃpadyante dvādaśā māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhati iti tad  ekacitike agnau na sāmañjasyena vacanam bhavati tasmāt  nitya eva ṣaṭcitikaḥ ekacitiḥ  vā naimittikaḥ syāt  kutas  apavṛkte hi yāge codyate apratiṣṭhayā nimittena yaḥ  na pratitiṣṭhati tasya eṣā citiḥ  ucyate naimittikī sā na nityā bhavitum arhati api cāpa vṛkte yāge codyate sā na vartamāne bhavitum arhati nanu citvā iti cayane nirvṛtte na yāge ucyate na etad  padārthe nirvṛtte citvā iti kim tarhi vākya arthe agnim citvā iti agneḥ  cayanena artham abhinirvartya iti kṛte ca yāge cayanena agneḥ  arthaḥ  nirvartitaḥ  bhavati na anyathā ṣaṣṭhī śabdaḥ  ca pañca pūrvāś citaya uktāḥ tā apekṣya avakalpiṣyate tasmāt  nirvṛtte yāga iti  ucyate tasmāt  vacanāt  ekacitiḥ  agniḥ dvayoḥ sūtrayoḥ  idam uttaram tābhiḥ  ca tulya saṃkhyānāt  arthavāda upapatteḥ  ca iti tābhiḥ  nityābhiḥ samāna saṃkhya tvam bhaviṣyati artha vādaḥ  ca upapatsyate pañca pūrvāś citayaḥ  bhavanti yābhiḥ  asau citibhiḥ  na pratitiṣṭhate atha iyam ṣaṣṭhī pratiṣṭhā artham iti tāḥ  ca sa purīṣā apekṣya dvādaśa tvena saṃstavaḥ  bhaviṣyati vipratiṣedhāt  ekasya ṣaṣ saṃkhyāyā dvādaśa saṃkhyāyāḥ  ca iti atulyānām api tulyavat  anukramaṇam bhavati yathā devāḥ  manuṣyāḥ pitaras te anyata āsann iti asti  āmāvāsye karmaṇi pitṛ yajñaḥ amāvāsyāyām aparāhṇe piṇḍa pitṛ yajñena caranti iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim āmāvāsyasya karmaṇaḥ piṇḍa pitṛ yajñaḥ  aṅgam uta anaṅgam iti kim prāptam aṅgam phalavat  saṃnidhānān niṣkraya vacanāt  ca āha nanu phalavat  saṃnidhau   aphalam tad aṅgam bhavati phalavat  ca idam kalpyeta svargeṇa iti ucyate satyam amāna asyaya eka vākya tvān na śakyaḥ svargaḥ kalpayitum iti āha kāla vacana tvāt  na karmaṇā eka vākya tvam saṃbhavati iti ucyate lakṣaṇayā api tāvat  karma eka vākya tvam saṃbhavati svarge kalpye na lakṣaṇā na śrutiḥ evam ca āmananti yad  pitṛbhyaḥ purvedyus  karoti pitṛbhya etad  yajñam niṣkrīya yajamānaḥ  devebhyaḥ pratanuta iti amāvāsyām prati niṣkretum ca śrūyate tasmāt  tad aṅga bhūtam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ pitṛ yajñaḥ sva kāla tvāt  anaṅgam syāt  anaṅga bhūtaḥ piṇḍa pitṛ yajñaḥ kasmāt  sva kāla tvāt  sva śabda abhihitena kālena asya saṃbandhaḥ na karmaṇā lakṣitena iti yathā darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām iṣṭvā somena yajeta iti yathā tad  etad  purastād upasadām saumyena caranti iti ca kāla eva ayam mukhyaḥ śabdaḥ  na karmaṇi karmaṇi lakṣaṇā śrutiḥ  ca lakṣaṇāyāḥ  balīyasī yad  ca uktam laksaṇayā karma eka vākya tā bhaviṣyati iti tad  ca na kasmāt  anuvāde hi lakṣaṇā nyāyyā na vidhau vidhiḥ  ca ayam tasmāt  na amāvāsyā karmaṇā saṃbandhaḥ ekasmin kāle dve karmaṇī paraspareṇa asaṃbaddha iti tulyavat  ca anyaiḥ pradhānaiḥ prasaṃkhyāyate catvāraḥ  vai mahāyajñāḥ agnihotram darśa pūrṇamāsau jyotiṣṭomaḥ piṇḍa pitṛ yajña iti mahāyajñaiḥ  tulyavat  prasaṃkhyāyate kā asya mahāyajña tā syāt  anyatas  phalavat tāyāḥ tasmāt  anaṅgam itas  ca anaṅgam pratiṣiddhe āmāvāsye piṇḍa pitṛ yajñam darśayati paurṇamāsīm eva yajeta bhrātṛvyavān na amāvāsyām hatvā bhrātṛvyam amāvāsyayā yajeta piṇḍa pitṛ yajñena eva amāvāsyāyām prīṇāti iti asatyām amāvāsyāyām piṇḍa pitṛ yajñam darśayati tad anaṅgatva upapadyate tasmāt  api na aṅgam piṇḍa pitṛ yajña iti kim prayojanam cintāyāḥ yadi paurṇamāsyām ādhānam tatas  anantarāyām amāvāsyāyām na kriyate yathā pūrva pakṣaḥ yathā tarhi siddhāntaḥ tathā kartavyaḥ idam aparam prayojanam kuṇḍapāyinām ayane māsam agni hotram juhoti māsam darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta iti yathā pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ tathā kartavyaḥ piṇḍa pitṛ yajñaḥ yathā siddhāntaḥ tathā na kartavya iti ślokam api  udāharanti ādhānam paurṇamāsyām ced  vṛtte darśe kariṣyate anaṅgam pitṛ yajñaḥ  ced  tatra eva na kariṣyate iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate āśvinam graham gṛhītvā trivṛtā yūpam parivīya āgneyam savanīyam paśum upākaroti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim paśu aṅgam raśanā uta yūpāṅgam iti kim prāptam paśu aṅgam kutas  tad āgame vidhānāt  paśu āgame hi vidhīyate paśunā asyāḥ saṃbandha utpatti vākye śrūyate parivyāṇam kṛtvā upākaroti paśum na anyathā iti evam śrutiḥ  bhavati kāla vacane lakṣaṇā syāt  parivyāṇena kālaḥ  lakṣyeta iti jyotiṣṭome pratyakṣaḥ  hi yūpasya saṃskāraḥ raśanā hi yā ca yāvatīm ca draḍhimnaḥ  mātrām yūpasya saṃjanayati draḍhimnā ca prayojanam yūpasya tasmāt  yūpasya eva draḍhimne raśanā syāt  dvitīyā ca vibhakti s tad prādhānya eva bhavati raśanāyām ca tṛtīyā tṛtīyā ca guṇa tve tasyāḥ tasmāt  yūpāṅgam yad  tu tad āgame vidhānāt  iti  uktam tad parihartavyam ucyate tad āgame vidhānam vākyam dvitīyā ca vibhaktiḥ śrutiḥ pratyakṣam ca vākyam bādheyātām iti yad  tu lakṣaṇa iti śruti asaṃbhave lakṣaṇā api nyāyyā eva evam ca mantra artha vādaḥ  arthavān bhaviṣyati yuvā su vāsāḥ parivīta āgāt  sa u śreyān bhavati jāyamānaḥ tam dhīrāsaḥ kavaya unnayanti svādhyaḥ  manasā devayanta iti tasmāt  yūpa aṅgam raśanā iti kim prayojanam cintāyāḥ agnau śrūyate eka yūpa ekādaśa paśavaḥ  niyojyā iti pratipaśu raśanā kāryā yadi pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ siddhānte dvairaśanyam eva ślokam api  udāharanti paśu aṅgam raśanā ced  yadi  ekasmin bahūn niyuñjīta pratipaśu raśanā kāryā yūpe ced  dvairaśanyam syāt  iti asti jyotiṣṭome paśuḥ  agnīṣomīyaḥ soma aṅga bhūtaḥ yaḥ  dīkṣitaḥ  yad  agnīṣomīyam paśum ālabhata iti tatra śrūyate svaruṇā svadhitinā vā paśum anakti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim yūpa aṅgam svaruḥ uta paśu aṅgam iti kim prāptam yūpāṅgam iti brūmaḥ kutas  eka deśa tvāt eka deśaḥ svaruḥ  yūpasya iti śrūyate yūpasya svarum karoti iti svarum antam yūpam kuryāt  iti  arthaḥ evam sa yūpaḥ  bhavati iti yathā caṣālam yūpāṅgam iva svarum niṣkraya vādaḥ  darśayati apaśyan ha sma vai purā ṛṣayaḥ  ye yūpam prāpayanti saṃbhajya sruvante manyante yajña vaiśasāya vā idam karma iti te prastaram sruva niṣkrayam apaśyan yūpasya svarum ayajña vaiśasāya iti niṣkraya śravaṇāt  tad aṅga tā vijñāyate tasmāt  yūpāṅgam iti paśu aṅgam vā tasya hi  añjana arthena svaruṇā prayojanam tathā hi śrūyate svaruṇā paśum anakti iti tad  añjanam paśoḥ svaroḥ  utpattim prayojayati yadi tad artha eṣaḥ svaruḥ tatas  dṛṣṭam prayojanam atha yūpa arthaḥ adṛṣṭam prayojanam tatas  kalpyam tasmāt  paśu aṅgam iti kayā bhaktyā evam āha yūpaḥ kila agnau pakṣetavyaḥ yad  svaruḥ prakṣipyate tena yūpaḥ prakṣipyata iti sa eṣa niṣkaya iva bhavati anayā bhaktyā stutiḥ  iti kim bhavati prayojanam eka yūpa ekādaśa paśavaḥ  yadā niyujyante tadā ekasya eva paśoḥ samañjanam pūrvasmin pakṣe sarveṣām siddhānte ślokaḥ  ca bhavati svaruḥ  yūpāṅgam iti ced  ekasma eva samañjanam bahūnām eka yūpa tve sarveṣām tu samañjanam iti staḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau tatra śrūyante āgneya agnīṣomīya upāṃśuya ajaindra agna sāṃnāyya yāgāḥ tathā āghārau   ājya bhāgau prayāja anuyājāḥ patnī saṃyājāḥ samiṣṭa yajuḥ sviṣṭakṛt  iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim sarve yāgāḥ pradhāna bhūtāḥ uta kecid  guṇa bhūtā iti kim prāptam darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  yāvatya ijyās tāḥ sarvāḥ pradhāna bhūtā iti yajeta svarga kāma  iti  aviśeṣeṇa yāgebhyaḥ phalam śrūyate phalavat  ca pradhānam sarve cāmī yāgāḥ tasmāt  sarve pradhāna bhūtā iti api vā kānicid  aṅgāni bhaveyuḥ kāni punar  tāni yeṣu  aṅga tvena saṃstutiḥ yathā abhīṣū vā etau yajñasya yad  āghārau cakṣuṣī vaitau yajñasya yad  ājya bhāgau yad  prayāja anuyāja aḥ  ca ijyante varma vā etad  yajñasya kriyate varma vā yajamānasya bhrātṛvyasya abhibhūtyai iti abhīśū rathasya aṅgam cakṣuṣī cakṣuṣmataḥ varma varmavataḥ sāmānyaḥ  hi  abhisaṃ  tavaḥ  yuktaḥ yadi ca aṅgāni tāni saṃstutāni tatas  saṃstavaḥ  arthavān bhavati tasmāt  aṅga saṃstutāni  aṅgāni iti evam ca kṛtvā anya artha darśanam upapannam bhavati prayāje prayāje kṛṣṇalam juhoti iti na ca prayājān yajati na ca anuyājān yajati iti ca aviśiṣṭam etad  kāraṇam saṃstavaḥ  nāma āgneya ādīnām api  aṅga tvena saṃstutiḥ  asti śiraḥ  vaitat  yajñasya yad  āgneyaḥ hṛdayam upāṃśu yāgaḥ pādau   agnīṣomīya iti śiraḥ śirasvataḥ  aṅgam hṛdayam hṛdayavataḥ pādau pādāvata iti sarvasya eva aṅga tvena saṃstutiḥ  iti sarvam eva aṅgam prāpnoti tad  pradhānam na syāt  asati pradhāne kasya aṅgam tasmāt  na etad  aṅgam iti atha yad  uktam anya artha darśanam para artha tvāt  na tad  sādhakam bhavati para artham hi tad  vākyam na dṛśyamānasya prayāja ādeḥ prāpaṇa artham tasmāt  anyat  asya pramāṇam anveṣṭavyam śruti antaram nyāyaḥ  vā tasmin   asati mṛgatṛṣṇā darśanam iva tad  bhavati saṃstutiḥ  api  asati nyāye asādhikā eva tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati tad  uktam sarvāṇi sama pradhānāni iti na etad  evam darśa pūrṇamāsa śabda vācyāni pradhānāni karmāṇi kutas  phala saṃyogāt  darśa pūrṇamāsa śabdakebhyaḥ phalam śrūyate darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti kāni punar  darśa pūrṇamāsa śabdakāni yeṣām vacane paurṇamāsī śabdaḥ  amāvāsyā śabdaḥ  vā āgneya ādīni tāni nanu  amāvāsyā śabdakānām na eva phalam śrūyate ucyate pṛthaktve samudāyayoḥ  niveśa etayoḥ  abhidhānayoḥ paurṇamāsī iti ca amāvāsyā iti ca triṣu  āgneya ādiṣu yaḥ samudāyaḥ tatra paurṇamāsī śabdaḥ itareṣu  amāvāsyā śabdaḥ katham paurṇamāsy amāvāsyā iti ca dvi śabdaḥ śrūyate dvi arthavat  vyapadeśāt  ca katham tad  vyapadeśaḥ dvivacat nirdeśāt  darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām iti eka arthau ca darśa amāvāsyā śabdau katham darśaḥ  vā etayoḥ pūrvaḥ pūrṇamāsa uttaras tayoḥ  atha yad  pūrṇamāsam pūrvam ārabhate tad  ayathāpūrvam prakriyate darśa pūrṇamāsam ārabhamāṇaḥ sarasvatyai carum nirvapet  sarasvate dvādaśa kapālam amāvāsyā vai sarasvatī pūrṇamāsaḥ sarasvān ubhau   etau yathāpūrvam kalpayitvā ārabhata ṛddhyai ṛdhnoti  eva arthaḥ  mithuna tvāya iti tatra darśa śabdena prakṛtyā amāvāsyā śabdena bruvan   ekārtha tām darśayati śakyate ca candrasya adarśanena amāvāsyā darśa iti lakṣayitum yathā cakṣuṣoḥ  abhāve sati cakṣuṣmān iti cakṣurbhyām lakṣyate etasmāt  vyapadeśāt  ca śrutitaḥ  ca loke śravaṇāt  eka artha tām eva adhyavasyāmaḥ tad  punar  mukhya lakṣaṇam yad  phalavat tvam yad  anyat  tad  saṃnidhau śrūyate tad  tad  aṅgam katham itikartavya tā kāṅkṣasya saṃnidhau śrūyamāṇam itikartavya tā viśeṣaṇa tvena paripūraṇa samartham tad aṅgam bhavitum arhati akalpyamāne vākya śeṣe phalam kalpayitavyam syāt  iti āha nanu darśa pūrṇamāsa phalam eva atra anuṣajyate ucyate śakyam anuṣaktum kim tu darśa pūrṇamāsa vākyam sa ākāṅkṣam eva syāt  anyāsya iti kartavya tā aśru tā kalpyeta eṣām api prayāja ādīnām anyā kalpyeta etad  itikartavya tau  agamyamāna utsṛjyeta tena aṅga tvam kāraṇam bhāgi iti eṣām anyena phalena saṃbandhaḥ  aśrutaḥ tasmāt  na sarvāṇi sama pradhānāni āghāra ādīni guṇa karmāṇi iti nāma viśeṣa saṃyuktāḥ  ca guṇa viśeṣā vidhīyante yathā caturhotrā pūrṇamāsīm abhimṛśet  pañca hotra amāvāsyām iti sarveṣu pradhāneṣu asmin samudāye caturhotrā asmin pañca hotra iti vibhāga avijñāna āt  ca idam na upapadyeta bhavati ca evaṃlakṣaṇakam guṇa vidhānam tasmāt  asmad pakṣa eva iti api ca aṅga tvena ādhāra ādīnām saṃstutiḥ  upapannā bhaviṣyati atha yad  uktam āgneya ādīnām api  aṅga tvena saṃstutiḥ  aṅga tvam khyāpayet  iti tad  parihartavyam na eṣa doṣaḥ pradhānānām api  eṣām satām utpatti apekṣā śira ādi stutiḥ  abhiviṣyati iti jāyamānasya hi puruṣasya agre śiraḥ  jāyate madhye madhyam paścāt  pādau evam āgneyaḥ  agratas  upāṃśu yājaḥ  madhye agnīṣomīyaḥ paścāt  iti etasmāt  sāmānyā doṣā stutiḥ  iti caturdaśa pūrṇamāsyām āhutayaḥ  hūyante trayodaśa amāvāsyāyām iti itarathā na caturdaśa paurṇamāsyām āhutayaḥ  bhaveyuḥ na vā amāvāsyāyām trayodaśa iti tasmāt  āgneya ādīni pradhānāni āghāra ādīni  aṅgāni iti siddham asti jyotiṣṭomaḥ jyotiṣṭomena svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti tatra dīkṣaṇīyādayaḥ  ca yāgā vidyante sautye ca ahani soma yāgaḥ tatra saṃdehaḥ kim atra yāga mātra pradhānam uta somayāga iti kim prāptam jyotiṣṭome tulyāni sarvāṇi bhaveyuḥ kutas  aviśiṣṭam hi kāraṇam yāgāt  phalam śrūyate sarve cāmī yāgāḥ phalavat  ca pradhānam tasmāt  jyotiṣṭome sarve yāgāḥ pradhānam iti guṇānām tu utpatti vākyena saṃbandhaḥ  bhavati keṣāṃ guṇānām jyotiṣām stomānām katamena utpatti vākyena saṃbandhaḥ  bhavati jyotiṣṭomena svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti jyotiṣṭomāt  yāgāt  svargaḥ śrūyate na yāga mātrāt yatra ca jyotīṃṣi stomāḥ sa jyotiṣṭomaḥ kasya jyotīṃṣi stomāḥ stoma yāgasya iti brūmaḥ evam hi  āmnāyate katamāni vaitāni jyotīṃṣi ya ete tasya stomāḥ trivṛt  pañcadaśa saptadaśa ekaviṃśā etāni vā jyotīṃṣi tāni  etasya stomā iti somayāgasya stomā aṅgam samabhivyāhārāt  graham vā gṛhītvā camasam vā unnīya stotram upākaroti iti te ca stomāḥ  trivṛt ādayaḥ katham trivṛt  bahiṣpavamānam pañcadaśāni  ājyāni iti evamādibhiḥ śravaṇaiḥ tasmāt  trivṛt ādi stomakaḥ soma yāgaḥ sa jyotiṣṭoma iti yaḥ  ca jyotiṣṭoma s tatas  phalam yatas  ca phalam tad  eva pradhānam iti katham punar  trivṛt ādayaḥ  jyotīṃṣi ucyate bhavantu vā jyotīṃṣi mā vā bhūvan jyotiḥ śabdena tāvat  uktāni vacana mātreṇa api śabdaḥ  bhavati viśeṣataḥ  lakṣaṇāyām api ca dyotateḥ  vā dīpti karmaṇaḥ  jyotayateḥ  vā jyotiḥ śabdam labhante dyotyate hi taiḥ śabdaiḥ dyotayanti iti vā stutyām tasmāt  somayāgaḥ  jyotiṣṭomaḥ sa ca pradhānam guṇa bhūtā dīkṣaṇīya ādaya iti śiraḥ  vā etad  yajñasya yad  dīkṣaṇīya iti evamādi ca liṅgam dṛśyate tathā guṇāḥ  ca jyotiṣṭoma vikāre dīkṣaṇīyādayaḥ  dṛśyante caturviṃśati mānam hiraṇyam dīkṣaṇīyāyām dadyāt  prāpaṇīyāyām dve caturviṃśatimāna iti tulya tve na pravartayiṣyante dīkṣaṇīya ādayaḥ tasmāt  api soma yāgaḥ pradhānam iti agnīṣomīye paśau śrūyate ekādaśa prayājān yajati ekādaśa anuyājān yajati iti cāturmāsyeṣu nava prayājān yajati nava anuyājān yajati iti agnau śrūyate ṣaṣ  upasada iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim prati prayājam ekādaśa saṃkhyā praty anuyājam ca tathā cāturmāsyeṣu nava saṃkhyā tathā agnau ca upasatsu ṣaṣ saṃkhyā uta sarva saṃpādyā saṃkhyā iti kim prāptam pratipradhānam saṃkhyā bhidyata iti kutas  bhinnāni hi tāni karmāṇi tāni ca pradhānāni prati saṃkhyā śrūyate pradhāna saṃnidhau ca guṇaḥ śiṣyamāṇāḥ pratidhānam bhidyate yathā pṛṣadājyena anuyājān yajati iti pratyanuyājam pṛṣattā guṇa u bhidyate evam iha api iti sarva saṃpādyā saṃkhyā kalpyeta kutas  pṛthaktva niveśinī hi saṃkhyā asati pṛthaktve abhyāsena kalpyeta yāvatī  asaṃbhavaḥ  bhedasya tāvatī  eva abhyasyeta yāvati saṃbhavati tāvati pṛthaktva niveśa eva nyāyyaḥ tasmāt  sarva saṃpādya eva saṃkhyā yad  tu pṛṣadājyavat  iti na pṛṣattā ekasya na saṃbhavati na asau pṛthaktva niveṣinī na ca ekasya kriyamāṇā sarveṣām tantreṇa upakaroti iti tasmāt  avaśyam bhettavyā tantreṇa tu upakaroti saṃkhyā itara apekṣā hi sā bhavati evam sati sahatvasya prāpakaḥ prayoga vacanaḥ  anugrahīṣyata iti upasatsu saṃdehaḥ kim āvṛttiḥ  daṇḍa kalitavat  uta sva sthānāt  vivardhanta iti kim tāvat  prāptam āvartanīyānām arthānām eṣa dharmaḥ yad  uta daṇḍa kalitavat  yaḥ  hi  ucyate tris  anuvākaḥ paṭhyatām iti sa ādita ārabhya parisamāpya punar  ādita ārabhyate tasmāt  daṇḍa kalitavat  āvṛttiḥ evam prāpte brūmaḥ sva sthānāt  vivardhitum arhati kutas  kṛta ānupūrvya tvāt kṛtam ānupūrvyam upasatsu prathamām kṛtvā madhyamā kartavyā tatas  uttama iti tatra yadi daṇḍa kalitavat  āvṛttiḥ syāt  uttamām kṛtvā punar ādyāyāḥ  abhyāse kriyamāṇe asthāne sā vivṛddhiḥ kṛtā bhavati sva sthāna vivṛddhau na eṣa doṣaḥ tasmāt  sva sthāne vivṛddhiḥ  iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ sāmidhenyaḥ sāmidhenīḥ  anvāha iti tatra kāmyāḥ sāmidhenī kalpāḥ ekaviṃśatim anubrūyāt  pratiṣṭhākāmasya iti  evamādayaḥ tatra āgamena saṃkhyā pūraṇam vakṣyate tatra saṃdehaḥ kim āgantūnām ante niveśaḥ uta samidhyamānavatīm samidhavatīm ca antareṇa niveśa iti kim tāvat  prāptam ante niveśaḥ ante tu bādarāyaṇaḥ iti  anena nyāyena iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ samidhyamānavatīm samidhavatīm ca antareṇa niveśa iti kutas  dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ  antarāle samarhaṇāt  saṃstavāt  iti  arthaḥ iyam vai samidhyamānavatī asau samidhavatī yad  antarā tad  dhāyyā iti  antarikṣa saṃstute asmin   antarāle vidhīyante tasmāt  na ante syuḥ  iti atha vā yā dhāyyā śabdikāḥ tāḥ  tatra bhavitum arhanti tena hi śabdena tatra saṃstavaḥ saṃstavāt  ca vidhānam yathā pṛthu pājavatyau dhāyye uṣṇikkakubhau dhyāyye iti kāḥ punar  etā dhāyyā iti nāma na asya śabdasya prasiddhim upalabhāmahe ucyate sāmidhenyaḥ  dhyāyyāḥ kutas  evam hi bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ  vacanam pāyyasāṃnāyya nikāyya dhāyyā māna haviḥ nivāsasāmidhenīṣu  iti asmāt  vacanāt  chrutim anumimīmahe katamāsu sāmidhenīṣu  iti ucyate aviśeṣāt  sarvāsu ati gamyate iha tu samidhyamānavatīm samidhavatīm ca antareṇa dhyāyyāḥ syuḥ  iti sarvāsu sāmidhenīṣu satīsu dhyāyyā vacanāt  viśiṣṭānām sāmidhenīnām dhāyyā śabda iti gamyate nanu pāṇinivacanāt  viśeṣeṇa sarvā dhāyyāḥ na iti  āha viśiṣṭāsu  api vacanam upapadyata eva yadi viśiṣṭāḥ tatas  kā iti ucyate yāsu dhāyyā śabdaḥ śrūyate tāḥ  tāvat  dhāyyāḥ tāsu ca dhāyyāsu satīṣu vacanam arthavat  bhavati arthavati ca sati vacane na anyā dhāyyāḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt  iti uṣṇikkakubhoḥ ca ante prayogaḥ  dṛśyate yaj jagatyā paridadhyāt  antam yajñam gacchet  atha yad  triṣṭubhā paridadhāti na antam gacchati iti nanu triṣṭubh  atra ante dṛśyate na uṣṇikkaku bhauv iti ucyate triṣṭubham eva ayam uṣṇih kakumau   iti brūte katham triṣṭubhaḥ  vīryam iti  evam ante saṃstuteḥ triṣṭubhaḥ  vā etad  vīryam yad  uṣṇikkaku bhāv iti kāraṇe kāryavat  upacāraḥ kṛtaḥ santi vivṛddha stomakāḥ kratavaḥ ekaviṃśena atirātreṇa prajā kāmam yājayeyuḥ  triṇavena ojaskāmam trayastriṃśena pratiṣṭhā kāmam iti tatra āgamena saṃkhyā pūraṇam vakṣyate atha bahiṣpavamāne vaikṛteṣu  ānīyamāneṣu bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim vaikṛtānām ante niveśaḥ uta prāk  paryāsāt  iti kim prāptam purastāt  paryāsāt  āgantavaḥ syuḥ tathā hi dṛṣṭam dvādaśa ahe stotrīya anurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ vṛṣaṇvantaḥ tṛcā bhavanti tṛca uttamaḥ paryāsa iti iha api prāk  paryāsāt  āgantubhiḥ  bhavitavyam prayāsa śabdaḥ  ca anta vacanaḥ  loke dṛśyate yathā kṣetra paryāsaḥ nadī paryāsa iti evam paryāsaḥ  ante kṛtaḥ  bhaviṣyati ante vaivaṃjātīyakam vaikṛtam syāt  uktam ante tu bādarāyaṇa iti atha yad  uktam tathā hi dṛṣṭam dvādaśa āha iti tad  parihartavyam atra ucyate vacanāt  dvādaśa ahe bhavati stotrīya anurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ vṛṣaṇvanta s tṛcā bhavanti tṛca uttamaḥ paryāsa iti na hi vacanasya ati bhāraḥ  asti na ca ayam tad vikāraḥ yad  tatas  dharmān gṛhaṇīyāt  iti yaḥ  api tad vikāraḥ tatra api  anta eva niveśaḥ kutas  apūrvāt  vṛṣaṇvatām tṛcānām vṛṣaṇvanta eva prāc paryāsāt  yāvat  vacanam vācanikam na sadṛśam upasaṃkrāmati iha api vivṛddha stomakāḥ kratava udāharaṇam tatra uttarayoḥ pavamānayoḥ sāmnām āgama iti vakṣyate tatra agamyamāneṣu sāmasu saṃdehaḥ kim teṣām ante niveśaḥ uta gāyatrī bṛhatī anuṣṭubh sv iti kim prāptam anta uttarayoḥ  dadhyāt  uktaḥ  atra nyāyaḥ ante bādarāyaṇa iti tasmāt  ante niveśa iti gāyatrī bṛhatī anuṣṭu upsu niveśaḥ kasmāt  vacanāt  trīṇi ha vai yajñasya udarāṇi gāyatrī bṛhatī anuṣṭu bh  iti atra hi  eva avapanti ata eva udvapanti iti vacanena asti  upālambhaḥ tasmāt  na eṣām ante niveśa iti aupānu vākye kāṇḍe grahā iṣṭakāś ca samāmnātāḥ eṣa vai haviṣā havir yajate yaḥ  dābhyam gṛhītvā somāya yajata iti tathā parā vā etasya āyuḥ prāṇa eti yaḥ  aśum gṛhṇāti iti tathā iṣṭakāś citriṇīḥ  upadadhāti vajriṇīr upadadhāti bhūta iṣṭakā upadadhāti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim graha iṣṭakam aupānu vākyam savana śeṣaḥ  citi śeṣaḥ  ca atha kim kratu śeṣaḥ  agni śeṣaḥ  ca iti kim prāptam savana citi śeṣaḥ kutas  grahaiḥ savanāni  ārabhyante iṣṭakā abhiḥ  citayaḥ yad  ca yena ārabhyate tad  tad  aṅgam kratu agniśeṣaḥ syāt  kutas  codita tvāt  agniḥ  cetavyaḥ śrūyate ya evam vidvān agnim cinuta iti na citiḥ  cetavyā iṣṭakā cayanena agniḥ  cetavyaḥ śrūyate agnim iti dvitīya anirdeśāt tathā yaḥ  dābhyam gṛhītvā somāya yajata iti  adābhyasya yajatinā saṃbandhaḥ tathā aṃśoḥ tasmāt  sakṛt  yāga saṃbandham kṛtvā kṛtārthaḥ śabdaḥ  bhavati śrutam saṃbandham abhinirvartya tathā sakṛt  agni saṃbandham kṛtvā kṛtī manyeta acodanā citi savanayoḥ na hi te kartavya tayā codyete para artham hi tayoḥ śravaṇam kim prayojanam savana citi śeṣa tve pratisavanam grahaṇam praticiti ceṣṭakā upadhānam kratu agni śeṣa tve sakṛt  grahaṇa upadhāne aupānu vākye śrūyate citriṇīḥ  upadadhāti vajriṇīr upadadhāti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim etāḥ pañcabhyām citau   upadheyāḥ uta madhyamāyām iti kim prāptam pañcabhyām eva iṣṭakāḥ kṛta kramāḥ anyā na etābhiḥ  vyaveṣyante āvapanam vā uttamā citiḥ anyā iṣṭakā upadadhāti iti na eva etāntyāyām citau kasyām tarhi madhyamāyām kutas  brāhmaṇavatī etā iṣṭakāḥ tāsām madhyamā citiḥ  āmnāyate yām vai kāṃcid  brāhmaṇavatīm iṣṭakām abhijānīyāt  tām madhyamāyām citau   upadadhyāt  iti nanu sarvā eva iṣṭakā brāhmaṇavatyaḥ na iti  āha aparā liṅga kramāt  samākhyānāt  ca tasmāt  etā na ante syuḥ  iti aupānu vākye kāṇḍa iṣṭakāḥ samāmnātāḥ vajriṇīr upadadhāti citriṇīḥ  upadadhāti bhūta iṣṭakā upadadhāti iti tatra idam samadhigatam madhyamāyām citau   upadheyā iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim prāk  lokāṃpṛṇāyāḥ uta paścāt  iti kim prāptam ante tu bādarāyaṇa iti evam prāpte ucyate prāk  lokaṃpṛṇāyāḥ tasyāḥ saṃpūraṇa artha tvāt saṃpūraṇa artha tā tasyāḥ śrūyate yad  eva asya ūnam yad  chidram tad  anayā pūrayati lokam pṛṇa chidram pṛṇa iti apūrva tvāt  vā arthasya vidhiḥ  eva ayam saṃstavena iti gamyate tasmāt  prāk  lokaṃpṛṇāyāḥ syāt  ādhāne santi pavamāna iṣṭayaḥ santi ca niyatāni karmāṇi agnihotra ādīni aniyatāni ca aindra agna ādīni tatra saṃdehaḥ kim pavamāna iṣṭīḥ kṛtvā karmāṇi pratipattavyāni uta ahita mātreṣu  agniṣu  iti kim prāptam āhita pātreṣu  iti kutas  āhita mātreṣu  asau   agniṣu karmāṇi kartum samarthaḥ  bhavati yathā āhitāgniḥ  na klinnam dārvā dadhyāt  iti darśayati ca agnim vai sṛṣṭam agni hotreṇa anudravanti iti  āhita mātreṣu  agni hotram darśayati tasmāt  na pavamāna iṣṭayaḥ pratīkṣitavyā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ pavamāna iṣṭibhiḥ saṃskṛteṣu  agniṣu karmāṇi varteran kutas  saṃskārāṇām tad artha tvāt saṃskāra śabdā eta āhavanīya ādayaḥ saṃskārasya kasyacid  abhāvena āhavanīya ādiṣu pratipattiḥ syāt  tasmāt  saṃskṛteṣu  agniṣu karmāṇi iti yad  tu āhitāgniḥ  na klinnam dārvā dadhyāt  iti evamādi yuktam yad  āhita mātreṣu kriyate āhitāgneḥ  tad vratam ucyate sa ca āhita mātreṣu  āhitāgniḥ saṃvṛttaḥ tasmāt  anantaram vratam syāt  tad bhūta tvāt atha yad  uktam āhita mātreṣu  agni hotram darśayati pūrvam iṣṭibhya iti tasya kaḥ parihāra iti  ābhāṣā antam sūtram arthavāda eṣaḥ kutas  arthasya vidyamāna tvāt  vidyamānaḥ  hi tatra anya eva agnihotra homaḥ katham hotavyam agni hotram na hotavyam iti mīmāṃsante brahma vādinaḥ yad  yajuṣā juhuyāt  ayathāpūrvam āhutī juhuyāt  yadi na juhuyāt  agniḥ parāpatet  tūṣṇīm eva hotavyam iti tasya tūṣṇīm homasya praśaṃsā arthaḥ  ayam artha vādaḥ nyāya vipratiṣedhaḥ  ca bhavet  yadi  anantaram agnihotra ādayaḥ syuḥ yaḥ pūrva uktaḥ  nyāyaḥ sa vipratiṣidhyeta na vā tāsām tad artha tvāt  iti tasmāt  saṃskṛte karmāṇi bhaveyuḥ  iti agni cit  varṣati na dhāvet  na striyam upeyāt  tasmāt  agni citā pakṣiṇaḥ  nāśitavyā iti evamādayaḥ padārthāḥ śrūyante teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim saṃcita mātre pratipattavyā uta kratvanta iti kim prāptam saṃcita mātra eva iti agnim yaḥ  citavān saḥ  agnicit  iti tasya śrūyamāṇāś citavataḥ  anantaram eva prāpnuvanti prāpte nimitte naimittikam kartavyam tasmāt  anantaram eva prayoga vacanaḥ  hi  atra tān padārthān prāpayati yeṣām kratu artha tvam na ca eṣām kratu artha tvam asti puruṣa arthā hi  ete katham pratiṣedhe puruṣaḥ śrūyate varṣati na dhāvet  na striyam upeyāt  iti evamādi na ca kratu arthā ete prasaktāḥ yena pratiṣedhaḥ kratoḥ  upakuryāt  nanu puruṣa arthā api citavataḥ śravaṇāc cayana anantaram prāptāḥ na iti brūmaḥ agni artham cayanam tad  yad  agneḥ svam kāryam kurvataḥ sāhāyye vartate tad  tad artham kaś ca tasya sva arthaḥ yāga asiddhiḥ siddhe ca yāge cayanena upakṛtam bhavati tasmāt  siddhe yāge agni cit  tena kratvanta iti jyotiṣṭome śrūyate āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśa kapālam nirvapet  dīkṣiṣyamāṇa  iti tathā daṇḍena dīkṣayati mekhalayā dīkṣayati kṛṣṇājinena dīkṣayati iti  evamādi tatra saṃdehaḥ kim sarvaiḥ  dīkṣitaḥ  bhavati atha veṣṭi ante dīkṣita iti kim tāvat  prāptam sarvaiḥ  iti kutas  dīkṣā abhisaṃbandhāt dīkṣā saṃbandhaḥ  bhavati daṇḍena dīkṣayati dīkṣām asya karoti iti  arthaḥ yadi iṣṭi ante dīkṣitaḥ syāt  katham asya daṇḍena dīkṣām kuryāt  tena iṣṭyā na dīkṣitaḥ na ca asya iṣṭi ante dīkṣita śabdam paśyāmaḥ āvedane tu  asya dīkṣita śabdaḥ tasmāt  na tāvati dīkṣitaḥ syāt  na ca saṃbhavati sam uccaye vikalpaḥ  nyāyyaḥ pakṣe bādhaḥ syāt  tatra prayoga vacanaḥ  bādhyeta tasmāt  bhinneṣu  api dīkṣā saṃbandha vākyeṣu prayoga vacanena saha eka vākyata iti  āvedana kāle dīkṣitaḥ syāt  iṣṭi ante vā dīkṣitaḥ syāt  tad arthā hi sā dīkṣaṇa arthā katham dīkṣiṣyamāṇasya adīkṣitasya sā bhavati yadi tasyāḥ  uttara kāle dīkṣitaḥ evam sā dīkṣiṣyamāṇasya tasmāt  vākyāt  avagamyate bhavati tadā dīkṣita iti dīkṣā kāraṇe padārthe nirvṛtte kim iti na dīkṣitaḥ syāt  vākyam hi nirapekṣam dīkṣita iti jñāpayati yad  tu dīkṣā saṃbandhaḥ  daṇḍena dīkṣayati iti katham sa dīkṣita tve syāt  iti daṇḍena evam dīkṣitam saṃpādayati iti  avagacchāmaḥ yad  tu anantaram dīkṣita śabdaḥ  na asti iti na śabdasya aprayogaḥ  artha abhāve hetuḥ sati  api  arthe tad avasara abhāvān na prayujyate śabdaḥ anyena ca dīkṣita iti  avagamyate vākyena āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśa kapālam nirvapet  dīkṣyamāṇa  iti yad  ca āvedana kāle dīkṣita śabda iti iṣṭi ante api dīkṣitasya asau   aviruddhaḥ prayoga vacanaḥ  ca aviruddhaḥ yata ekam dīkṣā kāraṇam anyaiḥ  dīkṣitam saṃpādayati iti gamyate itas  ca paśyāmaḥ iṣṭa dīkṣaṇa arthā iṣṭi ante ca pravṛttiḥ  iti kasmāt  samākhyānam ca tadvat  iti yadvan nyāya upadiṣṭaḥ katham dīkṣaṇīya iti tādarthya karī samākhyā bhavati yathā snānīyam
