bhojanīyam ca iti tasmāt  ca paśyāmaḥ iṣṭiḥ  dīkṣaṇa arthā iṣṭi ante ca pravṛttiḥ  iti iha kāmyā iṣṭaya udāharaṇam aindrāgnam ekādaśa kapālam nirvapet  iti evamādayaḥ gavā ādayaḥ somāḥ saumya ādayaḥ paśavaḥ tatra saṃdehaḥ kim yena krameṇa adhītāḥ tena eva krameṇa prayoktavyāḥ uta aniyama iti kim tāvat  prāptam kratūnām ānupūrvyam yad  pāṭhe tad  eva prayoge bhavitum arhati evam pāṭha kramaḥ  anugṛhītaḥ  bhaviṣyati itarathā pāṭha kramaḥ  bādhyeta tad  mā bhūd iti krameṇa anuṣṭhātavyam na vā ayam kramaḥ  niyamyeta kutas  asaṃbandhāt  pṛthak  pṛthak  eṣām karmaṇām prayoga vacanāni tāni sva pada arthānām upasaṃhārakāṇi yaḥ  yasya na upakārakaḥ sa tasya na krameṇa na utkramaṇa yaḥ  yasya upakaroti kasyacid  tasya upakurvataḥ kramaḥ sāhāyye vartate na ca etāni karmāṇi  anyonyasya upakurvanti tasmāt  na eṣām kramaḥ sāhāyye vartate tasmāt  asaṃbandha iti kāmyāni ca etāni karmāṇi kāmāś ca krameṇa utpadyante tena nimittasya ākrama tvāt  na kramavanta iti iti yad  uktam pūrva pakṣe tad  eva punar  ucyate parihartum evam krameṇa pāṭhaḥ  arthavān bhaviṣyati iti etad  ābhāṣā antam sūtram syāt  arthavān krama pāṭhaḥ asati  api prayoge krame vidyā grahaṇa artha tvāt karma avabodhana arthāyām vidyāyām krama niyama adṛṣṭam tad āśrayam eva bhaviṣyati iti yathā tvad pakṣe pareṣu sarva svārāt  yasya api kramaḥ  aṅgam iti pakṣaḥ tasya api sarva svārāt  pareṣām sarva svāreṇa yaḥ kramas tasya adṛṣṭa artha tāvaśyam kalpanīyā jyotiṣṭome śrūyate eṣa vāva prathamaḥ  yajñānām yaj jyotiṣṭomaḥ ya etena aniṣṭvā atha anyena yajeta gartapatyam eva tad  jāyate pra vā mīyata iti tatra saṃdehaḥ ya etena iti kasya ayam vāda iti praśnena eva upakramaḥ ucyate ya etena iti  agniṣṭomasya vādaḥ kutas  prakaraṇāt  tasya hi prakaraṇe bhavati  etad  vacanam prakṛta vācīni ca sarva nāmāni bhavanti liṅgam api bhavati tatra śrūyate yasya navati śatam stotrīyā iti agniṣṭomasya hi bhavanti navati śatam stotrīyāḥ katham trivṛt  bahiṣpavamānam pañcadaśāni  ājyāni tāni catvāri sā ekonasaptatiḥ pañcadaśaḥ  mādhyaṃdinaḥ pavamānaḥ tena caturaśītiḥ saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni tāni catvāri sa aṣṭaṣaṣṭiḥ caturaśītyā saha dvipañcāśat  chatam saptadaśa ārbhavaḥ pavamānaḥ tena ṣaṣṭi adhikam śatam nava ca ekaviṃśam yajñāyajñīyam iti tad  etad  navati śatam agniṣṭomasya tasmāt  api  agniṣṭomaḥ atha anyena iti kim saṃsthānām vādaḥ atha jyotiṣṭoma vikārāṇām eva ekāha ādīnām iti kim tāvat  prāptam saṃsthānām iti kutas  saṃnidhānāt  saṃnihitā as tasmin prakaraṇe saṃsthāḥ tāsām vādaḥ prakaraṇa anugrahāya tad prakṛteḥ  vā gavā ādeḥ  vādaḥ syāt  āpatti vihārau hi prakṛti vikāra mātreṣu upapadyete na tulya śabdeṣu  eva jyotiṣṭoma śabdakeṣu na evam abhisaṃbandhaḥ kriyate atha anyena jyotiṣṭoma śabdakena iti katham tarhi anyena iti prakṛtāt  itarat  bravīti na sa jyotiṣṭomena viśiṣyate na hi śabdasya arthaḥ samīpa gatena kṛta prayojanena eka deśe avasthāpayitavyaḥ  bhavati na hi vākyena śrutiḥ  bādhyate atha jyotiṣṭomāt  anyena iti  abhisaṃbadhyate tatas  natarām saṃsthā vādaḥ katham punar  āpatti vihārau prajāpatiḥ  vāgniṣṭomaḥ sa uttarān eka ahān asṛjata te sṛṣṭvā abruvan na vai svena ātmanā prabhavāma iti tebhyaḥ svātantryam prāyacchat  tathā ca te prābhavan tad  yathā vā idam agneḥ  jāta āt  adhyagnayaḥ  vihriyante evam vā etasmāt  yajñād anye yajña kratavaḥ  vihriyante yaḥ  vai trivṛt  anyam yajña kratum āpadyate sa tam dīpayati yaḥ pañcadaśam sa tam yaḥ saptadaśam sa tam ya ekaviṃśam sa tam iti evam āhuḥ  ekaḥ  yajña iti ete vai sarve jyotiṣṭomāḥ bhavanti iti evam vaikṛtānām saṃkīrtanāt  teṣām eva vāda iti gamyate katham atha anyena iti yaḥ  asau   anyaḥ tatra prākṛtān dharmān vihṛtān darśayati atas  manyāmahe yasya yatas  vihṛtiḥ tena anyena iti yadi  evam na tarhi tad vikārāṇām vādaḥ tatra na vihāraḥ  na āpattiḥ prakaraṇa ādibhiḥ te dharmā jyotiṣṭomasya yadi hi gavādayaḥ  vihriyeran prakaraṇa ādīni bādhyeran tad āpattiḥ pratyakṣa viruddhā praśaṃsā tu  eṣā āpatti vihāra abhāvāt atra ucyate yadi  api  āpatti vihārau na vidhīyete te tathā api ca udakena vidhīyete ye prakṛtau kartavyāḥ te ca udaka vacanāt  vikṛtau   api kartavyā gamyante tad āpatti vihārau   iva yatra bhavataḥ tena anyena iti gamyate na hi  akasmāt  praśaṃsā syāt  yaḥ  asau   anyaḥ sa katham anayā praśaṃsayā lakṣyeta iti evam arthā praśaṃsā ya etena aniṣṭvā atha anyena yajeta iti śrūyate tatra eṣaḥ  arthaḥ samadhigataḥ tad vikārāṇām vāda iti atha idānīm saṃdihyate kim eka stomakasya aneka stomakasya ca iti kim prāptam eka stomakasya vādaḥ kutas  kratu saṃyogāt  eka stome kratu saṃyogaḥ  bhavati yaḥ  vai trivṛt  anyam yajña kratum āpadyate sa tam dīpayati yaḥ pañcadaśam sa tam yaḥ saptadaśam sa tam ya ekaviṃśam sa tam trivṛt ādaya eka stomakāḥ tasmāt  teṣām vāda iti sarveṣām ca eṣa vādaḥ eka stomakānām aneka stomakānām ca kutas  aviśeṣa vacanāt  anya śabdasya nanu  eka stomakāḥ kratavaḥ saṃkīrtyante satyam saṃkīrtyante praśaṃsā artham na viśeṣa artham kaḥ punar  praśaṃsā arthaḥ yaḥ  vai trivṛt  anyam yajña kratum āpadyate sa tam dīpayati ca udaka prāptā dharmā abhyastāḥ prakṛtau vikṛtau sukham pratipadyante iha pāṭha kramasya śruti artha kramābhyām saha bādhām prati vicāraṇam kim pāṭha kramas tābhyām tulyaḥ uta bādhyata iti kim prāptam tulya balau   etau pāṭhaḥ  api hi kāraṇam śruti arthau   api na ca prāmāṇye kaścid  viśeṣaḥ  asti tasmāt  aniyama iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ pāṭha kramaḥ  hi bādhyate śrutyā arthena ca kutas  śruti viśeṣāt  artha paratvāt  ca śruti viśeṣaḥ kaḥ yatra śravaṇam tatra pratyakṣam kāraṇam pāṭha kramas tu  ānumānikaḥ pāṭha krameṇa smaraṇam evam abhinirvartayitavyam iti  avagamyate tasya arthavat tvena ekayā upapattyā tasya eva anuṣṭhānam śrutyā punar  anuṣṭhānam eva evam bhavati iti pratyakṣāt  avagamyate tathā arthena kutas  artha paratvāt  artha artham hi sarvam pradhāna artham pradhānam abhinirvartayati iti sarvam kriyate tasmāt  pāṭhas tābhyām bādhyate kim udāharaṇam prayojanam ca śrutyām āśvinaḥ  daśamaḥ  gṛhyate tam tṛtīyam juhoti atra pāṭha kramasya balīyaḥ tve tṛtīyasya grahaṇam siddhānte tu daśamasya arthe agnihotra homaḥ pūrvam āmnāyate paścāt  chrapaṇam evam kartavyam yadi pāṭhaḥ  balavān siddhānte śrapaṇam pūrvam tatas  homaḥ staḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau tatra pūrvam dadhnaḥ dharmāḥ samāmnātāḥ paścāt  āgneyasya pradānam ca āgneyasya pūrvam tatra saṃdehaḥ kim prāvṛttikena krameṇa pūrvam dadhnaḥ avadāna abhighāraṇa āsādanāni uta mukhya krameṇa pūrvam āgneyasya iti kim prāptam aniyama iti  evam prāpte brūmaḥ avadāna ādiṣu prāvṛttikena pūrvam dadhna iti kutas  evam anujñātebhyaḥ  vyavadhāyakebhyaḥ  na abhyadhikaḥ  anyaḥ  vā vyavadhāyakaḥ kalpitaḥ  bhaviṣyati darśayati ca dadhnaḥ pūrvam eva deyam iti yathā pradānam vā kartavyāni yasya pradānam pūrvam tasya avadānāni pūrvam tasmāt  āgneyasya kutas  pradāna codanā gṛhīta tvāt  avadāna ādīnām pradāna upakramā ete na pṛthak padārthā ete iti  uktam abhighāraṇam avadānam ca tasya pradāna cikīrṣayā eva kriyate āsādanam api pradāna artham eva āsan   akaraṇam evam dṛṣṭa artha tā bhavati tasmāt  mukhya krameṇa aṅgānām prayoga iti yad  tu dadhnaḥ pūrvam pravṛttiḥ  iti arthāt  pūrvam pravṛttiḥ na pāṭhāt  prāvṛttikā c ca mukhya kramaḥ  balīyān mukhya krame gṛhyamāṇe prathama  ekaḥ padārthaḥ  viprakṛṣṭa kālaḥ syāt  prāvṛttike punar  gṛhyamāṇe sarveṣām viprakarṣaḥ tasmāt  mukhya kramaḥ  balīyān iti atha yal liṅgam uktam dadhnaḥ pūrvam avadeyam iti atra ucyate śṛta abhiprāyam etad  bhaviṣyati tasmāt  adoṣaḥ liṅgam api  asmin   arthe bhavati sa vai dhruvām eva agre abhighārayati tatas  hi prathamauv ājya bhāgau yakṣyan bhavati iti tasmāt  api mukhya krameṇa niyama iti iṣṭi pūrva tvam samānātam tatra saṃdehaḥ kim iṣṭi pūrva tvam soma pūrva tvam vā vikalpaḥ athavā iṣṭi pūrva tvam eva iti kim prāptam iṣṭi pūrva tvam eva syāt  kutas  vacanāt  vacanam idam bhavati eṣa vai deva rathaḥ  yad  darśa pūrṇamāsau yaḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau   iṣṭvā somena yajate ratha spaṣṭa eva avasāne vare devānām avasyati iti na asti vacanasya ati bhāraḥ tasmāt  iṣṭi pūrva tvam eva iti iṣṭi pūrva tvam iti  etad  gṛhṇīmaḥ kim tu somaś ca ekeṣām pūraḥ darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ syāt  kutas  agni ādheyasya ṛtu nakṣatra atikrama vacanāt  yaḥ somena yakṣyamāṇaḥ  agnīn ādadhīta naṛtum sa pratīkṣet  na nakṣatram iti yaḥ soma yāgam kartum ādadhīt  sa na pratīkṣeta nakṣatram na api  ṛtum tāvatī  eva āt adhīta iti  ānantaryam ucyate itarathā ṛtu nakṣatra atikrama vacanam anarthakam syāt  ānantarye anapekṣyamāṇe yasya eva ṛtu nakṣatre ukte tasya eva tayoḥ  anādaraḥ kīrtitaḥ syāt  tasmāt  asti somādhānayoḥ  ānantaryam iti api ca vispaṣṭā cādyatanī vibhaktiḥ somena yakṣyamāṇa  iti sā ca na iṣṭi pūrva tvam anujñāya vivakṣyate na tadādyatana kāla vivakṣā tatra ayam śabdaḥ  vipratiṣidhyeta tasmāt  ānantarya vivakṣā iti  avagamyate itas  ca somādhānayoḥ  ānantaryam kutas  tad artha vacanāt  yaḥ somena yajeta sa agnim ādadhīta iti ca sarvaiḥ  api  asau yakṣyamāṇaḥ  agnim ādhatte somena agnihotra ādibhiḥ  ca na asati somasya viśeṣe soma artha tā syāt  ayam asau viśeṣaḥ syāt  yad  ānantaryam somādhānayoḥ  iti somena ayakṣyamāṇasya ca pavamāna haviṣām kālaḥ  nirdiśyate yaḥ somena ayakṣyaṃāṇaḥ  agnim ādadhīta sa purā saṃvatsarāt  dhavīṃṣi nirvapet  iti na khalu kaścid  ayakṣyamāṇaḥ sarvasya vihita tvāt  tasmāt  anantaram ayakṣyamāṇa  iti gamyate idam prayojana sūtram varṇyate kṣīṇam adhikaraṇam kim prayojanam cintāyāḥ iṣṭiḥ  ayakṣyamāṇasya somena nirabhisaṃdhika ādhāne tad artha tve tu soma pūrva tvam soma artha tāyām tu  ādhānasya soma pūrva tvam syāt  asti  ādhānam tatra eṣaḥ  arhaḥ samadhigataḥ iṣṭi pūrva tvam soma pūrva tvam ca iti idānīm saṃdehaḥ kim trayāṇām varṇānām iṣṭi pūrva tvam soma pūrva tvam vā uta brāhmaṇasya soma pūrva tvam eva uta kevalā paurṇamāsy utkṛṣyate brāhmaṇasya ubhau kalpau   iti atha vā karma antaram idam yad  ūrdhvam somāt  atha vā ekam havir utkṛṣyate brāhmaṇasya ubhāv eva kalpau   iti kim prāptam trayāṇām varṇānām iṣṭi pūrva tvam soma pūrva tvam vā kutas  aviṣeśāt  na kiṃcid  viśeṣam avagacchāmaḥ evam prāpte brūmaḥ brāhmaṇasya soma pūrva tvam syāt  kasmāt  utkarṣāt  utkarṣaḥ  hi śrūyate āgneyaḥ  vai brāhmaṇaḥ  devatayā sa somena iṣṭvā agnī somīyaḥ  bhavati yad  eva ādaḥ paurṇamāsam haviḥ tatra hi  anunirvapet  tarhi  ubhaya devatyaḥ  bhavati iti kim iva hi vacanam na kuryāt  tasmāt  brāhmaṇasya soma pūrva tvam eva iti yad  uktam brāhmaṇasya soma pūrva tvam eva iti tad  na tasya api  ubhau kalpau kutas  aviśeṣāt  na hi kalpayoḥ  brāhmaṇasya kaścid  viśeṣa āmnāyate nanu  idānīm eva uktam brāhmaṇasya utkarṣa iti na iti brūmaḥ paurṇamāsī mātrasya tatra utkarṣaḥ śruti saṃyogaḥ paurṇamāsya aḥ  tatra yad  eva ādaḥ paurṇamāsam havir iti yāvat  vacanam vācanikam tatra na nyāyaḥ kramate tulyayoḥ  eka deśa utkṛṣṭe nūnam aparaḥ  api  eka deśa utkṛṣyata iti yad  ucyate kevalā paurṇamāsy utkṛṣyata iti tad  na kṛtsnasya darśa pūrṇamāsa karmaṇa utkarṣaḥ evam phalena saṃbandhaḥ itarathā na syāt  phalam eka deśa tvāt paurṇamāsyāḥ kevalāyām utkṛṣyamāṇāyām avaśiṣṭasya pūrvatra kriyamāṇasya na phalam syāt  eka deśa tvāt aphala tvāt  ca uktam api na kriyeta samudāye ca utkṛṣyamāṇe bhavati phalam tasmāt  arthāt  samudāyasya utkarṣaḥ evam kṛtsnā upadeśaḥ  arthavān bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt  sarvasya utkarṣaḥ soma pūrva tvam eva brāhmaṇasya iti na etad  asti yad  evam samudāyasya asati vacana utkarṣaḥ parikalpyeta tasmāt  anyat  eva evam nāmakam karma ūrdhvam somāt  syāt  evam eka deśasya aśrutam phalam na kalpayitavyam bhaviṣyati nāmadheyam tu dvayoḥ karmaṇoḥ  ekam akṣāḥ pādāḥ māṣā iti yathā paurṇamāsa dharmakam vā karma antaram codyata iti karma vidhānam śruteḥ  etad  bhavati tad  vākyasya bādhakam tasmāt  karma antaram iti karma antarasya etad vācakam iti pramāṇa abhāvaḥ prakṛtasya karmaṇaḥ  vācakam iti pratyakṣam yad  ca sa pramāṇakam tad  grāhyam anyāyaḥ  ca aneka artha tvam dharma grahaṇe lakṣaṇā śabdaḥ śruti saṃbhave kalpyaḥ syāt  api ca asya rūpam na gamyate rūpāvacanān na karma antaram tasmāt  prasiddhena nāmnā prakṛtasya karmaṇaḥ  grahaṇam kāla vidhāna artham syāt  phalavattva at  ca kṛtsnasya utkarṣaḥ brāhmaṇasya ca tathā eva yad  tu śrutiḥ  vākyāt  balīyasi iti atra ucyate yatra phalam na śrūyate vākya arthaḥ  api tāvat  tatra gṛhyate na ca iha phalasya śravaṇam asti kalpyam phalam iti yad  ucyate na tad  phala vacanam antareṇa tatra phala vacanaḥ śabdaḥ kalpyeta tena ca saha eka vākyatā kāla vacanena tu saha pratyakṣeṇa ekavākyatā iti tasmāt  na karma antaram sthitam tāvat  aparyavasitam adhikaraṇam yaḥ somena yakṣyamāṇaḥ  agnim ādadhīta naṛtum sa pratīkṣet  na nakṣatram iti atra saṃdehaḥ kim ādhānasya ayam kāla viśeṣa bādhaḥ uta somasya iti kim prāptam ādhānasya kāla bādhaḥ sva kāle syāt  somaḥ kutas  avipratiṣedhāt  aṅgam ādhānam tasya kāla bādhaḥ nyāyyaḥ na pradhānasya aṅga guṇa virodhe ca tādarthyād iti vakṣyate apanayaḥ  vā ādhānāt  soma kālasya syāt  kutas  ādhānasya sarva kāla tvāt na eva ādhāne kaścid  kāla niyamaḥ  asti yad  ahar eva enam śraddhā upanamet  tad  ahar ādadhīta iti aprāptam eva tad  ādhānasya yad  pratiṣidhyate tasmāt  somasya kāla bādha iti sthitāt  uttaram na vaitat  asti kṛtsnau darśa pūrṇamāsau   utkṛṣyete ūrdhvam somāt  kevalā paurṇamāsy utkṛṣyate kutas  vacanāt  vacanam idam yad  eva ādaḥ paurṇamāsam havis tad  tarhi  anunirvapet  iti na asti vacanasya ati bhāraḥ tasmāt  paurṇamāsī mātram utkṛṣyeta yad  tu phalam na asti iti samudāyāt  eva phalam bhaviṣyati iti vacanāt  evam vijñānāt  tasmāt  adoṣaḥ ekam vā havir utkṛṣyeta na kṛtsnā paurṇamāsī kutas  śabda sāmarthyāt  ekam havir utkraṣṭum śabdaḥ samarthaḥ yad  eva ādaḥ paurṇamāsam havir iti śrūyate yāvat  vacanam vācanikam tāvat  vacanena utkraṣṭum śakyate na anyat  api prāk  somāt  kṛtsnam vidhīyate tatas  yad  vacanena utkṛṣyate tad  ūrdhvam somāt  yad  na utkṛṣyate tad  prāk  bhavitum arhati tasmāt  ekam havir utkraṣṭavyam brāhmaṇasya ubhau kalpau   iti idam śrūyate āgneyaḥ  vai brāhmaṇaḥ  devatayā sa somena iṣṭvā agnīṣomīyaḥ bhavati yad  eva ādaḥ paurṇamāsam havis tad  tarhi  anunirvapet  tarhi  ubhaya devatyaḥ  bhavati iti yasmāt  tasmin kāle saḥ  agnīṣomīyaḥ bhavati na prācīne kāle tasmāt  adaḥ  havir anunirvapet  iti agnīṣomīyatvam vidhāya dvi devatāka tvam hetu tvena nirdiśyate tasmāt  agnīṣomīyam havir hetumat  syāt  na anya devatākam tadā asau   agnīṣomau yaṣṭum arhati na prāk  sā asya devatā iti bhavati puruṣasya api yaṣṭuḥ  devatā abhisaṃbandhaḥ tasmāt  puroḍāśaḥ  agnīṣomīyaḥ na anyat  dhaviḥ  iti siddham iti ced  paśyasy agnīṣomīyatvāt  puroḍāśa iti ājyam api hi  agnīṣomīyam tasmāt  tad  api  utkṛṣyeta miśradevatam hi  ājyam agnīṣomīyam prājāpatyam vaiṣṇavam iti ca puroḍāśa s tu  agnīṣomīya eva na tu  atra miśra devatasya vādaḥ miśra devatasya hi prāk  api bhāvaḥ avakalpyate yad  api tadānīm yajamānaḥ  na agniṣomīyas tad devatā arhaḥ tathā api  ājyam haviḥ kariṣyati  eva prajāpatim yakṣyati viṣṇum vā tasmāt  tasya ūrdhva bhāve na eṣa hetuḥ  agnīṣomīyatvam nāma yathā caturdhā karaṇam miśra devata tvāt  aindra agnena bhavati tadvat  tatra āgneya iti aindrāgnaḥ  na śakyate vaditum tad  dhitaḥ sa ākāṅkṣān na utpadyata iti evam iha agnīṣomīya śabdena na śakyam ājyam vaditum agnīṣomīyaḥ hi asau tasmāt  chakyam prāk  yajamānena kartum iti tasmāt  na tasya utkarṣe agnīṣomīyatā yajamānasya hetuḥ  iti miśra devatasya grahaṇa sāmānyāt  aindra agnavat  iti  uktam iha vaikṛtāni karmāṇi  udāharaṇam aindrāgnam ekādaśa kapālam nirvapet  iti evamādīni tatra saṃdehaḥ kim etā vikṛtayaḥ sadyaskālāḥ uta dvi ahakālā iti kim prāptam vikṛtiḥ prākṛtān dharmān   ca udakena gṛhṇāti atas te dharmā ānumānikāḥ paurṇamāsī ca anyaḥ kālaḥ sa yadi vā prakṛtyā gṛhyeta yadi vā vikṛtyā asaṃbhave anyatarasyāḥ kālas tyaktavyaḥ tatra anumānikaḥ  vaikṛtasya tyajyatām na pratyakṣa śrutaḥ prākṛtasya iti nyāyyam tasmāt  sadyaskālā etā vikṛtayaḥ bhaveyuḥ  iti dvaiyahakālye kriyamāṇe yathānyāyam kṛtam bhavati tasmāt  dvaiyaha kālyam syāt  ca udakaḥ  tathā anugṛhītaḥ  bhavati prakṛtau hi śrūyate pūrvedyus  agnim gṛhṇāti uttaram ahar devatām yajati iti tasmāt  dvi ahakālam ekam abhinirvartyam tad ahar eva upakramya aparedyus  parisamāpayet  na etad  evam dvi ahakālā vikṛtayaḥ bhaveyuḥ  iti sadyaskālāḥ syuḥ kasmāt  vacanam idam bhavati iṣṭyā paśunā somena āgrayaṇena vā yakṣyamāṇaḥ sa paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāyām vā yajeta iti sāṅgasya etad  vacanam tasmāt  sa aṅgam paurṇa māsyām amāvāsyāyām vā kurvīta iti gamyate tena sadyaskālā vikṛtayaḥ iha sāṃnāyya vikārāḥ  ca agnīṣomīya vikārāś ca udāharaṇam sāṃnāyya vikāra aḥ  tāvat  yathā āmikṣā paśuḥ  iti agnīṣomīyam ekādaśa kapālam nirvapet  chyāmākam brāhmaṇaḥ  vasante brahmavarcaskāma iti  evamādyaḥ tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ete prāk  ūrdhvam ca somāt  uta ūrdhvam iti kim prāptam prāk  ūrdhvam ca viśeṣān avagamāt evam prāpte brūmaḥ ūrdhvam somād syuḥ  iti prakṛtiḥ  hi  eṣām ūrdhvam somāt  ca udakena ebhiḥ  api ūrdhvam somāt  bhavitavyam sānnāyyasya ūrdhvam somāt  vacanena asoma yājī saṃnayet  iti agnīsomīyasya api āgneyaḥ  vai brāhmaṇaḥ  devatayā sa somena iṣṭvā bhavati yad  eva ādaḥ paurṇamāsam haviḥ tad  tarhi  anunirvapet  iti tarhi sa ubhaya devatyaḥ  bhavati iti tad vikṛtiḥ  api somād ūrdhvam bhavitum arhati soma vikārā gavādaya eka ahāḥ teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim darśa pūrṇamāsāt  prāk  ūrdhvam ca prayoktavyāḥ uta ūrdhvam iti kim prāptam aniyamaḥ aviśeṣāt  evam prāpte brūmaḥ tathā soma vikārāḥ darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām ūrdhvam syuḥ jyotiṣṭomaḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām ūrdhvam bhavati darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām iṣṭvā somena yajeta iti ca udakena eṣa dharmaḥ  gavā ādiṣu  api  eka aheṣu prāpnoti tasmāt  te api darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām ūrdhvam kartavyā iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate  yad āgneyaḥ  aṣṭākapālaḥ  amāvāsyāyām paurṇamāsyām vācuyataḥ  bhavati iti tatra yadi dvi avadāna mātram uddhṛtam vyāpadyate kim śeṣāt  punar  avadeyam na iti bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim prāptam dvi avadāna nāśe śeṣāt  punar  avadeyam kutas  tad artha tvāt agni artham hi tad  dhaviḥ agnaye yāgaḥ  nirvartayitavya iti tad avadāne vinaṣṭe yāgaḥ kartavya eva avatiṣṭhate prayojanam ca yāgena sa ca āgneyena kriyamāṇaḥ śruta eva abhinirvartitaḥ  bhavati iti kim iti na kriyeta tasmāt  cheṣāt  avadātavyam iti atha vānyat  dhaviḥ  āgamayet  na śeṣāt  avadātavyam kutas  nirdeśāt  nirdeśaḥ  hi bhavati madhyāt  pūrva ardha āt  avadeyam iti dvi avadānam ca homa saṃbaddham dvi avadānam juhoti iti tatra anya c chiṣṭam madhyasya pūrva ardhasya viśeṣaṇa artham yad  ca tad  dhoma saṃyuktam tad vinaṣṭam tad  cheṣeṇa kriyamāṇam amadhyena apūrva ardhena ca kṛtam syāt  nanu  avatte yad  chiṣṭam tatas  madhyāt  pūrva ardhāt  ca grahīṣyate ucyate kṛtsnasya yad  madhyam pūrva ardham ca tad  coditam na itarasya atha vā nirdeśāt  iti vinaṣṭe hi  anyat  dravyam nirdiśyate yasya sarvāṇi havīṃṣi naśyeyuḥ  duṣyeyuḥ  vā apahareyuḥ  vā ājyena tā devatāḥ parisaṃkhyāya yajeran   iti haviṣaḥ  nāśa ājyam prāptam tena na śeṣāt  avadātavyam iti apara āha śeṣa nirdeśāt  iti nirdiśyate hi tad  chiṣṭam aparebhyaḥ śeṣa kāryebhyaḥ  iti tad  na upapadyate na hi tāni śeṣa kāryāṇi havīṃṣi prayojayanti na ca anivṛtta prayojanam havir anyatra pratipādyam tasmāt  na ayam arthaḥ atha sviṣṭakṛt  artham avattam yadi vinaśyati tatra kim śeṣāt  avadeyam uta na iti kim prāptam punar  śeṣāt  avadeyam iti kutas  na atra kṛtsnasya uttara ardhāt  avadīyate kasya tarhi saṃnihitasya sati hi prayojane saṃnihitasya avadeyam iti tasmāt  avadīyamāne śrutam kṛtam bhavati tasmāt  śeṣāt  avadeyam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ śeṣa bhājām syāl lopaḥ kutas  viśiṣṭa kāraṇāt viśiṣṭam hi kāraṇam tasya avadāne katham pratipādyeta iti pratipattiḥ  ca vivikta karaṇena upakaroti tasya vivikta karaṇāya pratipādyamānasya niyamaḥ  ayam sviṣṭakṛt  dhomena pratipādayitavyaḥ tathā hi sa pratipāditaḥ  bhavati sa yadi homāya uddhṛtaḥ  vipadyeta kṛte viveke na punar  grahaṇam prayojayet  pratipādyamānaḥ  ca sviṣṭakṛt  dhomena pratipādayitavya iti pratipādyamāna abhāvāl lopa eva sviṣṭakṛtaḥ syāt  pradhāne kṛte śiṣṭam sarva śeṣa kārya sādhāraṇam tatra ekasya uddhṛtau śiṣṭam anyatra pratipādanīyam staḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau tatra bhakṣāḥ prāśitra caturdhā karaṇa śaṃyuvāka kālāḥ teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim anya eva teṣām bhakṣayitāraḥ uta prakaraṇa gatā iti kim prāptam śeṣa bhakṣaḥ  anyaiḥ  aprakaraṇa sthaiḥ kartavyaḥ kutas  nirdeśāt  nirdiśyante hi  adhvarya ādaya iḍā bhakṣe yajamāna pañcamā iḍām bhakṣayanti iti sarveṣu bhakṣayitṛṣu prāpteṣu parisaṃkhyāna arthaḥ  nirdeśaḥ kriyate iḍām eva ete bhakṣayeyuḥ  iti yathā āgneyaḥ  aṣṭākapāla iti sarvasmin   avayavini yāga aniyame prāpte dvi avadāna mātram śrūyate vidhiḥ  vā na prāpta tvāt  na anuvādaḥ  anarthaka tvāt  parisaṃkhyā tu  arthavat tāya evam eṣām parisaṃkhyā iti api ca yadi prakṛtā eva bhakṣayeyuḥ aśvamedhe doṣaḥ syāt  bahu tvāt  bhakṣāṇām bhakṣayantaḥ  mriyeran sarvaiḥ  vā prakṛtaiḥ  eva bhakṣyeta tad  dhi bhakṣaṇam puruṣa saṃskāra artham puruṣāḥ saṃskṛtāḥ pracariṣyanti iti teṣu vinigamanāyāḥ  abhāvāt  yāvantaḥ prakaraṇe samavetāḥ te sarve bhakṣayeyuḥ  iti atha yad  uktam nirdeśāt  iti guṇa arthaḥ saḥ anye karma kara tvāt  eva prāptāḥ tatra yajamānaḥ  teṣām pañcamaḥ  vacanāt  nirdiśyate tad prāpti artham ca idam vacanam tatas  na parisaṃkhyā yad  tu dvi avadāna mātram pradhāne nirdiśyate tad  vacana prāmāṇyāt  parisaṃkhyāna artham na hi tatra kasyacid  apūrvasya vidhiḥ iha yajamānaḥ  vidhīyate vidhi parisaṃkhyā saṃśaye vidhiḥ  jyāyān tatra sva arthe śabdaḥ parisaṃkhyāyām trayaḥ  doṣāḥ sva artha hānam asva artha parigrahaḥ prāpta bādhaḥ  ca iti tasmāt  prākṛtā eva bhakṣayeyuḥ  iti atha yad  uktam aśvamedhe virodhaḥ syāt  bahu tvāt  bhakṣāṇām iti tad  parihartavyam aśvamedhe na sarvam bakṣayiṣyanti arthāt  sarvam bhakṣayantaḥ  aśvamedham na samāpayeyuḥ tatra aśvamedha śrutiḥ pratyakṣā sā virudhyamānā ca udaka prāptam sarva bhakṣaṇam bādhate prakṛtau tu na virodhaḥ tasmāt  sarvam prakṛtā bhakṣayeyuḥ  iti staḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsau tatra āmananti bhinne juhoti skanne juhoti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim kṛtsne bhinne skanne ca prāyaścittam uta eka deśe api bhinne skanne ca iti kim punar  sarva bhinnam kim eka deśa bhinnam iti cūrṇīkṛtam ayogyam prayojanāya kṛtsna bhinnam yad  chakale vigate api prayojana samartham tad  eka deśa bhinnam iti kim prāptam eka deśa bhinne api prāyaścittam kasmāt  artha samavāyāt  samavetam tatra bhedanam eka deśa bhinnam api bhinnam iti evam prāpte nimitte naimittikam kartavyam bhavati tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na aśeṣe bhinne prāyaścittam syāt  vinaṣṭa saṃskāra artham hi prāyaścittam kutas  etad  bhedanavatā prayojanam asti na homena tena saṃskṛtena prayogaḥ kariṣyanta iti prāyaścittam kriyate na ca tena cūrṇīkṛtena prayogaḥ śakyate kartum tasmāt  prāyaścittam anarthakam eka deśa bhinnena tu saṃskṛtena śakyate prayogaḥ tasmāt  eka deśa bhinne prāyaścittam syāt  iti syāt  vā prāyaścittam kṛtsna bhinne api kutas  prāpta nimitta tvāt  prāptam hi nimittam bhedanam prāpte ca nimitte naimittikam kartavyam yad  ca uktam vyāpanna saṃskāra artham prāyaścittam iti na ayam tasya dharmaḥ kutas  nitya saṃyogāt  nityavat  dhomaḥ anityam hi bhedanam na hi nityam anityasya upakartum codyate yadi nityam darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  aṅgam na anityasya upakārāya kutas  kadācid  anityam na eva syāt  tatra katham tasya upakārakam bhavet  tatra kaḥ  doṣaḥ na śakyam nityena upakartum tena nityam upakuryāt  iti vacanam pralāpa eva atha naimittikam na doṣaḥ  bhavati tasmāt  asmad pakṣa eva asmin pakṣe yadā bhinnam tadā homaḥ yadā na bhinnam tadā na eva homaḥ  vidhīyate bhavadīye pakṣe bhavati doṣaḥ nitya anityayoḥ  na asti saṃbandha iti tasmāt  bhinna mātre prāyaścittam iti asti vacane na guṇa u guṇa arthaḥ  bhavitum arhati prakaraṇataḥ sarvam pradhāna artham bhinnam api homaḥ  api na ca bhinnam ādhāra bhāvena upadiśyate bhinnasya ādhāra bhāve hi na homa antaram vidhīyeta pradhānasya eva hi tadā bhinnaḥ guṇa iti gamyate tatra āhavanīya saṃyogaḥ  bādhyeta vacanāt  vikalpa iti ced  na nimitta tvena saṃbhavāt  homasya ca śrutyā vihita tvāt  yadā homaḥ  vidhīyate tadā śrutyā yadā bhinnaḥ guṇaḥ tadā vākyena tasmāt  na ādhāraḥ  bhinnaḥ
