tatra anyatara anugamane na śakyata eka eva ādhātum viguṇam syāt  atha dvitīyam api  ādadhīta sa yadi tāvat  āhavanīyaḥ tatra āhavanīyaḥ  anyaḥ  homa arthaḥ  vidyata eva iti na sa homāya syāt  yaḥ  ca homa artham utpādyate sa āhavanīyaḥ yata eṣa saṃskāra śabdaḥ saṃskāra śabdaḥ  ca ekena api saṃskāreṇa vinā na bhavati eṣaḥ  api ca saṃskāraḥ yad  dhomārtha tā yad  āhavanīye juhoti iti śrūyate tad  ekasmin   anugate ekasmin   ādhīyamāne vaiguṇyam dvayoḥ  api hi vaiguṇyam eva tasmāt  na ekasmin   anugate punar ādheyam aśakya tvāt  iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate yasya ubhayam havir ārtim ārcchet  aindram pañcaśara avam odanam nirvapet  iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim haviṣy ārte pañca śarāvaḥ pratinidhiḥ uta nimitte karma antaram iti katham pratinidhiḥ katham karma antaram iti yadi  evam abhisaṃbandhaḥ  bhavati pañca śarāvam nirvapet  kuyād iti tatas  sāṃnyāyasya kārye pañca śarāvaḥ pratinidhiḥ  iti atha na pañca śarāvaḥ  nirvapatinā kim tu devatayā saṃbadhyate pañca śarāvam aindram kuryāt  iti tatas  nimitte yajatiḥ  vidhīyate kim tāvat  prāptam pañca śarāvas tu dravya śruteḥ pratinidhiḥ syāt  pañca śarāvaḥ sāṃnyāyyasya pratinidhiḥ kutas  dravya śruteḥ dravyasya nirvāpe śravaṇam na indra saṃbandhaḥ kutas  evam nirvāpa vidhiḥ  bhaviṣyati tatra śrutiḥ  vidhāyikā itarathā dravya devatā saṃbandhe vākyam syāt  tad  ca durbalam śruteḥ tasmāt  pratinidhiḥ  iti nimitte vā yajatiḥ karma ānataram dravya devatā vidhiḥ dravya devatam iha śrūyate pañca śarāvam aindram kuryāt  iti itarathā hi  aindram iti pramāda pāṭhaḥ  avagamyeta aindra māha indrayoḥ  vā ayatha artha anuvāda aindram iti syāt  avācye hi te devate aindra śabdena indraḥ  mahā indraḥ  ca na śakyaḥ  anuvaditum viśeṣaṇa tve vākya bhedaḥ nanu śrutiḥ  balīyasi iti  uktam satyam evam kim tu  itarasmin pakṣe bādhyatetarām śrutiḥ aindra śabdasya atantra tvāt sa eṣa naimittikaḥ  yāgaḥ kim amāvāsyām pratyāmanet  na iti kim prāptam sa pratyāmanet  sthānāt  sa eṣa yāgaḥ  amāvāsyām pratyāmnātum arhati kutas  sthānāt  yāge vinaṣṭe yāga eṣa śrūyamāṇaḥ  yadi na naṣṭasya aṅgam tatas  arthavān bhavati atha aṅgam niṣprayojanasya artham kriyamāṇam niṣprayojanam eva bhavitum arhati viguṇam ca niṣprayojanam eva vinaṣṭam āmauvāsyam iti pratyakṣam idam api kartavyam iti śābdam yad  vinaṣṭam tad  niṣphalam iti na kartavyam idam ca kartavyam iti pratyāmnāya u avagamyate aṅgam vaitat  vidhīyate haviṣy ārtau nimitte yāgaḥ śrūyate tatra trayam āpatati yad  vā nimitte svatantram kalpyam phalam yad  vā amāvāsyāyā yad  kāryam tad  asya yad  vā tasya aṅgam iti sva pradhānam tāvan na kalpya tvāt  phalasya na amāvāsyāyāḥ kārye kim kāraṇam aśravaṇāt  na evam śrūyate tasyāḥ kārye vartata iti kartavyā upadeśena api na anyatama adhyavasānam triṣu  eṣu pakṣeṣu teṣu ca pakṣeṣu vivakṣiteṣu kartavyā upadeśaḥ  avakalpyate nanu  evam abhisaṃbandhaḥ  bhaviṣyati yasya ubhayam havir ārtim ārcchet  sa etena yāgena sādhayet  yad  sādhayitu kāmaḥ kim ca asau sādhayitu kāmaḥ yad  amāvāsyāyāḥ phalam iti atra ucyate phala padena saṃbandha abhāvāt  saṃbandhasya vidhāyakam vākyam śrutyā ca yāga kartavyatā vidhīyate sā ca vākyāt  balīyasī tasmāt  na tad kārye vartata iti kim tarhi prayojanam tasyāḥ  amāvāsyāyāḥ  aṅgam nanu  etad  api na asti tasyāḥ  aṅgam iti atra ucyate tad saṃbandhena samāmnānāt  tad prayoga vacanena gṛhyate darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām phalam sādhayet  sarvaiḥ  aṅgaiḥ saha asyām ca ārtau   eṣa yāga itikartavyatā iti tasmāt  evam avagamyate vinaṣṭe haviṣy āmāvāsyam yad  na śaknoti sva kāryam kartum tad  anayā itikartavya tayā sahitam śaknoti iti tasmāt  nimitte karma aṅgam iti etad  āmnāyate sarvābhyaḥ  vā eṣa devatābhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pṛṣṭhebhyaḥ ātmānam āgurate yaḥ sarvatrāyāgurate viśvajitā atirātreṇa sarva pṛṣṭhena sarva vedasa dakṣiṇena yajeta sarva abhya eṣa devatābhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pṛṣṭhebhyaḥ ātmānam niṣkrīṇīta iti sarvatra agoraṇe nimitte viśvajit  chrūyate tatra saṃdehaḥ kim sarvatra āgūrya yaḥ sarvatram prayuṅkte tasya viśva jit  uta yaḥ  na prayuṅkte tasya iti kim tāvat  prāptam yaḥ  ca prayuṅkte yaḥ  ca na iti  aviśeṣāt  athavā prayuñjānasya kutas  nimitte karma aṅgam evaṃjātīyakam iti  uktam tad  aprayujyamānasya katham aṅgam syāt  iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ viśva jit  tu  apravṛtte bhavet  sarvasya kriyāyāḥ  abhāve viśva jit  kim kāraṇam evam hi śrūyate yaḥ satrāya agurate sa viśvajitā atirātreṇa yajeta iti yaḥ satram kariṣyāmi iti  evam āgurate sa viśvajitā yāgena sādhayet  iti yad  artham asau satram kartum icchati tad  artham iti gamyate katham ya āgurate sa tena yajeta yāgena nirvartayet  iti vākya arthaḥ  gamyate na yāgam nirvartayet  iti kutas  yāgasya guṇa tvena śravaṇāt  katham tasya guṇa tvam tṛtīyā nirdeśāt prādhānye hi phalam kalpyeta itarasmin   tu pakṣe pratyakṣāt  vākyāt  phala avagamaḥ evam tatra śrūyate sarvābhyaḥ  vā eṣa devatābhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pṛṣṭhebhyaḥ  yad  ātmānam niṣkrīṇīta iti niṣkraya dvāreṇa ca saṃstavaḥ pravṛtte na yujyate tasmāt  apravṛtte viśva jit  iti atha kasmān na evam abhisaṃbandhaḥ kriyate āgūrya satrāya viśvajitā yajeta iti viśvajitaḥ satrasya ca saṃbandhaḥ  vijñāyeta āgoraṇa velāyām iti na evam āgoraṇa viśeṣaṇam hi satram satra viśva jit saṃbandhe vyavahita kalpanā syāt  śrutiḥ  ca puruṣeṇa viśvajitam saṃbandhayati viśvajitā yajeta puruṣa iti na satreṇa satrasya viśva jit  yāga iti āgūrya iti ca evam śravaṇam arthavat  bhavati satra aṅga tve tu  artha prāptam na vaktavyam na ca āgūrya yajeta iti  āgoraṇa ānantaryam śakyam vidhātum aśabda arthaḥ  hi tadā aśrīyeta samāna kartṛka tā hi śabdavatī pūrva kāla bhāvasya ca artha prāpta tvāt  na vaktavyatā tasmāt  āgūrya iti  atra eva viśvajitaḥ saṃbandhaḥ sa ced  āgūrya na satreṇa yajeta tasya viśva jit  iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate barhiṣā vai paurṇamāse vratam upayanti vatsena amāvāsyāyām iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim vatsa sādhanakam vratam vidhīyate uta vratasya kāla iti atha vatsaḥ  vrata aṅgam iti kim prāptam vatsa sādhanakam vratam vidhīyata iti amāna asyāyām vatsaiḥ  vratam kuryāt  iti vatsa vrata saṃyogaḥ  apūrvaḥ sa vidhīyate tasmin   ca vidhīyamāna ubhayam api vihitam bhavati vatsaḥ  vratam ca yathā uktasya vacana antareṇa prāptasya kālaḥ  ayam vidhīyate kutas  utpanna saṃyogāt  utpanna saṃyogaḥ  ayam vratasya na utpatti saṃyogaḥ katham amāṣam māṃsam bahu sarpiṣkam vratam vratayanti iti vihitam pūrvam vratam aprajñātaḥ  ca kālaḥ tasmāt  kāla vidhiḥ  iti na ca śakyaḥ  atra arthaḥ parimātum vatsena vratam upayanti iti kim vatsaḥ  atra vratayitavya evam vatsena vratam upagatam bhavati kim vatsena hasta sthānīyena vratayitavyam iti  evam tad  upetam bhavati uta vatsam saṃnidhāya tad  upeyāt  iti na eva vyavatiṣṭhate śāstra arthaḥ karaṇam hi  etad  nirdiṣṭam na itikartavyatā etāvat  uktam vatsa sādhanam vratam kuryāt  katham iti  etad  aviśeṣa ākāṅkṣam eva avatiṣṭheta na eva arthaḥ paricchidyate vrate kim vatsena kriyata iti athavā yad  vā tad  vā iti tathā vatsaḥ  vratena saṃbadhyamāna iṣṭaḥ syāt  apara artha tām āpadyeta parārtha tām ca asya dyotayati vibhakti s tṛtīyā sādhakatame hi sā bhavati tasmāt  api kāla arthaḥ saṃyogaḥ yad  uktam vihita tvāt  vratasya anuvāda iti satyam etad  yad  uktam kāla vidhāna artha iti tad  na vatsas tad aṅga tvena vidhīyate kutas  śruti saṃyogāt  vatse aṅge vidhīyamāne śrutiḥ  nimittam kāle lakṣaṇa śabdaḥ syāt  śruti lakṣaṇa aviśaye ca śrutiḥ  nyāyyā tasmāt  aṅgam vatsya iti kālas tu  eṣa nirdiśyate na vatsaḥ  aṅgam vidhīyate na eṣa codanā barhiṣā vai paurṇamāse vratam upayanti vatsena amāvāsyāyām iti katham avagamyate vidhinā eka vākya tvāt parastāt  ca vidhiḥ samāmnāyate purā vatsānām upākartoḥ  daṃpatī aśrīyatām iti yadi  eṣaḥ  api vidhiḥ syāt  vākyam bhidyeta anuvādaḥ  ca tathābhūtasya arthasya bhavati na ca vatsa aṅga tā aprāptā aprāpta s tu kālaḥ na ca śakyaḥ  vatsaḥ  atra vratayitum karma saṃyoge vatsena na arthaḥ śakyate kaścid  kartum tasmāt  api na vatsaḥ  aṅgam na ca etad  ucyate viśvasya śrapitam vatsam vratayiṣyata iti na ca asya arthasya sva śabdaḥ śrūyate vatsa iti  ākṛti śabdaḥ  māṃse na vartate tasmāt  eṣa kāla iti kāla arthaḥ saṃyoga iti  etad  samadhigatam idānīm saṃdehaḥ kim saṃnayat pakṣa eva kālaḥ uta asaṃnayataḥ  api iti kim prāptam saṃnayat pakṣe kutas  evam śrūyate purā vatsānām apākartoḥ  iti na ca asaṃnayataḥ  vatsa apākaraṇam asti tasmāt  saṃnayat pakṣa eṣa kālaḥ apākaraṇam liṅgam iti vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na saṃnayat pakṣa eva asaṃnayataḥ  api  eṣa kālaḥ syāt  kutas  kāla artha tvāt na vatsa apākaraṇena vrate kiṃcid  prayojanam asti kālena tu prayojanam yena ca tatra prayojanam sa lakṣyate katham punar  vatsa apākaraṇam kāla artham iti para artha tvāt  payase hi te apākriyante tathā hi dṛṣṭa artha tā bhavati itaratha adṛṣṭa artha tā syāt  tasmāt  na upādeya tvena vatsa apākaraṇam śrūyata iti yad  tu uktam tad liṅga saṃyogāt saṃnayat pakṣa eva iti tad  na asaṃnayataḥ  api kāla āhānāt yasya api na sāṃnāyyam tasya api vatsa apākaraṇam eva na syāt  na tu vatsa apākaraṇa kālaḥ  api kālena ca naḥ prayojanam na vatsa apākaraṇena yathā śaṅkha velāyām āgantavyam iti yasmin   api grāme śaṅkhaḥ  na adhmāyate tasmin   api sa tathākālaḥ  asti iti na āgamanam parihāsyate evam iha api  asati  api vatsa apākaraṇe tad kāle bhidyamāne vratam tasmin kāle na parihāsyata iti darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti tatra śrūyate saha śākhayā prastaram praharati iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim śākhā prastarasya aṅga bhūtā aṅga prayojana saṃbandha s tayoḥ atha kāla arthaḥ saṃyogaḥ prastara praharaṇa kāle śākhā prahartavyā iti kim prāptam prastare śākhā śrayaṇavat  prastarasya aṅga bhūtā śākhā kutas  saha śākhayā prastaram praharati iti saha yukte apradhāne tṛtīyā vibhaktiḥ  bhavati sā ca śākhāyām tṛtīyā tasmāt  prastarasya śākhā guṇa bhūtā prastare ca dvitīyā saha yoge ca tṛtīyā tṛtīyā guṇataḥ dvitīyā pradhānataḥ nanu na śākhayā prastarasya kaścid  upakāraḥ kriyate satyam na dṛṣṭam kriyate kim tu  adṛṣṭam kriyate śrayaṇavat  yathā payasā maitrāvaruṇam śrīṇāti iti dvitīyā tṛtīyā saṃyogāt  adṛṣṭaḥ  ca upakāraḥ  gamyate evam iha api iti kāla vidhiḥ  vā syāt  kutas  ubhayoḥ  vidyamāna tvāt  prastaraḥ  tāvat  sruc dhāraṇa arthaḥ prāptaḥ  vidyate tasya praharaṇam api viśiṣṭe kāle vākya antareṇa vihitam tatas  śākhāyāḥ pratipādana artham tasya etad punarvacanam ucyate bhavatu prastarasya punarvacanam śākhā tu  atra vidhīyata iti ucyate ubhayoḥ  api vidyamāna tvāt  śākhā pūrvam vihitā vatsa apākaraṇa arthā idānīm punar  kim guṇa bhūtā codyate uta pratipādyata iti pratipādyamānāyām dṛṣṭam prayojanam deśa viyogāt  pracaritum avakāśaḥ syāt  yā yāvatī ca mātrā deśa antara saṃyogasya na dṛṣṭam kiṃcid  asti tasmāt  praharaṇam pratipattiḥ  tasyāḥ tasmāt  paratas  prayojana abhāvāt kāla niyamaḥ kriyate nanu tṛtīyā apradhānaḥ  bhavati sā ca śākhāyām atra ucyate yā asau śākhāyām tṛtīyā sā dvitīya arthe yā ca prastare dvitīyā sā tṛtīya arthe katham avagamyate saha yoge ekasmin kāla ubhayam api prahartavyam iti atra yasya nirjñātaḥ kālaḥ tasya anuvādaḥ yasya tu  anirjñātaḥ tasya vidhiḥ śākhāyāḥ  ca anirjñātaḥ prastarasya nirjñātaḥ tasya punar uccāraṇam anirjñāta artham tad  apradhānam itarasya uccāraṇam pradhānam prādhānyam ca dvitīya arthaḥ tatra tṛtīyā pārārthyam api tṛtīya arthaḥ tatra dvitīyā tasmāt  ayathārtham vibhakti vacanam na ca śākhayā prastarasya upakāraḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ kriyate kāṣṭam dahyamānasya tṛṇasya na upakāre vartate tṛṇam tu kāṣṭhasya upakuryāt tasmāt  na śākhā prastara arthā kim bhavati prayojanam yadi prastarasya guṇa bhūtā tathā api prastara prahāra kāle śākhā pratipādyata iti ucyate yadi prastarasya prahriyamāṇasya aṅga bhūtā śākhā tatas  vinā prastareṇa na prahartavyā bhavati atha aṅga bhūtā vinā api prastareṇa prahartavyā asmābhiḥ  uktam prastara kāle prahartavyā iti tasmāt  ca viprayoge syāt  tasmāt  eva kāraṇāt  prastara viprayoge api śākhāyāḥ praharaṇam syāt  iti yathā pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ tathā sati sāṃnyāyye sati  asati ca śākhā vidyata iti  upaveṣaḥ  sati ca asati ca syāt  yathā tu siddhāntaḥ tathā sāṃnyāyyapakṣe śākhā satī hi pratipādyata iti tatra eva upaveṣaḥ  na anyatra iti idam āmananti vi vā enam prajayā paśubhiḥ  ardhayati vardhayati  asya bhrātṛvyam yasya havir niruptam purastāt  candramā abhyudeti tredhā taṇḍulān vibhajet  ye madhyamāḥ syuḥ tān agnaye dātre puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālam nirvapet  ye sthaviṣṭhā as tān indrāya pradātre dadhaṃś carum ye kṣodiṣṭāḥ tān viṣṇave śipi viṣṭāya śṛte carum iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim kāla aparādhe yāga antaram idam codyate uta teṣu  eva prakṛteṣu karmasu nimitte devatā apanayana iti kim prāptam abhyudaye yaḥ kāla aparādhaḥ tatra ijyā codanā syāt  katham puroḍāśam agnaye dātre madhyamān kurvate ye sthaviṣṭhā as tān indrāya pradātre dadhani carum kuryāt  kṣodiṣṭhān viṣṇave śipiviṣṭāya iti yajati s tu phala bhoktṛ saṃyogāt  iti vidhānam gamyate yathā pañca śarāve dravya devatā saṃbandhena karma antaram gamyate yathā paśu kāma iṣṭyām yaḥ paśu kāmaḥ syāt  saḥ  amāvāsyāyām iṣṭvā vatsān apākuryāt  ye sthaviṣṭhāḥ tān agnaye sa nimate aṣṭākapālam nirvapet  ye madhyamāḥ tān viṣṇave śipi viṣṭāya śṛte carum ye aṇiṣṭhāḥ tān indrāya pradātre dadhaṃś carum iti evam iha api iti api ca na prakṛte dravye devatā śrūyte śṛte carum iti hi tatra bhavati vacanam na ca abhyudaya kāle śrapaṇam kṛtam asti tasmāt  karma antaram devatā apanayaḥ  vā kutas  vidyamāna tvāt  vidyante hi karmāṇi prakṛtāni teṣu vidyamāneṣu punar  devatā saṃbandhaḥ  haviṣaḥ  na upapadyate yasya anupapattyā yāgaḥ kalpyeta tasmāt  na yāga antaram teṣu  eva haviḥṣu devatā antarāṇi vidhīyante devatā apanaya sarūpa āḥ  cāmī śabdā bhavanti ye madhyamāḥ teṣām devatā antaram vidhīyate tatra dravyam prāptam aprāptā devatā vidhīyate katham punar  devatā vidhāna arthe na aneka guṇvidhāna doṣaḥ  jāyeta iti ucyate na eva atra anekaḥ  guṇa u vidhīyate kasmiṃścid  vākye taṇḍulān vibhajet  iti  atra tāvat  vibhāga mātram vidhīyate anyat  sarvam anūdyate tasmāt  adoṣaḥ ye madhyamāḥ teṣām agniḥ  devatā vidhīyate anyat  puroḍāśa ādi  anūdyate ye sthaviṣṭhāḥ teṣām dadhi sahitānām indraḥ  devatā asmin vākye vidhīyate tatra artha prāpte śrapaṇe sati caru tā saha saptamī arthena artha prāptena eva asmin vākye anūdyate ye kṣodiṣṭhāḥ teṣām śṛta sahitānām viṣṇuḥ śipiviṣṭaḥ  devatā vidhīyate anyat  sarvam anūdyate tasmāt  adoṣaḥ ātañcana abhyāsam ca darśayati katham evam śrūyate yadi bibhīyāt  abhimodeṣyati iti mahārātre havīṃṣi nirvapet  phalīkṛtaiḥ  taṇḍulaiḥ  upāsīta ardham dadhi havir ātañcana artham nidadhyāt  ardham na yadi  abhyudiyāt  anena atacya pracaret  yadi  u na brāhmaṇam bhojayet  iti yadi karma antaram upādeya tvena tadā taṇḍulā dadhi śṛtam ca tasmāl laukikāni  upādeyāni na hi  eṣa tadā prakṛtānām vyāpāraḥ tatra avinaṣṭe dadhani aparedyus  āmāvāsye kriyamāṇe vidyate dadhi iti na atañcanam āvarteta tasyām eva abhyudita iṣṭau dadhi vidyata iti na atañcanam syāt  atha nimitte devatā apanayaḥ tatas  tasmin dadhani caruḥ kṛta iti punar  āmāvāsye dohe ātañcanena kāryam evam ātañcana abhyāsasya darśanam devatā vidhāne yujyata iti atha yad  uktam yathā paśukāma iṣṭyām karma antaram yaḥ paśu kāmaḥ syāt  saḥ  amāvāsyām iṣṭvā vatsān apākuryāt  iti tad  parihartavyam tatra ucyate yuktam yad  tatra karma antara vidhānam kutas  apūrva tvāt  na tatra kaścid  pūrva prāptaḥ  yāgaḥ  vidyate saḥ  amāvāsyām iṣṭvā iti hi parisamāpte tasmin   idam ārabhyate tatra dravya devatā saṃyuktaḥ  nirvapati śabdaḥ  na antareṇa utsargam dravya devatayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ  vidyata iti yajatim gamayati na tu  iha evam iha hi yāgaḥ prakṛtaḥ  gamyate tasmin   eva vidyamānasya dravyasya devatā saṃbandha mātram vidhīyata iti na doṣaḥ  bhavati atha yad  upavarṇitam yathā pañca śarāve karma antaram vidhīyate evam iha api iti tad  parihartavyam iti atra ucyate yuktam pañca śarāve karma antaram duṣṭam hi tatra dravyam yasya devatā vidhīyate tatra avaśyam dravyam upādeya tvena codayitavyam tasmin   upādīyamāne devatā antare ca apūrvaḥ saṃbandhaḥ  vidhīyate tad  yāga antaram bhavati iti itarat  iha dravyam aduṣṭam tad  anūdya prakṛte yāge devatā vidhīyata iti  uktam tasmāt  adoṣa iti evam ced  paśyasi sāṃnyāyye api doṣaḥ tad  api hi  abhyudaye tad kāla apabhraṃśāt  duṣṭam iti na etad  evam pañca śarāve hi duṣṭam dravyam iha tādṛśam eva avatiṣthate nanu kāla apabhraṃśena duṣṭam na duṣyati aviśiṣṭam hi kāraṇam abhyudaye prāyaścitta vidhānam duṣṭe api  upapadyate kāla aparādhe aduṣṭe api tad  akāle hi  abhipravṛttasya śakyate devatā vidhānam na tu vinaṣṭasya atha yad  uktam na prakṛte dravye devatā śrūyate śṛte carum iti tatra bhavati vacanam na ca abhyudaya kāle śrapaṇam kṛtam asti iti tad  parihartavyam atra ucyate lakṣaṇa artheyam śṛtaśrutiḥ dharma lakṣaṇa arthā śṛte śṛta sahacarita dharmaka iti tasmin   eva abhyudaye saṃśayaḥ kim upāṃśu yāge api devatā apanayaḥ  bhavet  na iti kim prāptam upāṃśu yājaḥ  yathāprakṛti syāt  kasmāt  avacanāt  yathā amīṣu vacanam madhyamānām agnaye dātre puroḍāśāḥ sthaviṣṭhānām indrāya pradātre dadhani caruḥ kṣodiṣṭhānām viṣṇave śipi viṣṭāya śṛte caru iti na etad  upāṃśuyāje asti tasmāt  sa yathādevatam syāt  vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati upāṃśu yājasya apanayaḥ kena kāraṇena pravṛttyā akāle tantra pravṛttiḥ  devatā apanayasya kāraṇam kutḥ na hi  atra abhyudaye sati taṇḍulā vibhāga artham upādīyante kim tarhi abhyuditasya haviṣaḥ  vibhāga ucyate abhyudayena aparāhnasya iti katham avagamyate yasya abhyudiyāt  iti aviśeṣa śravaṇāt sarvasya eva hi  aparādhena abhyudeti aparādhaḥ  ca akāle tantra pravṛttiḥ evam ca sati na tad  dhavi s taṇḍulaiḥ śakyam viśeṣṭum tasmāt  upāṃśu yāgasya api vibhāgaḥ tredhā taṇḍulān vibhajet  iti hi  anena vākyena devatā apanayaḥ kriyate vidhiḥ  hi  atra vibhajet  iti vibhāgam kuryāt  iti  arthaḥ katham iti vibhāge viśeṣa parāṇi  uttarāṇi vākyāni idam idam ca dravyam asyai devatāyai idam idam ca asyā iti yasya dravyasya viśeṣa vibhāgaḥ  na asti tasya api vibhajet  iti sāmānya vibhāgaḥ tasmāt  yathā eva itareṣām vibhāgaḥ evam upāṃśu yājasya api iti athavā upāṃśuyāja dravyāt pūrveṇa vākyena apanītā devatā na tad  apareṇa vākyena devatā antare saṃyojitam tasmāt  prahīṇam eva tad  asmin   eva udāharaṇe saṃśayaḥ kim yadi nirupte abhyudayaḥ avagamyate tadā abhyudita iṣṭiḥ uta anirupte api iti kim prāptam nirupte avagate abhyudita iṣṭiḥ syāt  kutas  tad saṃyogāt nirvāpa saṃyogaḥ  hi bhavati yasya havir niruptam iti tasmāt  anirupte na etad  vidhānam iti vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati akāle tantra pravṛtti mātre syāt  etad  vidhānam prāptam hi tāvatī  eva nimittam yasya havir abhyudeti iti havir grahaṇam lakṣaṇa tvena yasya havir abhyudeti iti havir lakṣita udayaḥ nimittam pravṛttam havir lakṣayati na udāsīnam tasmāt  havir abhyudeti iti  ucyamāne pravṛttam havir abhyudeti iti gamyate na hi tad  niruptam iti  etena śakyam viśeṣayitum bhidyeta hi tadā vākyam yasya havir niruptam na aniruptam iti  evam apekṣyaṃāṇe havir abhyudeti iti na śakyate vidhātum tasmāt  anirupte api iṣṭiḥ  iti atha yad  uktam nirupta saṃyogaḥ  bhavati yasya havir niruptam iti lakṣaṇa mātram etad  niruptam iti kasmiṃścid  padārthe tasya pravṛtta iti  arthaḥ anya arthaḥ  api ca etam artham darśayati sa yadi  agṛhītam havir abhyudiyāt  prajñātam eva tadā eṣā vrata caryā yad  pūrvedyus  dugdham dadhi havir ātañcanam tad  kurvanti pratimuñcanti vatsān tān eva tad  punar  apākurvanti tān aparāhṇe parṇa śākhayā apākaroti tad  yathā eva ādeḥ prajñātam āmāvāsyam havir evam eva tad  yadi  u vrata caryām vā na udāśaṃseta gṛhītam vā havir abhyudiyāt  itarathā tarhi kuryāt  etān eva taṇḍulān sakṛt phalīkṛtān iti agṛhīte haviṣy anyam vidhim bruvan gṛhīte api  anirupte vā abhyudaye prāyaścittam darśayati pravṛtta mātram nimittam iti sthitam naimittikaḥ  tu devatā apanayaḥ  devatā antara saṃyogaḥ  ca kim nirvāpa uttara kālam taṇḍula avasthe haviṣi kartavyaḥ  nirvāpaḥ  tu prākṛtībhya eva syāt  jñāte abhyudaye uta vaikṛtībhya eva iti saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat  prāptam anirupte abhyudite prākṛtībhyaḥ  nirvapet  iti  āśmarathya ācāryaḥ  manyate sma kutas  taṇḍula bhūteṣu  apanayāt  taṇḍula bhūteṣu  apanayaḥ śrūyate yasya havir niruptam purastāt  candramā abhyudeti tredhā taṇḍulān vibhajet  iti  abhyudaya avagamāt  anantaram taṇḍula vibhāgam āha saḥ  ataṇḍula bhūteṣu na avakalpate tasmāt  anirupte taṇḍula abhāvāt  anapanītā devatāḥ prākṛtya iti prākṛtībhya eva nirvapet  iti tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati vyūrdhvam yā bhajante karma tābhyaḥ  nirvapet  iti  ālekhana ācāryaḥ  manyate sma kutas  tad kāri tvāt  devatā apanayasya yasmāt  akāle tantra pravṛtti kāritaḥ  devatā apanayaḥ tasmāt  apanītā devatā iti vyūrdhva bhāgbhyaḥ  nirvaptavyāḥ atha prārabdhe catur muṣṭiḥ nirvāpe aparisamāpte bhavati saṃśayaḥ yad  niruptam tad  niruptam eva avaśiṣṭam kim prākṛtībhyaḥ  nirvaptavyam kim vaikṛtībhyaḥ uta tūṣṇīm eva iti kim prāptam vinirupte sāminirupta iti  arthaḥ na tatra devatā apanayaḥ syāt  kutas  tad guṇa tvāt  nirvāpasya guṇa u devatā na muṣṭīnām sa ca nirvāpaḥ  tad  devatākaḥ kutas  catur saṃkhyā pūraṇa artha tvāt  abhyāsa mātram kartavyam tad  ca abhyāsa mātram punar  kriyate pūrvam eva kṛte tasmin nirvāpe na devatā apanītā sa eva ayam punar  kriyate punar  api kriyamānasya anapanīta eva devatā bhavitum arhati iti prākṛtībhya eva nirvaptavyam na ca uttaraḥ  muṣṭiḥ pṛthak  padārthaḥ yena devatā apanayaḥ  bhavet  kṛtasya nirvāpasya saṃkhyā pūraṇam etad  kriyate tasmāt  anapanaya iti na prākṛtībhyaḥ  nirvaptavyam kābhyas tarhi vaikṛtībhyaḥ kutas  aprākṛtena devatā viśeṣeṇa saṃyogaḥ śrūyate na adhikṛtena tredhā taṇḍulān vibhajet  iti prākṛtībhya ācchidya vaikṛtībhyaḥ  nirvaptavyaḥ  vidhīyate tā idānīm tad sthānīyāḥ tasmāt  vinirupte nivṛttā devatā anyāḥ anyāḥ  ca upajātāḥ tasmāt  vaikṛtīnām saṃyogena nirvāpa śeṣaḥ kartavya iti abhāvāt  itarasya ardhasya devatā saṃyuktasya na nirvāpaḥ  bhavati devatā saṃyuktaḥ yadi nirvāpaḥ  ardham anya devatyaḥ  ardhaḥ  api  anyasyai devatāyai na eva nirvāpa itara devatā kaḥ  vā itara devatā kaḥ vā tasmāt  tūṣṇīm eva nirvaptavyam avaśyam anyataratra saṃkalpa bhedaḥ  bhavati abhyuhita iṣṭiḥ  eva udāharaṇam tatra śrūyate dadhani carum śṛte carum iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim saṃnayataḥ  bhavati  abhyudaye prāyaścittam uta aviśeṣeṇa iti kim prāptam saṃnayataḥ  abhyudaye prāyaścittam kutas  sāṃnāyya saṃyogāt  saṃnyāyya saṃyogaḥ  hi bhavati śṛte carum dadhani carum iti śṛta ādi abhāvāt na asaṃnayataḥ  bhavitum arhati vaiguṇyam hi tathā syāt  vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati ubhayoḥ  api syāt  na kevalasya saṃnayataḥ auṣadha saṃyogāt  ye madhyamā ye sthaviṣṭhā ye kṣodiṣṭhā iti bhavati  auṣadha saṃyogaḥ sa ca śakyaḥ  asaṃnaya tā api iti tasmāt  na asati kāraṇe asaṃnayataḥ  nivarteta ubhayoḥ  api pakṣayoḥ prāyaścittam iti iti yad  uktam asaṃnayataḥ  dadhnaḥ śṛtasya ca abhāvāt  tad adhikaraṇa tā na asti tasmāt  vaiguṇyam tasmin pakṣa iti tad  parihartavyam iti idam āmananti yadi satrāya dīkṣitā atha sāmyut  tiṣṭheran somam apabhajya viśvajitā atirātreṇa sarva stomena sarva pṛṣṭhena sarva vedasa dakṣiṇena yajeran   iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim krīta rājakasya utthāne viśva jit  uta pravṛtta mātrasya iti kim prāptam sāmi utthāne viśva jit  krīte syāt  kutas  vibhāga saṃyogāt  somam apabhajya viśvajitā yajeran   iti ye hi  akrīte rājany uttiṣṭanti teṣām soma vibhāga abhāvāt  vaiguṇyam syāt  tasmāt  krīta rājakā uttiṣṭhantaḥ  viśvajitam kuryuḥ vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati pravṛtta mātrasya utthāne syāt  kutas  prāpaṇān nimittasya sāmī utthānam nimittam viśvajitaḥ tad  ca prāptam na ca tad  chakyam viśeṣayitum krīte some sāmi utthānam iti atha yad  uktam akrīte rājany uttiṣṭhantaḥ  vibhāga abhāvāt  viguṇam kuryuḥ  iti tad  pratihartavyam atra ūcayate na vibhāgaḥ  vidhīyate bhidyeta hi tathā vākyam sāmi utthāne viśvajitā yajeran somasya tu  apabhāgam kṛtvā iti tena apabhajya iti  anuvādaḥ katham prāptiḥ  iti ced  arthāt  uttiṣṭhatām vibhāgaḥ  bhavati dhanasya saḥ  ayam sarva dravyāṇām vibhāgaḥ soma vibhāgena lakṣyate somam vibhajya anyāni ca dravyāṇi iti  ādeśa artha itarā śrutiḥ  bhavati tasmāt  krīte ca akrīte ca rājany uttiṣṭhatām viśva jit  iti jyotiṣṭomam prakṛtya śrūyate ekā dīkṣā tisra upasadaḥ pañcamīm prasuta iti tisraḥ  dīkṣāḥ dvādaśa dīkṣā iti bahūni dīkṣā parimāṇāni  āmnātāni teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim aniyamaḥ yad  vā tad  vā parimāṇam upādeyam uta dvādaśa dīkṣā iti kim prāptam dīkṣā parimāṇe yathākāmī syāt  na asti niyamaḥ kutas  aviśeṣāt  na kaścana viśeṣa upādīyate tasmāt  yad kiṃcid  parimāṇam upādeyam iti dvādaśa āha eva parimāṇam upādīyeta kutas  liṅgāt  sāmarthyāt  iti  arthaḥ kim sāmarthyam dvādaśa rātrīḥ  dīkṣitaḥ  bhṛtim vanvīta iti nityavat  āmnāyate na pākṣikam tad  eva nityam kurvan na śaknoti  anyat  parimāṇam upādātum tasmāt  dvādaśa āha eva parimāṇam niyamyeta anyāni parimāṇāni vikṛtau bhaviṣyati iti na eṣām ānarthakyam iti gavāmayane śrūyate purastāt  paurṇamāsyāḥ  catur ahe dīkṣerat    iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kasyāḥ paurṇamāsyā iti kim prāptam paurṇamāsyām aniyama iti kutas  aviśeṣāt  na atra kaścid  viśeṣa vacanaḥ śabda upādīyate tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na etad  aniyama iti caitrī paurṇamāsī tu bhavet  kutas  ānantaryāt  paurṇamāsīm uktvā anantaram vākya śeṣe caitrī saṃkīrtyate purasāt  paurṇamāsyāḥ  catur ahe dīkṣeran ṛtu mukham vā eṣā paurṇamāsī saṃvatsa rasya yā caitrī paurṇamāsī iti atra saṃdigdheṣu vākya śeṣāt  iti caitrī niyamyeta vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na ca etad  asti caitri iti kim tarhi māghī iti kutas  ekāṣṭakā śruteḥ kraye hi  ekāṣṭakā śrutiḥ  bhavati teṣām eka aṣṭakāyām krayaḥ saṃpadyata iti tasmāt  māghyāḥ purastāt  catur ahe dīkṣitasya ekāṣṭakāyām krayaḥ śakyate kartum na caityāḥ tad  etad  sāmarthyam nāma liṅgam tad  vākyasya bādhakam bhavati tasmāt  māghī paurṇamāsī iti iti ced  paśyasi māghī paurṇamāsī evam eka aṣṭakāyām krayaḥ saṃpatsyata iti tad  na asarvā aṣṭamya ekāṣṭakāḥ dvādaśa eka aṣṭakā iti tena na doṣaḥ na etad  evam bhāktaḥ  hi  anyāsu  aṣṭamīṣu  ekāṣṭakā śabdaḥ eṣā hi mukhyā yā māghyām vṛttāyām mukhya gauṇayoḥ  ca mukhye saṃpratyayaḥ tasmāt  māghy eva paurṇamāsī iti eka aṣṭakāyām dīkṣeran eṣā vai saṃvatsarasya patnī yad  ekāṣṭakā iti  uktvā punar  catur ahe purastāt  paurṇamāsyā dīkṣām vidhāya teṣām eka aṣṭakāyām krayaḥ saṃpadyate tena ekāṣṭakām na chaṃvaṭ  kurvanti iti dīkṣātaḥ pracyutām ekāṣṭakām krayeṇa tu gṛhṇan māghyāḥ paurṇamāsyā adhikāram darśayati asyām ca māghyām aṣṭamyām abhījyamānāyām bhavati mantraḥ yām janāḥ pratinandanti rātrīm dhenum iva āyatīm saṃvatsarasya yā patnī sā naḥ astu sumaṅgalī iti  aṣṭakāyai surādhase svāhā iti yā asau māghy aṣṭamī tām ekāṣṭakām darśayati utthāne ca anupraroham darśayati tān uttiṣṭhata auṣadhayaḥ vanaspatayaḥ  anuttiṣṭhanti iti vasanta utthānam darśayati tasmin   oṣadhayaḥ  vanaspatayaḥ  ca uttiṣṭhanti tasmāt  api sā niyamyate ārtam vā ete saṃvatsarasya abhidīkṣante ya eka aṣṭakāyām dīkṣanta iti ārtā yasmin kāle bhavanti sa ārtaḥ kālaḥ śītena ca ārtā bhavanti tasmāt  māghy aṣṭamī  ekāṣṭaka iti tathā vyastam vā ete saṃvatsarasya abhidīkṣante ya eka aṣṭakāyām dīkṣanta iti ayana parivṛttiḥ  vyasta śabdena ucyate tathā apaḥ  na abhinandantaḥ  avabhṛtham abhyavayanti iti caitryām dīkṣitā abhinandantaḥ  abhyaveyuḥ tasmāt  api māghī paurṇamāsī iti idam śrūyate tasmāt  dīkṣitaḥ  na dadāti na pacati na juhoti iti jyotiṣṭome samāmananti yadi tu daivān mānuṣāt  vā pratibalāt  dīkṣitā kāla utkṛṣyate tatra saṃdehaḥ kim dāna homa pākānām utkarṣaḥ uta na iti kim prāptam anutkarṣaḥ niyatā hi dāna homa pākāḥ yāvat  jīvam agni hotram juhoti iti evamādibhiḥ śrutibhiḥ  teṣām apavādaḥ yeṣu  ahaḥsu sa aṅgaḥ  jyotiṣṭomaḥ  vihitaḥ tāvanti  ahāni muktvā anyeṣu  ahaḥsu kartavyāḥ jyotiṣṭoma vidhāna kālāt paratas  apratiṣiddhāḥ tasmāt  kartavyāḥ prāptaḥ  hi teṣām kāla iti vā śabdāt  pakṣaḥ  viparivartate yad  uktam na eṣam utkarṣa iti na etad  evam utkṛṣṭavyāḥ kutas  dīkṣita tvāt  dīkṣitasya te pratiṣiddhāḥ na dīkṣitaḥ  yasmin kāle lakṣaṇā hi evam syāt  yathā tu vayam brūmaḥ tathā śrutiḥ kāraṇam prāk  ca avabhṛthāt  ayam dīkṣita eva aviśiṣṭam hi kāraṇam yad  eva jyotiṣṭoma vidhāna kāle tad  eva atikrānte api ubhayatra hi dīkṣita tvam hi kāraṇam tasmāt  teṣām utkarṣa iti tatra utkṛṣyamāṇe jyotiṣṭome akṛteṣu homeṣu kim parisaṃkhyāya homāḥ kartavyāḥ uta na iti kim prāptam parisaṃkhyāya homāḥ kriyeran kim kāraṇam avaśya kartavya tayā hi te vihitā homāḥ atipannā api kartavyā eva tathā hi  eṣām avaśya kartavyatā anugṛhītā bhaviṣyati pradhāna mātram tu niyatam na atra kāla anurodhaḥ kartavyaḥ nadī vega sthānīya tvāt  yadi  api  atikrāntāḥ kālāḥ atikrāntānām parisaṃkhyāya pradhāna mātrāṇi kartavyāni yathā vaśya kartavyam bhukti bhṛtaka dāna ādi yad  atikrāntam bhavati tad  parisaṃkhyāya kriyate evam idam api iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ tatra pratihomaḥ  na vidyate yathā pūrveṣām kartavyam akṛtvā kuryāt  na akartavyam akartavyāḥ  ca ete pratiṣiddha tvāt  yathā pūrveṣām asati kāla atikrame akṛtānām na pratihomaḥ evam eṣām api iti kāla prādhānyam ca bhavati nimitta tvena tasya śruta tvāt  tad abhāve vihitam eva na bhavati pradhāna mātram yadi  api niyamyeta tathā api nimitte kāle sa ca nadī vega sthānīyaḥ kāle atikrāntaḥ atas  na pratihomaḥ kartavya iti ūrdhvam avabhṛthāt  ā udavasānīyāyā iṣṭeḥ  ye homāḥ teṣu  atipanneṣu daivena mānuṣeṇa vā pratibalena bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim pratihomaḥ kartavyaḥ uta na iti kim prāptam kartavya iti unmukta dīkṣaḥ  hi sa tadā bhavati dīkṣāṇām unmocana arthaḥ  hi  avabhṛthaḥ tasmāt  kartavyāḥ te na kṛtā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ūrdhvam avabhṛthāt  ā udavasānīyāyā iṣṭeḥ atipannānām na pratihomaḥ syāt  kutas  pratiṣedhāt  pratiṣedhaḥ  hi bhavati etayā punar ādheya sa smitayā iṣṭyā agni hotram hotavyam iti prāk  udavasānīyāyāḥ homasya pratiṣedhaḥ yāvat  udavasānīya utkṛṣyate tāvat  pratiṣedhaḥ evam śrutiḥ itarathā lakṣaṇā syāt  tasmāt  akartavyāḥ te na kṛtā iti na syāt  pratihoma iti eteṣu  eva udāharaṇeṣu bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim pratihome sāyam agnihotra prabhṛtīni  ārabhyeran uta prātar agnihotra prabhṛtīni iti nanu na asti  eva pratihoma iti sthitam ucyate asti iti kṛtvā cintayāmaḥ kṛtvā cintā iyam anyeṣu sadṛśa nyāyeṣu udāharaṇeṣu  asyāḥ prayojanam asti iti cintyate kim prāptam aniyamaḥ artha kṛta tvāt  evam prāpte brūmaḥ yadi pratihomaḥ kriyate sāyam agnihotra prabhṛtīni hūyeran kutas  sāyam agni hotrāt  ārabhya atipannāni tena eva ānupūrveṇa pratihotavyāni iti ṣoḍaśi saṃsthe somaḥ  atipanneṣu homeṣu saṃdehaḥ kim sāyam agnihotreṇa iti uta prātar iti kim prāptam sāyam agnihotreṇa iti pūrvasmin   adhikaraṇa uktam utsargeṇa sarvatra evam iti prāptam tathā prāpta ucyate prātar  tu ṣoḍaśini ṣoḍaśi saṃsthe prātar agnihotra ādīni  atipannāni iti prātar agnihotrāt  eva samārabhyāni iti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate bhinne juhoti skanne juhoti iti tatra kim darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  eva etad  bhinne skanne ca prāyaścittam uta yatra bhidyate skandati ca iti kim prāptam prakaraṇe yad  prāyaścittam evaṃjātīykam kiṃcid  utpannam tad  sarvatra yatra yatra bhidyate skandati vā tatra tatra syāt  kasmāt  doṣa sāmānyāt  samānam nimittam skandanam bhedanam vā sa eva atra doṣa iti  abhipretam prakaraṇāt  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ prāyaścittam vākyāt  anyatra api prakaraṇa āc ca vākyam balīyaḥ tasmāt  sarvatra skanne bhinne ca prāyaścittam iti prakaraṇa eva bhinne skanne vā prāyaścittam kutas  śabda hetu tvāt  tena prākṛtena arthena saha eka vākyatā eṣām homānām tatas  homavataḥ  yāgasya pratyāyane prakṛtaḥ  yajeta iti śabdaḥ  hetuḥ evam ced  tad upakāreṇa arthavān bhaviṣyati iti itarathā vinā vākyena phalam kalpayitavyam syāt  tasmāt  vākyam phala abhāvena eva bādhitam iti kṛtvā prakaraṇam anugṛhītavyam iti na ca atad vikāraḥ  agnihotram jyotiṣṭomaḥ  vā na darśa pūrṇamāsa vikāraḥ yadi tad vikāraḥ  bhavet  tatra api skanne bhinne vā prāyaścittam syāt  iti vyāpannam apsu praharati iti śrūyate kim vyāpannam iti  ucyata iti tad  abhidhīyate vyāpannam dūṣitam yena kāryena kriyate kim tad  yad  abhojyam āryāṇām keśa kīṭau   apannam anyena vā upaghātena upahatam tad  vyāpannam iti prastotrudgātroḥ  udgātṛ pratihartoḥ  vā yatra apacchedaḥ kim tatra prāyaścittam syāt  na iti bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat  prāptam prāyaścittam yaugapadye na vidyate kutas  vibhāga śruteḥ vibhakte apacchede prāyaścittam āmananti apacchedaś ca ayam vibhāgaḥ sa ubhābhyām sādhyate iha ca ekena sādhyamāne śrūyate prāyaścittam udgātrā pratihartrā vā na ca yad  apareṇa saha kriyate tad  kevalena kṛtam bhavati yadi hi kevalena kṛtam syāt  tena kṛtam aparaḥ kim kuryāt  tasmāt  na yugapad  apacchinnayoḥ prāyaścittam iti syāt  vā prāyaścittam yaugapadye api prāptam hi nimittam apaccheda udgātuḥ pratihata ś ca yatra hi dvayoḥ  apacchedaḥ tatra dvau   api  apacchinnau ekaḥ  api  aparaḥ  api saṃyuktasya hi pṛthak bhāvaḥ  apacchedaḥ sa ca ubhaya sthaḥ  api ekena api tatra apacchedaḥ kriyate anapekṣya aparam apareṇa api kāla mātram tu tatra ekam na ca kāla aikyāt  apacchedayoḥ  aikyam bhavati tasmāt  prāyaścittam yugapad  apacchede api yadi  udgātṛ pratihartroḥ yugapad  apacchedaḥ  bhavati tatra saṃdehaḥ kim adākṣiṇyam sarva svam vā vikalpaḥ uta samuccaya iti kim prāptam tatra vipratiṣedhāt  vikalpaḥ syāt  viruddhau hi  etau kalpau sarva svam adākṣiṇyam ca tasmāt  vikalpaḥ  bhavitum arhati vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na ca etad  asti vikalpa iti ubhayoḥ  vidhānāt  sarva aṅga upasaṃhārī prayoga vacana evam upapadyate vikalpe hi pakṣe bādhaḥ tasmāt  samuccayaḥ atha yad  uktam virodhāt  vikalpa iti ucyate prayoga antare vā ubhaya anugrahaḥ syāt  tena punar  yajeta iti  ucyate dvi s tasya prayogaḥ tatra ekasmin prayoge ekaḥ kalpaḥ anyasmin   aparaḥ  bhaviṣyati evam avirodhaḥ tasmāt  ubhayam prāyaścittam iti na ca etad  evam kutas  eka saṃyogāt sa eva yāgaḥ punar  kriyeta yadi  anyatareṇa vinā vaiguṇyam iti  avadhāryeta sarva sve kriyamāṇe adakṣiṇya abhāvāt  viguṇaḥ syāt  na anyasmin prayoge kriyamāṇe anyaḥ prayogaḥ  anugṛhyate na ca adākṣiṇyasya sarva sva dānasya ca prādhānyam guṇavatā prayogeṇa karma saṃbandhayitavyam tasmāt  vikalpaḥ yatra ānupūrveṇa bhavati  apacchedaḥ tatra kim pūrva nimittam prāyaścittam uta uttara nimittam iti bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim prāptam pūrvasya balīyaḥ tvam pūrva apacchede yad  naimittikam prāptam tasmin sati tad viruddham na śakyam kartum na ca aśakyam upadeśa arham bhavati pūrva vijñānam prāptam iti na saṃśayaḥ tasmāt  tad avirodhena anyat kāryam na viruddham kva tarhi tad  syāt  yatra kevalam nimittam tasmāt  pūrva vijñānam balavat  evam prāpte brūmaḥ paurvāparye pūrva daurbalyam syāt  kutas  ākhyātena hi yaḥ  arthaḥ kartavya iti  ucyate tatra etad  anubuddham yathā śakyeta tathā iti tad  pūrva vijñāna bādhena śakyate na anyathā tena pūrva vijñānam bādhitvedam kartavyam iti bhavati śabda arthaḥ nanu pūrva vijñāna idam upapadyate yad  anyat  virodhakam vijñānam bhaviṣyati tad  mithyā iti abhūtam hi tad  na śakyam āśrayitum idam nāma tad  iti na ca apratiṣiddhe tasmin na pūrva vijñānam saṃbhavati tasmāt  apratiṣiddham bhaviṣyat  yadā tu tad  bhavati tadā pūrva vijñānam bādhamānam eva utpadyate tad  idānīm bādhitam na śaknoti  uttaram bādhitum iti prakṛtivat  yad  dhi prākṛtam vaikṛtena bādhyate tatra api  etad  eva kāraṇam na ābādhitvā pūrva vijñānam vaikṛtam saṃbhavati iti prākṛtam ca pūrvam yatas  vikṛtau tad  apekṣā pratyakṣa tvāt  vaikṛtam ānumānikam prākṛtam bādhata iti ced  pratyakṣa tve api sati na eva bādheta yadi yathāvarṇitaḥ  ayam ākhyāta arthaḥ  na bhavet  sati pūrva vijñāne aśakya tvāt  prākṛtam bādheta eva tasmāt  para balīyaḥ tvam nyāyyam eva iti yadā pratihartuḥ pūrvam apacchedaḥ tatas  udgātuḥ tatra adakṣiṇena iṣṭvā punar  yaṣṭavyam tatra saṃdehaḥ punar  yāge kim dvādaśa śatam dātavyam uta sarva svam iti kim prāptam dvādaśa śatam kutas  evam hi  āmnāyate tatra tad  dadyāt  yad  pūrvasmin dāsyan syāt  pūrvasminś ca prayoge jyotiṣṭoma dakṣiṇā eva prāptā tasmāt  dvādaśa śatam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ tatra punar yajñe sarvam dadyāt  yathā itarasmin pūrvasmin   ahani sarva svam katham tatra sarva svam iti ced  pratihartuḥ  apacchedāt  pratihartari  apacchinne dvādaśa śatam bādhitvā sarva svam dāsyan bhavati nanu pūrvasmin   ahani dvādaśa śatam api  asau dāsyan   āsīt  satyam sarva sva dānena ta ubhayam pradattam bhavati tasmāt  tad  deyam nanu  arvāk  api dvādaśa śatāt  sarva svam na etad  evam adhikṛte dvādaśa śate sarva svam api  adhikam bhavati api ca pūrvasmin   ahani na eva dvādaśa śatam dāsyan bhavati iti etāvat  dāsyan   iti  ucyate yasya uttara kāle tāvat  dānam bhavati na ca pūrvasmin   ahani dvādaśa śatam dīyate tasmāt  na tad  dāsyan   iti  avagamyate mithyā buddhiḥ sā tattvena vyavahāraḥ nanu ca sarva svam api pratiṣiddham bhavati tad  api  asau na dāsyan   iti sā api  asya mithyā buddhiḥ na iti  āha sa abhyāsasya jyotiṣṭomasya prayogaḥ tatra prathama prayoge adākṣiṇya virodhāt  sarva svam bādhyate dvitīya prayoge tad dānam codyate tatra virodhaḥ  na asti tasya eva yajñasya sa eva prayogaḥ pratihartā ca tasmin   apacchinna iti dvādaśa śatam bādhitvā sarva svam eva dāsyan bhavati tasmāt  sarva svam tatra deyam iti ahar gaṇe yadā bhavati kasmiṃścid  ahani  udgātuḥ  apacchedaḥ tadā saṃdehaḥ kim kṛtsnaḥ  ahar gaṇa āvartate uta tad  eva ahar iti kim prāptam kṛtsnaḥ  ahar gaṇaḥ kutas  aparaiḥ  ahobhiḥ  vinā tadā viguṇam bhavati tasmāt  gaṇa eva āvarteta iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ yasmin   apacchedaḥ tad  eva āvarteta kutas  karma pṛthaktvāt  pṛthak  etāni karmāṇi na anyat  ahar anyasya guṇa bhūtam iṣṭvā iti ca yāgam parisamāpya iti gamyate na sa aṅgam iti yāni  ahar antarāṇi sāhāyyena upakariṣyanti vidyanta eva tāni atas  sāhāyyam kariṣyanti iti tasmāt  tad  eva āvarteta satrāṇi  udāharaṇam saptadaśa avarāḥ satram āsīran ya evam vidvāṃsaḥ satram āsate ya evam vidvāṃsaḥ satram upayanti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim samāna kalpānām bhinna kalpānām ca saha adhikāra uta samāna kalpānām eva iti ke punar  samāna kalpāḥ rājanyātri badhryaśva vasiṣṭha vainya śunakānām kaṇva kaśyapa saṃkṛtīnām nārāśaṃsaḥ  dvitīyaḥ prayājaḥ tanūnapād itareṣām evam kecid  nārāśaṃsa kalpāḥ kecid  tanūnapāt kalpāḥ tatra kim tāvat  prāptam saṃnipāte bahūnām yajamānānām ya eva tulya kalpāḥ ta eva saha satram āsīran kutas  avaiguṇyāt  itarathā yasya kalpaḥ  na upasaṃhriyeta tasya vaiguṇyam syāt  yathā prakṛtau   eva vinā sādguṇyena phala abhāva evam iha api iti vā śabdāt  pakṣaḥ  viparivartate na ca etad  asti bhinna kalpānām anadhikāra iti te api  adhikriyeran kutas  aviśeṣeṇa sarveṣām yajamānānām prāptiḥ na ca bhinna kalpānām pratiṣedhaḥ nanu vaiguṇyam bhinna kalpānām atra ucyate vacanāt  sāmānya vacanena bhinna kalpā api gṛhītāḥ tatra śirovat  bhādhaḥ syāt  yathā puruṣa śīrṣam upadadhāti iti vacana sāmarthyāt  chava śirasām sparśanam smṛti vipratiṣiddham api kriyate evam iha api athavā āśiḥ avat  yathā ṛtapeye ghṛta vrataḥ  bhavati iti vacanāt  vrata duhi nivṛttāyām anyāmāśire gām kalpayanti evam etad  api vacanāt  bhaviṣyati syāt  vā bhinna kalpānām adhikāraḥ kutas  yajña artha tvāt kalpasya vasiṣṭha ādīnām nārāśaṃsa kalpaḥ  yajñasya sādhakaḥ sa ca yajñaḥ sarveṣām sādhāraṇaḥ para kalpena api siddhaḥ siddhaḥ  bhavati yathā yajamānena saṃmāya audumbarīm parivāsayanti iti yasya kasyacid  parimāṇena siddhaḥ  yajñaḥ  anyeṣām api siddhaḥ  bhavati ucyate nanu prayājasya vākyena puruṣa saṃbandhaḥ sa ca prakaraṇa prāptām yāga artha tām bādhiṣyata iti na iti brūmaḥ phalam hi tadā kalpayitavyam nanu  itarathā api  adṛṣṭam avaśyam kalpanīyam tatra ucyate satyam kalpanīyam pramāṇena tu prayoga vacana eka vākyena dvitīye tu pakṣe kalpayitvā śabdam tena eka vākyatā syāt  atha ucyeta kvacid  samāmnātena saha eka vākyatā bhaviṣyati tathā api  aprakṛtena vyavahitena ca kalpyamānā prakṛta kalpanāyā gurutarā syāt  na etad  evam tad pradhāna tvāt  puruṣa arthaḥ  hi  eṣa kalpaḥ katham vasiṣṭha ādīnām nārāśaṃsaḥ  yajña aṅgam iti yad  ca yasya yajña aṅgam tena saha phala dam karma tasya bhavati tena evam abhisaṃbandhaḥ kriyate vasiṣṭhānām nārāśaṃsena sahitam karma phala dam bhavati iti atha yad  upavarṇitam yathā audumbarī tathā iha iti pārārthyam audumbaryāḥ yajamānaḥ  guṇa tvena śrūyate nanu tatra api prayoga vacanaḥ puruṣa prādhānyam kuryāt  na eṣa doṣaḥ ekena api yajamānena saṃmitā ca iyam sarveṣām yajamāna saṃmitā bhavati na tu  iha ekasya saṃgṛhīte sarveṣām saṃgṛhītaḥ tasmāt  audumbaryāḥ pārārthyam kapālavat  yathā puroḍāśa kapālena tuṣā upavapanti iti para artha kapālena tuṣā upavaptavyā iti  upādīyate evam etad  api iti evam ced  bhavān paśyati yajamānena saṃmānam tad  prayaḥ janam svena anyena vā yajamānena iti tathā prayoga antare yaḥ  yajamānaḥ  tena api saṃmānam prāpnoti atra ucyate na prayoga antarasya yajamānaḥ prasajyate na tu yajamāna śabde kaścid  viśeṣaḥ yatas  yajamāna śabdāt  vyavasthā syāt  kim tarhi eka tvasya vivakṣita tvāt  na dvābhyām yājamānāni kartavyāni iti na anya ānīyate āha anya eva tarhi sarva yājamāneṣu bhavatu na evam kāminam hi  adhikṛtya sa aṅgasya yāgasya vacanam yajamāna śabdaḥ  ca avibhakta iha audumbaryāḥ saṃmāne tasmāt  na anyaḥ  bhaviṣyati tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati bahuṣu yajamāneṣu saṃnipātān nimitta vighātaḥ syāt  kutas  vibhakti śiṣṭa tvāt  vasiṣṭha nirvartye prayoge nārāśaṃsaḥ  naimittikaḥ anyasmin   tanūnapān naimittikaḥ yatra idānīm ubhaye kartāraḥ sa mahāyena tatra nirvṛttiḥ  na kevalena tasmāt  na kevalaḥ kartā na ced  vāsiṣṭhaḥ kevalaḥ kartā tasmāt  tad nimittam tatra na kartavyam na ca itara nimittam ubhayoḥ  api  anyonyena vighātaḥ bṛhadrathantaravat  tad  yathā bṛhadrathantaram pṛṣṭham bhavati iti na bṛhadsādhanakam na rathantara sādhanakam iti na eva tatra bṛhan nimittam bhavati na rathantaram vā evam iha api iti api vā iti pakṣam vyāvartayati kṛtsnam prati kevalasya kartṛ tvena saṃyogaḥ  bhavati tasmāt  avighātaḥ naimittikānām katham punar  kārtsnyena kartavya tvam svāmi tvena abhisaṃbandhāt  karma prati svāmi tvena kevalānām vasiṣṭha ādīnām abhisaṃbandhaḥ  bhavati karma puruṣāṇam upakārakam tad  dhy ekaikasya śaknoti phalam nirvartayitum tasmāt  ekaikaḥ kṛtsnasya kartā iti tad  naimittikam sarvam prāpnoti yathā tuṇḍa mātre dīyatām iti yadi  api sā tuṇḍaḍa pitthayoḥ  mātā tathā api tasyai dīyate kārtsnena hi tasya sā mātā bhavati na hi vyāsajyate mātṛ tvam tadvat  iha api draṣṭavyam tasmāt  asamāna kalpānām anadhikāraḥ atha yad  uktam bṛhat rathantaravat  iti tad  pariharaṇīyam bṛhat rathantarayoḥ sāmnoḥ  naimittika karma vṛddhyā eka deśena saṃyogaḥ  bhavati tatra hi  ubhayoḥ sādhaka tvam na ekasya stotra eka deśena tu tatra sāmnoḥ saṃbandhaḥ na kṛtsnena stotreṇa guṇa tvena hi tatra sāma śrūyate stotram prādhānyena tasmāt  tatra vighātaḥ syāt  idam samāmananti etena rāja purohitau sāyujya kāmau yajeyātām iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim rājñaḥ  dvau purohitau yajeyātām uta rājā ca purohita ś ca iti kim prāptam rājñaḥ  dvau purohitau   iti kutas  purohita śabdāt  param dvivacanam śrūyate tad śabda vācyasya dvi tvam śaknoti vaditum purohita ś ca tad śabda vācyaḥ śrutyā na rājā purohita vacanaḥ purohita śabdaḥ lakṣaṇayā yugapad  adhikaraṇa vacana tāyām hi tad  bhavati nanu  ekasya dvau purohitau na staḥ purohitam vṛṇīta iti hi  upādīyamānasya vivakṣitam eka tvam iti ucyate vacanāt  etad  bhaviṣyati kim hi vacanam na kalpayet  etena eva kāraṇena dvau bhaviṣyataḥ yathā vacanena añjalinā juhoti iti  ekasya eva dvau pāṇī bhavataḥ yadi  api savyaḥ prāpta s tathā api iti tuśabdāt  pakṣaḥ  viparivartate na evam syāt  dvau purohitau   iti kutas  artha abhāvāt na eva ayam arthaḥ  asti dvau purohitau   iti ekasya rājña eka eva purohita upādeya tvena hi śrūyate purohitam karoti iti eka tvam vivakṣitam nanu vacanāt  iti  uktam ucyate na tu vacanāt  etad  chakyam saṃskāra nimitta tvāt  purohita śabdasya kriyamāṇaḥ  api na purohitaḥ syāt  arthānām ca vibhakta tvam śrūyate tejaḥ san  tavaḥ  brāhmaṇasya vīrya sanstavaḥ  rājanyasya tābhyām varṇābhyām tena tena phalena saṃbandhaḥ  anūdyate tasmāt  api na dvau purohitau   iti atha yad  uktam etasmāt  eva kāraṇāt  ekasya eva puruṣasya dvau pāṇī bhavata iti yuktam tatra pāṇeḥ pratyaṅga bhūta tvāt  añjalim pratyaṅga bhūtaḥ  dakṣiṇasya pāṇeḥ svayaḥ pāṇiḥ tena vinā añjaliḥ  eva na bhavati na hi dvābhyām dakṣiṇābhyām añjaliḥ  iti  ucyate tasmāt  rājā ca purohita ś ca syāt  nanu tatra rāja purohita ś ca rāja purohita ś ca rāja purohitau yajeyātām iti ucyate na tau sāyujya kāmau bhavataḥ sa rājā purohitena saha eka kāryaḥ  bhavati na tu purohitaḥ purohitena ubhau   api tau hi rājānam abhicarantau purohitau   iti  ucyete na hi tau   icchantau saṃskāra śabdaḥ  hi purohita iti nanu lakṣaṇā bhavati bhavat pakṣe ucyate śruti abhāve lakṣaṇayā api vyavahāraḥ  bhavati yathā agnau tiṣṭhati avaṭe tiṣṭhati iti tasmāt  rājā ca purohita ś ca rāja purohitau   iti iha satrāṇi  udāharaṇam ya evam vidvāṃsaḥ satram āsate ya evam vidvāṃsaḥ satram upayanti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim satrāṇi trayāṇām api varṇānām uta brāhmaṇānām eva iti kim prāptam satrāṇi sarva varṇānām bhaveyuḥ  iti kasmāt  aviśeṣāt  na hi kaścid  viśeṣa āśrīyate amīṣām varṇānām satrāṇi bhavanti amīṣām na iti tasmāt  trayāṇām api varṇānām adhikāra iti itas  ca paśyāmaḥ trayāṇām satrāṇi iti kutas  liṅga darśanāt  kim liṅgam bhavati evam āha bārhadgiram brāhmaṇasya brahmasāma kuryāt  pārthu raśyam rājanyasya rāyā uvājīyam vaiśyasya iti dvādaśa ahe bhavati vacanam brāhma sāma vidhāna param tasmin rājanya vaiśyānām darśanam bhavati tasmāt  api sarva varṇānām adhikāra iti vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na ca etad  asti trayāṇām api varṇānām iti kim tarhi brāhmaṇānām eva syāt  kutas  itarayoḥ  ārtvijya abhāvāt itarayoḥ  hi varṇayaḥ rājanya vaiśyayoḥ  ārtvijyam pratiṣiddham svayam eva ārtvijyena ca vinā viguṇa tvam tasmāt  brāhmaṇānām eva syāt  iti ced  paśyasi rājanya vaiśyayoḥ  vaiguṇyam āpadyata iti vacanāt  yajamānāḥ santa ṛtvijaḥ  bhaviṣyanti ye yajamānā aḥ  ta ṛtvija iti ke punar  yajamānāḥ ye tatra phalam kāmayamānāḥ satra karmaṇi pravṛttā aḥ  te rājanyā api vaiśyā api teṣām ṛtvij karma vidhīyate tatra etad  syāt  yeṣām ārtvijyam śakyam kartum teṣām eva tad  brāhmaṇānām pratiṣiddham hi rājanya vaiśyānām na teṣām idam ārtvijya vidhānam iti na etad  evam yathā eva brāhmaṇānām yajamānānām aprāptam vacana vidhānāt  bhavati evam abrāhmaṇānām api yajamānānām vacana prāmāṇyāt  eva bhavitum arhati iti tasmāt  ārtvijya saṃskṛtā rājanya vaiśyā api satram āsīran   iti na etad  evam svāmi tvam anena vacanena vidhīyate evaṃkāmāḥ satram āsīran   iti vidhīyate na ārtvijyam atha ye yajamānā aḥ  ta ṛtvija iti  anena vacanena vihitam ārtvijyam iti ucyate tad  api na katham na atra eṣā vacana vyaktiḥ ye yajamānā iti  uddeśa padam ṛtvija iti vidheya padam tathā hi sati ārtvijyam aṅgam yajamāna saṃskārakam vidhīyeta na yajamānā ārtvijyasya aṅgam tatra prākṛtārtha tā na eṣām ārtvijyānām syāt  saṃskāraḥ  ca adṛṣṭaḥ kalpyeta sa ca yajamāna viṣaya iti punar  adṛṣṭam tasmāt  na yajamānānām satām ārtvijyāḥ padārthā vidhīyante kim tarhi ārtvijānām padārthānām ananya kartṛka tā eṣā ca vacana vyaktiḥ ṛtvija iti  uddeśa padam ta iti vidhīyate ye yajamānā aḥ  ta eva ṛtvijaḥ  bhavanti na anya iti ārtvijeṣu padārtheṣu yajamānāḥ kartāraḥ  vidhīyante pratyāmnānāt anye nivartante evam sati prākṛta prayojanā eva artvijāh padārthāḥ na yajamāna saṃskāraḥ  adṛṣṭaḥ  vidhīyata iti yajamāna kartṛ kalpanāyām api  eṣām adṛṣṭam iti yadi kalpyeta tatra brūmaḥ itarasmin   api pakṣe yajamāna viṣayaḥ saḥ  adṛṣṭaḥ saṃskāra iti avaśyam kalpanīyam yaḥ  ca ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ  doṣaḥ  na tam ekaḥ  codyaḥ  bhavati gārhapate padārthe rājanya vaiśyau bhaviṣyataḥ na ca tatra ārtvija prayojanam tasmāt  avipratiṣedha s teṣām iti na ca etad  asti gārhapate vā padārthe rājanya vaiśyauv iti kalpa virodhaḥ  hi syāt  yajamāna camasaḥ soma maya ekeṣām phala maya camasa ekeṣām tathā brahmasāma bārhadgiram brāhmaṇānām pārthu raśmam rājanyānām rāyā uvājīyam vaiśyānām tasmāt  gārhapate niveśa iti  etad  api na asti atha yad  uktam liṅga darśanāt  iti tad  parihartavyam atra ucyate ahīnam eva satra śabdena vakṣyati yatas  svāmi tvam ṛtvijām vidhīyate ata ṛtvijām svāmi tvāt  rājanya vaiśyānām satram na avakalpata iti tasmāt  ahīne liṅga darśanam etad  samadhigatam brāhmaṇānām eva satram na rājanya vaiśyānām iti atha idānīm idam saṃdigdham kim sarveṣām brāhmaṇānām uta vāsiṣṭhānām sa uta bhṛgu śunaka vasiṣṭhān varjayitvā anyeṣām iti kim prāptam sarveṣām aviśeṣāt  na hi kaścid  viśeṣa āśrīyate amīṣām brāhmaṇānām satram amīṣām na iti tasmāt  sarveṣām iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ vāsiṣṭhānām brahma tvasya niyamāt  vāsiṣṭhānām satram syāt  na anyeṣām kutas  brahma tvasya niyamaḥ  bhavati vāsiṣṭhaḥ  brahmā bhavati iti atas  vāsiṣṭhānām tad  samāna kalpānām ca satram syāt  iti sarveṣām vā satram syāt  aviśeṣāt  nanu vāsiṣṭhaḥ  brahma iti  ucyate na iti  āha punar  pratisūyate ya eva kaścana stoma bhāgam adhīyīta sa eva brahmā bhavet  iti vāsiṣṭha upadeśa idānīm kim artha iti ced  stoma bhāga praśaṃsā arthaḥ stoma bhāgān adhīyānaḥ  avāsiṣṭhaḥ  api vāsiṣṭha kāryam samarthaḥ kartum iti bhṛgu ādīnām anadhikāraḥ syāt  kutas  vaiśvāmitrasya hautram niyamyate viśvāmitraḥ  hotā bhavati iti tasmāt  vaiśvāmitrāṇām taiś ca samāna kalpānām adhikāra iti satrāṇi  eva udāharaṇam ya evam vidvāṃsaḥ satram āsate ya evam vidvāṃsaḥ satram upayanti iti teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim sa agnīnām angnīnām ca tāni bhavanti uta sa agnīnām eva iti kim prāptam sa agnīnām anagnīnām ca kutas  vihārasya prabhu tvāt  prabhavati hi parakīyaḥ api vihāraḥ sarveṣām upakartum kartavyaḥ  hi tena sidhyati iti sa yadīyena tadīyena vā siddhim upaiti tasmāt  anagnīnām api bhavitum arhati iti sārasvate ca satre bhavati darśanam para rathaiḥ  vā ete svargam lokam yanti ye anāhitāgnayaḥ satram āsata iti anāhitāgnīnām satram darśayati tasmāt  api sarveṣām prāyaścittam vidhīyate agnaye vivicaye aṣṭākapālam puroḍāśam nirvapet  yasya āhitāgneḥ  anyaiḥ  agnibhiḥ  agnayaḥ saṃsṛjyeran    iti saṃsarge agnīnām prāyaścittam darśayati sa evam syāt  anāhitaiḥ na anyathā tasmāt  api  anagnīnām satrāṇi iti sa agnīnām vā satrāṇi na anagnīnām kasmāt  iṣṭi pūrva tvāt  iṣṭi pūrva tvam somānām āmnātam darśa pūrṇamāsau   iṣṭvā somena yajeta iti jyotiṣṭomasya iṣṭi pūrva tvam tad  ca u daka paramparayā satrāṇi prati prāptam tasmāt  anagnīnām tāni bhaveyuḥ  iti sva arthena ca agnayaḥ prayuktāḥ katham upagraha viśeṣāt  upagraha viśeṣaḥ  hi bhavati agnīn ādadhīta iti tasmāt  anyasya agnibhiḥ  anyasya na siddhiḥ yadi  api kratu arthā agnaya iti sāvitrāṇi hoṣyantaḥ saṃnivaperan   iti tena api sa agnayaḥ satrāṇi  upāsata iti gamyate evam liṅga parihārau   aśiṣṭe adhikaraṇe anya t  cintyate kim juhvā ādīni pātrāṇi kasyacid  eva yajamānasya upādāya prayogaḥ kartavyaḥ uta anyāni sādhāraṇāni kartavyāni kim prāptam yasya kasyacid  eva yajamānasya upādāya prayogaḥ kartavyaḥ kutas  na hi svam pātram yajamānaḥ prayuṅkte svena pātreṇa prayogaḥ kartavya iti tasmāt  parakīya pātraiḥ  anye yajeran   iti api vā iti pakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ na etad  evam anyāni hi pātrāṇi sādhāraṇāni kartavyāni kasmāt  vipratiṣedhāt  vipratiṣedhaḥ  bhavati kadācid  tāni pātrāṇi  upāttāni bhaveyuḥ atha maraṇam kasyacid  yajamānasya āpadyeta tatra vipratiṣedhaḥ syāt  āhitāgnim agnibhiḥ  dahanti yajña pātraiḥ  ca iti yadi tam taiḥ  daheyuḥ itareṣām yajñaḥ  virudhyeta atha taiḥ  yajñam samāpayeyuḥ  itarasya śarīra saṃskārāḥ parilupyeran anyeṣu punar  sādhāraṇeṣu upādīyamāneṣu na kiṃcid  api virudhyeta tasmāt  tathā kāryam iti atha idānīm pūrva uktasya liṅgasya parihāra ucyate prāyaścittam asmad pakṣe parikalpiṣyate katham araṇye kāntāre gacchatām sthitānām vā dasyu bhayāt  śvāpada bhayāt  vā trāse jāte dāva agninā vā saṃsṛjyeran mithas  vā sa viṣayaḥ prāyaścittasya bhaviṣyati iti adhara kalpā udāharaṇam āgrayaṇa iṣṭiḥ paśuḥ  iti evaṃlakṣaṇakāni karmāṇi yeṣu saptadaśa sāmidhenyaḥ teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim trayāṇām api varṇānām ebhiḥ karmabhiḥ  adhikāraḥ uta vaiśyasya eva iti kim prāptam etasyām vikṛtau puruṣa kalpena kartā niyamyeta kutas  yajñaḥ  ayam adhvara kalpa ādiḥ etad  saṃkhyā guṇakaḥ iyam ca saṃkhyā vaiśyasya uktā tena vaiśya eva etad  karma kṛtsnam kartum samarthaḥ saptadaśa guṇakam etad  karma tad  ca sāptadaśyam avaiśyena kriyamāṇam asādhu itarān prati hi tad  na codyate tena yajeta iti  asāmarthyāt  brāhmaṇa kṣatriyān na adhikariṣyati iti liṅgam ca bhavati yathā vaiśyasya sāptadaśyam iti saptadaśaḥ  vaiśya iti tena vaiśyasya sāptadaśyam atas  vaiśyasya evaṃjātīyakāni karmāṇi yathā ijyā viśeṣaḥ  vaiśyasya bhavati vaiśyaḥ  vaiśya stomena yajeta iti vaiśya saṃbandhāt  evam sāptadaśyam tasya eva iti na ca etad  asti pṛthak  etau saṃyogau ekam vākyam saptadaśa vaiśyasya anubrūyāt  iti vākya antaram adhvara kalpa ādiṣu saptadaśa anubrūyāt  iti sa ca guṇa ijyā pradhānaḥ  bhavati na ijyā guṇa arthā kim atas  yadi  evam yatra ijyā tatra tad guṇena bhavitavyam na yatra guṇaḥ tatra ijyayā vaiśyasya guṇa anurodhena ijyā api trayāṇām varṇānām ijyā sā tatra guṇam ākāṅkṣati iti api cejyā guṇa bhūtasya aparā codanā na sā vaiśya saṃyuktā sā tu  avaiśyakam guṇam pratyāyayati prathamam sa vaiśyakam iti ced  na vaiśyasya pradhāna tvāt  pradhāna bhūta s tatra vaiśyaḥ śrūyate tasmāt  sarva adhikāraḥ atha yad  uktam vaiśya stome yathā tathā iha api iti yuktam tatra ijyā vaiśyasya śrūyate tatra vācanikena eva viśeṣeṇa niyamyeta tasmāt  tatra adoṣa iti idam āmananti viśvajiti sarva svam dadāti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim yāvat  kiṃcid  sva śabdena ucyate yathā mātā pitā iti evamādy api sarvam deyam uta yatra prabhutva yogena sva śabda s tad  eva deyam iti kim prāptam aviśeṣāt  mātā pitā iti evamādy api dātavyam nanu dānam iti  ucyate svatva nivṛttiḥ para svatva āpādanam ca tatra pitṛ ādīnām aśakyam sva tvam nivartayitum na hi kathaṃcid  pitā na pitā bhavati ucyate satyam na asau na pitā bhavati śakyate tu para vidheyaḥ kartum para svatva āpādanam ca dānam arthāc ca svatva tyāgaḥ tasmāt  sarvam deyam iti vā śabdena pakṣaḥ  viparivartate yasya prabhutva yogena sva tvam tad  eva deyam na itarat  kasmāt  prabhutva yoginaḥ śakya tvāt  itarasya ca aśakya tvāt na hi pitṛ ādīnām śakyate sva tvam parityaktum nanu ca uktam para vidheyīkaraṇam tasya śakyam iti ucyate prabhutva yoginaḥ svasya atra dīyamānasya sarva tvam ucyate na aprabhutva yoginaḥ svasya dānam na ca etad  nyāyyam yad  pitṛ ādīnām paricāraka tvam yasya ca etad  nyāyyam api bhavet  sa dadyāt  api atra āha nanu yatra sva śabdaḥ  vartate tad  deyam iti  ukte pitṛ ādayaḥ  dātavyā gamyante tasmāt  tān prati prabhu tvāya smṛtim bādhitvā api yatitavyam iti atra ucyate sva śabdaḥ  ayam ātmīya dhana jñātīnām pratyekam vācakaḥ  na samudāyasya tatra ātmīye sarva tāyām kṛtāyām kṛte śāstra arthe na aśakyeṣu jñātiṣu sarvatā kalpanīyā na api smṛtiḥ  bādhitavyā api ca gavā ādīnām ātmīyānām ca udakena prāptau satyām avaśyam ātmīya gatā sarvatā upadeyā tasyām ca upāttāyām kṛtaḥ śāstā artha iti jñātīnām upādāne na kiṃcid  kāraṇam asti tasmāt  na pitṛ ādayaḥ  deyāḥ tasmāt  yatra eva prabhutva yogena sva tvam tad  eva deyam iti atra eva sarva dāne saṃśayaḥ kim bhūmiḥ  deyā na iti kā punar  bhūmiḥ  atra abhipretā yad  etad  mṛdā ārabdham dravyān atram pṛthivī golakam na kṣetra mātram mṛttikā vā tatra kim prāptam aviśeṣāt  deyā prabhutva saṃbandhena hi tatra sva śabdaḥ  vartate śakyate ca mānasena vyāpāreṇa svasya svatā nivartayitum iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ na bhūmiḥ  deyā iti kutas  kṣetrāṇām īśitāraḥ  manuṣyā dṛśyante na kṛtsnasya pṛthivī golakasya iti āha ya idānīm sārvabhaumaḥ sa tarhi dāsyati saḥ  api na iti brūmaḥ kutas  yāvatā bhogena sārvabhaumaḥ  bhūmeḥ  īṣṭe tāvatā anyaḥ  api na tatra kaścid  viśeṣaḥ sārvabhauma tve asya tu  etad  adhikam yad  asau pṛthivyām saṃbhūtānām vrīhi ādīnām rakṣaṇena nirviṣṭasya kasyacid  bhāgasya iṣṭe na bhūmeḥ tad nirviṣṭāḥ  ca ye manuṣyāḥ taiḥ  anyat  sarva prāṇinām dhāraṇa vikramaṇa ādi yad  bhūmi kṛtam tatra īśi tvam prati na kaścid  viśeṣaḥ tasmāt  na bhūmiḥ  deyā viśvajiti  eva saṃdehaḥ kim aśvādayaḥ  deyāḥ na iti kim prāptam sarvasya vihita tvāt  deyā aśvā iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ yasya ca dānam akāryam tad  ca na deyam yathā aśvānām teṣām hi dānam akāryam eṣa hi viśeṣaḥ  aśvānām anyebhyaḥ  dravyebhyaḥ yad  eṣām dānam pratiṣidhyate na kesariṇaḥ  dadāti na ubhaya todataḥ pratigṛhṇāti iti viśvajiti  eva samāmnāyate tasmāt  na aśvā deyā iti viśvajiti  eva saṃdehaḥ sarva svam dadāti iti kim arjayitvā upakaraṇāni yāvanti manuṣyasya yāvanti ca śaknoti  upārjayitum sarvāṇi tāni dadyāt  kṛta bhāṇḍa ādīni uta yāni  eva asya vidyante tāni sarvāṇi deyāni na avidyamānāni kartavyāni iti kutas  saṃśayaḥ ubhayathā vacana vyakteḥ saṃbhavāt  yadi vaivam vacanam vyajyate yāni sarvāṇi svāni kāni tāni yāni puruṣasya upakārakāṇi śayana ādīni tāni sarvāṇi dadyāt  iti vidhīyate yad  vā yāni svāni puruṣasya dāne śakyāni tāni sarvāṇi iti sarva tvam vidhīyate yadi dānam vidhīyate tatas  aprāpta dānānām kṛta bhāṇḍakānām api dānam atha sarvatā vidhīyate tatas  vidyamānānām eva kim tāvat  prāptam kṛta bhāṇḍakāni deyāni iti tathā dāna vidhāne śrutiḥ  anugṛhyate itarathā vākyam tayoś ca śrutiḥ  balīyasī tasmāt  kṛta bhāṇḍakāni deyāni iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ nitya tvāt  ca anityaiḥ  na asti saṃbandhaḥ caśabdaḥ  anvādeśe na aśvā dātavyā iti  uktam kṛta bhāṇḍakāni ca na deyāni iti nityam hi viśvajiti dānam ca udakena prāptam anūdyate anityāni ca kṛta bhāṇḍakāni na śakyāni sarvāṇi viśvajiti kriyamāṇa  upasaṃhartum tatra kṛta bhāṇḍakānām syāt  na nityam nityavat  ca tad  ca udakena vidhīyate na nimitta saṃyogena tasmāt  avaśyam etad  abhyupagantavyam sākalpyam deyānām prāptānām vidhīyata iti śruti asaṃbhave ca vākya arthaḥ  gṛhītavya eva bhavati tasmāt  na kṛta bhāṇḍakāni dātavyāni viśvajiti  eva saṃdihyate kim paricārakaḥ śūdraḥ  deyaḥ na iti kim prāptam sarvasya svasya vihita tvāt  deya iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ śūdraḥ  ca na deya iti  anvādeśaḥ kutas  dharma śāstra tvāt  dharma śāsana upanata tvāt tasya evam asau tasmai traivarṇikāya upanata idam śuśrūṣamāṇaḥ  dharmeṇa saṃbhantsyata iti saḥ  anyasmai dīyamāṇaḥ  na icchet  api na ca anicchata s tasya sa prabhavati na ca balāt  svīkartavyaḥ yaḥ  tu  anyāyena svīkuryāt  sa dadyāt  api dharma upanata mātreṇa tu na śakyaḥ  dātum viśvajiti  eva saṃdehaḥ kim prāk  dakṣiṇā kālāt  vidyamānam niyogataḥ  dakṣiṇā kāle nidhātavyam ūrdhvam ca dakṣiṇā kālāt  bhaviṣyat  anāgatam api dakṣiṇā kāle deyam uta yad  eva dakṣiṇā kāle vidyate tad  eva deyam iti kim prāptam yasya api prāk  ūrdhvam ca svatā tad  api deyam sva mātrasya dāna vidhānat evam prāpte brūmaḥ dakṣiṇā kāle yad  svam vidyate tad  eva deyam na yad  prāk  ūrdhvam ca kutas  svasya atra dānam anūdya sākalyam vidhīyate tad  ca dānam dakṣiṇā kāle prāpta tvāt  tasmin   eva kāle anūdyate tasmāt  dakṣiṇā kāla eva vidyamānam deyam iti tasmin   eva viśvajiti saṃdehaḥ kim dakṣiṇā kāla eva viśva jit  utsraṣṭavyaḥ uta na sarvam dātavyam parisamāpanīya iti kim prāptam utsraṣṭavya iti kutas  aśeṣa tvāt  katham aśeṣa tā viśvajiti sarva svam dadāti iti na ca śakyam antareṇa dravyam parisamāpayitum tasmāt  tad antar  syāt  api vā iti pakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ śeṣa karma syāt  na sarva svam dakṣiṇā kāle deyam yāvatā tad karma parisamāpyate tāvac cheṣayitavyam kutas  kratoḥ pratyakṣa śiṣṭa tvāt  kratoḥ parisamāptiḥ pratyakṣa śiṣṭā viśvajitā yajeta iti viśvajitam upakramya parisamāpayet  iti  arthaḥ parisamāpayatā yad  chakyate dātum tāvat  sarvam iti  arthaḥ tasmāt  na tad antam utsraṣṭavyam iti evam ca kṛtvā anya artha darśanam upapadyate avabhṛthāt  udetya vatsa tvacam āc chādayati iti śeṣe sati  avakalpate tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati etad  samañjasā bhūtam yad  aśeṣam pratīyata iti evam sarva svam dadāti iit śabda upapannaḥ  bhavati iti yad  tu pratyakṣā samāptiḥ  iti tatra brūmaḥ ādānena śeṣa karma bhaviṣyati iti ucyate ādānam tu  anuityam nityam ca śeṣa karma na hi tayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ  avakalpate tasmāt  cheṣayitavyam kiṃcid  iti tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na etad  asti kiṃcid  cheṣayitavyam iti dīkṣāsu tu vinirdeśaḥ  bhavati prakṛtau   eva jyotiṣṭome sa iha ca udakena prāptaḥ idam kratu artham idam bhakṣya artham idam ānamanāya iti tad  iha yad  ānamanāya dātavyam tasya ayam vikāraḥ sarvatā nāma kuta etad  yatas  svam dadāti iti  anūdyate sarva tā eva vidhīyate tena na adātavyasya dānam vidhīyate na ca bhakṣya artham kratu artham ca dātavyam tasmāt  avirodhaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti asti  ahar gaṇaḥ  aṣṭa rātraḥ atha etasya aṣṭa rātrasya viśva jit  abhijitā   eka āhāv abhitas  ubhayatas  jyotiḥ  madhye ṣaṣ ahar  paśu kāmaḥ  hi  etena yajeta iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ahar gaṇa sthasya api sarva svam eva dakṣiṇā syāt  āhaḥ dvādaśam śatam iti kim prāptam sarva svam kutas  sarveṣām viśva jitām aviśeṣāt  ya eva prakṛtau viśvajitaḥ  dharmaḥ sa eva ca asya ca udakena bhaviṣyati tasmāt  sarva svam deyam iti dvādaśa śātam vā deyam iti prakṛtivat  kartavyam jyotiṣṭoma ś ca prakṛtiḥ tatra dharmā vihitāḥ na viśvajiti kṛtsnāḥ pratīyante tasmāt  dvādaśa śatam atra deyam iti tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na evam bhavitum arhati kutas  na eva yatas  viśvajitaḥ  guṇa u dvādaśa śatam nāmadheyena hi  atra dharma grahaṇam tasmāt  viśvajitaḥ  bhaviṣyati na jyotiṣṭomāt  iti liṅgam khalu  api darśayati kim liṅgam bhavati iti evam āha hīyate vā eṣa paśubhiḥ  yaḥ  viśvajiti sarvam na dadāti iti niyatam sarva sva dānam darśayati  ahar gaṇe viśvajiti sarva svam dadāti iti tatra eṣaḥ  arthaḥ sāṃśayikaḥ kim yasya dvādaśa śatam adhikam ūnam vā vidyate tasya api viśva jita adhikāraḥ uta yasya sakalam adhikam vā tasya eva iti kim prāptam vikāraḥ san   ubhayatas  aviśeṣāt  na viśeṣaḥ kaścid  āśrīyate yasya dvādaśa śatam adhikam ūnam vā asti iti tasmāt  sarvasya viśva jita adhikāra iti na ca etad  asti sarvasya viśva jita adhikāra iti kasya tarhi yasya dvādaśa śatam asti adhikam vā iti kutas  pratiprasavāt  pratiprasavaḥ  hi jyotiṣṭome sarva svasya ucyate dvādaśa śatam vidhāya āha etāvatā vāva ṛtvija āneyā api vā sarva svena iti yadi etāvatā na iccheyuḥ sarva svena api  ānamayitavyā iti tad  yadi dvādaśena śatena na icchanti na icchantitarām tatas  nyūnena tasmāt  dvādaśa śatam jyotiṣṭome yad  vā sarva svam tad  iha ubhayam api prāptam tatra ekaḥ pakṣaḥ  niyamyate sarva svam deyam iti sa eṣa na vidhiḥ prāpta tvāt  aniyata prāpta s tu niyamyate sa ced  niyamyate yādṛśas tatra tādṛśa eva iha tatra ca dvādaśa śatam adhikam vā sarva svam iha api tadvat  eva tasmāt  na nyūna dhanasya adhikāra iti caśabdena anvācayaḥ itas  ca adhikam sarva svam adhike hi dīyamāne tad antargata tvāt  dvādaśa śatam api dattam bhavati pādavat  yathā kārṣāpaṇe dīyamāne pādaḥ  api dattaḥ  bhavati evam iha api iti ādhāne śrūyate ekā deyā ṣaṣ  deyāḥ dvādaśa deyāḥ caturviṃśatiḥ  deyāḥ śatam deyam sahasram deyam aparimitam deyam iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim yad  parimitam ekā deyā iti evamādi tad  na dātavyam iti pratiṣedhaḥ  vidhīyate uta aparimitam nāma kiṃcid  tasya dānam vidhīyata iti kim prāptam aparimite śrūyamāne brūmaḥ śiṣṭasya eka ādeḥ saṃkhyeyasya yā saṃkhyā sā pratiṣidhyate kutas  tad śruti tvāt  parimita śabda śravaṇāt  gaṇitam avagamyate tad  ca eka ādikam tasya na śabdena pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate tatra śrutaḥ  arthaḥ kṛtaḥ  bhavati itarathā parimita śabde prasiddhi s tyajyeta lakṣaṇayā bahu tvam asya arthaḥ kalpyeta tasmāt  aprimitasya pratiṣedha iti kalpa antaram vā syāt  aparaḥ  dāna kalpaḥ  vidhīyate yathā ekā deyā iti dāna vidhi kalpaḥ evam eṣaḥ  api dāna vidhi kalpa eva syāt  tena hi pūrveṇa tulyam eva idam prasaṃkhyāyate kā asya pūrveṇa tulya tā pratijñātasya arthasya avagamikā śrutiḥ  asti iti pūrvatra hi deya śabda śrutyā dānam vidhīyata iti iha api deya śada śrutiḥ sā śrūyamāṇā śaknoti dānam vidhātum pratiṣedhe hi vidhīyamāne vākyasya vyāpāraḥ tad  ca durbalam śrutim prati tasmāt  kalpa antaram yad  ca aparimita śabde prasiddhiḥ  bādhyata iti samudāya prasiddhiḥ  avayava prasiddheḥ  bādhikā eva samadhigatā nanu na atra prasiddhiḥ lakṣaṇā iyam yad  bahu tad  na śakyam parimātum tasmāt  aparimita tvena lakṣyate bahu tvam iti tad  ca na anekasmin   aśakya parimāṇe sati bahuṣu rūḍhaḥ aparimitam asya dhanam bahv iti gamyate yathā kuśalaḥ pravīṇa iti bahuṣu kuśānām lātuḥ guṇeṣu satsu nipuṇa tāyām eva kuśala śabdaḥ  rohāt  rūḍhi śabda eva bhavati bahuṣu ca vīṇā    ādasya guṇeṣu satsu nipuṇa eva pravīṇa śabdaḥ  vartamānaḥ  rūḍha iti  ucyate tasmāt  sati  api lakṣaṇātve śruti sāmarthyāt  rohati śabdaḥ tasmāt  samudāya prasiddhyā parimita śabde avayava prasiddhiḥ  bādhyate aśvakarṇa śabdavat  atas  kalpānataram iti aparimite kalpānataram iti samadhigatam atha idānīm saṃdihyate kim sahasrāt  ūnam aparimitam uta sahasrāt  adhikam iti kim tāvat  prāptam aniyamaḥ  aviśeṣāt  na kaścid  iha bahu tve viśeṣa āsrīyate sahasrāt  ūnam adhikam vā iti anāśrīyamāṇe yathākṛtam tathā sādhu tasmāt tvam ca āpekṣikam kiṃcid  apekṣya tatas  adhikam bahv iti  ucyate asatyām apekṣāyām apraripūrṇam etad  yathā putra iti kiṃcid  apekṣya bhavati na anyathā tatra prakṛtam saṃnihitam ca apekṣya nirṇayaḥ sahasram ca saṃnihitam tasmāt  tatas  adhikam aparimitam iti katham evam tatra utkṛṣṭam vai aparimitam iti tad ūnatām sahasrasya darśayati iha para kṛtayaḥ purā kalpa āḥ  ca udāharaṇam yathā iti ha jñāyate sa ca viśiṣṭa gotrāṇām śrūyate tasmāt  tad gotrāṇām eva kartavyaḥ pañcāvattavat  yathā pañca avattam jamadagnīnām iti tad gotrāṇām eva bhavati evam iha api iti tuśabdāt  eṣaḥ  api pakṣaḥ  vyāvartate vidhā   eteṣām upadeśaḥ syāt  vidhau vedena stuti nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ na vidhi āśraye puruṣe puruṣa grahaṇam vidhi praśaṃsā artham vidhiḥ  iti kriyām āha etasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ  bhāvaḥ yasmāt  anena bahuvacana antānām asamāsa iti ca abhiyukta vacanāt  na hi  etāvat  āyuṣā rasāyanānām saṃbandhaḥ  dṛṣṭa pūrvaḥ na ca saṃbandha adarśane anumānam asti nanu sāmānyatodṛṣṭam bhaviṣyati dṛśyante tāvat kenacid  guṇena avakalpyate na eṣaḥ api pakṣaḥ  yujyate atra api hi sa eva doṣaḥ na tāvaj jīvanam asti yāvatā etad  avakalpyeta dāra agni kāla soma pūrvatva apekṣayā iti tena etasmin   ca kriyamāṇe aparisamāpta eva āyuḥ paryupayuktam syāt  tathā ca adhyayanāt  eva adṛṣṭam kalpyeta evam tarhi dvādaśa ahaḥ prakṛtiḥ  iti pañca pañcāśataḥ  dvādaśa ahā bhaviṣyanti iti tathā ca dṛśyate dvādaśa vai dvādaśa ahe divase dṛṣṭaḥ na dvādaśa rātre tasmāt  na evam vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na ca etad  asti pañca pañcāśataḥ  dvādaśa rātrā iti ahāni  eva trivṛt  chabdena ākhyāyante tasmāt  ahaḥsu saṃvatsara śabda iti athavā vā śabdaḥ pakṣa antaram vyāvartayati na pañca pañcāśātaḥ  māsāḥ kim tarhi divasāḥ dvādaśa ahe trivṛt ahar  prakṛtam tatra saṃvatsara śabdaḥ  dṛśyate ādityaḥ  vā sarva ṛtavaḥ sa yadā eva uditi atha vasantaḥ yadā saṃgavaḥ  atha grīṣmaḥ yadā madhyaṃdinaḥ  atha varṣā yadā aparāhnaḥ  atha śarad  yadā astama iti  atha hemanta śiśirau   iti sarvān ṛtūn ahani saṃpādayati sarve cartavaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ tasmāt  āhar  saṃvatsara śabdena ucyate api ca pañca pañcāśatas trivṛta iti trivṛtām pañcapañcāśat tvam na ca dvādaśa rātra s trivṛt  ekam hi dvādaśa ahe trivṛt ahar  na tatra trivṛt  saṃkhyāyāḥ  dvādaśa rātreṇa mukhyayā vṛttyā sāmānādhikaraṇyam trivṛt ahar  saṃbandha lakṣaṇayā syāt  abhisaṃkhyam trivṛt ahar  tena śrutyā eva sāmānādhikaraṇyam śrutiḥ  ca lakṣaṇāyāḥ  jyāyasī tasmāt  pañca pañcāśat  ahāni saṃvatsaraḥ syāt  iti iha catur hotṛṣv āmnāyate prajā kāmam caturhotrā yājayet  catur gṛhītam ājyam gṛhītvā catur hotāram vyācakṣīta pūrveṇa graheṇa ardham juhuyāt  tad uttareṇa ardham iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim pavamāna iṣṭi saṃskṛteṣu agniṣu  evamādayaḥ uta asaṃskṛteṣu  api tathā pakṣa antara āśrayaṇam api vakṣyamānam vicārayiṣyate kim tāvat  prāptam saṃskṛteṣu  agniṣu  evaṃjātīyakaḥ  akratu śeṣaḥ  api homaḥ syāt  yadi  api  apūrvā darvi homā na kutaścid  dharmān ākāṅkṣanti tathā api  āhavanīyāt ayaḥ  homa ādīn ākāṅkṣanti yad  āhavanīye juhoti tena saḥ  asya abhīṣṭaḥ prītaḥ  bhavati iti evamādibhiḥ śrutibhiḥ evam iṣṭi pūrva tvāt  sarva homānām saṃskṛta agni vṛtti tvam evaṃjātīyakānām iti tuśabdāt  pakṣaḥ  viparivartate catur hotṛ homā asaṃskṛteṣu  agniṣu bhaveyuḥ tathā hi darśayati eṣā vā anāhitāgne r iṣṭiḥ  yad  catur hotāra iti anāhitāgneḥ  iṣṭayaḥ  na vidyante ye tu  ete catur hotārāḥ tasya eṣā eva iṣṭiḥ  iti anāhitāgneḥ  evaṃjātīyakān homān darśayati tasmāt  asaṃskṛteṣu bhaveyuḥ nanu liṅgam asādhakam prāptiḥ  vaktavyā iti tad  ucyate evam tarhi akratu śeṣāṇām vidhiḥ  eṣā bhaviṣyati eṣā anāhitāgneḥ kriyā iti evam arthavat vacanam bhaviṣyati vāda mātram anarthakam bhavati asya ca asti vidhi sāmarthyam tasmāt  vidhiḥ  asaṃskṛteṣu  iti āha etad  gṛhyate vidhiḥ  iti yad  tu akratu śeṣāṇām iti tad  na sarveṣām kratu śeṣāṇām akratu śeṣāṇām ca catur hotṛ homānām kutas  aviśeṣāt  na kratu śeṣāṇām eva ayam dharma ucyate na akratu śeṣāṇām iti tasmāt  sarveṣām api vā iti pakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ akratu śeṣāṇām eva ayam dharmaḥ  na kratu śeṣāṇām kutas  anāhitāgneḥ kratu bhāvāt  na hi  anāhitāgneḥ kratavaḥ santi na ca kratu aṅgam kevalam prayujyamānam kasmaicid  prayojanāya syāt  na ca asya anyat  phalam prakalpyeta pramāṇa abhāvāt  vacanasya hi  anyat  api prayojanam asti na ca anena vacanena śakyate anāhitāgneḥ kratuḥ kalpayitum tasmāt  akratu śeṣāṇām ayam dharma iti vā śabdāt  pakṣaḥ  viparivartate na asaṃskṛteṣu  agniṣu  evaṃjātīyakā homḥāḥ syuḥ kutas  ādhānasya sarva śeṣa tvāt nanu vacanam idam eṣā anāhitāgneḥ  iṣṭiḥ  iti na iti brūmaḥ japa arthavada eṣa bhaviṣyati ye japa rūpa as teṣām artha vādaḥ na sarveṣām catur hotṝṇām evam yad āhavanīye johoti iti evamādīnām vacanānām arthavat tā bhaviṣyati yad  uktam eṣā vānāhita tā agneḥ kriyā iṣṭi tulya iti japānām eṣa vāda iti tad  na na eṣā vacana vyaktiḥ yā eṣā anāhitāgneḥ kriyā sa iṣṭi tulya iti kim kāraṇam sādṛśya mātra anuvādaḥ  anarthakaḥ syāt  itarasmin pakṣe vidhiḥ  arthavān yā iyam iṣṭiḥ eṣā anāhitāgneḥ  iti tad iṣṭi saṃstavāt  dhomānām eva vādaḥ katham iṣṭiḥ  yāgaḥ sa eva āsecana adhikaḥ  homaḥ yad  uktam sarva homa artha āhavanīya iti tad  na catur hotṝn eva adhikṛtya ucyate kim tu  aviśeṣeṇa homān sa catur hotṛṣv asaṃbhavāt  anyeṣu bhaviṣyati catur hotṛṣu ca anāhitāgneḥ  ucyamāneṣu  āhavanīyaḥ  na aṅgam iti na etad  asti anāhitāgneḥ  eva catur hotāra iti ubhayoḥ syuḥ pitryajñavat  yathā pitṛ yajña āhitāgneḥ  anāhitāgna īḥ  ca evam catur hotāraḥ  api katham avagamyate varṇitam etad  yadā anuvāda pakṣaḥ tad ā āhitāgneḥ yadā vidhi pakṣaḥ tadā anāhitāgneḥ ubhayathā vacana vyaktiḥ pratīyate na ca pratīyamānaḥ  arthaḥ śakyate apahnotum tasmāt  ubhayoḥ  catur hotāra iti na ca etad  asti ubhayoḥ  catur hotāraḥ  bhaveyuḥ  iti katham eṣa hi  anāhitāgni nirdeśaḥ eṣā veṣṭiḥ  anāhitāgneḥ  iti vacanena adhikṛtaḥ na āhitāgniḥ nirdeśa sāmarthyāt  artha vāde ca upakṣīṇam tatra eva na virudhyata iti yad āhavanīye juhoti iti vacanam na catur hotṝn eva adhikṛtya ucyata iti  uktam tasmāt  anāhitāgneḥ  evaṃjātīyakā homāḥ atha yad  uktam pitṛ yajñavat  iti yuktam pitṛ yajñe tatra āhitāgni saṃyuktasya punar  etad vacanam bhavati api  anāhitāgninā kārya iti etad vacanam anāhitāgneḥ  api iti  anāhitāgnau   anvāhāryakam karoti iha tathā na asti vacanam niyogata ekaḥ  nirdeśaḥ eṣā vā anāhitāgneḥ  iti na atra api śabdaḥ  asti tasmāt  pitṛ yajñena atulyam etad  idam āmananti upanayaṃ   tisṛbhiḥ  juhuyāt  iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ayam homa ādhāna saṃskṛteṣu  agniṣu uta asaṃskṛteṣu  iti kim prāptam uapanayan   ādadhīta iti kutas  homa saṃyogāt  āhavanīyasya yad  āhavanīye juhoti tena saḥ  asya abhīṣṭaḥ prītaḥ  bhavati iti tasmāt  ādhāna uttara kālā ete homā iti sthitiḥ na ca etad  asti ādhāya evaṃjātīyakam hotavyam iti kim tarhi laukika eva pravarteta iti kutas  vidyā karma ānupūrva tvāt vidyā grahaṇa arthā ime homāḥ vidyāvataḥ  ca ādhānena adhikāraḥ sāmarthyāt  ata ādhāna uttara kālatā na eṣām avakalpate yathā sthapati iṣṭyām ādhānam ca bhāryā saṃyuktam śrūyate vidyā grahaṇa uttara kālaḥ  ca dāra saṃgrahaḥ tasmāt  api na avakalpate pūrva kālatā ādhānasya tatra āha yā pūrvam ādhānāt  dārakriyā sā karma arthā bhaviṣyati vacanāt  ca ūrdhvam ādhānāt  apatya arthā dvayoḥ  api kālayoḥ piṇḍa pitṛ yajñavan na eṣa doṣaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti atra ucyate akarma ca dārakriyā yādhāna uttara kāle kutas  āhavanīya ādi samavāyaḥ  hi karmabhiḥ  bhavati svārthaṇ ca agnaya ādhātavyā iti niyamaḥ tasmāt  ubhayasmin   api kāle dāra saṃgraha iti  etad  na asti na evam śruti vipratiṣedhaḥ  hi bhavati evam kriyamāṇe dārakarmaṇi vidyā grahaṇa uttara kālam śrūyamāṇam pūrvam kriyata iti vipratiṣiddham arthāt  anyat  eva idam iti ced  na artha prāptasya eva kāla niyama eṣaḥ upanayanam ca karma artham tad  dvitīyasyām vipratiṣidhyeta atha ucyate prāk ādhānāt  ca karma artha eva ūrdhvam cāpatya artha eva asya bhaviṣyati tena evam sati  asya na kiṃcid  virotsyata iti ucyate na etad  evam sva arthā hi sā na kevalam apatya artha tām eṣyati tad  uktam phala utsāhā viśeṣāt  iti tasmāt  api na dvis  dāra saṃgrahaḥ api ca evam smaryate dharme ca arthe ca kāme ca na ati caritavyā iti evam sati  ati caritā syāt  atas  na dvis  dāra saṃgrahaḥ ekā eva bhāryā karma artha apatya arthā ca tasya āś ca vidyā grahaṇa uttara kālatā atas  na ādhāna saṃskṛteṣu  ete homā iti gṛhyata etad  prāk upanayanān na asti patnī iti yad  uktam ekā eva patnī iti tad  na mṛṣyate yathā eva smṛtiḥ dharme ca arthe ca kāme ca na ati caritavyā iti dharma prajā saṃpanne dāre na anyām kurvīta iti ca evam idam api smaryata eva anyatara apāye anyām kurvīta iti tasmāt  yasya na dharma saṃpannā na prajā saṃpannā vā patnī saḥ  anyām kurvīta iti soma pānāt  iti ca artha vādam vyapadiśati sma somapaḥ  na dvitīyām jāyām abhyaṣūyata iti dvitīyām api jāyām darśayati atha katham pitṛ yajñasya dvau kālauv iti ucyate vacanam hi tatra dṛśyate api anāhitāgninā kāry iti tasmāt  prāk ādhānāt  pitṛ yajña iti asti sthapati iṣṭiḥ etayā niṣāda sthapitam yājayeta iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim ādhāna saṃskṛteṣu  agniṣu syāt  uta laukikeṣu  iti kim prāptam saṃskṛteṣu  iti katham yad āhavanīye juhoti iti evamādi vacanāt  nanu śūdrasya āhavanīya abhāvān na asti tasya śrutiḥ  iti ucyate sā hi  āhavanīyam prayojayet  yathā prayājān aśrutān prayojayati evam ca udaka sāmarthyāt  iti tādarthyā c ca apavṛjyeta sthapati iṣṭi artham ca āhitā agnayaḥ tasyām apavṛktāyām apavṛjyeran dhāraṇam hi teṣām dṛṣṭa kāryam āmnātam atikrānte kārye na syāt  iti api vā iti pakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ laukikeṣu  agniṣu syāt  na saṃskṛteṣu kutas  ādhānasya asarva śeṣa tvāt sarva karma śeṣa bhūtā agnayaḥ tad aṅgam ādhānam na karma aṅgam śruti ādīnām abhāvān na karma prayukta ādhānasya vākya sāmarthyāt  ca agni prayukta tvam yad  ca darśa pūrṇamāsa prayuktam tad  ca udakena prāpyate na dravya prayuktam tasmāl laukikeṣu  agniṣu sthapati iṣṭiḥ  iti asti  avakīrṇi paśuḥ brahmacārī avakīrṇī nairṛtam gardabham ālabheta iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim tad artham ādhānam kartavyam uta laukikeṣu  agniṣu tad  varteta iti avakīrṇi paśuḥ  ca tadvat  iti  adhikaraṇa atideśaḥ pūrvasya adhikaraṇasya yaḥ pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ saḥ  atra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ yaḥ siddhāntaḥ sa siddhāntaḥ sarva artham ādhānam tasmāt  āhitāgniṣu  iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ ādhānasya aprāpta kāla tvāt  iti siddhāntaḥ aprāptaḥ  ayam ādhānasya kāla iti  etad  uktam tasmāt  idam api karma laukikeṣu  iti daivāni karmāṇi  udāharaṇam upanayana prabhṛtīni tatra saṃdehaḥ kim aniyate kāle daivāni kartavyāni utoda gayana pūrva pakṣa ahaḥ puṇya aheṣu  iti aniyata iti prāpte udagayana ādiṣu  iti  ucyate kutas  evam smaranti teṣu kāleṣu daivāni iti rūpa artha vādaḥ  ca etad  vai devānām rūpam yad  udagayanam pūrva pakṣaḥ  aha iti na ca vayam deva ādīnām rūpam vidmaḥ atha tu  eṣu kāleṣu daivāni kriyante tatas  etena saṃbandhena rūpa vacanam avakalpate anya artham ca vākyam etad  darśayati pūrvāhnaḥ  vai devānām madhyaṃdinaḥ  manuṣyāṇām aparāhnaḥ pitṝṇām iti tasmāt  eteṣu kāleṣu daivāni syuḥ  iti ahani ca viśeṣaḥ sakalam karma ahani  eva śakyate kartum iti na rātrau kariṣyati śrāddha ādīni  apara pakṣe aparāhne ca smṛti rūpa anyārtha darśanāt  idam samāmnāyate jyotiṣṭome dvādaśa rātrīḥ  dīkṣitaḥ  bhṛtim vanvīta iti tathā somam krīṇāti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim yasya na vidyate bhṛtiḥ tena vanitavyā yasya ca na vidyate somaḥ tena kretavyaḥ uta ubhathā api sati ca asati ca kim prāptam yāñca ākrayaṇam avidyamāne bhṛti dhane some ca syāt  kasmāt  dravya sadbhāva artham yāñca ākrayaṇam tad  vidyamāne anarthakam anarthakam ca uktam api na kartavyam tasmāt  avidyamāne bhavet  lokavat  yathā yasya loke na asti dravyam sa yācate krīṇāti ca evam iha api draṣṭavyam niyatam vā yāñca ākrayaṇam tad  vidyamāne avidyamāne ca dravye syāt  evam yāñca ākrayaṇam arthavat  bhavati jyotiṣṭoma prayuktam hi tad  chrūyate na dravya prayuktam tad  ca nityam jyotiṣṭomasya na evam vacanam bhavati yadā dravyam na asti tadā kartavyam iti jyotiṣṭomasya ca nityam aṅgam uktam dravya abhāvaḥ  nimittam uktam iti parikalpyeta kalpanāyām śabdaḥ  bādhyeta atas  yāñcākrayaṇa saṃskṛtam dravyam iha upayoktavyam anyathā vaiguṇyam bhavati tasmāt  sati ca asati ca dravye yāñca ākrayaṇam anuṣṭātavyam iti atha yad  uktam lokavat  iti loke karma artha lakṣaṇam bhavati na śabda lakṣaṇam yathārthaḥ tathā kriyate na yathā śabdaḥ vede tu śabdena eva arthaḥ  avagamyate tathā eva anuṣṭheyam iti tasmāt  vidyamāne api kartavyam jyotiṣṭome śrūyate payaḥ  vratam brāhmaṇasya yavāgū rājanyasya āmikṣā vaiśyasya iti tathā darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ praiṣaḥ prokṣaṇīḥ  āsādaya idhmam bahis  upasādaya srucaḥ saṃmṛḍḍhi patnīm saṃnahya ājyena udehi iti tathā vājapeye śrūyate darbha mayam vāsaḥ  bhavati iti paśau saṃjñapta homaḥ yad  paśuḥ  māyum akṛta uraḥ  vā padbhiḥ  āhata agniḥ  mā tasmāt  enasaḥ  viśvān muñca tvam hasa iti tathā yaḥ  asmān dveṣṭi yam ca vayam dviṣma iti vacanam etāni  udāharaṇa vacanāni teṣu saṃdehaḥ kim yasya aparam bhojanam na vidyate sa payaḥ  vratayet  yavāgūm āmikṣām vā uta vidyamāne api iti tathā yaḥ  preṣitaḥ praiṣa artham na pratipadyate sa preṣitavyaḥ uta pratipadyamānaḥ  api iti tathā yasya sūtra mayam vāsaḥ  na asti sa darbha mayam paridadhīta uta vidyamāne api iti tathā yasya paśuḥ  māyum kuryāt  uraḥ  vā pādau vā hanyāt  sa etena mantreṇa juhuyāt  uta anyaḥ  api iti tathā yaḥ  dveṣṭi kiṃcid  anyena ca dviṣyate sa eva mantram brūyāt  yaḥ  asmān dveṣṭi iti uta adviṣat    adviṣyamāṇaḥ  ca api iti tatra adhikaraṇa atideśaḥ  ayam tatra yaḥ pūrvasmin   adhikaraṇe pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ sa iha pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ yaḥ  tatra siddhāntaḥ sa iha siddhāntaḥ avidyamāne kuryāt  iti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ niyatam vā arthavat tvāt  iti  uttaraḥ sa eva atra nyāyaḥ yaḥ pūrvatra jyotiṣṭome śrūyate madhyaṃdine apararātre vā vratam vratayati iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim niyatam apararātre vratam uta aniyatam iti kim prāptam niyatam ca arthavat tvāt  syāt  iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ anarthakam tu  anityam syāt  yadā evam manyeta asmin kāle vratam me jariṣyati iti tadā vratayet  yadā tu khalu manyeta na samyak  jariṣyati iti tadā tad vratam kriyamāṇam anarthakam syāt  yadi hi  ajīrṇena yajamānaḥ  mriyeta tadā tantra lopaḥ tantra lope ca sarva lopaḥ tasmāt  aniyatam tasmin kāle vratam vratayitavyam iti jyotiṣṭome paśuḥ  agnīṣomīyaḥ yaḥ  dīkṣitaḥ  yad  agnīṣomīyam paśum ālabhata iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim yaḥ kaścid  paśuḥ  ā lambhīyaḥ uta chāga iti vakṣyamāṇena abhiprāyeṇa bhavati saṃśayaḥ nanu  ekeṣām āmnāyate ajaḥ agnīṣomīya iti sarva śākhā pratyayam ca ekam karma iti atra ucyate pratiśākham bhinnāni karmāṇi iti kṛtvā cintā kim tāvat  prāptam paśu codanāyām aniyamaḥ utsarge kartavye dravyam śakyata utsraṣṭum na paśu tvam dravyam hi sādhakam atas  atra dravyam antreṇa utsargaḥ  na saṃbhavati iti dravyam upādīyate tasmin   upādīyamāne aniyamaḥ yad kiṃcid  utsraṣṭavyam iti kuta etad  aviśeṣāt  na hi paśutva saṃbaddheṣu kaścid  viśeṣa upalabhyate tasmāt  yaḥ kaścid  paśuḥ  iti vā śabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na etad  asti yatra kvacana dravye paśu tvam upādeyam iti asti  utsraṣṭavyasya niyama kāraṇam mantra varṇaḥ agnaye chāgasya vayāyā medasaḥ  anubrūhi iti chāga prakāśana samarthaḥ  mantra varṇaḥ samāmnāyate yadi chāgaḥ  na upādeyaḥ tatas  tad prakāśana samarthasya upādānam anarthavat  tena avagamyate chāgam adhikṛtya utsargam vidadhāti iti māntra varṇikaḥ  dravya niyama vidhiḥ  iti na etad  evam na śaknoti mantra varṇa ś codanāyām pratyarthinyām dravyam niyantum yatra hi dravyasya prakāśakam na śrūyate tatra aprakāśitam eva tad  kartavyam iti tasmāt  na mantra varṇāt  prakāśya niyama vidhiḥ kalpyate evam atra prakāśyam prakāśayitavyam iti atra punar  śabdena avagamyate paśutvena prakāśayitavyam iti tasmāt  na mantra varṇa s tad sadbhāve samarthaḥ mantra varṇāt  dhi kalpyā prayoga vacana śrutiḥ iha kḷptā prayoga vacanena upasaṃhartavyā anya eva paśu śabdasya arthaḥ paśu tvam anyaḥ  mantra varṇena niyamyate chāgaḥ tasmāt  na mantra varṇa ś codanā virodhena niyantum arhati iti iti ced  paśyasi na paśu tvam anyebhyaḥ paśubhya ācchetavyam iti yathā ārṣeyam vṛṇīte trīn vṛṇīta iti sāmānya śruti s triṣu  eva avatiṣṭhata iti tri tvam viśeṣaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ  na anye vivakṣitā iti evam iha api paśu tvam chāgam prakalpayitum vivakṣitam na anyān viśeṣān iti na etad  evam tatra hi  acoditam dravyam utsraṣṭavyam mantra varṇe varaṇe punar  coditam tatra tritva saṃkhyā saṃbandhasya varaṇe codita tvāt  na anyā saṃkhyā kriyate ārṣeya śabdāt  api na anā ārṣeyam tri śabdasya hi tad sāmarthyam yena ārṣeya śabdaḥ  viśiṣṭa saṃkhyā viṣayaḥ  niyamyate iha na mantrasya sāmarthyam tasmāt  aniyama iti niyamaḥ  vā aikārthyam hi paśu chāga śabdayoḥ sāmānyam paśuḥ  iti chāga āt ayaḥ  viśeṣā ucyante katham taiḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyāt paśuḥ  chāgaḥ paśuḥ  uṣṭraḥ paśuḥ  meṣaḥ paśuḥ  usra iti evam sati na mantra varṇaḥ paśu śabdena virudhyate tena chāgaḥ  api  ālabdha vyaś coditaḥ mantra varṇa upādīyamāne idam avagamyate chāgam vivakṣitvā ayam paśu śabda uccarita iti na
