anyān viśeṣān iti chāga upakaraṇam asya upadaṃśitam yad  upadaṃśane paśu śabdaḥ  chāga abhiprāya iti gamyate yathā yuga varatra upadaṃśite īṣā cakra ādi saṃnidhāne ced  akṣam ānayā iti  ucyate tadā yāna akṣam adhikṛtya brūta iti gamyate na tu videvana akṣam iti yadi hi  artha bhedaḥ  bhavet  paśu chāga śabdayoḥ pṛthaktvena abhidhānam tatas  bhedaḥ syāt  na chāga eva niyamyeta avihita ś chāga artha  iti  aśva upādānam api ca chāga pakṣe tam mantra varṇaḥ prakāśayet  chāga artha abhidhāne punar  paśu śabdasya chāga prāptau   anyeṣām aprāptiḥ  iti  anyasmin prāpte liṅgena niyamaḥ kriyata iti aniyamaḥ  vā yaḥ kaścid  paśuḥ  upādeyaḥ artha antara tvāt  artha antaram paśu tvam artha antaram chāga tvam arthayoḥ  atra sāmānādhikaraṇyam na śabdayoḥ katham punar  artha antaram gamyate vyatirekāt  chabda bhedāt  ca vyatirekaḥ  hi bhavati kaścid  paśuḥ  na chāgaḥ tathā chāgaḥ paśuḥ  iti śabda bhedaḥ śabda bhedāt  eva artha bhedaḥ  nyāyyaḥ ekasmin vākye samavāyāt  paśum chāgam ānaya iti itarathā anyatareṇa kṛtārtha tvāt  anyataraḥ  vākye na samaveyāt  samavaiti ca tasmāt  anyat  paśu tvam anya t  chāga tvam tasmāt  aniyamaḥ yaḥ kaścid  paśuḥ  upādeya iti tatra utsūtrikā pakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ anya tve api sati niyama eva kutas  mantrasya prayoga vacanena gṛhīta tvāt  mantra sādhanam hi karma iti gamyate yadi chāgam upādāsyāmahe sa guṇam karma śakṣāmaḥ kartum mantram upādadānāḥ mantrasya āpākṣika tvāt  atha anyam upādāsyāmahe mantrasya viṣaya abhāvān mantram apajahataḥ  na sa guṇam karma nirvartayema atas  na ca śrutim bādhāmahe anyasmin paśu śabdaḥ  vartata iti na ca anyam upādāsyāmahe vaiguṇyāt  bibhyataḥ tasmāt  chāga eva upādātavya iti nanu  aśvam upādadānā na eva mantra varṇam apahāsyāmaḥ sa eva aśvaś chāgaḥ  bhaviṣyati yaḥ  chinna gamanaḥ  aśvaḥ sa chāgaḥ chideḥ  gameś ca cchāga śabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ kvacid  muṣkarā bhaviśyanti iti śrūyate yadi  antareṇa vacanam amuṣkarās tadā idam upapadyate tasmāt  chinna gamanaḥ  aśvaḥ api chāga iti karma ākhyā bhaviṣyati atra ucyate  chāge karma ākhyā rūpa liṅgābhyām na avakalpate na hi chāga śabdaḥ  chinna gamana vacanaḥ samudāyaḥ  hi  asau pṛthak  artha antare prasiddhaḥ na asau   avayava prasiddhyā bādhitavyaḥ tasmāt  na aśvaḥ  chāgaḥ idam anya pada uttaram sūtram atha kasmān na vayaḥ vacanaḥ  bhavati vayaḥ vacanā hi  ete śabdāḥ chāgaḥ  chāgalaḥ  vatsa iti tena aśvaḥ api vayaḥ vacanaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti ucyate na etad  evam satyam vayaḥ vacanaḥ ajāpati gatam tu vayaḥ  vaditum śaknoti yathā śoṇa iti varṇa vacanaḥ  aśva jāti gatam varṇam vadati na anyam tasmāt  rūpa anyatvān na vayaḥ mātra vacanaḥ kim tu jāti śabdaḥ syāt  jāti āśrayam vayaḥ  vadet  atas  chāga eva niyamyate idam api pada uttaram iha aśva ādīnām vikāraḥ  chāga śabdaḥ kiṃcid  atra aśva ādīnām uccāryate na kiṃcid  anyat  eva tasmāt  āśvaḥ  api chāga iti na utpattika tvāt  autpattikaḥ hi nāmi nāmnoḥ saṃbandha iti  uktam na ākhya avikāraḥ saṃbhavati iti tasmāt  na aśvaḥ  chāgaḥ atas  chāga eva upādātvaya iti na utpattika tvāt  ṃś pada uttaram eva idam sūtram atha kasmān na chidra nimittaḥ  chāga śabdaḥ  bhavati evam śrūyate śuṣiraḥ  vā etarhi paśuḥ yarhi vapām utkhadanti iti na iti  ucyate chidra tvasya guṇasya paśoḥ  acodita tvāt  avyaṅgam paśum ālabheta iti hi codyate tasmāt  acchidraḥ paśuḥ na ca avayava prasiddhyā samudāya prasiddhiḥ  bādhyata iti  uktam eva tasmāt  chāga eva upādeyaḥ  na āśvādaya iti vā śabdaḥ  avadhāraṇāyām yasmāt  avayava prasiddhyā samudāya prasiddhiḥ  na bādhyate tasmāt  jāteḥ  eva chāga śabdaḥ  vācakaḥ evam samudāyasya arthavat tā anugṛhītā bhaviṣyati iti tad prāya vacanam upapadyate viśveṣām devānām usrāṇām chāgānām meṣāṇām vapānām medasaḥ  anubrūhi iti jāti prāye vacanam upapadyate prāyeṇa api hi niyamaḥ kriyate yathā agrya prāye likhitam dṛṣṭvā agnyaḥ  ayam iti buddhiḥ  bhavati tasmāt  chāga eva upādātavya iti kṛtvā acintāyām prayojanam na vaktavyam pūrveṇa adhyāya ṣaṭkena pratyakṣa vihita dharmaṇām karmaṇām darśa pūrṇamāsa ādīnām itikartavya tā cintitā uttareṇa idānīm avihita iti kartavya tākeṣu  aindra agna ādiṣu cintayitum iṣyate tatra yadi darśa pūrṇamāsa ādīnām prakaraṇe ye vihitā dharmāḥ te sarva karmasu vihitā bhavanti tatas  taiḥ  eva dharmaiḥ  aindra agna ādayaḥ  api dharmavanta uktāḥ tathā kartavyāḥ  ca iti na artha uttareṇa ṣaṭkena atha ye yasya prakaraṇa ucyante te tatra eva uktā bhavanti tatas  adharmakāṇi  aindra agnīdīni teṣu cintā bhavati kim eṣām dharmāḥ santi uta na iti yadā ca santi tadā ke kiyantaḥ  vā katham ca anuṣṭātavyā iti tad  artham uttaraḥ ṣaṭkaḥ pravartanīyaḥ tatra saptamena tāvat  santi dharmā iti  ucyate aṣṭamena ca ime asya iti ittham prayoktavyā iti navamena daśam aikādaśa dvādaśaiḥ  etāvantaḥ prayoktavyāḥ na atas  adhikā iti tatra idam vicāryate kim yaji prayuktā ete dharmāḥ katham yajir guṇavān syāt  iti  evam artham āmnāyante āhosvit  apūrva prayuktāḥ katham apūrvam syāt  iti yadi yaji prayuktāḥ tatas  sarva arthāḥ atha apūrva prayuktāḥ tatas  yathāprakaraṇam vyavatiṣṭhante kim punar  atra yuktam apūrva prayuktā iti apūrvam hi phalavat  aphalaḥ  yajiḥ phalavati ca prayāsaḥ  vidhīyamānaḥ  arthavān bhavati tasmāt  apūrva prayuktā dharmāḥ atas  parama ācāryasya sūtra upanyāsaḥ śruti pramāṇa tvāt  cheṣāṇām mukhya bhede yathā adhikāram bhāvaḥ syāt  iti mukhyāni  apūrvāṇi tāni hi phalavat tvāt  pradhānāni pradhāne ca mukhya śabdaḥ teṣām bheda uktaḥ śabda antara ādibhiḥ  hetubhiḥ tasmin mukhya bhede sati yathā adhikāram bhāvaḥ syāt  śeṣāṇām ye yasya apūrvasya adhikāre prakaraṇe śiṣyante te tasya eva bhaveyuḥ śruti pramāṇa tvāt  ayam asya apūrvasya śeṣaḥ ayam asya iti  atra śrutiḥ  eva pramāṇam kramate na pratyakṣa ādīnām anyatamat  śrutyā ca ye yasya prakaraṇe śrūyante te tasya eva bhavitum arhanti na ca anyasya uktaḥ  arthaḥ  anyasya bhavati na hi yad  devadattasya grāmāt  chādana ādikam tad  yajñadattasya bhavati tasmāt  yathāprakaraṇam vyavasthā dharmāṇām atha vā na etad  evam yathāprakaraṇam dharmāṇām vyavasthā iti kim tarhi aika dharmyam syāt  iti samāna dharma tā sarve dharmāḥ sarva arthāḥ kutas  utpatti artha avibhāgāt utpattiḥ  iti yajim brūmaḥ apūrvasya utpādanāt  artha iti  apūrvam brūmaḥ yaji prayojana tvāt  tayoḥ  avibhāgaḥ sarvāṇi  apūrvāṇi yajimanti yaji saṃyogena dharmāḥ śiṣyante yajeta iti  uktvā uktāḥ te yajau na saṃbhavanti tasya aphala tvāt  tatra asaṃbhavanta s tad saṃbaddheṣu  apūrveṣu vijñāyante sa ca yaji saṃbandhaḥ sarveṣām apūrvāṇām tulyaḥ tasmāt  sarva arthā bhavanti satva dharmavat  yathā satva dharmāḥ gauḥ  na padā praṣṭavya iti gaḥtva saṃbandhena śrūyamāṇā as tatra asaṃbhavanta s tad saṃbaddheṣu piṇḍeṣu vijñāyante tasya ca gaḥtva saṃbandhasya aviśeṣāt  sarva gavīṣu śukla nīla kapilakapotikāsu bhavanti evam iha api ucyate viṣama upanyāsaḥ tatra gaḥ sāmānya saṃbandhena dharmā vidhīyante gauḥ  na padā praṣṭavya iti iha punar  yaji viśeṣa saṃbandhena dharmā vidhīyante darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta iti jyotiṣṭomena yajeta iti viśiṣṭa yaji saṃbaddha eva apūrve bhavitum arhanti na sarvatra iti tatra brūmaḥ darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta ittham iti yadi yajir vidhīyeta na dharmaiḥ saṃbadhyeta na hi dvayoḥ  vidhīyamānayoḥ paraspareṇa saṃbandhaḥ  bhavati anuvādaḥ  ca san   aviśeṣāt  sarva yāga anuvādaḥ tasmāt  sarvathā dharmāḥ nanu darśa pūrṇamāsa śabdaḥ  viśeṣa kaḥ  bhaviṣyati na darśa pūrṇamāsa śabdaḥ śaknoti yāgam viśeṣṭum ayam hi vidhiḥ  vā syāt  anuvādaḥ  vā yadā anuvādaḥ tadā dharma saṃbandha arthaḥ sa ca dharma saṃbandhaḥ  yāga anuvādena eva tayoḥ siddhaḥ nanu nivṛtti karaḥ  bhaviṣyati darśa pūrṇamāsau   eva ittham kuryāt  na anyān iti na evam śakyam yad  kāraṇam na tasya anya nivṛttiḥ arthaḥ nanu parisaṃkhyayā kariṣyati na atra parisaṃkhyā yujyate yadi  anyena vākyena yāga mātre dharma prasaṅgaḥ kṛtaḥ syāt  tatas  etad  punarvacanam parisaṃkhyām kuryāt  atha punar  asati prasaṅge anena eva prasaṅgaḥ  anena eva nivṛttiḥ  iti  atibhāra ekasya eva vākyasya bhavati evam tarhi na atra yajeta iti śabdaḥ  dharma vidhibhiḥ saṃbadhyate yajeta ittham iti kena tarhi darśa pūrṇamāsa śabdena pratyakṣaḥ  hi tena asya saṃyogaḥ darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta iti parokṣaḥ  dharma vidhibhiḥ kas tadā vākya arthaḥ darśa pūrṇamāsau kuryāt  iti na evam śakyam evam sati dharmā asaṃbaddhāḥ pāriplavā bhavanti katham kṛtvā yā iyam ākhyātikī vibhaktiḥ yajeta iti sā darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ kartavyatām vidadhāti tatra katham yāga mātreṇa yāga viśeṣeṇa vā dharma saṃbandhaḥ syāt  vidhāyikā vibhaktiḥ  na asti iti  asaṃbaddhā dharmā bhavanti na eṣa doṣaḥ na vayam vākyena dharmāṇām saṃbandham kariṣyāmaḥ kena tarhi prakaraṇena katham kartavyatāyām coditāyām itikartavya tā kāṅkṣā bhavati katham kuryāt  iti prakaraṇena dharmāḥ saṃbadhyanta ittham kuryāt  iti na evam śakyam yadā hi darśa pūrṇamāsau kartavya tayā codyate tadā itikartavya tā kāṅkṣā eva na asti prajñāta iti karti avyatatvāt tayoḥ asatyām ca iti kartavya tā kāṅkṣāyām prakaraṇam eva na asti evam hi  uktam asaṃyuktam prakaraṇāt  itikartavya tā arthi tvāt  iti evam tarhi na eva atra yāge dharmā vidhīyante na api darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ kartavyatā ucyate kim tarhi darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta iti pada dvayena viśiṣṭam yāgam anūdya atra dharmā vidhīyante darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta ittham iti evam api darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām iti  anuvādaḥ  na yujyate tṛtīya arthasya asiddha tvāt pūrvān anuvādaḥ  bhavati apūrvaḥ  ca tṛtīya arthaḥ saḥ  avaśyam vidhātavyaḥ tasmin   ca vidhīyamāne anyat  eva asaṃbaddham āpadyate darśa pūrṇamāsau yajeḥ karaṇam iti tasmāt  sa eva prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ  astu yāga anuvādena dharmāṇām vidhiḥ  iti nanu tatra api darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām iti  etad  na saṃbadhyate nanu saṃbhantsyate kāla vacanaḥ san prāyikaḥ  nitya anuvādaḥ  bhaviṣyati prāyeṇa yāgānām darśa pūrṇamāsa kāla tvāt tṛtīyā ca kālasya artha kṛtam guṇa bhāvam ālocya upapadyate tathā ced  sarve dharmāḥ sarva arthāḥ bhavanti karma codanāyāḥ śeṣa bhūtaḥ  dharma samāmnāya eka deśa bhūta  iti  arthaḥ darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta anayā agni avādhānādikayā itikartavyatayā iti tasyām codanāyām yajeḥ  guṇa bhāvaḥ śrūyate darśa pūrṇamāsa śabdaḥ  yajivacanaḥ karaṇa bhāvaḥ  atra yajeḥ śrūyate darśa pūrṇamāsa ākhyena yāga samudāyena anyat kuryāt  iti yad  tatas  anyat  tad kartavya tayā codyate na yajiḥ apūrvam ca tad  nanu phalam atra vākye śrūyate svarga kāmaḥ  yateta iti tad kartavyam syāt  satyam śrūyate na tu tad yajinā kriyate vinaṣṭe yajau tad  bhavati apūrvam tu tena kriyate tasmāt  tasya kartavyatā ucyate yasya kartavyatā tad  itikartavya tayā saṃbadhyate tasmāt  apūrva arthā dharmāḥ teṣām ca apūrvāṇām bhedaḥ atas tad bhedāt  yathāprakaraṇam vyavatiṣṭhante dharmā iti atha etasmin pakṣe katham darśa pūrṇamāsa śabdena yāgaḥ  viśeṣyate ucyate na eva atra yāgaḥ  viśiṣyate kim tarhi apūrva bhāvanā eva ubhaya pada viśiṣṭa ucyate yathā aruṇayā piṅga akṣya eka hāyanyā somam krīṇāti iti viṣama upanyāsaḥ tatra hi  anyat  dravyam anyaḥ  guṇaḥ tena tatra ubhaya viśeṣaṇa tvam yujyate iha punar  yāgaḥ eva tau darśa pūrṇamāsau tena iha ubhaya viśeṣaṇa tvam na yujyate ucyate iha api yajeta iti sāmānyam darśa pūrṇamāsau   iti viśeṣaḥ anya t  ca sāmānyam anyaḥ  viśeṣaḥ evam api śrutyā sāmānyena bhāvanā vākyāt  viśeṣeṇa na ca etad  yugapad  bhavati iti evam tarhi na eva atra śruti arthe parigṛhyate kim tarhi vākya arthaḥ kim kāraṇam śruti arthe parigṛhyamāṇe darśa pūrṇamāsa śabdaḥ  anartha kaḥ  bhavati yajatiḥ  ca anuvādaḥ yajati  ātmaka tvāt  darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ yajati sāmānādhikaraṇyā c ca darśa pūrṇamāsa śabdasya yad  tu satvavat  iti atra gavākṛtau dharmaḥ śrūyate ākṛteḥ padārtha tvāt na ca tatra saṃbhavati atas  asau   ākṛtiḥ sahacāri piṇḍa lakṣaṇa arthā vijñāyate yathā gaṅgāyām gāva iti tad  ca sāhacaryam sarva piṇḍānām aviśiṣṭam iti sarva piṇḍeṣu vihitam bhavati tasmāt  tad  sārvatrikam pratīyeta iha tu yajeḥ  guṇa bhavena śravaṇān na eva yajau dharmāḥ śrūyante kim tarhi apūrva iti  evam apadiṣṭaḥ  hetuḥ tasmāt  anupanyāsaḥ satvavat  iti atha tuśabdaḥ pakṣa vyāvṛttau na etad  evam apūrva prayuktā dharmā iti yaji prayuktā eva kutas  avibhāgāt  yajina avibhāgaḥ  dharmāṇām pratyakṣam kecid  dravye śrūyante kecid  devatāyām kecid  mantreṣu eṣa ca yajiḥ yad  dravyam devatām uddiśya mantreṇa tyajyate sa eṣa pratyakṣaḥ  yajinā saṃbandhaḥ  dharmāṇām apūrveṇa tu  ānumānikaḥ phale api yajeḥ pratyakṣa śrutaḥ  guṇa bhāvaḥ svarga kāmaḥ  yajeta iti ānumānikaḥ  apūrveṇa anumānāc ca pratyakṣam balīyaḥ tasmāt  yaji arthāḥ dharmāḥ nanu yajir bhaṅgi tvāt  kāla antare phalam dātum asamarthaḥ tatra kṛtā dharmā asamarthā eva bhavati iti  uktam atra sthitasya nyāyasya ākṣepeṇa pratyavasthānam kriyate taila pānavat  etad  bhaviṣyati yathā taila pānam ghṛta pānam vā bhaṅgi tve api sati kāla antare medhā smṛti bala puṣṭi ādīni phalāni karoti evam yajir api kariṣyati kim naḥ adṛṣṭa aśrutena apūrveṇa kalpitena iti evam ca sati sarve dharmāḥ sarva arthā bhavanti tathā ca aindra agna ādiṣu prayāja ādayaḥ santi tatra saurye karmaṇi prayājānām darśanam upapadyate prayāje prayāje kṛṣṇalam juhoti iti itarathā prayājāḥ  ca vidhātavyāḥ prayājeṣu ca kṛṣṇa lahomaḥ tathā ca dvi artham tad  syāt  dvi artha tvam ca vipratiṣiddham tasmāt  yaji prayuktā dharmā iti na etad  evam yaji prayuktā dharmā iti codanāyām pravṛttiḥ syāt  codanā iti  apūrvam brūmaḥ codanā artha tvāt  apūrva artha tvāt  apūrva prayuktā dharmāḥ phalavat tvāt  iti  uktaḥ  hetuḥ yad  tu prayakṣaḥ  yaji saṃbandhaḥ  dharmāṇām iti atra brūmaḥ utpattau vidhi abhāvāt  utpattiḥ  iti yajim brūmaḥ utpattau yajau na asti vidhiḥ yaji arthā dharmā iti kevalam yajau śrūyante kriyante ca na etāvatā tad arthā bhavanti yathā vāsasi rāgaḥ śrūyate vāsaḥ  rañjayati iti vāsasi ca kriyate na ca asau tad arthaḥ strī arthaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ  vā bhavati evam iha api yajau śrūyamāṇāḥ kriyamāṇāś ca apūrva arthā bhaveyuḥ  arthavat tvāya tatas  ca karma bhedaḥ syāt  yatas  apūrva arthā iti yad  tu yajeḥ pratyakṣam phale guṇa bhāva iti na kṛtvā apūrvam bhavati iti prāṇālikaḥ  vijñāyate praṇāḍya api ca yena kriyate tad  kāraṇam bhavati yathā gomayaiḥ pacati tuṣa pakvā bhavanti iti yad  tu taila pānavat  yajitaḥ phalam bhavati iti atra brūmaḥ taila pānasya api na kāla antare phalam bhavati dhātu sāmyam tasya phalam tad  ca tad kālam eva yad  ca phalam bala puṣṭi ādi tad  samyak  āhāra pariṇāma āt  bhavati tasmāt  viṣama upanyāsaḥ yadi  api  apūrvam prayojakam dharmāṇām tathā api sarva dharmaḥ syāt  sa sa padārthaḥ abhidhānavat  sāmānyāt  abhidhānam tāvat  eteṣām samānam apūrvam iti  abhidhānavat  dharmeṇa api  asya samānena bhavitavyam vāhīkavat  yathā vāhīkaḥ  atithiḥ  āgataḥ yava annam asmai prakriyatām iti  ukte yaḥ  yaḥ  vāhīka s tasya tasya yava annam kriyate yathā vā akṣi āmaye mudga odanaḥ  bhoktavyaḥ udara āmaye payaḥ pātavyam iti sarvatra ca hi  akṣi āmaye mudga odanaḥ  bhujyate udara āmaye api payaḥ pīyate evam iha api  ekasya apūrvasya ye dharmāḥ śrutāḥ  te sarva apūrvāṇām bhavitum arhanti api ca aruṇa parāśarā nāma śākhinaḥ teṣām paricareṣu smṛti rūpam brāhmaṇam bhavati ye darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  dharmāḥ te sarva iṣṭīnām agnīṣomīyasya ca iti  ārabhya yāvat  sarvāḥ prakṛti vikṛtayaḥ anukta antā iti tad  ca anukramaṇam etam eva nyāyam sūcayati tasmāt  apūrva prayukta tve api sarve dharmāḥ sarva arthā iti upavarṇanā parihāra s tāvat  ucyate yad  uktam vāhīkavat  iti atra brūmaḥ arthasya tu  avibhakta tvāt  tathā syāt  abhidhāneṣu arthaḥ  vāhīka tvam tad deśa saṃbandhaḥ saḥ  avibhaktaḥ sarva vāhīkeṣu  anugata iti  arthaḥ tad nimitta ś ca prīti viśeṣaḥ  na puruṣa nimittaḥ katham jñāyate pūrvavat tvāt  prayogasya pūrvavān atra prayogaḥ bahuśas  vāhīkāś ca āvāhīkāś ca bhojitāḥ tatra anvaya vyatirekābhyām jñatam etad  deśa nimittā iyam yavānn apriya tā na puruṣa nimitta tā tasmāt  tathā syāt  vāhīka ādiṣu  abhidhāneṣu atha iha karmaṇaḥ śabda bhāvya tvam na anyatas  śakyam etad  jñātum kasya apūrvasya dharmā iti śabdena ca vyavasthitā vijñātā dharmāḥ apūrvāṇām ca vibhāgaḥ atas  śeṣāṇām anyatra vihitānām anyatra apravṛttiḥ syāt  atha yad  uktam smṛtiḥ  iti tasya kaḥ parihāraḥ pūrvavatī hi iyam smṛtiḥ ca udakam dharma grāhakam vakyati vidhyantaḥ  vā prakṛtivat  iti tena prāpitānām dharmāṇām ayam anuvādaḥ etad  nyāya pūrvikā na aprāptānām vidhāyikā yad  kāraṇam vyavasthā dharmāṇām etena nyāyena bhavati idam nigamana sūtram nigamanam ca pratijñāyā hetoḥ  ca punarvacanam tad  idam ucyate yasmāt  evam tasmāt  arthasya agni anvādhānādeḥ śabda bhāvya tvāt  pratiprakaraṇam ca nibandhanāt  chabdāt  eva anyatra bhāvaḥ syāt  yathā gandharva apsarasaḥ  vā etam unmādayanti ya unmādyati  etā vai gandharva apsarasaḥ  yad rāṣṭra bhṛtam tasmai svāhā tābhyaḥ svāhā iti juhoti iti  agni prakaraṇe utpannānām rāṣṭrabhṛtām udvāhe upadeśaḥ eteṣām rāṣṭrabhṛtaḥ  juhoti  abhyātānām juhoti iti asti  etasmin vacane yathā adhikāram vyavatiṣṭheran dharmā iti evam ca sati  adharmakāṇi  aindra agna ādīṇi tad artham uttaraḥ  adhyāya ṣaṭkaḥ prārabdhavya iti tatra saptam ena tāvat  aindra agna ādīnām karmaṇām dharmāḥ santi iti  ucyate te ca ati deśena iti atideśaḥ  nāma ye paratra vihitā dharmās tam atītya anyatra teṣām deśaḥ yathā devadattasya bhojana vidhim kṛtvā śāli sūpa māṃsa apūpaiḥ  devadattaḥ  bhojayitavya iti tam eva vidhim yajñadatte atidiśati deva dattavat  yajñadattaḥ  bhojayitavya iti ślokam api udāharanti prakṛtāt  karmaṇaḥ  yasmāt  tad samāneṣu karmasu dharma pradeśaḥ  yena syāt  saḥ  atideśa iti sthitiḥ iti sa ca nāmnā vacanena vā tatra nāma trividham atideśakam karmanām saṃskāranām yaugikam iti vacanam punar  dvividham pratyakṣa śrutam ānumānikam ca tayoḥ  ānumānikam upariṣṭāt  vakṣyate pratyakṣa śrutam tu  idānīm eva cintyate asti iṣunām aika ahaḥ aparaḥ śyenaḥ tau dvau   api  ābhicārikau tatra iṣau kāṃścid  dharmān vidhāya āha samānam itara t  chyenena iti etad  cintyate kim ayam anuvādaḥ vidhiḥ  iti yadi vidhiḥ tatas  atideśaḥ śyena dhamān iṣau   atidiśati atha anuvādaḥ tatas  na iti tatra kim prāptam tad  sūtreṇa eva upakramyate samānam itara t  chyenena iti atra utpanna adhikāraḥ syāt  anuvāda iti  arthaḥ kutas  pūrvavat tvāt  ayam iṣuḥ pūrvavān jyotiṣṭoma pūrvakaḥ jyautiṣṭomikaḥ  atra vidhyanta iti  arthaḥ atra ca udakena utpannā jyautiṣṭomikā dharmāḥ santi śyenaḥ  api jyotiṣṭoma pūrvakaḥ tatra api te santi ye iṣau śyene ca samānā bhanti tān adhikṛtya ayam vādaḥ  yujyate tasmāt  utpanna adhikāra tvāt  anuvādaḥ kim ca itarad iti ca abhāve na upapadyate itara śabdaḥ  ca āsannihite anupapannaḥ sannihita eva bhavati yathā itara ādhāraḥ  dīyatām itaraḥ kambalaḥ  dīyatām iti sannihitaḥ  dīyate na prāvāra mātram kambala mātram vā jyautiṣṭomikāś ca sannihitāḥ tasmāt  teṣām vādaḥ teṣām ca idam anuvādaḥ vihitā hi te ca udakena iti iti ced  paśyasi jyautiṣṭomikānām anuvāda iti na evam śyenasya vaiśeṣikāṇām lohita uṣṇīṣa ādīnām dharmāṇām vidhiḥ kutas  śyena grahaṇa sāmarthyāt  evam śyena grahaṇam arthavat  bhaviṣyati dharmān viśeṣayat  itaratha anarthakam syāt  sarveṣām hi  eka ahā hīna satrāṇām te samānāḥ tatra yāvat  uktam syāt  samānam itarat  iti tāvat  eva samānam itara t  chyenena iti na ayam śyena vaiśeṣikāṇām vādaḥ  yujyate kasmāt  asannidhānāt  ayam itara śabdaḥ sannihite bhavati na ca śyena śabdena vaiśeṣikā iṣau sannihitāḥ yad  tu śyena śabdaḥ  vaiśeṣikaḥ  bhavati iti vidhi pakṣe avaiśeṣika tvam doṣaḥ syāt  anuvāda pakṣe tu na eva kaścid  vidhīyate kim viśeṣyati jyautiṣṭomikā s tu sarva sādhāraṇāḥ santaḥ śyenasya api bhavanti iti  anuvādaḥ  yujyate tasmāt  jyautiṣṭomikānām eva anuvādaḥ api vā iti pakṣa antara parigrahe vidhiḥ  ayam śyena vaiśeṣikāṇām jyautiṣṭomikānām anuvādaḥ kutas  apūrva tvāt  evam apūrvam artham vidhāsyati tathā pravṛtti viśeṣa karaḥ  bhaviṣyati anuvādaḥ san   apravṛtti viśeṣa karaḥ  anarthakaḥ syāt  nanu  itara śabdaḥ  ayam sannihite bhvati ucyate itarat  adhika arthe samānam itarat  samānam adhikam iti  arthaḥ nanu sannihita vacanaḥ  ayam na adhika artha iti ucyate na kevalam ayam sannihita vacana eva pūrva ukta sadṛśam asannihitam api brūte avaśiṣṭam ca yadā hi vastrāṇi  anukramya itara śabdaḥ prayujyate devadattāya kambalaḥ  dīyatām viṣṇu mitrāya kauśeyam yajñadattāya kṣaumam itara t  caitrāya iti tadā vastram eva pradīyate na hiraṇyam rajatam vā iha jyautiṣṭomikebhyaḥ  adhikān dharmān anukramya itara śabdaḥ prayuktaḥ tena atra api  adhikān eva vaktum arhati tathā adhika vacanaḥ  bhvati atha jyautiṣṭomikān brūte tathā sannihita vacanaḥ tatra avaśyam anyatara d dheyam yadi  adhika artha tām hitvā sannihita artha tā śrīyate anuvāda mātram anarthakam bhavati śyena śabdaḥ  ca avivakṣita arthaḥ atha sannihita artha tām hitvā adhika artha tā gṛhyate na kaścid  doṣaḥ  bhavati tasmāt  sūtrakāra āha itarat  adhika artha iti atas  jyautiṣṭomikāt  vidheḥ  adhikāḥ śyena vaiśeṣikā ye ta iha atidiśyante tad vācakam samānam syāt  samāna śabdaḥ syāt  iti  arthaḥ bhavati śyena śabdaḥ  ca vivakṣitaḥ cāturmāsyānām vaiśvadeva āgneya ādīni havīṃṣi sārtha vāda vākyaiḥ  vihitāni dharmāś ca teṣām uktāḥ varuṇa praghāseṣu kevalāni havīṃṣy āmnāya yad  vaiśvadevikānām brāhmaṇam tad  teṣām atidiśyate etad  brāhmaṇāni  eva pañca havīṃṣi yad  brāhmaṇāni itarāṇi iti tatra kim arthavāda mātrasya ayam atideśaḥ uta sārthavādakasya sa vidhikasya kāṇḍasya iti katham punar  arthavāda mātrasya atideśaḥ  bhavati yathā pampā kulāya pratimāḥ  ca vṛkṣā iti ke punar  vidhayaḥ ke artha vādāḥ tredhā sannaddham barhis  bhavati tredhā sannaddha idhmaḥ nava prayājā nava anuyājā iti evamādayaḥ  vidhayaḥ vārta ghnāni vaitāni havīṃṣi iti  artha vādāḥ tatra idam ucyate pañcatāni havīṃṣi sarva parvasu saṃcaranti iti pañca saṃcarāṇi iti  ucyante teṣu pañca saṃcareṣu  arthavāda mātrasya atideśa iti kutas  sannidhānāt  dhaviṣām sannihitā artha vādāḥ vidhibhiḥ  eka vākya saṃbaddha tvāt  na dharma vidhayaḥ kim atas  ata etad  bhavati yad  pūrveṣām brāhmaṇam iti vyapadeśaḥ  yujyate tad  dhi teṣām brāhmaṇam yena vidhīyante kaḥ  anyaḥ  haviṣām brāhmaṇasya ca saṃbandhaḥ  anyatra vidheya vidhāyaka bhāvāt  arthavādaiḥ  ca etāni vidhīyante na dharma vidhibhiḥ dharma vidhibhiḥ  tu yāni vidhīyante na tāni havīṃṣi tasmāt  artha vādānām atideśaḥ  na dharma vidhīnām api ca varuṇa praghāseṣu  api kecid  vaiśvadevikā dharmā vidhīyante yathā agnim mathnanti prasuvaḥ  bhavanti iti teṣām atideśena vihitānām punar  āmnānam anarthakam syāt  yadi vidhayaḥ  atidiśyeran tasmāt  arthavāda atideśa iti na etad  evam arthavāda mātrasya atideśa iti sa vidhikasya sārthavādakasya kāṇḍasya atideśa iti kutas  aika śabdyāt  samāna śabda tvāt  iti  arthaḥ samānaḥ  ayam brāhmaṇam iti śabdaḥ  vidhīnām artha vādānām ca sa yathā artha vādān gṛhṇāti evam vidhīn api gṛhṇāti ced  tān api  atidiśati yad  tu vidhīnām havirbhiḥ saṃbandhaḥ  na asti iti vidheya vidhāyaka saṃbandhaḥ  na asti upakāra lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ  bhaviṣyati ka upakāraḥ yaḥ  eṣām aṅgāni vidadhāti asti ced  saṃbandhaḥ brāhmaṇa śabda śrutyā sarva atideśaḥ  nyāyya iti liṅgam ca vidhīnām atideśam darśayati kim liṅgam varuṇa praghāseṣu triṃśat āhutayaḥ  vājinaḥ  yajanti  āhutīnām saṃpattyai triṃśat tvāya iti varuṇa praghāse triṃśatam āhutīḥ  darśayati yadi vidhayaḥ  na atidiśyeran tā na syuḥ tasmāt  atidiśyante vihitāmnānād iti yad  uktam tasya kaḥ parihāraḥ ābhāṣā antam sūtram atra ucyate vidhi ati deśe api sati na agni manthana ādīnām āmnānam anarthakam itarasya haviṣaḥ  arthena bhaviṣyati dakṣiṇa vaihārikasya mārutyāḥ tasmāt  na etad  jñāpakam vidhīnām anatideśasya bhaviṣyati vaiśvadeve eka kapāla āmnātaḥ dyāvāpṛthivīya eka kapāla iti varuṇa praghāseṣu  api kāya eka kapāla iti tatra aparaḥ aindrāgnaḥ  dvādaśa kapālaḥ  māruti āmikṣā iti tathā sākamedheṣu  api  ekakapāla aindra agnau   āmnātau aindrāgna ekādaśa kapāla indrāya vṛtra ghne caruḥ vaiśvakarmaṇa eka kapāla iti tatra idam āmnātam etad  brāhmaṇa aindrāgnaḥ etad  brāhmaṇa eka kapālaḥ yad  brāhmaṇa itara itaraḥ  ca iti tatra idam ucyate ekakapāla aindra agnau ca tadvat  yadvat  pañca saṃcarāṇi atra api sa vidhikasya sārthavādakasya kāṇḍasya atideśaḥ tena eva nyāyena iti prāpti sūtram etad  uttara cintā artham sākamedhe śrūyate etad  brāhmaṇa eka kapāla iti tatra cintyate vaiśvadevikasya eka kapālasya idam grahaṇam uta vāruṇa prāghāsikasya iti kim prāptam vaiśvadevikasya iti brūmaḥ kim kāraṇam tasya vihitā dharmāḥ alaṃkṛtya abhipūrya upāṃśu yaṣṭavyaḥ āviḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kārya iti evamādayaḥ vāruṇa prāghāsikaḥ  tu  adharmakaḥ yasya vihitā dharmāḥ tatra etad  yujyate vaktum tadvat  idam kartavyam iti tasmāt  vaiśvadevikasya grahaṇam nanu  aindrāgna samuccāraṇāt  eka kapālaḥ  api vāruṇa prāghāsika eva syāt  na avaśyam eka parvaṇa ūḥ  eva samuccāraṇena bhavitavyam nānā parvaṇa ūḥ  api samuccāraṇam aviruddham tasmāt  vaiśvadevikasya grahaṇam iti prāpte ucyate vāruṇa prāghāsikasya eka kapālasya grahaṇam iti kutas  tatas  eka kapālānām vaiśvadevikaḥ prakṛtiḥ katham jñāyate āgrayaṇe sarva homā parivṛtti darśanāt  āgrayaṇe dyāvāpṛthivīyasya eka kapālasya sarva homam aparyāvṛttim ca darśayati yad  sarva hutam karoti sā tu  ekā paricakṣā hutaḥ  hutaḥ paryāvartate sā dvitīyā ājyasya eva dyāvāpṛthivyau yaja iti iti ājya yāga vidhi pare vākya eka kapālasya sarva homam aparyāvṛttim ca prāptām darśayati etasmāt  darśanāt  avabhṛthe ca sakṛt  dvi avadānasya vacanāt  avabhṛte ca avadhāraṇam bhavati idam eva eka kapālasya dvis  avadyati iti tena jñāyate nūnam anyatra na dvis  avadānam iti tad  ca etad  sarvam vaiśvadevika eka kapāle vihitam tasmāt  eka kapālānām vaiśvadevikaḥ prakṛtiḥ kim atas  sākamedhike api  eka kapāle vaiśvadevikā dharmāḥ prāptāḥ teṣām atideśaḥ  anarthakaḥ vāruṇa prāghāsikasya ye dharmāḥ vaiśeṣikā aprāptāḥ teṣām atideśaḥ  arthavān tasmāt  vāruṇa prāghāsikasya eka kapālasya idam grahaṇam iti ucyate liṅgam etad  kutas  prāptiḥ  iti prāptim uttaratra vakṣyāmaḥ svarasāma eka kapālāmikṣam ca iti  atra ke punar  te dharmāḥ hiraṇya mayaḥ sruvaḥ śamī mayaḥ  vā iti evamādayaḥ idam śrūyate rathantaram uttarayoḥ  gāyati kavatīṣu rathantaram gāyati iti evamādīni samāmnāyante tatra cintā kim iha atidiśyate iti nanu yad  rathantara ādibhiḥ śabdaiḥ  ucyate tad  atidiśyate bāḍham tad  eva tu na jñāyate kim ebhiḥ śabdaiḥ  ucyata iti nanu siddham etad  gīteṣu sāma ākhyā iti tathā siddhasya ākṣepaḥ kariṣyate sa eva tu nirṇayaḥ  bhaviṣyati yadiaḥ sa eva nirṇayaḥ kim arthaḥ ākṣepaḥ dārḍhya arthaḥ sthūṇā nikhananavat tatra kim prāptam tad  ucyate sa stobha svara kāla abhyāsa vikārāyām hiṅkāra praṇava prastāva udgītha pratihāra upadrava nidhanavatyām ṛci gītau sāma śabdaḥ  abhiyuktaiḥ  upacaryate tasmāt  saṃśayaḥ ucyate nanu gītau satyām bhāvāt  nānā ākhyasya saṃskāra karmaṇaḥ  vācakā ete śabdā iti  uktam tad  eva idam uktam ākṣipyate na ime saṃskārasya vācakāḥ kim kāraṇam akarma kāle prayogāt  akarma kāle sāma prayujyate na ca saṃskāra karmaṇi prokṣaṇa avakṣepaṇa paryagni karaṇa ādīni  akarma kāle prayujyante prayojana abhāvāt atha nu mantrā ete tatas  anv aham svādhyaḥ  adhyetavya iti niyamāt  akarma kāle prayogaḥ  yujyate tasmāt  ṛcām nāmāni kim ca saṃjñā bhedāt  saṃjñā bhedaḥ  ca bhavati rathantaram bṛhad iti evamādiḥ sa eka tvāt  saṃskāra karmaṇaḥ  anarthakaḥ ekena eva hi tadā paryāptam yathā gītiḥ  iti atha ṛcām nāmāni tatas  tāsām bhedāt  saṃjñā pṛthak tvam yuktam api ca yadi gānam rathantaram gānam ca bṛhat  idam rathantaram idam bṛhad iti pṛthaktvena saṃjñā niveśaḥ  na upapadyate ṛc nāma tve tu upapadyate kim ca vikāra pṛthaktvāt  tu pratisāma ca vikāra pṛthaktvāt  pratisāma ca vikāra pṛthak tvam dṛśyate tad  eka tvāt  gānasya anupapannam saṃskāra bhede hi vikāra pṛthak tvam dṛṣṭam tad  yathā avahanteḥ  taṇḍulībhāvaḥ piṣeś cūrṇam na tu  ekasya taṇḍulībhāvaḥ  cūrṇanam ca athar  nāmāny etāni tatas  ṛcām bhedāt  vikāra pṛthak tvam yujyate tasmāt  ṛc nāmāni iti tatas  uttaram paṭhati sāmnaḥ  abhidhāna śabdena pravṛttiḥ syāt  yathāśiṣṭam iti sāmnaḥ  abhidhāna śabdena yathāśiṣṭam pravṛttiḥ syāt  yad  chiṣṭam pravaktṛbhiḥ śiṣyebhyaḥ kim ca śiṣṭam stoma ādi viśiṣṭā ṛc  sāma sā pravarteta kim kāraṇam tasyāḥ  rathantara ādi nāmadheyam iti tuśabdaḥ pakṣa nivṛttau na tu  evam syāt  ṛcaḥ pravṛttiḥ  iti katham iha kavatīṣu rathantaram gāyati iti kavatīnām vā kārye abhivatyaḥ  atidiśyeran kavatīnām vā upary ādhārya ādheya bhāvena tatra kārye tāvat  atideśaḥ  na ghaṭate kutas  śabdaiḥ  artha vidhi tvāt  śabdānām artha vidhānam kāryam na ca kavatīṣu rathantaram gāyati iti kavatībhiḥ  yaḥ  arthaḥ  abhidhīyate tam abhivatyaḥ śaknuvanti vaktum tasmāt  na karyā atideśaḥ ādheya tve api na saṃbhavati pṛthak bhāvāt  na hi śabdaḥ śabde samavaiti pṛthak  eva avatiṣṭhate abhi tvā kayā na iti kriyāyāḥ  hi gāna kriyāyāḥ śabdena abhisaṃbandhaḥ  bhavet  na śabdasya tasmāt  ādheya tvena api na ati deśaḥ atas  na ayam ṛcaḥ pradeśa iti sva artha vā pravartamānā abhivatyaḥ kavatīnām aṅga bhāvena upadiśyeran katham punar  kavatīṣu gāyati iti  aṅga bhāvaḥ śakya upadeṣṭum śakyaḥ  yathā yena karmaṇā īrtset  tatra jayān juhuyāt  iti kim punar  prayojanam kavatīnām abhivatya u nirvartayanti iti ucyate prayojanam adṛṣṭam kalpyam kutas  kriyāyāḥ yasmāt  kriyā śrūyate kavatīṣu rathanataram gāyati iti yathā prayāja ādīnām prayojanam kriyāyāḥ ucyate ayam eva asmin pakṣe doṣaḥ yad  prayojanam kriyāyāḥ kalpayitavyam tasmāt  ayam api pakṣaḥ  duḥśliṣṭaḥ iti ced  paśyasi kavati aṅga bhāvena abhivatīnām upadeśaḥ  duḥśliṣṭa iti tena tarhi śabda mātram pradiśyatām ratha ntara śabdam kavatīṣu prayuñjīta kavatīḥ rathantara śabdena abhilapet  iti kim kāranam śabda uccarite tatra tāvan mukhyā pratipattiḥ śabde kāryasya asaṃbhavāt arthe kāryam vijñāyate yathā gām ānaya iti iha tu śabda eva kāryam saṃbhavati na arthe atas  atra śabdam vijñāsyāmaḥ pūrvasmāt  eṣa vādaḥ pāpīyān kasmāt  autpattika tvāt  autpattikaḥ hi nāmi nāmnoḥ saṃbandhaḥ yaḥ śabdaḥ  yasmin artha autpattikena saṃbandhena prasiddhaḥ na sa tatas  anyam pratyāyayitum śaknoti na hi gaḥ śabdena aśvaḥ abhidhātum śakyate evam ca sati  atideśa śāstram anarthakam syāt  aśakya artha tvāt tasmāt  na śabdasya api pradeśaḥ  yuktaḥ vṛtti kāra s tu mene gāna śāstram aukthikyam anarthakam syāt  iti tasya abhiprāyaḥ satyām gatau na etāvān prayāsaḥ śiṣṭānām aphalaḥ  abhyupagantum nyāyya iti iti ced  paśyasi nāmnaḥ  atideśaḥ  ayukta iti tena tarhi svarasya atideśaḥ  bhavatu svaraḥ sāma śabdena loke abhidhīyate susāmā devadatta iti su svaraḥ  devadatta iti svaraḥ  ghoṣaḥ  nāda iti samāna arthāḥ sa sāma śabdena ucyate sāma ca rathantaram tasmāt  tasya atideśaḥ na etad  evam svarasya atideśa iti kutas  artha abhāvāt  arthasya abhāvat  arthasya abhivatīsvarasya kavatīṣu  abhāvāt  nanu  asann eva asau   atideśena bhāvyate ucyate bhāvayitum api na śakyate na hi  abhivati akṣarāṇām abhivyañjakaḥ  nādaḥ kavatīṣu bhāvayitum śakyaḥ yadi bhāvyeta na kavatyaḥ  bhaveyuḥ na ced  bhāvyate na bhūtaḥ kavatīṣu rathantaram gāyati iti  etasyāḥ śruteḥ pada antareṇa abhisaṃbandhaḥ  na syāt  tasmāt  na svarasya atideśaḥ tuśabdaḥ pakṣa antara parigrahe yadi  abhivatīsvarasya kavatīṣu pradeśaḥ  na upapadyate anuvādaḥ  bhavatu kavatīṣu rathantaram gāyati iti katham tad  ucyate iha kavatīṣu rathanatram gāyati iti  asya vākyasya dve vacana vyaktī bhavataḥ kavatīṣu yad  rathantaram tad  gāyati iti  ekā rathantaram yad  tad  kavatīṣu gāyati iti  aparā tayoḥ  yā eṣā dvitīyā rathantaram yad  tad  kavatīṣu gāyati iti sā svarasya sāma tve na saṃbhavati iti  uktam na hi  abhivatīsvaraḥ kavatīṣu samāveśayitum śakya iti pūrvā tu saṃbhavati kavatīṣu yad  rathantaram tad  gāyati iti nanu sā api na saṃbhavati na hi kavatīṣu rathantaram asti atas  param ucyate svaras tu utpattiṣu syāt  svaras tu  abhivatīsvaraḥ kavatīnām utpattiṣu uccāraṇeṣu syāt  katham mātrā varṇa avibhakta tvāt  bahavaḥ  mātrā varṇāś ca abhivatīnām kavatīnām ca avibhaktā abhibhavatīṣu  api vidyante kavatīṣu  api saḥ  asau   abhivatīsvaraḥ kavatīṣu sādhāraṇa varṇa samavetaḥ  vidyate tasya anuvādaḥ  ayam ghaṭate kavatīṣu rathantaram gāyati iti tasmāt  svarasya anuvādaḥ liṅgam ca dṛśyata etasmin   arthe asti rathantaram uttarayoḥ  iti kim tad liṅgam bhavati evam āha rathantaram uttarayoḥ  na paśyāmi iti viśvāmitra s tapas tepe bṛhad uttarayoḥ  na paśyāmi iti vasiṣṭha iti yad  ca vidyamānam na dṛśyate tad darśanāya yatnaḥ kriyate yathā ghaṭam na paśyāmi iti pradīpam karoti na śaśa viṣāṇam na paśyāmi iti tasmāt  asti  uttarayaḥ  rathantaram bṛhac ca tayoḥ  anuvāda iti tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati na etad  evam svarasya anuvāda iti kutas  evam sati  uttarāsu vikāraḥ  na kaścid  chrutaḥ  bhavati tadā uttarā yathāśrutāḥ prayoktavyāḥ yathā svādhyāya kāle śrutāḥ tatra rathantaram uttarayoḥ  gāyati iti  etad  anuvāda mātram apravṛtti viśeṣa karam anarthakam eva apavadyate atas  na svarasya anuvādaḥ  yuktaḥ rathantara ādīnām ca sāma śabdānām asāmañjasyam syāt  rathantaram uttarayoḥ bṛhad uttarayoḥ  iti katham tad  ucyate ayam rathantara śabdaḥ  bṛhat śabdaḥ  vā svarasya sāma śabda tve svara samudāya ānupūrvyā vyavasthite svara viśeṣe prayuktaḥ sa eka deśe bhinna ānupūrvye vāsam añjasaḥ bhavati tasmāt  na etad  yuktam svarasya sāma śabdaḥ tasya ca anuvāda iti atra āha evam bhavatā sarve pakṣā niruddhāḥ tatas  kim apravṛttiḥ  eva iti ucyate ṛca eva pradeśaḥ  bhavatu nanu uktam na śakyā ṛca ṛc antare pradeṣṭum iti bāḍham deśa lakṣaṇā bhaviṣyati kavatīṣu rathantaram gāyati iti  ucyate na ca śakyate kavatīṣu rathantaram gātum tatra deśa lakṣaṇā bhavati kavatī deśa iti yathā agnau tiṣṭhati kūpe tiṣṭhati iti dharma lakṣaṇā vā syāt  rathantara dharmā vā kavatīṣu rathantara śabdena atidiśyante yathā rathantare prastūyamāne pṛthivīm manasā dhyāyet  iti evamādayaḥ yathā ācārye proṣite ācāryānī bhavatām ācārya iti  ācārya śuśruṣa ācāryā anyām atidiśyate api tu na evam syāt  ṛcaḥ sāma śabdaḥ tasya āś ca pradeśa iti tathā deśa lakṣaṇā dharma lakṣaṇā vā āśrayaṇīyā agatiḥ  ca eṣā yad lakṣaṇā parigrahaḥ kim tarhi karma śabdaḥ syāt  rathantara ādiḥ  gāna ākhyasya saṃskāra karmaṇaḥ  vācakaḥ kutas  uktaḥ  nyāyaḥ  gītiṣu sāma ākhyā iti  atra tatra gīti viśiṣṭāyām ṛci eṣa śabdaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ na ca agṛhīta viśeṣaṇā viśeṣye buddhiḥ  utpadyate tasmāt  viśeṣaṇam tāvat  abhidhīyate viśeṣaṇa pratyaya āt  ca sahacarite viśiṣṭe pratyayaḥ atas  na asti  ṛcaḥ śabdena saṃsparśa iti tena eva nyāyena gīti nāmadheyam iti brūmaḥ kim ca prasiddha grahaṇa tvāt  ayam ca gāyati iti śabdaḥ  gāna kriyāyām prasiddhaḥ kā punar  asau śabdasya uccāraṇa viśeṣaḥ gāyati gānam karoti iti tad grahaṇaḥ  ca rathantara ādi śabdaḥ tad vacana iti  arthaḥ tena samuccāraṇāt  dvitīya asāmarthyā t  ca yathā āsāritakam gāyati iti vardhamānakam gāyati iti nanu śabda vacanena api samuccāraṇam bhavati gāthām gāyati ṛcam gāyati iti satyam vipariṇamya tu śabdam gānena ṛcam saṃskaroti iti yathā nipatitena arthena na saṃbadhyate gānam karoti iti  ṛcam iti tasmāt  gīti vacanaḥ itas  ca gīti vacanaḥ kutas  vikāraḥ  hi  aviśiṣṭaḥ  anyaiḥ vikāraḥ  ca atra ṛgdravyasya dṛśyate hrasvānām akṣarāṇām dīrgha tā dīrghāṇām ca hrasva tvam vivṛtānām saṃvṛta tvam saṃvṛtānām vivṛta tvam saḥ  aviśiṣṭaḥ  anyaiḥ saṃskāra karmabhiḥ yathā avahantinā vrīhīṇām taṇḍulībhāvaḥ piṣiṇā taṇḍulānām piṣṭībhāvaḥ tasmāt  chabdānām saṃskāraḥ  gāna ākhyaḥ  rathantara ādibhiḥ śabdaiḥ  ucyate tasya ayam pradeśaḥ rathantaram uttarayoḥ  gāyati iti evamādiḥ api ca adravyam sāma dṛśyate dravya śabdaḥ  chandaḥ gaiḥ  ṛkṣv ācaritaḥ adravyam anṛcam iti  arthaḥ anṛcam sāma dṛśyate prajāpateḥ  hṛdayam anṛcam gāyati iti prajāpati hṛdayam nāma sāma tad  anṛcy utpannam yadi  ṛci sāma śabdaḥ katham prajāpati hṛdayam anṛcam syāt  atha gīteḥ sāma śabdaḥ tatas  vinā api  ṛcā gītiḥ  bhavati tatra etad  upapadyate prajāpateḥ  hṛdayam anṛcam gāyati iti tasmāt  api gītiḥ sāma nanu uktam saṃskāra karma tve anartha kaḥ  akarma kāle prayoga iti tatra brūmaḥ tasya kriyā karma kāle grahaṇa arthā śikṣitum abhyasitum ca nānā artheṣu nānā bhūteṣu  artheṣu bhinneṣu  iti  arthaḥ virūpi tvāt  āśraya bhedāt  vividha rūpam tad gānam bhavati tad  praty ṛcam śikṣitavyam abhyasitavyam ca prayoga prāśubhāvāya bhūmi rathikavat  tad  yathā bhūmi rathikaḥ  bhūmau ratham ālikhya yogyām karoti sā tasya yogyā prayoga kāle saukaryam utpādayati arthaḥ  hi  āsām rathantara ādi saṃjñānām na laukike vyavahāre siddhaḥ yathāvahanti ādīnām kutas  vidhānāt  vidhīyate hi  asau śiṣya upādhyāya saṃbandhena evaṃrūpam rathantaram bhavati iti na laukikaḥ  vijñāyate tasmāt  na paricodanā eṣā akarma kāle prayogāt  iti atha yad  uktam saṃjñā pṛthaktvāt  iti tatra ucyate tasmin   ekasmin   api gāna ākhye saṃskāre saṃjñā viśeṣā bhaveyuḥ kutas  vikāra pṛthaktvāt  tulye api gāne viśeṣaḥ  bhavati gāna viśeṣa āt  ca saṃjñā pṛthak tvam yathā āsāritakam vardhamānakam iti anyathā lakṣaṇa āsāritaka gītiḥ anyathā lakṣaṇā vardhamānaka gītiḥ evam iha api  anyathā lakṣaṇā rathantara gītiḥ anyathā lakṣaṇā bṛhadgītiḥ tasmāt  saṃjñā pṛthak tvam yoniḥ  ca asau śasyā ca yoniśasyā yoniśasyāḥ  carcas tulyavat  itarābhiḥ  ayoniśasyābhiḥ  vidhīyante yāmyāḥ śaṃsati śipiviṣṭavantīḥ śaṃsati rathantarasya yonim anuśaṃsati bṛhataḥ  yonim anuśaṃsati iti kā tatra tulya tā śaṃsati śabdena abhidhānam iha etau stauti śaṃsati śabdau samāne api stuti artha tve vyavasthita viṣayau pragīteṣu mantra vākyeṣu stauti śabdaḥ apragīteṣu śaṃsati śabdaḥ yathā praügam śaṃsati niṣkevalyam śaṃsati iti ājyaiḥ stuvate pṛṣṭhaiḥ stuvanta iti atas  śaṃsati śabdena vidhānāt  apragītām ṛcam rathantarasya yonim darśayati yadi ca gītiḥ rathantaram tatas  tasya apragītā ṛc yoniḥ anyathā ayam vyapadeśaḥ  na upapadyate rathantarasya yonim iti tasmāt  gītiṣu sāma ākhyā ayonau ca sāma dṛśyate sthālyām saktv avadhīyata iti  āhuḥ  yad  bṛhad gāyatrīṣu kriyate api ca enām rujati na ca asyām saṃbhavati iti bṛhataḥ  bṛhatī yoniḥ tasya gāyatrīṣu prāptiḥ  na asti yadi  ṛcaḥ sāma śabdaḥ atha nu gīteḥ tatas  sā bṛhadgītiḥ  gāyatrīṣu vacanāt  prāptā tasyāḥ  ayam anuvādaḥ  ghaṭate yad  bṛhad gāyatrīṣu kriyata iti atathā yoni ca sāma darśayati yādṛśī yasya yoniḥ tatas  anyādṛśe yaḥ  vai vicchandasi sāmohati sa ṛcam saṃśṛṇāti sāma vā viliśati sāma saṃśṛṇāti ṛcam viliśati iti yatara t  varṣīyaḥ tasya saṃśaraḥ tad  ca gītau   eva sāmni yujyate narci ūhati śadaḥ  ca gītau   eva samarthaḥ narci ṛc  ced  sā eva yathāmnāyam padyate tatra na asti  ūha prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt  api gītau sāma śabdaḥ yad  uktam tasya kriyā grahaṇa artha iti tatra paricodyate aikārthye na asti vairūpyam iti rathantara gīteḥ  bṛhadgītiḥ  artha antaram tena rathantara gītau gṛhītāyām bṛhadgītiḥ  agṛhītā bhavati iti yuktaḥ  rathantare gṛhīte bṛhataḥ śikṣā artham akarma kāle prayogaḥ rathantara gīteḥ  tu  eka eva arthaḥ tasya yonyām prayoge śikṣite punar  uttarāsu na śikṣitavyam tāsu  akarma kāle prayogaḥ saṃskāra karma tve na yuktaḥ  bhavati tasmāt  na saṃskārasya sāma śabda iti sthitāyām pratijñāyām sūtreṇa paricodayati syāt  vairūpyam kuta etad  arthān atreṣu  aniṣpatteḥ ṛc antareṣu  āśraya bhedāt  yathā pāke yathā eka eva ayam arthaḥ pākaḥ  nāma tasya artha antare vairūpyam bhavati anyathā lakṣaṇa odanasya pākaḥ anyathā lakṣaṇaḥ  guḍasya yena odana pākaḥ  gṛhītaḥ na asau   aśikṣitvā guḍam paktum jānāti tasmāt  tasya api  akarma kāle prayoga upapadyate evam ca sāma śabdānām ṛc śabdānām ca sāmañjasyam bhavati kavatīṣu rathantaram gāyati iti kavatī śabda ṛca eva vakṣati rathantara śabdaḥ  ca sāma itarathā kavatī śabde vā deśa lakṣaṇā syāt  rathantara śabde vā dharma lakṣaṇā tasmāt  gītau sāma śabda iti nāmnā dharma pradeśam vakṣyāma iti  ādau pratijñātam saḥ  ayam ucyate kuṇḍapāyinām ayane śrūyate māsam agni hotram juhoti iti tatra etad  samadhigatam naiyamikāt  agnihotrāt  karma antaram etad  iti adhunā agnihotra śabaḥ  cintyate katham ayam prayukta iti tad artham ārabhyate uktam kriyā abhidhānam tad śrutau   anyatra vidhi pradeśaḥ syāt  iti uktam ādau kriyā abhidhānam karma nāmadheyam agnihotra śabda iti tad prakhyam ca anya śāstram iti  atra tasya anyatra śrutau kauṇḍapāyinām ayanīye juhotau vidhi pradeśaḥ syāt  dharma pradeśaḥ naiyamikasya agnihotrasya ye dharmās te asmin   anena nāmnā atidiśyeran kim kāraṇam ucyate para śabdaḥ  ayam paratra vṛttaḥ para śabdasya paratra vṛttau tadvat bhāvaḥ  gamyate sa yatra vijñātaḥ  bhavati tatra anūdyate yathā siṃhaḥ  devadatta iti yatra avijñāta s tatra vidhīyate yathā amī piṣṭa piṇḍāḥ siṃhāḥ kriyantām iti iha ca avijñātaḥ  asya juhoteḥ  agnihotravat bhāvaḥ tasmāt  sa vidhīyate māsam agni hotram juhoti iti agni hotra vaj juhoti iti katham punar  asati vati pratyaye vati arthaḥ śakyaḥ  avagantum iti ucyate sāhacaryāt  agnihotra śabdaḥ  ayam karmaṇā saṃbaddhaḥ tad sahacarita dohana ādi dharmavat tām lakṣaṇayā śaknoti gamayitum śaknoti ced  gamayitum pradeṣṭum api śaknoti evam anatreṇa api vatim vati arthaḥ śakyaḥ  avagantum iti vāpi iti viparyāsena prayukte api vā iti  arthaḥ api vāpūrve ete ubhe api karmaṇī syātām na kauṇḍapāyinām ayanīyaḥ  juhotiḥ  naiyamika pūrvaḥ sādhāraṇam ca nāmadheyam ubhayoḥ kutas  bhāgi tvāt  ayam api juhotiḥ  bhāgī etasya nāmadheyasya yathā eva tatra agni hotram juhoti iti samuccāraṇam evam iha api tatra tulye samuccāraṇe tasya eva etad  nāmadheyam na asya iti  atra viśeṣa hetuḥ  na asti tasmāt  ubhayoḥ sādhāraṇam nāma iti na asti dharma pradeśaḥ na etad  yuktam kutas  autpattikaḥ hi nāmi nāmnoḥ sambandhaḥ yad  nāma yasmin   artha autpattikena saṃbandhena prasiddham tasmin   eva sadā vijñeyam na anyatra ca tathā avyavasthāyām śabda arthe viśvāsaḥ  na syāt  uktam anyāyaḥ  ca aneka artha tvam iti yadā ca na ubhaya arthaḥ tadā naiyamikam tāvat  āha tad sādṛśya vidhāna artham ca itaratrā api prayoga upapadyata iti na asti itara abhidhāna tve hetuḥ tasmāt  vidhi pradeśaḥ syāt  naiyamike agnihotre pratyakṣaḥ  guṇa saṃyogaḥ pratyakṣa vihitā dharmāḥ santi ittham dogdhi ittham śrapayati catur  unnayati khādiry agnihotra samid bhavati ittham juhoti evam pratyakṣāt  guṇa saṃyogāt  naiyamikasya tad  nāmadheyam iha prayujyamānam dohana ādi kriyā abhidhānam syāt  dharma pradeśakam iti  arthaḥ asya punar  juhoteḥ  na kecid  dharmāḥ santi tad abhāve teṣām dharmāṇām abhāve aprasiddham syāt  na prajñāyeta kim artham ayam agnihotra śabda iha prayukta iti evam vā pratyakṣaḥ  guṇa asaṃyogaḥ  naiyamikasya dravya devatā saṃyogaḥ dadhnā juhoti payasā juhoti agnaye ca prajāpataye ca sāyam juhoti iti etasmāt  pratyakṣāt  guṇa saṃyogāt  kriyā abhidhānam syāt  karma nāmadheyam itthaṃrūpaḥ  juhotiḥ  agnihotra ākhya iti atha itara juhoteḥ rūpam na asti tad abhāve aprasiddham syāt  na jñāyet  kīdṛśam tad agnihotram iti nanu māsaḥ  asya rūpam bhaviṣyati na māsaḥ karma aṅgam kartṛ dharmaḥ saḥ api ca agni hotram tu māse vidhīyate na māsena agni hotram rūpyate tasmāt  naiyamikasya etad  nāmadheyam itaratra tadvat  atideśa iti kim eṣa eva utsargaḥ sarvam karma nāma anyatra śrūyamāṇam dharmāṇām grāhakam iti evam khalu prāptam evam prāpta idam ārabhyate gavāmayane śrūyate vaiśvānaraḥ  jyotiṣṭomaḥ prāyaṇīyam ahar bhavati iti asti tu dvādaśa ahe prathamam ahar  prāyaṇīyam nāma prāyaṇīyaḥ  atirātra iti tayoḥ  nānā tvam tena eva nyāyena siddham prakaraṇa antare prayojana anya tvam iti tatra ayam prāyaṇīya śabdaḥ paratra api śrūyamāṇaḥ  na dharmāṇām grāhakaḥ kim tarhi guṇa arthā eṣā śrutiḥ katham lakṣaṇayā nāmadheyam dharmāṇām grāhakam uktam asati ca śruti arthe lakṣaṇa arthaḥ  grāhyaḥ iha tu śruti artha eva saṃbhavati guṇa artha eṣa śabdaḥ guṇena kriyā yogena tasmin karmaṇi śrutyā eva prayujyate prayanti  anena iti prāyaṇīyam pravartate anena satram iti vākya śeṣaḥ  ca asya etam eva artham āha jyotiḥ  eva purastād dadhāti iti yena jyotiḥ prāyaṇīyam bhavati tena jyotiḥ purastāt  kriyata iti  arthaḥ jyotiḥ  eva purastād dadhāti iti tasmāt  na ayam atideśaḥ viśva jit  sarva pṛṣṭhaḥ  bhavati iti śrūyate tatra vicāryate kim ayam anuvādaḥ vidhiḥ  iti kim prāptam anuvāda iti kutas  yaḥ  hi  asarva pṛṣṭhaḥ tasya sarva pṛṣṭha tā vidheyā yaḥ  tu sarva pṛṣṭha eva tasya tayā kim vihitayā ayam ca sarva pṛṣṭha eva katham tad pūrvaka tvāt  jyotiṣṭoma pūrvaka tvāt  jyautiṣṭomikāni stotrāṇi  atra prāpyante teṣu māhendra stotra ādīni catvāri santi tāni sarvāṇi  asya taiḥ  ayam sarva pṛṣṭhaḥ  bhavati nanu na tāni pṛṣṭhāni ucyate asti ca pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ teṣu  asti pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni iti tasmāt  anuvādaḥ na ayam anuvādaḥ kim tarhi vidhiḥ anuvādaḥ  apravṛtti viśeṣa karaḥ  arthakaḥ syāt  api ca jyotiṣṭome na pṛṣṭha bahu tvam asti yasya ayam anuvādaḥ syāt  ṣaṣ ahe tu tad  asti tatra hi codanāḥ pṛṣṭhānām rathantaram pṛṣṭham bhavati iti evamādyāḥ tasmāt  ṣāḍahikānām atideśa kaḥ vidhiḥ  iti liṅgam ca etam artham darśayati pavamāne rathantaram karoti  ārbhāve bṛhat  madhya itarāṇi vairūpam hotuḥ sāma vairājam maitrāvaruṇasya raivatam brāhmaṇāt  chaṃsinaḥ śākvaram ac chāvākasya iti viniveśa pare vākye ṣāḍahikāni pṛṣṭhāni darśayati atha yad  uktam asti ca pṛṣṭha śabda iti tatra brūmaḥ na tu eṣa autpattikaḥ pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ utpannānām stotrāṇām asau   adhikāraḥ yāni  etāni pṛṣṭhāni iti jñāte ca teṣām pṛṣṭha tve tad  upapadyate na ca tatra jñātam katham tarhi ayam anuvādaḥ liṅga samavāyāt ekam tatra pṛṣṭham māhendra stotram iti ṣāḍahikānām punar  pṛṣṭha tvam jñātam katham tatra hi codanā iti  uktam teṣām vāde śrautaḥ pṛṣṭha śabdasya arthaḥ parigṛhītaḥ  bhavati itarathā lākṣaṇikaḥ tasmāt  ṣāḍahikānām pradeśa iti iti ced  paśyasi ṣāḍahikānām pṛṣṭhānām vidhiḥ  iti na etad  yuktam kim kāraṇam dvi kara evam sarva pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ  abhyupagamyate pṛṣṭhāni ca vidadhāti teṣām ca sarva tvam astu kaḥ  doṣaḥ asaṃbhava iti  āha yadi pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ pṛṣṭhāni vidadhāti sarva śabdena na śakyate viśeṣayitum atha anuvadati tathā śakyate pṛṣṭhāni tu  avihitāni bhavanti teṣu  asatsu kasya idam sarva tvam vidhīyate ubhaya kriyāyāś ca asaṃbhavaḥ atha atra bṛhat rathantarayoḥ  vikalpena prāptayoḥ sāmastyam kevalam vidhīyate sarva pṛṣṭhaḥ  bhavati iti ubhe api bṛhat rathantare bhavataḥ na ekam iti tatas  ayam doṣaḥ  na bhavati tasmāt  dvayoḥ  adhikāraḥ na evam etad  kutas  vyartha tvāt  sarva śabdasya evam sati sarva śabdaḥ  vyarthaḥ  bhavati  artha śūnyaḥ ayam hi bahu viṣayaḥ  dvayoḥ  na yujyate ṣāḍahikānām tu vidhāne na eṣa doṣaḥ nanu ca tatra api dvi karaḥ śabdaḥ  bhaviṣyati ucyate na bhaviṣyati sarva tvam kevalam pṛṣṭhānām vidhāsyati na pṛṣṭhāni nanu uktam pṛṣṭheṣu  asatsu kasya idam srva tvam vidhīyata iti ucyate pṛṣṭhānām sarva tvam hi vihitam tad  saṃpādayitavyam na ca pṛṣṭhāni  akurvatā tad  saṃpādayitum śakyate tatra arthāt  pṛṣṭhāni kariṣyati evam na dvi arthaḥ śabdaḥ  bhaviṣyati sarva śabdaḥ  ca samarthitaḥ tasmāt  ṣāḍahikānām atideśa iti varuṇa praghāseṣu śrūyate vāruṇyā niṣkāsena tuṣaiḥ  ca avabhṛtham yanti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim dārśa pūrṇamāsike apām vyutseke tuṣa niṣkāsam vidhīyate uta saumikād avabhṛthāt  dharma atideśa iti kim yuktam dārśa pūrṇamāsike guṇa vidhiḥ evam sannihita pratyayaḥ anugṛhyate sannihitaḥ  hi  asau ca udakena prāpitaḥ nanu na asau   avabhṛthaḥ ucyate asti tatra avabhṛtha śabda iti eṣa vai darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  avabhṛtha iti evam prāpta idam āha tathā avabhṛthaḥ somāt  yathā ṣaṣ ahāt pṛṣṭhānām atideśaḥ evam saumikād avabhṛthāt  iha dharma atideśaḥ kutas  abhihitaḥ  nyāyaḥ uktam kriyā abhidhānam tad śrutau   anyatra vidhi pradeśaḥ syāt  iti atha yad  uktam dārśa paurṇamāsike avabhṛthe guṇa vidhiḥ  bhavatu  iti tasya kaḥ parihāra iti  ābhāṣā antam sūtram na etad  yuktam kutas  yatas  na asti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  avabhṛthaḥ nanu eṣa vai darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  avabhṛtha iti śrūyate satyam śrūyate na tu  evam avabhṛtha tvam asya bhavati katham ucyate eṣa vai darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  avabhṛtha iti  etasya vākyasya dvayī vacana vyaktiḥ nirjñāta avabhṛtha tvasya padārthasya vā darśa pūrṇamāsa saṃbandha ucyate yathā devadattaḥ  yajñadattasya putra iti nirjñāta putra tvasya devadattasya yajñadatta saṃbandhaḥ ucyate nirjñāta saṃbandhasya vānirjñāta avabhṛtha tvasya avabhṛtha tvam yathā ayam āmraḥ  yajñadattasya putra iti nirjñāta yajña datta saṃbandhasya āmrasya putra tvam ucyate tad  asya apām vyutsekasya darśa pūrṇamāna saṃbandhaḥ prakaraṇān nirjñātaḥ na avabhṛtha tvam atas  asya avabhṛtha tvam ucyate na ca ayam avabhṛthaḥ nanu  ayam api  avabhṛthaḥ  bhavatu na etad  yuktam anyāyaḥ hi  aneka artha tvam katham tarhi śabda prayogaḥ sādṛśyāt  kim sādṛśyam apsu saṃbandhaḥ sa eṣa bhaktyā praśaṃsā vādaḥ  apām vyutsekasya avabhṛtha iva ayam iti yathā āmre putra vādaḥ tasmāt  na asti darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  avabhṛthaḥ atas  na atra guṇa vidhiḥ liṅgam ca etam artham darśayati kim liṅgam bhavati evam āha na āyuḥ dāṃ juhoti na sāma gāyati na vā gamana mantram japati iti saumikā avabhṛtha dharmāṇām pratiṣedham brūvaṃ   tad dharma prāptim darśayati tasmāt  saumikād avabhṛthāt  dharma pradeśa iti vāruṇa prāghāsikaḥ  avabhṛthaḥ saumikād avabhṛthāt  dharmāṇām grāhaka iti  yuktam tatra idam cintyate kim puroḍāśa dravya kaḥ asau uta tuṣa niṣkāsa dravyaka iti kim prāptam puroḍāśa dravyaka iti kutas  nāmnā puroḍāśaḥ prāpyate nanu pratyakṣa śrutam tuṣa niṣkāsam satyam pratyakṣa śrutam na tu śakyate vidhātum avabhṛthaḥ  atra vidhīyate avabhṛtham yanti iti yadi tuṣa niṣkāsam aparam vidhīyeta tatas  vākyam bhidyeta avabhṛtham yanti tad  ca tuṣa niṣkāsena iti tuṣa niṣkāsa śravaṇam idānīm kim artham anarthakam saṃbandha abhāvāt  evam prāpte brūmaḥ dravya ādeśe tad dravyaḥ dravya ādeśa etasmin tuṣa niṣkāsena avabhṛtam yanti iti tad dravyaḥ syāt  tuṣa niṣkāsa dravyaḥ kutas  śruti saṃyogāt  tuṣa niṣkāsam pratyakṣa śrutam puroḍāśa s tu  ānumānikaḥ atideśena prāpyate nanu puroḍāśaḥ  api pratyakṣa śrutaḥ  nāmnā yadi  api pratyakṣa śrutaḥ sāmānyena tu prāpyate tuṣa niṣkāsam tu viśeṣeṇa bādhyate ca sāmānyam viśeṣeṇa api ca lakṣaṇayā puroḍāśaḥ  gamyate śrutyā tuṣa niṣkāsam śruti lakṣaṇayoḥ  ca śrutiḥ  nyāyyā tasmāt  tuṣa niṣkāsa dravyaka iti atha yad  uktam na saṃbadhyate avabhṛthena tuṣa niṣkāsam vākya bheda prasaṅgāt  iti tatra brūmaḥ yadi  avabhṛtham vihāya tuṣa niṣkāsam vidhīyate tatas  vākya bhedaḥ syāt  tuṣa niṣkāsa dravya kaḥ  apūrvaḥ  avabhṛthaḥ  codyate tathā sa guṇa karma vidhānam aviruddham avidhīyamāne ca tuṣa niṣkāse tad grahaṇam anarthakam eva syāt  tasmāt  tuṣa niṣkāsa dravyakaḥ puroḍāśa s tu  anādeśe tad prakṛti tvāt yadi  atra pratyakṣa śrutam na dravyam syāt  tatas  puroḍāśa s tuṣa prakṛti tvāt  syāt  atra tu pratyakṣa śrutam tuṣa niṣkāsam tasmāt  na puroḍāśaḥ ātithye śrūyate vaiṣṇavaḥ  nava kapālaḥ  bhavati iti tathā rājasūye pūrvasmin   tri saṃyukte vaiṣṇvas tri kapāla iti tatra vicāraḥ yaḥ  ayam tri saṃyukte vaiṣṇava s tri kapāla iti vaiṣṇava śabdaḥ ayam ātithya dharmāṇām grāhakaḥ na iti kim yuktam grāhaka iti kutas  vihita dharmake karmaṇi dṛṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ  anyasmin   avihite śrūyamāṇaḥ  grāhaka iti  uktam uktam kriyā abhidhānam iti tatra ayam api vihita dharmaka ātithye dṛṣṭaḥ idānīm avihita dharmake tri saṃyukte dṛśyate tasmāt  dharmāṇām grāhaka iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ guṇa vidhiḥ  ayam ātithyasya guṇam viṣṇu devatā saṃyogam vidadhāti sa eṣa dharmān grahītum na śaknoti kutas  sama tvāt  samaḥ  hi  ayam ātithye tri saṃyukte ca yathā tatra viṣṇum devatām vidadhāti evam atra api śruti artha asaṃbhavāt  ca lakṣaṇayā dharmāṇām grāhakaḥ kalpyate iha ca pratyakṣa śruti artha eva saṃbhavati devatā vidhiḥ tasmāt  na ayam grāhaka iti paśauv agnīṣomīye dharmavān nirmanthyaḥ  agniḥ  āmnātaḥ sādhyā vai devāḥ  iti  ārabhya agnau śrūyate nirmanthyena iṣṭakāḥ pacanti iti tathā darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  barhi rājye dharmavatī paśau śrūyate barhiṣā yūpāvaṭam avastṛṇāti iti ājyena yūpam anakti iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim nirmanthya ādayaḥ śabdāḥ dharmāṇām grāhakāḥ na iti tatra adhikaraṇa atideśaḥ kriyate nirmanthya ādiṣu ca evam yathā vaiṣṇava śabde atra api  ayam yaugikaḥ  nirmanthya śabdaḥ sadyonirmathitam agnim āha tathā barhis  ājyam iti dravya śabdau te trayaḥ  api sva artham vidhāya kṛtārthā bhavanti dharmān grahītum na śaknuvanti tasmāt  na grāhakāḥ cāturmāsyeṣu śrūyate dvayoḥ praṇayanti tasmāt  dvābhyām eti iti asti tu some praṇayanam dharmavat  tathā darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  adharmakam tatra saṃdehaḥ kim saumikam etad  praṇayam uta dārśa paurṇamāsikam iti tatra sūtreṇa eva upakramaḥ saumikam etad  praṇayanam kim kāraṇam avācyam hi itarat  dārśa paurṇamāsikam ca udakena prāpta tvāt  katham punar  ayam praṇayati śabdaḥ praṇayana mātra vacanaḥ san saumikam praṇayana viśeṣam śaknoti vaktum lakṣaṇayā iti brūmaḥ tīrtha śabavat  tad  yathā tīrtha śabdaḥ tīrtha mātra vacanaḥ san tīrtha viśeṣam dharma sādhanam kadācid  brūte tīrtha yātrām gata iti na vaiśvadeva uttara vedim upavayanti na sunāsīrīya iti prāpti pūrva kaḥ  hi pratiṣedhaḥ  bhavati saumike ca praṇayana uttara vediḥ  na dārśa paurṇamāsike prākṛtam vaitat  praṇayanam dārśa paurṇamāsikam kutas  anāma tvat  praṇayana śabdaḥ saumikasya praṇayanasya na nāmadheyam na etad  tasya vācakam iti  arthaḥ yadi  ayam tasya vācakaḥ syāt  tatas  tad  iha brūyat  idam tu padārtha nāmadheyam padārthasya prāk nayanasya vācakam yasya vācakam tad  iha śaknoti  agneḥ prācīnam nayanam vaktum tad  ca iha asti  eva tasmāt  tasya vācakaḥ evam sannihita pratyaḥ na bādhitaḥ  bhavati atha yad  uktam tīrtha śabavat  bhaviṣyati iti atra brūmaḥ tīrtha śabdaḥ  api tīrtha mātram eva brūte tīrtha yātrām gata iti tu  uktvā kānicid  tīrthāni  anukrāntāni yatas  asau tad viśiṣṭa arthaḥ  vijñāyate yatra tu kevalaḥ prayujyate tatra tīrtha mātram eva brūte yathā tīrthe snāti tīrtham eva hi samānānām bhavati iti api ca saṃbhavati śruti arthe lakṣaṇa arthaḥ  agrāhyaḥ saṃbhavati ca atra śruti arthaḥ tasmāt  na lakṣaṇa arthaḥ  grāhya iti tatra āha yad  uktam avācyam hi itarat  iti tasya kaḥ parihāraḥ ucyate parisaṅkhyā artham vā syāt  dvayoḥ praṇayanti na caturṣu  iti guṇa artham artha vāda artham vā tasmāt  dvābhyām eti iti tatra parisaṅkhyāyām tāvat  trayaḥ  doṣāḥ guṇa u api na kaścid  vidhīyate pariśeṣāt  artha vāda artham nanu  artha vādaḥ  api niṣprayojanaḥ praṇayanasya prāpta tvāt  artha vādasya prayojanam uttarasmin   adhikaraṇe vakṣyāmaḥ madhyamayoḥ  vā gati artha vādāt  iti dvayoḥ praṇayanti iti śrūyate tatra saṃdehaḥ katarayoḥ  dvayoḥ  iti aniyame prāpte ucyate prathama uttamayoḥ praṇayanam kutas  uttara vedi pratiṣedhāt  tatra uttara vediḥ pratiṣidhyate na vaiśvadeva uttara vedim upavayanti iti na sunāsīrīya iti asmin praṇayane uttara vedyām agni nidhānam vihitam atas  yatra praṇayanam tatra uttara vedi prāptiḥ prāptau ca satyām pratiṣedhaḥ prathama uttarayoḥ  ca asau tasmāt  tayoḥ praṇayanam iti madhyamayoḥ  vā parvaṇoḥ praṇayanam kutas  gati artha vādāt  gati artha vādena etad  dvayoḥ praṇayanam ucyate tasmāt  dvābhyām eti iti ūru saṃstute vaite parvaṇī ūru vaitau yajñasya yad  varuṇa praghāsa āḥ  ca sākamedha āḥ  ca iti ūru ca gamana sādhane tatra evam stuti saṃbandhaḥ  vijñāyate ūru yajñasya varuṇa praghāsa āḥ  ca sāka medhāḥ  ca iti tayoḥ  dvayoḥ praṇayanti tasmāt  dvābhyām ūrubhyām yajñaḥ samāptim yānti praṇayanena hi tau balavantau bhavataḥ aṅga bhūyaḥ tvāt  iti etad  tad artha vādasya prayojanam atha yad  uktam uttara vedi pratiṣedhāt  iti tatra brūmaḥ anārabhya kiṃcid  parva viśeṣam cāturmāsyeṣu uttara vediḥ  āmnātā upātra vapanti iti tasya anārabhya vidheḥ  ayam pratiṣedhaḥ nanu varuṇa praghāsānām guṇa vākya prāptau   eva ayam teṣām eva atra iti vādaḥ syāt  na etad  evam prakaraṇa āc cāturmāsyānām eva yadi varuṇa praghāsānām vādaḥ syāt  tatra pratiṣedhe trīṇi  api parvāṇi  utkīrtayet  atha ucyeta dvayoḥ parvaṇa ūḥ  vādaḥ  bhavatu  iti atra brūmaḥ na dvayoḥ parvaṇoḥ prakaraṇam cāturbhāsyānām vā prakaraṇam varuṇa praghāsānām vā varuṇa praghāsānām dvayoḥ prakaraṇe parvaṇa ūḥ  utkīrtanam pratiṣedhe na syāt  tasmāt  cāturmāsyānām eva vādaḥ nanu evam api  arthavādena etad  jñātam madhyamayoḥ praṇayanam iti kim artham prāptasya praṇayanasya punar śravaṇam iti atra prayojanam na uktam asati prayojane anyasmin parisaṅkhyā artham eva bhavati tatra doṣā uktāḥ tasmāt  guṇa artham eva etad  chravaṇam nanu na asti kaścid  guṇaḥ ucyate guṇaḥ śrūyate uttara vedyām agni nidhānam tasmāt  tad arthā punar  śrutiḥ gavāmayane śrūyate abhitas  divākīrtyam ahar trayaḥ svara sāmānaḥ  bhavanti iti teṣām viśeṣa dharmā āmnātāḥ yathā saptadaśā bhavanti santata tayā ati grāhyā gṛhyanta iti evamādayaḥ punar  anyatra śrūyate pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaṣ ahaḥ dvau svara sāmānau   iti tathā vaiśvadeve śrūyate dyāvāpṛthivya eka kapāla iti tatra āmnātā viśeṣa dharmāḥ sarva hutam juhoti  aparyāvartayan  juhoti iti punar  aparatra kāya eka kapāla iti tatra eva śrūyate vaiśvadevya abhikṣā iti tatra api viśeṣa dharmāḥ kecid  āmnātāḥ punar  anyatra maitrāvaruṇy āmikṣa iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim svarasāma śabdaḥ  anyatra śrūyamāṇaḥ  gavāmayanikebhyaḥ svarasām abhyaḥ  dharmāṇām grāhakaḥ uta na iti evam eka kapāla āmikṣā śabdau   api tatra guṇa vidhi s tu na gṛhṇīyāt  sama tvāt  iti  agrahaṇe prāpte idam ucyate svarasāma eka kapālāmikṣam ca dharmāṇām grāhakam kim kāraṇam liṅga darśanāt  liṅgam tatra tādṛśam dṛśyate yena jñāyate sarva ete dharmāṇām grāhakā iti svarasāmasu tāvat  pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaṣ ahaḥ dvau svara sa mānau   iti  uktvā āha tatra yad  tṛtīyam saptadaśam ahar  tad  trayastriṃśasya sthānam abhiparyāharanti sa uttarāṇām stomānām avyavāyāya trayāṇām ca saptadaśānām anūcīna tāyāi iti yadi  etau svarasāmānau gavāmāyanikānām dharmāṇām grāhakau tatra etā   api saptadaśau tathā atra trayaḥ saptadaśā anūcīnā bhavanti tatra etad  vacanam yujyate trayāṇām saptadaśānām anūcīnatāyāḥ  iti tathā āgrayaṇe dyāv āpṛthivyam eka kapālam vidhāya āha yad  sarva hutam karoti sā tu  ekā paricakṣā hutaḥ  hutaḥ paryāvartate sā dvitīyā ājyasya eva dyāv āpṛthivyau yajeta iti ājya vidhi pare vākye sarva homam aparyāvṛttim ca vaiśvadevikau dharmau prāptau darśayati tathā maitrāvaruṇyām āmikṣāyām na vājinena pracaranti iti vājinā ijyām vaiśvadevikam dharmam pratiṣedhaṃ   tatas  dharma prāptim darśayati etebhyaḥ  liṅgebhyaḥ  etad  jñāyate yathāsvam dharmāṇām grāhakā iti pratipatti artha karma vājinā ijyām su iṣṭakṛt tulyām matvā etad  uktam āha liṅgam apadiṣṭam kutas  prāptiḥ  iti ucyate lakṣaṇayā prāptiḥ  liṅgāt  tu lakṣaṇa aparigrahaḥ svara sāmatva sāmāyāt  eka kapālatva sāmānyāt āmikṣā sāmānyāt  vā yasya liṅgam artha saṃyogāt  iti  anena prāptiḥ  iti kvacid  chrūyate vāsaḥ  dadāti anaḥ dadāti iti tatra vicāryate kim vāsasaḥ anasaḥ  ca kriyā prāpyate uta na iti tatra āha evam tāvan naḥ parīkṣyam kim karma nimittau   etau śabdau uta ākṛti nimittau   iti yadi karma nimittau tatas  prāpyate atha ākṛti nimittau tatas  na iti kim tāvat  prāptam karma nimittau   iti kutas  karma āgame tad darśanāt  yadā tasmin dravye dāruṇi sūtre vā dārukāreṇa tantuvāyena vā karma kṛtam bhavati tadā etau śabdau pravartete na prāk  atas  vijñāyate karma nimittau   iti yadā karma nimittau tad  etad  ārabhyate karma ja etasmin vāsa ādau dravye śrūyaṃāṇe karma prāpyate katham yūpavat  yathā yūpa śabdaḥ  joṣaṇa ādi kriyā nimittaḥ sa yatra śrūyate tatra joṣaṇa ādyāḥ kriyāḥ prāpyante evam iha api iti atra ucyate na etau karma nimittau kim kāraṇam ye naimittikāḥ śabdāḥ te nimittam upalabhya prayujyante yathā daṇḍī chatri iti imau tu  anupalabhya kriyām ākṛti mātre prayujyete tasmāt  na etau kriyā nimittau   iti atra ucyate ākṛtyā kriyām anumāya tatas  śabdam prayuṅkta iti atra brūmaḥ pratyakṣām nimitta tām gamyamānām utsṛjya adṛṣṭāyām kriyāyām nimittatva kalpanāyām hetuḥ  na asti iti yad  tu uktam kriyā uttara kālam pravṛtti darśanāt  iti atra brūmaḥ prāk  kriyāyāḥ  ākṛtiḥ  anabhivyaktā sā kriyayā abhivyajyate yatas  kriyā uttara kālam śabda prayogaḥ tasmāt  ākṛti nimittau yadā evam tadā siddham rūpam deyam kutas  aśeṣa bhūta tvāt  na atra kriyā śeṣa bhūtā kriyā vācinaḥ śabdasya abhāvāt  yūpe tu pratyakṣa vihitā joṣaṇa ādyāḥ kriyāḥ tasmāt  yūpavat  iti  atulya upanyāsaḥ garga tri rātra ājya dohāni sāmāni prakṛtya śrūyate agnim upanidhāya stuvata iti tatra viśayaḥ kim laukikaḥ  agniḥ  upanidheyaḥ uta vaidika iti kim prāptam vaidika iti kutas  sarva karma artha utpannaḥ  asau yāni  aham karmāṇi kariṣye yaiḥ  ca asmi  adhikṛta iti atas  vaidika upanidheya iti evam prāpte ucyate viśaye laukikaḥ syāt  sarva artha tvāt etasmin viśaye laukikam vaidikam iti laukikaḥ syāt  atha yad  uktam vaidikam sarva karma artham utpannam tasmāt  tad upanidheyam iti atra brūmaḥ na vaidikam agni dravyam śāstreṇa utpāditam tasya śāstreṇa eva kāryam nirdiṣṭam yad āhavanīye juhoti itīy ārabhya tasmin sarva arthe kalpyamāne nirdeśaḥ  anarthakaḥ syāt  tasmāl laukikaḥ  agniḥ  upanidheyaḥ sarva artha tvam ca eṣām sve sve kārye vartamānānām bhaviṣyati evam ubhayam aviruddham sarva artha tvam nirdeśaḥ  ca iti atha dhaiṣṇā agnayaḥ kasmān na upanidhīyante atra ucyate itareṣām api  agnīnām dhaiṣṇyānām tathā utpattiḥ na sarva artha iti  arthaḥ kutas  sama tvāt  ete api itaraiḥ  agnibhiḥ samāḥ eteṣām api nirdiṣṭam kāryam prāk  āsīnaḥ  dhiṣṇyān āghārayati iti atas te na upanidheyā iti ekādaśinyām śrūyte upaśayaḥ  yūpaḥ  bhavati iti tatra saṃdehaḥ kim etad  upaśaya dravyam saṃskṛtam joṣaṇa ādayaḥ saṃskārā atra kartavyāḥ uta na iti kim yuktam saṃskṛtam syat  kartavyā atra joṣaṇa ādayaḥ saṃskārāḥ kutas  tad śabda tvāt  ayam yūpa śabdaḥ saṃskāra nimittaḥ sa eṣaḥ  asatsu saṃskāreṣu na upapadyate tasmāt  te kāryā iti na vā kartavyāḥ kutas  ayajña śeṣa tvāt  ete saṃskārā asmin kāṣṭhe kriyante etena dvāreṇa yajatinā saṃbhatsyante ittham saṃskṛte kāṣṭhe niyuktena paśunā yajiḥ kriyamāṇaḥ  apūrvam nirvartayati asmin   ca upaśaye na paśuḥ  niyujyate tatra kṛtāḥ saṃskārā anarthakāḥ syuḥ nanu vacana sāmarthyāt  adṛṣṭa arthā bhaviṣyanti ucyate na atra vacanam yūpaḥ kartavya iti vartamāna apadeśaḥ  ayam nanu vartamāna apadeśaḥ  api na ghaṭate saṃskārāṇām abhāve ucyate bhaktyā bhaviṣyati yathā yaja mānaḥ  vai yūpa iti āha tatra sādṛśyāt  iha punar  katham iti ucyate guṇānām abhidhāna tvāt  yūpa guṇānām yūpa saṃskārāṇām abhidhāna tvāt  yūpa saṃskārāḥ tatra kecid  artha prāptāḥ  chedana ādayaḥ  tūṣṇīṃkṛtāḥ santi taiḥ  ayam abhidhīyate yūpa iti  ayūpaḥ san yathā snātā kanyān alaṃkṛtā mālāguṇena api  alaṃkṛtā iti evam eka deśena api saṃskārāṇām saṃskṛta iti stutyā abhidhīyate agnau śrūyate pṛṣṭhaiḥ  upatiṣṭhanta iti tatra cintyate kim pṛṣṭha dharmāḥ kartavyāḥ uta na iti ke punar  te sāmānya dharmā hiṃkāra ādayaḥ viśeṣa dharmāḥ rathantare prastūyamāne pṛthivīm manasā dhyāyet  bṛhati samudram iti evamādayaḥ kim tāvat  prāptam tatas  āha etad  tāvan naḥ parīkṣyam kim ayam pṣṭha śabdaḥ karmaṇaḥ  vācakaḥ uta dravyasya iti nanu siddham etad  karma nāmadheyam pṛṣṭha śabda iti yasmin guṇa upadeśaḥ pradhānataḥ abhisaṃbandha iti  atra tāsu  eva codanāsu  etad  uktam saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni vairūpam pṛṣṭham vairājam pṛṣṭham iti idānīm pṛṣṭhaiḥ  upatiṣṭhanta iti  asyām cintyate kim punar  atra yuktam tatas  āha karmaṇaḥ pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ syāt  kutas  tathābhūta upadeśāt tathābhūtaḥ san   upadeśaḥ yatra ayam pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ karma nāma adhigataḥ tathābhūta u ayam api kim asya tathā tvam pṛṣṭha śabda sāmānyam pṛṣṭha śabdas tatra karma vacanaḥ  adhigataḥ sa eva ayam tasmāt  iha api tad vacana eva avagantavyaḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt yadi  anya arthaḥ kalpyate ekaḥ śabdaḥ  aneka arthaḥ syāt  tatra kaḥ  doṣaḥ śabda uccarite saṃśayaḥ syāt  na artha pratyayaḥ tatra vyavahāraḥ  na sidhyet  vyavahāra arthaḥ  ca śabda prayogaḥ kāraṇa antaram ca prakaraṇa ādi apekṣyam ekārtha tve tu nirapekṣaḥ  artha pratyayaḥ tasmāt  aneka artha tvam anyāyyam tasmāt  karma nāma pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ yadā karma nāma tadā yadi tāvat  tāni karmāṇi iha upadiśyante tatra utpattiḥ  eṣām anarthikā atha mā bhūd eṣa doṣa iti  etad  upasthānam tatra vijñāyate tatas  idam prakaraṇam bādhyeta tasmāt  sādṛśya vidhiḥ  ayam pṛṣṭheḥ  upatiṣṭhante pṛṣṭha sadṛśaiḥ karmabhiḥ  upatiṣṭhanta iti tad sādṛśyam ca dharmaiḥ  bhavati tasmāt  kartavyā dharmā iti na ca etad  evam karmaṇaḥ pṛṣṭha śabda iti kim tarhi dravyeṣu pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ syāt  ṛc dravyeṣu  abhitvā śūra na unuma iti evamādīnām ṛcām vācakaḥ kutas  abhidhāna upadeśāt abhidhāna upadeśaḥ  ayam pṛṣṭhaiḥ  upatiṣṭhanta iti pṛṣṭhaiḥ  abhidadhāti iti  arthaḥ katham punar  ayam upasthāna vacanaḥ  abhidhāna arthaḥ śakyaḥ  vijñātum ucyate upagraha viśeṣāt  mantra karaṇa upatiṣṭhateḥ  ātmanepadam bhavati mantras tu  abhidhānasya karaṇam na upa sthānasya upasthānam śarīreṇa kriyate manasā vā tasmāt  abhidhāna arthaḥ sa eṣa vipratiṣedhaḥ yadi pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ karmasu kalpyate ātmanepadam bādhyate na hi tadā mantraḥ karaṇam bhavati atha ātmanepadam anurudhyate upasthāna vipratiṣedhaḥ tadā abhidhāna artha tā āpatati tatra ātmanepada anurodhaḥ  nyāyyaḥ pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ  hi lakṣaṇayā pṛṣṭha sādhanam mantram bruvan   arthavān bhavati ātmanepadam tu mantra karaṇena eva upapadyate atas  pṛṣṭha sādhaneṣu mantreṣu pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ āha na etad  yuktam upasthāna artha tā hi śrutyā upatiṣṭhateḥ ātmanepadāl liṅgāt  abhidhātā artha tā na ca liṅgena śrutiḥ  bādhitavyā ucyate na eva atra śrutiḥ  bādhyate sva artham eva upatiṣṭhatiḥ  āha samīpa sthānam tad  tu  abhidhānāya abhidhānam nirvartayitum agni samīpe tiṣṭhet  iti tiṣṭhatiḥ  āha ātmanā īpadāt  tatas  avirodhaḥ āha evam api  abhidhānasya mantraḥ karaṇam na upatiṣṭhateḥ tatra asaṃbandha eva upasthānasya mantreṇa tathā pṛṣṭhaiḥ  upatiṣṭhanta iti samuccāraṇam anarthakam syāt  ucyate abhidhānam abhinirvartayan mantra upasthānasya karaṇam bhavati yatas  asya prayojanam nirvartayati na hi niṣprayojanam anuṣṭhīyate tasmāt  mantreṣu  eva pṛṣṭha śabdaḥ mantreṣu ced  na asti dharmāṇām prāptiḥ na hi mantrāṇām dharmāḥ adharmakāḥ  ta iti anārabhya kiṃcid  chrūyate sauryam carum nirvapet  brahmavarcasa kāma iti tatra eṣaḥ  arthaḥ samadhigataḥ yāgaḥ  ayam codyata iti yajati s tu dravya phala bhoktṛ saṃyogāt  eṣām karma saṃbandhāt  iti tathā idam api  uktam karma phalayoḥ saṃbandhe karma guṇataḥ phalam pradhānata iti pratyartham ca abhisaṃyogāt  karmataḥ  hi  abhisaṃbandhaḥ tasmāt  karma upadeśaḥ syāt  iti idam api ca uktam yajir apūrvam sādhayati tatas  ca apūrvāt  kāla antare phalam bhavati iti codanā punar  ārambha iti  atra evam etasmin sati sauryam carum nirvapet  brahmavarcasa kāma iti  atra saurya yāgena apūrvam kṛtvā brahmavarcasam sādhayet  brahmavarcasa kāma iti  evam vijñāyate āha yatra tṛtīyā yuktaḥ  yajiḥ tatra yuktaḥ  guṇa bhāva abhyupagamaḥ yathā jyotiṣṭomena svarga kāmaḥ  yaja iti iti iha tu  asatyām tṛtīyāyām katham tṛtīya arthaḥ  gamyata iti ucyate kim atra tṛtīyā nirdiṣṭena yajinā kāryam yadā svabhāva siddhaḥ karmaṇām phalam prati guṇa bhāvaḥ yatra api  asau śrutaḥ tatra api  akiṃcitkara eva gata artha tvāt tathā yatra api dvitīyā śrutiḥ yathā agnihotram juhuyāt  iti tatra api vibhakti vyatyayaḥ vā īpsita tvasya vā avivakṣā kāmam vānarthakyam syāt  na tu kathaṃcid  api karmaṇaḥ prati guṇa bhāvaḥ śakyaḥ  apahnotum tasmāt  yāgena apūrva sādhanam atra ucyate tatra yāgaḥ  vijñāyate laukikaḥ  asau padārthaḥ tena tu katham apūrvam sādhyata iti  etad  na vijñāyate iha tu yāgena apūrvam sādhayet  iti  etāvat  eva uktam katham sādhayet  iti itikartavyatā na uktā yeṣām ca arthānām jñāyata eva iti kartavyatā teṣām kartavyatva mātram upadiśyate yathā odanam pacet  iti yeṣām tu na jñāyate te saha iti kartavya tayā eva upadiśyante yathā darśa pūrṇamāsau evam ced  nūnam jñāyate yāgena apūrva nirvṛttau   itikartavya tā yasmāt  uktā tasmāt  nūnam asau   asti iti āha yadi  asti loke tatas  jñāyeta eva atha na asti  eva katham śakyā jñātum iti ucyate bāḍham asti laukikī vaidikī ca laukikī tāvat  pārvaṇa sthālī pāka ādiṣu vaidikī darśa pūrṇamāsa ādiṣu yadi tad pūrvā etāḥ  codanās tad apekṣāḥ saurya yāgena apūrvam sādhayet  yathā ajñātayā itikartavyatayā iti tatas  yukta itikartavya tāyā avidhiḥ na ca vidhīyate ata itikartavya tāyā avidheḥ  yajateḥ pūrvavat tvam vihita iti kartavya tāka tvam iti atha ya āhuḥ yajeta yāgam kuryāt  iti juhuyāt  homam kuryāt  iti teṣām kim na eva dharma ākāṅkṣā bhavati bhavati iti brūmaḥ yadi  api prajñāta iti kartavyataḥ  yajir dravyam devatām pratyutsṛjyata iti tathā api yadā phala arthaḥ kriyate tadā dharmān ākāṅkṣati na hi  adharmāt  phalam bhavati katham jñāyate yaḥ  hi  amedhyam dravyam ucchiṣṭaḥ śayānaḥ  vā prauḍha pādaḥ  vāmena hastena vā pādena yathā kathaṃcid  devatāyai utsṛjati tasya phalam na bhavati iti śiṣṭāḥ smaranti yaḥ  tu medhyam dravyam śucau deśe prayataḥ prāṅmukhaḥ  dakṣiṇena hastena samāhita manā mantravan niyama vac ca devatāyai utsṛjati tasya phalam bhavati iti smaranti tasmāt  yāvān yajatiḥ phalāyāmnāyate sa sarvaḥ  dharmān ākāṅkṣati atas teṣām api  asti dharma ākāṅkṣā satyām ākāṅkṣāyām sannihitaiḥ  dharmaiḥ  avipratiṣiddhaḥ saṃbandhaḥ prakṛtau vikṛtau tu  ānumānikaiḥ adhunā evam cintyate kim aniyamaḥ  laukikī vaidikī vetikartavyatā uta laukiky eva āhosvit  vaidikī iti atra viśeṣa abhāvāt  aniyame prāpte ucyate sa laukikaḥ syāt  sa khalu kartavyatā upāyaḥ  laukikaḥ syāt  kutas  dṛṣṭa pravṛtti tvāt  dṛṣṭā hi  asya tatra tatra pravṛttiḥ yathā pārvaṇa sthālīpāke aṣṭakācarau āgrahāyaṇīya karmaṇi iti  evam yatra yatra yāgena apūrvam sādhyate tatra tatra asya pravṛttiḥ  dṛṣṭā atas  anvayāt  vijñāyate yāgasya apūrvam sādhayataḥ  ayam abhyupāya iti ayam ca api yāgaḥ tasmāt  asya api sa eva abhyupāyaḥ āha kim eṣa eva utsargaḥ sarvatra lokikī itikartavyatā iti evam khalu prāptam evam prāpte brūmaḥ vacanāt  tu tatas  anya tvam iti yatra pratyakṣam vacanam vaidikyāḥ tatra na laukikī syāt  vacana sāmarthyāt  vaidikī eva syāt  yathā upasatsu gṛhamedhīye ca liṅgena vetikartavyatā niyamyeta katarā yasyāḥ  liṅgam vaidikya āś ca liṅgam tasmāt  vaidikī kim punar  liṅgam saurye tāvac carau śrūyate prayāje kṛṣṇalam juhoti iti tathā aindra bārhaspatye ardham barhiṣaḥ  lunāti ardham na svayam ditam ardham vedyām karoti  ardham na iti tathā pitṛ yajñena hotāram vṛṇīte na ārṣā iyam iti etaiḥ  liṅgaiḥ  jñāyate vaidikī iti kartavyatā iti katham tad guṇa tvāt  ete hi prayājādayaḥ  vaidikasya apūrvasya guṇāḥ yadi ca tadīyā iti kartavya tā pravartitā tatas  eteṣu karmasu  ete santi tatra etāni vacanāni  upapadyante prayāje prayāje kṛṣṇalam juhoti iti evamādīni tasmāt  vaidikī iti kartavya tā niyamyeta api vā na evam syāt  vaidikī iti kartavyatā iti yad  kāraṇam etaiḥ  liṅgaiḥ  na śakyate vaidikī niyantum kutas  anyāya pūrva tvāt  nyāya pūrvakam hi vacanam tad sādhakam bhavati na ca etāni nyāya pūrvāṇi na hi vaidikyāḥ pravṛttiḥ  yuktā nibaddhā hi sā prakaraṇa ādibhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ  darśa pūrṇamāsa ādiṣu katham tarhi  etāni liṅgāni ucyate yatra nitya anuvāda vacanāni syuḥ iha tāvat  ardham barhiṣaḥ  lunāti  ardham na iti barhis  yatra eva bhava eṣyati yad  kāraṇam sataḥ  barhiṣa ucyate na ca iha asti barhiḥ na hotāram vṛṇīte na ārṣā iyam iti nitya anuvādaḥ  bhaviṣyati nanu nitya anuvādaḥ san   anartha kaḥ bhavati kim kriyatām yasya arthaḥ  na asti prayāje prayāje kṛṣṇalam juhoti iti vacanam prayājānām bhaviṣyati katham punar  atra prayājāḥ  ca kṛṣṇa lahomaś ca śakyaḥ  vaktum bhidyate hi tathā vākyam evam tarhi na prayājān vakṣyati prayāje kṛṣṇa lahomam vidhāsyati na ca asatsu prayājeṣu kṛṣṇa lahomaḥ śakyate kartum iti  arthāt  prāyājān kariṣyati tasmāt  na liṅgena vaidikyā niyamaḥ yathā uktena nyāyena laukikī itikartavyatā iti tatra āha atha kasmān nobhe api itikartavyate saha pravartete iti kim evam bhaviṣyati evam tulya apekṣā karmaṇām anyataratas  na bādhitā bhavati ucyate saha pravṛttau   ekayā ced  karma nirapekṣam kṛtam dvitīyasyāḥ pravṛttiḥ  vipratiṣiddhā atas  mithas  pravṛtteḥ  vipratiṣedhāt  yathā artha kalpanā syāt  ekasyāḥ pravṛttiḥ syāt  iti arthaḥ katham ekasyāḥ pravṛtteḥ  dharmāṇām yathā artha kalpanā bhavati ye dharmā yeṣu kāryeṣu pravṛttau   utpannāḥ ta iha api teṣu  eva bhavanti itarathā dvitīyasya dharmā ayathārthā bhaveyuḥ pūrvaiḥ  dharmaiḥ teṣām kāryāṇām nirvartita tvāt  evam ekasyāḥ pravṛtteḥ  yathā artha kalpanā bhavati atas  yathā artha kalpanā syāt  iti  anena ekasyāḥ pravṛttiḥ  iti  uktam bhavet  ekasyāḥ pravṛttau yathā uktena eva nyāyena laukikyāḥ pravṛttiḥ  iti tuśabdaḥ pakṣa nivṛttau na tu  evam syāt  laukikī itikartavyatā iti kim tarhi vaidikī niyamyeta kutas  bhāgi tvāt  vaidiky api bhāginī pravṛtteḥ sā api hi  apūrvasya iti kartavyatā samāne ca bhāgitva ubhayoḥ  vaidiky eva syāt  guṇānām abhidhāna tvāt  guṇā ete prayāja ādayaḥ saurya ādiṣu dṛśyamānā abhidhāyakā bhavanti  etasya arthasya yathā vaidiky atra itikartavyatā iti bodhakā bhavanti iti  arthaḥ kasmāt  saṃbandhāt  ete hi tayā iti kartavya tayā saṃbaddhāḥ atas  sāhacaryāt  tām gamayanti abhidhānavat  yathā kauṇḍapāyinām ayana agnihotram iti  abhidhānam karmaṇaḥ  vācakam tad karma sahacaritān dharmān ānayati teṣu  asatsu  etad  abhidhānam iha na yujyata iti teṣām dharmāṇām tatra bhāvaḥ vijñāyate evam iha api prayāja ādīnām darśanam asatyam vaidikyām na yujyata iti tasyāḥ  api iha bhāvaḥ vijñāsyate nanu  asati nyāye liṅgam akāraṇam satyam evam ukta s tu nyāyaḥ  bhāgi tvāt  iti yad  tu dṛṣṭa pravṛttiḥ  laukikī iti tatra brūmaḥ yadi  api dṛṣṭa pravṛttiḥ syāt  tathā api vaidiky eva niyamyeta katham yathā dhenuḥ kiśoreṇa tad  yathā kṛṣṇa kiśorā dhenuḥ  iti yadi  api dhenu śabdaḥ  godhenvām dṛṣṭa pravṛttiḥ tathā api  abhidhāna sāmānyāt  aśvadhenvām api bhāgi iti kiśoreṇa liṅgena aśvadhenvām vijñāyate evam iha api yadi  api laukikī dṛṣṭa pravṛttiḥ tathā api iti kartavyatā sāmānyena bhāgi tvāl liṅgena vaidikī vijñeyā atha vā na eva liṅgena niyama iti kutas  utpattīnām sama tvāt  dharmāṇām prayāja ādīnām utpattayaḥ samāḥ sarveṣām āgneya ādi aṅga bhāvena na paraspara aṅga tvena kim atas  yadi prayāja ādīnām anuyājādayaḥ  aṅgāni syuḥ tatas  yatra pradhānam tatra aṅgāni iti prayāja darśanena anuyājādayaḥ  anumīyeran yadā tu sama pradhānā ete tadā prayāja darśanena kāmam prayājā anumīyeran prayāja dharmā vā na tu  anuyāja ādayaḥ tasmāl liṅgam aniyāmakam yad  tu  abhidhānavat  iti atra brūmaḥ yuktam tatra tatra hi para śabdaḥ paratra prayuktaḥ san dharmān atidiśati iti  uktam api ca vidhiḥ  asau agnihotravat  dhotavyam iti ayam punar  anuvādaḥ tena atra prayāja ādīnām eva na asti prāptiḥ kutaḥ anuyāja ādīnām tasmāt  viṣama upanyāsaḥ abhidhānavat  iti atas  yathā adhikāram bhāvaḥ syāt  ye dharmā yasya apūrvasya adhikāra āmnātā as te tatra eva bhaveyuḥ evam tarhi sauryam carum nirvapet  iti  anena ākhyātena pradhānasya vidhāna utpattiḥ śeṣāṇām ca vacanam bhavatu katham kṛtvā na anaṅgam pradhānam ucyamānam kasmaicid  prayojanāya kalpata iti tena ca prāpitānām aṅgānām etebhyaḥ  liṅgebhyaḥ  viśeṣa avadhāraṇam bhaviṣyati tatra idam ucyate ekasmin  śabde pradhānasya utpattiḥ  aṅgānām ca vacanam na saṃbhavati kim kāraṇam utpannam hi pradhānam aṅgān apekṣate apekṣayā ca tāni gṛhyante tasmāt  na etad  api yuktam yadi ca nirvapet  iti  anena śabdena aṅgāni  api vidhīyeran tatas  teṣām api phala saṃbandhaḥ syāt  tathā aṅga tvam eva vyāhanyeta tatas  ayam api vādaḥ  na ghaṭate tasmāt  yathā uktaḥ  laukika eva abhyupāyaḥ vidhyantaḥ  vā saurya ādikāyām codanāyām pravarteta na dharmā laukikāḥ kaḥ punar  ayam vidhyantaḥ  nāma vidheḥ  antaḥ vidhyantaḥ atha vidhiḥ kaḥ yad  vākyam upalabhya puruṣaḥ kasmiṃścid  arthe pravartate kutaścid  vā nivartate sa vidhiḥ vidhīyate hi  anena arthaḥ yathā loke devadatta gām abhyāja śuklām iti tasya abhyāja ityādiḥ itaraḥ  antar  vede api darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta iti vidhi ādiḥ vidhyantaḥ  api pradhāna vidhi varjitam kṛtsnam pauroḍāśikam brāhmaṇam tena sametaḥ  ayam vidhi ādiḥ  viśiṣṭa apūrva nirvṛttim prati puruṣam pravartayati tasmāt  saḥ  asya antar  tathā somena yajeta iti vidhi ādiḥ saumikam api brāhmaṇam vidhyantaḥ eṣa vidhyantaḥ  nāma eteṣu ca saurya ādiṣu vidhi ādiḥ  asti vidhyantaḥ  na asti eteṣu  api sa vidhyantaḥ kalpyeta katham kṛtvā aparipūrṇam yad  vākyam tad  adhyāhāreṇa vā pūryeta vyavahita kalpanayā vā tatra adhyāhārāt  vyavahita kalpanā jyāyasī adhyāhāre hi  aśrutaḥ kalpyeta itaratra śrutena saṃbandhaḥ tasmāt  vyavahitaḥ  brāhmaṇa avayavaḥ  asya paripūrakaḥ kalpyate yathā vasantāya kapiñjalān ālabhate grīṣmāya kalaviṅkān ālabhata iti tena vaidikī iti kartavya tā prāpyate yadi tad  brāhmaṇam asya antar  kalpyate tatra na bhavati tad  etad mayūra nṛtyam āpadyate tad  yathā mayūrasya nṛtyataḥ  anyat apāvriyate anyat  saṃvriyate evam iha api idam saṃvriyate tad apāvriyate na eṣa doṣaḥ pratyakṣas tasya tatra bhāvaḥ iha punar  ānumānikaḥ na ca anumānikam pratyakṣam bādhate iha tarhi na prāpnoti pratyakṣa virodhāt  syāt  evam yadi virodhaḥ syāt  na tu  asti virodhaḥ tatra api bhaviṣyati iha api tad  etad  uktam vidhyantaḥ  vā prakṛti vac codanāyām pravarteta iti ucyate prakṛtivat  iti kim āha aṣṭame prakṛti niyamam kariṣyati iyam asya prakṛtiḥ  iti tad  ucyate vidhyantaḥ  vā prakṛteḥ  iva pravarteta yā yā tasya karmaṇaḥ prakṛtiḥ  iti yasya āgneyaḥ prakṛtiḥ tasya āgneyāt  eva yasya agnīṣomīyaḥ tasya agnīṣomīyāt  iti  evam sarvatra atha kasmān na laukikaḥ  vidhyantaḥ kalpyate ucyate laukikasya vidheḥ  abhāvāt  vidhyanta eva na asti kutas  tad  kalpanā iti āha laukikī itikartavya tā prāpyatām kim vidhi anta kalpanayā iti ucyate vaidikī hi  atra iti kartavyatā na laukikī kasmāt  tathā hi liṅga darśanam prayāja ādi samarthitam bhavati yadi liṅgāt  vaidikaḥ  abhyupāyaḥ bhavati tena tarhi  aliṅge laukikam syāt  yatra karmaṇi kiṃcid  liṅgam na asti tatra laukikam syāt  vidhānam yathā aindrāgnam ekādaśa kapālam nirvapet  yasya sajāta  īyuḥ  iti atra ucyate syāt  evam yadi liṅga hetukaḥ vaidika upāyaḥ syāt  na tu  asau liṅga hetukaḥ kiṃhetuka s tu vidhi anta hetukaḥ vidhyantaḥ  api nyāya pūrvaḥ sa ca nyāya s tulyaḥ sarveṣām karmaṇām vaikṛtānām liṅgavatām ca kutas  codanā śabda sāmānyāt karma codanāyām śābdaḥ samānaḥ sarvatra vidhi ādiḥ  asti na vidhyantaḥ tulya ś cāpekṣayā anyatra śrutena vidhyantena saṃbandhaḥ tad  etad  nyāya pūrvakam liṅgam ekatra api dṛśyamānam tulya nyāyānām sarveṣām dharmavat tām jñāpayati yathā sthālyām tulya pākānām pulākānām ekam upamṛdyāni  eṣām api siddha tām jānāti tulyaḥ  hetuḥ  asya ca anyeṣām ca siddhatvasya iti tasmāt  sarvatra vaidikī iti kartavya tā atha yad  uktam dṛṣṭa pravṛttiḥ  laukikī itikartavyatā iti atra brūmaḥ sāmānyatodṛṣṭam etad  upadiśyate sāmānyatodṛṣṭam ca yad  avyabhicāri tad  pramāṇam savyabhicāram ca etad  dṛṣṭā hi gaṇa yāgāt ayaḥ  aneva miti kartavya tākāḥ tasmāt  dṛṣṭa pravṛtti tvāt  iti  ahetuḥ yad  tu vaidikyā bhāgi tvāt  tad pūrvakāṇi liṅgāni bhaviṣyanti iti atra brūmaḥ bhāgi tvasya apūrva iti kartavya tāka tvam kila hetuḥ tad  bhāvaḥ  ca tasyāḥ śabda pūrvaḥ śabdena ca darśa pūrṇamāsayoḥ  asau vijñāyate na sarvatra iti tasmāt  na bhāgi tvam atas  vidhyantena eva itikartavyatā prāpyate na anyathā atha kasmāt  etāni vaikṛtāni vākyāni nyūnāni  eva na anumanyante kim ebhiḥ pūritaiḥ nyūnāni  anarthakāni bhavanti bhavantu kaḥ  doṣaḥ śiṣṭaiḥ  eṣām saṃparigrahaḥ  na yujyate pramādāt  bhaviṣyati iti na asti  akṣare mātrāyām vā pramādaḥ kutaḥ etāvati granthe bhaviṣyati katham tulyam ca sāṃpradāyikam iti  uktam vyāmohaḥ  api viduṣām yuga sahasrāṇi bahūni na anuvarteta yujyate ca eṣām apekṣayā pūraṇam tasmāt  ūnāni na anumanyante atas  vaidikī iti kartavyatā iti siddham prajā kāmā gavāmayanam upeyuḥ  iti satram vidhāyām nāyate jyotiḥ  gauḥ  āyuḥ  iti gavāmayane dvādaśa ahikaḥ  vidhyanta iti vakṣyati gaṇeṣu dvādaśa ahasya iti tatra ca udakena dvādaśa ahikā dharmāḥ prāpyante eka ahānām api yathā svam nāmabhiḥ prātisvikāḥ ye tatra dvādaśa ahikā aikāhikaiḥ  aviruddhāḥ te yathāprāptam kriyante viruddheṣu saṃśayaḥ kim dvādaśa ahikaḥ  dharmaḥ kartavyaḥ uta ekāhika iti kim prāptam tatra sūtreṇa eva upakramaḥ dvādaśa ahikam ahar gaṇe tad prakṛti tvāt dvādaśa aha prakṛti tvāt  vidhyantena eva prāpyante nanu  evam nāmadheyam bādhyate na bādhiṣyate nāmadheyam jyotiḥ  ādi adhika āgamāt  bhaviṣyati ye jyautiṣṭaumikebhyaḥ  adhikāḥ stotra śastra vikārāḥ tad āgamāt ekāhavat yathā tasmin   eva jyotiṣy eka ahe jyotiḥ śabdaḥ  adhika āgamāt  bhavati satsu jyautiṣṭaumikeṣu jyotiṣṭome abhāvāt  adhika dharma arthaḥ  ayam śabdaḥ na ca adhikānām dvādaśa ahikaiḥ  virodhaḥ  asti tasmāt  dvādaśa ahikam dharma jātam viruddham kartavyam iti adhika āgamāt  tad ākhyam syāt  eka ahava d iti  etasya aparā vyākhyā ye dvādaśa ahe adhikā aikāhikebhyaḥ kecid  dharmā ucyante abhiplavaḥ  anvaham bhavati gorivītam anvaham bhavati iti teṣām adhikānām āgamāt  tad ākhyam syāt  etad  dvādaśa ahikam aharjyotiḥ ākhyam āyuḥ ākhyam vā katham ekāhavat yathā tasmin   eva eka ahe ayam jyotiḥ ādi śabdaḥ  jyautiṣṭaumikebhyaḥ  adhikeṣu vaiśeṣikeṣu dharmeṣu  āgateṣu bhavati evam iha api  adhika āgama sāmānyāt  gauṇaḥ  bhaviṣyati yathā ṣāḍahikānām pṛṣṭhānām bhāvāt  eka ahaḥ viśva jit  ṣaṣ aha iti  uktam tam eka aham ṣaṣ aha iti  ācakṣata iti evam iha api gauṇaḥ  ced  na prāpakaḥ tasmāt  na asti nāmadheyāt  dharma prāptiḥ  iti liṅgāt  ca etad  jñāyate yathā dvādaśa ahikam kartavyam iti kim liṅgam bhavati dvābhyām lomāvadyati dvābhyām tvacam dvābhyām asṛk  dvābhyām māṃsam iti evam ṣaṣ dvikān anukramya āha yad  dvādaśa upasadaḥ  bhavanti ātmānam etad  nirvadyata iti dvādaśa ahikam dharmam dvādaśa upasattvam darśayati tad  upapadyate yadi dvādaśa ahikam dharma jātam virodhi kartavyam itarathā ca ekāhikam ṣaṣ upasattvam syāt  tasmāt  paśyāmaḥ dvādaśa ahikam kartavyam iti tathā idam aparam liṅgam yasya atiriktam ekādaśinyām ālabheran na priyam bhrātṛvyam atiricyeta atha yad  dvau paśū samasyeyus  kanīya āyuḥ kurvīran yadi  ete brāhmaṇavantaḥ paśava ālambhante na apriyam bhrātṛvyam atyatiricyate na kanīya āyuḥ kurvīta iti ekādaśinyām vihāram dvādaśa ahikam dharmam darśayati katham vihāre sati  atirekaḥ paśūnām āpadyate atireka bhayāt  ca dvayoḥ  dvayoḥ samāsaḥ eka aha dharma prāptau vihāraḥ  na syāt  tatra etad darśanam na yujyate tasmāt  dvādaśa ahikam kāryam na vā dvādaśa ahikam kāryam kim tarhi ekāhikam kim kāraṇam ca udakena dvādaśa ahikam prāpnoti nāmadheyena eka āhikam nāmadheyam ca ca udakāt  balīyaḥ kutas  pratyakṣa tvāt  pratyakṣam nāmadheyam ca udakam tu  ānumānikam nanu vidhyantaḥ  api pratyakṣaḥ satyam prakṛtau pratyakṣaḥ  vidhyantaḥ vikṛtau tu  ānumānikaḥ nāmadheyam punar  vikṛtau   api pratyakṣam pratyakṣam ca anumānāt  balīyaḥ tasmāt  aikāhikam kāryam nanu  adhikāryam nāmadheyam iti  uktam atra ucyate adhikānām aśabda tvam adhikānām śabdaḥ  na asti ime jyotiḥ ādayaḥ śabdāḥ karma nāmadheyāni iti  uktam api vā nāmadheyam syāt  yad  utpattau   apūrvam avidhāyaka tvāt  iti yad  tu adhika āgamāt  tad ākhyam syāt  iti tatra brūmaḥ vacanāt  adhika āgamaḥ  na nāmadheyena yad  tu teṣu  asatsu śabdasya abhāvāt  iti na ete kadācid  āyuḥ ādiṣu na santi katham teṣām abhāve śabdasya abhāvaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ yad  tu jyotiṣṭome na asti jyotiḥ ādiḥ śabda iti karma antara tvāt jyotiṣṭoma āyuḥ ādiḥ śabdaḥ  na asti na dharma abhāvāt tasmāt  aikāhikam viruddham dharma jātam kartavyam iti adhika āgamāt  tad ākhyam syāt  eka ahava d iti  etasya dvitīya vyākhyā parihāraḥ gauṇaḥ san   anu vāda mātram anarthakam syāt  tasmāt  pūrva uktena nyāyena nāmadheyam dharmāṇām prāpakam iti atha yal liṅgam upadiṣṭam dvādaśa upasattva darśanam tasya parihāra ucyate liṅgam saṃghāta dharmaḥ syāt  liṅgam etad saṃghāta dharmaḥ syāt  dvādaśa ahaḥ  ahar saṃghātaḥ sa phalāya codyate dvādaśa aham ṛddhi kāmā upeyuḥ  iti gavāmayanam api ahar saṃghāta antaram tasmin   eva kārye phala siddhau vidhīyate tasya tad kārya āpattyā dvādaśa aha dharmān gṛhṇāti na ca udakena dravyavat  yathā dravye vrīhau dharmāḥ śrutāḥ  te tad kārya āpanneṣu pratinidhi bhūteṣu prāpyante na ca udakena tadvat  na etad  yuktam kutas  artha dharma tvāt  apūrva dharma tvāt  iti  arthaḥ apūrva dharmaḥ  dvādaśa upasattvam na saṃghāta dharmaḥ kasmāt  saṃghātasya guṇa tvāt  ahāni  atra pradhānāni dvādaśa ahena iti dvādaśa tvam teṣām guṇaḥ viśeṣaṇam iti  arthaḥ viśiṣya eva kāryam pratīyate na viśeṣaṇe yathā rāja puruṣa ānīyatām iti  ukte puruṣa ānīyate na rājā yathā ca mṛṣṭam bhuṅkte devadatta iti  ukte na śākam sūpaḥ  vā pratīyate yad  eva pradhānam tad  pratīyate kim atas  atas  ahāni phalavanti na saṃghātaḥ phalavataś ca dharmāḥ tasmāt  na dvādaśa upasattvam saṃghāta dharmaḥ evam ced  na gavāmayane kārya āpattitaḥ  dharmāḥ prāpyante atas  aparihāraḥ  ayam gavāmayane dvādaśa ahikam prathamam ahar  prāyaṇīyaḥ  atirātraḥ tasya dharmaḥ  dvādaśa upasattvam tad upādāne mukhyasya anugrahaḥ ṣaṣ upasattva upādāne jaghanyānām jyotiḥ ādīnām mukhyasya prāpta kālam anugraham atikramitum kiṃcid  kāryam na asti atas tad anugraha artham dvādaśa upasattvam bhavati tathā mukhyayā pravṛttyā niyatasya etad darśanam na ca udaka prāptyā yasmāt  codakaḥ  nāmadheyāt  abalaḥ vakṣyati ca vipratiṣiddha dharmāṇām samavāye bhūyasām syāt  sadharma tvam mukhyam vāpūrva coda nāl lokavat  iti atha yad  dvitīyam liṅga darśanam uktam ekādaśinyām vihāra darśanam tatra ucyate anārabhya ekādaśinyām vihāraḥ śiṣṭaḥ tad ādi prabhavāḥ paśavaḥ syuḥ tathā tān eva anūcīnān aharahar ālabheran āgneyam eva prathame ahani  ālabheran sārasvatīm meṣīm dvitīye saumyam babhrum tṛtīye vāruṇam antatas  atha punar  paryāvarteṣu  āgneyam eva prathame ahani  ālabheran sārasvatīm meṣīm dvitīye saumyam babhrum tṛtīye vāruṇam antata iti tad  anārabhyavādānām prakṛti artha tvāt  jyotiṣṭomam praviṣṭam tatra ahnām bahutvasya abhāvāt  asaṃbhavāt  aparām prakṛtim dvādaśa aham āgatam tatra api punar  jyotiḥ ādīnām paryāvarteṣu  iti  etad  na yujyata iti tṛtīyām prakṛtim gavāmayane praviṣṭam evam āgatasya etad  darśanam iti
